yaḥ śrīmāñ chrīghano loke saddharmaṃ samupādiśat । śāsanāni trilokeṣu jayantu tasya sarvadā ।। athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ pramoditaḥ । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।।
bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tad yathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā deṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ । upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cāpy anumodaya ।। purāsau bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho dayānidhiḥ । dharmarājo jagacchāstā sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ ।।
sarvavidyākalābhijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ । mārajil lokavin nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ ।। śravastyāṃ jetakāraṇye mahodyāne manorame । anāthapiṇḍadākhyasya gṛhasthasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
nānāvṛkṣaiḥ samāpanne nānāpuṣpapraśobhitaiḥ । nānāphalabharānamraiḥ kalpapādapasannibhaiḥ ।। aṣṭāṅgaguṇasaṃpannajalaiḥ padmotpalādibhiḥ । puṣpaiś ca paripūrṇābhiḥ puṣkariṇībhir āśrite ।।
nānājantugaṇaiś cāpi mithasnehanivandhitaiḥ । nānāpakṣigaṇaiś cāpi saṃrāvair upasevite ।। tasmin divyamanoramya ārāme pariśobhite । puṇyakṣetre jināvāse vihāre maṇimaṇḍite ।।
śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvagaṇair api । sarvasatvahitārthena tasthau dharmaṃ prakāśituṃ ।। evaṃ tatra samāsīnaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ dharmadeśinaṃ । dṛṣṭvā dharmottamaṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāyayuḥ ।।
devā daityāś ca siddhāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । grahā vidyādharāś cāpi nāgāś ca garuḍā api ।। sarve api lokapālāś ca munayaś ca maharṣayaḥ । brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo janāḥ ।।
amātyāḥ sādhavaḥ śūdrāḥ sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ । dhanino vaṇijaś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā api ।। tathā jānapadāś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api । evam anye api satvāś ca saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ ।।
pūjāpaṃcopahārāṇi gṛhītvā bhaktisaṃyutāḥ । saddharmaṃ saugataṃ śrotum anumodya samāyayuḥ ।। sarve tatra praviṣṭās te dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ jinaṃ । vismitānaṃditāḥ pūjāṃ kṛtvā natvā yathākramaṃ ।।
sarve tatra samāsīnāḥ parivṛtāḥ puraskṛtāḥ । taṃ dṛṣṭvā sadguruṃ dharmaṃ śrotuṃ tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā lokān sarvān samāhitān । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।।
evaṃ nityam asau nāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthikaḥ । dharmaṃ prakāśayan loke tasthau bhānur ivoditaḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śrāvastyāṃ sanmahājanaḥ । āḍhyaḥ śreṣṭhī mahābhogo vistīrṇasuparigrahaḥ ।।
śrāddho bhadrāśayo dhīmān sarvabandhusuhṛtpriyaḥ । tīrthikaśrāvako mānī babhūva dhanagarvitaḥ ।। tadāsau sundarīṃ bhāryyāṃ kuladharmasamānikāṃ । nītvā kāmaguṇāsakto reme nityaṃ tayā saha ।।
tasyaivaṃ ramatas tasyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ sucirād api । putro na duhitā vāpi nodbabhūva kathaṃ cana ।। tad aputro gṛhastho asau putrābhidarśanotsukaḥ । kapolaṃ svakare dhṛtvā vyacintayad raho gataḥ ।।
aho daivān na me putraḥ putrī vādyāpi nāsti yat । tan me syuḥ saṃpado vyarthāyāsāṃ bhoktā na vidyate ।। kiṃ mamaitair dhanai ratnaiḥ kevalaṃ duhkhasādhanaiḥ । yeṣāṃ bhoktā na vidyeta vyarthaṃ mayā hy upārjitaṃ ।।
hy aputrasya jagac chūnyaṃ saṃsāre niḥsukhaṃ mama । yato na varddhate dharmas taj janmāpi ca nisphalaṃ ।। kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yato bhāgyaṃ na vidyate । daivo hi valavāṃl loke kim upāyair guṇair valaiḥ ।।
kutrātra śaraṇaṃ yāsye hy aputro ahaṃ kulāntakaḥ । tan me syāt ko atra sanmitraṃ saṃkaṭe yaḥ samuddharet ।। nūnaṃ me pitaraḥ sarve piṇḍavichedadarśinaḥ । matparaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā bhaviṣyanti nirāśitāḥ ।।
sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo asmi kuladharmavināśakaḥ । kiṃ paratra prabhokṣyāmi ko me piṇḍaṃ pradāsyati ।। iti cintāviṣaṇṇaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve ca bāndhavāḥ । samupetya samāmaṃtrya duhkhahetum apṛchan ।। kiṃ duḥsthito asi sādho atra kiṃ cāpi duḥkhacintayā ।
vaktavyaṃ cet tad asmākaṃ sarvathā vaktum arhasi ।। iti pṛṣṭe gṛhastho asau dīrghaniśvāsam utsṛjan । sarvāṃs tān bāndhavān dṛṣṭvā duḥkhahetum udaharat ।। bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ sarvair mama duḥkhasya kāraṇaṃ ।
yad adyāpi na me putraḥ putrī vāpi na vidyate ।। saṃpado me gṛhe santi sarvaratnasamanvitāḥ । sarvadravyasamṛddhāś ca tāsāṃ bhoktā na vidyate ।। tat sarvaṃ nakṣyate vyarthaṃ mayā yātnair upārjitaṃ ।
aputrasya hi sarvasvaṃ nūnaṃ rājā grahīṣyti ।। aputro ahaṃ hy apuṇyātmā gantavyaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ । pretībhūtasya me ko anyaḥ piṇḍadānaṃ pradāsyati ।। mayā na prakṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃpadarthaprasaṃginā ।
tan me sarvaṃ nirarthaṃ syāt ko māṃ pāpāt samuddharet ।। iha bhogyaṃ prabhuktvāpi kiṃ me sāram avasthitaṃ । kevalaṃ dhanasaktasya paratra sadgatiḥ kathaṃ ।। iti cintā hṛdi sthitvā cittaṃ me tudate aniśaṃ ।
evaṃ cittavyathākrāntaḥ śalyaviddha ivāsmy ahaṃ ।। tad vyathāharaṇopāyaṃ dātavyaṃ mama taddhitaṃ । anyathā ced ihāmutra vinaṣṭaḥ syāṃ nirāśitaḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te bāndhavā janāḥ ।
karuṇāviṣṭacittās taṃ bodhayantaḥ samabruvan ।। mā mā bhaiṣṭhā mahābhāga tyaja cintāṃ vacaḥ śṛṇu । tadupāyaṃ vayaṃ brūmas tat kuruṣva samāhitaḥ ।। devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā kuruṣva vaṃśayācanāṃ ।
nūnaṃ vaṃśaṃ pradāsyanti devatās te prasāditāḥ ।। eṣa loke pravādo asti yad āyācanahetutaḥ । putrā duhitaro vāpi jātā devaprasādataḥ ।। tathā naiva pramāṇaṃ syāc chāstre karmapramāṇataḥ ।
tat tu devaprasādena karmaś śīghraṃ prasiddhyate ।। tad eva devavairuddhe karma vighnair nihanyate । tasmād daivaprasiddhyarthaṃ śraddhābhaktisamāhitaḥ ।। devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā sarvakāryyaṃ prasādhayet ।
iti matvā bhavāṃś cāpi satputrapratipattaye ।। bhāryyayā saha bhaktyā ca devatāyācanāṃ kuru । tato raktaiḥ priyāṃ bhāryām ṛtusnātāṃ prakāmataḥ ।। gāḍham āliṃgya saṃrakto dharmavījaṃ praropaya ।
tato devaprabhāvena suniṣpannaḥ prasiddhitaḥ ।। tvatputraḥ saṃprajāyeta satyam evaṃ pramāṇaya । iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā gṛhastho asau vinoditaḥ ।। tatheti ca pratiśrutya bhāryyayā saha moditaḥ ।
śivabrahmādideveśān iṃdrādidigadhīśvarān ।। jalāśrayavanārāmacatvaramaṇḍapālayān । sūryyādīṃś ca grahān sarvā bhairavādyāś ca mātṛkāḥ ।। svakulādhipatīṃ devān anyāṃś ca tribhavasthitān ।
sarvān evaṃ samārādhya pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ ।। saṃtānaṃ prārthayitvāsau patnyā saha tathāramat । tadā kaścin mahāsatvaḥ svargāc cyutvā bhuvaṃ gataḥ ।। tasya gṛhapateḥ patnyā garbhe sa samupāviśat ।
tataḥ sā śreṣṭhino bhāryyāpannasatvāśu gurviṇī ।। garbhe satvaṃ samutpannaṃ matvā bharttāram abravīt । svāmin prasīda mā bhūs tvaṃ viṣaṇno atra sukhī bhava ।। tava bhāgyād dhi me garbhe nūnaṃ satvaḥ pravarttate । yad garbhe dakṣiṇe bhāge sthitaḥ saṃparivarttate ।।
tan nūnaṃ dārako ayaṃ syāt satyam eva na saṃśayaḥ । iti bhāryāvacaḥ śrutvā gṛhastho asau pramoditaḥ ।। bhāryāyā garbham ālokya satyam ity anvamanyata ।। tato asau sahasā vandhusuhṛnmitrasahāyakān ।
prāhūya puratas teṣāṃ mudaivaṃ samudānayat ।। aho bhāgyān mamotpannaṃ yad abhivāṃchitaṃ mayā । dhanyo asmi nāvagītaḥ syād devatānuprasādataḥ ।। cirābhilaṣitaṃ putramukhaṃ paśyeya sāṃprataṃ ।
kṛtyā me pratikurvīta bhṛtaś ca prativibhṛyāt ।। dāyādyaṃ pratipadyeta vaṃśo me sthitiko bhavet । suhṛdo me prasannāḥ syur dviṣantaś ca viṣāditāḥ ।। mayā yāvanti dānāni puṇyāni prakṛtāni ca ।
etatpuṇyaphalair nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ bhavatu dvayoḥ ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena bhūyān mātā nirāturā । sukhaṃ sunotu satputraṃ mā pāpaṃ samudāgamat ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve bandhusuhṛtsakhāḥ ।
tathāstv ity anumodantaḥ svasvālayaṃ samāyayuḥ ।। tato asau garbhiṇī kāntā kramād garbhapravarddhitā । vaidyopadiṣṭam āhāraṃ bhuktvācarad yathā sukhaṃ ।। tataś ca samaye asūta putraṃ kāntaṃ manoharaṃ ।
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ bhadrāṃśaṃ maṃgalānvitaṃ ।। tac chrutvaiva gṛhastho asau suprasannaḥ pramoditaḥ । dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ saumyaṃ naiva tṛptiṃ samāyayau ।। tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ mudā ।
putranāmābhisaṃskartuṃ bhūya etān samabravīt ।। bhavanto dṛśyatāṃ siddhaṃ mamabhilaṣitaṃ cirāt । tan nāmāsya yathāyogyaṃ prasiddhaṃ kriyatāṃ śubhaṃ ।। iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te jñātayo mudā । dārakaṃ taṃ samālokya naṃditāḥ samabhāṣata ।।
yasmin dine hy ayaṃ jātas tadā sarve api paurikāḥ । nanditās tad bhavatv ayaṃ nāmnā nanda iti śrutaḥ ।। athāsau dārako nandaḥ samyag dehopacāraṇe । pitrāṣṭāsu ca dhātrīṣu paritoṣya samarpitaḥ ।।
tato asau kramaśas tāsāṃ dhātriṇām upacārataḥ । dine dine pravṛddho abhūd dhradasthaṃ paṃkajaṃ yathā ।। evaṃ pravarddhamāno asau ṣaḍvarṣiko yadābhavat । tadā kuśīdasaṃvṛtto babhūva viratotsavaḥ ।।
sadā śayyāsanasthas tat samutthātuṃ na caichata । śayyāsanasthitaś caiva bhuktvā naivācarat kvacit ।। sadā svāntargṛhastho api sutīkṣṇabuddhimān sudhīḥ । adhītya sarvaśāstrāṇi satyadharmarato abhavat ।।
atha śreṣṭhī pitā dṛṣṭvā putram evaṃ kuśīditaṃ । sarvavidyāguṇādhāraṃ dṛṣṭvā caivaṃ vyacintayat ।। kathaṃ cid yo mayā prāpto devatāsaṃprasādataḥ । so api putro mamābhāgyād bhavaty evaṃ kuśīditaḥ ।।
sarvavidyāguṇādhāraṃ sarvaśāstravicakṣaṇaḥ । kiṃ mamānena putreṇa dusthiteneva roginā । yataḥ svasthaśarīro api bhuktvaivaṃ paśuvat sthitaḥ ।। kim atrāhaṃ kariṣyāmi yat putro ayaṃ ni rudyamaḥ ।
kim īdrigjantunā kāryyaṃ kuladharmopahāriṇā ।। dhig me daivaṃ prayatnaṃ ca sarvaṃ tat syān nirarthakaṃ । kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi sarvathāhaṃ vibhagnitaḥ ।। evaṃ cintāparīto asau gṛhasthaś ca vyacintayat ।
pūraṇo me asti śāstā yaḥ pṛcheyaṃ tad upāyakaṃ ।। iti matvā gṛhastho asau tad āśramaṃ samāgataḥ । pūraṇaṃ taṃ guruṃ natvā papraccha tadupāyatāṃ ।। bhagavan bho mahābhijña śāstāsi me prasīda tat ।
yan mayā pṛchyate kāryyaṃ tat samādeṣṭum arhasi ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā tīrthiko mānagarvitaḥ । āśu siddhaṃ kariṣyāmo yat kāryyaṃ te atra tad vada ।। iti proktvaivam āśvāsya pūraṇo atyabhimānikaḥ ।
pravadaṃs taṃ gṛhasthaṃ vai sarvathaivam abodhayat ।। iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā gṛhapatir mudā । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā taṃ guruṃ samabhāṣata ।। bhagavan bho vijānīyā yo me putraḥ prajāyate ।
sa pravṛddho nirutsāhī kuśīdo varttate adhunā ।। sadā śayyāsthito bhuṅkte bhuktvā śete nirudyamaḥ । notsahati kvacid gaṃtuṃ paśuvat tiṣṭhate gṛhe ।। na śayanāt samutthāya śrotuṃ draṣṭuṃ samicchati ।
gṛhe śayyāsanārūḍho rogīva vasate sadā ।। tadupāyaṃ kathaṃ kuryyāṃ yenāyaṃ śayanotthitaḥ । śrotuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca gaṃtuṃ ca karttuṃ kāryyaṃ yathotsahet ।। tathā me bhagavan putraṃ kuladharme niyojaya ।
bhavān eva hi me śāstā tad dhitaṃ kartum arhasi ।। ity evaṃ prārthitaṃ tena śrutvāsau pūraṇo yatiḥ । tasya gṛhapateś cittaṃ praharṣayan samabravīt ।। are mā gā viṣādaṃ tvaṃ cintayā kiṃ pratapyase ।
asmāsu vidyamāneṣu ṣaṭsu vijñeṣu śāstṛṣu ।। tad ahaṃ te mahābhāga sārddhaṃ sarvaiś ca tīrthikaiḥ । ṛddhyā gatvā kariṣyāmi dārakaṃ vistayotthitaṃ ।। yadāsau dārako hy asmān sarvān dṛṣṭvā samutthitaḥ ।
kṛtvā praṇāmam asmākaṃ dharmmaṃ śrotuṃ samutsahet ।। śrutvā dharmasamutsāhāt kuśalāni samācaret । tatkuśalaiḥ samāpanno vīryavān sa bhavet sudhīḥ ।। tatas te sarvakāryāṇi sādhayet sa samudyataḥ ।
svakuladharmakarmāṇi kuśalī saṃcariṣyate ।। evaṃ me vacanaṃ satyaṃ dṛṣṭvā samyak pramāṇaya । tad viṣādaṃ parityajya karttavyaṃ hi tathā kuru ।। iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhabhṛn mudā ।
sahasā svagṛhaṃ gatvā tad bhojyaṃ samasādhayat ।। athāsau pūraṇo anyaiś ca tīrthikaiḥ sārddham āgataḥ । gṛhe gatvā puras tasya paryyaṅke samupāśrayat ।। tathāsau tān samāgatvā kramaśa āsane sthitān ।
dṛṣṭvā saṃharṣitaḥ śreṣṭhī sahasā putram abravīt ।। putra paśya gṛhe asmākaṃ śāstāraḥ samupasthitāḥ । tat samutthāya natvaitāñ chāstṝn bhojyaiḥ pravāraya ।। ity uktvā janakenāsau dārako na samutthitaḥ ।
draṣṭum api na cotsehe kiṃ namec ca pravārayet ।। bahuśaḥ preryyamāṇo api pitrā sa bandhubhiḥ saha । dārakas tān samāsīnān draṣṭum api na caichata ।। kiṃ punar utthito natvā bhojaṇaiḥ saṃpravārayet ।
tathā śayyāsanārūḍha evaṃ tasthau nirutsavaḥ ।। tatas te tīrthikāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvaivaṃ nirutsavaṃ । nānāvidhiprayatnais tam utthāpayitum ārabhan ।। tathāpi naiva śayyāyā udatiṣṭhat sa dārakaḥ ।
svadharmadeśakāṃś cāpi tān draṣṭum api naihata ।। evaṃ cānutthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ te sarve ca tīrthikāḥ । haṭhāc cainaṃ samutthāpya vaśīkarttuṃ parākraman ।। tathaitāṃs tīrthikān sarvān eva garvābhivāditān । dṛṣṭvābhisaṃmukhāyātān bhīto arautsīt sa dārakaḥ ।।
tathā taṃ ruditaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te lajjayā bhiyā । pratijagmur vibhinnāsyāḥ svasvālayāni bheditāḥ ।। tathā gṛhapatir dṛṣṭvā sarvān etān parāyitān । pratibhinnaviṣaṇnātmā tasthau cintāvimohitaḥ ।।
atha śrībhagavān buddhaḥ sarvadarśī vināyakaḥ । paśyan satvān samuddhartuṃ dadarśa taṃ kuśīditaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvā tasya kuśīdasya karmavṛttiparaṃparāṃ । tat kuśīdaṃ samuddhartum aryānaṃdaṃ samabravīt ।।
paśyānaṃda gṛhasthasya śrāvastīpuravāsinaḥ । putro naṃda iti khyātaḥ sāmprataṃ saṃkuśīdikaḥ ।। asau me darśanād eva nūnaṃ vīryyaṃ samārabhan । sahasotthāya sa natvā dharmaṃ praśṛṇuyān mudā ।।
tato me śāsane dharmaṃ pracaret sa sudhīḥ sadā । kramād bodhicarīṃ pūryya saṃbodhiṃ cāpi lapsyati ।। tasmāt tasya gṛhe gatvā tīrthikadarppachittaye । saddharme saṃpratiṣṭhāpya sarvān bodhau niyojaye ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānandaḥ sa harṣitaḥ । karttavyaṃ bhagavann evam ity anumodito abhavat ।। tato bhagavatā tena suvarṇābhā marīcayaḥ । utsṛṣṭās taiś ca tad geham avabhāsya vyaśodhayat ।।
yadā tair dārakaḥ spṛṣṭo buddhamaitrīmarīcibhiḥ । tadā prahlāditaś cāsāv ity evaṃ samacintayat ।। aho kasya prabhāvo ayaṃ yenaivam avabhāsitaṃ । prahlāditaś ca me kāyas tan na jāne kutaḥ kathaṃ ।।
iti cintāṃ samālambya kautukākrāntamānasaḥ । samantato nirīkṣyaivaṃ tasthau gehe suvismitaḥ ।। tathā taṃ vismitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ saha । sahasā tadgṛhaṃ gatvā prādur āsīt prabhāsayan ।।
tatra sa dārako apaśyad bhagavantaṃ tam āsthitaṃ । kāntaṃ divyātiriktābhaṃ samantabhadrarūpiṇaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvaiva sahasotthāya natvā pādau pramoditaḥ । svayam evāsanaṃ tasmai prajñapyaivam abhāṣata ।।
svāgataṃ bhagavan nātha vijayasva munīśvara । prasīdānugrahārthena niṣīdātra śubhāsane ।। iti tenodite tatra bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ saha । tat prajñaptāsane sthitvā dharmaṃ deṣṭuṃ samārabhat ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā dārakasyaivaṃ dharmotsāhaṃ samutthitaṃ । pitarau jñātivargāś ca sarve apy āsan suvismitāḥ ।। tatrāsau dārako harṣād utphullanayano mudā । natvā pādau muneś cāgre dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayat ।।
athāsau bhagavāṃs tasya jñātvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dharmaṃ deṣṭuṃ tam abravīt ।। śṛṇu vatsa mahābhāga pāpapuṇyārthasādhane । hetuṃ vakṣye śubhārthe te tad atra tvaṃ samācara ।।
mānuṣyaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya vidyuttaraṃgacaṃcalaṃ । pāpakṣaye matiḥ kāryā puṇyārthasādhaneṣu ca ।। pāpena durgatiṃ yāyāt puṇyena sadgatiṃ vrajet । pāpamitrānurāgeṇa matiḥ pāpe pravarttate ।।
tataḥ pāparataḥ kuryāt pāpāni dāruṇāny api । tato duṣṭaḥ supāpiṣṭhaḥ saddharmāṇi vinindayet ।। tato dharmaviruddhatvāt kuśaktiḥ kutsito bhavet । tataḥ sa kutsitātmā hi sarvasatvair vinindyate ।।
paribhūto viṣādena bhavet mūḍho nirutsahaḥ । utsāhavarjite citte ālasyaṃ samupāśrayet ।। ālasvī sādhayen naiva kiṃcid dharmaṃ guṇāni vā । dharmakarmaviraktātmā nirguṇī kiṃ kariṣyati । bhogya eva sadāsaktaḥ paśor apy adhamo naraḥ । kiṃ tena puruṣeṇāpi nirguṇena sukhāśinā ।
yasya puṇye guṇe vāpi kadāpi notsahen manaḥ । puṇyotsāhavipannātmā duṣṭakleśair vihanyate । kleśito mārasaṃghaiś ca vaśīkṛtya nivaddhyate ।। mārasya vaśagaḥ strīṇāṃ dāsatvaṃ samupāśrayet ।
sa dāsanirato bhuktvā paśuvat tiṣṭhate gṛhe ।। naiva dharmaṃ kvacic chrotuṃ draṣṭuṃ vāpi na cotsahet । dharmaṃ vinā vrajen naiva sadgatiṃ hi kadā cana ।। tasmād dharme samācartuṃ puṇyotsāhaṃ pravarddhayan ।
trimaṇḍalaviśuddhena dānaṃ dadyāc chubhāptaye ।। dānena siddhyate dharmaṃ dharmāc cittaṃ viśuddhyate । śuddhacittaś carec chīle śīlavān hi bhavet sudhīḥ ।। sudhīro bhāvayet kṣāṃtiṃ kṣāntimān duṣṭajit kṛtī ।
kuśalī prārabhed vīryyaṃ vīryyavān puruṣottamaḥ ।। mahāsatvo labhed dhyānaṃ dhyātā brahmavihārikaḥ । saṃsmṛtaḥ sādhayet prajñāṃ prajñāvān hi guṇālayaḥ ।। guṇajñaḥ samupāyaiś ca satvān dharme niyojayet ।
etat puṇyānubhāvena bodhau praṇidhim ācaret ।। bodhipraṇidhicittena balāni sādhayed daśa । tad balaiś ca mahāghorāṃ mārasaṃghān parājayet ।। jitvā māragaṇān sarvān saṃbodhijñānam āpnuyāt ।
tataḥ sarvatra lokeṣu dharmacakraṃ pravarttayet ।। evaṃ pravarttayan dharmaṃ śāstā lokādhipo bhavet । sarvalokahitaṃ kurvan mahatpuṇyaiḥ samṛddhitaḥ ।। sadaivaṃ sadgatau sthitvā saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।
evaṃ matvā tvayā vatsa caritavyaṃ tathā śubhe ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ jinendreṇa śrutvā sa dārako mudā । kṛtāṃjaliḥ punar natvā bhagavantam abhāṣata ।। adyārabhya sadā śāstar bhavataḥ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tadyathā bhavatājñaptaṃ tathā satyaṃ carāmy ahaṃ ।।
kṛpādṛṣṭim upasthāpya samanvāhara māṃ sadā । bhavān eva hi sarvajñas traidhātukavināyakaḥ ।। yadaivaṃ te dayā nāsti mayy udyamavivarjite । ka evaṃ samupāgatya proddharen māṃ kuśīdikaṃ ।।
pavitrībhūtam ātmānaṃ manye ahaṃ te prasādataḥ । dhanyo asmi tan mahābhadro yac chāstraivaṃ pradarśitaḥ ।। iti tenodite bhūyaḥ sarvajñaḥ sa munīśvaraḥ । sucaṃdanamayīṃ yaṣṭiṃ datvainaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
vatsemāṃ yaṣṭim ādhāya prakoṭaya samāhitaḥ । tatas tvaṃ sarvadāvaśyaṃ labheḥ puṇyamahotsavaṃ ।। iti śāstrā pradattāṃ tāṃ natvāsau dārako agrahīt । yathādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tathā kartum udācarat ।।
ity evaṃ taṃ samādiśya sa saṃbuddhaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । svaṃ vihāram upāśritya dharmaṃ diśan samāvasat ।। athāsau dārako harṣāt tāṃ yaṣṭiṃ svayam ādadhat । yathādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa prākoṭayat samāhitaḥ ।।
tasyām ākoṭyamānāyāṃ puṇyaśabda udācarat । gṛhe ratnanidhānāni prādur āsan bahūni ca ।। tacchabdaśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā dārako asau pramoditaḥ । gṛhe ratnanidhānāni dṛṣṭvāścaryyaṃ samāyayau ।।
tataś ca vismito harṣāt punar evaṃ vyacintayat । batedaṃ sumahāśauryyaṃ vīryyaṃ prārambhaye tataḥ ।। tathā ratnākaraṃ gatvā ratnāni samupārjayan । sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ nityaṃ upatiṣṭheya saṃbhajan ।।
iti dhyātvā samutsāhaṃ saṃnibadhya sa dārakaḥ । ratnākaraṃ samāgantuṃ prārebhe saha vāṇijaiḥ ।। tato asau dārako vīras tasyāṃ pūryyāṃ samantataḥ । sārthavāhaṃ svam ātmānaṃ kṛtvā ghoṣam akārayat ।।
tathā tad ghoṣaṇāṃ śrutvā ye vīrās te vaṇigjanāḥ । tena sārddhaṃ mahotsāhair mahābdhiṃ gantum aichan ।। tato asau puruṣo vīraḥ sarvais taiś ca vaṇigjanaiḥ । saha ratnākaraṃ gatvā bahuratnāny asādhayat ।।
tataḥ sārthapatiḥ sarvaiḥ sārthaiḥ sārddhaṃ mahodadheḥ । kṣemena sahasottīryya svadeśaṃ samupāyayau ।। atha sārthapatis tatra yātrāsiddhipramoditaḥ । sarvān sārthān samāmaṃtrya dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ sarvair yat svasti prāgatā vayaṃ । tat prabhāvaṃ vijānīdhvaṃ jinendrasya prasādatāḥ ।। tasmād asya munīndrasya kṛtvā darśanam ādarāt । pūjayitvā praṇatvā ca paścād gehaṃ vrajema hi । iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarvve api te vaṇigjanāḥ । dṛṣṭasatyānumodantaḥ tatheti pratimenire । iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarvvasārthasamanvitaḥ ।
tataḥ sārthapatiḥ śīghraṃ vihāraṃ samupāyayau । tatra dṛṣṭvā jinendraṃ taṃ sarvve te saṃpraharṣitāḥ । pādau natvā munes tasya parivṛtyopatasthire ।। athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvān sārthagaṇān api ।
dharmotsāhaprāvṛddhyarthaiḥ samāmaṃtrya samabravīt ।। āgatāḥ stha samāyāta mā stha śrāntāś ca kheditāḥ । yātrāsāphalyasiddhiś ca kaccid vaḥ kuśalāni ca ।। evaṃ pṛṣṭe jinendreṇa sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā saṃbuddhaṃ procur ādarāt ।। bhagavan bhavatām evaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । yātrāsiddhiḥ kathaṃ na syāt sarvatra kuśalaṃ hi naḥ ।। yad vayaṃ śāstar āyātāḥ śubharatnasamanvitāḥ ।
tat sarvaṃ tvatprabhāvena satyam etat pramāṇyate ।। tad bhavantaṃ suśāstāraṃ draṣṭuṃ sarve samāgatāḥ । pūjayituṃ samichāmas tat prasīda jagadguro ।। iti vijñāpanāṃ kṛtvā saha sārthaiḥ sa sārthabhṛt ।
sasaṃghaṃ pūjayitvā ca ratnāni samaḍhaukata ।। namas te bhagavan nātha vrajāmaḥ śaraṇaṃ tava । pāhi naḥ sarvadāpy evaṃ tvam eva jagadīśvaraḥ ।। evaṃ stutvā munīndraṃ taṃ sarve te saṃprasāditāḥ ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā svagṛhaṃ gantum īhire ।। tataś ca bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān svagṛhotsukān । datvāśīrvacanaṃ spṛṣṭvā vrajateti vyasarjayat ।। tataḥ sarve api te sārthāḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ ।
śāstāraṃ sugataṃ natvā svaṃ svaṃ gehaṃ samāyayuḥ ।। tato bhūyas tathānyaiś ca prārthyamānaḥ sa vīryyavān । ṣaḍḍhā ratnākaraṃ gatvā bahuratnāny asādhayat ।। tataś ca gṛhapatiḥ śreṣṭhī sārthavāhaḥ suvīryyavān ।
sasaṅghaṃ sugataṃ gehe praṇītvārcitum ārabhat ।। tato bhojanasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvā niveśane । sasaṃghaiḥ buddham āmaṃtrya nyaveśayac chubhāsane ।। tataḥ pūjopahāraiś ca pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ ।
pratyekaṃ cīvaraṃ datvā bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। tataś ca bhojanānte asau sārthavāhaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ । sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ natvā praṇidhānaṃ tathākarot ।। yat kiñcit prakṛtaṃ dānaṃ saṃbuddhaśāsane mayā ।
etatpuṇyaphalena syāṃ saṃbuddho ayaṃ jino yathā ।। iti tasya gṛhasthasya cittaṃ saṃbodhivāṃchitaṃ । jñātvāsau bhagavān buddhaḥ smitaṃ kṛtvābhyanaṃdata ।। tadā bhagavato vaktrān niśceruḥ paṃcavarṇikāḥ । raśmayas tāḥ samantāc ca trailokyaṃ śāmabhāsayan ।।
yāḥ kāś cid raśmayo yātā adhastān narakeṣv api । tāś ca niścaritās tāvat saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtrakaṃ ।। saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ cāpi mahārauravaviśrutaṃ । tapanākhyaṃ tathā caivaṃ pratāpanāhvayaṃ tataḥ ।।
avīcim arbudaṃ caivaṃ nirarbudaṃ tathāṭaṭaṃ । hahavaṃ huhuvaṃ caivam utpalaṃ padmakaṃ tataḥ ।। mahāpadmākhyam etāni ṣoḍaśa nilayāni hi । tatroṣṇanarakā ye tu teṣu sarveṣu niḥsṛtāḥ ।।
śītībhūtā viniḥpatya prabhāsayan samaṃtataḥ । ye śītanarakās teṣu tūṣṇībhūtāpy abhāsayan ।। teṣu ye nārakāḥ satvā nānāduḥkhābhivedinaḥ । te tābhī raśmibhiḥ spṛṣṭā mahatsaukhyaṃ prarebhire ।।
atha sarve api te satvā mahatsaukhyasamanvitāḥ । vismitās tatra saṃmīlya mithaś caivaṃ vabhāṣire ।। aho bhavanta āścaryyaṃ kiṃ cāsmākaṃ bhavet khalu । yad vayaṃ sarvadāpītthaṃ nānāduḥkhaiḥ prapīḍitāḥ ।
tanmuktāḥ sāṃprataṃ sarve vayaṃ saukhyasamanvitāḥ ।। kiṃ tato hi vayaṃ muktā anyatra caritā nanu । iti vismitacittānāṃ sarveṣāṃ cittabodhane ।। bhagavān nirmitaṃ teṣāṃ purastāt samadarśayat ।।
tatra taṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve api te ativismitāḥ । parasparaṃ mukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathaivaṃ saṃvabhāṣire ।। bho bhavanta itaś cyutvā nānyatra gamitā vayaṃ । kiṃ tv ayaṃ sugatākāra āyāto apūrvadarśanaḥ ।।
nūnam asyānubhāvena vayam itthaṃ sukhānvitāḥ ।। iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve tasmiṃ saugatanirmite । cittaṃ prasādya buddhāya nama iti praṇemire ।। tatas te nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā natva cittaprasāditaḥ । sarvapāpavinirmuktāḥ sarve api sugatiṃ yayuḥ ।।
yāś ca kāś cid gatā ūrddhvaṃ tā mahārājikān gatāḥ । trayastriṃśāṃś ca yāmāṃś ca tuṣitāṃś ca gatās tataḥ ।। nirmāṇaratim ābhāsya nirmitavaśavarttikān । brahmakāyikalokāṃś ca gatā brahmapurohitān ।।
mahābrahmālayaṃ cāpi parītābhāṃs tathā gatāḥ । apramāṇābhalokāṃś ca tata ābhāsvarān gatāḥ ।। parīttaśubhalokāṃs tadāpramāṇaśubhān gatāḥ । śubhakṛtsnān anabhrāṃś ca puṇyaprasavakāṃs tataḥ ।।
bṛhatphalāṃs tataś caivam avṛhān atapān gatāḥ । ḥsudṛśāṃś ca tato yātā tathā caivaṃ sudarśanān ।। akaniṣṭhaṃ tathā gatvā sarvān etān vyabhāsayan । teṣu ye saṃsthitā lokāḥ sarve tābhiś ca raśmibhiḥ ।।
parispṛṣṭāḥ sukhaprāptā dṛṣṭvā tāṃ caivam ūcire । aho citraṃ śubhā kāmyā kasya puṇyaprabhā imāḥ ।। yābhir vayaṃ parispṛṣṭā mahatsaukhyaṃ labhāmahe । iti vismitacittānāṃ teṣāṃ cittavinodane ।।
tathā tā raśmayaś caināṃ gāthābhiḥ samacodayan । anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ ।। ataḥ kleśagaṇāṃs tyaktvā bhajadhvaṃ sugataṃ sadā । niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ kaṃ yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane ।।
dhunīta mārasainyāṃś ca naḍāgāram iva dvipaḥ । yo hy asmiṃ dharmavaineye atyapramattaś caret sudhīḥ ।। prahāya sa bhave kleśān duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati । iti tā raśmayaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samantataḥ ।। prerayitvā śubhe satvān punar muneḥ purogatāḥ ।
tato bhagavatas tasya kṛtvā trayapradakṣiṇāṃ ।। tathā tā raśmayaḥ sarvā uṣṇīṣe antarhitaṃ yayuḥ । athānandaḥ samutthāya kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā ।। bhagavantaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ papraccha smitakāraṇaṃ ।
bhagavaṃs tava śubhā raśmiḥ smitodbhavā vinirgatā ।। yayāvabhāsitā lokāḥ sūryyeṇodayatā yathā । nākasmād darśayanty evaṃ smitaṃ buddhā jināḥ kvacit ।। tat kasmād bhagavān smitaṃ saṃdarśayati sāṃprataṃ ।
yasyārthe bhavatāpy evaṃ smitaṃ saṃdarśitaṃ tathā ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve śrotum ichanti sajjanāḥ । tad atra bhagavāñ chāstā hy esāṃ dharmābhikāṃkṣiṇāṃ ।। sarveṣāṃ tat samādiśya saṃdehaṃ chettum arhati ।
ity ānaṃdoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavāṃś ca tam abravīt ।। evam etat tathānaṃda yathā tvaṃ bhāṣase kila । nākāraṇe jinaṃ sarvaṃ smitaṃ saṃdarśitaṃ kvacit ।। tad arthaṃ śṛṇu vakṣye ahaṃ yad arthaṃ saṃsmitaṃ mama ।
paśyānanda gṛhastho ayaṃ dārako yaḥ kuśīditaḥ ।। mama saṃdarśanād evaṃ viryyotsāhaṃ samāpnuvan । itthaṃ ratnāni saṃsādhya buddhimāṃś ca samṛddhitaḥ ।। evaṃ śrāddhaḥ prasannātmā śāsane me anumoditaḥ ।
satkṛtya śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajati māṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।। yad ayaṃ sārthabhṛn nando mama dharmābhisaṃrataḥ । asya puṇyavipākena bodhicittaṃ samāpnuyāt ।। tataḥ cikṣāḥ samāsādya pūryya pāramitā daśa । kramān māragaṇāñ jitvā saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyāt ।।
tato arhann abhivandyo atibalavīryyaparākramaḥ । iti nāmnā prasiddho ayaṃ saṃbuddhaḥ sugato jinaḥ ।। sarvadharmādhipaḥ śāstā sarvavidyāguṇākaraḥ । sarvajñas trijagadbharttā tathāgato bhaviṣyati ।।
tasmād evaṃ sadānaṃda karttavyaṃ buddhadarśanaṃ । buddhadarśanapuṇyena dharmotsāhaṃ samāpuṇyāt ।। tato vīryyasamārūḍhaḥ saddharmaṃ sādhayen mudā । tato dharmabalair mārāñ jitvā saṃbodhim āpnuyāt ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । anumodya guruṃ natvā tatheti prābhyanaṃdata ।। evaṃ me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ dharmotsāhapravṛddhaye । tathā tava mayā khyātaṃ satyam etat pradhāryyatāṃ ।।
evaṃ rājaṃs tvayāpy evaṃ kṛtvānumodanāṃ tathā । dharmaprotsāhanāṃ kṛtvā karttavyaṃ buddhadarśanaṃ ।। saddharmacaraṇotsāhe cāraṇīyāḥ prajāḥ sadā । ity etad guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ ।।
satyam evaṃ pratiśrutya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। tat kauśīdyāvadānaṃ munivarakathitaṃ śraddhayā yaḥ śṛṇoti । śrutvā yaḥ śrāvayed yaḥ pratidinam aniśaṃ buddhasevānuraktaḥ । hitvā kleśān praduṣṭān sakalakalivalān mārapakṣāṃś ca jitvā । pāraṃ gatvā guṇābdher vrajati sa subhagaṃ śrīghanasya caritraṃ । athāśoko nṛpendro asau saddharmacaraṇotsavaḥ । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā kṛtāñjalipuṭo avadat ।।
bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā te guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā me khyātum arhasi ।। iti tena nṛpeśena prārthyamāno jināṃśajaḥ । upaguptaḥ samāmaṃtrya taṃ kṣitīśaṃ samabravīt ।।
sādhu suṣṭhu mahāraja śṛṇu dharmaṃ samāhitaḥ । yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathātra te pracakṣyate ।। puraikasamaye yo abhūc chākyasiṃho dayākaraḥ । dharmarājo jagacchāstā sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ ।।
sarvavidyākalāvijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ । samantabhadrakṛn nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ ।। sa śrāvastyāṃ mahodyāne jetārāme manohare । anāthapiṇḍadasyaiva vihāre maṇimaṇḍite ।।
śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvair upāsakaiḥ । devāsuramahārājair manujendraṃ sapārṣadaiḥ ।। sarvalokādhipaiś cāpi traidhātukanivāsitaiḥ । caturvarṇaiś ca pauraiś ca tathānyaiś ca śubhārthibhiḥ ।।
satkṛto mānitaś cābhivanditaḥ saṃstuto arcitaḥ । gurukṛtaḥ puraskṛtya parivṛto avalokitaḥ ।। ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dharmaṃ loke prakāśayan । sarvasatvahitārthena vijahāra samāhitaḥ ।।
tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śrāvastyāṃ ye vaṇigjanāḥ । te paṃcaśatamātrāṇi ratnākaraṃ samāgatāḥ ।। tataḥ pratyāgatāḥ sarve kāntāraṃ samupāviśan । tatra te bhramitā mārgāt paribhraṣṭā vicerire ।।
vimārgeṇa carantas te vālukāsthalam upāviśan । tatra praptāś ca te sarve madhyāhne dyotitātape ।। bhānos tīkṣṇakarais taptā gharmatāpābhikheditāḥ । kṣīṇapathyādanāś cāpi kṣuttṛṣṇā paripīḍitāḥ ।। tīvraduḥkhābhisaṃtaptāḥ paryāvarttanta tatra ca ।
sthalaprāptā yathā mīnā mṛtyubhayavikaṃpitāḥ ।। tadā sarve api te sārthāḥ śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । svasvakuleśasvasveṣṭadevatāḥ saṃyayācire ।। kecit svayaṃbhuvaṃ smṛtvā kecin nārāyaṇaṃ tathā ।
kecic chivaṃ mahāraudraṃ kecit sūryyagrahādhipaṃ ।। kecic caṃdraṃ ca tāreśaṃ kecid iṃdraṃ surādhipaṃ । kecid agniṃ yamaṃ caiva naiṛtyaṃ ca tathāpare ।। vāruṇaṃ ca tathā vāyukuveraṃ ca maheśvaraiḥ ।
bhairavaṃ mātṛkāś caivaṃ kecit skandhaṃ vināyakaṃ ।। mahākālaṃ tathā caivaṃ kecid ṛṣīn yatīśvarān । kecid daityādhipān vīrān kecin nāgādhipāṃs tathā ।। kecic cāturmahārājān kecid yakṣādhipān tathā ।
evam anyāṃs tridhātusthāṃs sarvān smṛtvā yayācire ।। tair evaṃ yācyamānānāṃ devatānaṃ na kaś cana । eko apy āsīt tadā trātā vāṇijāṃ duḥkhabhāgināṃ ।। tatas te vaṇijaḥ sarve mṛtyubhayavikaṃpitāḥ ।
nirāśayā viṣīdantas tasthur niśceṣṭamānasāḥ ।। tatra yaḥ sugatopāsī dṛṣṭasatyaḥ sa dhīravān । tān sārthān vipannāśāṃ dṛṣṭvāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। bhavanto mā viṣīdadhvaṃ kiṃ viṣādena setsyate ।
tasmāt tyaktvā viṣādatvaṃ dhīryyam ālambya tiṣṭhata ।। dhairyyeṇa tārayed duḥkhaṃ mahākṛcchraṃ vipatsv api । tasmād dhairyyaṃ samādhāya smaradhvaṃ ca jinaṃ drutaṃ ।। jina eva jagannāthas trātā sarvānukaṃpakaḥ ।
tad asmadvacanaṃ śrutvā saṃbuddhaṃ smaratādarāt ।। tatrāpy evaṃ bhaye asmākaṃ trātā ko anyo bhaviṣyati । buddha eva jagadbaṃdhus tad vrajadhvaṃ jinaṃ drutaṃ ।। sarvathā no jinendro asau sarvasatvānukanipakaḥ ।
ḍṛṣṭvāsmān karuṇādṛṣṭyā saṃrakṣet sahasā khalu ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutva sarve te vaṇijas tathā । saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā smṛtvābhayaṃ yayācire ।। namas te bhagavan nātha sarvajño asi jagatprabhuḥ ।
bhavataiva jagat sarvaṃ pālitaṃ putravat sadā ।। adyāgreṇa vayaṃ sarve yāvajjīvaṃ sadāpi hi । bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmas tad rakṣāsmāñ jagadguro ।। bhavān eva jagaddharmaṃ saṃsāre pālitaṃ sadā ।
bhagavan sarvavin nātha trātum arhasi sarvathā ।। paṃcaśatasarvāṇi vāṇijāś ca samāgatāḥ । vimārgeṇa carantas te madhyāhne dyotitātape ।। tatra prāptāś ca te sarve vālukāsthale saṃsthitāḥ ।
bhāno tīkṣṇakare taptā kṣuttṛṣārttā paripīḍitāḥ ।। tīvrātivedanākrāntā mṛtyubhayaṃ samāgatāḥ । namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti namo namaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvāsmān karuṇā sarvān paṃcaśatāni vāṇijān ।
bhavān eva jagatsvāmiṃ tathā buddhānubhāvatāṃ ।। tadā sa bhagavān tebhya māhendravṛṣṭim ācaran । śītalā vāyavo yāti tena śītatvam āgatāḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā sārthapatinā sarvān sārthān samabravīt ।
bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ sarve yan mayā procyate hitaṃ ।। tad bhavadbhiḥ samādhṛtvā karttavyaṃ kṛtavedibhiḥ । yad vayaṃ mṛtyusaṃprāptā paralokād ivāgatāḥ ।। tad jñeyaṃ jinendrasya kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ ।
tasmāt sarve vayaṃ tasya buddhasya śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। saddharmmaṃ samupāśritya caremahi sadāpi hi । anityaṃ khalu saṃsāram anityaṃ jīvitaṃ sukhaṃ ।। kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca bhave nityaṃ na kiṃ cana ।
dharma eva mahāsāraṃ yenaivaṃ rakṣyate jagat ।। tasmād dharmaṃ samādhartuṃ gantavyaṃ śaraṇaṃ muneḥ । iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te vaṇijo mudā ।। tathety abhyanumodantas tato gaṃtum upākramat ।
atha sārthapatiś caivaṃ kṛtvā taṃ saha saṃmataṃ ।। vihāre sugataṃ draṣṭuṃ dharmaṃ cāptum agān mudā । tatropetya praviṣṭo asau sarvasārthagaṇānvitaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ natvā viṣasāda puro muneḥ ।
athāsau bhagavāṃs teṣāṃ dṛṣṭvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । āryyasatyāryyamārgāṅgaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tadā sarve api te satvāḥ śrutvā taṃ dharmam ādarāt । satkāyadṛṣṭinirmuktā bodhicittaṃ pralebhire ।।
tatra kecin mahāśrāddhā dharmānusāriṇo abhavan । śrotāpannās tathā kecit sakṛdāgāmino pare ।। tathānāgāminaḥ kecit kecid bhavaparāṅmukhāḥ । saṃsārakleśasaṃghāṃś ca hitvā suvimalāśayāḥ ।।
sākṣāt saddharmmam āsādya babhūvur dharmacāriṇaḥ । kecic chrāvakabodhau ca pratyekāyāṃ tathāpare ।। kecid anuttarāyāṃ ca saṃbodhau praṇidhiṃ dadhuḥ । evaṃ tāḥ parṣadaḥ sarvāḥ saṃbuddhaśaraṇe sthitāḥ ।।
saddharmmācaraṇe raktāḥ saṃghabhaktā babhūvire । atha te bhikṣavo dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। saṃbuddhaṃ prayatā natvā paprachur vismayānvitāḥ । āścaryyaṃ bhagavan yāvad yad ime vaṇijas tathā ।।
kāṃtārapatitāḥ sarve bhavatā paripālitāḥ । bhavaccintitamātre api māhendravṛṣṭim ācaran ।। śītalā vāyavo vātās tat kathaṃ vaktum arhasi । iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭo bhagavāṃs tān abhāṣata ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ karmma yan mayā kṛta kṛtaṃ kathyate । yan mayā prakṛtaṃ karma ko anyo bhuṃjyād dhi tatphalaṃ ।। yena yat prakṛtaṃ karma sa evādyād dhi tat phalaṃ । abhuktaṃ kṣīyate karma naiva kvāpi kathaṃ cana ।।
agnibhir dahyate naiva vāyubhir nāpi śuṣyate । udakaiḥ klidyate nāpi bhūmiṣu ।। api tu pacyate skandhaṣaḍdhātvāyataneṣu hi । anyathā cāpi karmāṇi na dadanti phalāni ca ।।
yathaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tathaiva tat phalaṃ mataṃ । śubhakarma śubhaṃ dadyāt pāpakarmāśubhaṃ khalu ।। miśritam ubhayaṃ dadyād iti matvā śubhe caret । na praṇaśyaṃti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api ।।
sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti khalu dehināṃ । yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ tat phalaṃ prāpyate adhunā ।। kathyate tat purāvṛttaṃ sādhu śṛṇuta sādaraṃ । puraikasamaye buddhaś caṃdano nāma dharmarāṭ ।।
sarvajño arhañ jagannāthaḥ śāstā lokādhipeśvaraḥ । vidyācaraṇasaṃpannaḥ sugato lokavij jinaḥ ।। tathāgato mahābhijñaḥ saṃbuddho abhūd vināyakaḥ । tadaikasamaye tatra caṃdanaḥ sa munīśvaraḥ ।।
bhikṣubhiḥ saha saddharmmaṃ prakāśayan samaṃtataḥ । hitāya sarvasatvānāṃ jānapadeṣu saṃcaran ।। anyatamāṃ purīṃ ramyāṃ rājadhānīm upāśrayat । tatra satvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan ।।
śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ vijahāra jināśrame । atha tadādhipo rājā śrutvā taṃ buddham āgataṃ ।। sa maṃtrijanapauraiś ca saha pratyudyayau mudā । tatrāsau sahasopetya dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ muniṃ ।।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā tasthāv ekāṃtike mudā । athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ nṛpaṃ samupasthitaṃ ।। ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ । śṛṇu rājan bhave sāraṃ dharmaṃ nityam ataṃdritaṃ ।।
dharmeṇa jāyate loko dharmeṇa svargam āruhet । tasmād dharmaṃ puraskṛtya saṃpālayan prajā sadā ।। prajārakṣāvrataṃ dharmaṃ mūlaṃ rājñāṃ vidur budhāḥ । prajārakṣāvrataṃ tyaktvā kim anyair bahubhir vrataiḥ ।।
tena rājan tvayā dharme pālanīyāḥ prajāḥ śubhe । tad daśākuśalebhyaś ca vinivārya tvayā sadā ।। yojanīyāḥ prajā dharme tatpuṇyais tvaṃ pramokṣyase । ādau dāne prajān yojyāḥ saṃbodhipadakāraṇe ।।
tatpuṇyaiḥ pracariṣyanti prajāḥ saṃvarddhitāḥ śubhe । śubhakarmarate loke tatpuṇyaiḥ varddhyate nṛpaḥ ।। tasmād dānaṃ svayaṃ datvā prajā śīle niyojaya । śīlena śuddhyate kāyaḥ śuddhakāyo bhavet sudhīḥ ।।
subuddhiḥ kṣamayā sarvāc chatrūṃ jitvā virājate । tato vīryyabalaiḥ sarvān satvān saukhye niyojayet ।। tataḥ kleśān vinirjitya dhyātvā bodhiṃ prasādhayet । bodhipraṇidhicittena kṛtī prajñāṃ prasādhayet ।।
tataḥ prājña upāyaiś ca jagad bodhau niyojayet । tato mārān vinirjitya saṃbodhijñānam āpnuyāt ।। tatra prāpya rasābhijñā daśabhūmīśvaro bhavet । tataḥ kṛtvā vaśe sarvāṃs traidhātukanivāśinaḥ ।।
saṃsthāpya saugate dharme svayaṃ nirvṛtim ācaret ।। evaṃ jñātvā mahārāja nirvāṇagatisādhanaṃ । yadi te nirvṛtau vāṃchā tadaitāsu samācara ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ saṃvṛttisukham āpnuyāḥ ।
kramāt pāramitāḥ pūryya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ ।। nirvāṇaṃ paramaṃ jñānaṃ nirvāṇaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ । nirvāṇaṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ nirvāṇaṃ paramāṃ gatiṃ ।। evaṃ hi sukṛtaṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā nirvāṇakāraṇaṃ ।
tathā dharme svayaṃ sthitvā preraṇīyāḥ prajā api ।। evaṃ sa caṃdano buddho bodhayitvā ca taṃ nṛpaṃ । bodhimārge pratisthāpya virarāma kṣaṇaṃ tataḥ ।। atha sa nṛpatī rājā śrutvā tad dharmam ādarāt ।
pramoditaḥ samutthāya uttarāsaṃgam udvahan ।। jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo nataḥ । suprasannamukhaḥ pādau natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ ।। namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । saddharmam ādiśann atra vijayasva gaṇaiḥ saha ।।
iti tena nṛpendreṇa prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ । tatheti pratisaṃśrutya traimāsyam adhyavāsayat ।। tataḥ sāntaḥpurā rājā taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । sadā satkārapūjāṅgair bhojyaiḥ prārāgayan mudā ।।
tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra lokānācarakopitāḥ । varṣādhidevatā meghāvṛṣṭiṃ na mumucur bhuvi ।। tatas tasyām anāvṛṣṭyāṃ taḍāgādi jalāśrayāḥ । dine dine prahīnāṃbhaḥ paṃkaśeṣaviśoṣitāḥ ।।
niḥpuṣpā niṣphalā vṛkṣāḥ śākhāpattraviśīrṇṇitāḥ ।। sthāṇukalpā nirābhogyāḥ pakṣisaṃpātavarjitāḥ । mahīśasyavipannāś ca bījāṃkulaviśoṣitāḥ ।। nistṛṇā prakhalībhūtā marukalpābhavat tadā ।
annapānaviyogena mṛtā anekajantavaḥ ।। kṣutpipāsahatāḥ kecin nyaṣīdanta mṛtā iva । kecid gehe viṣaṇṇāsyā mṛtyuśaṃkāviṣāditāḥ ।। parasparaṃ mukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā niḥśvasanto niṣedire ।
kecin meghaṃ ca khe dṛṣṭvā prāyācanta divāniśaṃ ।। hā hatāsma iti proktvā kecit tasthur nirāśitāḥ । evaṃ nānāprakāreṇa vilapanto vikheditāḥ ।। sarve api paurikās tatra cikhedur mṛtyuśaṃkitāḥ ।
tad dṛṣṭvā nṛpatiś cāpi mṛtyutrastānukaṃpitaḥ ।। maṃtriṇaḥ sacivān sarvān samāmaṃtryābravīd iti । hā kaṣṭaṃ katham atraivaṃ durbhikṣaṃ varttate adhunā । kiṃ karomi na manye ahaṃ vadadhvaṃ tat pratikriyāṃ ।।
yena tadā mahāpāpadurbhikṣaṃ śāmyate drutaṃ । tadupāyaṃ prakuryāma tat kurudhvaṃ yathāvidhiṃ ।। iti śrutvā nṛpājñāṃ te samaṃtrijanapaurikāḥ । devatā vidhinārādhya tac chāntiṃ saṃyayācire ।।
bho devatāḥ prasīdadhvaṃ namo vaḥ praṇatā vayaṃ । aparādhaṃ yad asmāsu kṣantavyaṃ sarvathāpi tat ।। imaṃ durbhikṣanirvṛṣṭiṃ prāptaṃ śamayata drutaṃ । suvṛṣṭiṃ kārayitvātra subhikṣaṃ kuruta dhruvaṃ ।।
evaṃ kecid vidhātāraṃ kecid viṣṇuṃ janārdanaṃ । kecic chivaṃ maheśānaṃ iṃdraṃ kecit surādhipaṃ ।। kecid grahādhipaṃ kecil lokapālān maharddhikān । kecic ca mātṛkādevīṃ skaṃdavighneśabhairavān ।।
mahākālagaṇāṃś cāpi kecin nāgāñ jalādhipān । kecin meghān samālokya natvā vṛṣṭiṃ yayācire ।। evaṃ sarve api lokāś ca svasveṣṭakuladevatāḥ । vidhinārādhya saṃprārthya suvṛṣṭiṃ prayayācire ।।
evaṃ taiḥ prārthyamānās tāḥ sarvāś ca devatā api । tatra vṛṣṭiṃ samutsraṣṭuṃ naiva śekur vighātitāḥ ।। tataḥ sarve ca te lokā dṛṣṭvā tad vṛṣṭighātitāṃ । hāhākāravirāvanto vicikhedur nirāśitāḥ ।।
atha rājā sa tān dṛṣṭvā durbhikṣākṣobhitāśāyān । tathā ca grahām ālokya visaṇṇāsyo vyacintayat ।। aho kaṣṭaṃ mahotpātaṃ mama rājye bhaviṣyati । katham atra pratīkāraṃ tat praśāntyai kariṣyate ।।
kiṃ mayā nṛpabhūtena yaśodharmavighātinā । na śakyaṃte prajā yena rakṣitum ītipīḍite । dhig māṃ nṛpādhamībhūtaṃ kiṃ pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ mayā । yena yasya prajā eva kṣutpipāsahatā mṛtāḥ । kim eva mama rājye na bhogyaiś cāpi dhanair api ।
kiṃ tena jīvitenāpi yaśodharmavināśinā ।। yena rājñā na rakṣyante prajāḥ svaviṣayāśritāḥ । sa kiṃ rājā baliṣṭho api kṛtānta iva manyate ।। yaś ca rājā svabhogyārthaṃ kevalaṃ daṇḍam āharan ।
na vipatsu prajāḥ pāti sa kiṃ rājāpi cauravat ।। yeṣām eva hitārthāya yaś ca rājābhiṣicyate । sa teṣāṃ na hitaṃ kuryyāt sa kiṃ rājā kṛtārthahā ।। dhik pravādahataḥ so atra yaśodharmasukhārthahā ।
svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parān hatvā narakeṣu vrajed dhruvaṃ ।। kiṃ cāham api mānuṣyaḥ samāna iṃdriyair api । yato me kriyate sarvaiḥ sevo nityaṃ samāhitaiḥ ।। yadi na kriyate rakṣā mayāpy eṣāṃ vipatsv api ।
katham etadṛśair muktaḥ kadā yāsyāmi sadgatiṃ ।। sarvadaitadṛṇair baddhaḥ sarvathā pratibaṃdhitaḥ । karmabhiḥ preryyamāṇo ahaṃ yāsyāmi narakān dhruvaṃ ।। tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi yamadūtair adhiṣṭhite ।
dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhīṣaṇāṃ krūrān patiṣyāmi vimohitaḥ ।। tadā tatra na vidyeta kaścit trātā dayānvitaḥ । dharma eva tadā rakṣet tad dharmaṃ sādhayec chubhaṃ ।। dharmāś ca bahudhā proktās teṣāṃ prāhur munīśvarāḥ ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ saugataṃ dharmam uttamaṃ ।। yenaiva śubhatāṃ kṛtvā sarvatra bhuvaneṣv api । sarvasatvāś ca pālyante sarvadeha paratra ca ।। tathātrāpi śubhaṃ kartuṃ saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajan ।
saddharmaṃ samavāptuṃ ca sevitavyaṃ sasāṃghike ।। tenātra sahasā kṛtvā puṣkaraṇīmanoramāṃ । saṃbuddhasugataṃ tatra snāpayitvā sasāṃghikaṃ ।। mahatsatkārapūjābhir bhojanaiś ca pratoṣayan ।
tatas taṃ sugataṃ natvā tad durbhikṣaṃ praśāṃtaye ।। suvṛṣṭicāraṇe loke prārthayiṣyāmi sādaraṃ । tadā sa bhagavān atra suvṛṣṭiṃ cārayed dhruvaṃ ।। sarvatra śubhatāṃ kṛtvā subhikṣaṃ kārayet sadā ।
tato atra sarvadāpy evaṃ durbhikṣaṃ na kadā cana ।। subhikṣaṃ sarvato bhadraṃ bhaven nūnaṃ samaṃtataḥ । iti dhyātvā viniścitya manasā sa narādhipaḥ ।। sahasā sacivān sarvān samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā । śṛṇudhvaṃ maṃtriṇo yan me manasā saṃviciṃtitaṃ ।।
tad anumodya yuṣmābhiḥ prakarttavyaṃ samāhitaiḥ । yad adya jāyate avṛṣṭiṃ durbhikṣaṃ copavarttate ।। tad asmatpāpato nūnaṃ tat pāpaparihāṇaye । saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saddharmasamavāptaye ।।
sasaṃghaṃ sevituṃ nityam iche tad anumodyatāṃ । sa eva bhagavān nāthaḥ kṛtvātra śubhatāṃ sadā ।। suvṛṣṭiṃ cārayitvā ca subhikṣaṃ kārayed dhruvaṃ । tato asmākaṃ tadāpy atra maṃgalaṃ syāt samaṃtataḥ ।।
sadā saddharmam ādhāya saukhyaṃ bhuktvā bhajemahi । dharmeṇa śubhatā nityaṃ dharmeṇa jīyate vipat ।। dharmeṇa pālyate sarvaṃ dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ vrajet । dharmaṃ tu saugataṃ bhadraṃ sarve prāhur munīśvarāḥ ।।
saddharmaṃ samavāptuṃ taṃ saṃbuddhaṃ bhajatādarāt । buddha eva jagadbaṃdhuḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ ।। buddha eva jaganmitraṃ sarvasatvasukhapradaḥ । buddha eva jagattrātā sarvasatvānukaṃpakaḥ ।।
buddha eva jagadbhartā dharmārthasukhasaṃpradaḥ । buddha eva jagacchāstā sarvasattvānubodhakaḥ । buddha eva jagannātho bodhisaṃbhārapūrakaḥ । buddha eva jagatsvāmī saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ ।
buddha eva mahāvīraḥ sarvamāraprabhaṃjakaḥ ।। buddha eva mahāsatvaḥ ṣaḍabhijño jagatprabhuḥ । buddha eva trilokeṣu dharmarūjā munīśvaraḥ । yenaiva trijagallokaṃ pālitaṃ putravat sadā ।।
sa eva bhagavān buddhaḥ sevanīyaḥ śubhārthibhiḥ । yenaivaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sarvalokādhipeśvaraḥ ।। rājate jayate tena siddho ayaṃ dharmmarāj jinaḥ । yathā ca triṣu lokeṣu bodhicaryāḥ prakāśayan । karoti bhadratāṃ nityaṃ tathātrāpi kariṣyati ।। saṃsthāpayati saddharme yathā traidhātuvāsinaḥ ।
satvān prabodhayann asmān niveśayet tathā khalu ।। tataḥ sarve vayaṃ dhṛtvā saddharmaṃ śubhadaṃ śivaṃ । yaśopuṇyasukhaṃ bhuktvā yāsyāmo ante sukhāvatīṃ ।। iti matvā tathāsmābhiś candano ayaṃ jineśvaraḥ ।
mahatsatkārapūjābhiḥ sevitavyo mudā sadā ।। iti saṃbhāṣya taiḥ sarvais tathety abhyanumoditaiḥ । maṃtribhiḥ saha rājā sa prayayau taj jināśramaṃ ।। tatra prāptaḥ praviṣṭaś ca dṛṣṭvā taṃ caṃdanaṃ muniṃ ।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā cakāra prārthanām iti ।। namas te bhagavac chāstaḥ vayaṃ te śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । tat prasanno bhavāsmākaṃ kṣantavyā cāparādhatā ।। yad avṛṣṭiḥ pravṛttātra tad asmatpāpataḥ khalu ।
tatpāpaparihāṇāya saddharmaṃ deṣṭum arhasi ।। tad bhavantaṃ vayaṃ sarve snāpayitvā sasāṃghikān । yathāśakty upacāraiś ca samichāmo arcituṃ pure ।। tat prasīda munīndro asi yathāsmākaṃ hitaṃ bhavet ।
tathāsmatpuram āgatvā śubhaṃ kartuṃ samarhasi ।। iti tenārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā sa caṃdano muniḥ । tūṣṇībhūtvā tathety evaṃ adhyuvāsa sa sāṃghikaḥ ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatir jñātvā tad adhivāsitaṃ muneḥ ।
pādau natvā punar dṛṣṭvā sahasā svaṃ puraṃ yayau ।। tataḥ pure ca mārgeṣu śodhayitvā samaṃtataḥ । sugaṃdhijalasaṃsiktam akārayan mahītalaṃ ।। tataḥ puṣpāvakīrṇṇaṃ ca kārayitvā samaṃtataḥ ।
dhvajacchatravitānaiś ca tatpuraṃ paryyabhūṣayat ।। tatas tan nagare madhye kārayitvā saro varaṃ । tad gaṃdhodakasaṃpūrṇam akārayat praśobhitaṃ ।। tatra puṣpābhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā tīre samaṃtataḥ ।
chatradhvajapatākāni vitatya paryyamaṇḍayat ।। āsanāni ca prajñapya sasaṃghasya kramān muneḥ । svarṇakuṃbhāṃś ca saṃsthāpya śucigaṃdhāmbupūritān ।। tato pūjopacārāṃ bhojyopakaraṇāni ca ।
sādhayitvopasaṃsthāpya saṃgītisahitāni ca ।। tato rājā sa sāmātyaiḥ paurikaiś ca samanvitaḥ । taṃ buddhaṃ puram ānetuṃ jināśramam agān mudā ।। tatra sa sahasā prāpto dṛṣṭvā taṃ candanaṃ muniṃ ।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā gamanaṃ prārthayad iti ।। sarvajña bhagavaṃ gantuṃ samayo varttate adhunā । sarvaṃ ca sādhitaṃ siddhaṃ tadāśv āgantum arhasi ।। evaṃ tenārthite rājñā sa saṃbuddhaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ ।
pātracīvaram ādāya prāgāt tatpurasaṃmukhaḥ ।। yadāsau bhagavān buddhāḥ prātihāryyaṃ pradarśayan । lokān bhāsāvasaṃbhāsya prācaran prāptagopuraṃ ।। tadākampad rasā sābdhir vavau vāyuḥ sumaṃgalaṃ ।
kṣutpipāsā hatā ye ca te sarve paritṛptitāḥ ।। ye ca hīnendriyāḥ satvās te ca pūrṇendriyā babhuḥ । nirdhanā dhanināś cāsan rogino nirujo abhavan ।। baṃdhanasthā vimuktāś ca duḥkhitāḥ sukhino abhavan ।
unmattāḥ susmṛtiṃ prāptā nagnā āsan suvastrikāḥ ।। gurviṇyā yāś ca tāḥ sarvāḥ pramadāḥ sukhasūtikāḥ । ciravairānusaṃbaddhā maitrībhūtāḥ samācaran ।। ye ca pāparatāḥ satvā daśākuśalacārikāḥ ।
te sarve parisaṃtṛptāḥ puṇyakāmāḥ pracerire ।। evam anye ca ye tatra pāpakā upasargikāḥ । te sarve vilayaṃ yātāḥ te sarve saṃśubhāṅkitāḥ ।। evaṃ sarvaprakāreṇa hatvā sarvam amaṅgalaṃ ।
kṛtvā bhadraṃ ca sarvatra sasaṃghaḥ sa pure aviśat ।। kramāt pradakṣiṇenaivaṃ pracaritvā mahotsavaiḥ ।।vaṃdyamānas tu taiḥ sarvaiḥ sadevāsuramānavaiḥ ।। taṃ nṛpaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā rājamārgam upāsaran । tat sarovarasaṃprāpto dṛṣṭvā tīre samāśrayat ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān buddho yathā prajñapta āsane । ekacīvarakas tasthau snātuṃ tatra sarovare ।। tato nṛpādayaḥ sarve lokās taṃ caṃdanaṃ muniṃ । sasaṃghaṃ snāpayām āsuḥ svarṇakumbhāmbubhiḥ kramāt ।।
kṛtvā snānaṃ tato anyatra yathāprajñapta āsane । sasaṃgho bhagavān tasthau svaprabhāvaṃ pradarśayan ।। atha rājā sa taṃ buddhaṃ samāsīnaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । cīvaraprāvṛtaṃ kṛtvā pūjāṅgaiḥ samapūjayat ।।
tataś ca bhojanaiḥ śuddhaiḥ praṇītair vyañjanair api । paṃcāmṛtaiś ca pānaiś ca sutṛptiṃ samatoṣayat ।। tataś ca bhojanāṃte saṃśodhayitvā mukhādikaṃ । nīcāsane samāsīnaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo nṛpaḥ ।।
suprasannamukhāmbhojaḥ sa maṃtrījanapaurikaiḥ । natvā kṣamāpayitvā taṃ sasaṃghaṃ prārthayat tathā ।। sarvajña bhagavan nātha kṣamasva no aparādhatāṃ । prasīda sarvathā rakṣa dṛṣṭvāsmān pāpacāriṇaḥ ।।
tad durbhikṣavināśāya suvṛṣṭiṃ cāraya drutaṃ । sarvasatvahitārthāya saddharmaṃ ca samādiśa ।। ity evaṃ prārthite tena rājñā lokahitārthinā । saṃbuddho bhagavāṃś caivaṃ svāśīrvacanam abravīt ।।
ārogyam astu te rājan sarvatrāpi ca maṃgalaṃ । subhikṣaṃ sarvadāpy atra nirvighnaṃ bodhim āpnuhi ।। iti svāśīrvaco datvā saṃbuddhaḥ sa sasāṃghikaḥ । tataś ca svāśramaṃ prāgāt sa nṛpajanam anvitaḥ ।।
evam asya munīndrasya traimāsyaṃ ca niraṃtaraṃ । tenākāri nṛpendreṇa sevā satkārapūjanaiḥ ।। tataḥ śakro mahendro asau dṛṣṭvā tat sugatārcitāṃ । tad durbhikṣapraśāṃtyarthaṃ suvṛṣṭiṃ samacārayat ।।
tato jalāśrayāny ambupūritāni samaṃtataḥ । padmotpalādipuṣpaiś ca channāni rurucus tadā ।। tṛṇair navāṅkurodbhūtaṃ sādvalaiś ca prarūḍhitaiḥ । pratichannā haridvastraiḥ prāvṛtaiva rarāja bhūḥ ।।
vṛkṣāś cāpi haritpatraiḥ samāchannāḥ praśobhitāḥ । puṣpaiḥ prasphullitair amyaiḥ phalaiś ca saṃcakāsire ।। kramāc caivaṃ prarūḍhāni śasyāni varddhitāni ca । pariniṣpannasiddhāni pravipecuḥ samaṃtataḥ ।
tataḥ sarve janāś caivaṃ saṃprayātāṃ subhikṣatāṃ । dṛṣṭvānaṃdaṃ samuccāryya pracerire praharṣitāḥ ।। atha rājā sa tān sarvān mahāharṣapramoditān । dṛṣṭvā bhūyaḥ samāmaṃtrya vabhāṣa saṃprabodhayan ।।
bhavanto dṛśyatām asya saṃbuddhasyānubhāvatā । yasya puṇyānubhāvena prajātaiva subhikṣatā ।। tasmān nityaṃ tathaivāsya saṃbuddhasya jagatprabhoḥ । mahatsatkārapūjābhiḥ karttavyaṃ bhajanaṃ sadā ।।
evaṃ yadi sadā cāsya saṃbuddhasya jagatprabhoḥ । pūjābhiḥ satkariṣyanti sadātra maṃgalaṃ bhavet ।। tasmād asya munīndrasya nakhakeśavidarbhitaḥ । gandhastūpaḥ pratisthāpya sevitavyaḥ sadārcanaiḥ ।।
iti saṃbhāṣya rājāsau tais tathety anumoditaiḥ । saha bauddhāśramaṃ gatvā natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ ।। namas te bhagavaṃ chāstar vayaṃ te śaraṇasthitāḥ । sadā caivaṃ kariṣyāmo bhavatsevām upāsthitāḥ ।।
tat prasīda sadā pātra vihṛtya dharmam ādiśan । vijayasva na cānyatra mā vraja no anukaṃpayā ।। tenaivaṃ prārthite rājñā bhagavāṃś ca sa caṃdanaḥ । taṃ nṛpaṃ sajanaṃ dṛṣṭvā prasannāsyo abravīt tathā ।। naiva rājan mayā bodhir ekasyārthe prasādhitā ।
api ca sarvasatvānāṃ hitārthe hy anukaṃpinā ।। tasmād atra sadā naiva sthāsyāmy ahaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ । sarvatrāpi careyāhaṃ saddharmaṃ saṃprakāśituṃ ।। yadi me śraddhayā nityaṃ sevāṃ kartuṃ samichatha ।
keśastūpaṃ pratisthāpya sevyata sarvadārcanaiḥ ।। tatas te atra sadā rājye subhikṣaṃ maṃgalaṃ bhavet । durbhikṣatā ca kutrāpi nākramiṣyati kadā cana ।। iti matvā tvayā gatvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ svayaṃ ।
sarvasatvāś ca saddharme preraṇīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।। ity ādiśya munīṃdro asau chitvā svān nakharāṃs tathā । keśāṃś cāpy avatāryyaivaṃ tasmai rājñe svayaṃ dadau ।। tato rājā sa taṃ buddhaṃ natvā keśāṃ nakhāṃś ca tān ।
samādāya praharṣeṇa pratyāyayau svam ālayaṃ ।। tatra prāptaḥ pure madhye puṣkariṇyās taṭāntike । tat keśanakharān ropya gaṃdhastūpam akārayat ।। tasmiṃ siddhe pratisthāpya vidhinā ca mahotsavaiḥ ।
nityaṃ satkārapūjābhiḥ sevāṃ cakre prasannadhīḥ ।। etat puṇyānubhāvena loke aṃdhe apariṇāyake । jagalloke hitaṃ kartuṃ bhaveyaṃ sugatas tathā ।। iti dhṛtvā pracitte asau praṇidhānaṃ narādhipaḥ ।
gaṃdhajalaiś ca taṃ stūpaṃ snāpayitvā sadārcayat ।। pratisthāpya mahaṃ cāpi gatvā ca śaraṇe mudā । aṣṭāṃgaiś ca praṇatvaivaṃ mahotsāhair asevayat ।। tathā sarve janāś cāpi śraddhayā taṃ prabhejire ।
ye gatāḥ śaraṇaṃ tatra te sarve nirvṛtiṃ yayuḥ ।। aham evāvasiṣṭaḥ sa teṣāṃ yo abhūn narādhipaḥ । saṃbodhipraṇidhiṃ dhṛtvā naivaṃ nirvāṇam āyayau ।। etat puṇyānubhāvaiś ca suvṛṣṭiḥ saṃpracāritā ।
sarvadāpy abhavat tatra subhikṣaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।। etad dharmānubhāvaiś ca sarvatra sāṃprataṃ labhe । pūjāsatkāramānyāni yaśodharmasukhāni ca ।। yatra yatra pragachāmi tatra tatra samaṃtataḥ ।
itthaṃ satkārapūjābhir mānito ahaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tac chāstāraṃ samārādhya yaśodharmasukhepsubhiḥ । śubheṣu sarvadā nityaṃ caritavyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। śubhena sukhatā nityaṃ bhavel loke samaṃtataḥ ।
pāpena duḥkhatā caivaṃ miśritenāpi miśritā ।। tasmāt pāpaṃ viramyaivaṃ miśritāni vihāya ca । śubheṣv eva prayatnena caritavyaṃ sukhārthibhiḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve te sāṃghikās tathā ।
śrutvā pramenire satyaṃ karmabhāvaṃ bhavālaye ।। pāpebhyo viratā nityaṃ miśritebhyo api te sadā । sadā śubheṣu niratāḥ sarve saṃcerire samāhitāḥ ।। evaṃ rājaṃs tvayā nityaṃ pāpāc ca miśritād api ।
viramya sarvathā dharme caritavyaṃ sukhāptaye ।। prajāś cāpi vinirvāryya sarvathā pāpacāraṇāt । śrāvayitvā ca saddharmaṃ yojanīyāḥ śubhe sadā ।। tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api ।
suvṛṣṭiḥ pracarec caivaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।। iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena śāsinā । śrutvāśoko nṛpo astv evam ity anandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। snātāvadānaṃ tad idaṃ niśamya ye śrāvayanti pratibodhya lokān ।
te pāpanirmuktaviśuddhadehāḥ prayānti nūnaṃ sugatālayeṣu ।। athāśoko narendro asau bhūyo natvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ । upaguptaṃ guruṃ prāha śrotum anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi bhūyo apy anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
yathā te guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā me vaktum arhasi ।। iti tenārthite rājñā bhūyo apy asau jināṃśajaḥ । upagupto yatir bhikṣus taṃ nṛpam evaṃ abravīt ।। yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ vakṣye ahaṃ te subhāṣitaṃ ।
sādhu cittaṃ samādhāya śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ ।। yaḥ purāsīn mahābuddhaḥ sarvajñaḥ śrīghano jinaḥ । sarvavidyākalābhijño dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। śāstārhan sugato nāthas traidhātukavināyakaḥ ।
sa śākyādhipatir loke hitāya ca samaṃtataḥ ।। saddharmadeśanāṃ kṛtvā bodhimārgaṃ prakāśayan । bhikṣuśrāvakasaṃghaiś ca bodhisatvaiś ca sāṃghikaiḥ ।। upāsikāgaṇaiś caivam upāsakagaṇaṃ saha ।
rājagṛham upāśritya veṇuvane jināśrame ।। kalaṃdake nivāpākhye mahodyāne samāśritaḥ । ādimadhyāṃtakatyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ devāsuramanuṣyakāḥ ।
yakṣakinnaragaṃdharvāḥ siddhavidyādharādayaḥ ।। garuḍā nāgarājāś ca mahāharṣasamanvitāḥ । brāhmaṇā kṣatriyāś caiva rājāno rājaputrakāḥ ।। vaiśyāś ca śreṣṭhinaḥ śūdrā maṃtriṇo mātṛkājanāḥ ।
sārthavāhāś ca paurāś ca dhaninaś ca vaṇigjanāḥ ।। evam anye api lokāś ca sarve te saṃpraharṣitāḥ । mahatsatkārapūjābhiḥ sarvopakaraṇais tathā ।। pūjayitvā pravaṃditvā saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ muniṃ ।
parivṛtya puraskṛtya tasthau sarvānya tasthire ।। saddharmavāṃchitāḥ sarve śrotuṃ tatra samāgatāḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye pūryyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ subhago vaṇik । anyattamaḥ sārthavāha āsīn mahādhanaḥ sudhīḥ ।।
tena bhāryyā subhadrāṃgī jātidharmasamānikā । pariṇītā kulasthityai kuladharmānusārataḥ ।। tatas tau daṃpatī raktau snehānubandhitau mudā । yathākāmaṃ prabhuṃjānau sanramāte yathechayā ।।
tatas tasya gṛhasthasya bhogyeṣv evābhirāgiṇaḥ । svakulavṛttidharmeṣu pramādād anapekṣiṇaḥ ।। vyavahāre viraktasya prodyamarahitasya ca । arjanopāyamaṃdasya kevalaṃ vyayakurvataḥ ।।
dine dine kraṃān nityaṃ ativyayān nirāgamat । saṃpadaḥ kṣīṇatāṃ yātā griṣmakāla iva hradāḥ ।। tatas tasya gṛhasthasya bhāryā yā kuladharmikā । saṃpadaḥ kṣīnatāṃ dṛṣṭvā gṛhe caivaṃ vyacintayat ।।
ayaṃ me puruṣo bharttā sārthavāho vaṇik dhanī । bhāgyam eva gṛhe bhuktvā nivasati nirudyamaḥ ।। atyarthavyayatā yatra vidyate na tathāgamaḥ । sā ca saṃpat kiyat kālaṃ tiṣṭhet kṣīṇaṃ vrajet kramāt ।।
tad ayaṃ puruṣaś cāpi kathaṃ sustho bhaviṣyati । kena saṃdhāryyate lokair vihīne bhogyasaṃcaye ।। vṛddho apy ayaṃ bhaven nūnaṃ daridro api bhavet tathā । tadā kiṃ paribhuktvaivaṃ gṛhe tisthet kathaṃ sukhī ।।
yasya saṃpad gṛhe nāsti kathaṃ sa puruṣaḥ sukhī । svayaṃ bhoktuṃ na śaktaḥ syāt kiṃ punar dānam ācaret ।। dānaṃ vinā na saṃsāre kiṃ sārasukham āpsyate । dānenaiva hi labhyante yaśodharmasukhāni ca ।। dānena śuddhyate cittaṃ śuddhacitto bhavet sudhiḥ ।
sudhiyā sādhyate śīlaṃ śīlavān syāc chubhaṃkarī ।। śubhakarmā ca saddharmaṃ kṛtvā yāsyati sadgatiṃ । tasmād aham imaṃ nāthaṃ bharttāraṃ puruṣaṃ prabhuṃ ।। saddharmasukhasaṃprāptyai prerayeyaṃ dhanārjane ।
dhanavān puruṣo loke sarvārthasādhane kṛtī ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ mūlaṃ prāhur dhanaṃ budhāḥ । bhartur hi puruṣasyāpi trivargakāryyasādhane ।। sahāyaḥ kathyate prājñaiḥ satī bhāryyānucāriṇī ।
asya bhartur hy ahaṃ bharyyā satī dharmārthasādhane ।। manaḥ protsāhitaṃ kṛtvā prerayeyaṃ dhanārjane ।। iti niścitya sā sādhvī dṛṣṭvā bharttāram ādarāt । dharmārthasādhane caivaṃ protsāhayitum abravīt ।।
svāmi bharttāsi me nātho devatāpi tvam eva hi । tan mayā vakṣyate tathyaṃ paratreha sukhāya te ।। tathyaṃ ca tacchṛṇuṣvaivam anyathā cet tu mā kuru ।। yad bhavān purusaḥ prāḍhyaḥ sārthavāho vaṇik prabhuḥ ।
sadā bhogyāni bhuktvaiva sthitvā naivaṃ praśobhati ।। tat pramādaṃ parityaktvā yaśodharmasukhāptaye । satyadharmānusāreṇa kuruṣva dhanasādhanaṃ ।। dhanena sādhayed bhogyaṃ bhogyena pālayet tanuṃ ।
dehena sādhayed dharmaṃ dharmeṇa satsukhaṃ labhet ।। kiṃ ca yatra gṛhe svāmī vyavahāranirudyamaḥ । tatra sarve janāś cāpi niṣatsyaṃty avasādinaḥ ।। api yatra gṛhe svāmī vyavahārasamudyataḥ ।
tatra sarve janāś caiva pracareyuḥ samudyamāḥ ।। yac ca dānamahotsāhaṃ yatra gehe na vidyate । sa kiṃ geho na ramyaḥ syāc chūnyāraṇye śmaśānavat ।। yasmin gṛhe sadā nityaṃ dānapuṇyamahotsavaṃ ।
sa eva mandiro ramyasvargavat pratibhāsyate ।। yasmiṃś cāpi gṛhastho hi dānapuṇyanirutsahaḥ । svayam eva prabhuktvaivaṃ vasate paśuvat sa kiṃ ।। dhanyās te puruṣā vīrā yaśodharmasukhānvitāḥ ।
kṛtvā dānavṛṣotsāhaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā vasaṃti ye ।। teṣām eva hi saṃsāre susāraṃ jīvitaṃ khalu । ye kṛtvā dānapuṇyāni svayaṃ saukhyaṃ ca bhuṃjate ।। dānenaiva hi lobhyaṃte yaśodharmasukhāni ca ।
anyathā naiva lapsyante tataḥ saṃpan nirarthitā ।। kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyur ye bhuktvaiva sukhaṃ sthitāḥ । avaśyaṃ sarvaśo hitvā mṛtā yāyur yamālayaṃ ।। tatra karmasahāyāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā dharmādhipo yamaḥ ।
nirṇayitvā ca tat karma prerayet karmabhuktaye ।। ye ca pāpakarā duṣṭā prerayet tān tu durgatau । ye tu puṇyakarā bhadrāḥ prerayet tāṃś ca sadgatau ।। tatra karmaphalāny evaṃ duḥkhāni ca ।
sukhāni ca sarvatheha paratrāpi bhuṃjate sarvajāṃtavaḥ ।। śubhena sadgatiṃ yayād yaśodharmasukhānvitāḥ । pāpena durgatiṃ yāyād dhikpravādāsukhānvitāḥ ।। evaṃ matvā prabho svāmin yaśodharmasukhāptaye ।
svakulavṛttim ādhāya prodyamasva dhanārjane ।। sadā dānamahotsāhaṃ kṛtvā sadgatilabdhaye । yathechayā sukhaṃ bhuktvā pālayasva sadā janān ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bhaved iha paratra ca ।
saphalaṃ mānuṣaṃ janma nūnaṃ sadgatim āpnuyāt ।। iti bhāryāvacaḥ śrutvā sa gṛhastho vaṇik sudhīḥ । bhāryāṃ tāṃ vallabhāṃ kāntāṃ dṛṣṭvā caivaṃ samabravīt ।। ayi priye subhadrāsi mama bhāryānucāriṇī ।
yat tvayā bhāṣitaṃ satyaṃ tat kariṣyāmi sarvathā ।। kiṃ tu tvaṃ me priyā bhāryā vallabhātimanoharā । tat kathaṃ tvāṃ priyāṃ tyaktvā kutra yāsye dhanārthataḥ ।। sārthavāho hy ahaṃ cāpi tat kathaṃ nīcavṛttibhiḥ ।
ratnārjanaṃ kariṣyāmi tato ratnākaraṃ vraje ।। tasmāt priye subhadrāṃgī sati dharmānucāriṇī । gṛhakāryyaṃ samādhāryya vasa bhuktvā yathāsukhaṃ ।। yāvan nāhaṃ gṛhe prāptas tāvad dhairyyaṃ samāśraya ।
śīghram evāgamiṣyāmi maṃ smṛtvā mānvatapyathāḥ ।। iti bharttoditaṃ śrutvā sā ca bhāryānutāpitā । galadaśrumukhī natvā svāminaṃ tam abhāṣata ।। he nātha supriya svāmin māṃ vihāya kathaṃ vrajeḥ ।
tvayā vinā kathaṃ gehe tiṣṭheyāhaṃ yathā vane ।। darśane śravaṇe vāpi gaṃdhatailānulepane । sparśane bhojane pāne suvastraparibhūṣaṇe ।। saurabhyā aṅgane cāpi bhāṣane gamane kvacit ।
nidrābhoge tathā naiva vidyeta me abhilāṣatā ।। tavaiva smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā niḥśvasantī muhur muhuḥ । virahānalasaṃtaptā vrajeyaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। mṛtāyāṃ mayi te gehe ko anurakṣen nu saṃpadaḥ ।
śrutvā me maraṇaṃ nūnaṃ dhakṣyase virahānalaiḥ ।। tadaitābhiś ca saṃpattiratnaiś ca kiṃ kariṣyasi । aputrasya hi sarvasvaṃ nūnaṃ rājā grahīṣyati ।। tadātmanā vikhidyaivaṃ dūraṃ mā gā vihāyatāṃ ।
gṛhe sthitvā mayā sārddhāṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvodyamaṃ kuru ।। atrāpi bahavaḥ santi vaṇiksaṃghā mahājanāḥ । paṇyaṃ prasāryya taṃ sārddhaṃ sādhayasva dhanaṃ sukhaṃ ।। kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveva santatiś ca na vidyate ।
tat kiṃ nau bahubhī ratnair mā gā ratnākaraṃ hy ataḥ ।। yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā dānaṃ kṛtvā sadārthine । saṃvṛtyā prārjaya dravyaṃ svagehe saṃsthito rama ।। mā dhāva priya kutrāpi kiṃ vā ratnākare labhet ।
svagṛhe api labhej jantuḥ svakarmanirmitaṃ dhanaṃ ।। svakṛtaṃ karma tad bhāvi nirmāṇasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ । sarvatrāpi labhanty eva mahāntaḥ kṣudrikā api ।। tathā ye sujanā loke sadhanā sadguṇāśrayāḥ । te api kṣaṇād bhavanty eva nirdhanā bhikṣutāśritāḥ ।।
ye cāpi durjanā loke nirdhanā nirguṇāś ca ye । te api labhanti mānyārhaṃ sevyante cāpi sajjanaiḥ ।। tathā ye vaṇijo dhīrāḥ sārthavāhā maṇīchayā । ratnākaraṃ gatās teṣāṃ ke cit svastisamāgatāḥ ।।
ke cit tatra samudre vā bhagnanaukā dhanaiḥ saha । patitāḥ sannimajjantā mṛtāś ca vilayaṃ gatāḥ ।। ke cid vīryabalenaivaiḥ samuttīrya prayatnataḥ । akiṃcanyāḥ paribhraṣṭā riktahastā gṛhāgatāḥ ।
evaṃ sarve api satvāś ca svakṛtakarmanirmitaṃ । phalaṃ bhuktvā bhramanty evaṃ saṃsāre ṣaḍgatiṣv api ।। iti karmapramāṇatvaṃ jñātvā saṃpadvipattitā । mā khedaya svam ātmānaṃ dharmaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa ।।
tathā nau maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet khalu । yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā sadgatiṃ ca vrajemahi ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhātmajaḥ sa ca । taṃ priyāṃ ramaṇīṃ bhāryyāṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
bhadre satyaṃ tvaṃ yā proktaṃ yat svakarmapramānatā । iti matvāham ichāmi gantuṃ ratnākare api hi ।। yad abhāvi na tad bhāvi bhāvi cen na tad anyathā । sarvatrāpi bhaven nūnaṃ tenābdhiṃ gantum īhyate ।।
yadi bhāgyaṃ mamāsty evaṃ svasti syād gamane khalu । ratnāni bahuśo labdhā pratyāgacheya siddhitāḥ ।। atha me bhāgyatā naiva nūnaṃ tatra vipattitā । mahattīrthe nimagno ahaṃ mṛto yāsye surālayaṃ ।।
yathā bhaṭṭā mahāvīrā yaśodharmasukhāptaye । śatruṃ jetuṃ mahotsāhair viśanti raṇamaṇḍale ।। tatra ke cid dhatā vīrā yaśodharmānvitā mṛtāḥ । sahasā te prayānty evaṃ svargasaukhyānubhoginaḥ ।।
aham api vaṇikputraḥ sārthavāhātmajo hy ahaṃ । tat tathāhaṃ gaṃiṣyāmi ratnākaraṃ na cānyataḥ ।। yadi svasti gṛhaṃ prāpsye yaśoratnasukhānvitaḥ । mṛto atha nirmalībhūtvā svarge saukhyam avāpnuyāṃ ।। iti matvā priye bhadre mā viṣīda sukhāṃ vasa ।
yāvan nāhaṃ gṛhaṃ prāptas tāvad bhajeṣṭadevatāṃ ।। sarvathāhaṃ gamiṣyāmi svakulakīrtilabdhaye । anivarttī hy ahaṃ kāryye tan māṃ tvaṃ mā nivāraya ।। iti bharttur vacaḥ śrutvā nirbandhaṃ gamanaṃ prati ।
sā satī taṃ svabharttāraṃ natvā prāha kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। svāmiṃs tvaṃ sarvathā gantuṃ yadīchasi mahāmbudhiṃ । dhairyyam ālamvya saṃpaśyan mārge vraja samāhitaḥ ।। svasti te vrajato mārge sarvatrāpi divāniśaṃ ।
svasti pratyāgate caivaṃ bhūyān nityaṃ śubhaṃ sadā ।। yātrāsiddhimahāsaṃpadyaśodharmasukhānvitaḥ । svasti śīghraṃ samāgacha vrajā te astu sadā śivaṃ ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhas tatheti saḥ ।
pratijñāya vaṃksaṃghān sarvān āhūya cābravīt ।। bhavanto ahaṃ samichāmi yośodharmasukhāptaye । svakulavṛttim ādhāya gantuṃ ratnākarāṃbudhau ।। tatra gantuṃ mayā sārddhaṃ yadi yūyaṃ samichatha ।
tat paṇyaṃ sahasādāya samāyāta caremahi ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te vaṇijo mudā । sahasā paṇyam ādāya tatra gantum upākraman ।। atha sārthapatiḥ śīghraṃ taiś ca paṃcaśataiḥ saha ।
svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratasthe saṃpramoditaḥ ।। tataḥ kramād atikramya grāmajanapadāni te । vilaṃghyāraṇyadeśāṃś ca tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ ।। tato nāvaṃ samāruhya tāni paṃcaśatāni ca ।
pravitatya dhvajaṃ śubhraṃ jagāhire ambudhau kramāt ।। tathā te vahanārūḍhā vātānukūlato dhruvaṃ । kramād dvīpāṃś ca laṃghitvā ratnākaraṃ samāyayuḥ ।। tatra ratnākaraṃ prāptā devatā supramodataḥ ।
te mithaḥ kalahaṃ kṛtvā pratyāgaṃtuṃ na śekire ।। ciram evaṃ virodhitvād ratnāni ca na lebhire । bāṃdhavāṃś ca muhuḥ smṛtvā tasthuḥ sarve vilaṃvitāḥ ।। atrāṃtare ca sā nārī sārthavāhapriyā satī ।
bharttrā vinā gṛhaṃ śūnyam amanyata nirutsavāt ।। yad dine prasthito bhartā sārthavāhaḥ purād vahiḥ । tad dinārabhya sā nārī gaṇayantī dinaṃ prati ।। bharttur eva muhuḥ smṛtvā virahavedanāturā ।
niḥśvasantī muhuś caivam adhairyyā paritāpinī ।। kṛśāṅgā pāṇḍuvarṇā ca virukṣākīrṇakeśinī । prasādhanānabhīchantī malinavasanāvṛtā ।। darśanaśravaṇe cāpi gaṃdhānvāharaṇe api ca ।
bhojaneṣv api pāne ca sparśane gamaneṣv api ।। kutūhare tathānyatra manorame api cādbhute । sarvatra viṣayeṣv evaṃ na protsahe yathāturā ।। bharttur viyogaduḥkhārttā roginīva viṣādinī ।
asahyamadanākrāntā dhairyyopāyavicetanā ।। bhartur āgatim ālambya kṣaṇaṃ dhairyyasamāśritā । bhartāram eva saṃsmṛtvā gṛha eva nyaṣīdata ।। na nidrāṃ śayane bheje nānyasmṛtau mano anudat ।
prabhum evaṃ samādhyātvā tasthau dhyāyīva yogavit ।। athaivaṃ vikalībhūtāṃ yauvanīṃ tāṃ pativratāṃ । kācid ekā sakhī bhadrā saṃnirīkṣyābravīd rahaḥ ।। bhadre kin te viṣāda tvaṃ vibhāsi tvaiḥ yathāturā ।
mā viṣīda yad arthan te tad vadasva mayi priye ।। kathaṃ notsahase bhadre svakuladharmacāriṇi । kautuke cādbhute cāpi sarvatra viṣayeṣv api ।। bhojane bhūṣaṇe cāpi draṣṭuṃ śrotuṃ na vāṃchasi ।
kiṃ viṣādena siddhaṃ te tat prabhukṣva yathāsukhaṃ ।। iti tayodite sakhyā sārthavāhapriyāpi sa । tāṃ sakhīṃ pramadāṃ kāntāṃ dṛṣṭvā caivam abhāṣata ।। nāhaṃ bhogārthinī bhadre nāpi kāmātirāgiṇī ।
kiṃ tu dharmānuraktāsmi tat kathaṃ svāminaṃ vinā ।। tenāhaṃ viṣayāṃ tyaktvā smṛtvā bharttāram eva taṃ । svāgāra eva tiṣṭhāmi bhogyeṣv api ca nispṛhā ।। kadā sa me priyo bharttā gṛhe pratyāsariṣyati ।
iti ciṃtāṃ samādhāya tiṣṭhāmi yoginī yathā ।। yāvac ca sa priyaḥ svāmī nāyāti svagṛhaṃ prati । tāvad evaṃ na bhokṣye ahaṃ bhogyāni surasāny api ।। viṣayeṣv api sarveṣu na me vāṃchā priyaṃ vinā ।
nānyacciṃtā ca me citte tasmād evaṃ sthitā sadā ।। yāvat svāmī na me dṛṣṭas tāvat sthāsyāmy ahaṃ tathā । api me jivitaṃ yātu na ca yāyāṃ gṛhād bahiḥ ।। strīṇāṃ hi devatā svāmī dharmo api bhartṛsevayā ।
tasmāt smṛtvaiva bharttāraṃ bhājāmy ahaṃ pativratā ।। kutra dharmaṃ cariṣyāmi yasyā nāsti gṛhe pumān । tat manasaiva bharttāraṃ dhyātvā bhaje divāniśaṃ ।। dhig me janma nirarthaṃ syād yasyā na yauvane patiḥ ।
vṛddhatve kiṃ kariṣyāmi svāminā ca dhanair api ।। varam evādya me mṛtyur na mithyā cirajīvitaṃ । yasmāc ciram api sthitvā mṛtyuduḥkhaṃ tad eva hi ।। yam evālaṃvya jīvāmi sa yadi nāgamiṣyati ।
kim eva jīvitenāpi kevaladuḥkhabhāvinā ।। dhanyās tā hi striyo bhadrāḥ svasvāmisahacārikāḥ । kṛtvā dharmaṃ sadā gehe saukhyaṃ bhuktvā vasanti yāḥ ।। mā bhūt tu mādṛśi kācid abhadrā duḥkhabhāginī ।
samyagbhogyaiś ca kiṃ tasyā yasyā bharttā na yauvane ।। tathāpi kiṃ kariṣyāmi nāryy ahaṃ hi pativratā । tasmāt tam eva bharttāraṃ smṛtvā sthāsyāmi sarvadā ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā sakhī hitakāriṇī ।
tadupāyahitaṃ kartuṃ tāṃ sakhīṃ ca samabravīt ।। bhadre satyaṃ tvayā proktaṃ strīṇāṃ hi devatā patiḥ । tathāpi vakṣyate bhadre tava prītyā ca tac chṛṇu ।। yāvan nivasate gehe bhartā kāmarasārataḥ ।
tāvat strī sevayen nityaṃ dharmaṃ bhartur anujñayā ।। yadā bharttā gṛhe na syād dūradeśaṃ gatas tathā । yāvad gṛhaṃ na cāyātas tāvad devaṃ bhajet patiḥ ।। pates te devatāsmākaṃ viṣṇur nārāyaṇo hariḥ ।
tasmād enaṃ prabhor nāmnā smṛtvā nityaṃ bhajārcaya ।। sa eva kāmado devaḥ kāmadhātvīśvarādhipaḥ । saṃsārasthitidharmastho ratibhogyasukhapradaḥ ।। tasyaiva hy anubhāvena preryyamāno mano bhuvāḥ ।
bharttā te sahasā prāyāt svasti ratnaiś ca saṃyutaḥ ।। tatas te saphalaṃ janma saṃsāre prabhunā saha । dānaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ bhuktvā yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ vasa ।। evaṃ sakhyoditaṃ śrutvā ramaṇī sā pativratā ।
tatheti pratisaṃśrutya punas tām avadat sakhīṃ ।। satyaṃ bhadre yathā proktaṃ tvayā me hitakāraṇaṃ । tathāhaṃ saṃbhajiṣyāmi smṛtvā nāmnā prabhor hariṃ ।। yathā svasti samāyātaḥ svāmī ratnasamṛddhibhṛt ।
tadā hy ekaṃ suvarṇasya cakraṃ dāsyāmi viṣṇave ।। ity evaṃ sā pratijñāya viṣṇum evaṃ samasmarat ।। namas te bhagavan viṣṇo hare nārāyaṇa prabho । prasīda paśya māṃ nārīṃ prabhuṃ ca prāpayāśu me ।।
yadā me puruṣo bharttā svasti gehasamāgataḥ । tadopaḍhaukayiṣyāmi svarṇacakraṃ hare tava ।। iti sakhyāḥ puraḥ proktvā smṛtvā nityaṃ hariṃ mudā । svarṇacakraṃ ca saṃkalpya tasthau bhartuḥ smaranti sa ।।
tadaiva sārthavāho asau sarvasārthagaṇaiḥ saha । bahuratnāni saṃgṛhya pratasthe sahasā tataḥ ।। tataḥ svasti samuttīryya mahodadhes tadāgataḥ । sarvasārthagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ sahasā gṛham āyayau ।।
tatas taṃ gṛhasaṃprāptaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā naṃditā satī । pādau natvā puraḥ sthitvā svaṃ pravṛttam abhāṣata ।। svāmin yadā bhavān gehāt prasthito māṃ vihāya ca । tadārabhya sadā smṛtvā tvām evāsmi sthitā gṛhe ।।
tadāham anayā sakhyā dṛṣṭvā tvadvirahāturā । tad duḥkhaṃ me vinodārthaṃ preritā smaraṇe hareḥ ।। tadārabhya sadā nityaṃ smṛtvā taveṣṭadevatāṃ । bhajāmi satataṃ bhaktyā tavāśu gamanārthinī ।।
cakraṃ ekaṃ suvarṇasya saṃkalpya śraddhayā mayā । prārthanāpi kṛtā nityaṃ tava yātrāprasiddhaye ।। yathā me prārthitaṃ sarvaṃ tathā siddhaṃ hi sāṃprataṃ । tan me saṃkalpitaṃ deva pūrayeyaṃ tathā prabho ।।
tat pūjāṃgaṃ samādāya śakraṃ samupaḍhokituṃ । devakulaṃ gamiṣyāmi tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāho anumoditaḥ । pūraya tvaṃ priye satyaṃ gacchety evam abhāṣata ।।
tataḥ sānujñayā bhartuḥ satī sārddhaṃ sakhījanaiḥ । pūjāṃgāni ca taṃ cakraṃ dhṛtvā devakulaṃ yayau ।। tasmiṃ kṣaṇe sa saṃbuddho bhagavān karuṇāmayaḥ । loke satvān samuddhartum apaśyad buddhacakṣuṣā ।।
tām evaṃ prasthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhadrāṃ saddharmacāriṇīṃ । praikṣac ca bhagavān enāṃ pratyekabodhilābhinīṃ ।। tato asau bhagavān buddhaḥ saṃnirīkṣya ca tāṃ satīṃ । sarvān bhikṣugaṇāṃ chiṣyān samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā ।।
paśyadhvaṃ bhikṣavo yūyaṃ dārikaṃ tāṃ subhadrikāṃ । nūnaṃ maddarśanād eṣā bodhicittam avāpnuyāt ।। samyakkuśalamūlāni samavaropayiṣyati । dhruvaṃ pratyekabodhau ca praṇidhānaṃ kariṣyati ।।
tasmāt saṃdarśanaṃ datvā dārikāṃ tāṃ subhāvinīṃ । pratyekabodhicaryāyāṃ supratisthāpayāmy ahaṃ ।। tatra ca gantum ichanti ye mayā saha bhikṣavaḥ । pātracīvaram ādāya te prāyātaṃ caremahi ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ jinendreṇa śrutvā sarve api sāṃghikāḥ ।
pātracīvarasaṃyuktās tatra gaṃtum upācaran ।। tato asau bhagavān buddhaḥ svaprabhāvaṃ pradarśayan । sarvaiś ca sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ rājagṛham upāsarat ।। tatra mārge samāyātā dārikā sasakhīvṛtā ।
taṃ buddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ dūrād dadarśa saṃprabhāsvaraṃ ।। dvātriṃśallakṣaṇopetam aśītivyaṃjanānvitaṃ । divyātikrāntasaundaryyaṃ samantabhadrarūpakaṃ ।। sahasreṇātiriktābhaṃ saumyaṃ kāntaṃ manoharaṃ ।
puṇḍarīkam ivodbhāsaṃ ratnāṅgam iva jaṃgamaṃ ।। sākṣāt puṇyāvatāraṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cātyanumoditā । sahasopetya tac cakram upaḍhaukitum aichata ।। evaṃ tāṃ cakram ādāya saṃbuddham upaḍhaukituṃ ।
prayātaṃ tāṃ sakhī dṛṣṭvā nivārayitum abravīt ।। nāyaṃ nārāyaṇo bhadre sugato ayaṃ jitendriyaḥ । tad asmai mā pradehīdaṃ cakraṃ saṃkalpitaṃ hareḥ ।। evaṃ nivāryyamānāpi sakhībhiḥ sā ca bhadrikā ।
saddharmaguṇavāṃchantī tāḥ sakhīḥ punar abravīt ।। sakhyo bhāgyān mayāpy evaṃ saṃbuddho dṛśyate adhunā । tad adya saphalaṃ janma saṃsāre jīvitaṃ ca me ।। yadābhāsparśitā cāpi satvāḥ kleśavimocitāḥ ।
saṃvṛttisukhasaṃprāptā nirvṛttim api cāpnuyuḥ ।। yannāmoccāraṇād vāpi saṃbhāvyasmaraṇād api । mārapāśavinirmuktāḥ saṃbodhipadam āpnuyuḥ ।। yaddharmaśravaṇād evaṃ nityānumodanād api ।
sarvapāpavinirmuktāḥ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।। yatsaṃgheṣu supātreṣu kiṃcinmātrārppanād api । saṃsāre anantasaukhyāni bhuktvā yāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ ।। yenaivaṃ pālitāḥ satvāḥ ṣaḍgaticaritā api । bodhayitvā ca saddharme sthāpitā nirvṛtāv api ।।
yasya dharmānubhāvāc ca maṃgalaṃ bhuvanatraye । sarve satvā sukhāḍhyāś ca saṃbodhipadacāriṇaḥ ।। so apy ayaṃ bhagavān nāthaḥ śāstā trailokyādhipaḥ । nūnaṃ me puṇyabhāgyena dṛśyate ayatnato adhunā ।।
tad ahaṃ kuśalinī syāṃ hi saṃbuddhena darśitā । mahābhāgyavatī cāsmi yad ayaṃ sadguruḥ sudhīḥ ।। amṛgyamāna evetthaṃ labhyate purato mayā । tad ahaṃ pūjayitvemaṃ cakraṃ ca samupaḍhaukituṃ ।।
ichāmy asmai munīṃdrāya nirvṛtipadalabdhaye । api cātra sadā naiva saṃbuddho lapsyate tathā ।। kadā cid dhi jinotpattiḥ puṣpam audunvaraṃ yathā । mānuṣye api sadā naiva janma bhavānucāriṇāṃ ।
puṇyair eva hi mānuṣyaṃ lapṣyate janma dullabhaṃ ।। mānuṣye alabhyamāne tu kathaṃ buddhānusevanā । buddhasevāṃ vinā kena bodhicittam avāpnuyāt ।। bodhicittaṃ vinā kasya saddharmeṣu matiś caret ।
vinā dharmamatiṃ ko hi bodhicaryyāṃ samācaret ।। bodhicaryāṃ vinā loke hitaṃ kartuṃ kathaṃ caret । loke hitam akṛtvaiva kutaḥ puṇyam avāpnuyāt ।। apuṇyena kathaṃ kleśān hitvā nirvṛtim āpnuyāt ।
tasmāt kleśavimuktyarthaṃ nirvṛttipadalabdhaye ।। imaṃ buddhaṃ jagannātham ichāmy abhyarcituṃ mudā । buddha eva jagannāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthadaḥ ।। saddharmadeśakaḥ śāstā saṃbodhijñānanāyakaḥ ।
tasmād enaṃ samutsṛjya nānyam ichāmi cārcituṃ ।। asyaiva śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajiṣyāmi sadāpy ahaṃ ।। iti sā dārikā proktvā cakram ādāya moditā । saṃbuddhaṃ cārppituṃ tasmai pūjāṃ kartum upāyayau ।।
atha sā taṃ muniṃ natvā pūjābhiś ca samarcayat । taṃ cakraṃ samupasthāpya natvaivaṃ praṇidhiṃ vyadhāt ।। yathāyaṃ sugato buddho niḥkleśo vijitendriyaḥ । tathāham api śuddhātmā nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāṃ ।।
tathāsau bhagavān buddho dṛṣṭvā tatpraṇidhiṃ tataḥ । suprasannamukhāmbhojād vyasṛjat saṃsmitāmṛtaṃ ।। tatsmitasahoccāryamāṇā paṃcavidhāṃśavaḥ । ke cid ūrddhvaṃ gatāḥ ke cid adho yātāś ca te aṃśavaḥ ।।
ye ca yātā adholoke te saṃjīvanarake gatāḥ । kālasūtre ca saṃghāte tathā ca raurave tataḥ ।। mahārauravake cāpi tapane ca pratāpane । avīcau cārbude cāpi nirarbude tathāṭaṭe ।।
hahave huhuve caivam utpale padmake tathā । mahāpadme api caiteṣu ṣoḍaśeṣu samaṃtataḥ ।। tathopanārakeṣv evaṃ sarveṣv api ca te aṃśavaḥ । prasṛtā bhāsayitvaivaṃ prākāśayan samaṃtataḥ ।।
ye śītanarakās teṣu tūṣṇībhūtā nipātitāḥ । ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā vyabhāsayan ।। teṣu ye pāpinaḥ satvā duḥkhātivedanāturāḥ । te sarve taddyutispṛṣṭās tadduḥkhavedanojjhitāḥ ।।
śāṃtasaukhyānubhūtāś ca vismayoddhatamānasāḥ । dṛṣṭvaiva saha saṃmīlya mithaś caivam abhāṣata ।। aho citraṃ bhavanto adya kiṃ nu vayam itaś cyutāḥ । anyatra caritāḥ smaḥ kiṃ vatāhosvin na manyate ।।
iti saṃdigdhacittānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane । bhagavān nirmitaṃ tatra praiṣayac ca samaṃtataḥ ।। atha taṃ nirmitaṃ saumyaṃ dṛṣṭvā te saṃprasāditāḥ । bhūyo dṛṣṭvābhimodanto mithaś caivaṃ vabhāṣire ।।
bhavanto nu vayaṃ sarve nānyatra caritā itaḥ । api tv ayam ihāyātaḥ satvo hy apūrvadarśanaḥ ।। nūnam asyānubhāvena nirduḥkhā susukhā vayaṃ । iti te nirmite tasmin bauddhe cittaṃ prasādya ca ।।
namo buddhāya te tāyinn ity uktvā śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ । tataḥ sarve ca te satvās tadbuddhasmṛtidhāriṇaḥ ।। niḥpāpāḥ kuśalādhyāś ca sadgatiṃ sahasā yayuḥ । ye tathorddhaṃ gatās te ca buddhasmitotsṛtāḥ karāḥ ।।
gatvā cāturmahārājabhuvaneṣu tato gatāḥ । trayastriṃśāś ca yāmāś ca tathā ca tuṣitāṃ gatāḥ ।। nirmāṇaratikāṃ cānyanirmitavaśavarttinaḥ । brahmakāyikalokaṃ ca tathā brahmaprohitaṃ ।।
mahābrāhmaṇalokāṃś ca parīttābhaṃ tathā gatāḥ । apramāṇaṃ tato yātā ābhāsvarāṃ tathā gatāḥ ।। parīttaśubham evaṃ ca hy apramāṇaśubhaṃ tathā । śubhakṛtsnam anabhraṃ ca puṇyaprasavasaṃjñikaṃ ।।
bṛhatphalaṃ tathā caivam abṛham atapaṃ tathā । sudṛśaṃ bhuvanaṃ caiva sudarśanaṃ tathā gatāḥ ।। akaniṣṭhaṃ tathā gatvā proccair evam aghoṣayan ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ ।
iti matvā triratnāni saṃbhajadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane । dhunīta mṛtyusainyāś ca naḍāgāraṃ yathā karī ।। yo apy asmin dharmavaineye hy apramattaś cariṣyati ।
sa hitvā jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। evaṃ tā arciṣaḥ sarvāṃl lokadhātūn samaṃtataḥ । avabhāsya śubhe satvān vinīya punar āgatāḥ ।। bhagavato agrataḥ sthitvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ ।
ūrṇāyāṃ ca munīndrasya sarvā antardadhus tviṣaḥ ।। tadānandaḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo nataḥ । jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitvā bhagavantaṃ samabravīt ।। nānāraṅgakalāpas te vaktrān niṣkasito muneḥ । yenāvabhāsitāḥ sarvā sūryeṇodayatā yathā ।।
vigatoddhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ । nākāraṇaṃ śaṃkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ ।। tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya dhīrabuddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇajinendra kāṃkṣitānāṃ । dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ ।।
nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ । yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrās taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti janaughāḥ ।। ity ānaṃdavacaḥ śrutvā saṃbuddho bhagavān asau । tat smitahetum ādeṣṭuṃ tam ānandaṃ samabravīt ।।
evam etat tathānanda nāhetvapratyayaṃ smitaṃ । prāviṣkurvanti saṃbuddhā arhantaḥ sugatā jināḥ ।। paśyānandānayā nāryyā cakraṃ me samupārppitaṃ । pūjayitvā praṇatvā ca bodhau ca praṇidhiḥ kṛtā ।।
anena dānadharmeṇa kuśalaiś ca samanvitāḥ । dārikeyaṃ subhadrāṃśā divyabhogyaṃ samāpnuyāt ।। na paṃcadaśakalpāni vinipātaṃ gamiṣyati । tataś cakrāntaro nāma pratyekasugato sudhīḥ ।।
arhaṃ kleśavimuktātmā paṃcābhijño jitendriyaḥ । sarvasatvānukaṃpī ca brahmacārī bhaviṣyati ।। yan mayi sugate buddhe cittam asyāḥ prasīdati । tena puṇyabaleneyaṃ pratyekabodhim āpsyati ।।
sugateṣu kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana । kramāt tena viśuddhātmā saṃbodhim api cāpnuyāt ।। iti matvā triratneṣu cittam evaṃ prasādya ca । śraddhayā saṃprakarttavyaṃ satkāraṃ bodhivāṃchibhiḥ ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve janāś ca te । tathety abhyanumodantas triratnasevino abhavan ।। tato buddhānubhāvena tac cakraṃ khe samudgataṃ । kṣaṇaṃ buddhopari sthitvā chatram ivojjvalan babhau ।। tataś ca viyato gatvā hariharmyopari sthitaṃ ।
sudarśanam ivoddīptaṃ babhau rasmisamutkiran ।। tato asau bhagavān buddho dṛṣṭvā tāṃ dārikāṃ svayaṃ । śirasi pāṇinā spṛṣṭvā svāśīrvacanam ādiśat ।। bhadre te maṃgalaṃ bhūyā vinipātaṃ na cāpnuhi ।
kramāt pāramitāḥ pūryya pratyekaṃ bodhiṃ āpnuhi ।। ity āśīrvacanaṃ datvā saṃbuddho asau munīśvaraḥ । tato rājagṛhaṃ gaṃtuṃ upācarat sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tato asau dārikā cāpi natvā taṃ sugataṃ punaḥ ।
dṛṣṭvaivaṃ muhuḥ smṛtvā svagehaṃ samupāyayau ।। tatra gehe praviṣṭvāsau dārikā saṃpramoditā । bharttur agre ca tadvṛttam ācakhye sarvam ādarāt ।। bharttāpy asau tathā śrutvā buddhadharmānumoditaḥ ।
tayaivaṃ bhāryayā sārddhaṃ bheje ratnatrayaṃ sadā ।। evaṃ me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā te kathyate mayā । tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja triratnāni sadā bhaja ।। prajāś cāpi triratnānāṃ bhajane preraya prabho ।
tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bodhiṃ cāpi samāpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenopaguptena bhāṣitaṃ tat subhāṣitaṃ । śrutvāśoko narendro asau mumoda saha pārṣadaiḥ ।। etac cakrāvadānaṃ munivaraguṇadaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti prasādya ।
śrutvā yaś cānumodya pramuditamanasā śrāvayaty evam anyān । sa jitvā kleśasaṃghān vigatakalimalo buddhadharmānucārī । pūtātmā sadguṇāḍhyaḥ munivaranilayaiḥ saṃprayāti pramodāt ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ saddharmacaraṇotsavaḥ ।
upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā kṛtāñjalipuṭo avadat ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punaranyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā me guruṇā proktaṃ tathā vaktuṃ samarhasi ।। iti tena narendreṇa prārthite asau jināṃśajaḥ ।
upagupto mahābhijñas taṃ nareśam abhāṣata ।। yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā vakṣyāmi te adhunā । tathāpi śrūyatāṃ rājan tava dharmapravṛddhaye ।। puraikasamaye cāsau saṃbuddho bhagavāñ jinaḥ ।
cailakaiś ca tathānyais tatsaddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ ।। rājagṛham upāśritya veṇuvane jināśrame । karaṇḍakanivāpākhye tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat ।। tad dharmmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sadevāsuramānuṣāḥ ।
siddhavidyādharāś cāpi yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।। garuḍā nāgarājāś ca rākṣasāś ca mahoragāḥ । sarve lokādhipāś cāpi sasainyaparivārakāḥ ।। rājāno rājamātrāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca mahājanāḥ ।
maṃtriṇo śreṣṭhinaś cāpi sārthavāhāś ca paurikāḥ ।। ṛṣayo yoginaś cāpi yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ । evam anye api lokāś ca parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।। satkṛtya svaryya pūjāṅgaiḥ sarvopakaraṇair api ।
mānayitvā ca taṃ nāthaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra maudgalyāyana ātmavit । sa pretabhuvane gatvā caran pretīm apaśyata ।। svakeśaromasaṃchannāṃ dagdhasthūnāmahākṛtiṃ ।
sūcīmukhīṃ mahatkāyīṃ parvatasaṃnibhodarāṃ ।। piṅgalakeśinīṃ raudrīṃ pradīptāgniśikhām iva । tīvrātivedanākrāntāṃ tṛṣārttaṃ parimūrchitāṃ ।। tatrāyuṣmān sa maudgalyo dṛṣṭvā tāṃ pretikāṃ ciraṃ । kaiṣeti sahasopetya papracha samupāgatāṃ ।।
kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenaivaṃ duḥkhabhāginī । tṛṣārttā jalamārgantī bhramitvā carase adhunā ।। iti tena yatīśena pṛṣṭvā sā pretikā tataḥ । taṃ yatiṃ saugataṃ natvā praruditvāvadat tathā ।।
bhadanta tad vijānīyāḥ pāpakāriṇy ahaṃ yataḥ । evaṃ tṛṣṇāprataptāṅgā bhramāmi jalalālasā ।। yatrāham udakaṃ pātuṃ gachāmi tṛṣṇayānvitā । atra paśyāmi nadyādijalādhārān viśoṣitān ।।
yadā varṣati deve ca dṛṣṭvā tadambupātitaṃ । pātum ichantl tṛṣṇārttā sahasāhaṃ pradhāvitā ।। tadā paśyāmi tadvinduvisphuliṅganibhojvalān । dṛṣṭvaivaṃ nirāśāndhā bhramāmi dikṣu sarvataḥ ।।
kiṃ mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenāsmy evaṃ supāpinī । tan me pāpaṃ jagacchāstā pṛchyatāṃ bhavatādarāt ।। nūnaṃ so bhagavāñ chāstā yan me karmapurākṛtaṃ । vyākariṣyati tat sarvaṃ tathā lokaprabodhane ।।
yac chrutvānye api satvāś ca saṃvignamanaso drutaṃ । viramya pāpamārgebhyaś cariṣyanti śubhe sadā ।। tasmād bhadanta sarvajñas tava śāstā sa pṛchyatāṃ । vyākuryān mama sarvatra yat karma prakṛtaṃ purā ।।
asmannāmnā sa saṃbuddho vaṃdyatāṃ bhavatā yathā । ity uktvā sā tam ātmajaṃ natvā pretā gṛhaṃ yayau ।। sa maudgalyas tathety uktvā tat saṃdeśam anusmaran । sahasaitat paripraṣṭuṃ veṇuvanam upāyayau ।।
tadādau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tan maudgalyam upāgataṃ । prahasan suprasannāsyaḥ samāmaṃtryaitad abravīt । kaṃcit te kuśalaṃ vatsa kuto atrāsi samāgataḥ । lokeṣu kiṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ tat pracakṣva mahāmate । iti pṛṣṭe jinendreṇa sa maudgalyaḥ purogataḥ ।। ādau tasya muner natvā tat pravṛttam udāharat । āgato asmi bhadanto ahaṃ caritvā pretabhūmiṣu ।। tatra sthito aham īkṣan tāṃ pretīm ekāṃ bhayānakīṃ ।
dagdhasthūṇānibhāṃ nagnāṃ parvatasannibhodarāṃ ।। sūcīchidramukhacchidrāṃ kaṃkārayantrikām iva । svakeśaromasaṃchannāṃ jvalitāgniśikhām iva ।। tivrātivedanākrāntām ārttasvarānurodināṃ ।
durgandhām aśucivyāptāṃ svakeśaparitāpitāṃ ।। viṇmūtrānubhoktuṃ ca sākṣāt pāpāvatārikāṃ । bhagavan sā mayā dṛṣṭvā tṛṣṇārttā jalalālasā ।। bhramantī jalamārgantī jalāśrayeṣu sarvataḥ ।
nadīkūpataḍāgādin udapānajalāśrayān ।। svechāmbupūritān dṛṣṭvā prādhāvat sahasā yadā । tasyā darśaṇamātreṇa te sarve api jalāśrayāḥ ।। nirjalāḥ paṃkaśeṣeṇa śuśuṣuś ca samaṃtataḥ ।
tathā viśoṣitāṃ dṛṣṭvā nadyādīṃs tāñ jalāśrayān ।। nirāśā paritaptāṅgā sā pretī paryamūrchata । tataś ca punar utthāya kṣuttṛṣṇonmādacāriṇī ।। jalaṃ cānnaṃ samanveṣṭuṃ babhrāma dikṣu sarvataḥ ।
tathāpi sā jalaṃ nāsādayat kuhāpi vā ।। tato atitṛṣṇayā taptā viṇmūtrabhoktum aichata । tad api kṛcchrato anviṣya bhuktvā tṛptiṃ na sā yayau ।। tathāmedhyāni bhuktvāpi kadācin naiva tṛptitā ।
kṣuttṛṣṇāhatāklāntā patitā kheditāvasat ।। māṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya śanair mandasvarāvadat । svāgataṃ bho bhavān aitu rakṣa māṃ pāpinīṃ laghu ।। pānīyaṃ dehi me bhadra pānīyaṃ dātum arhasi ।
iti proktābhidhāvanti pānīyaṃ mām ayācata ।। tato aham avadaṃ caināṃ pānīyaṃ nātra vidyate । kātvam evaṃ nu duḥkhāni bhuktvātra vasase kathaṃ ।। kiṃ tvayā hi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenaivaṃ duḥkhatādhunā । vaktavyaṃ cec ca tat pāpaṃ sarvaṃ me vaktum arhasi ।।
iti me gaditaṃ śrutvā sa pretī punar abravīt । kiṃ mayā vakṣyate pāpaṃ yat purā kudhiyā kṛtaṃ ।। sarvajño hi bhavacchāstā sa evaṃ paripṛchyatāṃ । tat sarvāṇi ca me pāpaṃ sa vyākuryāt sa sarvavit ।।
asmannāmnā ca saṃbuddho vaṃdyatāṃ bhavatādarāt । iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā pratijñāya tatheti ca ।। bhavantaṃ praṣṭum āyāmi tat samādeṣṭum arhasi । ārttasvarā rudantī sā pretī vindati vedanāṃ ।।
yena viṇmūtradhānāni tena dhāvati duḥkhitā । tad api kṛcchrato labdhvā bhuṃkte kiṃ cit kadā cana ।। evaṃ sā pāpinī pretī dṛṣṭātiduḥkhitā mayā । kiṃ tayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ martyaloke sudāruṇaṃ ।।
yenaivaṃvidhaduḥkhaṃ sā hy anubhavati sāṃprataṃ । kadā sā pāpato muktā kathaṃ ca sugatiṃ vrajet ।। tat sarvaṃ vadatāṃ śāsta sarvasatvaprabodhane । iti tenārthite cāsau bhagavān punar abravīt ।।
maudgalyāyana sā pretī pāpinī matsarī kudhīḥ । tayā yat prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yena sā duḥkhabhāginī ।। tat sarvaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu śrotuṃ yadīchasi ।। purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo nāma sarvavit ।
sarvavidyādhipo nātho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। samantabhadrakṛc chāstā traidhātukavināyakaḥ । jino arhan sugatas trāyī saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ ।। sa satvānāṃ hitārthena bodhicaryāḥ prakāśayan ।
vārāṇasīm upāśritya mṛgadāve jināśrame ।। śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvagaṇair api । tasminn eva parṣatmadhye tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tasya bhikṣur anyatamo yatiḥ ।
anyatranagare gatvā pratyāgachat svam āśramaṃ ।। tatra mārge tṛṣārtto asau dūrāt kūpaṃ vilokayan । sahasā samupāgatya kūpāntikam upāyayau ।। tadaikā dārikā tatra pūrayitvā ghaṭaṃ jalaiḥ ।
sahasā śirasohitvā gṛhaṃ gantum upācarat ।। sa tṛṣārtto yatir dṛṣṭvā tām ambughaṭavāhikāṃ । samupetya jalaṃ pātuṃ prārthayan samupācarat ।। bhaginyo ahaṃ tṛṣārtto asmi dūradeśād upāgataḥ ।
tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasopetya jalaṃ pātum ihāgataḥ ।। tad bhaginī jalaṃ dehi jīvaya māṃ tṛṣāturaṃ । datvā me jīvanaṃ tvaṃ tac ciraṃ jīvyā niroginī ।। iti tenārthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā dārikāsau durāśayā ।
mātsaryyaprahatatvātā taṃ bhikṣuṃ paryyabhāṣata ।। are bhikṣo atra māyāhi mriyase yadi vā khalu । na te dadāmi pānīyaṃ ghaṭo pūrṇo bhaven mama ।। kūpe yatnāt samuddhṛtya pūrayitvāmbunā ghaṭe ।
prohitvāyaṃ mayānītas tvadarthe kiṃ na manyate ।। nirlajja kva nu te lajjā parakīyāmbum ichasi । rājā kiṃ tvaṃ dhanī vāsi gurur vā kiṃ na manyate ।। ity ākṣepaṃ pratikṣipya taṃ bhikṣuṃ saugataṃ yatiṃ ।
adatvaivāmṛtaṃ kiṃ cit satvarā sā gṛhaṃ yayau ।। tato bhikṣus tṛṣārtto api lajjayāsau nyavarttate । anyatraivaṃ samāyācya pītvā yayau svam āśramaṃ ।। tatrāśrame taror mūle paryaṇkam upabhujya saḥ ।
