anuśocaya tāṃ nārīṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। aho sā durmatī nārī mātsaryyaprahatāśayā । kathaṃ na manyate hy evaṃ mānuṣyajanma durllabhaṃ ।। mānuṣyaṃ puṇyato labdhvā nisphalaṃ kriyate tayā ।
dhik tāṃ durāśayāṃ mūḍhāṃ yasyā janma nirarthakaṃ ।। kadaiṣā pāpato muktvā sadgatiṃ samavāpsyati । mā gāt sā narake duḥkhaṃ bhūyād dharmānumodinī ।। śīghraṃ lokeśvarasmārttaṃ labdhvā vrajatu sanmatiṃ । ity evaṃmanasā bhāṣya sa bhikṣur vijitendriyaḥ ।।
triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ । tato asau dārikā gehe prāptā bhartuḥ purogatā ।। etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ vistareṇābravīn mudā । svāmin nadyāmbusaṃpūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ dhṛtvāgatā pathi ।।
tato bhikṣur upāgatya pānīyaṃ māṃ prayācati । adatvaivaṃ jalaṃ tasmai bhikṣave satvarāgatā ।। vahuśo yācyamānāpi kiṃ cin naiva dadāmy ahaṃ । iti tayoktamātre asau bharttā sādhur api krudhā ।
tāṃ bhāryāṃ rukṣaṇetreṇa dṛṣṭvā caivam abhāṣata ।। are pāpini durbuddhe kathaṃ na dīyate tvayā । kiyad vyeti jalaṃ datvā bhikṣave tṛṣitāya te ।। jalamātrapradāne api yasyāḥ śraddhā na vidyate ।
sā kim annaṃ dhanaṃ ratnaṃ kathāṃ dātuṃ samutsahet ।। dhik tvāṃ pāpinīṃ duṣṭāṃ yasyā nāsti dayārthine । kiṃ tvayā mama satyāpi yaśodharmapraghātayā ।। yady evaṃ na pradadyās tvaṃ kasmai cid arthine jalaṃ ।
preyasīm api bhārye tvāṃ parityakṣyāmy ahaṃ khalu ।। yadi me priyatāṃ kartum ichasi snehacetasā । arthino mānayitvā tad dānaṃ kartuṃ samutsaheḥ ।। no ced evaṃ mayā tyaktā vraja mā tiṣṭha me gṛhe ।
avaśyaṃ nau viyogaḥ syād ekānte maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। kiṃ tvādṛśyā striyā puṃsaḥ kevalaṃ dharmahānaye । dharmaṃ vinā na me kāryyaṃ dākṣiṇyāpi ca bhāryayā ।। kiṃ tvayā kāṃtayāpy evaṃ mātsaryyakuladurdhiyā ।
dharma eva vinaśyeta tad vraja mā gṛhe vasa ।। dharmeṇa rakṣyate lokaḥ kāntayā kiṃ hi rakṣyate । tat kāntāpi parityājyā yadi pāpanuraginī ।। bhāryā hi pālanīyā sā yadi dharmārthinī satī ।
kiṃ tvaṃ pāpārthinī duṣṭā yaśodharmavināśinī ।। naivāhaṃ ca tvayā sārddhaṃ bhoktuṃ rantuṃ samutsahe । kriyate cet tvayā dharmas tathā vasa mayā saha ।। no ced evaṃ mayā tyaktā tvaṃ mā tiṣṭha gṛhe vraja ।
evaṃ bharttrocyamānāpi pramadā sā na bodhitā ।। mātsaryyālīḍhacittatvād roṣitā caivam abravīt । naiva sthāsyāmy ahaṃ yāsye kiṃ sthitvaivaṃ vininditā ।। kiyat tvayy aparādhaṃ me yat tathāhaṃ vimocitā ।
kiṃ sa bhikṣur gurur rājā mitraṃ vā te pitā suhṛt ।। jñātir vā sa sakhā vandhuḥ kiṃ ca bhrātā prabhur dhanī । pradattaṃ kiṃ adattaṃ ca kiyan naṣṭaṃ bhavet yataḥ ।। naiva kiṃcic ca dāsyāmi kasmai cid bhikṣave arthitaṃ ।
adatvā me bhavet kiṃ hi dāsyāmy ahaṃ yathechayā ।। dāsyāmi vā na dāsyāmi kā carcātra tathā tava । pāpaś cen mayi pacyeta dharmo vāpi tathā mama ।। tvam atra mā kṛthāś cintāṃ kiṃ tvayātra vicāryyate ।
śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vā me tava kiṃ tad vicāratā ।। tathāpi mama doṣaṃ ced yāsyāmi na vasāmy ahaṃ । varaṃ prāṇaparityājyaṃ na tu dānaṃ dadāmy ahaṃ ।। ity asau pramadākruṣya bhartur ākṣipya garvitā ।
kvacit kiṃcic ca kasmaicid dadau naiva kadācana ।। gṛhe tithīn upāyātān dṛṣṭvaivātipraroṣitā । vahudhā kruṣya tān gehān nyakāsayad balādapi ।। tadāśīrvacanāny evaṃ śrutvāpi parikopitā ।
hasati nindayitvaināṃ paribhāṣya nyakāsayat ।। sadā badhvā gṛhadvāraṃ yācakāgatiśaṃkayā । koṣṭha eva samāsīnā kadācin na viniryayau ।। sarvadā svāminā sārddhaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ kalahaṃ muhuḥ ।
svayam eva prabhuktvāsau kālam evam ayāpayat ।। tataḥ kāla upāyāte pramadā sā rujānvitā । tadāpy evaṃ na cotsehe kiṃcid dātuṃ samarthine ।। tataḥ pravṛddharogārttā tṛṣṇārttā pariśoṣitā ।
mṛtā sā narake yātā pretī bhavati sāṃprataṃ ।। yā cābhūd dārikā duṣṭā mātsaryyaprahatāśayā । saivaiṣā hi tvayā dṛṣṭā pretī narakavāsinī ।। iti maudgalya dṛṣṭvaivaṃ pratyakṣaṃ pāpaduḥkhinīṃ ।
sarvādā śraddhayārthibhyo dātavyaṃ jalam ādarāt ।। sarvavastupradānānāṃ jaladānaṃ mahattaraṃ । sarveṣāṃ jīvanaṃ yasmād amṛtaṃ saṃvaraṃ jalaṃ ।। jalapānaṃ vinā sarve na jīvanti hi jantavaḥ ।
tad amṛtaṃ jalaṃ śuddhaṃ dātavyam arthine sadā ।। jalam eva hi pītvā te nirāhārās tapasvinaḥ । yogino anekavarṣāni jīvanti prāṇino yathā ।। sarvāhārābhisaṃtyaktā jivaṃti prāṇino jalaiḥ ।
sarvān na paribhuktvāpi na jīvanti jalair vinā ।। tad amṛtapradānaṃ taj jīvadānaṃ pracakṣyate । sarvavastupradānebhyo jaladānaṃ praśasyate ।। viśeṣād grīṣmakāle tu tṛṣārttāya ca rogine ।
bālavṛddhāturebhyaś ca dātavyaṃ jalam āditaḥ ।। jaladānaṃ mahādānaṃ jaladānasamaṃ na hi । yenābhidhāryyate prāṇaṃ tat phalaṃ saṃpraśasyate ।। sarvadhātupradānebhyaḥ sarvaratnapradānataḥ ।
sarvānnabhogyadānebhyo jaladānaṃ mahīyate ।। kanyākoṭipradānāc ca gajakoṭipradānataḥ । gavāṃ koṭipradānāc ca jaladānaṃ mahīyate ।। saptaratnamayībhūmipradānāc ca mahīyate ।
evaṃ sarvapradānebhyo jaladānaṃ mahattaraṃ ।। tṛpyante devatāḥ sarve pitṛlokās tathāpare । sarve bhūtāś ca satvāś ca jalenaiva sadāpi hi ।। tathā dravyāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni hy aśuciny api ।
jalābhiṣiktamātreṇa śuddhyante sarvadā khalu ।। jalaṃ vinā na tṛpyante bhuktvāpi divyabhojanaṃ । tasmāt sarvapradānānāṃ jaladānaṃ mahīyate ।। tathā ye ca sudhāṃ pītvā divyakāntā samarpitā । ramanti tridaśāḥ svarge te hi sarve jalapradāḥ ।।
cakravarttī nṛpendro yo ramaṇībhiḥ sahāmṛtaṃ । bhuktvā ramati saṃmodī so api cāmbupradānataḥ ।। evaṃ cānye api ye lokā yathechā sukhabhoginaḥ । niḥkleśā nirujā bhadrās te hi sarve jalapradāḥ ।।
ye tu nīcāśayādīnāḥ kṣutpipāsāturāḥ kṛśāḥ । yācakāḥ preṣyakāś cāpi sarve te ambho'pradānikāḥ ।। jaladānodbhavaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃkhyātuṃ naiva śakyate । sarvair api munīṃdraiś ca kim anyair vibuddhair janaiḥ ।।
matveti śraddhayā nityaṃ divyāmṛtābhivāṃchibhiḥ । arthibhyaḥ sarvasatvebhyo dātavyaṃ jalam ādarāt ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve ca bhikṣavaḥ । sarvebhyaḥ sarvadā kartuṃ jaladānaṃ samaichan ।।
athānandaḥ samutthāya natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ guruṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo pṛchan tatpāpaparimocanaṃ ।। kadā sā bhagavan pretī tatpāpāt parimokṣyate । sarvasatvābhibodhārthaṃ tat samādeṣṭum arhasi ।।
ity ānandena pṛṣṭe asau sarvajño bhagavāṃs tadā । tam ānaṃdaṃ samārabhya prāha pāpavimocanaṃ ।। śṛṇv ānaṃda samādhāya yena sā parimokṣyate । sarvasatvaprabodhāya tad upāyaiḥ pracakṣyate ।।
sā pretī narakeṣv evaṃ sarveṣu bhramitā sadā । duḥkhābhivedanākhinnā paritaptānutāpitā ।। tataḥ kālāntare saivaṃ smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ yadi । namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vaded yadā ।। tadā lokeśvaro sarvalokanātho jinātmajaḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sahasopetya svaprabhābhiḥ parispṛśet ।। yadā lokeśvarābhābhiḥ sparśitā sā sudhī satī । tadātisaukhyatāṃ labdhvā vismitaivaṃ vyacintayet ।। aho saukhyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ kasyānubhāvato adhunā ।
kim āhosvid itaś cyutvāgato anyatra vasāmy ahaṃ ।। iti cintāri tiṣṭhantī vismayoddhatamānasīṃ । dṛṣṭvā lokeśvaraś caināṃ bodhayitum upācaret ।। upetya tarpayitvā ca svatanuniḥsṛtair jalaiḥ ।
vividhair bhojanaiś cāpi pratarppayet sa bodhirāṭ ।। tato asau pāpinī pretī pītvā tat tanujāmṛtaṃ । paritṛptā viśuddhāṅgā natvā taṃ prārthayet tathā ।। namas te bhagavan nātha kṛpayā māṃ samuddhara ।
darśaya dharmamārgaṃ me sadā te śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। tayaivaṃ prārthite cāsau lokanātho dayānidhiḥ । darśayitvāryamārgaṃ ca śrāvayed dharmadeśanāṃ ।। yāṃ śrutvaiva ca sā pretī sarvapāpavimocitā ।
tataś cyutvā viśuddhātmā janma bodhikule labhet ।। tatra bodhicarīḥ prāptuṃ cared vratam upoṣadhaṃ । tadvratapuṇyabhāvaiś ca bodhicaryyāḥ samācaret ।। kramād bodhicarīḥ pūryya bodhipraṇidhimānasaḥ ।
bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। tato lokahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃbodhipadam āśrayan । sarvadā ca sukhaṃ bhuktvā sukhāvatīṃ gamiṣyati । tatrāmitābhasaṃbuddhaṃ sevitvā samupāśrayan ।
saṃbodhijñānaṃ āsādya nirvṛtiṃ cāpy avāpsyati ।। yady asau smarate pretī triratnānāṃ samāhitā । tadā caivaṃ tataś cyutvā saukhāvatīṃ gamiṣyati ।। no ced evaṃ hi sā pretī sadāpi narake vaset ।
yāvan na smarate buddhaṃ tāvan na mokṣyate tataḥ ।। evaṃ sarve api ye satvā yāvanto narakāsthitāḥ । tāvantas te api sarve ca duṣṭāḥ pāpānucārikāḥ ।। yadaiṣāṃ ye triratnānāṃ smaranty anutāpitāḥ ।
namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vadaṃti ca ।। tadā tatpāpanirmuktā viśuddhāṅgāḥ śubhāśayāḥ । saddharmācaraṇaṃ kartum utsaheyuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tato lokeśvaro dṛṣṭvā tān satvān dharmabhājanān ।
bodhayitvā prayatnena bodhimārge niyojayet ।। tataḥ sarve ca te satvā bodhipraṇidhimānasāḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena samicheyuḥ śivāṃ carīṃ ।। tatas te narakāc cyutvā saṃprayāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ ।
tatrāmitābhanāthasya dharmaṃ śrutvānumoditāḥ ।। bodhicaryyāḥ samāśritya kuryur lokahitāni te । kramād bodhicarīḥ pūryya sarvakleśavimuktigāḥ ।। saṃbodhijñānam āsādya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।
evam anye api ye satvā lokeśasaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। te āśu pāpanirmuktāḥ sukhāvatīṃ vrajanti hi । ye ye lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā bhajanti satataṃ mudā । te te sarve ca niḥpāpā bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ ।।
tasmāl lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ sadā । trimaṇḍalaviśuddhena caritavyaṃ vratottamaṃ ।। vratottamaṃ samākhyātam āryāṣṭāṃgikapoṣādhaṃ । sarveṣāṃ api puṇyānāṃ tadvratapuṇyam uttamaṃ ।।
yenaivāśu viśuddhyaṃte ghorapātakināpi ca । tasmād etat mahatpuṇyaṃ vratarājaṃ vidur jināḥ ।। yasya puṇyānubhāvena pūryya pāramitāgaṇāḥ । sarvakleśān vinirjitya śīghraṃ bodhim avāpnuyuḥ ।।
ye apy atītāś ca saṃbuddhāḥ sarvajñāḥ sugatā jināḥ । te api tadvratapuṇyais tu śīghraṃ bodhim avāpnuvan ।। ye apy etarhi ca saṃbuddhāḥ saṃbodhidharmadeśakāḥ । te apy etadvratapuṇyaiś ca bhavanti bodhipāragāḥ ।। ye cāpy anāgatā buddhā bhaviṣyanti tathāgatāḥ ।
te apy etadvratapuṇyais tu lapsyante bodhisaṃpadaṃ ।। evam anye api ye prājñāḥ saṃbodhipadavāṃchitāḥ । te apy etadvratam ādhāya labhanti bodhisaṃpadaṃ ।। tasmād etadvrataṃ dhṛtvā dātavyaṃ dānam adarāt ।
etat phalaṃ sadākṣīṇaṃ sūte kalpatarur yathā ।। etadvratadharāḥ satvāḥ saddharmācaraṇodyatāḥ । sarvathā na vrajaṃty eva durgatiṣu kadācana ।। sadaiva sugatiṃ prāptāḥ sarvasatvānukaṃpinaḥ ।
saddharmācaraṇaṃ dhṛtvā bodhisatvā bhavanti te ।। ye ca lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā caranty etadvrataṃ sadā । te paśyanti sadāpy enaṃ lokanāthaṃ jagatprabhuṃ ।। tena lokeśvareṇāpi dṛśyaṃte te api sarvadā ।
ye ca lokeśasaṃdṛṣṭās te sarve bodhibhāginaḥ ।। bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ । ye smaranti sadā nityaṃ lokeśaṃ karuṇāmayaṃ । sahasā durgatiṃ tyaktvā muktvā yāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ ।।
ye ca taccharaṇaṃ gatvā bhajaṃti taṃ jinātmajaṃ । sarvapāpavinirmuktās te api yāyuḥ sukhāvatiṃ ।। ye sugandhair jalaiḥ śuddhaiḥ snāpayanti jagadguruṃ । mandākinyāṃ ca te snātvā śuddhā yāṃti sukhāvatiṃ ।।
paṃcagaṃdhādisaurabhyair lokeśaṃ lepayaṃti ye । cakravarttipadaṃ bhuktvā te api yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ ।। cīvaraṃ ye dadaṃty asmai te divyavastrasaṃyutāḥ । sarvadharmādhināthāś ca yāṃti cāṃte sukhāvatīṃ ।।
satkṛtya śraddhayā ye api puṣpais tam arcayanti ye । te surendrapadaṃ prāpya yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। saurabhyayojitair dhūpair ye bhajanti tam īśvaraṃ । te narendrapadaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti cānte sukhāvatiṃ ।। ye dadanti ca bhaiṣajyaṃ tasmai lokādhipāya ca ।
cakravarttipadaṃ prāpya yāṃti te ca sukhāvatīṃ ।। ye dadanti pradīpāni tasmai lokeśvarāya ca । te mahendrapadaṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। naivedyaṃ ye dadanty asmai te bhavanti nareśvarāḥ ।
divyabhogyāni bhuktvā ca yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। ye ca pānaṃ dadanty asmai te pītvā satataṃ sudhāṃ । svarge ramanti devendrā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। phalamūlādikaṃ dattaṃ yaiś ca tasmai sutāyine ।
yathepsitasukhaṃ bhuktvāṃte api yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ ।। tāmbūlaṃ pūgasaṃyuktaṃ lokeśāya dadanti ye । surūpāḥ satsukhaṃ bhuktvāṃte api yānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। śayyāsanaṃ pradattaṃ yais tasmai satvānukaṃpine ।
te kṣitīśaśriyaṃ bhuktvā yānty aṃte ca sukhāvatīṃ ।। siṃhāsanaṃ pradattaṃ yais tasmai dharmānuśāsine । te vaṃdyāḥ sarvalokaiś ca yānty ante ca sukhāvatīṃ ।। chatraṃ tasmai pradattaṃ yais te nṛpāś cakravarttinaḥ ।
yaśodharmasukhaṃ bhuktvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। patākāṃ ye prayachanti tasmai lokādhipāya cā । te api sarvāṃ mahīṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। tasmai ye ca prayachanti dhāturatnagaṇāni ca ।
te narendrāś caturdvīpāṃ bhuktvā yānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। ye vitānaṃ vitanvaṃti gehe tasya kṛpānidheḥ । te narendrāḥ surendrāś ca bhūtvā yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ ।। trailokyādhipates tasya ye kurvanti pradakṣiṇāṃ ।
te narendraśriyaṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। saṃgītair ye prakurvanti pūjāṃ tasya jagat prabhoḥ । sadā subhāṣitāny eva śṛṇvanti te guṇākarāḥ ।। cāmarair vyajanair vāpi taṃ nāthaṃ vījayanti ye । te nṛpāḥ suralakṣmīṃ ca bhuktvā yāṃti jinālaye ।।
śodhayanti ca ye nityaṃ vihāre kāruṇānidheḥ । divyanetrāś ca te saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti surālayaṃ ।। kṛtvā ramyaṃ vihāraṃ ca lokeśāya dadanti ye । te mahendraśriyaṃ bhuktvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।।
vihāre tatra saṃsiddhe yaṣṭim āropya ye narāḥ । suvarṇakalaśāṃś chatradhvajaghaṇṭāvalīyutān ।। paṃcavarṇapatākābhiḥ puṣpasragbhiś ca saṃyutān । saṃpratisthāṃ prakurvati mahotsāhair vidhānataḥ ।।
te narendrāḥ surendrāś ca yaśodharmasukhānvitāḥ । māheśvaryyaśriyaṃ bhuktva yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। padyagadyamayaiḥ stotrair ye stuvaṃti taṃ īśvaraṃ । niḥpāpāḥ sukhinaḥ prājñās te prayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।।
ye cāṣṭāṃgapraṇāmāni asmai śāstre prakurvaṃte । cakravartīpadaṃ bhuktvā te prayānti jinālayaṃ ।। ye smaranti sadā nityaṃ tam īśaṃ sugatātmajaṃ । te sadyaḥ pāpanirmuktā ante yānti sukhāvatīṃ ।।
ye ye satvāś ca taṃ nāthaṃ smṛtvā bhajanti sarvadā । te te sarve na yānty eva durgatiṣu kadācana ।। sadāpi sadgatiṣv eva yātāḥ saukhyasamanvitāḥ । saddharmācaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।।
evaṃ ye pāpinaś cāpi lokeśaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । te api pāpavinirmuktāḥ śuddhā yāṃti jinālayaṃ ।। evaṃ lokeśvaro nāthaḥ puṇyakṣetraṃ śubhapradaḥ । ciṃtāmaṇiḥ kalpavṛkṣo yathepsitaphalapradaḥ ।।
na hi tena samaḥ kaścin mahatpuṇyaphalapradaḥ । kuto adhikas tu vidyeta traidhātubhuvaneṣv api ।। tenaiva sakalāḥ satvā bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । āryyamārge pratiṣṭhāpya preritā nirvṛtāv api ।।
pāpiṣṭho api satvāś ca tenopetya svayaṃ tathā । narakebhyaḥ samuddhṛtya saṃpreritāḥ sukhāvatīṃ ।। evaṃ sarve api satvāś ca nānopāyavidhānataḥ । darśayitvāryyamārgāṇi tena bodhau niveśitāḥ ।।
tasmāt sarvādhikeśaḥ sa lokeśvaro maheśvaraḥ । sarvadharmānubhartā sa lokanāthaḥ pratīyate । kenāpi gaṃtuṃ tasya puṇyaskaṃdhaṃ na śakyate । mayāpi śakyate naivaṃ sarvaiś cāpi munīśvaraiḥ ।
evaṃ matvā tvam ānaṃdaḥ lokanathaṃ dayodadhiṃ ।। sarvadevādhideveśaṃ smṛtvaiva satataṃ bhaja । tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvadāpi samaṃtataḥ ।। kutaś cin naiva vidyeran bhayāni vividhāny api ।
yatra lokeśvarasmṛtis tatrotpātabhayaṃ na hi ।। agner api bhayaṃ naiva nāpy utpātamarudbhayaṃ । na codakabhayaṃ tatra na ca bhūmibhayaṃ khalu ।। vidyutpātabhayaṃ nāpi na cāśanibhayaṃ sadā ।
na ca śatrubhayaṃ kvāpi nāpi rājabhayaṃ tathā ।। na ca caurabhayāny evaṃ na ca rogabhayāni ca । sarvabhayaḥ praśāmyante lokeśasmṛtibhāvataḥ ।। sarve apy upadravāś caivaṃ prayāṃti vilayaṃ tataḥ ।
evaṃ lokeśvaro nātho mahatpuṇyānubhāvavān ।। yenaivaṃ trijagallokaṃ pālitaṃ putravat sadā । tasmāl lokeśvaro nityaṃ sevitavyaḥ śubhārthibhiḥ ।। yasya dharmānubhāvena sarvatrāpi śivaṃ sadā ।
iti matvā tvayānaṃda tad dharmāñ chrāvayan sadā ।। prerayitvā ca tadbhaktau saṃbodhau saṃpraveśaya । etatpuṇyānubhāvais tvam apy evaṃ kuśalī bhavan ।। bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bhaven nūnaṃ jinātmajaḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ ।
tatheti pratimoditvā sadā lokeśam asmarat ।। evaṃ rājaṃs tvayā cāpi smṛtvā lokeśvaraḥ sadā । sevitavyaḥ prayatnena bodhipraṇidhicetasā ।। tatas tvaṃ sahasā sarvapāpebhyaḥ parimocitaḥ ।
bodhisatvo viśuddhātmā prayāsyasi sukhāvatīṃ ।। ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena dhīmatā । śrutvā rājānumoditvā so abhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। idaṃ śrutvāvadānaṃ ye śrāvayitvā parān api ।
bhajaṃti lokanāthaṃ te saṃprayāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ ।। athāśoko mahīpālo bhūyaḥ śrotuṃ subhāsitaiḥ । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā kṛtāṃjalir avocat ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
tad arhasi samādeṣṭuṃ lokānāṃ puṇyavṛddhaye ।। iti vijñāpite tena nṛpendreṇa prasādinā । upagupto yatiś cāpi taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga sarvalokahitārthabhṛt ।
yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ vakṣye ahaṃ te tathā khalu ।। puraikasamaye buddho bhagavāñ chrīghano jinaḥ । śrāvastyāṃ jetakāraṇye vihāre maṇimaṇḍite ।। śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ saṃghair bodhisatvagaṇaiḥ saha ।
saddharmadeśanāṃ kartuṃ vyaharal lokaśāsituṃ ।। taddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve satvāḥ samāgatāḥ । brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi rājāno rājamātrikāḥ ।। vaiśyāḥ śūdrā amātyāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ sādhavo janāḥ ।
śreṣṭhinaḥ sārthavāhāś ca dhaninaś ca vaṇiggaṇāḥ ।। paurājānapadāś cāpi nānādeśasamāgatāḥ । devā daityāś ca gandharvā yakṣakinnararākṣasāḥ ।। siddhāvidyādharāḥ sādhyā vasavaś ca grahādhipāḥ ।
nāgeṃdrā garuḍāś caivam ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇāḥ ।। yogino yatayaś cāpi lokapālāḥ sasainyakāḥ । sarve taṃ sugataṃ natvā dharmaṃ śrotum upāgatāḥ ।। satkṛtya pūjayitvā ca kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā ।
parivṛtya puraskṛtya dṛṣṭvā tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān dharmavāṃchinaḥ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tatra devādayaḥ sarve tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ mudā ।
pītvā cābhyanumodantaḥ prāpur jñānaviśeṣatāṃ ।। śrāvasteyāt tadāneke dārikā dārakāś ca te । kusumān yācitaṃ śālabhaṃjikākhyaṃ giriṃ yayuḥ ।। tatra te sahasā gatvā dṛṣṭvā puṣpāṇy anekaśaḥ ।
prādāya samupāgatvā śrāvastyām acaran mudā ।। tatraikā dārikā vālā śreṣṭhiputrī pramoditā । śanaiḥ sā śālapuṣpāṇi prādāya pṛṣṭhato acarat ।। tadā ca bhagāvān buddho bhikṣusaṃghasamanvitaḥ ।
śrāvastyāṃ bhojanaṃ bhuktvā tato bahir viniryayau ।। tatra sā dārikādrākṣīd bhagavantaṃ tam āgataṃ । dvātriṃśal lakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaṃ samalaṃkṛtaṃ ।। vyāmaprabhāvirājantaṃ sahasreṇādhikaprabhaṃ ।
jaṃgamam iva ratnāṅgaṃ samantabhadrarūpikaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvaivaṃ śrīghanaṃ nāthaṃ dārikā sā pramoditā । śraddhayārcayituṃ puṣpair manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। aho puṇyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ yat saṃbuddho dṛśyate adhunā ।
evaṃ kadā kathaṃ kutra drakṣyate ayaṃ munīśvaraḥ ।। bhāgyenaivaṃ mayā labdhaṃ saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ tathā । nūnaṃ bhāgyavatī cāsmi yat puṇyanidhir āpyate ।। tasmāt puṇyaṃ mahāratnaṃ prāptum upetya sādaraṃ ।
etaiś ca kusumaiḥ sarvair arhāmy etaṃ samarcituṃ ।। kadāyaṃ lapsyate bhūyaḥ paravaśyā striyā mayā । tad ahaṃ sahasopetya puṣpāṇy asmāy upākire ।। sadā notpadyate nātra saṃbuddho hi kadā cana ।
atisudurllabhaṃ hy asya darśanaṃ ca sadā na hi ।। mānuṣyaṃ durllabhaṃ janma vinā puṇyair na labhyate । mānuṣye alabhyamāne api saṃbuddhe sevyate kathaṃ ।। mānuṣye labhyamāne api kṣaṇaṃ saṃpat sudurllabhā ।
narair apy akṣaṇaprāptaiḥ kathaṃ buddhe anusevyate ।। tad adya mānuṣī bhūtvā prāpyaivaṃ sukṛtau kṣaṇaṃ । yady atra kusumair ebhiḥ saṃbuddhaṃ nārcayāmy ahaṃ ।। tato me niṣphalaṃ janma mānuṣye vyartham eva hi ।
kiṃ mamānena dehena sarvathaikāntanāśinā ।। kim anenāpi jīvena mṛtyau nityaṃ puraḥsthite । kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyaṃ gacheyaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ciraṃ sthitvāpi kiṃ sāraṃ saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ vinā ।
varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ sarvadehādikaṃ dhanaṃ । etad eva tu satsāraṃ yad buddhe bhajanaṃ sadā ।। tadaitaiḥ kusumaiḥ sarvaiḥ pūjayāmi munīśvaraṃ ।
kathaṃ na pūjayisyāmi saṃbuddhaṃ trijagadguruṃ ।। iti niścitya sā vālā dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ mudā । sahasopetya taiḥ sarvaiḥ sālapuṣpair avākiran ।। tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇamya taṃ praharṣitā ।
kiṃ cid dūre parāvṛtya tasthau dṛṣṭvā muniṃ mudā ।। tato asau bhagavān buddhas tasyā āyurvihīnatāṃ । matvā tāṃ saṃnrīksyaivaṃ svaṃ vihāraṃ samāyayau ।। atha sā dārikā bhūyas tathānyatkusumāni ca ।
gṛhasyārthe samādātuṃ tataḥ śālavanaṃ yayau ।। tatra śālataruṃ dṛṣṭvā praphullakusumānvitaṃ । tatpuṣpāṇi samācetuṃ sahasā sā ruroha taṃ ।। tatrāvaruhya puṣpāṇi cinvantī sā pramodataḥ ।
agraśākhāsamārūḍhā papāta sahasā tataḥ ।। patitā sā virugnāṅgā tīvrātivedanāturā । hā hatāsmīti niścitya saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ vyadhāt ।। namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya sugatāya ca ।
iti proktvaiva saṃbuddhaṃ smaranti maraṇaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ svargopapannā sā vismitaivaṃ vyacintayat । kutaś cyutvā kuhotpannā kena vā kuśalena ca ।। iti cintāparītā sā sahasaivaṃ vyabuddhyata ।
martyāc cyutvāgatā svarge buddhe puṣpapradānataḥ ।। iti buddhvā ca sā bhadrā suprasāditamānasī । tam eva sugataṃ nāthaṃ smṛtvā natvābhyanandata ।। tato devair upanītaṃ divyapuṣpasvalaṃkṛtaṃ ।
vimānaṃ sā samāruhya devasabhām upāyayau ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye śakraḥ sudharmāyāṃ suraiḥ saha । saṃbuddhavarṇanāṃ kṛtvā tasthau devān pramodayan ।। tathā tāṃ samupāyātāṃ śālapuṣpābhyalaṃkṛtāṃ ।
dṛṣṭvā divyātivarṇābhāṃ papracha vismito hariḥ ।। gātraṃ kena vimṛṣṭakāṃcananibhaṃ padmotpalābhaṃ tava । divyaśrīr atulākṛteyam iha te kena prabhā niḥsṛtā । vaktraṃ kena vibuddhapadmasadṛśaṃ cāmīkarābhaṃ tava ।
kasya tvaṃ varadevate phalam idaṃ yat karmajaṃ bhujyate ।। iti prokte surendreṇa sā bhadrā devakanyakā । taṃ devādhipatiṃ natvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo abravīt ।। saśrāvakā narāditya ākīrṇaśālapuṣpakaiḥ ।
tatkarmakuśalaṃ kṛtvā rājate me adhikaṃ tanuḥ ।। jalajenduviśuddhābhaṃ vadanaṃ me abhirocate । etatkarmānubhāvena vijānīyāḥ sureśvara ।। tayeti proditaṃ śrutvā devendro asau suvismitaḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā caināṃ subhadrāṅgīṃ praharṣayann abhāṣata ।। aho guṇamayaṃ kṣetraṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitaṃ । yatra nyastaṃ tvayā vījam itthaṃ svargopapattaye ।। ko nārcayet pravarakāṃcanarāśigauraṃ buddhaṃ vibuddhakamalāyatapatranetraṃ ।
yatrādhikārajanitāni viśobhitāni kāṃtāmukhāni kamalāyatalocanāni ।। dhanyo asi tvaṃ subhadrāṃgi saṃbuddhaguṇabhāvini । sarvathā hi sa saṃbuddhaḥ sevitavyaḥ sadāpi ca ।। yasya puṇyaprasādāt tvaṃ sadyaḥ svarge samāgatā ।
sa eva bhagavān nāthaḥ saṃsmṛtvā sevyatāṃ sadā ।। tatas te sarvadā nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ syāt samaṃtataḥ । ciraṃ divyasukhaṃ bhuktvā yāyāś cānte sukhāvatīṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ surendreṇa sā devakanyakā sudhīḥ ।
anumodya ca taṃ śakraṃ natvā svam ālayaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sā saṃsthitā devīprāsāde divyamaṇḍite । divyabhogyasukhaprāptā moditvaivaṃ vyacintayet ।। yac cyutvāhaṃ manuṣyebhyo adhunā svargasamāgatā ।
tat saṃbuddhaprasādena jānāmi nānyathā khalu ।। yan mayā pūjito buddhaḥ śālapuṣpair vanodbhāvaiḥ । tatpuṇyaphalabhogyārthe āgatāhaṃ surālayaṃ ।। yad divyasukhasaṃprāptaṃ tat saṃbuddhaprasādataḥ ।
tena tam evaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ punar gacheya vaṃdituṃ ।। na yuktaṃ saugate gantuṃ paryyuṣitena vāsasā । yuktaṃ tu saugate gaṃtum aparyuṣitavāsasā ।। iti sā manasā matvā devakanyā subhadrikā ।
snātvā saurabhyaliptāṃgā divyaśuddhāmvarāvṛtā ।। divyālaṃkāramālādimaulīkuṇḍalamaṃḍitā । anekadevakanyābhir apsarobhiḥ samanvitā ।। divyapūjopacārāṇi gṛhītvā sahasā yayau ।
tasyām eva niśi svarddhyā bhāsayantī samaṃtataḥ ।। jetavanam upetyāsau praviveśa jinālayaṃ । tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇamya caraṇau muneḥ ।। paṃcopahārapūjābhiḥ pūjayitvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।
natvā ca purataḥ tasthau saddharmaśravaṇotsukā ।। athāsau bhagavāṃs tasyā jñātvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। catvāri cāryyasatyāni niḥkleśapuṇyalabdhaye ।
daśakuśalamūlāni samyaksatvaviśuddhaye ।। āryyāṣṭāṅgikamārgāṃś ca saṃbodhimārgalabdhaye । bodhipākṣikadharmāṃś ca saṃbuddhaguṇalabdhaye ।। athāsau devakanyā tāṃ saddharmadeśaṇaṃ muneḥ ।
śrutvānumoditā cāpi prāpya dharmaviśeṣatāṃ ।। jñānavajreṇa satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ vibheda sā । śrotāpattiphalaṃ prāptā dṛṣṭasatyābhavat tadā ।। tato bhūyaḥ praṇamyaivaṃ bhagavantaṃ kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।
suprasannamukhāmbhojo trir udānam udāharat ।। bhagavann idam asmākaṃ mahāpuṇyasukhodayaṃ । jananyāpi kṛtaṃ nāpi na pitrā na ca vaṃdhubhiḥ ।। na jñātibhir na mitraiś ca na sahāyasuhṛjjanaiḥ ।
nāpi sālohitaiś cāpi pitṛlokair na cāparaiḥ ।। na rājñā na cāmātyair na maṃtribhir na ca paurikaiḥ । na gurubhir na vipraiś ca na yatibhir na tāpasaiḥ ।। na devair nāpi daityaiś ca nāpi lokādhipair api ।
tathānyaiś ca kṛtaṃ naiva yad idaṃ bhavatā kṛtaṃ ।। uchoṣito yad asmākaṃ rudhirāśrusaritpatiḥ । asthimayo mahāchailo yad asmābhiś ca laṃghitaḥ ।। tavānubhāvāt pihitaḥ sughoro hy apāyamārgo bahudoṣayuktaḥ ।
apāvṛtā svargagatiḥ supuṇyā nirvāṇamārgaś ca mayopalabdhaḥ ।। bhavatprasādān nirupetadoṣaṃ mayādya labdhaṃ suviśuddhacakṣuḥ । prāptaṃ ca śāntaṃ padam āryyakāntaṃ tīrṇaś ca duḥkhārṇavapāram asmi ।। naravarendrasurāsurapūjite vigatajanmajarāmaraṇādayaḥ ।
bhavasahasrasudullabhadarśane saphalam adya mune tava darśanaṃ ।। tataḥ praṇatvā caraṇāraviṃdau muneḥ prakṛtvā tṛpradakṣiṇāṃ ca । prajātaharṣā sugataṃ jineṃdraṃ smṛtvā ca bhūyo divam āyayau sā ।। tathā svargasamāyātā devakanyā mumoda sā ।
yathā vaṇig labdhalābho rogamukto yathāturaḥ ।। samyagniṣpannaśasyāpto yathā ca kṛṣikārmikaḥ । siddhayātrāpralabdhārthaḥ sārthavāho vaṇig yathā ।। atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvaivam avabhāsitaṃ ।
saṃdigdhavismitāś caivaṃ paprachus taṃ munīśvarāṃ ।। bhagavann adya rātrau ko bhavato antikam āgataḥ । brahmā vā surarājo vā lokapālagaṇā api ।। asmābhir jñāyate nāyaṃ yo adya rātrāv ihāgataḥ । tad asmān vismitān sarvān bodhayituṃ samarhasi ।।
iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭo bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tāṃś ca bhikṣugaṇān sarvān samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā ।। na hi sa bhikṣavo brahmā nāpi vāsau surādhipaḥ । naiva lokādhipālāś ca yādya rātrāv ihāgatā ।।
api tu dārikā dṛṣṭā yuṣmābhiḥ sagatā pathi । yayāhaṃ sālapuṣpaiś ca prāvakīryyābhitoṣitaḥ ।। sā māṃ puṣpair avākīryya gṛhasyārthe punar vanaṃ । gatā puṣpāṇy upāhartuṃ vṛkṣārūḍhāpatat taroḥ ।।
tato asau patanodvignā vedanākrāṃtacetasā । triratnāni smaranty eva dehaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau ।। tatra svarge samāsādya smṛtva māṃ sugataṃ punaḥ । draṣṭuṃ dharmaṃ ca me śrotum ihāsau samupāgatā ।।
tan mayā deśitaṃ tasyai saṃbodhidharmam uttamaṃ । śrutvā sā cānumodyaivaṃ saṃharṣitā divaṃ yayau ।। ity evaṃ bhikṣavo matvā triratnāni śubhārthibhiḥ । sevitavyāni saṃsmṛtvā gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ sadā ।।
ye bhajanti triratnāni saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । durgatiṃ te na gachaṃti vrajanti sadgatiṃ sadā ।। ye nindanti triratnāni pratikṣipya pramādataḥ । sadgatiṃ te na gachanti vasanti narake sadā ।।
tasmān nityāṃ triratnāni saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya bhāvayitvā ca bhajadhvaṃ bodhivāṃchayā ।। tathā vo maṅgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatra sarvadā bhavet । kramād bodhicarīṃ pūrya saṃbodhim api lapsyatha ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te bhikṣavo mudā । tathety abhyanumodantas triratnāni sadābhajan ।। ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭaṃ mayaivaṃ te pracakṣyate । śrutvaitac chrāvayitvā ca triratnāni sadā bhaja ।।
tatas tvaṃ kramaśaś caiva bodhicaryāṃ samācaran । sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sukhāvatīṃ samāvrajeḥ ।। ity etad guruṇādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena bhikṣuṇā । śrutvā rājā tathety evam abhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। tat saṃbuddhānubhāvaṃ munivarakathitaṃ śālapuṣpāvadānaṃ ।
ye śrutvā śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā bodhikāmāḥ । te sarvakleśamuktāḥ sakalaguṇadharā bodhicaryyānuraktāḥ । kṛtvā loke hitārthaṃ jinavaravasatiṃ saṃprayaṃti praharṣaiḥ ।। punar evaṃ yatīśo asāv upagupto jināṃśajaḥ ।
triratnasmṛtijaṃ puṇyaṃ khyātuṃ nṛpam abravīt ।। mahatpuṇyānubhāvatvaṃ triratnasmṛtisaṃbhavaṃ । tad ahaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ ।। dharmatā khalu devānāṃ svargacyavanadharmmiṇāṃ ।
paṃcapūrvanimittāni prādurbhaveyur ātmani ।। akliṣṭāni hi vāsāṃsi kliśyeyuś cyavanāntike । amlānāni ca mālyāni mlāyeran sahasā khalu ।। daurgandhaṃ niḥsared dehāt kakṣābhyāṃ sveda udbhavet ।
pracyutisamaye prāpte svāsane na dhṛtiṃ labhet ।। etatpaṃcanimittāni svargāc cyavanadharmiṇāṃ । sarveṣāṃ prodbhaveyuś ca pracyutisamayāgame ।। puraikadevaputrasya tathā cyavanadharmiṇaḥ ।
etatpaṃcanimittāni prādur āsaṃś cyuteḥ puraḥ ।। atha cyavanadharmāsau devaputro viṣāditaḥ । avaśyaṃ cyavanaṃ svargān matvā rautsīd adhīritaḥ ।। āvartya svavimānasthaḥ parivarttya vimūrchitaḥ ।
punaś caitanyam āsādya vilapaṃ paryyadevataḥ ।। hā mandākini hemāvjavyāpte puṇyāmbuvāhini । tvayi snātvapy ahaṃ cyutvā yāsyāmi durgatiṃ kathaṃ ।। hā caitraratham utsṛjya kva krīḍeyaṃ yathechayā ।
hā nandanavanaṃ ramyaṃ tyaktvāhaṃ kva rameya ca ।। hā miśrikāvanaṃ divyaṃ tyaktvā ramye kuhādhunā । hā pāruṣyavanaṃ tyaktvā kva ramyāmy apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। kva sukhaṃ lapsyate pāṇḍukaṃvalakaśilāṃ vinā । hā devasamitiṃ tyaktvā kva śroṣyāmi subhāṣitāṃ ।।
hā hā sudarśanaṃ ramyaṃ puraṃ tyaktvā vraje cyutaḥ । prāsādaṃ vaijayaṃtañ ca kadā drakṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ ।। hā śakrapramukhair devaiḥ sārddhaṃ kṛdāpramoditaḥ । adhunā me kva tat saukhyaṃ śrotuṃ cāpi na lapsyate ।।
hā devyam amṛtaṃ tyaktvā kiṃ prabhokṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ । divyakāmasukhaṃ bhuktvā punar durgatim āśrayan ।। kiyad duḥkhaṃ ca saṃbhoktuṃ yāsyāmi narakeṣv ahaṃ । etad divyamahotsāhād bhraṣṭo ahaṃ narake gataḥ ।।
mahadduḥkhābhisaṃtaptaḥ sahiṣyāmi kathaṃ tadā । hā hato asmi svapāpena kiṃ pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ mayā ।। yenetaḥ svargataś cyutvā punar yāsyāmi nārakān kiṃ । upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi na yāyāṃ yena durgatiṃ ।।
ko me śāstātra vidyeta yo māṃ dharme niyojayet । dharmeṇa rakṣyate prāṇī narake saṃsthito api ca ।। dharmaṃ vinātra devo api svargāt prabhransyate punaḥ । kiṃ karomi kva yāsyāmi nātropāyaṃ tu manyate ।।
sarvathāham itaś cyutvā gacheyaṃ durgatiṃ khalu । itaś cyutasya me janma labdhavyaṃ bhuvane kuha ।। iti dhairyaṃ samādhāya manasaivaṃ vyalokayat । cyutvetaḥ saukaraṃ janma prāptavyaṃ saptame dine ।।
evaṃ svāptagatiṃ dṛṣṭvā papāta savimūrchitaḥ । athādrākṣīn mahendras taṃ patitaṃ bhuvi mūrchitaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvā ca sahasopetya sudhāsekair asiṃcayat । tato asau cetanāṃ labdhvā śanair utthāya taṃ prabhuṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā pādau pariṣvajya natvaivaṃ prārthayad rudan । hā hā nātha mahendro asi sarvalokādhipaḥ prabhuḥ ।। mām adhaḥ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nopekṣāṃ kartum arhasi । bhavān hi jagatāṃ rājā svāmī bharttā patiḥ prabhuḥ ।। nātho dharmānuśāstā ca tan māṃ rakṣatum arhasi ।
tvadṛte anyo na me kaścid rakṣako vidyate atra hi ।। tad anukaṃpayā dṛṣṭyā dhṛtvā mām uddhara prabho । yadi māṃ rakṣituṃ nātha na śaknoti bhavān api ।। ko māṃ samuddhared anyo hā hato narake vraje ।
maṃḍākinyāṃ tvayā sārddhaṃ snātvā pūtātmako apy ahaṃ ।। kathaṃ ca narake gatvā vaseyam aśuciṃ caran । sahāpsarogaṇair nityaṃ caritvā naṃdane vane ।। divyasaṃgītivādyaiś ca ramāmi saṃpramoditaḥ ।
adyetaḥ patito pṛthvyāṃ rājagṛhopajāṃgale ।। saukaraṃ janma lapsyāmi saptame divase khalu । tatra mūtrapuriṣādīn amedhyān api kṛcchrataḥ ।। labdhvā bhuktvā cariṣyāmi vyādhasaṃghair upadrutaḥ ।
bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi bhūtvaivaṃ sūkarātmajaḥ ।। amedhyakardame nityaṃ vatsyāmy āvartya saṃcaran । evaṃ divyāmṛtaṃ bhuktvā ramitvā bhavatā saha ।। kathaṃ hi nārake gatvā bhokṣye amedhyāni saṃcaraḥ ।
imaṃ kalpataruṃ tyaktvā yathepsitaphalapradaṃ ।। jāṃgalaṃ vṛkṣam āśritya sthito bhokṣyāmi kiṃ tadā । sarvathāhaṃ cyuto asmītaḥ prerito hi svakarmaṇā ।। vividhāni ca duḥkhāni bhoktuṃ yāsyāmi nārake ।
tad upāyaṃ pradātavyaṃ bhavatā me anukaṃpinā ।। yenāśu durgater muktaḥ prāgacheyaṃ ca svargatiṃ । sarvathā rakṣa māṃ nātha yady asti te kṛpā mayi ।। bhavān māṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nopekṣāṃ kartum arhati ।
bhavān eva jagacchāstā sarvalokādhipaḥ prabhuḥ ।। tad āśu māṃ prayatnena samuddhartuṃ samarhati । idaṃ te darśanaṃ nātha paścimaṃ me bhavet khalu ।। janmaśatasahasraiś ca durlabhaṃ syād dhi saṃgamaṃ ।
ity evaṃ vilapaṃ devaputras sa taṃ surādhipaṃ ।। natvā pādau nirīkṣyaiva tasthāv aśrugalanmukhaḥ । atha śakraḥ surendro asau dṛṣṭvaivaṃ pravilāpitaṃ ।। kāruṇyā krāntacittas tam āśvāsayann abhāṣata ।
mā kṛthā rodanaṃ bhadra samāśvasi hi dhīraya ।। kriyante kiṃ prayatnāni sarvathā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ । mṛtyur mahāvaliṣṭho hi sarvasatvāntakārakaḥ ।। hrīyante mṛtyunā sarve mṛtyuḥ kena nihanyate ।
anirvāyo hi sarvatra sarvatraidhātukeṣv api ।। sarveṣām api jantūnām ekānte maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ । tasmān mā bhes tathā mṛtyoḥ kiṃ viṣādena sidhyate ।। tad dhairyyataiḥ samālaṃvya triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।
gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ smara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। tatas tvaṃ durgatiṃ muktvā sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ । etad eva hi saṃsāre mahopāyaṃ śubhāptaye ।। nānyad dhi vidyate kiṃcin mṛtyau sādhāraṇe dhruve ।
tad anyaccetanāṃ hitvā triratnāny abhisaṃsmaran ।। namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vadan bhaja । ye triratnasmṛtiṃ dhṛtvā mṛtās te puṇyabhāginaḥ ।। kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya yāyuś cānte sukhavatīṃ ।
tvaṃ cāpi triratnānaṃ smṛtvā mṛtaḥ supuṇyadhṛk ।। kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya saṃprayāyāḥ sukhāvatīṃ । itīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā devasuto atha saḥ ।। tathety anusaṃmodya punar natvaivam abravīt ।
adyārabhya mahendrāhaṃ triratnānaṃ sadā smaran ।। gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ upāsako bhave khalu । ity uktvā sa mahendrasya puraḥ sthitvā kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। anusmṛtya triratnānāṃ namaskṛtim udāharat ।
namo buddhāya bhadrāya namo dharmāya tāyine ।। namaḥ saṃghāya nāthāya sarvadāpi name bhaje । adyārabhya triratnānāṃ sadāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। upāsako bhaven nityaṃ namāmi satataṃ smaret ।
ity uktvā devaputro asau kāladharmayutaś cyutaḥ ।। tuṣite devaloke abhūd upapannaḥ supuṇyataḥ । dharmatā khalu devānāṃ ye devāḥ svargataś cyutāḥ ।। te adholokeṣu gacheyur na tūrddhvabhuvaneṣu hi ।
atha śakro narendro asau dṛṣṭvā taṃ svargataś cyutaṃ ।। kutrāsau labhate janma ity adhastād vyalokayat । kim asau sūkarīgarbha utpanno vā na veti ca ।। apaśyat sarvataś cainaṃ na dadarśa kuhāpi sa ।
tato asau vismitaḥ śakro divyena cakṣuṣā punaḥ ।। kutrāsau labhate janma ity evaṃ samalokayat । vata tiryyakṣu jāto asau preteṣu ca prajāyate ।। atha narakeṣu vā jāta ity evaṃ samalokayat ।
teṣu triṣv apy apāyeṣu nādrākṣīt taṃ samaṃtataḥ ।। tato manuṣyalokeṣu jāto veti dadarśa ca । tatrāpi ca sa sarvatra nādrākṣīt taṃ sureśvaraḥ ।। tataś caturmahārājabhuvaneṣu prajāyate ।
iti teṣu ca sarvatra vilokayan dadarśa na ।। tataś ca vismitaḥ śakras trayastriṃśe vyalokayan । tatrāpi taṃ na cādrākṣīt kutrāpi ca samaṃtataḥ । evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu vilokayaṃs tadudbhavaṃ ।
adṛṣṭvā vismitaḥ śakraḥ punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat । aho vata mahāścaryyaṃ yan mayāpi na dṛśyate ।। kutrāsau jāyate nūnaṃ na manye tat pravṛttitāṃ । ko nu jñāsyati tadvṛttiṃ buddhād anyo na kaścana ।।
buddha eva jagaddarśī ṣaḍabhijñas trikālavit । tasmād aham ito gatvā saṃbuddhe samupācaran ।। vijñapyaivaṃ ca tadvṛttiṃ praṣṭum arhāmi sāṃprātaṃ । ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā devendro asau savismayaḥ ।।
sahasā jetakāraṇye jināśramam avātarat । tatrāsau sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā saharṣavismayānvitaḥ ।। praṇamya purataḥ sthitvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo avadat । bhagavaṃs tad vijānīyā yad ihāham upāgataḥ ।।
tathāpi praṣṭum ichāmi tat samādeṣṭum arhasi । ekaḥ kālagato devaputraḥ svargāc cyuto gataḥ ।। ṣaṭsu lokeṣu sarvatra dṛśyate na mayā hy asau । kutrāsau jāyate śāstar mayā na dṛśyate kvacit ।।
tasyotpattiḥ kuha sthāne tat samādeṣṭum arhasi । itīndravacanaiḥ śrutvā sa saṃbuddho munīśvaraḥ ।। tasya puṇyātmanaḥ sthānaṃ iṃdrāya samacakṣatac । kauśika tuṣito nāma lokadhātuḥ prasiddhitaḥ ।।
tatrāsau modate devo gatvā triśaraṇaṃ cyutaḥ । ityādiṣṭaṃa munīndreṇa śrutvā sa tridaśādhipaḥ ।। vismitaḥ suprasannātmā praṇatvaivaṃm udānayat । aho buddham aho dharmam aho saṃghaṃ śubhaṃkaraṃ ।।
yat saṃśaraṇamātre api satvā yānti śubhālayaṃ । ye buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ ।। prahāya pātakān sarvān divyalokam upāsate । ye dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ ।
prahāya mānuṣān kāyān divyān kāyān upāsate ।। ye saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ । prahāya sarvaduḥkhāni divyasaukhyāny upāsate ।। dhanyās te puruṣā bhadrāḥ saṃbodhipadagāminaḥ ।
ye saṃsmṛtvā triratnāni vrajanti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। athāsau bhagavāñ chrutvā śakreṇaivaṃ subhāṣitaṃ । tathānuvarṇayan prāha kauśikaṃ taṃ surādhipaṃ ।। evam etad dhi devendra yathaivaṃ tvaṃ prabhāṣase । dhanyās te puruṣā bhadrā triratnaṃ bhajaṃti ye ।।
ye buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ । kleśavairīṃ vinirjitya saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।। ye dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ । māradharmavinirmuktā bodhidharmān avāpnuyuḥ ।
ye saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāṃti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ । pātakebhyo vinirmuktāḥ saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। na bhajanti munīndraṃ ye te bhramaṃti bhavārṇave । saṃbodhimārgato bhraṣṭā naṣṭā gachanti durgatiṃ ।।
ye śṛṇvaṃti na saddharmaṃ te kleśaparidāhitāḥ । māradharmaratā duṣṭāḥ praṇaṣṭā yāṃti durgatiṃ । na mānayaṃti ye saṃghaṃ na te jānaṃti sadgatiṃ । sadā duḥkhābhisaṃtaptā bhraṣṭā gachaṃti durgatiṃ । nindanti ye triratnāni te duṣṭā mārapākṣikāḥ । naiva caraṃti sanmārge vinaṣṭā yaṃti durgatiṃ । tasmād ye mānavāḥ santo vāṃchanti sadgatiṃ sadā ।
taiḥ saṃsmṛtvā triratnānāṃ karttavyaṃ śaraṇaṃ mudā ।। ye smaranti triratnānāṃ na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ । prahāya pātakān sarvāñ śīghraṃ yānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। sukhāvatyāṃ jinendrasya dharmaṃ śrutvānumoditāḥ ।
bodhicittaṃ samāsādya caranti bodhicārikāṃ ।। tatas tāḥ kramataḥ pūryya saṃvṛttipāram āgatāḥ । paramārthacarīṃ prāpya nirvṛttiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।। idaṃ hi bodhimārgānāṃ vījaṃ vijñāya kauśika ।
triratnasmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ karttavyaṃ bodhivāṃchibhiḥ ।। kadāpi naiva moktavyaṃ triratnasmaraṇaṃ sadā । gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ triratnānāṃ samācara ।। evaṃ tena munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ sa kauśikaḥ ।
śrutvaivam ity anujñāya prābhyanandat prasāditaḥ ।। tato asau bhagavantaṃ taṃ natvā sa racitāṃjaliḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya punar natvā divaṃ yayau ।। tato devapure gatvā sudharmamaṃdire sthitaḥ ।
devalokān samāmaṃtrya tat pravṛttaṃ samabravīt ।। bho bho devagaṇāḥ sarve śṛṇudhvaṃ tat samāhitaḥ । yad adbhutaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ saṃbodhihetum ucyate ।। dharmatā khalu devānāṃ ye ye devā hi nākataḥ ।
cyutās te te prayānty adho na tūrddhvaṃ yānti ke cana ।। idānīṃ tu vrajeyus te ye devāḥ svargataś cyutāḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvorddhvagatiṃ na tv adhogatiṃ ।। dṛśyatām amuko devaputras triśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
svargāc cyutvā samutpannas tuṣite asau pramodate ।। yūyam api ca tad dṛṣṭvā triratnānāṃ samāhitāḥ । gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ nityaṃ smṛtvā bhajadhvam ādarāt ।। tato yūyaṃ na yāyāta durgatiṣu kadā cana ।
sadā divyasukhaṃ bhuktvā prayāsyatha sukhāvatīṃ ।। ye buddhe śaraṇaṃ yāṃti na te gachanti durgatiṃ । kleśavairān vinirjitya saṃbodhipadam āpnuyuḥ ।। ye dharme śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ ।
māradharmavinirmuktā buddhadharmāṇy avāpnuiyuḥ ।। ye saṃghe śaraṇaṃ gatvā na te gachanti durgatiṃ । sarvapātakanirmuktā prayāsyaṃti sukhāvatīṃ ।। na bhajanti triratnaṃ ye te bhramanti bhavārṇave ।
saddharmanindakā bhraṣṭā naṣṭā gachanti durgatiṃ ।। durgatiṣu bhramaṃtas te duḥkhāni vividhāni ca । bhuktvā caranti duṣṭāṃśā naiva gachaṃti sadgatiṃ ।। tad duḥkhaṃ hātum ichaṃti sukhaṃ prāptuṃ ca ye sadā ।
te triratnaṃ sadā smṛtvā bhajaṃtāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। tato vo maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ naiva yāyāta durgatiṃ । sadgatim eva yāyāta saṃbodhim api lapsyatha ।। iti tena surendreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ hitārthinā ।
śrutvā sarve api te devās tathety uktvā nanandire ।। tadā sarve api devāś ca triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । sarvadānusmarantaś ca satkṛtyaivaṃ prabhejire ।। evaṃ devās tadā ye ye triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । te te svargād api cyutvā naivāgachann adhogatiṃ ।।
tata ūrddhvaṃ samudgamya prāgachaṃs tuṣitālaye । triratnaśaraṇaṃ yātā maitreyaṃ samupāśrayan ।। tathā śakraś ca tān sarvān maitreyasamupāśritān । dṛṣṭvānumodanāṃ kurvan prābhyanandat suraiḥ saha ।।
iti me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā te vakṣyate mayā । evaṃ matvā mahārāja triratnaśaraṇaṃ vraja ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhicarīḥ prāpya saṃbodhipadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । triratnaśaraṇe sthāpya tvayā dharmapravṛddhaye ।। ity evam upaguptena samādiṣṭaṃ subhāṣitaṃ । śrutvā rājā tathety evaṃ prānvamodat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
ye puṇyaprāptukāmās tad idam avirataṃ sūkarīkāvadānaṃ । śṛṇvanti śravayanti pramuditamanasā durgatiṃ te na yānti । nirjitya kleśasaṃghāṃs triguṇahitakarā bodhicaryyānuraktā । maitreyaṃ bodhisatvaṃ tuṣitabhuvanāgāḥ saṃbhajanti prakāmaṃ ।।
athaśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । sarvasatvahitārthāya tat samādeṣṭum arhasi ।।
iti saṃprārthite tena rājñāśokena bhūbhujā । upagupto yatiś cāsau dṛṣṭvā taṃ nṛpam abravīt ।। sādhu rājan samādhāya śrūyatāṃ puṇyavṛddhaye । yathā me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā te vakṣyate mayā ।।
purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ śrīghanaḥ śakyakeśarī । sarvavidyāguṇācāryyas traidhātukavināyakaḥ ।। sugato arhan mahābhijño dharmarājas tathāgataḥ । jinaḥ samantabhadrāṃśaś caturbrahmavihārakaḥ ।।
sa ekasamaye tatra kapilākhye purottame । nyagrodhāramake ramye vyaharac chrāvakaiḥ saha ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra dharmmaṃ śrotuṃ samāgatāḥ । devāsuramahārājā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।।
garuḍā nāgarājāś ca siddhavidyādharā grahāḥ । yogino yatayaś cāpi munayo brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāmātyāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ । śreṣṭhinaḥ sārthavāhāś ca paurā jānapadā api ।।
evam anye api satvāś ca ye saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ । te sarve samupāgatya vaṃditvā taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। pūjayitvā puraskṛtya parivṛtya samantataḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo dharmaṃ śrotuṃ samupatasthire ।।
athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān dharmakāṃkṣiṇaḥ । ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। taṃ ca dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajanta upatasthire ।। bhagavāṃś ca tathā nityaṃ sarvasatvahitārthataḥ ।
saddharmadeśanāṃ kṛtvā vyaharat sāṃghikaiḥ saha ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra pure kapilavastuni । āsīc chākyo mahāsādhur mahābhogo mahādhanaḥ ।। tena kalatram ānītaṃ svakulasadṛśāt kulāt ।
tayā sa kāntayā sārddhaṃ rarāma paricārayan ।। tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya sā bhāryāsīt sugarbhiṇī । tato asau samaye asūta dārakaṃ divyasuṃdaraṃ ।। martyātikrāntavarṇābhaṃ divyakalpasuvarṇitaṃ ।
sūkṣmachaviṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ gauravarṇaṃ manoharaṃ ।। maheśākhyaṃ manāpaṃ ca darśanīyaṃ prasādikaṃ । abhirūpaṃ supuṣṭāṃgaṃ sarvalakṣaṇamaṇḍitaṃ ।। tatrāsau janako dṛṣṭvā dārakaṃ taṃ subhadrikaṃ ।
moditaḥ sahasā jñātiṃ samāhūyābravīt tathā ।। bhavantaḥ paśyatāṃ putro mamāyaṃ divyasuṃdaraḥ । asya jātimahaṃ kṛtvā nāmadheyaṃ pracakṣyatāṃ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā jñātayas te sasaṃmatāḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ vālakaṃ divyaṃ kalyavarṇaṃ susuṃdaraṃ ।। saṃmīlya saṃmataṃ kṛtvā dṛṣṭvā tasyāṅgalakṣaṇaṃ । kṛtvā jātimahaṃ nāma sthāpituṃ saṃvabhāṣire । yad ayaṃ dārako divyavapuḥ kalyātisuṃdaraḥ ।
tasmād bhavatu nāmnāyaṃ vapusmān iti viśrutaḥ । iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te jñātivargikāḥ ।। purastāt tasya śākyasya gatvā caivaṃ vabhāṣire । yad ayaṃ bhavataḥ putro divyavapur guṇānvitaḥ ।।
tasmād bhavatu nāmnāyaṃ vapuṣmān iti viśrutaḥ । tatheti samabhikhyāya pitrā sa suta ātmajaḥ ।। aṣṭābhya upamātṛbhya upanyasto abhipālane । tato asau dārakas tābhir dhātrībhir upacāraṇaiḥ ।।
pālito varddhitaḥ puṣṭa āsīt padmaṃ yathā hrade । kramāt pravarddhitaś cāsau kumāro abhūd yadā tataḥ ।। tadā suhṛtsahāyaiś ca sārddhaṃ krīḍitum ācarat । yatra yatra vapuṣmān sa cakrāma bhuvi saṃcaraṃ ।।
tatra tatrābhavan medhyā bhūpradeśāḥ samaṃtataḥ । evaṃvidhamahāpuṇyamaheśākhyaḥ śivāśayaḥ ।। kāruṇiko mahāśrāddhaḥ svaparātmahitārthabhṛt । dharmakāmaḥ subhadrātmā pūjyo mānyo jitendriyaḥ ।।
abhivādyaḥ kumāro api vapuṣmān sa vyarājata । tataḥ karmavipākena preryyamānaḥ kumārakaḥ ।। sa vapuṣmān suhṛtsaṃghaiḥ sārddhaṃ puro viniryayau । tato asau jetakāraṇyaṃ dūrād dṛṣṭvā pramoditaḥ ।।
ramituṃ tatra mahodyāne sahasā samupācarat । tataḥ samupaviṣṭo asau dṛṣṭvodyānaṃ pramoditaḥ ।। śāntarūpān yatīn paśyan vihāre harṣito aviśat । tatrāsau bhagavantaṃ taṃ dadarśa samitisthitaṃ ।।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyañjanaparimaṇḍitaṃ । vyāmābhālaṃkṛtaṃ kāmyaṃ śatasūryyādhikaprabhaṃ ।। samaṃtabhadrarūpaṃ ca ratnāṃgam iva jaṃgamaṃ । dṛṣṭvāsau suprasannātmā samupetya purogataḥ ।।
pādau tasya muner natvā dharmaṃ śrotum upāviśat । athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasya cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ ।। aryyasatyāni mārgaṃ ca dideśa bodhisādhanaṃ । tac chrutvā sugatoditaṃ vapuṣmān sa praharṣitaḥ ।।
bhavābhisaraṇodvignaḥ saddharmaguṇam aichata । bhitvā sa jñānavajreṇa satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ ।। śrotāpattiphalaṃ labdhvā dṛṣṭasatyo abhavat sudhīḥ । saṃsāraṃ cāsthiraṃ matvā bhavabhogyasunispṛhaḥ ।।
pravrajyāṃ caritum aichat svākhyāte sugatāśrame । tato asau purato gatvā munīndrasya kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। pādau natvā prasannāsyaḥ pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। namas te bhagavañ chāstaḥ śaraṇaṃ bhavatāṃ vraje । tat pravrajyāvrataṃ dehi cariṣye brahmacārikāṃ ।।
iti tenārthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavāṃs taṃ kumārakaṃ । pravrajyācaraṇāraktaṃ matvā caivaṃ samabravīt ।। kumāra yadi te vāṃchā pravrajyācaraṇe asti hi । pitror ādeśam āsādya prāgacha dāsyate tadā ।।
iti śrutvā munīndrasya nirdeśaṃ tat tatheti saḥ । naṃditaś caraṇau natvā svagṛhaṃ sahasāgataḥ ।। tato gṛhe samāsādya pitroś ca purataḥ sthitaḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā vṛttāṃtaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
adyāmba tāta saṃbuddho dṛśyate apūrvadarśanaḥ । sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇo divyātikāntasuṃdaraḥ ।। saṃsthitaḥ parṣadāṃ madhye bhāṣati dharmam uttamaṃ । apūrvaṃ śrūyate tasya subhāṣitavaco'mṛtaṃ ।।
tatsubhāṣitasudhāṃ pītvā cittaṃ me tṛpyate na hi । bhūyas tad amṛtaṃ pātuṃ vratam ichāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। anye api bahavo dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavo brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। śāntaśīlāḥ śubhātmāno dayākāruṇyamānasāḥ ।
tat sabhāgavrataṃ cartum ichāmi khalu sāṃprataṃ ।। tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me kṛpāsti yadi vāṃ mayi । evaṃ tasya svaputrasya vacanaṃ vajrasannibhaṃ ।। tau mātāpitarau śrutvā mūrchitau petatur bhuvi ।
tataḥ putraprayatnena cetanāṃ prāpya tau punaḥ ।। pariṣvajya svakaṃ putraṃ tam evaṃ paryyadevatāṃ । hā putra katham ajño asi hātmaja vallabho asi naḥ ।। hā suta vaṃcyase kena hā tāta kiṃ nu vāṃchasi ।
hā jīva katham ekānte tyaktvāsmān kva nu yāsyase ।। nandanaḥ supriyāś cāsi kena duḥkhena yāsyase । kiṃcid duḥkhaṃ na te dattaṃ asmābhir vā kadā cana ।। kutaḥ kiṃ jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad vadasva yadīhasi ।
ity evaṃ paridevitvā pitāsau cetasātmajaṃ ।। nivārayan pravaṃdhena bodhayituṃ samabravīt । tvaṃ kumāra vayastho asi sukomalaḥ sukhaidhitaḥ ।। śītatāpāsahiṣṇuś ca yathechābhogyasaṃrataḥ ।
kiṃcid duḥkhānabhijñas tvaṃ tat kathaṃ pravrajeḥ suta ।। pravrajito gṛhaṃ tyaktvā bahirdeśe vases sadā । cīvaraprāvṛtaḥ piṇḍaṃ yācitvā svayam āhareḥ ।। anekajantusaṃcāre vane araṇye kathaṃ vaseḥ ।
jaṃgale durgame naikacaurākīrṇe kathaṃ careḥ ।। ekākī ca kathaṃ tiṣṭher vṛkṣamūle ca nirjane । śmaśāne saṃsthitaḥ paśyan mṛtakānto traseḥ kathaṃ ।। śayithāś ca kathaṃ śūnye gṛhe bhūtanivāsite ।
evaṃ suduṣkarīṃ caryyāṃ carituṃ katham ichasi ।। tat pravrajyāvrate cittaṃ mā kṛthās tvaṃ nivarttaya । iti madvacanaṃ śrutvā gṛhe sthitvā sukhaṃ rama ।। nityaṃ pravrajatāṃ duḥkhaṃ kiṃ siddhaṃ duḥkhacaryyayā ।
dharme vaṃchāsti cet putra gṛhe sthitvā cara vrataṃ ।। śṛṇvaṃś ca dharmaśāstrāṇi śrāvayaṃś ca bahūñ janān । dānaṃ kṛtvā viśuddhātmā triratnaṃ satataṃ bhaja ।। yasya kiṃcid gṛhe nāsti jñātir vaṃdhuś ca kaścana ।
nāpi mitragatiś cāpi pravrajyā tasya yujyate । kiṃ tava setsyate putra pravrajyāṃ pākuniṣṭhayā । sarvathā tyaja tadvāṃchā gṛhe dharmaṃ sukhaṃ cara । iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā vapuṣmān sa viśaṃkitaḥ ।।
pitroḥ pādān punar natvā pratyuvāca prabodhayan । satyaṃ tāta gṛhe saukhyaṃ dharmāṇāṃ caram uttamaṃ ।। saṃpado api samṛddhās te kāmabhogyaṃ mahatsukhaṃ । gṛhe parigrahāḥ poṣyās tad arthaṃ dhanam arjayet ।।
arjane hi mahatkaṣṭaṃ rakṣaṇe api prayatnatā । aneke saṃpado apāyā rājāgnyudakataskarāḥ ।। kṣaṇād dhareyur ākṛṣya tad duḥkhaṃ sahituṃ kathaṃ । saṃpado ante vipattiḥ syāt kasya saṃpadviniścalā ।।
vipattau hīyate dhairyyam adhairyyāt kleśito bhavet । kleśito doṣam āpnoti tadā puṇye matiḥ kutaḥ ।। apuṇye kupitā lakṣmir naivāśraye gamiṣyati । lakṣmīvirahite gehe kuto dharmasya gocaraṃ ।।
saṃpattau tu labhen mānaṃ mānād dhi jāyate madaḥ । madād pramādito dharme tadā dharmo gṛhe kutaḥ ।। adharmāt kāmabhogyaṃ tu kevalaṃ pāpasādhanaṃ । kāmārthe kleśitā lokāḥ kāmārthe duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।।
kāmārthe pratihanyante tena kāme sukhaṃ kathaṃ । saṃty evaṃ tāta sarvatra bhayāni vividhāni hi ।। traidhātukabhavasthānāṃ kasya nāsti bhayaṃ kuha । daivāt sarvatra jāyante duḥkhāni ca sukhāni ca ।।
kleśacittasamutthāni duḥkhāni ca bhayāni ca । yatra yatrāpi saṃyāti kleśitātmā sukhechayā ।। tatra tatrāpi karmotthair duḥkhair bhayaiś ca hanyate । yatra yatrāpi saṃyāti dharmacitto hitechayā ।
tatra tatrāpi sarvatra nirbhayaś carate sukhaṃ । yal lokānāṃ bhayasthānaṃ tatraiva ramate yatiḥ । vivikte nirjane araṇye vṛkṣamūle guhāsu ca ।। śūnyagehe śmaśāne api sukhaṃ dhyātvā yatir vaset ।
svadharmai rakṣito yogī saṃyatātmā kuto bhayaḥ ।। kim eva vahuvādena nirvāṇārthimano mama । tan nirvātuṃ svadehe api nirapekṣaḥ parivraje ।। tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me pravrajyāvratasādhane ।
yadi na dīyate anujñā mariṣye ahaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। iti tasyātmajasyaivaṃ nirvandhavacanaṃ pitā । śrutvā viyogaduḥkhārttaḥ punas taṃ sutam abravīt ।। mā putra sahasā kārṣī maraṇābhilāṣitaṃ manaḥ । sarvathāpy anivarttī tvam avaśyaṃ ced gamiṣyasi ।।
yad ichasi vrataṃ kartuṃ saddharmārthimanas tava । pravraja śraddhayā putra svākhyāte buddhaśāsane ।। evaṃ bharttroditaṃ śrutvā tan mātā mūrchitāpatat । cirāt sā cetanāṃ prāptā rudantī cāvadat sutaṃ ।।
hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihāya kva yāsyasi । hā me jīvo asi kiṃ paśyaṃ pravrajituṃ samīhasi ।। kiṃcid duḥkhaṃ na te dattaṃ mayāmvāyā kadā cana । kena duḥkhena te cittaṃ pravrajituṃ samichati ।।
pravrajyā śobhate putra vṛddhatve vā daridrite । tvaṃ tu dahara ityaś ca tat pravrajyāṃ careḥ kathaṃ ।। yāvac ca jivitaṃ me asti tāvan mā gāḥ suta kvacit । yāvac cāsti gṛhe saṃpat tāvad bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa ।।
yadāhaṃ maraṇaṃ yātā yadā cāpattitā gṛhe । jñātimitraparityaktas tadā vrajasva vāṃchayā ।। ity ukte api tayoḥ pitror udator vighnaśaṃkitaḥ । pādāṃ natvā vapuṣmān sa sahasā niryayau gṛhāt ।।
tato veṇuvanaṃ gatvā praṇamya munim ādarāt । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo bhūtvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। pitṛprāptābhyanujño ahaṃ nātha sāṃpratam āgataḥ । tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ dehi paṃcaśikṣāpadāni ca ।।
upasampacchubhācāram anuśikṣāpadaṃ ca me । brahmacaryyaṃ cariṣyāmi saṃbodhau kṛtaniścayaḥ ।। adyāgreṇa mahābuddha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । sadharmasāṃghikānāṃ cṃ kāyavākcittabhaktitaḥ ।।
ity ukte bhagavān dṛṣṭvā pṛṣṭvā hastena tac chiraḥ । ehi bhikṣo kumāreti saṃvadaṃs taṃ samagrahīt ।। ehīti prokte sugatena muṇḍaḥ pātrī vapuṣmān sakaṣāyavāsāḥ । sadyapraśāntendriya eva tasthau svarṇṇaprabho buddhamanorathena ।। saccittalabdhaḥ sa muneḥ prasādāt prayujyamāno vyaharat samādhau ।
vyāyachamānaḥ khalu bodhimārge saṃbuddhadharme ghaṭamāna evaṃ ।। sarvaṃ ca saṃsāram anityatāhataṃ matvā ca traidhātugatiṃ vighātinīṃ । kleśāṃś ca sarvān pravihāya saṃyataḥ sākṣād varo arhaṃ sa babhūva sāṃghikaḥ ।। suvītarāgaḥ samaloṣṭahema ākāśacittaśubhagaṃdhivāsī ।
bhindann avidyāṃgam ivāṇḍakośaṃ prāptād abhijñāḥ pratisaṃvidaś ca ।। satkāralobheṣu parāṃmukhatvāt sa śakradevāsuramānuṣāṇāṃ । pūjyaś ca mānyo apy abhivandanīyo babhūva sa brahmavihāracārī ।। atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayānvitāḥ ।
bhagavantaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ paprachus tasya karmatāṃ ।। kenāyaṃ karmaṇā nātha vapuṣmān atisuṃdaraḥ । pravrajya sahasārhatvaṃ prāpto bhavati cātmavit ।। iti pṛṣṭe ca tair nātho bhagavāṃs tān samabravīt ।
bhikṣavaḥ śrūyatāṃ vakṣye tasya ca karma yat kṛtaṃ ।। etena yat kṛtaṃ karma tat kenānyena bhokṣyate । yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva tad dhi bhujyate ।। puraikanavate kalpe vipaśvī nāma sarvavit ।
samudapādi loke arhan dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। vidyācaraṇasaṃpannaḥ sugato bhadrakṛj jinaḥ । sarvajño anuttaro nāthaḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ ।। śāstā traidhātukasthānāṃ vināyako guṇākaraḥ ।
saddharmaratnadāta sa bhagavān puṇyabhāskaraḥ ।। purīṃ vaṃdhumato rājño rājadhānīm upāśrayan । sārddhaṃ bhikṣugaṇaiḥ śiṣyai bodhisatvagaṇair api ।। hitāya sarvasatvānāṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।
ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ bodhicaryyānusārikaṃ ।। tataḥ sa buddhakāryyāṇi kṛtvā sarvāṇy aśeṣataḥ । nirvāṇam āyayau śānto vahnir ivendhanakṣayāt ।। tato vandhumatā rājñā tat tanuḥ saṃskṛto agninā । taddhātūś ca samāropya stūpa uccair mahān kṛtaḥ ।।
tatra ratnamaye stūpe sadvidhāne pratiṣṭhite । nityasatkārapūjābhiḥ kāritaṃ ca mahotsavaṃ ।। saṃgītivādyanṛtyaiś ca mahānaṃdapracāribhiḥ । kārayitvā mahotsāhaṃ sthāpitaṃ sumahanmahaḥ ।।
ekasmin divase tatra pumān eko daridritaḥ । tanmahāṃte dine anyasmiṃ stāpāṃgaṇam upāviśat ।। tatra stūpāṅgaṇe cāsau praviṣṭaḥ samalokayat । mlānībhūtāni puṣpāṇi prakīrṇṇāni samaṃtataḥ ।।
tāni nirmālyapuṣpāṇi vikīrṇṇāni samaṃtataḥ । glānībhūtāny aśuddhāni dṛṣṭvā caivaṃ vyacintayat । ayaṃ caityo munīndrasya vipaścino guṇāṃbudheḥ ।। dhāturatnamayastūpaḥ sarvalokābhiḥ pūjitaḥ ।
etan nirmālyapuṣpais tu mlānitaiḥ pavaneritaiḥ ।। ākīrṇo malinībhūto hy aśuddheḥ syād aśobhitaḥ । tasmād etāni puṣpāṇi nirmālyāni samaṃtataḥ ।। apanīya viśuddhāya mārjayeyam iha drutaṃ ।।iti dhyātvā daridro asau nirmālyāny apanīya vai ।।
saṃmārja nyāsamamārkṣī stūpāṃgaṇaṃ samaṃtataḥ । tataḥ stūpāṃgaṇaṃ sarvaṃ virajaṃ pariśodhitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā prasannacitto asau natvaivaṃ praṇidhiṃ dadhe । yan mayātra jinastūpe nirmālyāny apanīya vai । saṃmṛjya śobhanaṃ kṛtvā kuśalaṃ samupārjitaṃ ।
anena kuśalenāhaṃ sadā durgatimocitaḥ ।। evaṃvidhaguṇajñānalābhi bhūyāsam ātmavit । evaṃvidhaṃ ca śāstāraṃ saṃbuddhaṃ jñānabhāskaraṃ ।। ārāgayaṃ samāśritya labheyaṃ saugatiṃ gatiṃ ।
praṇidhānaṃ tathā dhṛtvā nityam evam upāśrayan ।। tatstūpe śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaje ratnatrayaṃ sadā । bhikṣavaḥ kiṃ nu manyadhve yo puruṣaḥ daridrikaḥ ।। ayam eva vapuṣmān sa jñeyo hi nānyathā khalu ।
yat stūpāṃgaṇaṃ tena saṃbuddhaguṇabhāvinā ।। samantataḥ susaṃmṛjya pariśuddhīkṛtaṃ tadā । tena puṇyavipākena jāta āḍhyakule adhunā ।। divyābhisundaraḥ kāntaḥ sa vapuṣmān bhavaty ayaṃ ।
yat praṇidhiḥ kṛtaḥ stūpe natvā tena sucetasā ।। tena me śāsane apy adya pravrajyārhan bhavaty ayaṃ । ārāgitas tathārhañ ca saṃbuddhaḥ sugato jinaḥ ।। anena bhikṣuṇā bodhiprāptena brahmacāriṇā ।
ity evaṃ karma jānīta sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ bhave ।। yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva tat phalaṃ gataṃ । na naśyanti hi karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api ।। sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalaṃti khalu dehināṃ ।
abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kathaṃ cana ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karma vāyubhiś ca na śuṣyate । jalaiś ca klidyate nāpi kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu ।। anyathāpi bhaven naiva karmaṇāṃ gatir ābhavaṃ ।
śuklānāṃ śubhataiva syāt kṛṣṇānāṃ durgatis sadā ।। miśritā miśritānaṃ tu bhujyaṃte sarvajantubhiḥ । tasmād apāsya kṛṣṇāni karmāṇi miśritāni ca ।। caraṇīyāṃ śubheṣv eva karmasu sukhavāṃchibhiḥ ।
tatheti bhikṣavaḥ sarve te ca lokāḥ sabhāśritāḥ ।। buddhavāco amṛtaṃ pītvā nananduḥ śubhakāminaḥ । evam etan mahārāja śrutaṃ me gurubhāṣitaṃ ।। evaṃ śrutvā tvayāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ puṇyam eva hi ।
puṇyam eva bhavet trātā suhṛn mitraṃ hitaṃkaraḥ ।। nānyaḥ kaścid ihāmutra vidyate bhavacāriṇāṃ । tasmāt puṇyaṃ svayaṃ śrutvā karttavyam ādarāt sadā ।। prajāś ca śrāvayitvaivaṃ puṇye saṃsthāpaya sadā ।
ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena bhikṣuṇā ।। śrutvā rājā janaiḥ sārddhaṃ tatheti prābhyanaṃdata । śṛṇvanti ye śrāvayantīha yaś ca vapuṣmato adaḥ prathitāvadānaṃ । te kleśanirmuktaviśuddhacittāḥ prayānti nūnaṃ sugatālayeṣu ।।
athāśoko mahīpālaḥ saṃbuddhaguṇalālasaḥ । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā prāṃjaliś caivam abravīt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā me khyātum arhasi ।।
iti tena narendreṇa pṛṣṭe asau ca jināṃśajaḥ । upagupto yatir bhūyas taṃ nṛpeśam abhāṣata ।। śṛṇu rājaṃs tathā vakṣye yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । śrutvā ca bhavatāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ dharmasādhanaṃ ।।
puraikasamaye cāsau śākyasiṃhos dayākaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugato nāthaḥ śāstā traidhātukādhipaḥ ।। sarvavidyādhipo buddhaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ । mārajiṣṇur vinetārhaṃ dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।।
sarvasatvahitārthāya śrāvastyāṃ vahir āśrame । jetavane vihārasthe vyaharac chrāvakaiḥ saha ।। bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi sūpāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ । devāsuragaṇaiś cāpi caturvarṇṇādimānavaiḥ ।।
caturbhiś ca mahārājaiḥ sasainyaparivārakaiḥ । sarvasatvaiś ca pauraiś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ ।। satkṛtya pūjayitvā ca parivṛtya puraskṛtaḥ । sa bhagavān sabhāmadhye siṃhāsane sthito vabhau ।।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sabhāṃ samupasthitāṃ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। te tad dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ । bhagavantaṃ punar natvā svasvasthānaṃ pratīyire ।।
tato asau bhagavān rātrau dhyānāgāre samāviśan । paryyaṅkaṃ samupāśritya tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। tadaikā devatā tasyāṃ rātrau svargāt samāgatā । svakāntyā bhāsayaṃty evaṃ jetavanam upāviśat ।।
tatas tāṃ bhagavān dṛṣṭvā devatāṃ samupāgatāṃ । saṃnirīkṣya samāmaṃtrya tathaināṃ samabodhayat ।। devate svāgataṃ kacci kuśalaṃ te samehi bho । prāyātāsi yad arthena tad vadasva prapūraye ।।
ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa tenāsau devatā mudā । saṃpṛchāvasaraṃ labdhvā harṣitā samupākramat ।। tatrāsau purato gatvā natvā pādau kṛtāṃjaliḥ । pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā tasthāv ekāntike muneḥ ।।
sarvajetavanaṃ tasyā devatāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ । udāreṇāvabhāsena pravisphuṭaṃ vabhau tadā ।। tathāvabhāṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te bhikṣusāṃghikāḥ । vismitāḥ sahasotthāya dṛṣṭvā tam upatasthire ।।
atha sā devatotthāya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo agragā । bhagavantaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivam apṛchata ।। sarvajña bhagavaṃ chāstaḥ yenāhaṃ samupāgatā । tadarthaṃ tvaṃ samādiśya cittaṃ me paribodhaya ।।
ke narāḥ sugatiṃ yānti ke narāḥ svargagāminaḥ । keṣāṃ cāpi divārātrau sadā puṇyaṃ pravarddhate ।। ke cāpi durgatiṃ yāṃti ke cādhaḥ patitā narāḥ । keṣāṃ cāpi divārātrau sadā pāpaṃ pravarddhate ।।
kiṃdado valavāṃ syāc ca kiṃdadaś ca praśobhitaḥ । kiṃdadaḥ sukhito lokaḥ cakṣuṣmān api kiṃpradaḥ ।। kiṃ nu vā niśitaṃ śastraṃ kiṃ vā hālāhalaṃ viṣaṃ । kiṃ ca prajvalito vahniḥ kiṃ mahad dāruṇaṃ tamaḥ ।।
gṛhītaṃ kiṃ nu martyena kin teneha samujjhitaṃ । abhedyaṃ kavacaṃ kiṃ ca kiṃ vā tīkṣṇam ihāyudhaṃ ।। ko nv asau procyate cauro dhanaṃ kiṃ vā satāṃ mataṃ । ke vā traidhātuke loke procyante muṣitaiti ।।
kaś ceha satsukhī loke ko vā ca parameśvaraḥ । ko vibhūṣito nityaṃ kaś cāpy atra vidaṃvitaḥ ।। vatsalo vāṃdhavo ko nu ko vā duṣṭāśayo ripuḥ । kiṃ mahad dāruṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ kiṃ mahat paramaṃ sukhaṃ ।।
kiṃ ca loke priyo pathyaḥ kiṃ vāpathyaṃ na cāpriyaṃ । ko nu pīḍākaro vyādhiḥ ko nu vai ko bhiṣagvaraḥ ।। kenāyam āvṛto lokaḥ kena loko vaśīkṛtaḥ । kena tyajati mitrāṇi kena svargaṃ na gachati ।।
kena mitrāṇi varddhyaṃte kena śāmyaṃti śatravaḥ । kena svargam avāpnoti kena mokṣaṃ ca gachati ।। kenāyaṃ badhyate lokaḥ kena loko vimucyate । kasyeha viprahāṇena nirvāṇam iti kathyate ।।
kiṃ nu rājā ca caurāś ca syaṃdamānāḥ samudyatāḥ । no śaknuvanty apāhartuṃ striyo vā puruṣasya ca ।। kiṃ na dahati saptārciḥ kiṃ na bhinatti mārutaḥ । kiṃ vā na kledayaṃty āpaḥ kiṃ na kṣīṇaṃ ca bhūmiṣu ।।
imaṃ saṃśayam adyāpi mama tac chetum arhasi । asmāl lokāt paraṃ lokaṃ ko gato atyaṃtavaṃcitaḥ ।। kiṃ nu hatvā sukhaṃ śete kiṃ ca hatvā na śocati । kasya caikasya dharmasya vadhaṃ saṃśasi gautama ।।
mayaitad bhagavan pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajño asi yato sudhīḥ । tan mama saṃśayaṃ chetuṃ samyag ādeṣṭum arhasi ।। tayaivaṃ pṛchyamāno asau bhagavān sarvavij jinaḥ । devatāṃ tāṃ samālokya tat praśnottaram abravīt ।।
śṛṇu tvaṃ devate samyak kṛtvā cittaṃ samāhitaṃ । tavaitat paripṛchāyāḥ pratyuttaram udāhare ।। ārāmāropakā ye atra ye ca vā setukārakāḥ । prapātodakayānaṃ ca pradadanti pratiśrayaṃ ।।
śraddhāśīlena satyena kṣamayā vītamatsarāḥ । te narāḥ sugatiṃ yānti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। teṣām eva hi martyānāṃ divārātrau niraṃtaraṃ । avichinnāḥ puṇyadhārāḥ pravarddhyante sadā khalu ।।
daśākuśalakarttāro yena saddharmaniṃdakāḥ । te narā durgatiṃ yānti bhramanti pāpacāriṇaḥ ।। ye cātatāyino martyāḥ svakuladharmanaṣṭakāḥ । te narāḥ patitā yanti narake duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ pāpiṣṭhasatvānāṃ divārātrau niraṃtaraṃ । avichinnāḥ pāpadhārāḥ pravahante sadā khalu ।। annado valavān bhogī vastradaḥ śobhito bhavet । pānadaḥ sukhitaḥ tṛptaś cakṣuṣmān bhavati dīpadaḥ ।।
duṣṭavāg niśitaṃ śastraṃ rāgo hālahalaṃ viṣaṃ । dveṣaḥ prajvalito vahnir avidyā dāruṇaṃ tamaḥ ।। gṛhītaṃ yat svayaṃ dattaṃ yad gṛhe tad ihojjhitaṃ । abhedyaṃ kavacaṃ kṣāntiḥ prajñā tīkṣṇaṃ mahāyudhaṃ ।।
vitarko akuśalaś cauraḥ śilaṃ dhanaṃ satāṃ mataṃ । te eva muṣitā loke yaiḥ śīlaṃ vinipātitaṃ ।। alpechaḥ satsukhī loke saṃtuṣṭaḥ parameśvaraḥ । śīlavān bhūṣito nityaṃ naṣṭaśīlo vidaṃvitaḥ ।।
vatsalo vāndhavaḥ puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ duṣṭāśayo ripuḥ । nārakaṃ dāruṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ skaṃdhābhāvaparaṃ sukhaṃ ।। kāmāḥ priyā apathyā hi mokṣaḥ pathyo priyaḥ satāṃ । dveṣaḥ pīḍākaro vyādhiḥ buddha eko bhiṣagvaraḥ ।।
ajñānenāvṛto loko mohanaḥ pravaśīkṛtaḥ । lobhāt tyajati mitrāṇi saṃgāt svargaṃ na gachati ।। tyāgān mitrāṇi varddhante maitryā śāmyanti śatravaḥ । śīlāt svargam avāpnoti jñānān mokṣaṃ su gachati ।।
ichayā badhyate loko nīchayā ca vimucyate । tṛṣṇāyā viprahāṇena nirvāṇam iti kathyate ।। puṇyaṃ rājā ca caurāś ca syaṃdamānāḥ samudyatāḥ । na śaknuvaṃty apāhartuṃ striyo vā puruṣasya ca ।।
puṇyaṃ na dahate vahnir bhinatti ca na mārutaḥ । puṇyaṃ na kledayaṃty āpo naiva kṣīṇvaṃti bhūmayaḥ ।। vidyamāneṣu bhogyeṣu puṇyaṃ yena na saṃcitaṃ । asmāl lokāt paraṃ lokaṃ sa gato atyaṃtavaṃcitaḥ ।।
krodhaṃ hatvā sukhaṃ śete krodhaṃ hatvā na śocati । krodhasyaikasya dharmasya vadhaṃ saṃśāmi sarvadā ।। etat praśnottaraṃ śrutvā devatāsau pramoditā । bhagavaṃtaṃ punar natvā prasaṃśyaivam avocata ।। dhanyo asi bhagavan buddha sarvapraśnottarapradaḥ ।
sarvajño jagatāṃ śāstā ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ ।। vīrasya ca na paśyāmi brāhmaṇyaṃ parinirvṛtiṃ । sarvavīro bhayātītas trātuṃ loke abhiśaktibhāg ।। ity uktvā devatā bhūyaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ ।
natvā pādau munīndrasya tata eva divaṃ yayau ।। atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve śrutvā śāstrānudeśitaṃ । satyam evaṃ parijñāya samyak karmasu cerire ।। evam etan mahārāja guruṇā me prabhāṣitaṃ ।
śrutvā caivaṃ parijñāya saddharme nirato bhava ।। dharmeṇa sugatiṃ yāyāt pāpena durgatiṃ vrajet । tasmād dharmaṃ puraskṛtya prajāḥ samyak prapālaya ।। daśākuśalakarmāṇi tyaktvā saṃvṛtim ācara ।
sarvopakaraṇaṃ dānaṃ dātavyaṃ svargavāṃchinā ।। duṣṭasaṃgaṃ parityajya hatvā rāgaviṣaṃ muhuḥ । dveṣāgniśamanaṃ kṛtvā hy avidyā saṃpraghātyatāṃ ।। kāmavitarkatāṃ tyaktvā bodhipraṇidhicetasā ।
trikāyaśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śīladhanam upārjyatāṃ ।। skaṃdhābhāvaṃ parijñāya matvā duṣṭāśayaṃ ripuṃ । kṣamāsv āvaraṇaṃ dhṛtvā duṣṭasaṃghān vijīyatāṃ ।। māradharmān vinirjitya saṃbodhidharmasādhane ।
dhairyavīryamahotsāhair udyamaṃ kriyatāṃ sadā ।। kleśamānamadāñ jitvā kṛtvā cittaṃ samāhitaṃ । sarvasatvahitārtheṣu dhyātāṃ bodhisādhanaṃ ।। lokaṃ māyāsamudbhūtam ajñānatamasāvṛtaṃ ।
dṛṣṭvā prajñāpradīpena preryatāṃ sugateḥ pathi ।। evaṃ rājan bhavān matvā duṣṭasaṃgān vivarjayet । satsaṃgaṃ nirato nityaṃ triratnasevako bhava ।। sarvā api prajāś caivaṃ paribodhya prayatnataḥ । preraṇīyā tvayā rājan saṃvṛtticaraṇe sadā ।।
evaṃ matvā bhavāṃ rājā saṃsārasāram āpnuvan । kramād bodhicarī pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। ity etad guruṇādiṣṭam upaguptena bhikṣuṇā । śrutvā tatheti rājāsāv abhyanaṃdat saparṣikāḥ ।।
devatāparipṛchākhyasūtraṃ śṛṇvaṃti ye mudā । śrāvayaṃti ca te saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ ।। athāśoko nareṃdraś ca kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punaḥ śrotuṃ samarthayat ।।
bhadaṃta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।। iti pṛṣṭe nṛpeṇāsauv upagupto jināṃśajaḥ । tam aśokaṃ mahīnāthaṃ saṃnirīkṣya samabravīt ।।
śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te rājaṃ yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । śrutvaitad bhavatāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ dharmam ādarāt ।। puraikasamaye rājaṃ śākyasiṃho dayāṃbudhiḥ । sarvajño dharmarāṇ nāthaḥ śāstā traidhātukādhipaḥ ।।
sarvavidyādhipo buddhaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ । jino arhan sugato buddhas tathāgato vināyakaḥ ।। bhagavān satvahitārthena pure kapilavastuni । nyagrodhamaṇḍitodyāne karaṇḍakanivāpake ।।
śrāvakabhikṣusaṃghaiś ca bodhisatvagaṇaiḥ saha । saddharmadeśanāṃ kartuṃ vijahāra jināśrame ।। tad dharmaṃ śrotum āyātair upāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ । devāsuragaṇaiś cāpi caturbhi lokapālakaiḥ ।।
cāturvarṇṇyair manuṣyaiś ca paurajānapadādibhiḥ । saṃbodhicaraṇotsāhaiḥ saddharmaguṇalālasaiḥ ।। satkṛto pūjitaś caivaṃ parivṛtya puraskṛtaḥ । bhagavān sa sabhāmadhye siṃhāsanasthito vabhau ।।
tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sabhāṃ tāṃ samupasthitāṃ । ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāś ca moditāḥ । tathainaṃ śrīghanaṃ nityaṃ bhejire dharmalālasāḥ ।।
tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra pure kapilavastuni । rohiṇākhyo mahāchākyo dhanāḍhyo dhanadopamaḥ ।। mahābhogo mahāśrāddhaḥ suviśālaparigrahaḥ । dātā sādhur mahā dhīraḥ pratyuvāsa sukhānvitaḥ ।।
samaye tena śākyena svakulasadṛśāt kulāt । bhāryā nītā subhadrāṅgī svakuladharmacāriṇī ।। tato asau rohiṇaḥ śākyas tayaiva kāntayā saha । mahāragānurāgeṇa rarāma paricārayan ।। tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya kṛīḍato apy anurāgataḥ ।
na putro na sutā vāpi sucireṇāpy ajāyata ।। tato asau rohiṇaḥ putrīputralābhe samutsukaḥ । putracintāparaḥ koṣṭhe sthitvaivaṃ ca vyacintayat ।। īyatsaṃpad gṛhe me asti na ca putrasutāpi na ।
etā me saṃpado rājā mamātyayād grahīṣyati ।। hā me saṃpad vinaṣṭā syāt paratrāpi gatir na hi । vyarthas majjanma saṃsāre yato me santatir na hi ।। ko me kuryāc ca saṃskāraṃ kaś ca piṇḍaṃ pradāsyati ।
kutrāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāyāṃ hā daivanihato asmy ahaṃ ।। iti cintāviṣaṇṇo asau śokāgāre vyavasthitaḥ ।। kapolaṃ svakare dhṛtvā tasthau bhogyanirutsukaḥ । evaṃ cintāsamākrāntaṃ rohiṇaṃ taṃ nirutsukaṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā sarve suhṛnmitrā vāndhavāś ca vyabodhayan । kim evaṃ tiṣṭhase bhadra kiṃ ca duḥkhaṃ prajāyate ।। vaktavyaṃ cet tathāsmākaṃ vaktum arhasi sarvathā । iti pṛṣṭe ca taiḥ sarvair vandhumitrasuhṛjjanaiḥ ।।
rohiṇo asau puras teṣāṃ sarvam evam abhāṣata । bhavantaḥ śṛṇuta sarve kathyate duḥkhatā mayā ।। mahatī me gṛhe saṃpad asyā bhoktā na vidyate । kathaṃ me vidyate vaṃśas tat prakāraṃ na manyate ।।
yadi vo asti mayi snehas tad upāyaṃ pracakṣyatāṃ । evaṃ tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te snehavaṃdhitāḥ ।। tasya vaṃśasamutpatter upāyaṃ samupādiśan । mā kārṣīḥ śokatāṃ bhadra tad upāyaṃ nu vidyate ।।
devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā yācasva putram ātmanā । avaśyaṃ devatānāṃ te prasannānāṃ prasādataḥ ।। putro vā duhitā vāpi bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । ity etat taiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau rohiṇo mudā ।।
devatārādhanāṃ kartuṃ prayatātmā samārabhat । pūjāṅgaiḥ pūjāyitvā ca brāhmaṇaṃ harim īśvaraṃ ।। iṃdrādilokapālāñ ca saṃtatiṃ samayācata । evaṃ putrābhinandī sa sadāraḥ vaṃśakāmyayā ।।
devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā tasthau nityaṃ samutsukaḥ । tathāpi tasya śākyasya svadaivaparimāṇataḥ ।। na putro na ca putrī vā suciram apy ajāyata । tato asau rohiṇaḥ śākyo devatāsu nirāśayā ।।
putravāṃchāviraktātmā tasthau gehe nirutsavaḥ । asti caiṣa mahārāja pravādo laukikodbhavaḥ ।। yad devatāprasādena jāyate saṃtatiḥ khalu । evaṃ ced vā tathā rājann ekaikasya bhavet khalu ।।
yathā putrasahasraṃ vā nṛpasya cakravarttinaḥ । api tu saṃmukhībhāvāt tristhānānāṃ nṛpeśvara ।। putrā vāpi sutāś cāpi jāyaṃte prāṇināṃ khalu । tadyathā pitarau raktau kalyā cartumatī prasūḥ ।
gaṃdharvaḥ prasthitaḥ kāle tadā garbhe samudbhavet ।। tataś ca samaye tasya rohiṇasyānurāgiṇaḥ । bhāryyā kalyāvatībhūtā snātvā ratiṃ samārabhat ।। tadaikā devatā svargāc cyutvā karmānubhoginī ।
tasya śākyasya bhāryyāyā garbhe sā samupāviśat ।। tataḥ svāpannasatvā sā matvā garbhasamudbhavaṃ । svāmino agre rahaḥ sthitvā harṣitaivaṃ nyavedayat ।। svāminn āpannasatvāsmi vaṃśa āvāṃ samudbhavet ।
tad bhavān sarvakṛyāni kārayatv anumoditaḥ ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā rohiṇo asau pramoditaḥ । bhāryāṃ tāṃ garbhiṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsmitaḥ pratyabhāṣata ।। satyaṃ me bhāṣitaṃ bhadre matvā bhava samāhitā ।।
pramādam atra mā kārṣī yadi snehāsti te mayi । evaṃ te kuśalaṃ bhadre yadi putraṃ janiṣyasi ।। tadā niṣkāśayāmi tvāṃ yadi putrīṃ janiṣyasi । iti bhartur vacaḥ śrutvā sā strī vivṛddhadohadā । bhartur viyogaśaṃkārttā babhūva parikheṭitā ।। yāvat sā samaye sūta dārikāṃ divyasuṃdarīṃ ।
śuklavastraparītāṅgāṃ garbhamalāviliptitāṃ ।। tatas tāṃ dārikāṃ jātāṃ śrutvāsau rohiṇo ruṣā । pratyākhyātuṃ svayaṃ bhāryāṃ viveśa sūtikāgṛhe ।। prajāpatyā tayā bhartur upanītā puraḥ sutā ।
śuklavastraparītāṅgā bhadrāṅgī divyasuṃdarī ।। tataḥ sa rohiṇo dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sutāṃ divyasuṃdarīṃ । śuklavastraparītāṅgāṃ paravismayam āyayau ।। aho bhāgyān mayā labdhā suteyaṃ bhadrarūpiṇī ।
yad eṣā sahajaiḥ śuklavastraiḥ prāvṛtya jāyate ।। tasmān nūnaṃ iyaṃ sākṣād devakanyāvatāritā । saddharmacāriṇī bhadrā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। ity uktvāsau pitā śākyaḥ paśyaṃs tāṃ dārikāṃ cirāt ।
atṛpto niścalākṣaś ca tasthau saṃmūrchito yathā ।। tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ mudā । tan nāmakaraṇaṃ tasyās tān punaḥ sa samabravīt ।। bhavanto asyāḥ sutāyā me bhadrāṅgyā anurūpataḥ ।
nāmadheyaṃ prasiddhena karttavyaṃ kriyatāṃ śubhaṃ ।। iti tenārthite tasyāḥ sarve te jātayas tathā । sahajaśuklavastrāṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ saṃvabhāṣire ।। yad iyaṃ dārikā saumyā bhadrāṃgī divyasuṃdarī ।
śuklavastrāvṛtā jātā tac chukleti prasidhyatu ।। iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te jñātayas tathā । rohiṇaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya tathaivaṃ samudāharat ।। yad iyaṃ te sutā bhadra bhadrāṅgī divyasuṃdarī ।
śuklavastrāvṛtā jātā tac chukleti pracakṣyatāṃ ।। tathety anumataṃ kṛtvā tena pitrā prasāditā । śuklā sā duhitāṣṭāsu dhātrīṣu samupārpitā ।। tatas tāsāṃ ca dhātrīṇām upacārapracārataḥ ।
varddhitābhūt suramyāṅgī hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ ।। yathā yathā ca sā śuklā parivṛddhābhavat kramāt । tathā tathā ca tad vastraṃ vavṛddhe nirmalī abhavat ।। na ca kāyo apy abhūt tasmāt malābhiliptadurbhagaḥ । vabhau tu nirmalaḥ śuddhaḥ sugaṃdhiparivāhakaḥ ।।
yadā sā dārikā śuklā parivṛddhā kramād abhūt । kumārī sarvalokānāṃ manonetrābhihāriṇī ।। tataḥ sā śikṣituṃ vidyā guruṇāṃ samupāśritā । śikṣitvā kramaśo vidyāṃ pāram āśu yayau sudhīḥ ।।
tadā ye ye ca tāṃ śuklām apaśyad divyasuṃdarīṃ । te te sarve api paśyanto vismitā moham āyayuḥ ।। tatas te brāhmaṇādyāś ca tadguṇākṛṣṭamānasāḥ । svasvadūtena tāṃ śuklāṃ rohiṇaṃ prārthayan muhuḥ ।।
jātiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ vipras tac chuklāṃ me dātum arhasi । iti tāṃ brāhmaṇaputrā rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan ।। rājaputro asmy ahaṃ vīras tat sutā me pradīyatāṃ । iti rājakumārās taṃ rohiṇaṃ tāṃ samarthayan ।।
ahaṃ vaiśyaḥ prajābhartā tac chuklāṃ me dātum arhasi । iti vaiśyakumārās tāṃ rohiṇaṃ prārthayari muhuḥ ।। ahaṃ maṃtrisuto vijñas tac chuklā me pradīyatāṃ । iti maṃtrisutāḥ sarve rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan ।।
mahāmātyasuto ahaṃ hi tac chuklāṃ me prayachatāṃ । ity āmātyakumārās tāṃ rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan ।। evam anye api lokāś ca rūpadravyābhimāninaḥ । svasvadūtena tāṃ śuklāṃ rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan ।।
evaṃ sarvaiś ca tair nityaiḥ prārthyamāno mahājanaiḥ । rohiṇaḥ sa viṣaṇṇātmā sthitvaivaṃ ca vyacintayat ।। hā me duḥkhāni jātāni katham atra pratikriyā । sarvathāhaṃ praṇaṣṭaḥ syāṃ sutayāḥ kāraṇe adhunā ।।
yady ekasmai pradāsyāmi sutām etāṃ manoharāṃ । anye sarve api me vairā bhaviṣyaṃti tadā khalu ।। avaśyaṃ me sutā hīyaṃ vairiṇī māṃ haniṣyati । evaṃ duḥkhānudāyinyā putryāpi kiṃ mamaitayā ।।
iti cintāviṣaṇṇo asau tac cintākulamānasaḥ । kapolaṃ svakare sthāpya tasthau koṣṭhe nirutsavaḥ ।। evaṃ cintāvibhinnāsyaṃ pitaraṃ taṃ viṣādinaṃ । sā śuklā duhitā dṛṣṭvā praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।। kim evaṃ tiṣṭhase tāta kiṃ te duḥkhaṃ nu jāyate ।
kathyatāṃ tad yadi sneho mayi te varttate pitaḥ ।। iti putryā vacaḥ śrutvā pitā sa ruṣitāśayaḥ । niḥsnehas tāṃ sutāṃ śuklāṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ paryyabhāṣata ।। tvan nimitte mahad duḥkhaṃ jāyate me kuputrike ।
kiṃ tavāgre kathitvaitaṃ yato naiva pratikriyā ।। avaśyaṃ tvaṃ sutā śatruḥ sarvathā māṃ haniṣyasi । evaṃ duḥkhābhidāyinyā putryāpi kiṃ mama tvayā ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sā śuklā prahatāśayā ।
sahasā pitaraṃ natvā rudaṃtyaivaṃ abhāṣata । tāta kiṃ me nimittena duḥkhaṃ te jāyate kathaṃ । sarvathaitat pravaktavyaṃ yadi te ahaṃ sutātmajā । tad upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yena duḥkhaṃ nihanyate ।।
tad etat sarvathā tāta mamāgre vaktum arhasi । iti putryodite bhūyaḥ pitāsau rohiṇo avadat ।। tat kin te kathyate putri yato nāsti pratikriyā । bahavaḥ prārthayitāras tava rājasutādayaḥ ।।
kumārā brāhmaṇā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtrinaṃdanāḥ । amātyanaṃdanāś cāpi sārthavāhasutādayaḥ ।। evam anye api ye cānyā guṇadravyābhimānitāḥ । paurikā grāmikāś cāpi kularūpābhimānikāḥ ।।
etaiḥ sarvair ahaṃ nityaṃ sumudritas tvadarthibhiḥ । katham atra kariṣyāmi cetanā me na vidyate ।। tvam evaikā hi me putrī bahavo yācakāś ca te । ekasmai yadi dāsyāmi sarve anye syur mamāhitāḥ ।।
atas tvāṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ kṛtvā sarvebhyo apy arpaye ca vai । evaṃ tu kriyamāṇe me kuśalatvaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। anyathā ced bhaven naiva kuśalaṃ me sadāpi hi । iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā śuklā sā mṛtyuśaṃkita ।। moditeva pituḥ pādau praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।
prasīda mā kṛthāḥ khedaṃ mamaitat kāraṇe pitaḥ ।। tathāhaṃ te kariṣyāmi yathā doṣo na vidyate । nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। pravrajitvā cariṣyāmi bhagavacchāsane vrataṃ ।
ity etad bhāṣitaṃ putryā śrutvāsau rohiṇaḥ pitā ।। putrīviyogam āśaṃkya punar evam abhāṣata । mā kṛthāḥ sarvathā putri pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ ।। tvaṃ strī vālā na śaknuyāḥ pravrajyāṃ carituṃ sute ।
pravrajyāyāṃ vrataṃ kaṣṭaṃ puruṣair api duṣkaraṃ ।। tvaṃ tu vālā subhadrāṃgī komalā divyasuṃdarī । kathaṃ tad duṣkarasthāne vrataṃ kartuṃ saheḥ sute ।। tan mā kṛthās tathā vāle pravrajyāyāṃ manas tyaja ।
yadi kāmārthinī nāsi kasmai cid dāsyate na hi ।। tat putri svagṛhe sthitvā vrataṃ dhṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa । yadi kāmārthinī vāsi putri teṣāṃ tvadarthināṃ ।। svayaṃvaravidhiṃ kṛtvā svayaṃ vara yam ichasi ।
tadā me dūṣaṇaṃ nāsti tavāpi dūṣaṇaṃ na hi ।। sarvatrāpi hi lokeṣu vidhir eṣa pravarttate । tasmāt teṣāṃ kumārāṇāṃ patiṃ bhadraṃ svayaṃ vara ।। tenaiva patinā sārddhaṃ vrataṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ cara ।
tadā santatim utpādya bhuktvā bhogyaṃ yathā sukhaṃ ।। saṃvṛtticaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tathānte svargam āpnuyāḥ । tenaivaṃ mā kṛthāḥ putri pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ ।। kiṃ te pravrajyayā siddhyen mahadduṣkaracaryyayā ।
ity ukte janakenāsau śuklā kāmaparāṅmukhā ।। saddharmacaraṇaprepsuḥ pitaram evam abravīt । nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta saṃbodhipadavāṃchinī ।। tasmād bhogyāny api tyaktvā caritum ichāmi sadvrataṃ ।
sabhayāḥ saraṇāḥ kāmāḥ sakleśāś ca viṣopamāḥ ।। tasmāt kāme na me vāṃchā nirvāṇe eva me manaḥ । sadevāsuramānuṣyā ye satvāḥ kāmarāgiṇaḥ ।। sarve te kleśitāś cāndhāś caranti pātakeṣv api । kṛtvā te pātakāny evaṃ gachanti durgatiṣv api ।।
vividhāni ca duḥkhāni bhuṃjate narakāsthitāḥ । brāhmaṇā api dhīrāś ca vaidikā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। te api kāmānurāgena bhraṣṭā gacchaṃti durgatiṃ । tapasvino mahābhijñāḥ śuddhātmānā jitendriyāḥ ।
te api kāmānurāgena bhraṣṭā gacchaṃti durgatiṃ । yatayo yoginaś cāpi nirgraṃthāś ca digaṃvarāḥ ।। te api kāmānurāgena bhraṣṭā gacchanti durgatiṃ । rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi kṛtvā yuddhaṃ parasparaṃ ।।
āhave nidhanaṃ yānti tad api kāmakāraṇe । amātyā maṃtriṇaś cāpi mārayanti parārdhinaḥ ।। tatpāpair durgatiṃ yānti tad api kāmahetunā । yodhāraś ca mahāvīrā yuddhaṃ kṛtvā parasparaṃ ।।
saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ yānti tad api kāmakāraṇe । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca ratnadravyātilālasāḥ ।। samudre patitāḥ kecin mṛtāḥ kecic ca jaṃgale । kecin mṛtā mahāraṇye cauraiḥ kecid upadrutāḥ ।।
kṣutpipāsāhatāḥ kecin mṛtā mārge rujānvitāḥ । śītavātātapākrāntā mṛtā kecic chramāturāḥ ।। kecid gṛhagatā eva mṛtāḥ kecic ca roginaḥ । kecid bhāraṃ vahantaś ca mṛtāḥ kecid bhayānvitāḥ ।।
jantubhiḥ khāditāḥ kecit tat sarvaṃ kāmahetunā । kṛṣiṇaś ca dinaṃ yāvat kṣatrakarmasamudyatāḥ ।। dinānte gṛham agatya śerate te mṛtā iva । evam anye api lokāś ca śilpipreṣyajanādayaḥ ।।
dāsadāsījanāś cāpi svasvakarmasamudyatāḥ । evaṃ nityam aviśrāntaṃ kuṭuṃvadhanasādhane ।। vahaṃti kheditāḥ kleśaṃ tat sarvaṃ kāmahetunā । evaṃ caurādiduṣṭāś ca paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ ।।
pātakāny api kurvanti tad api kāmakāraṇe । kecic ca paradravyāṇi haranti hārayanti ca ।। kecid dhatvāpi sarvaṃ haranti krūramānasāḥ । dhanārthe kiṃ na kurvanti duṣṭā lubdhāś ca nirdayāḥ ।।
praghnanti pitarau kecit te api ghnanti gurūn api । kecid vighnanti mitrāṇi jñātivandhujanān api ।। patnīputraduhitṝś ca bhrātrīṃś ca bhāginīr api । kecid ghnanti sahāyāṃś ca dāsadāsījanāny api ।।
bālān vṛddhāṃś ca nārīṃś ca tat sarvaṃ kāmakāraṇe । kecic ca prāṇinaḥ pakṣimṛgamatsyādijantukān ।। hatvā khādanti pāpiṣṭhās tad api kāmakāraṇe । evaṃ tiryyaggaṇāś cāpi pakṣisiṃhādijantavaḥ ।।
parasparaṃ nihatyaivaṃ khādanti kāmahetunā । evaṃ śathāvaṃcayantas trāsayanto api vālakān ।। adattaṃ pratigṛhnanti tad api kāmakāraṇāt । mithyākāmaratāḥ kecit paradārāṃś ca kāminīḥ ।।
haranti chadmanā cāpi tad api kāmakāraṇe । yac ca mṛṣāvadaṃto api parakāryyābhighāṭakāḥ ।। sādhayanti svakāryāṇi tad api kāmahetunā । yac ca piśunavādena suhṛnmitrānucāriṇāṃ ।
virodhaṃ kārayanty evaṃ tad api kāmahetunā ।। yac ca pāruṣyavādena gurusādhujanān api । paribhāṣya vinindanti tad api kāmakāraṇe ।। yat saṃbhinnapralāpena suhṛnmitrānuyāyināṃ ।
cittāni bhedayanty evaṃ tad api kāmakāraṇe ।। yac ca māyānurāgeṇa sādhūnāṃ dharmacāriṇāṃ । prabhedayanti cittāni tad api kāmahetunā ।। yad īrṣyāmatsarālīḍhā dṛṣṭvā paraguṇarddhitāṃ ।
vyāpādaṃ cintayanty evaṃ tad api kāmakāraṇe ।। yan mithyādṛṣṭikā loke sarvadharmaprahāsikāḥ । bhogyāni bhuṃjate hṛtvā tad api kāmakāraṇe ।। kecij jātiparibhraṣṭā nīcajātiprasaṃgatāḥ ।
svakuladharmabhraṣṭāś ca tad api kāmakāraṇe ।। evaṃ sarve api satvāś ca sadgatiparivartinaḥ । kāmarthe kleśitātmāno bhramanti durgatau sadā ।। evaṃ yāvanti duḥkhāni saṃsāre ṣaḍgatiṣv api ।
tāni sarvāṇi satvānāṃ jāyante kāmahetunā ।। evaṃ matvā tu ye vijñāḥ kāmaṃ tyaktvā virāgiṇaḥ । pravrajitvā suniḥkleśā brahmacaryyaṃ caranti te ।। tato me sabhaye kāme saraṇe ca viṣopame ।
vidvadbhir garhite tāta manovāṃchā na varttate ।। tatpravrajyāṃ samāśritya bhagavaccharaṇaṃ gatā । brahmacaryyaṃ caritvāhaṃ prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ ।। buddho hi jagatāṃ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।
tat tasya śaraṇe gatvā caritum ichāmi saccarīṃ ।। yady asti te mayi snehaḥ saddharme cānurāgatā । tad anumodanāṃ kṛtvānujñāṃ me dātum arhasi ।। yadi tu saugate dharme apy anujñāṃ me dadāsi na ।
tīrthayātrāṃ bhramiṣyāmi sarvadāhaṃ virāginī ।। iti putrīvacaḥ śrutya śākyo asau rohiṇaḥ pitā । sutādharmaviyogatvaṃ vijñāyaivam acintayat ।। yad iyaṃ me sutā bhadrā nirāśravā virāginī ।
avaśyaṃ svagṛhaṃ tyaktvā pravrajet sarvathā khalu ।। avaśyaṃ me anayā putryā viyogaṃ sarvathā bhavet । sarvathā hy anivāryyeyaṃ vrajatu saugatāśrame ।। yadāyaṃ saugate dharme pravrajitvā nirāśravā ।
brahmacaryyaṃ caraty evaṃ tato nirvṛtim āpnuyāt ।। yad iyaṃ me sutā kāntā subhadrā divyasuṃdarī । yadi gehaṃ parityaktvā tīrthayātrāṃ kariṣyati ।। tadā nūnam iyaṃ bhrāṃtā tīrthikadharmasaṃratā ।
kuladharmaparibhraṣṭā vinaṣṭā syān na saṃśayaḥ ।। tato asmākaṃ yaśodharmavinaṣṭo api bhavet khalu । tasyāś ca dūragāminyā darśanaṃ syāt sudullabhaṃ ।। tasmād asyā na karttavyā vāraṇā dharmasādhane ।
caratu saugatīṃ caryyām iyaṃ hi nirvṛtaye ।। tathā cet saphalaṃ janma mānuṣye syān mamāpi ca । teneyaṃ jagatāṃ bhartuḥ śāsane caratu vrataṃ ।। ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā śākyo asau rohiṇaḥ pitā ।
śuklāṃ tāṃ svātmajāṃ bhadrāṃ saṃnirīkṣyaivam abravīt ।। satyam evaṃ sute bhadre yathoddiṣṭaṃ tvayā khalu । kiṃ tu tvaṃ dārikā nārī pravrajyāṃ tat kathaṃ careḥ ।। pravrajyā duṣkarasthānaṃ nārīṇāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।
tat pravrajyāvrate sthitvā mā paścāt paritapyathāḥ ।। yadi tvaṃ niścayenaiva pravrajyāvratam ichasi । tac carasva munīndrasya śāsane vratam ādarāt ।। yathā ca guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā tathā samāhitaḥ ।
samyak chikṣāḥ samādhāya cara nityam atandritā ।। saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā śraddhābhaktisamanvitā । triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bodhivrataṃ samācara ।। iti pitrā samādiṣṭe śuklā sā pratimoditā ।
natvā pādau pituś caivaṃ jananyāś caraṇe anamat ।। tataḥ sā jananī dṛṣṭvā tāṃ śuklāṃ svātmajāṃ priyāṃ । pariṣvajya rudanty evaṃ pravrajyāyāṃ nyavārayat ।। hā putri katham ekānte māṃ tyaktvā kva vrajiṣyase ।
hā jīva kiṃ nu paśyantī pravrajituṃ tvam īhase ।। kiṃ cid duḥkhaṃ na te dattaṃ mayāmvayā kadā cana । kenaivaṃ hetunā putrī pravrajituṃ tvam ichasi ।। tvaṃ tu nārī subhādrāṅgī kumārī divyasuṃdarī ।
kiṃcid duḥkhānabhijñā ca tat pravrajyāṃ kathaṃ care ।। yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ caiva tāvat mā gāḥ kuhāpi hi । yāvac cāsti gṛhe saṃpat tāvad bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa ।। yadāhaṃ maraṇaṃ yātā yadā cāpi gṛhe vipat ।
jñātimitrajanais tyaktvā tadā vrajasva vāṃchayā ।। iti mātrā niṣiddhe api śuklā sā vighnaśaṃkitās । mātuḥ pādau praṇatvaiva sahasā niryayau gṛhāt ।। tataḥ sā satvarā gatvā nyagrodhārama āśrame ।
dadarśa bhikṣuṇībhikṣūn śantaśīlāñ jiteṃdriyān ।। tān sarvān kramato natvā vihāre samupāviśat । tatrasthaṃ sugataṃ nātham apaśyac chrighanaṃ jinaṃ ।। dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṃḍitaṃ ।
sahasreṇādhikābhāsaṃ vyāmābhaparirocitaṃ ।। śāntātmānam subhadrāṃśaṃ samantabhadrarūpiṇaṃ । ratnarāśim ivojjvālaṃ sumerum iva jaṃgamaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvaiva niścalā tasthau harṣotphullatanūruhā ।
dṛṣṭvaivaṃ sucirāt tasya śrīghanasyāntike yayau ।। tathaivaṃ samupāyātāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhagavān muniḥ । svāgataṃ dārike bhadre ehīty uktvā samagrahīt ।। tato asau dārikā śuklā svāgatāsmi munīśvara ।
ity uktvā prāṃjaliṃ kṛtvā nanāma caraṇau muneḥ ।। tato bhagavatā tena preṣitā mātur antike । sā śuklā sahasā gatvā gautamyāc caraṇe anamat ।। tathā tāṃ samupāyātāṃ śuklāṃ sadvratavāṃchinīṃ ।
dṛṣṭvā sā gautamī spṛṣṭvā hastenaiva samagrahīt ।। tataḥ pravrājayitvā sā gautamyā bhikṣuṇī kṛtā । khikkhirīpātrahastāṅkā saṃgatābhūj jitendriyā ।। yenaiva śuklavastreṇa prāvṛtā samajāyata ।
tataḥ paṃcasuraktaṃ jātāni cīvarāṇy api ।। tair eva civarai raktaiḥ prāvṛtā pariśobhitā । sā śuklā suprasannāsyā muṇḍitāpy abhyarocata ।। tato buddhānubhāvena supraśāntasubhāvinī ।
jitvā kleśārivargāṃś ca śikṣāpāraṃ samāyayau ।। matvānityaṃ ca saṃsāraṃ bhavagatiṃ vighātinīṃ । nihatya sarvasaṃskāragatīsatanadharmiṇī ।। māracaryyāvinirmuktā sākṣād arhatvam āyayau ।
avidyāṅgaṃ vinirbhidya prāptavidyā śubhāśayā ।। abhijñā guṇasaṃpannā pratisaṃvidvatī sudhīḥ । suvītarāgiṇī dhīrā loṣṭhahemasamānikā ।। ākāśasamacittā ca pāṇītalasamāśayā ।
niraṃjanāvikalpā ca śrīkhaṇḍatulyavāsinī ।। svātmasatkāralābheṣu parāṇmukhī sunispṛhā । sarvasatvahitādhāni saṃbuddhadharmacāriṇī ।। sadevāsuralokānāṃ pūjyā mānyā samantataḥ ।
vaṃdanīyā cābhitoṣyā ca vabhūva brahmacāriṇī ।। atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā tāṃ brahmacāriṇīṃ । vismitāḥ sugataṃ natvā paprachur iti sādaraṃ ।। bhagavan kim iyaṃ śuklā purā karmākaroc chubhaṃ ।
yena vastrāvṛtā jātā bhavaty evaṃ ca bhikṣuṇī ।। tat sarvaṃ naḥ samādeṣṭum arhasi sarvavid guro । yad anayā kṛtaṃ karma bhikṣuṇyā śuklayā purā ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tān bhikṣusāṃghikān sarvān saṃnirīkṣyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anayā kṛtaṃ purā । tat sarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi sarvalokābhibodhane ।। purāsminn eva bhadrākhye kalpe abhūt kāśyapo jinaḥ ।
