saṃbuddhaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā traidhātukavināyakaḥ । sarvajño bhagavān arhan brahmacārī hitaṃkaraḥ ।। sa munīndro jagannātho vārāṇasīm upāśrayan ।
mṛgadāve vane ramye vyaharac chrāvakaiḥ saha ।। bhikṣubhir bodhisatvaiś ca bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ । sārddham upāsikābhiś ca yatibhiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।। tatrastho bhagavān buddho sarvasatvahitāya saḥ ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tadaikānyatarā kācic chreṣṭhibhāryā śubhāśayā । sukalyāṇārthinī śrāddhā saddharmamānasī sudhīḥ ।। kena cit karaṇiyena mṛgadāvam upācarat ।
tatra bhikṣūn kramād dṛṣṭvā saṃbuddhāntikam upāyayau ।। tatra sā samupāgatya dadarśa taṃ munīśvaraṃ । dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanair upalakṣitaṃ ।। vyāmābhālaṃkṛtaṃ saumyaṃ śatasūryyādhikaprabhaṃ ।
supraśāntendriyāṃ kāmyaṃ samaṃtabhadrarūpakaṃ ।। ratnarāśim ivojjvālaṃ sumerum iva jaṃgamaṃ । tathā dṛṣṭvaiva prāmodāt sāṃjaliṃ samupāgatā ।। natvā pādau munes tasthāv ekāntike kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।
tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasyāś cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ ।। ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sā śūdrī pariharṣitā ।। sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ nāthaṃ bhojayituṃ samaichata ।
tataḥ sā svagṛhe gatvā sādhayitvā subhojanaṃ ।। saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ svāṃtargehe nyamaṃtrayat । tatra svasvāsanāsīnaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।। pūjayitvā tadarhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।
tataḥ sā śraddhayā tebhyaḥ sarvebhyo api prasannitā ।। buddhapramukhasaṃghebhyaḥ pratyekaṃ cīvaraṃ dadau । tato nityaṃ ca sā bhaktyā cakre saṃbuddhasevanāṃ ।। tatpuṇyaiś cāpi saddharme pravrajituṃ samaichata ।
tato asau pitarau natvābhyanujñāpya prasādinī ।। bhagavacchāsane gatvā pravrajyāvratam ācarat । tasmāt kiṃ bhikṣavo yūyaṃ manyadhve yābhavat tadā ।। śreṣṭhibhāryā na cānyā sā śuklaivaiṣeti manyata ।
yad anayā prasādinyā buddhapramukhasāṃghike ।। pratyekaṃ cīvaraṃ dattaṃ pravrajyā cāpi sādhitā । etatpuṇyavipākena prāvṛtya śuklavāsasā ।। jātā pravrajitā caiṣā bhavati brahmacāriṇī ।
ity evaṃ karmajaṃ bhogyaṃ prāṇino bhuṃjate bhave ।। yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ । na naśyaṃti hi karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api ।। sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalaṃti khalu dehināṃ ।
abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kathaṃ cana ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karma vāyubhiś ca na śuṣyate । jalaiś ca klidyate nāpi kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu ।। anyathā ca bhaven naiva karmagatiḥ kathaṃ cana ।
śuklānāṃ śubhatā nityaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ duḥkhatā sadā ।। miśritā miśritānāṃ ca jaṃtubhir bhujyate gatiḥ । tasmād apāsya kṛṣṇāni karmāṇi miśritāni ca ।। caritavyaṃ śubheṣv eva karmasu sukhavāṃchibhiḥ । tatheti bhikṣavaḥ sarve te ca lokaḥ sabhāsthitāḥ ।।
śrutvā tat sugatādiṣṭam abhyanandan prasāditāḥ । evam etan mahārāja guruṇā me prabhāṣitaṃ ।। evaṃ rājaṃs tvayāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ puṇyam ādarāt । puṇyam eva bhave vandhubhrātā mitraṃ suhṛtsakhā ।।
nānyaḥ puṇyāt paraḥ kaścid vidyate bhavacāriṇāṃ । tasmāt puṇyaṃ svayaṃ kṛtvā lokeṣv api pracāraya ।। prajāś ca bodhayitvaivaṃ puṇyamārge pracāraya । ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭam upaguptena bhikṣuṇā ।।
śrutvā tatheti rājāsau prābhyanandaj janaiḥ saha ।। śṛṇvanti śravayanti pramuditamanasaḥ sadguṇaprāptukāmāḥ । satsaukhyāny eva bhuktvā munivaranilaye saṃprayātā vasanti ।। athāśoko mahīpāla upaguptaṃ jināṃśajaṃ ।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā te guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā vaktuṃ samarhasi ।। evaṃ tena nṛpendreṇa prārthite sa jinātmajaḥ ।
upagupto mahābhijñas taṃ nṛpaṃ caivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu rājaṃs tathā vakṣye yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । śrutvā caivaṃ sadā bodhicaryāṃ cara samāhitaḥ ।। puraikasamaye asau ca śākyamunis tathāgataḥ ।
sarvajñaḥ sugato nāthaḥ śāstā traidhātukādhipaḥ ।। sarvavidyādhipas tāyī ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ । jino arhaṃ bhagavān buddho dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। śrāvastyāṃ vahir udyāne jetavane jināśrame ।
anāthapiṇḍadārāme vihāre maṇimaṇḍite ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ । triratnopāsikābhiś ca cailakaiś ca śubhāśayaiḥ ।। bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi sahānyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।
osaddharmadeśanāṃ datvā tasthau lokahitārthataḥ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ prājagmuḥ sadguṇārthinaḥ । devā daityāś ca nāgāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।। siddhavidyādharādyāś ca lokapālagaṇādayaḥ ।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ ।। amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaś cāpi dhaninaś ca mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca tadanye api ca sajjanāḥ ।। paurā jānapadāś cāpi sarve te samupāgatāḥ ।
taṃ buddhaṃ sugataṃ natvā pūjayitvā samaṃtataḥ ।। parivṛtya paraskṛtya tasthuḥ sāṃjalayo mudā । athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupāsthitān । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāḥ surādayaḥ । harṣitā anumodanto vabhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। evaṃ nityaṃ ca te satvāḥ pītvā dharmāmṛtaṃ muneḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhejire samupāśritāḥ ।।
tadaiva samaye tasyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ puri saṃsthitaḥ । āsīd gṛhapatiḥ prāḍhyo mahābhogyasamṛddhimān ।। kuvelavan mahāśrīmān suvistīrṇaparigrahaḥ ।। śrāddho dātā mahābhogī sarvalokahitārthabhṛt ।
evaṃ maharddhikasyāpi tasya gṛhapateś ciraṃ । na putro na ca putrī vā samudapādi daivataḥ ।। tato aputro gṛhastho asau vaṃśavichinnakheṭitaḥ । kapolaṃ svakare sthāpya viṣādyaivaṃ vyacintayat ।।
anekadhanaratnādyāḥ saṃpado me maharddhikāḥ । viśālaparivārāś ca vidyante suparigrahāḥ ।। putro me duhitā vāpi vidyate na kathaṃ cana । saṃpado api nirarthāḥ syur yato bhoktā na vidyate ।।
hā hā sarvaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ syād yato me santatir na hi । kiṃ me anayā samṛddhyāpi yatra vaṃśo na vidyate ।। vyartham eva mayā dravyaṃ kaṣṭena samupārjitaṃ । kiṃ kariṣyāmi taddravyaṃ sarvathā maraṇe sati ।।
ke hi grastā na saṃsāre mṛtyusarppeṇa jaṃtavaḥ । mayi mṛtyuprayāte atra saṃskāraṃ kaḥ kariṣyati ।। durgatiśodhanaṃ kaś ca piṇḍam ekaṃ pradāsyati । nūnaṃ madatyayād rājā sarvasvam āhariṣyati ।।
tadā nāmāpi me loke na kaś cana grahīṣyati । yad artham eva saṃpattīḥ sādhayāmi prayatnataḥ ।। tad eva yadi nāsty evaṃ tat kiṃ me syāt sujīvite ।। varam evādya mṛtyur na mithyācirajīvanaṃ ।
yasmāc ciram api sthitvā mṛtyuduḥkhaṃ tadaiva hi ।। tan me bhogye api vāṃchā na bhuktvāpi kiṃ sukhaṃ vinā । aputrasya sukhaṃ naiva paratreha niranvayāt ।। tan me janmāpi vyarthaṃ syād dhy aputro asmi niranvayāt ।
hā hato ahaṃ svadaivena kiṃ mayātra kariṣyate ।। kasyāgre saṃvadiṣyāmi ko me buddhiṃ pradāsyati । kasyāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāsye ko māṃ samuddhariṣyati ।। iti cintāviṣaṇno asau tasthau koṣṭhe yathāturaḥ । nirutsāhī gṛhān naiva nirapāyāt kadācana ।।
etac cintāviṣaṇṇābhaṃ taṃ gṛhasthaṃ suhṛjjanāḥ । dṛṣṭvaiva sahasopetya bodhayituṃ samabruvan ।। kiṃ te duḥkhaṃ samutpannaṃ kenaivaṃ tiṣṭhase sakhe । vaktavyaṃ cet tadā āśu sarvathā vaktum arhasi ।।
iti pṛṣṭe suhṛdbhis tair gṛhasthaḥ sa viniśvasan । tān sarvān suhṛdo dṛṣṭvā tad duḥkhaṃ samudāharat ।। suhṛdo me bhavanto hi tan mayātra pracakṣyate । saṃpattir mahatī me asti putro naiva sutāpi naḥ ।।
tena me saṃpadaḥ sarvā vinakṣyanti nirarthitāḥ । etac cintāviṣārttāhaṃ tiṣṭhāmi putravāṃchitaḥ ।। aputrasya sukhaṃ nāsti paratreha samaṃtataḥ । tan me janmāpi vyarthaṃ syād aputrasya niranvayāt ।।
tathā hato ahaṃ svadaivena kiṃ mayātra cariṣyate । iti tenodite sarve jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanāḥ ।। tasya grīhapateś caivāṃ tad upāyaṃ samādiśat । kiṃ bhadrātra viṣādena yatra devādhikāratā ।।
tathāpi kriyatāṃ yatnaṃ klaibyaṃ tyaktvā tvayādhunā । yad aśakyaṃ valair dravyais tad upāyena śakyate ।। tasmāt klaibyam iha tyaktvā kuru yatnaṃ samāhitaḥ । devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā sarvakāryyaṃ hi sādhayet ।।
tadādau devatāḥ pūjya yācasva putram ātmanā । tato devaprasādena tavadharmānubhāvataḥ । putro vā duhitā vāpi samupapatsyate dhruvaṃ ।। tatas te saṃtatiś caivaṃ varddhiṣyati kramāt tathā ।
tadāpi bhṛśato muktaḥ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāt ।। iti taiḥ samupādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsāv anumoditāḥ । devatārādhanaṃ kartuṃ prayatātmā samārabhat ।। pūjāṃgaiḥ pūjayitvaivaṃ brahmāṇaṃ harim īśvaraṃ ।
iṃdrādilokapālānāṃ saṃtatiṃ samayācata ।। evaṃ putrābhilāsī sa sadā ca santatīchayā । devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā tasthau nityaṃ samutsukaḥ ।। nityam evaṃ kṛtasyāpi tasya daivapraṇāmataḥ ।
na putro duhitā vāpi nodapādi cirād api ।। tathā cāpi gṛhastho asau devatāsu nirāśayā । santatyucchinnacintārttas tasthau bhūyo viṣāditaḥ ।। tataḥ kaścit suhṛt sādhuḥ saṃbuddhopāsakaḥ sudhīḥ ।
taṃ gṛhastham upāgatya tathaivaṃ paryyabodhayat ।। sādho kin te viṣādena tad dhīraṃ samupāśraya । yadi te santatau vāṃchā tan me śrutvā tataś cara ।। kim evaṃ devatāḥ pūjya yācase putram ādarāt ।
yatra daivādhikāratvaṃ tatra kiṃ devatā valaṃ ।। vaṃśārthe yadi te bhaktir asty evaṃ devatāsu tat । saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saddharmaṃ samupāśraya ।। tato dharmānubhāvena buddhasyāpi prasādataḥ ।
nūnaṃ te satsutaḥ śīghram utpatsyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। yadi notpatsyate putras tava devavirodhataḥ । puṇyam utpatsyate nūnaṃ tena sadgatim āpnuyāt ।। ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ yānti te labhanti śubhāśayaṃ ।
ye viśuddhāśayā loke saddharmaṃ te śṛṇvanti hi ।। ye saddharmānuśṛṇvan to bodhicittaṃ labhanti te । pralabdhabodhicittā ye te caranti guṇārthinaḥ ।। guṇakāmāś ca ye loke te bhajanti jinātmajān ।
bodhisatvānubhāvena bodhicaryāṃ samāpnuyuḥ ।। bodhicaryāratā ye ca na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ । sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā saukhyāvatīm avāpnuyuḥ ।। evaṃ matvā jinaṃ smṛtvā saddharmaṃ samupāśrayeḥ ।
tatas te saṃbhaved bhadram ihāmutrāpi sarvataḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā gṛhastho asau anumoditaḥ । tatheti pratisaṃśrutya saṃbuddhaṃ smartum aichata ।। tato gṛhapatir nityaṃ sadāraḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ ।
saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā vaṃśam evam ayācata ।। namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tan māṃ karuṇāya dṛṣṭyā draṣṭum arhasi sarvathā ।। bhavān eva hi jagannāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthadaḥ । tvayā mahyaṃ hitārthāya satputraṃ dātum arhasi ।।
ity evaṃ sa gṛhī sādhuḥ putrābhilaṣitaḥ sadā । sabhāryyaḥ sugataṃ smṛtvā tathā nityaṃ samutsukaḥ ।। tadaiva samaye kaścid devaputro divaś cyutaḥ । sa saṃbuddhānubhāvena tadbhāryāgarbham āviśat ।।
tataḥ svāpannasatvābhūt sā bhāryā gṛhiṇaḥ satī । dohadalakṣaṇopetā kṛśāṅgī bhāvinī kramāt ।। pravṛddhagarbhā sā dṛṣṭvā svayaṃ ca garbham ādarāt । dakṣapārśvagataṃ satvaṃ matvā caivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
nūnaṃ me jāyate garbhe satvo buddhānubhāvataḥ । yad ayaṃ dakṣiṇe vartti tena putro bhavet khalu ।। iti niścitya sā nārī putrotpatyāśayā mudā । svasvāmino pure sthitvā rahasyaivaṃ nyavedayat ।।
dṛṣṭyāryyaputra varddhasva yad ahaṃ garbhiṇī bhave । nūnam ayaṃ bhavet putro yat sthito dakṣiṇodare ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ pramoditaḥ । daksiṇaṃ vāhum unnamya nandann evam udānayat ।।
cirābhilaṣitaṃ putramukhaṃ paśyeyaṃ sāṃprataṃ । jātaḥ syān nāmajātā me kulavaṃśasthitir bhavet ।। kṛtyāni ca prakurvīta bibhṛyād bharaṇaṃ prati । nūnaṃ buddhānubhāvena satputro api bhaviṣyati ।।
yad asmākaṃ kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ karma dānādikaṃ śubhaṃ । etat puṇyānubhāvena bhavet kuśalam etayoḥ ।। tatas tena sadā bharttā saha saṃmodacāriṇī । pathyāhāropacāraiś ca varddhito sukhacāriṇī ।।
tataḥ sā samaye sūta putraṃ divyātisuṃdaraṃ । darśanīyaṃ susaumyāṅgaṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ ।। sarvāṅgalakṣaṇopetaṃ sadīnārakaradvayaṃ । sarvasatvamanāpīśam abhirūpaṃ subhadrikaṃ ।।
tataḥ sā jananī tasya vālakasya karadvayaṃ । dīnārāṃkitam ālokya saharṣaṃ vismitābhavat ।। tato asau janakaś cāpi jātaṃ putramahādbhutaṃ । sakhībhir veditaṃ śrutvā vismito draṣṭum āyayau ।। tataḥ prajāpatiḥ sāpi vismito svāmino agrataḥ ।
darśayitvā sutaṃ putraṃ śaṃkitaivaṃ nyavedayat ।। svāmiṃ paśya mahāścaryyam asya hemānvitau karau । tac chubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vā darśayitvā vicāraya ।। iti bhāryyoditaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā taṃ vālakaṃ ciraṃ ।
dīnāraṃ bhujayoḥ paśyaṃ tasthau savismayānvitaḥ ।। tatas tasya gṛhastho asau nimittaṃ jñātum ādarāt । naimittikaṃ samāhūya dārakaṃ tam adarśayat ।। bhavanto dṛśyatām asya dārakasya karadvayaṃ ।
tan nimittaṃ parijñāya tat phalaṃ vaktum arhatha ।। ity ukte tena te sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ śubhaṃ । dīnāre bhujayoś cāpi parijñāyaivam abravīt ।। sādho gṛhapate hy asya dārakasya karadvayaṃ ।
suvarṇalakṣaṇopetaṃ tat te bhadraṃ bhavet khalu ।। tavāyaṃ dārako dātā maheśākhyo bhavet kila । svahastaṃ saṃprasāryyaiva hemavṛṣṭiṃ kariṣyati ।। apanīya svayaṃ hastād idaṃ dīnāram arpayet ।
apanīte punar anyat prādur bhavet tato adhikaṃ ।। ity evaṃ taiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā saṃharṣito gṛhī । tato jātimahaṃ kṛtvā jñātīn evam abhāṣata ।। bhavanto dārakasyāsya śubhākṣarasamanvitaṃ ।
nāmadheyaṃ yathāyogyaṃ kriyatāṃ saṃprasiddhitaṃ ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayas tathā । dṛṣṭvā tasya nimittāni saṃmatenaivam abruvan ।। yasmād dhastadvayo apy asya hiraṇyenopalakṣitaṃ ।
tan nāmnā prasiddho astu hiraṇyapāṇir ity ayaṃ ।। evaṃ jñātisamudiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau sa gṛhādhipaḥ । tatheti tasya putrasya cakre nāmavyavasthitaṃ ।। tato hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa dārakaḥ pratipālane ।
aṣṭāsu yo api dhātrīṣu tena pitrā samarpitaḥ ।। tābhiḥ prapālyamāno asau pathyapuṣṭopacāraṇaiḥ । varddhito abhūt kramād āśu hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ ।। tathā kramāt pravṛddho asau hiraṇyapāṇir ātmavit ।
śrāddho bhadrāśayo dhīmān svaparārthahitārthikaḥ ।। tataḥ sa śikṣituṃ vidyāḥ sadguruṃ samupāśrayat । kramāt teṣāṃ prasādāc ca vidyāpāraṃ yayau laghuḥ ।। tato asau dārako vidvān dātā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ ।
svahastaṃ saṃprasāryyaiva dadau dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ ।। gurubhyo brāhmaṇebhyaś ca yācakebhyaḥ sa dārakaḥ । svahastaṃ saṃprasāryyaiva dadau hemaṃ yathepsitaṃ ।। tathā tad dānam ākarṇya śravaṇabrāhmaṇādayaḥ ।
arthino dhanalubdhāś ca saṃpratīyuḥ samaṃtataḥ ।। tathā taṃ samupetyaivaṃ sarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatāḥ । vālāvṛddhādayo dīnā yayācire yathepsitaṃ ।। tadā hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa dṛṣṭvaitān arthino mudā ।
sarvopakaraṇaiś cāpi sarvāṃs tān samatoṣayat ।। tatas te yācakāḥ sarve tenaiva paritarpitāḥ । yathechayā sukhaṃ bhuktvā pracerur dharmamānasā ।। tathā vīthigataś caivaṃ hastadvayaṃ prasārya saḥ ।
hemarāśiṃ samutthāpya sarvebhyaḥ pradadau mudā ।। tathā sarve api te lokā dhanāḍhyāḥ sukhino abhavan । naiko abhūt kṛpano duḥkhī no api kaścid daridritaḥ ।। sarve api dhaninaḥ prāḍhyā dātāro bhogino abhavan ।
satyadharmānuraktāś ca saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ ।। tadā tasyaiva tat kīrttiḥ sarvatra bhuvaneṣv api । lokair udgīryamāno asau prasasāra samaṃtataḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇo lobhī mātsaryyaprahatāśayaḥ ।
tad yaśaḥ pratilabdhaṃ sa manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। yad asya bhujayor hema cintāmaṇisamaṃ khalu । tenāyaṃ bhavate śrīmān prārthitārthādhikapradaḥ ।। yac cāyaṃ dārakaḥ śrāddhaḥ prārthanāsaṃpradāyakaḥ ।
tad ahaṃ prārthanāṃ kṛtvā pratigṛhṇīya tat maṇiṃ ।। ity asau manasā dhyatvā lobhākṛṣṭo tvarānvitaḥ । taṃ hiraṇyabhujaṃ pretya tad dīnāraṃ samayācata ।। jayo astu te sadā sādho dīrghāyuś ca sumaṃgalaṃ । tathaiva tvaṃ sadā bhūyā arthināṃ kalpapādapaḥ ।।
tvatkīrttyā samāhūtaḥ prāgato asmi yad āśayā । tadarthaṃ pūrayitvā me cittaṃ harṣaya sarvataḥ ।। ity evaṃ prārthite tena vipreṇābhipragalbhinā । dṛṣṭvā hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa taṃ vipraṃ pratyabhāṣata ।।
sādhu vipra prasīda tvaṃ yadarthaṃ samupāgataḥ । tadarthaṃ saṃpradatvādya harṣayiṣyāmi te manaḥ ।। tac chaṃkā mā kṛthā hy atra yad yat te hṛdi rocate । tat tan nūnaṃ pradāsye te tad vadasva yad īhitaṃ ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā vipro asau saṃpraharṣitaḥ । svastīty āśīrvaco datvā tad dīnāram ayācata ।। sādho hiraṇyapāṇe yat tava hastasamudbhavaṃ । tad dīnāraṃ pradatvā me cittaṃ saṃharṣayārthadaḥ ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tat pitāsau suvismitaḥ । savandhujñātimitras taṃ putram evam abhāṣata ।। śṛṇu putra mayā proktaṃ tavaiva hitakāraṇaṃ । yadi te svāminī prītis tat karttavyaṃ hi sarvathā ।।
tvaṃ hi putra mayā labdhaḥ saṃbuddhasyānubhāvataḥ । tat saṃbuddhaśāsane kāryyam eva dātu samarhasi ।। yac cedan bhujayor jātaṃ dīnāraṃ maṇisaṃnibhaṃ । tad api sugatasyaiva prabhāvān manyatāṃ khalu ।।
yac cedaṃ te karodbhūtaṃ jīvitaṃ sahajendriyaṃ । tat svakarāt samuddhṛtya kathaṃ dadyā dvijātaye ।। yadīdaṃ dāsyate hastāt samuddhṛtya valād api । tadā te jīvitaṃ vāpi sahānena vrajaṃ khalu ।।
tasmād evaṃ parijñāya yadi te jīvita priyaṃ । tad evaṃ sahajaṃ hema mā pradāhi dvijātaye ।। tad anyad dīyatāṃ tasmai yad yad vastu samīchitaṃ । idaṃ tu sarvathānyasmai dātavyaṃ naiva yatnataḥ ।।
yenaiva tvaṃ maheśākhyo sarvārthiprārthitārthadaḥ । tena yadā paribhraṣṭas tadā kiṃ tena manyase ।। yenāpi ca tvayā sarve yācakāḥ saṃpratarpitāḥ । tac cintāmaṇisāmānyaṃ kathaṃ dātuṃ samichasi ।। yat tvayā sukṛtaṃ karma prakṛtvā puṇyam ācitaṃ ।
nūnaṃ tasya vipākatvaṃ bhuṃjayos te pratiṣṭhitaṃ ।। tasmād idaṃ mahāratnaṃ kasmiñcin mā pradīyatāṃ । datvā tv idaṃ mahāratnaṃ kim anyal labdham ichasi ।। yadi tv idaṃ mahāratnaṃ dātum evaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ।
saṃpradehi jinendrāya tat puṇyam akṣayaṃ vahuṃ ।। puṇyena labhyate janma śuddhavamṣe mahatkule । puṇyena dīyate kīrttiṃ nirvṛtiṃ ca samāpnuyāt ।। yadi puṇye asti te vāṃchā tad buddhaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
dehi buddhānuśāsinyā tad dānaṃ hi mahatphalaṃ ।। tato nityaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā kṛtvā saṃbodhisādhanaṃ । kramād bodhicariṃ prāpte nirvṛtiṃ vā samāpnuyāḥ ।। iti pitrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau hemabhṛt sudhīḥ ।
tatheti niścayaṃ kṛtvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। satyaṃ tāta tvayādiṣṭaṃ tat sarvaṃ hitam eva me । tasmāt tathā cariṣyāmi tvadājñāṃ śirasā vahan ।। kiṃ tu satyaṃ mayā proktām idaṃ dātuṃ dvijātaye ।
tat katham anyathā kṛtvā puṇyam eva samāpnuyāt ।। tat satyaṃ pūraṇe tāta pradadyāmi mamātmanaḥ । atha na dāsyate hy atra kiyat kālaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।। yad idaṃ bhujayor hemaṃ mamātmasahasaṃbhavaṃ ।
tathaivaṃ sahajīvena vinakṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। yathedaṃ tu mahāratnaṃ mama devasamudbhavaṃ । tathaivaṃ saṃpradatvāsmai punaḥ prāpsyāmi te adhikaṃ ।। yathā buddhānubhāyena saṃjātaṃ karayor idaṃ ।
tathā satyānubhāvena punar anyaj janiṣyate ।। dharmeṇa tuṣyate buddho mūlaṃ dharmasya satyavāk । tat satyapāraṇārthena dāsyāmy aham idaṃ maṇiṃ ।। satyaṃ vinā na phullante puṇyāni prakṛtāny api ।
mlānibhūtāni naśyante śasyānīvāmṛtaṃ vinā ।। satyena varddhate dharmaṃ dharmeṇa pālyate naraḥ । dharmiṣṭhaḥ sadgatiṃ yāti tasmāt satyaṃ mahadvalī ।। tasmāt satyavalenātra yaśodharmārthalabdhaye ।
sarvathāsmai pradāsyāmi mā kṛthās taṃ nivāraṇaṃ ।। iti putravacaḥ śrutvā pitā sa vismayānvitaḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā tasthau tūṣṇī vilokayan ।। tato hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa matvā pitrādhivāsitaṃ ।
tad dīnāraṃ sahasotkṛtya viprāya pradadau mudā ।। tat pradattam asau vipraḥ pratigṛhya pramoditaḥ । datvāśīrvacanaṃ tasmai svagṛhaṃ sahasā yayau ।। tataś cānantaraṃ tasya bhuje anyat tadguṇādhikaṃ ।
dīnāraṃ divyaratnābhaiḥ prādurāsīn mahādbhutaṃ ।। tad dattānaṃtarodbhūtaṃ dīnāraṃ tadguṇādhikaṃ । dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca sarve te lokā āśu suvismitāḥ ।। tato hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa evaṃ lokān praharṣayan ।
saṃbuddhaśāsane dātuṃ jetavanam upācarat ।। tatra bhikṣūn yatīn dṛṣṭvā saddharmacaraṇotsukaḥ । saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ draṣṭuṃ vihāraṃ samupāviśat ।। tatrāsau bhagavantaṃ tam adrākṣīt samitisthitaṃ ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṃḍitaṃ ।। vyāmaprabhāsam ujvālaṃ sahasreṇādhikaprabhaṃ । śānteṃdriyaṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ saumyarūpaṃ manoharaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvāsau suprasannātmā sahasā samupāgataḥ ।
natvā pādau munes tasya purastāt samupāśrayan ।। tatrāsau bhagavān tasya dṛṣṭvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। taṃ dharmaṃ sugatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau saṃpramoditaḥ ।
ānaṃdaṃ samupāśritya praṇamyaivaṃ vyajijñapat ।। bhadanta dātum ichāmi saṃghebhyo bhojanaṃ khalu । tad ājñāṃ dehi me śāsta yadi te asti kṛpā mayi ।। iti vijñāpite tena hiraṇyapāṇinā mudā ।
sa ānaṃdaḥ samālokya dārakaṃ taṃ samādiśat ।। sādhu vatsa mahābhāgyād bhadram ālocitaṃ tvayā । yady atra dāsyate bhojyaṃ kārṣāpaṇaṃ pradīyatāṃ ।। evaṃkṛte tu te vatsa maṃgalaṃ sarvadā bhavet ।
ataś ca durgatiṃ hitvā sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ ।। ity ānaṃdasamādiṣṭe dārako asau pramoditaḥ । svayaṃ hastau prasāryyaiva hemarāśiṃ vyadhāt punaḥ ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismitāḥ saṃpraharṣitāḥ । taddravyaiḥ sādhayāmāsa bhojyāni surasāni ca ।।
tataḥ sa dārako bhojyais taiḥ praṇītasusādhitaiḥ । saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ sarvasāṃghikaṃ samatoṣayat ।। tato asau bhojanānte ca saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ kramāt । sarvasaṃghaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ punas tasthau kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।।
tataḥ śrībhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasyāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । āryyasatyaṃ samāyuktaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tac chrutvā hemapāṇiḥ sa satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ । prabhitvā jñānavajreṇa viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ ।।
śrotāpattiphalaṃ prāpto dṛṣṭasatyo abhavat tataḥ । saṃbuddhasagaṇaṃ natvā svagehaṃ harṣito yayau ।। tatra sarvaṃ sa tadvṛttaṃ pitror ākhyāya harṣitaḥ । pravrajyācaraṇānujñāṃ pitarau pratyayācata ।।
cittaṃ me rocate tāta pravrajyāvratasādhane । tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me hitaṃ mayi yadīcchatha ।। iti putroditaṃ śrutvā svātmajaṃ sa pitāvadat । mā kṛthā sahasā putra pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ ।।
pravrajyācaraṇe bhaikṣyaṃ duḥkhinām eva tadvrataṃ । tvaṃ vṛddhimān mahādātā tat pravrajyāṃ kutaś careḥ ।। kiṃ vāpyate vivāhas tvaṃ daharaś ca kumārikaḥ । pravrajyā duṣkaraṃ sthānaṃ tat kathaṃ pracaret sutaḥ ।।
tat tāvat tvaṃ yuvā putra vivāhitvā kulastriyaṃ । bhuktvā saukhyaṃ yathākāmaṃ gṛhe dharmaṃ samācara ।। tato vaṃśaṃ samutpādya kulasthitiprasiddhaye । kuladharmaṃ pratisthāpya tataḥ pravraja vārddhikaḥ ।।
yadā vṛddho daridraś ca pravrajyāṃ hi tadā caret । yāvad yuvā samṛddhaś ca tāvat tvaṃ pravraja kathaṃ ।। saṃpattiḥ kṣaṇayauvanyam etan māravaladhruvaṃ । tadetadā kathaṃ putra pravrajyāvratam ācareḥ ।।
ity etad duṣkaraṃ matvā pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ । sarvathā tvaṃ vinirvārya kuladharmaṃ samācara ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ imu putra bhaved dhruvaṃ । yaśodharmasukhānvetya sadgatiṃ cāpy avāpnuyāḥ ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā dārako asau viśaṃkitaḥ ।
bodhayan pitaraṃ dharme punar evam abhāṣata ।। satyam eva tathā tāta yad etad bhāṣyate tvayā । tathāpi śrūyatāṃ tāta yad abhiprāyakaṃ mama ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi bhaṃguraṃ ।
kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca kṣaṇasaṃpad ghanopamaṃ ।। evaṃ paśyan ahaṃ tāta saṃsārabhoganispṛhaḥ । pravrajyāvratam āśritya prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ ।। api ca dullabhaṃ janma mānuṣaṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ ।
sarveṣām api jantūnāṃ maraṇaṃ sarvathā dhruvaṃ ।। mānuṣye labhyamāne tu kuto dharmānubhāvanā । vinā dharmānubhāvena kathaṃ sadgatim āpnuyāt ।। saṃbuddho api sasaṃgho ayaṃ sthāsyati na sadeha ca ।
anyatrāpi vrajen nūnaṃ nirvṛtiṃ vā gamiṣyati ।। saṃbuddhe nirvṛtiṃ yāte saddharmo api vinakṣyate । saddharmāntargate loke mlechadharmavalī bhavet ।। mlechadharmavalīkrānte sarvatra bhūmimaṃḍale ।
sarvalokāś ca kāmāṃdhā bhaveyuḥ kleśamāninaḥ ।। tada dharmānusaṃvṛttau matiḥ kasyāpi no caret । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhartuṃ kaḥ samartho bhaviṣyati ।। naiva saṃyujyate cittaṃ pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ vinā ।
aviśodhitacittātmā na yāyāt paramāṃ gatiṃ ।। tac cittaye viśuddhyarthaṃ nirvāṇapadalabdhaye । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dharttuṃ ichāmi tāta sāṃprataṃ ।। tad yadi me hitaṃ draṣṭum ichasi tāta sarvadā ।
tad anujñāṃ samādātum arhasi mātra cāraye ।। iti puroditaṃ śrutvā pitā sa paribodhitaḥ । tathety anumataṃ kṛtvābhavat tūṣṇīvyavasthitaḥ ।। tadā tajjananī cāsau dṛṣṭvā taṃ sutam ātmajaṃ ।
snehād aśru vimocantī nivārayitum abravīt ।। hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihāya kva yāsyase । mā putra sahasā gacha kiṃcit kālaṃ vinodaya ।। yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ tāta tāvan mā gāḥ kuhāpi ca । mṛtāyāṃ mayi bho putra tadā vrajasva vāṃchite ।।
acireṇaiva māṃ mṛtyur grahīṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । tāvad eva gṛhe sthitvā dānaṃ kurvan sukhaṃ vasa ।। iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā putro asau parimoditaḥ । natvā tāṃ jananīm evaṃ bodhayitum abhāṣata ।।
yat tvayāmve rudanty evaṃ mṛtyunāma prakīrtitaṃ । tena me coditaṃ cittaṃ pravrajyāvratasādhane ।। dhruvaṃ janmavatāṃ mṛtyur mṛtānāṃ janma ca dhruvaṃ । parivarttini saṃsāre mṛtaḥ ko hi na jāyate ।।
dharmiṣṭho vīryāvāṃś cāpi maraṇaṃ yāti sarvataḥ । pāpiṣṭho nighnitaś cāpi maraṇaṃ yāti sarvataḥ ।। dharmiṣṭhaḥ satsukhaṃ bhuktvā mṛto yāty eva sadgatiṃ । pāpiṣṭho duḥkhatāṃ bhuktvā mṛto gachati durgatiṃ ।।
yadā saṃtyajate jantuḥ saṃsāraprāṇavāyunā । tadā saṃtyajyate sarvair vaṃdhumitrajanair api ।। tadā na vidyate ko api hitakārī sahānugaḥ । dharma ekaḥ sahāyaḥ syāt sarvatrāpi hitārthakṛt ।।
tasmāt mātaḥ prayatnena karttavyaṃ dharmam ādarāt । dharmeṇa rakṣyate sarva ihāmutra sahāpi hi ।। dharmeṇaivābhipālyante vālavṛddhāturādayaḥ । dharmeṇa sudhṛtāḥ satvā nimagnā duḥkhasāgare ।।
dharmeṇa jīyate duṣṭo dharmeṇa jīyate kaliḥ । dharmeṇa jīyate rāgo mṛtyur dharmeṇa jīyate ।। dharmeṇa sukule janma lakṣmī dharmeṇa sthīyate । vidyāyaśo arthamoksāś ca prāpyante dharmataḥ khalu ।।
dharmaṃ tu saugataṃ kāryaṃ sarvalokahitaṃkaraṃ । sugatasyāpi dharmeṣu pravrajyādharmam uttamaṃ ।। yam āśritya mahāsatvā jitvā kleśagaṇān laghuḥ । sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya vrajanti nirvṛtiṃ parāṃ ।।
iti matvā hi te sarve bhikṣavo bhavanispṛhāḥ । pravrajyāvratam āśritya bhavanti brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। tathātrāhaṃ samichāmi pravrajyāvratam uttamaṃ । tad anujñāṃ pradatvā me nātra kāryo viṣāditaḥ ।।
yadi na dīyate anujñā tad api no viyogataḥ । akasmān mṛtyunā ghrāya grasiṣyati puro hi naḥ ।। tadā kiṃ te kariṣyāmi mamāpi kiṃ kariṣyasi । kṛtvānuśocanāṃ caiva yāsyāmo maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
iti mātaḥ parijñāya tad anujñāṃ pradehi me । viṣādaṃ mā kṛthā atra prasādīnī bhavet prabhu ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityam ihāmutrāpi saṃbhavet । ahaṃ ca saugataṃ dharmaṃ dhṛtvā nirvṛtim āpnuyāṃ ।।
iti putroditaṃ śrutvā mātāsau paribodhitā । tathānumodanāṃ kṛtvā tasthau tūṣṇīvyavasthitān ।। atha hiraṇyapāṇiḥ saḥ pitror matvābhisaṃmataṃ । tayoś ca caraṇe natvā sahasā niryayau gṛhāt ।।
tatra jñātigaṇāṃś cāsau vandhumitrasuhṛjjanān । kṛpaṇātithisaṃghādiṃ vāṃchitārthair atoṣayat ।। tato asau vāṃdhavān sarvān saṃtarpya paribodhayan । āśu jetavanaṃ gatvā vihāraṃ samupāviśat ।।
tatrāsau sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। namas te bhagavac chāsta bhavatāṃ caraṇaṃ vraje । tat pravrajyāvrataṃ datvā brahmacaryaṃ pradehi me ।।
iti tenārthite asau śrībhagavān tam abhāṣata । ehi bhikṣo kumāra tvaṃ brahmacaryaṃ carehi sa ।। iti prokto munīndro asau pāṇinā tac chiraḥ spṛśan । samyakpravājayitvāśu svasaṃghe taṃ samagrahīt ।।
ehīti proktamātre api jinendreṇa sa muṇḍitaḥ । khikkhirīpātrahastābhūc lcīvaraprāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ ।। tataḥ śikṣāsu śikṣitvā prāpyopasaṃpado api ca । vyāyacchad ghaṭamānaś ca samādhiṣu samāhitaḥ ।।
tad idaṃ paṃcagaṃdaṃ ca bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ । viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatiś cāpi vighāṭinī ।। bhiṃdan sarvam avidyāṅgaṃ prāpya vidyāḥ śubhaṃkarāḥ । pratisaṃvidguṇaprāpto jitakleśagaṇo yatiḥ ।।
sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya vītarāgo jitendriyaḥ । samaloṣṭasuvarṇaś ca vāsīcaṃdanasaṃnibhaḥ ।। ākāśasamacittaś ca nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ । saṃsārabhogyasatkāralābhalobhasunispṛhaḥ ।।
paṃcābhijñapadaprāpto caturbrahmavihārikaṃ । sadevāsuramartyānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ ।। pūjyo mānyo abhivaṃdyaś ca babhūva sa hiraṇyabhṛt । tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ yatiṃ ।।
vismitāḥ śrīghanaṃ natvā paprachus tasya karmatāṃ । bhagavan kena dharmeṇa hiraṇyapāṇir ayaṃ sudhīḥ ।। sarvārthino hi saṃtarpya sākṣād arhan bhavaty api । iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān tān tathābravīt ।।
śrūyatāṃ bhikṣavaḥ sarvair yuṣmābhir vismitāśayaiḥ । anena yat kṛtaṃ karma tan mayā kathyate adhunā ।। purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo arhan munīśvaraḥ । sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā tathāgato vināyakaḥ ।।
sasāṃghiko jinendro asau vārāṇasīm upāśritaḥ । bodhicaryāṃ samādiśya kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat ।। sarvāṇi buddhakāryāṇi samāpya nirvṛtiṃ yayau । tadā rājā kṛkī nāma matvā taṃ nirvṛtiṃ gataṃ ।।
vidhivad agnisaṃskāraṃ kārayitvā mahārcanaiḥ । tatas taddhāturatnāni garbha āropya sādarāt ।। hemaratnamayaṃ stūpaṃ kārayām āsa sa prabhuḥ । tat susiddhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sadvidhānair mahotsavaiḥ ।।
mahaś cāpi tadā tatra sthāpayitvā bhajan nṛpaḥ । tasminn āropyamānāyāṃ yaṣṭyāṃ pūjāparigrahī ।। kintavo kaṃdaro nāma nidadhe rūpakadvayaṃ । tataḥ sa pādayor natvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tathā ।।
yan mayā śraddhayā bhaktyāropitaṃ rūpakadvayaṃ । yat puṇyaṃ ca vipākena jāyeyaṃ sukule sadā ।। karodbhavasuvarṇaiḥ saṃtarpayitvārthino janān । evaṃvidhaṃ ca śāstāram ārogya samupāśritaḥ ।।
etad dharmaṃ samāsādya prāpnuyāṃ paramāṃ gatiṃ । tena puṇyavipākena praṇidhānena bhūyasā ।। hiraṇyapāṇir ayaṃ dātā bhavaty arhaṃ sa sāṃprataṃ । evaṃ sarve api saṃsāre bhuṃjate karmajaṃ phalaṃ ।।
yenaivaṃ yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva bhuṃjyate phalaṃ । abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana ।। śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vāpi bhuktaṃ tu kṣīyate khalu । nāgnibhir dahyate karma klidyate nodakair api ।।
vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate nāpi bhūmiṣu kṣīyate na hi । anyathāpi bhaven naiva saṃsāre karmaṇo gatiḥ ।। śubhasya śubhataiva syāt kṛṣṇasya kṛṣṇataiva hi । miśrasya miśritaiva syād anyathā na sadā bhavet ।।
evaṃ matvātha saṃsāre caritavyaṃ sadā śubhaṃ । na praṇasyaṃti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api ।। sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu । ity asau bhagavān buddhaḥ satkarmadeśanāmataiḥ ।।
tarpayan sa kalāṃl lokān tato viśrāntam ādadhau । iti śāstroditaṃ śrutvā sarve te bhikṣusāṃghikāḥ ।। śubheṣv eva sadā nityaṃ saṃpraceruḥ samāhitaḥ । mahārāja tvayāpy evaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।।
bodhayitvā prajāñ caivaṃ sthāpanīyāḥ śubhe sadā । tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet khalu । kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya saṃbodhipadam āpuṇyāḥ ।। iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatīśvaraḥ ।
tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। śṛṇvanti ye śrāvayantīha yaś ca hiraṇyapāṇer avadānam etat । te kleśamuktāḥ sugatānubhaktāḥ prayānti nūnaṃ sugatālayeṣu ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā ।
upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā bhūyo apy evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā te guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā me vaktum arhasi ।। iti tena narendreṇa pṛṣṭo asau sugatāṃśajaḥ ।
upagupto mahābhijñas taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi tad anumodanāṃ kuru ।। puraikasamaye caivaṃ śrīghano asau tathāgataḥ ।
saṃbuddhaḥ sugataḥ śāstā sarvadharmānudeśakaḥ ।। śrāvastyāṃ vahir udyāne jetavane manorame । anāthapiṇḍadodyāne vihāre sugatāśrame ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ upāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ ।
bodhisatvair mahāsatvais tadanyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।। vyaharat sarvahitārthāya dharmāmṛtaṃ pravarṣayan । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ prayayur bodhikāminaḥ ।। lokapālā mahārājā svasvasainyajanaiḥ saha ।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇo janāḥ ।। amātyāḥ sādhavaḥ paurā dhaninaś ca mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca tathānye sarvajātikāḥ ।। sarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatya sarve te samupāgatāḥ ।
taṃ buddhaṃ sugataṃ nāthaṃ pūjayitvā samaṃtataḥ ।। parivṛtya purodhāya śakhyāviguṇakāmitāḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo tasthuḥ saddharmacaraṇotsukāḥ ।। athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokādhipādayaḥ । harṣitās te anumodanto vabhūvuḥ paribodhitāḥ ।। tadaiva samaye tasyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ purisaṃbhavaḥ ।
āsīd gṛhapatiḥ prāḍhyaḥ kuveravat samṛddhimān ।। śrāddho dātā mahābhogī sarvahitārthabhṛt । triratnasevako dhīmān suviśālaparigrahaḥ ।। saṃgṛhī vidhivad bhāryāṃ svakuladharmacāriṇī । pariṇītā yathākāmaṃ saṃrame paricārayan ।।
tasyāsau ramaṇī bhāryā saṃvṛttā garbhiṇī satī । asūta samaye putraṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ ।। sa ca jātismaro vālo jātamātraḥ svakau bhujau । saṃdṛṣṭvāliṃgya cuṃvitvā pariṣvajyaivam abravīt ।।
aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau । aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā ।। tenaivaṃ jātamātreṇa dṛṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ prabhāṣitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca sā mātā trāsitā vismitābhavat ।।
kim etad iti saṃtrastā dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ mudā । bharttāraṃ sahasāhūya agram enam adarśayat ।। tadāsau dārakaś cāpi dṛṣṭvā taṃ janakaṃ mudā । hastau dṛṣṭvā tathāliṃgya cuṃvayitvā caivam abravīt ।।
aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau । aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā ।। iti saṃdarśayaṃ hastāv evaṃ cāpy avadac chiśuḥ । dārako asau punaḥ supto nidrāṃ bheje yad ichayā ।।
tato asau janako apy etad dṛṣṭvā śrutvā pravismitaḥ । kiṃ etad iti sāśaṃkā jñātin āhūya cābravīt । bhavanto adya prajātaṃ me putraratnaṃ manoharaṃ । tan nimittaṃ nirīkṣyaitat satyaṃ me vaktum arhatha । iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayo mudā । tat putraṃ dārakaṃ draṣṭuṃ tat koṣṭhaṃ samupādiśat । tathāsau dārakaś caivaṃ tān dṛṣṭvā samupasthitān । bhujau paśyan pariṣvajya cuṃvitvaivam abhāṣata । aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā । bhavanto arhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadā cana । kharāṃ vācaṃ ca mārhatsu niścārayata sarvadā । evaṃ saṃdarśayaṃ hastau vacanaṃ saṃvadaṃ śiśuḥ । dārako asau punaḥ supto nidrāṃ bheje yad ichayā । etat te jñātayo dṛṣṭvā śrutvā sarve api vismitāḥ ।
kim etad iti bhāṣanto vabhūvuḥ parisaṃkitāḥ ।। tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve vijñāya tasya lakṣaṇaṃ । saṃmīlya tam upāmaṃtrya gṛhasthaḥ pratiharṣitaḥ ।। tasya jātimahaṃ kṛtvā punar evam avocata ।
bhadanto dārakasyāsya nāmadheyaṃ pramāṇataḥ ।। yathāyogyaprasiddhena karttum arhatha sāṃprataṃ । iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayas tataḥ ।। saṃmīlya saṃmataṃ kṛtvā taṃ gṛhasthaṃ samabruvan ।
yad ayaṃ te suto vālo jātamātraḥ svakau bhujau ।। paśyan āliṃgyā cuṃvitva mudā caivaṃ prabhāṣate । tad ayaṃ dārako nāmnā hastaka iti viśrutaḥ ।। bhavatu sarvalokeṣu suciraṃ cāpi jīvatu ।
tatheti pratinaṃditvā gṛhastho asau pramoditaḥ ।। tena nāmnā prasiddhena prathayām āsa taṃ sutaṃ । tato asau dārakas tena pitrā putrābhinaṃditaḥ । upanyastopadhātrīṣu dhāraṇapratipālane ।।
tatas tāsāṃ prayatnaiḥ sa pathyopacāraṇaiḥ kramāt । dine dine pravṛddho abhūd hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ ।। evaṃ sa hastakas tābhiḥ pālyamānaḥ pravarddhitaḥ । kumāraḥ sakhibhiḥ sārddhaṃ krīḍāsthānaṃ gato aramat ।।
tatra teṣāṃ sakhīnāṃ ca hastako asau puraḥsthitaḥ । hastāv āliṃgya saṃrakṣya cuṃvitvaivam abhāṣata ।। aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau । aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā ।।
bhavanto arhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadācana । kharāṃ vācaṃ ca mārhatsu niścārayata keṣu cit ।। iti saṃrakṣitau hastau tenaivaṃ ca prabhāṣitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā śrutvābhavan sarve sakhāyātīvavismitāḥ ।।
tataś ca janakenāsau lipiśālāniveśitaḥ । guruṃ samyag upāśritya vidyāpāraṃ yayau laghu ।। tatra teṣāṃ guruṇāṃ ca hastako asau puraḥsthitaḥ । hastau dṛṣṭvā samāliṃgya cuṃvitvā caivam abravīt ।।
aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau । aho labdhav imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā ।। bhavanto arhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadā cana । kharāṃ vācaṃ ca mārhatsu niścārayata keṣu cit ।।
iti dṛṣṭvā ca saṃśrutya sarve te guravo api ca । sarve śiṣya gaṇāś cāpi vabhūvur vismayānvitāḥ । yasmiṃś ca samaye tatra deśe bhayaupakrame । janakāyaḥ samudbhrānto agopāyat svasvabhāṇḍakaṃ । tadāsau hastako apy evaṃ samudbhrāntaḥ svakau bhujau । saṃbhujya gopayitvaivaṃ janakāyam abhāṣata । aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau । aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā । bhavanto arhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadā cana । kharāṃ vācaiva mārhatsu niścārayata keṣu cit । evaṃ hastau susaṃrakṣya tenaivaṃ ca prabhāṣitaṃ ।
dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca te sarve lokā āsan suvismitāḥ ।। tato asau hastako anyasmiṃ divase sakhibhiḥ saha । jetavanaṃ mahodyānaṃ jināśrame upāyayau ।। tatrādrākṣīt mahābuddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ sabhāsthitaṃ ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṃḍitaṃ ।। vyāmaprabhāsamuddīptaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ । śāntendriyaṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ saumyakāntaṃ manoharaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvāsau suprasannātmā sahasā samupāgataḥ ।
pādau tasya muner natvā dharmaṃ śrotuṃ puro aviśat ।। tato asau bhagavān tasya dṛṣṭvāśayaṃ viśodhitaṃ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। taṃ sugatoditaṃ dharmaṃ āryyasatyasamanvitaṃ ।
śrutvāsau hastako vijñaḥ satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ ।। saṃbhidya jñānavajreṇa viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ । śrotāpattiphalaṃ prāpto dṛṣṭasatyo abhavat tataḥ ।। saṃbuddhasugataṃ natvā svagehaṃ sahasā yayau ।।
tatraitat sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ pitror ājñāya harṣitaḥ । pravrajyāsādhane anujñāṃ pitarau pratyayācata ।। cittaṃ me rocate tāta pravrajyāvratasādhane । tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me hitaṃ mayi yadīchatha ।।
iti putroditaṃ śrutvātmajaṃ taṃ pitāvadat । mā kṛthāḥ sahasā putra pravrajyāsādhane manaḥ ।। pravrajyā duṣkaraṃ sthānaṃ tad anyadvratam ācara । pravrajyāgrahaṇaṃ vṛddhe daridrite suśobhite ।।
tvaṃ ca putra kumāro asi daharo atisukomalaḥ । kiṃcid duḥkhe anabhijñāya tat pravrajyāṃ careḥ kathaṃ ।। tad yāvad yauvanaṃ dehaṃ yāvat saṃpac ca te gṛhe । tāvad gehe sukhaṃ bhuktvā gṛhī dharmaṃ samācara ।।
yadā vṛddho daridro ca pravrajyāyāṃ tadā cara । yāvad yuvā samṛddhaś ca tāvat tvaṃ pravrajeḥ kathaṃ ।। saṃpattikṣaṇayauvanyaṃ etan mārasya gocaraṃ । tad etasmiṃ kathaṃ putra pravrajyāvratam ācareḥ ।। ity etad duṣkaraṃ matvā pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ ।
yatnenāpi vinivārya kuladharme samāśraya ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityam ihāmutrāpi sarvataḥ । yaśodharmasukhāny evaṃ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ ।। iti vākyaṃ pituḥ śrutvā hastako asau viśaṃkitaḥ ।
pitarau bodhayan dharme punar evam abhāṣata ।। satyam etat tathā tāta tvayaivaṃ satyam ucyate । atrāpi śrūyatāṃ tāta mamābhiprāyam ucyatāṃ ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi caṃcaraṃ ।
kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca saṃpac cāpi ghanopamā ।। evaṃ dṛṣṭvā ha tātāhaṃ saṃsārasukhaniḥspṛhaḥ । pravrajyāvratam ādhāya prāptum ichāmi sadgatiṃ ।। api ca janma mānuṣyaṃ dullabhaṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ ।
tatrāpi maraṇaṃ nityaṃ purataḥ sarvasaṃmukhaṃ ।। mānuṣyaṃ labhyamāne hi kuto dharmānucāritaṃ । vinā dharmānucāreṇa sadgatiṃ katham āpnuyāṃ ।। saṃbuddho api sadā nātra saṃsthāpyati sasāṃghikaḥ ।
ato anyatrāpi yāyād vā nirvṛtiṃ cāvrajet khalu ।। saṃbuddhe nirvṛtiṃ yāte saddharma lapsyate kutaḥ । saddharmāntargate loke māracaryyā samācaret ।। māracaryyāsamākrānte sarvatra bhuvaneṣv api ।
sarve satvāś ca kāmārttā bhaveyuḥ kleśabhāginaḥ ।। tadā dharmānucāreṣu buddhiḥ kasya kathaṃ caret । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ sthātuṃ kaḥ samartho bhavet tadā ।। na ca saṃśuddhyate cittaṃ pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ vinā ।
aviśodhitacitte hi naiva yāyāc chivāṃ gatiṃ ।। tac cittapariśuddhyarthaṃ nirvṛte ca yad āptaye । pravrajyāvratam ādātum ichāmi tāta sāṃprataṃ ।। yad atra yadi me tāta hitaṃ kartuṃ samichasi ।
pravrajyāsādhane anujñāṃ dātuṃ me prārhasi drutaṃ ।। iti putravacaḥ śrutva sa gṛhastho anubodhitaḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā tad anujñāṃ vyasṛjata ।। tac chrutvā jananī cāsau dṛṣṭvā taṃ putram ātmajaṃ । viyogaduḥkhasaṃkārtā rundanty evaṃ nyavārayat ।।
hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihāya kva yāsyasi । sahasā putra mā kārṣī pravrajyācaritaṃ manaḥ ।। yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ jīva tāvan mā pravrajātmaje । mṛtāyāṃ mayi putra tvaṃ pravrajasva yathechayā ।।
acireṇa hi me mṛtyur bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । tāvad eva gṛhe dharmaṃ kurvan bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa ।। iti mātur vacaḥ śrutvā putro asau paricoditaḥ । mātaraṃ tāṃ praṇatvaivaṃ bodhayitum abhāṣata ।।
yat tvayāmve rudanty evaṃ mṛtyunāmātra kīrttyate । tena me preritaṃ cittaṃ pravrajyāvratadhāraṇe ।। dhruvaṃ janmavatāṃ mṛtyuḥ saṃsāre parivarttinaḥ । jāto na mriyate ko hi mṛtaḥ kaś ca na jāyate ।।
gṛhastho dharmakṛc cāpi yāty evaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ । brahmacārī vanastho api yāty evaṃ maraṇaṃ khalu ।। gṛhastho bahubhir yatnaiḥ prakṛtvā dravyasādhanaṃ । kṛcchreṇa sādhayan dharmaṃ mṛto yāti surālayaṃ ।।
yāvad dharmaphalaṃ svarge tāvad bhuktvā sukhaṃ vaset । tato dharmaphale hīne svargāc cyuto yated adhaḥ ।। adholokeṣv avīcyādau narakeṣu bhramec ciraṃ । vividhāni ca duḥkhāni bhuktvā jīvaṃ ciraṃ vaset ।।
yāvan na jāyate tasya puṇyānumodanā matau । tāvat karmajaduḥkhāni prabhuktvā narake caret ।। yadā tu jāyate tasya triratnasmaraṇe matiḥ । tadā tatsmṛtipuṇyena dharme anumodyate matiḥ ।।
yadā puṇyānurāgeṇa saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ vrajet । tadā taṃ sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā dharmākaraiḥ parispṛśet ।। sugate dṛkprabhāspṛṣṭe pāpaduḥkhair vimocitaḥ । narakebhyaḥ samuttīrya prayāyāt sugatālayaṃ ।।
tatrāpi yadi dharmeṣu caran nityam ataṃdritaḥ । kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya prayāyāt paramāṃ gatiṃ ।। evaṃ māta gṛhastho hi kṛtvāpi dharmam ādarāt । sukhaduḥkhāni saṃbhuktvā saṃsāre carate bhraman ।। kathaṃ cit sucireṇaivaṃ sugatasya prasādataḥ ।
bhavacārakanirmuktaṃ prayāyāt paramāṃ gatiṃ ।। pravrajyārhatpadaṃ prāpya prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ । tan mamātra tvayā māta naiva kāryā nivāraṇā ।। yadi puṇye asti te vāṃchā tad anujñāśu dīyatāṃ ।
yadi na dīyate anujñā tad api nau viyogatā ।। akasmāt mṛtyur āgatya bhaviṣyati purāpi nau । tadā te kiṃ kariṣyāmi kiṃ mamāpi kariṣyasi ।। sadānuśocanām eva kṛtvā jīvaṃ tyajevahi ।
iti mātar viditvā tvaṃ tadanujñāṃ pradehi me ।। vighnatāṃ mā kṛthā hy atra dharme bhavānumodinī । tathā cec chubhatā nityam ihāmutrāpi te bhavet ।। ahaṃ ca saugatiṃ caryāṃ kṛtvā yāsyāmi nirvṛtīṃ ।
iti putroditaṃ śrutvā matāsau paribodhitā ।। tathānumodanāṃ kṛtvābhavat tūṣṇīvyavasthitā ।। athāsau hastako vijñaḥ pitror matvābhisaṃmataṃ । tayoḥ pādān praṇatvaivaṃ sahasā niryayau gṛhāt ।।
tato jñātigaṇān sarvān vandhumitrasuhṛjjanān । sarvān atithivargāṃś ca vāṃchitārthaiḥ pratoṣayan ।। santarpya bodhayitvā ca sahasā saṃpraharṣitaḥ । jetavanaṃ pragatvā sa vihāraṃ samupāviśat ।।
tatrasthaṃ sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā samupāyataḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ dehi cariṣye brahmasaṃvaraṃ ।।
iti tenārthite buddho bhagavān tam abhāṣata । ehi bhikṣo kumārātra cara brahmavrataṃ varaṃ ।। ity ādiśya munīndro asau pāṇinā tac chiraḥ spṛśan । samyak pravrājayitvāśu svasaṃghe taṃ samagrahīt ।।
ehīty ādiṣṭamātre api munīndreṇa sa hastakaḥ । muṇḍitaḥ khiṣkhirīpātrahasto abhūc cīvarāvṛtaḥ ।। kramāc chikṣā samāsādya prāpyopasaṃpado api ca । vyāyaccha ghaṭamānaś ca samādhiṣu samāhitaḥ ।।
tad idaṃ paṃcagaṃḍaṃ ca bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ । viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatiś cāpi vighātinī ।। bhindan sarvam avidyāṅgaṃ prāpya vidyāgaṇāḥ śivāḥ । pratisaṃvidguṇāḥ prāpya jitvā kleśagaṇāṃ yatiḥ ।। sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāptaḥ vītarāgo jiteṃdriyaḥ ।
samaloṣṭahiraṇyaś ca vāsīcaṃdanasaṃnibhaḥ ।। ākāśasamacittāṃgo nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ । saṃsārabhogyasatkāralābhalobhaparāṅmukhaḥ ।। paṃcābhijñāpadaprāptaś caturbrahmavihārakaḥ ।
sadevāsuramartyānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ ।। pūjyo mānyo abhivaṃdyo abhūd dhastako arhaṃ yatiḥ sudhīḥ । sahasā kleśagaṇāñ jitvā sākṣād arhan bhavaty api ।। tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ yatiṃ ।
vismitāḥ śrīghanaṃ natvā paprachus tasya karmatāṃ ।। tad adya bhagavac chāstaḥ sarvasatvānubodhaye । yad anena kṛtaṃ karma tat samādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti te bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tān svaśiṣyān yatīn bhikṣūn samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ sarve yūyaṃ hi vismayānvitāḥ । yad anena kṛtaṃ karma tan mayā vaḥ pracakṣyatāṃ ।। purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo nāma sarvavit ।
ssarvatraidhātukādhīśaḥ sarvavidyādhipo jinaḥ ।। dharmarājo jagacchāstā tathāgato vināyakaḥ । sarvadharmānusaṃbharttā saṃbodhisaṃprakāśitaḥ ।। sasāṃghiko munīndro asau vārāṇasīm upāśritaḥ ।
sarvasatvahitārthena tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat ।। tasya saddharmarājasya kāśyapasya jagadguroḥ । śāsane dvau yatī bhikṣū saṃśītikau vabhūvatuḥ ।। tayor eko mahādhīro vinīto arhaṃ vahuśrutaḥ ।
dvitīyo alpaśrutaḥ bhikṣuḥ pṛthagjanasamānikaḥ ।। yo asāv arhan mahāvijño vahuśruto vicakṣaṇaḥ । sa jñāto arhan mahāpuṇyaḥ sarvalokaiḥ prapūjitaḥ ।। yo abhūc cālpaśruto bhikṣuḥ saṃśītikaḥ pṛthagjanaḥ ।
sa kena cit pūjito naivaṃ yathā so arhaṃ yatiḥ sudhīḥ ।। yadā so arhan mahābhijño yatra yatra nimaṃtritaḥ । tenaiva sarvataḥ paścācchramanena sahācarat ।। tathānyasmin dine so arhaṃ dātrānyena nimaṃtritaḥ । gantukāmas tadā tatra paścācchramaṇam aicchata ।।
tad āgamanam anviṣya naiva pratyalabhat kvacit । tatas taddarśanābhāvād anyam āhūya bhikṣukaṃ ।। taṃ paścācchramaṇaṃ kṛtvā dātur gṛham upācarat । tadanantaram evāsau tatrāśrame upāgataḥ ।।
tam arhantam apaśyan sa tasthau tūṣṇī nirāśitaḥ । tathaivaṃ taṃ niṣīdantaṃ dṛṣṭvā te bhikṣavo narāḥ ।। tasyauddhatyamanaḥ kartum evam ūcuḥ parasparaṃ । bhadanta paśyatādyāyaṃ tenāhato na nīyate ।।
anyo adya nīyate paścācchramaṇaḥ kena hetunā । iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ proktaṃ śrutvāsau pratibheditaḥ । tasyārhato antike cittaṃ praduṣyābhyaśapat tathā ।। yad adya māṃ parityajya samāhūyānyato harāt ।
gachata bhojanaṃ bhoktuṃ tad ahasto bhavatv asau ।। tadāsau bhojanaṃ bhuktvā tenaivaṃ bhikṣuṇā saha । svāśramaṃ samupāyātas tam adrākṣīd ruṣākulaṃ ।। ity evaṃ śapitaṃ vāpi matvā so arhaṃ mahāmatiḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā tūṣṇībhūtvā vyaciṃtayat ।। aho ayaṃ mahāmūḍha īdṛg mayi prabhāṣate । etat karmaphalaṃ ghoraṃ kathaṃ bhokṣyati nārake ।। yad ayaṃ mama doṣeṇa krodhenaivaṃ khalīkṛtaḥ ।
tad etat karmavaipākyaṃ mayaiva paripācyatāṃ ।। ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā sa mahārhaṃ kṛpānidhiḥ । tatpāpapariśuddhyarthaṃ samādhiṃ vidadhe ciraṃ ।। tataḥ so apy ayatir bhikṣur dṛṣṭvā taṃ dhyānasaṃsthitaṃ ।
paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptes tatpādapraṇato avadat ।। bhadanta yan mayā rauṣyāt krodhābhibhūtacetasā । procitaṃ pātakaṃ ghoraṃ tad bhavān kṣantum arhati ।। yan mayā duṣṭacittena bhavato apy upabhāṣyate । tadatyayaṃ bhavāñ chāstaḥ pratihartuṃ samarhati ।।
adyāgreṇa sadā cāpi bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tan me yad aparādhatvaṃ tat sarvaṃ kṣantum arhati ।। punar naitat kariṣye ahaṃ akarttavyaṃ yady atra hi । avaktavyaṃ ca yat kiṃ cin na tad vakṣyāmi sarvathā ।।
abhāvyaṃ cāpi yat kiṃcid bhāvayiṣye na tat punaḥ । yad eva taṃ prakarttavyaṃ tad eva hi karomy ahaṃ ।। vaktavyam eva vakṣye ahaṃ bhāvyam eva prabhāvaye । etat sarvaṃ samāsena samādeṣṭuṃ samarhati ।।
bhavadājñāṃ śirodhṛtvā satyam evaṃ caret sadā ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa samādheḥ samutthitaḥ । taṃ bhikṣuṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā paśyann evaṃ samabravīt ।। śṛṇu vatsa samādhāya tvām atrāhaṃ prabodhaye ।
yathā me gaditaṃ śrutvā tathā kuru samāhitaḥ ।। prāṇihiṃsā na karttavyā tathādattapratigrahaṃ । strīṇāṃ saṃgānurāgaṃ ca akarttavyaṃ kadā cana ।। mṛṣāvādaṃ na vaktavyaṃ paiśūnyavacanaṃ tathā ।
saṃbhinnapralāpaṃ ca pāruṣyaṃ ca kadā cana ।। mithyādṛṣṭir abhidhyā ca vyāpādaṃ ca tathā sadā । bhikṣubhir manasā naiva ciṃtanīyā kadā cana ।। etāni daśapāpānāṃ mūlāni duḥkhadāni hi ।
tasmād evaṃ parijñāya tyaktavyāni sukhārthibhiḥ ।। punar anyac chṛṇuṣvātra vakṣye dāruṇapātakaṃ । saddharmāṇāṃ pratikṣepaṃ kartavyaṃ na kadā cana ।। tathā vāryāpavādatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ na kadā cana ।
paṃcānaṃtaryapāpāni naiva kāryāṇi kena cit ।। yāni śrutvāpi dṛṣṭvāpi bhāvayitvānumodya ca । patanto narakeṣv eva kleśāndhāni ca santi hi ।। tasmād etāni karmāṇi mānasāpi ca mā kṛthā ।
varjanīyāni yatnena saddharmasukhavāṃchibhiḥ ।। karttavyaṃ tu sadā nityam āryasatyānubhāvitaṃ । āryāṣṭāṃgikamārge ca caritvā vratam ādarāt ।। vratānām api sarveṣām āryāṣṭāṃgam upoṣadhaṃ । pravaraṃ vratam ākhyātaṃ sarvair api munīśvaraiḥ ।।
yasya puṇyānubhāvena pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalāḥ । niḥśeṣapāpanirmuktāḥ prayānty arhatpadaṃ drutaṃ ।। evam etat parijñāya vrataṃ kṛtvā samācaran । tatas te kramataḥ pāpaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ kṣiṇuyād drutaṃ ।।
tataś ca kramaśaḥ śikṣāḥ śikṣitvātra samāhitaḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā brahmacaryyaṃ samācara ।। tatas tvaṃ kramaśaś caivaṃ śodhayitvā trimaṃḍalaṃ । sarvakleśavinirmuktaḥ sākṣād arhan bhaviṣyasi ।।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau paribodhitaḥ । tatheti ca parijñāya tadvrataṃ kartum aichata ।। tathā tasyārhataḥ śāstuḥ sadaivaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । kramāc chikṣāś ca śikṣitvā tad upoṣadham ācarat ।।
adhītya sakalā vidyā triratnasamupāśrayan । sarvakleśān vinirjitya brahmacaryaṃ samācarat ।। bhikṣavo jñāyatām eṣa yo asau bhikṣuḥ pṛthagjanaḥ । yad anenārhate śāstre śapitaṃ ruṣṭacetasā ।।
tenāhasto vabhūvāyaṃ paṃcajanmaśatāny api । yac cānenārhataḥ śastur gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ sadā ।। adhītya sakalā vidyā brahmacaryaṃ samāśritaṃ । tenāyaṃ śāsanenātra pravrajyārhaṃ bhavaty api ।।
iti hi bhikṣavo matvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā । śubhena sadgatiṃ yāṃti kṛṣṇena durgatiṃ sadā ।। miśritenāpi miśratvaṃ bhuṃjate sarvajaṃtavaḥ । yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tasyaiva karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ ।।
tenaiva bhujyate loke nānyena spṛśyate kvacit । abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana ।। bhuktaṃ tu kṣīyate karma śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ tathā । nāgnibhir dahyate kena vāyubhiś ca na śuṣyate ।।
klidyate nodakaiś cāpi kṣīyate naiva bhūmiṣu । na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api ।। sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu । evam etat prabhaṣitvā jinendro asau mahāmuniḥ ।।
bodhayan sakalāṃl lokān samādhiṃ vidadhe tataḥ । iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve ca sāṃghikāḥ ।। śubheṣv eva sadā raktāḥ pracerire samāhitāḥ ।। ity evaṃ me samākhyātaṃ guruṇā śāṇavāsinā । tathaivaṃ te mayā khyātaṃ śrutvā caivaṃ śubhe cara ।।
prajāś ca śrāvayitvaivaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । saddharmācaraṇeṣv evaṃ preraṇīyā narādhipa ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhipathaḥ prāpya saṃbodhim āpnuyāḥ khalu ।।
iti tenopaguptena bhāṣitaṃ sa nareśvaraḥ । śrutvā tatheti vaṃditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। ye cāpi śrāvayanti pratidinam aniśaṃ bodhicaryābhiraktāḥ । bhuktvā saukhyaṃ prakāmaṃ munivaranilayaṃ saṃprayāṃti pramodāḥ ।।
athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । yathā te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā me khyātum arhasi ।।
iti tena narendreṇa pṛṣṭe asau sugatātmajaḥ । upagupto yatiś caivaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। śṛṇu rājan samādhāya yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi tac chrutvā mudito bhava ।।
puraikasamaye caivaṃ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā sarvadharmānudeśakaḥ ।। sarvavidyādhipo nāthas traidhātukavināyakaḥ । dharmarājo munīndro asau sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ ।।
śrāvastyāṃ vahir udyāne jetāhvaye mahāvane । anāthapiṇḍadārāme vihāre saugatāśrame ।। śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddham upāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ । bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi tathānyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।।
vyaharat satvahitārthena dharmāmṛtaiḥ pravarṣayan । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ prāyayur bodhivāṃchinaḥ ।। lokapālagaṇāḥ sarve svasvasainyagaṇaiḥ saha । brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ ।।
amātyā dhaninaḥ paurāḥ sādhavaś ca mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca tathānye sarvajātikāḥ ।। sarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatya sarve te samupāgatāḥ । saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā pūjayitvā samaṃtataḥ ।।
parivṛtya puraskṛtya saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo dṛṣṭvā saṃtasthuḥ saṃmukhānatāḥ ।। athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupāśritān । ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokādhipādayaḥ । harṣitās te anumodanto nananduḥ paribodhitāḥ ।। tadaiva samaye tasyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ puri saṃsthitaḥ । āsīt sāṃyātrikotsāhī sārthavāho mahodyamī ।। svakuladharmabhṛd vīraḥ svakulavṛttimānitaḥ ।
yaśodharmārthakāmāptyai samudraṃ gantum aichata ।। tato asau svāṃ priyāṃ bhāryāṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । svasahāyāś ca tāṃ sarvāṃ samāhūya samabravīt ।। bhavaṃto śrūyatāṃ sarve yad abhilaṣitaṃ mama ।
atrāsti yadi vo vāṃchā tan me svāgantum arhatha ।। ahaṃ ratnākaraṃ gantum iche ratnasamṛddhaye । tat prāyāta mayā sārddhaṃ yadi saṃpattim ichatha ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te ratnalobhitāḥ ।
sahasā gaṃtum ichante ratnākare mahodadhau ।। tato asau sārthabhṛc chīghraṃ sarve sārthagaṇaiḥ saha । svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratasthe saṃpramoditaḥ ।। tataḥ kramād vyatikramya grāmāraṇyavanāni ca ।
sarve te pracaranto vai tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ ।। tato bhāṃḍāni naukāyām āropyāruhya ca svayaṃ । karṇadhāraprayatnais te jagāhire ambudhiṃ kramāt ।। tataḥ kramāt samullaṃghya bahudvīpāntarāṇi te ।
ratnākaraṃ samāsādya ratnāni samasādhayan ।। tatas te bahuratnāni samāsādya pramoditāḥ । tataḥ pratyāgatā abdhes tīrāntikaṃ samāyayuḥ ।। tatra tat karmadoṣeṇa kālavātair vighaṭṭitaṃ ।
bhidyate vahanaṃ teṣāṃ hṛdayaiḥ sā sahāśu tat ।। tadā te vaṇijaḥ sarve niḥprayatnapratikriyā । sarvabhāṇḍaiḥ sahāgāḍhe nipetur duṣkare ambudhau ।। kecit phalakam ālamvya samuttīrṇāḥ svavīryataḥ ।
kecid vāhuvalādhānaṃ samuttīrya sthalaṃ yayuḥ ।। kecic ca vilayaṃ prāptā nirālamvyanirāśrayāḥ । utpravanto nimajjantaḥ kheditā nidhanaṃ yayuḥ ।। tatas te vaṇijaḥ sarve ye viśiṣṭā viṣāditāḥ ।
te yaśodhanavibhraṣṭāḥ śūnyahastā gṛhaṃ yayuḥ ।। tathāsau sārthavāho api gṛhaṃ prāpto viṣāditaḥ । etad vṛttaṃ svabhāryāyāḥ kathitvaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। hā hā me mandabhāgyatvāj jāyate mīdṛśī vipat । atrāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi yato bhāgyaṃ na vidyate ।।
bhāgyavān puruṣo dhīro bhāgyavān kuśalī sudhīḥ । bhāgyena labhyate saṃpad yaśaḥ saukhyaguṇānvitaḥ ।। dhīḥ śrīlakṣmīyaśoratnaṃ valaṃ saṃpat kṣaṇādayaḥ । etadādyā guṇāḥ sarve śobhanti bhāgyam āśritāḥ ।।
nihīnabhāgyavṛttes tu puruṣasyāpi saṃmate । etadādyādiguṇāḥ sarve na prasiddhyaṃti sarvataḥ ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣye ahaṃ kva yāsyāmi dhanāptaye । dhanahīnā na śobhante gṛhasthāḥ sādhavo api hi ।।
varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ na tu dravyair vinā gṛhe । paśuvan nirasaṃ bhuktvā sthāsyāmy evaṃ nirutsavaṃ ।। bhāgyena labhyate dravyaṃ bhāgyaṃ dharmeṇa labhyate । dharme hi jāyate sveṣṭadevatāyāḥ prasādataḥ ।।
tad dharmabhāgyalabdhārthaṃ svakuladevatāṃ prati । samyag ārādhayitvaivaṃ yāyāṃ ratnākaraṃ punaḥ ।। manasīti viniścitya sa sārthavāhakaḥ punaḥ । svakuladevatāṃ samyag ārādhya samayācata ।।
namas te devate nityaṃ bhaje ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । kṣaṃtavyaṃ me aparādhatvaṃ prasīda parameśvara ।। itthaṃ sā devatā samyag ārādhya saṃpramoditā । sarvasārthān samāhūya punar evam abhāṣata ।।
bho bhavanto vijānīdhvaṃ vayaṃ sarve vaṇigjanāḥ । tad atra bhavatām agre kathyate me samīhitaṃ ।। yad bhavanto vayaṃ sarve sārthavāhakulodbhavāḥ । tat tathaiva gṛhe sthitvā naiva śobhāṃ vrajemahi ।।
tasmāt svakulavṛttisthaiḥ sarvair asmābhir udyataiḥ । yaśodharmasukhāptyarthaṃ karttavyaṃ dhanasādhanaṃ ।। dhanahīnā na śobhante gṛhasthā hi kuṭuṃvinaḥ । sārthavāho astu śobhante vahuratnārjanodyatāḥ ।।
tad viṣādaṃ parityaktvā yaśoratnasukhāptaye । dhairyyam ālamvya sarvaiś ca karttavyaṃ dhanasādhanaṃ ।। dhanavān puruṣo lokaiḥ sarvatrāpi pramānyate । dhanena sādhayed dharmaṃ dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ vrajet ।।
tasmān nityaṃ mahotsāhais ñltyaktvālasyakuśīdatā । arjanīyaṃ prayatnena dhanaṃ dānāya bhuktaye ।। dānaṃ vibhūṣaṇaṃ loke dānaṃ durgatinivāraṇaṃ । dānaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ dānaṃ śāntikaraṃ sadā ।। asmād dānaṃ sadā kartuṃ bhoktuṃ saukhyaṃ yathechayā ।
bhūyo ratnākaraṃ gaṃtum arhāmahe dhanārjane ।। tatra ratnāni saṃgṛhya svastipratyāgatā vayaṃ । yāvaj jīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā dānaṃ kṛtvā vasemahi ।। yadi daivo vipattiḥ syāt samudre patitā vayaṃ ।
tīrtharāje mṛtāḥ sarve yāsyāmaḥ svargatiṃ dhruvaṃ ।। yadi bhāgyād athāsmākaṃ devānāṃ ca prasādataḥ । yātrāsiddhir bhaven nūnaṃ yāvaj jīvaṃ sukhaṃ tadā ।। asmād ratnākare gantuṃ iche ratnapralabdhaye ।
tat prāyāta mayā sārddhaṃ yadi saṃpattim ichatha ।। iti tasyoditaṃ śrutvā te sarve vaṇijo mudā । tathā tena sahaichānta gantuṃ ratnākaraiḥ punaḥ ।। tato asau sārthabhṛc chīghraṃ dhṛtvā svastyayanaṃ mudā ।
sarve sārthagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ pratasthe svapurād vahi ।। tataḥ kramād vyatikramya grāmāraṇyavanāni ca । pracarantaś ca te sarve tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ ।। tatra sarve api te sārthā bhāṇḍāni vahane kramāt ।
āropya sahasārūḍhā jagāhire mahāmbudhau ।। tataḥ kramāt samullaṃghya vahudvīpāntarāṇi te । ratnākaraṃ samāsādya ratnāni samasādhayan ।। tatra te vahuratnāni samāgṛhya praharṣitāḥ ।
tataḥ pratyāgatāś cābdhes tīrāntikam upāyayuḥ ।। tatas taddaivayogena kālikāvātaghaṭṭitā । sā naukā bhidyate caivaṃ teṣāṃ vai hṛdayaiḥ saha ।। tadā te vaṇijaḥ sarve niḥprayatnapratikriyā ।
sarvabhāṇḍaiḥ sahāgāḍhe nyapatan duṣṭare ambudhau ।। tatra te vilayaṃ prāptā nirālaṃvā nirāśrayāḥ । unmajjanto nimajjantaḥ preritās tīram ūrmibhiḥ ।। kecit phalakam āśritya samuttīryya svavīryyataḥ ।
kecid vāhuvalādhānaiḥ samuttīryya sthalaṃ yayuḥ ।। kecin nihīnavīryyāṅgā hanyamānā mahormibhiḥ । utplavantā nimajjantaḥ kheditā nidhanaṃ yayuḥ ।। tatas teṣāṃ ca sārthānāṃ ye avaśiṣṭā sujīvinaḥ । yaśoratnaviyuktās te śūnyahastā gṛhaṃ yayuḥ ।।
tathāsau sārthavāho api gṛhaṃ gatvā viṣāditaḥ । etad vṛttaṃ svavaṃdhūnāṃ kathitvaivam abhāṣata ।। hā mayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenedrig jāyate vipat । dvidhāpi siddhyate naiva yato bhāgyaṃ na vidyate ।।
pāpair na siddhyate karma atra yatnasya kiṃ valaiḥ । dharmeṇa siddhyate karma tasmād dharmo valottamaḥ ।। tasmād dharmaṃ puraskṛtya karttavyaṃ dravyasādhanaṃ । dravyena sādhayet karma sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ ।।
karma tu siddhyate samyak kulavṛttiṃ ca cāriṇāṃ । kulavṛttiṃ parityajya yo anyavṛttau caret kudhīḥ ।। sa ihāpi paribhraṣṭaḥ paratra durgatiṃ vrajet । yenaivaṃ sadgatiprāptis tadaiva karmma sādhayet ।।
yato api durgatiṃ prāptis tat karma tarhitaṃ budhaiḥ । tad atra kiṃ kariṣye ahaṃ kva yāsyāmy artham arjituṃ । arthaṃ vinā kathaṃ dharmaṃ karttavyaṃ hi kuṭuṃvibhiḥ ।। vinā dharmaṃ hi saṃsāre janma jīvaṃ ca nisphalaṃ ।
kiṃ te na pauruṣeṇāpi yena dharmaṃ na sādhyate ।। dhig dhig me janma saṃsāre jīvituṃ na tathotsahe । varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ na tv evaṃ cirajīvitaṃ ।। avaśyaṃ jantubhir mṛtyur gantavyaṃ ekadhā dhruvaṃ ।
tato atra martum ichāmi na tv evam uṣituṃ gṛhe ।। evaṃjīvo na śobhe ahaṃ dhig pravādāgnidagdhitaḥ । kathaṃ me śāmyate duḥkhaṃ yenāhaṃ parikheditaḥ ।। kiṃ karttavyaṃ kva gantavyaṃ yatnaṃ cātra na vidyate ।
sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo asmi ko me asti rakṣako janaḥ ।। yaśodharmaparibhraṣṭo vrajeyaṃ durgatiṃ khalu । tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi dharmayaśaḥsukhānvitaḥ ।। mānuṣye labhyamāne hi kuto dharmānusādhanaṃ ।
vinā dharmmaṃ yaśodravyaḥ kiṃ saukhyaṃ gṛhavāsināṃ ।। vinā dharmayaśodravyair yo gṛhasthaḥ paśuḥ khalu । dharmeṇa sādhayed dravyaṃ yaśobhāgyasukhāptaye ।। dharmād dhi jāyate puṇyaṃ dānaśīlakṣamādibhiḥ ।
puṇyenaiva pralabhyante caturvargā api dhruvaṃ ।। tad eteṣāṃ mamaiko api na vidyate kathaṃ cana । hā hato asmi svadaivena kiṃ karomi vikheditaḥ ।। sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo asmi namo daivāya karmaṇe ।
evaṃ teṣāṃ svavaṃdhūnāṃ vilapītvā sa sārthapaḥ ।। tasthau cintākulībhūto dhanārjananirāśrayā । evaṃ vyavasthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ te sarve api vāṃdhavāḥ ।। datvāśvāsaṃ vinodāya bodhayante dhruvaṃ tathā ।
sādho sārthapate satyaṃ tat sarvaṃ yat tvayocyate ।। tad evaṃ dhairyyam ālaṃvya prodyamasva gṛhe vasan । sādho kutrāpi mā dhāva nirmāṇasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ ।। yāvad evāmbhasā kumbhaḥ siṃdhāv andhau avapūryate ।
yad abhāvi na tad bhāvi bhāvi naiva tad anyathā ।। avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavaṃti sarvadehināṃ । avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā na bhaveyus tathā yadi ।। pitrā tyaktaḥ kathaṃ rāmo rājyabhraṣṭo vanaṃ yayau ।
tatrāpi vasatas tasya bhāryā śītā pativratā ।। āhṛtya rakṣasā nītā kathaṃ laṃkāpure avasat । tato rāmeṇa vīryeṇa hatvāsau rāvaṇas tataḥ ।। pratyānīya punaḥ śītā tyaktā bharttrā svayaṃ kathaṃ ।
punar ṛṣeḥ samānīya sabhāmadhye parikṣitā ।। tataḥ pṛthyā svayaṃ gṛhya sītānītā rasātalaṃ । tatas tadvirahārttāsau rāmaḥ saṃsāranispṛhaḥ ।। nadyāṃ prāṇasvayaṃ tyaktvā janaṃ sārddhaṃ divaṃ yayau ।
evam anye api rājāno yudhiṣṭhirā nṛpādayaḥ । rājyabhraṣṭā vane gatvā vibhramus te api daivataḥ ।। evam anye api lokāś ca sarvatraidhātukabhavāḥ । uttamā adhamā madhyā saṃti te api svadaivataḥ ।।
kecid gṛhe mṛtāḥ kecij jāyamānā mṛtā api । kecid vālye mṛtāḥ kecit kaumāratve mṛtās tathā ।। yauvane api mṛtāḥ kecin mṛtā vṛddhe vadanti me । sarve apy evaṃ mṛtā lokāḥ svasvadaivapramāṇataḥ ।।
evaṃ devādayo lokāḥ sukhaduḥkhānuyoginaḥ । svasvadaivānubhāvena ṣaḍgatiṣu caranti te ।। kecid vālye sukhaṃ bhuktvā yauvane duḥkhabhāginaḥ । kecic ca yauvane saukhyaṃ bhuktvā vṛddhe suduḥkhitāḥ ।।
kecic ca duḥkhitā vālye yauvane saukhyabhāginaḥ । vṛddhatvasya sukhībhūtā bhavaṃti te api hi daivataḥ ।। sarve api sukham ichanti duḥkhaṃ nechati kaś cana । tathā sukhāni saṃprāptuṃ yatnaṃ kurvanty anekaśaḥ ।।
keṣāṃ cit siddhyate yatnaṃ keṣāṃ cid vā na siddhyati । keṣāṃ cid vighnatāṃ yāti tat sarvaṃ daivayogataḥ ।। tathā ca rogiṇāṃ rogā vaidyopacāraṇair api । varddhyante naiva śāmyante tad api daivayogataḥ ।।
keṣāṃ cid rogiṇāṃ rogā vinā vaidyopacāraṇe । śāmyaṃte yatnato cāpi tad api daivayogataḥ ।। tathā cald maṃtriṇāṃ maṃtrāḥ siddhyante yatnato laghuḥ । keṣāṃ cid vighnatāṃ yānti tad api daivakāraṇāt ।।
tathaivaṃ vaṇijāṃ lābhoḥ siddhyante yatnato api ca । keṣāṃ cin naiva yatnena tad api daivayogataḥ ।। tathā vīrā raṇe śatruṃ vinā yatnaṃ jayaṃty api । kecit tu ripunā yuddhe hanyamānā mṛtāḥ pare ।।
kecit kṛtvā mahāyuddhaṃ hanyamānāḥ parasparaṃ । tyaktvā dehaṃ gatāḥ svargaṃ tad api daivayogataḥ ।। evaṃ sāṃyātrikā ratnaṃ prāptuṃ ratnākaraṃ gatāḥ । kecid ratnāni saṃgṛhya svasti pratyāgatā gṛhaṃ ।।
kecid ratnam alabdhaṃ vai śūnyahastā gṛhāgatāḥ । kecic ca nidhanaṃ yātās tatraiva makarālaye ।। kecid yatnāt samuttīrya jīvanto gṛham āgatāḥ । kecic ca jāṃgale caurair nihatā maraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।
kecic ca jaṃtubhir mārge hiṃsyamāne mṛtā vane । keṣāṃ cit siddhyate yātrā mahallābhasamanvitāḥ ।। keṣāṃ cid vighnatāṃ yānti tathāpi daivayogataḥ । kaiś cid gṛhe nidhiḥ prāptaḥ kaiś cid deśāntare vane ।।
kaiś cid dūre bhramadbhiś ca naiva kiṃ cit kva cid dhanaṃ । keṣāṃ cid varddhate saṃpad yatnāyāsaṃ vinā laghu ।। keṣāṃ cid dhīyate saṃpad rakṣitāpi prayatnataḥ । keṣāṃ cit susthirā saṃpat keṣāṃ cid vala asthirā ।।
keṣāṃ cij jāyate naiva nānopāyārjanair api । evaṃ nānāprakāraiś ca satvās traidhātukodbhavāḥ ।। bhuṃjate sukhaduḥkhāni svasvadaivānusāriṇāḥ । sukhasyānte hi duḥkhāni duḥkhasyānte sukhāni ca ।। bhuṃjante jaṃtavaḥ sarve bhramante ṣaḍgatiṣv api ।
tathā bhavanti mitrāṇi dviṣo api hitakāriṇaḥ ।। mitrāṇy api dviṣo duṣṭā bhavaṃti daivayogataḥ । tathāmṛtaṃ viṣībhūtaṃ viṣaṃ cāpy amṛtī bhavet ।। tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahad varaṃ ।।
tathā ca brahmaṇaḥ śīrṣaṃ nikṛttaṃ śūlapāṇinā । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalī ।। tathā cakrī suvīro api vyādheṣu nihato mṛtaḥ । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahad valaṃ ।।
yaś ca bhūtādhipaś ceśaḥ so apy umatto digaṃvaraḥ । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। caṃdro api ca kalaṃkāṅko māse māse api hīyate । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahadvalaṃ ।।
evaṃ candradineśau ca graheṇāpi nipīḍitau । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalī ।। rāmo rakṣovijetāpi putreṇa nihato raṇe । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalī ।।
tathārjjunaḥ sudhīro api putreṇāpi hato raṇe । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalaṃ ।। tathā ca parśurāmeṇa mātāpi nihatā krudhā । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalaḥ ।।
biṃbisāro nṛpendro api putreṇājātaśatruṇā । vaṃdhane māritaṃ caivaṃ tad api daivayogataḥ ।। tasmāc ca brahmadattena dharmapālo sa nandanaḥ । māritaḥ pramadātuṣṭyai tad api daivayogataḥ ।।
rājñī ca durpatī mātā svātmajasyāpi rohitaṃ । pītvaiva nirdayā tuṣṭā tad api daivayogataḥ ।। kṣāntivādī muniś cāpi rājñā nirdayacetasā । asinā ghātito araṇye tad api daivayogataḥ ।।
prasenajin nṛpeśo api putreṇāpi svarājyataḥ । nirvāsito vane bhrāntas tad api daivayogataḥ ।। evam anye api rājāno hatvā jñātī svavāṃdhavān । bhuṃjate prāpya rājyāni tad api daivayogataḥ ।।
evaṃ pitrā sutās tyaktvā mātrā ca svātmajā api । vaṃdhumitrādibhis tyaktvā kecid daivānuyogataḥ ।। bhāryāpi svāminā tyaktvā bharttāpi bhāryyayā tathā । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ ।। putreṇāpi pitā tyaktaṃ mātāpi jananī tathā ।
dhātrī cāpi parityaktās tathā pautrapitāmahaḥ ।। tathā pitāmahas tyaktaḥ putraiś cāpy atinirdayaiḥ । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ ।। tathā rājñā svabhṛtyāś ca sevakā api sajjanāḥ ।
aparādhaṃ vinā tyaktās tad api daivayogataḥ ।। tathā sakhisahāyāṃ ca vaṃdhumitrasuhṛjjanān । parityaktvā nihaṃty ante tad api daivayogataḥ ।। tathā śiṣyān gurur hanti śiṣyo hanti gurum api ।
tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ ।। tathāpi ghnanti bharttāraṃ svāminaṃ sevakānn api । tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ ।। tathā ca svayam ātmānaṃ ghnanti kecid ruṣānvitāḥ ।
tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattamaḥ ।। kecic chastraiḥ svayaṃ hatvā kecid bhuktvā viṣādikaṃ । kecid agnau jale svabhre prapātāt patitā mṛtāḥ ।। kecit pāśaiḥ svayaṃ badhya mṛtāḥ kecic ca vaṃdhane ।
kecit pānāśanādīṃś ca tyaktvā yāṃti yamālayaṃ ।। evaṃ kṛtvāpi yānty eva kecid vāpi surālayaṃ । kecic ca narake yānti tat sarvaṃ daivayogataḥ ।। tathā mṛddārupāṣāṇe nānādhātupratiṣṭhitāḥ ।
devatāś ca dadanty evaṃ phalaṃ daivaniyogataḥ ।। pare api svajanā iṣṭāḥ sahajā api ca dviṣaḥ । bhavanti tat kṣaṇād eva tad api daivayogataḥ ।। evaṃ traidhātukotpannāḥ sarve satvāś ca jaṃtavaḥ ।
ṣaḍgatiṣu bhramantas te caranti daivayogataḥ ।। kecid vīrā guṇāḍhyāś ca suṃdarā bhāgyamāninaḥ । sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhāś ca cakravarttinṛpādayaḥ ।। kecic ca nirguṇāḥ prāḍhyāḥ kecin nirguṇinaḥ śaṭhāḥ ।
kecic ca vikalāṃgāś ca guṇasaṃpattibhāginaḥ ।। kecic ca suṃdarā mūrkhā nirdhanā nirguṇāḥ śaṭhāḥ । kecic ca guṇinaḥ prāḍhyā nīcakarmānucāriṇaḥ ।। kecin nīcakulotpannāḥ guṇāḍhyāḥ sādhuvṛttayaḥ । dātāro dhanino vīrāḥ sarvasatvānupālakāḥ ।।
kecid uccakulotpannā nirguṇā duṣṭavṛttayaḥ । kṛpaṇā vikalāṃgāś ca nirdayāś ca durāśayāḥ ।। kecid vīrā hy alābhijñāḥ kulīnāḥ sādhavo api ye । te api jātinihīne api bhajaṃti śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।
kecic ca guṇavanto api kucelāḥ kṛśagātrikāḥ । pretavad bhujyamānāś ca caraṃti bhikṣukā bhuvi ।। kecic ca nirguṇā vāpi vaṃcakā duṣṭamānasāḥ । mānyante sādhuval loke tad api daivayogataḥ ।।
evaṃ nānāvidhā lokāḥ ṣaḍgatiṣu samudbhavāḥ । sukhaduḥkhāni bhuṃjante bhramaṃti daivayogataḥ ।। tasmād daivaṃ mahāvīraṃ sarvatraidhātukeṣv api । kenāpi śakyate naiva vaśe netuṃ kathaṃ cana ।।
tena daivaṃ mahānāthaḥ sarvakarmādhipaḥ prabhuḥ । sraṣṭā bharttā ca harttā ca traidhātuvāsinām api ।। tasyāpy adhipatibrahmā sarvalokeśvaro vidhiḥ । tat tasya śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktyā nityaṃ samarcaya ।।
tasmiṃ tuṣṭe vidhau devaiḥ parituṣṭaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ । tato daivaprasādena sarvatra maṃgalaṃ bhavet ।। daive tuṣṭe susiddhyante sarvakarmāṇi yatnataḥ । viruddhe tu na siddhyante yatnaiḥ saṃsādhitāny api ।।
tasmād daivādhipaṃ devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ caturānanaṃ । bhaja daivaprasannāya sarvakāryaprasiddhaye ।। daivaṃ brahmaprasādena śubhadaṃ saṃmukhī bhavet । tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvakāryyeṣu saṃbhavet ।।
evaṃ sārthapate natvā vidhānaṃ kāryyasādhanaṃ । vidhinārādhya sadbhaktyā kuruṣva karmasādhanaṃ ।। tathā cet sarvathā nityaṃ yātrāyaṃ maṃgalaṃ bhavet । anyad vā cintitaṃ kāryaṃ sarvāpy evaṃ prasatsyate ।।
yadi vāṃchāsti te bhūyo gantuṃ ratnākaraṃ prati । tathābhyarcya vidhātāraṃ gachet svasti bhavet khalu ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhas tatheti saḥ । pratijñāya samabhyarcya brahmāṇaṃ prārthayat tadā ।।
namas te bhagavan brahmaṃ yātrāsiddhiṃ kuruṣva me । evaṃ vidhiṃ samārādhya sa sārthādhipatis tataḥ ।। ratnaṃ prāptyai punaḥ sārthān samāhūyābravīt tathā । bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ yan mayā samudīritaṃ ।। atrāsti yadi vo vāṃchā tathā kartuṃ samudyatāṃ ।
ahaṃ ratnākaraṃ bhūyo gantuṃ ichāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। tad yadīchatha ratnāni tathā yāta mayā saha । kiṃ cāpy atra vayaṃ sarve sārthavāhakulodbhavāḥ ।। tad gṛhe paśuvad bhuktvā kathaṃ śobhī vrajemahi ।
saṃsāre sarvajaṃtūnāṃ ekadhā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। tat kiṃ no maraṇe bhītyā mṛtyuṃ kena nivāryyate । yadi daivād vipattiḥ syād asmākaṃ karmmadoṣataḥ ।। sarvatīrthajalādhāre mṛtāḥ svargaṃ vrajemahi ।
yadi bhāgyāc ca no yātrā siddhā svastimatī bhavet । tadā jīvaṃ sukhaṃ dānaṃ kṛtvā svargaṃ vrajemahi । tad viṣādaṃ parityajya yaśodharmmasukhāptaye ।। vīryotsāhaṃ samādhāya samāyāta mayā saha ।
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te vaṇijo mudā ।। tatheti ca samutsāhaṃ kṛtvā gaṃtuṃ samudyatāḥ । tataḥ sarve api te sārthā dhṛtvā svastyayanaṃ vidhiṃ ।। paṇyam ādāya tenaiva saha sārthabhṛtā yayuḥ ।
tatas te prasthitāḥ sarve grāmāraṇyavanasthalīḥ ।। samuttīryya kramād yātās tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ । tatra nāvi samārūḍhā karṇadhāraprayatnataḥ ।। marutāṃte anukūlena jagāhire mahodadhiṃ ।
tatas teṣāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ daivayogānuyogataḥ ।। sā naukā kālikāvātasaṃkṣubdhābhūd vibheditā । tadā sarve api te sārthā dṛṣṭvā naukāṃ vibheditāṃ ।। trasitāḥ sahasā tasmāt pratyāyayuḥ prayatnataḥ ।
tatas te vaṇijaḥ sarve vipaṃnāśā viṣāditāḥ ।। rātrau svasvagṛhe gatvā vibhagnāsā viṣedire । tathāsau sārthavāho api lajjitaḥ khaṇḍitāśayaḥ ।। kheditātmā gṛhe tasthau mūkavad dhi natotsavaḥ ।
tato bhāryyā satī bhadrā patikhedavibheditaṃ । dṛṣṭvā taṃ vikalībhūtaṃ samupetyābravīt punaḥ ।। mā viṣādaṃ kṛthāḥ svāminn atra dhairyyaṃ samāśrayaḥ । dharmiṣṭhe śaraṇaṃ gatvā kuruṣva dharmasādhanaṃ ।।
dharmmeṇa jīyate pāpaṃ niṣpāpo nirmalāśayaḥ । śuddhacitto viśuddhātmā puṇyātmā bhāgyam āpnuyāt ।। tato bhāgyavataḥ puṃso yad yat karmaṇi sādhitaṃ । tat tat sarvaṃ prasiddhyeta tasmād dharmaṃ carottamaṃ ।।
dharmam eva suhṛd mitram ihāmutra sahānugaḥ । dharmmeṇa pālyate sarvaṃ tasmād dharmo jagatsuhṛt ।। dharmā nānāvidhā loke kulacaryyānusarataḥ । sarveṣām api dharmāṇāṃ dayā dharme viśiṣyate ।।
dayāluḥ sugato buddho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ । samantabhadra ātmajñaḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ ।। sarvajño mārajic chāstā jagannāthaḥ śubhārthadaḥ । ṣaḍabhijño jagadbharttā sarvalokādhipeśvaraḥ ।।
tasmāt tasya munīndrasya sadbhaktyā śaraṇaṃ vrajan । saddharmaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityam upāsakaḥ ।। tatas te naśyate pāpaṃ maṃgalaṃ ca bhaved dhruvaṃ । tadaiva sarvakāryāṇi sametsyaṃte na saṃśayaḥ ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatir mudā । tatheti saṃpratijñāya saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ yayau ।। namas te bhagavan nātha pāpistho ahaṃ sudurbhagaḥ । bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gache tan māṃ dṛṣṭvāśu rakṣatāṃ ।।
yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kāritaṃ vānumoditaḥ । tat sarvaṃ deśayiṣyāmi tan me dehi śubhāṃ gatiṃ ।। bhavatāṃ sarvadā nātha śaraṇaṃ yāmy upāsakaḥ । anyo me śaraṇaṃ nāsti tan māṃ rakṣa sadā bhaje ।।
tridhāpi me jagannātha yātrā bhagnā svadaivataḥ । gṛhasthaḥ sārthavāho ahaṃ tan me dehi susaṃpadaḥ ।। yanv ahaṃ sāṃprataṃ nātha bhavataṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajan । bhūyo ratnākaraṃ gantuṃ ichāmi ratnalabdhaye ।।
yadi yātrā bhavet siddhi yāval lābhaṃ ca lapsyate । tadupāyena saṃbuddhaṃ pūjayeyaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।। ity evaṃ niścayaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaṃ saṃsmaran muhuḥ । tāṃ bhāryyāṃ bhadrikāṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।।
bhadre tvayā yad ādiṣṭaṃ tathā kartuṃ samutsahe । adyāgreṇa jagannāthaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāsyāmy upāsakaḥ ।। bhadre nāmnā jinendrasya yāsye ratnākare punaḥ । yadi yātrā bhavet siddhi yāval lābhaṃ ca lapsyate ।।
tadupārddhena ratnena sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ tadā । yathārhaṃ pūjayiṣye aham iti saṃkalpitaṃ mayā ।। yadi daivād vipattiḥ syāt saṃbuddhanāma saṃsmaran । sarvatīrthajalādhāne mṛto yāyāṃ sukhāvatīṃ ।।
tad atra yadi me kāryyaṃ śubhaṃ kartuṃ samichasi । tad viṣādaṃ parityajya dhairyyaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa ।। iti bharttroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryyā bhadrikā satī । tatheti pratisaṃmodya svāminaṃ taṃ samabravīt ।।
yady evaṃ te samīhāsti kṛtv etaṃ niścayaṃ prabho । saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ dhṛtvā gacha svastiṃ samācara ।। yadi buddhakṛpādṛṣṭiḥ satveṣu vidyate kila । tathāvaśyaṃ sa saṃbuddhaḥ paśyan tvāṃ cāpy acet khalu ।।
tadā te maṅgalaṃ nityaṃ yātrā svastimatī bhavet । tatas te janma saṃsāre sāphalyaṃ ca bhavet khalu ।। tena svāmiṃ jineṃdrasya nāmasvastyayanaṃ dadhat । gacha yātrā susiddhāstu svasti pratyāgatāśu ca ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatir mudā । bhūyaḥ sārthagaṇān sarvān samāhūyābravīt tathā ।। bhavanta śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ yan mayātra samīhitaṃ । ahaṃ ratnākaraṃ bhūyo gantum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ ।।
tad asti yadi vo vāṃchā yaśaḥsaṃpatsukhāptaye । samāyāta mayā sārddhaṃ ratnākaraṃ vrajemahi ।। yadi bhāgyād dhi no yātrā siddhā svastimatir bhavet । yāvajīvaṃ sukhaṃ dharmaṃ kṛtvā svargaṃ vrajemahi ।
atha vā syād vipattir naḥ sarvatīrthajalāśraye । mṛtāḥ svargaṃ gamiṣyāmo hy avaśyaṃ maraṇe sati ।। paśuvat kiṃ gṛhe sthitvā sukhaṃ vā kiṃ yaśo vinā । yaśonvitā mṛtā ye hi tatpumāṃso narottamāḥ ।।
yad artham eva jīvāmas tad arthaṃ yan na vidyate । kiṃ tena jīvitenāpi kevalaṃ duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।। varam evādya me mṛtyur na vyarthaṃ cirajīvitaṃ । yasmāc ciram api sthitvā mṛtyur kena nivāryyate ।। iti mṛtyubhayaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvatrāpy anivāraṇaṃ ।
tyaktvā viṣādakauśīdyaṃ prodyamahyaṃ yaśorjane ।। evaṃ nānāprakāreṇa tena sārthabhṛtāpi te । bodhyamānā vaṇiksaṃghāḥ kiṃ cin naiva samūcire ।। abhadro ayaṃ pumāṃ cāpi yato yātrā na siddhyati ।
iti tena mahāṃbhodhau naiko api gantum aichata ।। atha sārthapatir dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān viratotsavān । eko api vā svayaṃ gantum aichad ratnākaraṃ prati ।। tato bhāryāṃ samāmaṃtrya paribodhya prasannadhīḥ ।
svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratasthe bhārakaiḥ saha ।। tataḥ paṇyaṃ samādāya bhāravāhajanaiḥ saha । purād vahi vinirgatya kramād deśāṃtaraṃ yayau ।। kramāc caṃcūryyamāno asau grāmāraṇyavanasthalīḥ ।
parikraman samullaṃghya prāpus tīraṃ mahodadheḥ ।। tatrāsau sārthabhṛd dṛṣṭvā taṃ samudraṃ mahāmbudhiṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā prārthayac charaṇaṃ gataḥ ।। namas te jīvam ādhāra sarvasatvārthasaṃpade ।
tvadāsayā samāyāmi tad āśāṃ me prapūraya ।। tato asau karṇadhāraṃ ca toṣayitvā prabodhayan । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā saṃdhṛtvā samayācata ।। karṇadhāra mahāvāho tavāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।
tat svasti cārayan naukāṃ yātrāsiddhiṃ prasādhaya ।। tathāsau vahanaṃ kṛtvā dṛḍhītaṃ gāḍhavaṃdhitaṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā saṃdhṛtvā samayācata ।। yathā mātā ca garbhasthaṃ vālakaṃ saṃprarakṣate ।
tathā mām eva garbhasthe nauke mātaḥ prarakṣatāṃ ।। tataś ca sugataṃ smṛtvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇamyaivam ayācata ।। namas te bhagavan nātha yathā trāsi jagattrayaṃ ।
tathā māṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā pāhi vraje ratnākare ।। ity evaṃ sārthavāho asau praṇatvā sugataṃ smaran । bhāṇḍāny āropya naukāyaṃ samārohaj janaṃ saha ।। tato asau naukrameṇaiva karṇadhāraprayatnataḥ । marutāṃ cānukūlena saṃjagāha mahāmbudhau ।।
yat tatra sārthavāho asau saṃsmaran sugataṃ muhuḥ । tena puṇyabalenaiva sā naukā svastim ācaran ।। tathā kramāc caranty evaṃ dvīpalokāntarāṇi ca । vyatikramya suśighreṇa ratnākaraṃ samāyayau ।।
tatra ratnākare prāpya ratnāni samasādhayan । tato ratnāni saṃgṛhya pratasthe vahanāsthitaḥ ।। tataḥ kramād vyatikramya dvīpalokāntarāṇi ca । tīraṃ prāpuḥ suśīghreṇa buddhadṛṣṭiprasādataḥ ।।
tataḥ sthalaṃ samāsādya śailāraṇyavanasthalīḥ । grāmāṃ deśāṃ parikramya śrāvastyāṃ puram āyayau ।। tato gṛhe praviṣṭo asau bharyyayā saha moditaḥ । suhṛnmitrajanaiś cāpi kṛtvālāpaṃ nyaṣīdata ।।
tataḥ sadyar gṛhastho asau bhāryyayā saha naṃditaḥ । bhāṇḍam udghāṭya ratnāni pratyavekṣitum ārabhat ।। tatra divyavicitrāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca । dṛṣṭvā harṣaṃ samāsādya punar evaṃ vabhāṣate ।।
mamaitāni suratnāni divyāny etādṛśāni hi । tatra divyavicitrāṇi nānāratnakulāni ca ।। labdhāni taj jinendrasya kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । tasmād yathāpratijñātaṃ śraddhayā sāṃprataṃ mayā ।।
yad upārddhaṃ pradātavyaiḥ śravaṇāyārhate api naḥ । tad upārddhaṃ kathaṃ cānudātavyaṃ munaye arhate ।। yadi rājā vijānīyād etad arddhaṃ hare mama । ratnalubdho nareśo yaṃ daṇḍaṃ vā praṇayaṃ mayi ।।
tadā me syād vipattiś ca tat kathaṃ kriyate mayā । aho daivād vipattir mām adyāpi ca na muṃcati । tat kathaṃ vā pratijñātaṃ pūrayituṃ na manyate । namas te bhagavan nātha sarvajño asi munīśvaraḥ ।।
rakṣa māṃ pāpinaṃ mūḍhanimagnaṃ duḥkhasāgare । ity asau sugataṃ smṛtvā taccintāvyathitāśayaḥ ।। kapolaṃ svakare dhṛtvā tasthau koṣṭhe nirutsavaḥ । tathaivaṃ sthitam ālokya svāmi naṃ taṃ viṣāditaṃ ।। sā bhāryā bhadrikopetya puraḥ sthitvābravīt tathā ।
svāmiṃ bharttaḥ kim eva tvaṃ sthito asi duḥkhito yathā ।। kiṃ vā te jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad vaca cet priyāsmi te ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatiḥ punaḥ । tāṃ bhāryyāṃ samupāmaṃtrya punaś caivam abhāṣata ।।
bhadre yaj jāyate duḥkhaṃ tat pravakṣye śṛṇu priye । yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ pūrayituṃ kathaṃ tathā ।। yady upārddhaṃ pradāsyāmi śravaṇāyārhate api nu । etad arddhaṃ hared rājā lobhān me daṇḍayed api ।।
ity evaṃ tadviṣādena vyathito ahaṃ nirutsavaḥ । tan me nātra pratīkāro kathaṃ kartuṃ na manyate ।। iti bharttroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryā punar abravīt । viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāḥ svāmiṃ śṛṇu yan me samīhitaiḥ ।।
tāvad imāni saṃkalpaḥ paścāt tat samayāgate । pūjayā saha bhojaiś ca sasaṃghāyārhate arcayet ।। evaṃ kṛte tathā svāmin pratijñā tena setsyate । bhītiś cāpi na vidyeta tasmād evaṃ kuru prabho ।।
iti bhāryāvacaḥ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatir mudā । tatheti pratisaṃśrutya punar evam abhāṣata ।। tāvad imāni sarvāṇi ratnāni te samarppaye । paścāt kāle sasaṃghaṃ taṃ pūjayiṣye munīśvaraṃ ।।
idānīṃ sugaṃdhadhūpena pūjayeyaṃ munīśvaraṃ । ity uktvā sarvaratnāni bhāryāyāṃ sa nyadhāpayet ।। tato asau cāguruṃ krītvā kārṣāpaṇadvayena vā । gatvā jetavane vihāre tatra dvāre sthito gurum adhūpayet ।।
tatrāpatramāno asau saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā saṃsmaran prārthayat tathā ।। bhagavac chāstāsi sarvajño vijānīyā mamāśayaṃ । tadyathā me pratijñātaiḥ pūrayituṃ samarhasi ।।
athāsau bhagavān tasya matvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । mahad ṛdhyabhisaṃskāraṃ cakāra tatprasādataḥ ।। yena sa dhūpa ākāśe prābhyudgamya purīṃ ca tāṃ । sphuritvā khe punar abhrakūṭībhūtvābhyaśobhayat ।। tatrāsau sārthabhṛd dṛṣṭvā prātihāryaṃ tad adbhutaṃ ।
mahānaṃdaprasaṃnātmā punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। naitan me pratirūpaṃ syād yad ayaṃ sugato jinaḥ । mayā nābhyarcito ratnair dhig me cittabhayād drutaṃ ।। yanv ahaṃ sāṃprataṃ nāthaṃ prārthayitvā sasāṃghikaṃ ।
saratnaiḥ pūjayiṣyāmi bhojanaiś ca svake gṛhe ।। ity asau niścayaṃ kṛtvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । saṃbuddhasaṃmukhaṃ gatvā praṇatvaivaṃ vyajijñapat ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña kṣamasva me aparādhatāṃ ।
bhavatāṃ pūjanāṃ kartum ichāmi me prasīdatu ।। ity evaṃ prārthite tena sa saṃbuddho munīśvaraḥ । tatheti pratisaṃmodya tūṣṇībhūtvā vyavasthitaḥ ।। tato asau sārthabhṛn matvā sugatenādhivāsitaṃ ।
praṇatvā ca muneḥ pādau sahasā svagṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa bhāryyayā sārddhaṃ vaṃdhumitra janair api । praṇītaṃ bhojyapūjāṃgaṃ sādhayām āsa satvaraṃ ।। tato bhojyārcanāṃgāni sajjīkṛtya pramoditaḥ ।
vihāre sahasā gatvā natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ ।। bhagavan nātha saṃbuddha samayo ayaṃ pravarttate । tad bhavān sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ samāgantuṃ samarhati ।। ity evaṃ prārthite tena sa saṃbuddhaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ ।
pratasthe sūryyavan mārge prātihāryaṃ pradarśayan ।। tataḥ kramāt purīṃ prāpya tad gṛhaṃ samupāviśat । tad datte pādyaṃ ādāya śuddhāsane nyaṣīdata ।। tatas tān sāṃghikān sarvān saṃbuddhapramukhān kramāt ।
svasvāsanasamāsīnān dṛṣṭvā samyak samarcayat ।। yathārhaṃ bhojanair vāpi varṇagandharasānvitaiḥ । saṃbuddhapramukhān saṃghān saṃtarpya paryatoṣayat ।। tataś ca bhojanānte sa śodhayitvā bhujādikaṃ । apanīya ca pātrāṇi tāmbūlādīn aḍhaukayat ।।
tato yāni suratnāni pūrvasaṃkalpatāni hi । etaiḥ sarvaṃ suratnais taṃ saṃbuddhaiḥ samavākiran ।। tāni ratnāni sarvāṇi saṃbuddhasyānubhāvataḥ । muner upari khe gatvā chatrībhūtvā sthitā vabhau ।।
tatas taṃ sa gṛhī dṛṣṭvā dviguṇasaṃpramoditaḥ । pādau tasya muner natvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tathā ।। anena dānadharmeṇa puṇyena kuśalena ca । bhaveyaṃ sugato buddho loke andhe apariṇāyake ।।
amukto mocayiṣyāmi tārayiṣyāmy atāritān । bhītān āśvāsya saṃbodhau sthāpayiṣyāmi nirvṛtau ।। tathāsau bhagavān buddhas tathāśayaviśodhitaṃ । saṃbodhau nihitaṃ cittaṃ jñātvā smitaṃ vyadhāt tathā ।।
tadā tasya munīndrasya mukhapadmād vinirgatāḥ । paṃcavarṇā vibhāsanto viniśceruḥ subhānavaḥ ।। tatas te bhāsvarāḥ sarve pravisṛtāḥ samaṃtataḥ । kecid ūrddhaṃ gatāḥ kecin madhyaṃ kecid rasātale ।।
kecid adho gatā yās te sarve te narakeṣu ca । nipataṃto vibhāsanto pravisasruḥ samaṃtataḥ ।। ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śitībhūtā vicerire । ye śītanarakās teṣu nyapatad uṣṇikāś ca te ।।
ye ye taiḥ kiraṇaiḥ spṛṣṭās te te sarve sukhānvitāḥ । yadā te sukhasaṃprāptās tadā te vismayānvitāḥ ।। aho naḥ sukham adyaivaṃ katham etad vyacintayan । kiṃ nu vayam itaś cyutvā kutra yātāsma sāṃprataṃ ।।
āhosvid upapannāḥ syur anyatra bhuvaneṣv api । iti saṃdehināṃ teṣāṃ satvānāṃ paribodhane ।। bhagavān nirmite buddhaṃ preṣayan narakān prati । dṛṣṭvā taṃ nirmitaṃ muniṃ vismitā harṣitāś ca vai ।।
te sarve narakā lokāḥ saṃmīlya saṃvabhāṣire । na bhavanta itaś cyutvā gatāsmānyatra bhūmiṣu ।। kiṃs tv ayaṃ nu mahāsatvaḥ hy apūrvadarśanaḥ pumān । nūnam asyānubhāvena duḥkhāni samitāni ca ।। tad vayam enam ānamya vaṃde mayā pramuktaye ।
iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve natvā tac charaṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vavandire । iti te nirmite tasmin prasādya cittam āratāḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktā martyadevālayaṃ yayuḥ ।
evaṃ te bhānavaḥ sarve sarvatra narakeṣv api ।। prodyante nārakān sarvān pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ । tathā tad bhānavaś caivam upariṣṭāṃ gatā api ।। te api sarve caturlokapālānāṃ bhuvanāni ca ।
avabhāsya kramāt sarvān devalokān abhāsayan ।। tathākaniṣṭhaparyantaṃ traidhātukān abhāsayan । evaṃ sarvāś ca tān sarvān avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ ।। gāthāḥ prodghoṣayantaś ca pralayaṃ saugate vṛṣe ।
anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaśūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ ।। tasmāt māraṃ parityajya gachadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ muneḥ । niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ kaṃ yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane ।। mṛtyusainyaṃ dhunītāśu naḍāgāraṃ karī yathā ।
yo apy asmin dharmavinaye hy apramattaś cariṣyati ।। tyaktvā jātisasaṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। atha te bhānavaḥ sarve traidhātubhuvaneṣv api । sarvān satvān samuddhṛtya punaḥ pratyāyayur muneḥ ।।
atha te bhānavaḥ sarve bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ । pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā mūrddhni cāntardadhur muneḥ ।। athaitat sabhāsīnā lokāḥ sarve sasāṃghikāḥ । tat tadadbhutam ālokya vabhūvur vismayoddhatāḥ ।।
athānaṃdaḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । bhagavantaṃ guruṃ natvā papracha smitakāraṇaṃ ।। bhagavan bhavato vaktrāt paṃcavarṇāḥ subhāṃsavaḥ । vinirgatā diśaḥ sarvān avabhāsya śatā punaḥ ।।
bhavān hi sugato śāstā saṃbuddho bhagavañ jinaḥ । nirmado nirahaṃkāraḥ mānamātsaryyavarjitaḥ ।। tad bhava bhagavaṃ kasmāt smitaiḥ karoti sāṃprataṃ । dṛṣṭvaivaṃ taṃ smitaṃ sarve ime lokāḥ pravismitāḥ ।। nāhetuḥ sugatā buddhā arhanto vigatoddhavāḥ ।
darśayanti smitaṃ kecit tat kena bhavataḥ smṛtaṃ ।। tad etad dhetum ichanti śrotuṃ sarve ime janāḥ । tad etat kāraṇaṃ śāstaḥ samādeṣṭuṃ samarhati ।। ity evaṃ prārthite tena śiṣyeṇānaṃdayoginā ।
tatheti pratisaṃmodya tam ānaṃdaṃ vabhāṣata ।। evam etat tathānaṃda yathaiva bhāṣasi tvayā । tat smitaṃ yadarthaṃ me tad vakṣye śṛṇutādarāt ।। paśyānaṃda mamānena sārthavāhena sādhunā ।
ebhī ratnaiś ca satkṛtya kṛtā pūjā svabhaktitaḥ ।। anena kuśalenaiva sārthavāho mahāsudhīḥ । kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya pūryya pāramitā daśa ।। saṃbodhipākṣikān dharmān prāpya brahmavihārikaḥ ।
saṃbodhiṃ samavāpyaivaṃ jitvā māragaṇān api ।। buddho ratnottamo nāma sarvajño arhaṃ tathāgataḥ । dharmarājo jagaṃnātho loke śāstā bhaviṣyati ।। tad anumodanāṃ kṛtvā saddharmaṃ bhajatādarāt ।
dharmeṇaiva jagaj jitvā māracaryāvinirgataḥ ।। bhadracarī samāsādya saṃbodhipadam āpnuyāt । dharnio hi jagatāṃ mitram ihāmutra samantataḥ ।। hitakārī suhṛd iṣṭaḥ sarvadāpi sahānugaḥ ।
