tasmād dharmaṃ samādhāya saṃcaradhvaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। tena vā maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvabhāvī bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvānaṃdaḥ sapārṣadaḥ । tatheti moditas taṃ ca guruṃ natvā sa naṃdataḥ ।।
so api sārthapatiś caiva svakaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ kila । munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvātīvābhyanaṃdatat ।। tataś cābhiprasannātmā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ vyatijñapat ।।
namas te bhagavan nātha sarvadharmādhipeśvaraḥ । bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhavāmy aham upāsakaḥ ।। yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kāritaṃ cānumoditaṃ । tat sarvaṃ deśayiṣyāmi tan me dehi śubhāṃ cariṃ ।। bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya triratnaṃ samupāśraye ।
kṣamasva me aparādhatvaṃ tan māṃ rakṣa mudā tathā ।। evaṃ tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa saṃbuddho abhyadhāt punaḥ । yathā te abhihitaṃ sādho tathā saṃsetsyate dhruvaṃ ।। tasmāc cittaṃ samādhāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā bodhicaryāṃ samācara ।। tatas tvaṃ kramato hy evaṃ pūrya pāramitā drutaṃ । bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bhaved bodhim avāpnuyāt ।। etat satyaṃ parijñāya saddharmaṃ saṃprasādhaya ।
tena te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। jayo astu te sadā bodhau siddhyatu praṇihitaṃ drutaṃ । ciraṃ jīvaṃ hitaṃ loke dharmaṃ dhṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa ।। ity asau bhagavān buddhas tasmai datvāśiṣaṃ śubhāṃ ।
saṃghaiḥ saha samutthāya svaṃ vihāraṃ yayau tataḥ ।। atha sārthapatiś cāsau sadāraḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saddharmeṣu sadācarat ।। tathā sarve api satvāś ca śrutvā tasya pravṛttitāṃ ।
bodhicittaṃ samādhāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। etat me guruṇākhyātaṃ saṃśrutaṃ yathā mayā । tathātraivaṃ tava prītyā kathyate saṃprabudhyatāṃ ।। tathā rājan tvayāpy evaṃ svayaṃ dhṛtvā vṛṣaṃ śubhe ।
bodhayitvā prajāś cāpi sthāpanīyāḥ sadā śubhe ।। evaṃ cet te sadāpy evaṃ sarvatrāpi sumaṃgalaṃ । bhaven nūnaṃ mahārājan satyam etan na saṃśayaḥ । dharmeṇa nirjitaṃ pāpaṃ dharmeṇa jīyate kudhīḥ । dharmeṇa nirjitā mārā dharmeṇa bodhim āpnuyāt । tasmād bodhipadaṃ prāptuṃ yadīcchatha narādhipaḥ । bodhicittaṃ samādhāya sadā ratnatrayaṃ bhaja । tathā taṃ kramaṇo rāja bodhicaryyāhitāya ca । sarvamāragaṇām jitvā saṃbodhim āpnuyā dhruvaṃ । etat tenopaguptena guruṇādiṣṭaṃ samādarāt । śrutvā rājo tathety evaṃ pratyanandan sapārṣadaḥ । ye śṛṇvantīdam evaṃ praṇihitamanasaḥ sārthavāhāvadānaṃ । ye cāpi śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ sarvalokahitārthaṃ । te sarve bodhisatvā vijitakalimalo buddhadharmānuraktāḥ । saṃbhuktvā satsukhāni prathitaguṇayutā buddhakṣetre prayānti । oṃ namaḥ śrīsarvabuddhabodhisatvebhyaḥ । yaḥ śrīmāñ chrīghano loke saddharmaiḥ samupādiśat ।
śāsanāni trilokeṣu jayantu tasya sarvadā ।। avadānatatvaṃ vakṣyāmi natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ guruṃ । purābhūt pāṭalīputre nagare svargasannibhe ।। aśoko nṛparājendras triratnasevakaḥ kṛtī ।
ekasmin samaye tatra sa rājā svajanaiḥ saha ।। paurikaiś ca sabhāṃ kṛtvā saddharmaṃ śrotum aicchata । tadā sa saugato bhikṣur upagupto jināṃśajaḥ ।। lokān dharmotsukān dṛṣṭvā samādheḥ sahasotthitaḥ ।
tatsabhāyāṃ samākramya siṃhāsane śubhāsane ।। bhāsayaṃs tatsabhālokāṃs tasthau pūrṇasudhāṃśuvat । athāśoko mahīpālaḥ sa maṃtripaurikaiḥ saha ।। pūjāṅgaiḥ pūjayitvā tam upaguptam avandata ।
sthitvā bhūmau svajānubhyām uttarāsaṅgam udvahan ।। kṛtāñjaliḥ puṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata । bhadanta śrotum icchāmi saddharmaṃ sukhasaṃpradaṃ ।। yathoktaṃ śrīmunīndreṇa tathā deṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।
evaṃ tena mahīndreṇa prārthite sa yatīśvaraḥ ।। upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samāmantryaivam abravīt । sādhu suṣṭhu mahārāja śṛṇu saddharmam ādarāt ।। yathā me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā vakṣyāmi te hite ।
purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śakyasiṃho śubhākaraḥ ।। dharmarājo jagacchāstā sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ । sarvavidyākalāvijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ ।। mārajil lokavin nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ ।
śrāvastyāṃ jetakāraṇye mahodyāne manorame ।। anāthapiṇḍadākhyasya gṛhasthasya mahātmanaḥ । nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāpuṣpapraśobhitaiḥ ।। nānāphalabharānamraiḥ kalpavṛkṣasamānikaiḥ ।
aṣṭāṅgaguṇasaṃpannajalaiḥ padmotpālādibhiḥ ।। supuṣpaiḥ paripūrṇābhiḥ puṣkariṇībhir āśrite । nānājantuguṇaiś cāpi mithaḥ snehānuvandhitaiḥ ।। nānāpakṣigaṇaiś cāpi saṃharṣair upasevite ।
tasmiṃ divyamanoramye munisaṃghaniṣevite ।। puṇyakṣetre jināvāse vihāre maṇimaṇḍite । śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvair upāsakaiḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena tasthau dharmmaṃ prakāśituṃ । evaṃ tatra sabhāsīnaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ dharmabhāṣiṇaṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā dharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarvalokāḥ samāyayuḥ ।। daivā daityāś ca siddhāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । grahā vidyādharāḥ sādhyā nāgeṃdrā garuḍā api ।। sarve api lokapālāś ca munayaś ca maharṣayaḥ ।
yatayo yoginaś cāpi tīrthikāś ca tapaśvinaḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ । amātyāḥ koṭṭavārāś ca sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ ।। śilpino vaṇijaś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā janāḥ ।
tathā jānapadāś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api ।। evam anye api satvāś ca sarvajātisamudbhavāḥ । pūjāpaṃcopahārāṇi gṛhītvā bhaktimānasā ।। saddharmaṃ śraddhayā śrotum anumodya samāyayuḥ ।
tatra sarve praviṣṭās te dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ jinaṃ ।। vanditvānanditāḥ sarve pūjāṃ cakrur yathākramaṃ ।। tato natvā samāsīnāḥ parivṛtya pramoditāḥ । dharmmaṃ śrotuṃ puraskṛtya tasthuḥ sāñjalayo mudā ।।
atha sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃl lokān dharmavāñchinaḥ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। evaṃ sa bhagavān nityaṃ sarvasatvahitārthikaḥ । dharmaṃ prakāśayaṃ loke tasthau dīptāṃśumān iva ।।
tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāṃ purisaṃbhavaḥ । āḍhyaḥ śreṣṭhī mahābhogaḥ suvistīrṇaparigrahaḥ ।। śrāddho bhadrāśayo dhīraḥ sarvalokasuhṛtpriyaḥ । tīrthikasevako mānī vabhūva śrīmadānvitaḥ ।।
tadā sa sundarībhāryāṃ kuladharmasamānikāṃ । ādāya ratisaṃrakto reme nityaṃ yathāsukhaṃ ।। tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya bhāryā sābhūt sugarbhiṇī । tataḥ pravṛddhagarbhā sā pāṇḍuvarṇā vyarājata ।।
tataḥ sā garbhasaṃjātaṃ putraṃ tasyām upāśritaṃ । putraṃ matvābhinaṃdaṃtī bharttāram evam abravīt ।। svāmin garbhe prajāto me yat kukṣau dakṣiṇāśritaḥ । dārako ayaṃ bhavet putraḥ nūnaṃ tasmāt pramodaya ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ praharṣitaḥ । garbhe sa vyāśritaṃ dṛṣṭvā mudaivaṃ samudānayat ।। vata me jāyate putras tad ahaṃ bhāgyavān bhave । putramukhaṃ hi paśyeyaṃ vaṃśasthitir bhaved api ।।
yan mama vidyate puṇyaṃ dānaśīlādisaṃcitaṃ । tenānayor dvayor astu jananīputrayoḥ śivaṃ ।। evaṃ proktvā gṛhasthaḥ sa śraddhayā saṃpramoditaḥ । bhikṣvarthibrāhmaṇebhyaś ca dadau dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ ।।
kuleṣṭadevatāś cāpi samabhyarcya yathāvidhi । tac chubhaṃ prārthayan nityaṃ tasthau putrasamutsukaḥ ।। tataḥ sā bhadrikā nārī pathyopacārabhoginī । asūta samaye putraṃ suṃdaraṃ lakṣaṇānvitaṃ ।।
tataḥ sa janakaḥ śrutvā saṃprajātaṃ sutaṃ mudā । sahasā samupāsritya dadarśa taṃ sasuṃdaraṃ ।। darśanīyaṃ subhadrāṅgaṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ । dṛṣṭvāpi suciraṃ paśyann eva tasthāv atṛptitaḥ ।।
tato jātimahaṃ kṛtvā tasya pitrā prasādinā । vaḍika iti nāmnā prakhyāpito abhūt sa dārakaḥ ।। tataḥ sa vālako aṣṭābhyo dhātrībhyaḥ pratipālane । mānayitvānusaṃbhāṣya pitrā samarpito abhavat ।।
tathā sa vaḍiko vālo aṣṭābhir dhātrībhir ādarāt । pālyamānaḥ pravṛddho abhūt hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ ।। yadā sa dārakaḥ paṃcavarṣito abhūn madānvitaḥ । tadā vidyopalabdhārthī lipiśālām upāviśat ।।
tatra sa sadguruṃ natvā kramāl lipīn mudāgrahīt । gurubhaktiprasādena lipipāraṃ yayau laghu ।। tataḥ sa gurubhiḥ samyac chiṣyamāṇaḥ subuddhimān । adhītya sarvaśāstrāṇi vidyāpāraṃ yayau laghu ।।
tadā tad vaḍikasyāpi pūrvakarmavipākataḥ । dehe kasmāt samutpanno mahāvyādhiḥ parākramat ।। tadā sa vyādhinā tena pīḍyamāno abhimūrchitaḥ । asahyavedanākrānto virurāva divāniśaṃ ।।
tathā taṃ vyādhināghrātam asahyavedanāturaṃ । krandantaṃ sa pitā dṛṣṭvā kṛpayaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। hā me daivaviruddhena putro ayaṃ vyādhimūrchitaḥ । asahyavedanākrānto bhoktum api na vāñchati ।।
avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ yāyāt kathaṃ jīved abhuktavān । mṛte putre mariṣye ahaṃ snehaduḥkhaṃ kathaṃ sahe ।। iti cintāvyathākrānto bhogye api viratotsavaḥ । tam eva svātmajaṃ paśyaṃs tasthau snehābhivandhitaḥ ।।
mātāpi taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā snehaduḥkhāgnitāpitā । mṛtyuśaṃkā paritrastā rudantī samupācarat ।। tadā tasya suhṛnmitravāṃdhavāḥ samupāgatāḥ । sarve te rogiṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā snehārttā evam abruvan ।। kiṃ bho svasthaṃ na te dehe bhoktuṃ kiṃ vā na vāñchasi ।
bhuṃkṣva yathepsitaṃ pathyaṃ tiṣṭha dhairyaṃ samāśrayan ।। iti prokte api taiḥ sarvaiḥ sa vaḍiko jvarānvitaḥ । dṛṣṭvaiva tān muhuḥ paśyan naiva kiñcid abhāṣata ।। tataḥ sarve api te dṛṣṭvā taṃ vaḍikaṃ rujāturaṃ ।
mṛtyuśaṃkāviṣādigdhaṃ pitaraṃ taṃ tathāvadan ।। sādho asya varddhate rogas tad rogavyupāśāntaye । sahasā vaidyam āhūya darśayasva samāhitaḥ ।। upadiṣṭaṃ yathā tena vaidyena sudhiyā tathā ।
paricaryyāṃ samādhāya kurūpacāram ādarāt ।। tathā pathyopacāreṇa siddhauṣadhyasahair api । kramād asya śarīrastho rogaḥ śāntiṃ vrajed dhruvaṃ ।। tatas te ayaṃ suto bhadraḥ paripuṣṭatanuḥkṛtī ।
svakuladharmam ādhāya sukhaṃ jīvec chubhe caran ।। iti matvā mahābhāga mā kṛthās tad viṣādanaṃ । dhairyam ālamvya devāṃś ca smṛtvā bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa ।। ity evaṃ samupādiśya tad gṛhasthāt samutthitāḥ ।
sarve te snehaduḥkhārttāḥ svasvageham upācarat ।। tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛt tasya putrasya rogaśāṃtaye । sadvaidyaṃ samupāhūya sādaraṃ samadarśayat ।। tasya roganimittaṃ sa vaidyo dṛṣṭvā samīkṣya ca ।
pathyauṣadhyupacāreṇa samāhita upācarat ।। tathāpi tasya tadrogaḥ parivṛddho dine dine । kenāpi hy upacāreṇa naiva śāntim upāyayau ।। tadrogaṃ varddhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā janakaḥ sa viṣāditaḥ ।
bhūtikaṃ sahasāhūya rogahetum apṛcchata ।। tataḥ sa bhūtiko dṛṣṭvā tasya rogapraśāntaye । sa bhūtadevatābhyaś ca valiṃ prādād yathāvidhi ।। tathāpi vṛṃhito rogas tasya karmavipākataḥ ।
kiñcid api viśeṣeṇa naiva śāntim upāyayau ।। tataḥ sa janako dṛṣṭvā tad rogaṃ parivarddhitaṃ । āyurvidam upāmaṃtrya rogahetum apṛcchata ।। sa ayurvidako dṛṣṭvā tasya grahadaśāphalaṃ ।
kudaśāvyupaśāntyarthaṃ grahapūjām upādiśat ।। tathā sa janakas tasya rogiṇo grahaśāntaye । brāhmaṇaṃ samupāmantrya grahapūjām akārayat ।। tathāpi tasya tadrogo varddhito na śamaṃ yayau ।
daivena samupāghrāte tadupāye na siddhyate ।। tathā sa janakas tasya putrasya rogavṛddhitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā nirāśayā bhinnacitto mūrcchām upāyayau ।। tadā sā supriyā bhāryā bharttāraṃ taṃ vimohitaṃ ।
dṛṣṭvaiva samupāgṛhya samāśvāsyaivam abravīt ।। svāmin dhairyyaṃ samālambya tyaja citte vimohatāṃ । kim asmākaṃ prayatnena daivasyātra pramāṇike ।। sarvathā bhāvino bhāvāḥ phalaṃti sarvajīvināṃ ।
yad abhāvi na tad bhāvi bhāvi cen na tad anyathā ।। tasmād daivaprasādāya svakuleśeṣṭadevatāḥ । anusmṛtya samārādhya yācasva putrajīvitaṃ ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhastho anumoditaḥ ।
kuladevaṃ samabhyarcya prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। prasīda me kuleśa tvaṃ kṣamasva hy aparādhatāṃ । tavaiva śaraṇastho ahaṃ tan me putraṃ prarakṣatāṃ ।। evaṃ tena gṛhasthena prārthite api divāniśaṃ ।
tasya rogo vivṛddho abhūn naiva śāmyam upākramat ।। tathā brahmādidevāṃś ca sarvān lokādhipān api । vihāramaṇḍapārāmakṣetrāraṇyasamāśritān ।। nadīkūpataḍāgādijalāśrayapratisthitān ।
balibhoktṝn kalaṃkasthān mārgaśṛṅgāṭakāśritān ।। evam anyatra sarvatra pratisthitān samarcayan । putrasyārogyakauśalyaṃ jīvitaṃ sa samarthayan ।। tathāpi tasya rogo na śamito abhūt pravarddhitaḥ ।
tatas taṃ janako dṛṣṭvā nirāśā mūrchito apatat ।। tadā sa vaḍiko rogī pitaraṃ taṃ vimūrchitaṃ । pṛthivyāṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śanair nīcasvaro avadat ।। hā hā me jāvate pāpaṃ yenāyaṃ patitaḥ pitā । snehaduḥkhāgnisaṃtaptaḥ putrato maraṇaṃ vrajet ।।
hā tātottiṣṭha māṃ paśya mā tyajātmajaṃ āturaṃ । dhairyyam ālamvya saṃdhāya rakṣa māṃ samupasthitaḥ ।। ity asau vilapan putraḥ pitaraṃ taṃ vimūrchitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā bhojanakety aśru muñcaṃs tasthau nirāśritaḥ ।।
tadā sā supriyā bhāryyā bharttāraṃ taṃ vimūrchitaṃ । dṛṣṭvaiva sahasāliṃgya samutthāpyaivam abravīt ।। svāmin dhairyaṃ samālaṃbya paśya māṃ te priyaṃ satīṃ । tyaktvā dainyaṃ samādhāya paśyan rakṣātmakaṃ priyaṃ ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhastho samutthitaḥ । dṛṣṭvā tāṃ supriyāṃ bhāryāṃ putraṃ caivam abhāṣata ।। hā daiva kiṃ mayā pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ dāruṇaṃ purā । yenāyaṃ sukṛtī putraḥ tyaktvā māṃ kva prayāsyati ।।
hā hā me saṃpadaś caitāḥ samṛddhāḥ samupārjitāḥ । ko nu bhoktā bhaved āsāṃ vyarthaṃ nakṣyanti sarvaśaḥ ।। kim atrāhaṃ kariṣyāmi yāsyāmi śaraṇaṃ ca kaṃ । ko nu māṃ sahasā rakṣed datvā putrasya jīvitaṃ ।।
kim atrāsya rujaḥ śāntyai kariṣyāmi pratikriyāṃ । na jāne parimūḍho asmi cetanā me na vidyate ।। iti cintāparītātmā putrasnehavimohitaḥ । kāruṇākulacitto api punar evaṃ vyacintayat ।।
yad ime tīrthikā vijñā bhagavanto vicakṣaṇāḥ । sarvajñāḥ sadguṇādhārāḥ śāstāro me hitaṃkarāḥ ।। tat tān sarvān samāmaṃtrya gṛhe bhokṣyaiḥ samarcayan । imaṃ putraṃ puraḥ sthāpya darśayeyaṃ śubhāptaye ।।
tat sudṛṣṭiprasādena nūnam asya bhavec chuvaṃ । tato hi kramaśo rogāḥ śāmyeyuḥ sarvathā laghu ।। tadāyam ātmajaḥ puṣṭo na rogī sutanuḥ sukhī । kṛtī śubharato bhogī kuladharme samācaret ।।
iti niścitya sa śreṣṭhī tatra tīrthyāśrame gataḥ । tān sarvāṃs tīrthikān natvā prārthayed evam ādarāt ।। namo vo brahmavijñebhyo bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । vijñapyate yad arthaṃ tad anugrahītum arhata ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikās te abhimānikāḥ । sarve taṃ samupāmaṃtrya pramodayitum abruvan ।। sādhu vada mahāsādho yat te kāryaṃ samīhitaṃ । tat sarvaṃ sarvathāsmābhiḥ kṛtam evaṃ kariṣyate ।।
iti tais tīrthikaiḥ prokte sa śreṣṭhī saṃprasāditaḥ । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhagavanto mahāvijñā bhavanto guravo mama । tat sarvaṃ pratijānīta yad arthaṃ samupācare ।।
tathāpi cārthayiṣye atra yan me kaṣṭaṃ pravarttate । tad vo vijñāpanaṃ kartuṃ bhavataḥ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tena me svātmajādhunā । rogaiḥ saṃpīḍyate atīvaniḥsvastho maraṇaṃ vrajet ।।
nānāsvastividhānair hi tasya rogo na śāmyati । bhiṣajāṃ kṛtayatnāni na siddhyanti kathaṃ cana ।। anekā devatāś cāpi prābhyarcya prārthito mayā । tathāpi śāmyate naiva tasya rogo vivarddhitaḥ ।।
yathā yathā rujāśāntisvastyupāyakṛtāni hi । tathā tathā na tadrogaḥ praśāmyati pravarddhyate ।। kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi kena śāmyeta tadgadaḥ । tad upāyaṃ pradātavyaṃ yenāśu śāmyate kramāt ।।
iti vijñāpanāṃ kartuṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tan me anukampayāsu no rogaśāntir vidhīyatāṃ ।। bhavanto me anuśāstāraḥ sarvajñā brahmacāriṇaḥ । tan me sukṛpayā dṛṣṭyā paritrātuṃ samarhata ।।
iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te tīrthikā api । śreṣṭhinaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samabruvan ।। śṛṇu sādho yad asmābhir hitārthaṃ te pracakṣyatāṃ । tat satyaṃ naḥ parijñāya pramāṇīkriyatāṃ kila ।।
vayaṃ hi sarvalokānāṃ śāstāro hitasādhakāḥ । tasmād atra viṣādatvaṃ mā kṛthā dhairyam āśraya ।। adyaiva sahasā gatvā vayaṃ dṛṣṭvā tavātmajaṃ । niḥpāpaṃ nīrujaṃ svāsthyaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ sujīvitaṃ ।।
apy etad vacanaṃ satyaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā pramāṇaya । anyathā na bhavet kvāpi hy asmākaṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ ।। iti tais tīrthikaiḥ proktaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasattamaḥ । tatheti pratiharṣitvā natvā tān svagṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa gṛha āsādya dāsidāsajanaiḥ saha ।
tadarhabhojyapūjāṅgasāmagrīṃ samasādhayat ।। tasminn eva kṣaṇe tatra sarve te tīrthikā mudā । sahasā samupāgatya svasvāsane upāviśat ।। tathā tān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā śreṣṭhī sa moditaḥ ।
pūjāṅgaiḥ kramato abhyarcya bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। tataś ca bhojanānte sa vaḍikaṃ taṃ priyātmajaṃ । rogiṇaṃ samupāhṛtya teṣāṃ puro abhyadarśayat ।। te sarve tīrthikā dṛṣṭvā vaḍikaṃ taṃ rujānvitaṃ ।
tadāmayanimittaṃ ca nirīkṣyaivam upādiśat ।। aho hy asya mahārogaṃ mahāpātakasaṃbhavaṃ । tatpātakavimuktyai tu dātavyaṃ dānam ādarāt ।। tadyathā navaratnāni hemalakṣapalāni ca ।
śraddhayā brahmacāribhyaḥ saṃpradadyāt samarcayan ।। yady etad dīyate dānaṃ tvayā gṛhapate tathā । bhagnakuṣmāṇḍadarinamahiṣīśatadakṣiṇā ।। purā dattā naṃdarājñā asmākaṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ ।
pādasphoṭāmayas tasya śāṃto abhūt tatprabhāvataḥ ।। tathāsya sarvapāpāni vinakṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ । tataḥ sarve api rogāś ca vinakṣyanti kramād drutaṃ ।। tato rogair vimukto ayaṃ kuśalī svāsthyam āpnuyāt ।
tataḥ puṣṭo viśuddhāṅgaḥ suśīlaḥ sukṛtī sudhīḥ । svakulācāradharmiṣṭho vaṃśāṃś cāpi samuddharet ।। iti matvā tvayā sādho dātavyaṃ dānam ādarāt । anyathā na bhavet svasti tavāsya naṃdanasya ca ।।
iti tair gaditaṃ śrutvā sa śreṣṭhī paribodhitaḥ । tasyātmajasya trāṇārthaṃ tathā dātum udācarat ।। tataḥ sa punar abhyarcya tān sarvāns tīrthikān patīn । pradadau navaratnāni svarṇalakṣapalāni ca ।।
tatas te tīrthikāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā tāni pramoditāḥ । sarvāny api pratigṛhya tathāśīrvacanaṃ daduḥ ।। svasty astu te sadā sādho kalyāṇam astu sarvathā । nīrogī suciraṃ jīvyā jayo astu te samantataḥ ।। etad eva samādiśya sarve te tīrthikās tataḥ ।
tāni sarvāṇi vastūni pratigṛhyāśramaṃ yayuḥ ।। tathāpi tasya rogā na śamitā varddhitāḥ kramāt । svadaivaphalabhogyāni bhoktavyāni hi sarvathā ।। tatas taj janako dṛṣṭvā svātmajaṃ taṃ rujāturaṃ ।
nirāśāmūrchito bhūmau nipataṃ vyalapat tathā ।। hā daiva kiṃ mayā pāpaṃ dāruṇaṃ prakṛtaṃ purā । yato ayaṃ svātmajaḥ putraḥ puro me maraṇaṃ vrajet ।। kṛtāny upāyayatnāni dānāni vividhāni ca ।
sarvāṇy etāni matpāpair nisphalāni bhavanti hi ।। kiṃ mayātrāpi karttavyaṃ ko atra me hitam ādiśet । sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo asmi ko api trātā na vidyate ।। kasyātra śaraṇaṃ yāsye ko no rakṣed dayādṛśā ।
sarve vayaṃ vinaṣṭāsma hā daiva śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। ity evaṃ vilapaṃtaṃ taṃ janakaṃ vaḍiko api saḥ । dṛṣṭvā śanaiḥ samāhūya pura evam abhāṣata ।। bho tāta kiṃ tvayātrāpi karttavyaṃ hi mayāpi ca ।
sarveṣām api jantūnāṃ daivagatiḥ pramāṇikā ।। iti matvā viṣādatvaṃ hṛdaye mā kṛthās tyaja । saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityam anusmaran ।। buddha eva jagacchāstā trātā lokahitaṃkaraḥ ।
durgatitārako nātho bharttā sadgatināyakaḥ ।। tad evaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā saddharmaṃ samupāśrayan । saṃghānāṃ bhajanaṃ kṛtvā cinu puṇyaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। triratne sādhitaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇuyāt kadā cana ।
yadi daivād vipattiḥ syāt puṇyaṃ tu labhate varaṃ ।। puṇyena rakṣyate lokaḥ puṇyena sadgatiṃ vrajet । tasmāt puṇyaṃ mahāratnaṃ cinu dhairyaṃ samāśrayan ।। avaśyamaraṇe loke kiṃ viṣādena siddhyate ।
iti matvāpi taṃ buddhaṃ smṛtvā bhaja samāhitaḥ ।। tathāhaṃ vā tam evātra saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajan । saṃsmṛtvā bhajanaṃ kurvan vrajeya maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। yadi tasya jinendrasya kṛpāsti mayi pāpini । tatkṛpādṛkprasādena jīveya nīrujaḥ punaḥ ।।
yadi daivabalenāhaṃ mṛte tatsmṛtipuṇyataḥ । sarvathā durgatiṃ tyaktvā sadgatiṃ punar āpnuyāṃ ।। evaṃ jñātvā tvayā tāta mā kriyatāṃ viṣādatā । saṃsāre avaśyaṃ marttavyaṃ sarveṣām api janmināṃ ।।
ity uktvā sa rujārtto api vaḍiko dhairyyam āśrayan । saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā smṛtvā tasthau samāhitaḥ ।। tathā sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī śrutvaitad ātmajoditaṃ । satyam etat parijñāya buddhaṃ smṛtvā tathāvadat ।।
namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya ca sadā smare । adyārabhya sadā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। yadi vo asti kṛpā loke rakṣantu naḥ suduḥkhinaḥ । sarvathā kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭvāśu trātum arhati ।।
yathānye tribhave lokā bhavadbhiḥ pratipālitāḥ । tathāsmān kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā trātum arhati sarvathā ।। rakṣatu bhagavan nātha jīvayeyaṃ mamātmajaṃ । kṛpayānugrahaṃ kṛtvā putraratnaṃ prayaccha me ।।
yadi jīved ayaṃ putro bhavaddṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitvā caratu vratam ādarāt ।। ity evaṃ smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ vrajan । sa śreṣṭhī taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthau mohavinoditaḥ ।।
tasminn eva kṣaṇe lokāṃ trātuṃ sa bhagavān muniḥ । saṃpaśyan kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā prādrākṣīt tān saduḥkhinaḥ ।। tathā tān duḥkhino dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa jineśvaraḥ । sahasā tān paritrātuṃ buddharasmiṃ vyamuñcata ।।
tābhiḥ kanakavarṇābhiḥ saṃbuddharaśmibhis tadā । samantāt samatikramya tad gṛham avabhāsitaṃ ।। tato maitryaṃśavaś cāpi tena bhagavatā punaḥ । samutṣṛṣṭās tanau tasya paryaspṛśan prasāditāḥ ।।
tatas tasya tanus taiḥ saṃspṛṣṭamātre samaṃtataḥ । prahlāditā sukhaprāptā svāsthyatāṃ samupāyayau ।। tataḥ sa vaḍikaḥ svāsthyaṃ prāpya nirmalamānasaḥ । vismitaḥ pitaraṃ paśyan samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।।
aho buddhasya māhātmyam aho dharmānubhāvatā । aho saṃghaprabhāvatvaṃ paśya tāta muneḥ prabhāṃ ।। yasyānusmṛtimātreṇa kṛpā loke prasāryate । dhanyo ayaṃ bhagavān buddho jayatv evaṃ sadā sthitaḥ ।।
yasya dayānubhāvena jīvema nīrujaḥ sukhī । pāpaiś cāpi vimukto aham iti satyaṃ pramanyate ।। tasmāt tam eva śāstāraṃ saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । yāvadbhavam anusmṛtvā bhajeya samupāśritaḥ ।।
evaṃ buddhaguṇān smṛtvā vaḍikaḥ sa pramoditaḥ । kṛtāñjaliḥ smaran bhūyaḥ praṇatvaivam ayācata ।। namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । yāvadbhavaṃ triratnānāṃ bhaveyaṃ sevakaḥ sadā ।।
ity evaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā vaḍikaḥ so abhibodhitaḥ । bhūyo bhūyaḥ smaran natvā tasthau svāsthyatvam āgataḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān buddho dṛṣṭvā taṃ śuddhamānasaṃ । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ tad dvāre samupāsarat ।।
taddvārasamupāsīnaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ raviprabhaṃ । dṛṣṭvaiva vismito dvāsthaḥ sahasā gṛham āviśat ।। tatra gṛhapatiṃ dṛṣṭvā vaḍikaṃ taṃ ca sādaraṃ । purataḥ samupetyaiva vyajñāpayat sasatvaraḥ ।।
gṛhapate munīndro atra gṛhadvāra upasthitaḥ । tad atra sahasopetya samāmaṃtrya praveśaya ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā vaḍikaḥ sa prasāditaḥ । utthitaḥ sahasopetya taṃ munīndraṃ mudānamat ।।
natvā taṃ sugataṃ gehe prajñapya svāsanaṃ mudā । vijñapya samupāmaṃtrya praveśayaṃs tathārthayan ।। svāgataṃ bhagavan vāṃche bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ mune । praviśatu jagannātha vijayasvāsane śubhe ।।
iti tenodite buddho bhagavān sa samāviśan । svāsane samupāsīno vaḍikaṃ taṃ tathāvadat ।। kiṃ te vaḍika duḥkhatvaṃ vādhakaś ca kathaṃ vada । iti bhagavatā pṛṣṭo vaḍikaḥ sa tathāvadat ।।
kāyikaṃ jāyate duḥkhaṃ cetasikaṃ ca me mune । tad bhavān kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā śamayet tat prabādhanaṃ ।। iti tad vijñāpitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । taccittaduḥkhaśāntyarthaṃ maitrīdharmam upādiśat ।। vaḍikātra sadā loke maitracittaṃ samācara ।
anena te manodāhaṃ praśāmyeta sadāpi hi ।। ity ādiśya munīndraḥ sa punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat । vatendrakṣīrikāṃ nāma mahauṣadhāṃ samānayet ।। iti cittamataṃ śāstuḥ parijñāya surādhipaḥ ।
ādāya kṣīrikāṃ nāma mahauṣadhīm upānayat ।। tatra so surarājas taṃ bhagavantaṃ praṇamya tāṃ । mahauṣadhīm upasthāpya pura evaṃ samabravīt ।। bhagavan pratigṛhṇātu divyauṣadhīm imāṃ bhavān ।
anayātra yathākāryaṃ sādhayatu sukhāptaye ।। ity ukte tena śakreṇa dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhagavān muniḥ । gṛhītvā vaḍikāyaivaṃ pradatvā caivam ādiśat ।। gṛhāṇa vaḍikemāṃ te kāyikaduḥkhaśāminīṃ ।
anayā te śarīre saṃskriyatām upacāraṇaiḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa vaḍikaḥ so anumoditaḥ । tatheti tāṃ samādāya yathādiṣṭam upācarat ।। tatas tasya tanū rogair vimuktā paripuṣṭitā ।
krameṇa śāmyasaundaryaṃ prāpyābhiparyaśobhata ।। tataḥ śāstrā yathādiṣṭaṃ vaḍikena tathā hṛdi । maitrī prabhāvitā loke svātmaje supriye yathā ।। tadā tasya mahadduḥkhaṃ cetasikaṃ śaśāma tat ।
mahāmaitryā pariṣikte hṛdaye agnir ivāmbubhiḥ ।। tataḥ sa vaḍikaḥ svasthaḥ pariśuddhendriyaḥ sudhīḥ । bhagavantaṃ tam ānamya prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। vande ahaṃ bhavatāṃ pādau sarvadā śaraṇaṃ vraje ।
tathā ca sarvadā nātha kṛpayā trātum arhati ।। yady evaṃ bhavatāṃ śāstaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭir na vidyate । mṛto ahaṃ narake adyāpi gato duḥkhāny avāpnuyāṃ ।। yad evaṃ svasthito jīve tat te kṛpāmbubhāvataḥ ।
tathā me anugrahaṃ kartuṃ nityam arhati sarvadā ।। ity evaṃ prārthanāṃ kṛtvā bhūyaḥ sa vaḍiko mudā । sāñjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā paśyaṃs tasthau munīśvaraṃ ।। tathā tajjanakaḥ śreṣṭhī sadāraḥ saṃpramoditaḥ ।
triratne śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ samarcayat ।। tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ mudā । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। vande te caraṇau śāstaḥ sarvadā śaraṇaṃ vraje ।
evaṃ no anugrahaṃ kartuṃm arhati kṛpayā sadā ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān buddhas tathāstv iti samādiśat । ṛddhyākāśaṃ samutplutya svam āśramam upāyayau ।। tatra sa bhagavān prāptaḥ sabhāmadhye samāśritaḥ ।
etad vṛṣṭi samākhyāya tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat ।। tadā sa vaḍiko bhūyo buddhaguṇān anusmaran । sa saṃghaṃ sugataṃ bhojyaiḥ pūjayituṃ samaichata ।। tadā sa nṛpate rājñaḥ prasenajita ānataḥ ।
etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivam abhāṣata ।। rājann ahaṃ mahārogī triratnaśaraṇaṃ vraje । tat triratnakṛpādṛṣṭer jīve rogair vimocitaḥ ।। tan mayā sa munīndro api sarvasaṃghaiḥ sahādhunā ।
samāmaṃtrya gṛhe bhojyaiḥ pūjayituṃ samicchyate ।। tan me anugrahaṇaṃ kṛtvā lokānāṃ puṇyavṛddhaye । tadadhivāsanāṃ kṛtvā samanujñāpaya prabho ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa rājābhyanumoditaḥ ।
vaḍikaṃ taiḥ samālokya praśaṃsyaiva samādiśat ।। vaḍika tvaṃ mahāsādhus tad buddhaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । tathānuśraddhayā nityaṃ bhaja ratnatrayaṃ sadā ।। iti rājñābhyanujñātaṃ śrutvā sa vaḍiko mudā ।
nṛpatiṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ svagṛhaṃ samupāyayau ।। tatra gṛhe samāsādya kṛtvānumataṃ pituḥ । śāstu nimaṃtraṇāṃ kartuṃ vihāre samudācaran ।। tatra sa samupāviṣṭo dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavaṃs tad vijānīyād yadarthaṃ samupāvraje । tathāpy atra bhavadagre prārthaye anugrahaṃ kuru ।। yad ahaṃ roganirmuktaḥ puna janma ivāptavān ।
tad bhavatāṃ kṛpādṛṣṭeḥ prasādād itin manyate ।। tad ahaṃ bhavatāṃ sarvasaṃghānāṃ bhojanair gṛhe । pūjayituṃ samiche tad anugrahītum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sa bhagavān muniḥ ।
tathety abhyanumoditvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa vaḍiko matvā bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ । mudā tasya muneḥ pādau natvāśu svagṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa sahasā gehe vandhumitrajanaiḥ saha ।
saṃghārhabhojyapūjāṅgaṃ sāmagrīṃ samasādhayat ।। tataḥ sa sarvasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvāsanāni ca । prajñapya śuddhite bhūmau maṃdayitvā samantataḥ ।। tatas taṃ śrīghanaṃ buddhaṃ sasaṃghaṃ svajanaiḥ saha ।
āmaṃtrituṃ vihāre sa sahasā samupācarat ।। tatra sa samupāviṣṭo dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā । sasaṃghaṃ sāṃjalir natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan sādhyate sādhyaṃ samayo varttate adhunā ।
tad bhavāṃ sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vijayituṃ samarhati ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā tatheti sa munīśvaraḥ । pātracīvaram ādhāya sarvasaṃghaiḥ sahācarat ।। tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra nagare ca samantataḥ ।
prakāśayan prātihāryaṃ tad gṛhaṃ samupāviśat ।। tatra gṛhe samāsādya pādārghaṃ pratigṛhya saḥ । svāsane samupāviśya kramāt tasthau sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tadā sa vaḍiko dṛṣṭvā taṃ buddhaṃ svāsane sthitaṃ ।
sasaṃghaṃ sarvapūjāṅgaiḥ sarvapuṣpaiḥ samarcayat ।। tataś ca surasair bhojyaiḥ supraṇītaiḥ suhādhitaiḥ । varṇagandharasopetaiḥ sarvais tāṃ samatoṣayat ।। tataś ca bhojanānte sa pātrādīny apanīya ca ।
mukhādīṃ śodhayitvā ca pūgauṣadhīn praḍhaukayat ।। tataḥ sa prāñjalir natvā sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ mudā । purastho manasā hy evaṃ praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt smaran ।। anena kuśalenāhaṃ loke andhe apariṇāyake ।
yathāyaṃ bhagavān buddhas tathā bhūyāsam ātmavit ।। yathānena munīndreṇa jagal loko abhipālitaḥ । tathāhaṃ sarvalokānāṃ pālayeyaṃ samantataḥ ।। atīrṇāṃs tārayiṣyāmi mocayiṣyāmy amocitān ।
anāsvastān samāśvāsya sthāpayiṣyāmi nirvṛtau ।। ity evaṃ manasā tena praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā । matvā sa bhagavān buddho smitaṃ prāvirvyadhān mudā ।। tadā tasya munīndrasya mukhāt paṃca surasmayaḥ ।
nisṛtya triṣu lokeṣu bhāsayantaḥ samāsaran ।। yāpi kāś cid adholoke prasṛtā narakeṣu tāḥ । uṣṇeṣu śītalībhūtā śītaleṣu tathoṣṇikāḥ ।। tadā tābhiḥ parispṛṣṭāḥ sarve nairayikā janāḥ ।
mahatsaukhyaṃ samāsādya vismitāś caivam ālapat ।। aho saukhyaṃ kathaṃ hy evam anyatra kiṃ gatā vayaṃ । kasya puṇyānubhāvena kvāsmākaṃ jāyate sukhaṃ ।। iti cintābhidagdhānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane ।
bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ saṃpreṣya samadarśayat ।। tatra taṃ nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve api te mudā । vismitāḥ sahasaṃmīlya punar evaṃ vabhāṣire ।। aho samantabhadro ayaṃ puruṣo dṛśyate adhunā ।
nūnam asyānubhāvena saukhyaṃ no jāyate khalu ।। iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve tasmin buddhe prasāditāḥ । namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya ceti prāvadan ।। tataḥ sarve api te satvās triratnasmṛtipuṇyataḥ ।
te durgativinirmuktāḥ sadgatiṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। evaṃ tā raśmayaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ । sarvasatvān samuddhṛtya muneḥ pratyāyayuḥ punaḥ ।। tathā yā raśmayaḥ kāścid upariṣṭāt prasāritāḥ ।
tāḥ sarvān devalokānāṃ avabhāsya samantataḥ ।। yāvad bhavāgraparyaṃtaṃ bhāsayantaḥ prasāritāḥ । evaṃ cāpi mahāśabdam udghuṣya samudācaran ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ ।
tad bhave sadgatiṃ hitvā saddharmaṃ bhajatādarāt ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane । dhunīta mṛtyusainyaṃ ca naḍāgāram iva dvipaḥ ।। yo apy asmin dharmavaineye hy apramattaś caret sadā । sa hitvā jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।।
ity evaṃ tan mahāśabdaṃ śrutvā sarve api te surāḥ । tathety abhyanumodantas triratnaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। tathā tā arciṣaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ । punaḥ pratyāgatās tasya muner antikam āyayuḥ ।।
tatas tā arciṣaḥ sarvāḥ saṃmīlya samupāsthitāḥ । kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ traidham uṣṇīṣe antardadhau muneḥ ।। athānaṃdas tam ālokya vismitaḥ sahasotthitaḥ । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā paprachaivaṃ munīśvaraṃ ।।
bhagavan bhavato vaktrāt paṃcavarṇāḥ suraśmayaḥ । vinisṛtā diśaḥ sarvā bhāṣayanti samantataḥ ।। nākāraṇaṃ jinā buddhā darśayanti smitaṃ kvacit । bhavatsmitaṃ samālokya sarve bhavanti vismitāḥ ।।
taddhetu śrotum ichaṃti sarve apīme sabhāśritāḥ । tad eṣāṃ saṃśayaṃ chetuṃ taddhetu samupādiśa ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tāṃ ca sarvāṃ sabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā tathānandam abhāṣata ।।
paśyānaṃda mamānena vaḍikenānumodinā । saṃgheṣu śraddhayā bhaktyā satkṛtya bhajanaṃ kṛtaṃ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena vaḍiko ayaṃ sudhīḥ kṛtī । kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya daśabhūmīśvaro bhavan ।।
sarvamāragaṇāṃ jitvā saṃbodhiṃ samavāptavān । ślakṣṇavāṇyabhidho buddhas tathāgato bhaviṣyati ।। yad anena triratneṣu śaraṇaṃ saṃprasādinā । praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tena saṃbuddho ayaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ ।।
evaṃ matvā tathānaṃda triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । satkṛtya samupāśritya bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। ye satvāḥ śraddhayā smṛtvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । durgatiṃ te na gachanti bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ ।।
evaṃ matvā triratnānāṃ satkṛtya śraddhayā mudā । saṃsmṛtya śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktavyaṃ bodhivāṃchibhiḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sa moditaḥ । sāṃghikaṃ saha lokaiś ca tatheti prābhyanaṃdata ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasmai vaḍikāya subhāgine । datvāśīrvacanaṃ bhūyaḥ samāmaṃtrya tam abravīt ।। vaḍika tvaṃ mahābhāga triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । bodhicaryyāṃ caran nityaṃ saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ ।।
iti satyaṃ parijñāya sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt । tathā ratnatrayaṃ smṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। ity ādiśya munīndraḥ sa saṃghaiḥ sārddhaṃ samutthitaḥ । vaḍikaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya svavihāraṃ yayau tathā ।।
tathā sa vaḍiko nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । sadā lokahitaṃ kṛtvā bodhicaryāṃ samācarat ।। etan me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā narādhipa । tathā te kathyate rājaṃ śrutvā caivaṃ prakāśaya ।।
tathā tvayāpi rājendra satvānāṃ hitasādhane । triratnaśaraṇaiḥ kṛtvā karttavyā bodhicārikāḥ ।। tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatra maṃgalaṃ bhavet । kramād bodhicarīṃ pūrya saṃbodhim api cāpnuyāḥ ।।
iti matvā mahārāja prajāś cāpi prabodhayan । saddharme saṃpratisthāpya sarvathā trātum arhasi ।। iti tenopaguptena samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya saḥ । rājā tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
śrutvāvadānaṃ vaḍikasya sādhor idaṃ narā ye abhyanumodayanti । sarve api te lokahitānuraktā bhavanti bodhiguṇalābhikā hi ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ śrotum anyat subhāṣitaṃ । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tad yathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti tena narendreṇa prārthitaṃ sa jinātmajaḥ । śrutvā taṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evaṃ samādiśat ।।
śṛṇu rājan mayākhyātaṃ yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathā śrūtvānumoditvā śubhe caritum arhasi ।। purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śrāvastyāṃ bahir āśrame । jetāraṇye mahodyāne vihāre maṇimaṇḍite ।।
bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ cailakair vratibhis tathā । bhikṣuṇībhis tathānyaiś cā mahāsātvair upāsakaiḥ ।। vihṛtya sarvasatvānāṃ samitisthitaḥ । saṃbodhisādhānaṃ dharmam upādeṣṭuṃ samārabhat ।।
tadā tasya munīndrasya vaktrapadmād vinisṛtaṃ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve satvā upagatāḥ ।। brahmaśakrādi devendrāḥ sarve lokādhipā api । daityendrāḥ sagaṇā yakṣāḥ siddhagaṃdharvarākṣasāḥ ।।
vidyādharagaṇāś capi nāgeṃdrāś ca mahoragāḥ । garuḍāḥ kinnarendrāś ca tathānye api samāgatāḥ ।। brāhmaṇā ṛṣayaś cāpi tāpasā brahmacāriṇaḥ । yatayo yogino vijñās tathānye tīrthikā api ।।
rajānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vīrā rājakumārakāḥ । amātyā maṃtriṇaś cāpi vaiśyāś cāpi prajādhipāḥ ।। śreṣṭhino vaṇijaś cāpi sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ । paurā jānapadā grāmyās tathā kārpaṭikā api ।।
evaṃ anye api satvāś ca sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tad vihāre upāviśat ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā samabhyarcya praṇamya ca । satkṛtya samupāśritya parivṛtya sāmāntataḥ ।।
taṃ muṇīndraṃ samālokya śrotuṃ tad dharmadeśanāṃ । sāñjalayaḥ prasannāsyā upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tathā tān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāñ jinaḥ । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāḥ pramoditāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā vabhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। tadāpi paṃcamātrāṇi gāṃdharvikaśatāni ca । śrāvastyāṃ puri jātāni samadāni pracerire ।। tadā tāṃ samadān dṛṣṭvā gaṃdharvādhipateḥ sutaḥ ।
supriyo nāma tan mādam īrṣyayā hantum udyayau ।। tataḥ sa supriyaḥ sarvagāndharvikasukauśalaḥ । divyavīṇāṃ samādāya tatraiva samupācarat ।। saptasvarān ekataṃtryām ekaviṃśatimūrchanāḥ ।
samudghoṣayamānaḥ ca svamatiṃ darśayan yayau ।। ṣaṇmahānagareṣv evaṃ paṭṭaneṣu samantataḥ । samudghoṣayamānaś ca śrāvastīṃ sa upāviśat ।। tatra taṃ samupāviṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve api paurikāḥ ।
śrutvā tad adbhutaṃ nādaṃ vismitāḥ samupācaran ।। tāni ca paṃcamātrāṇi gāṃdharvikaśatāny api । śrutvā dṛṣṭvā ca sarvāṇi vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। tada tāni ca sarvāṇi dṛṣṭvā paṃcaśatāny api ।
svasvamadābhimānatvāṃ pravihāya viṣedire ।। tataḥ sarve api te tena sahavāde bhayānvitāḥ । nṛpater antikaṃ gatvā tat pravṛttiṃ nyavedayan ।। jaya prabho vijānīyād yad vayaṃ samupāgatāḥ ।
tad atra no bhayatrastāṃ trātum arhati sarvathā ।। atrāsau supriyo nāma gandharvādhipateḥ sutaḥ । nūnaṃ no madaghātāya vijetuṃ samupāgataḥ ।। tat tasyāpy abhimānatvāṃ nihaṃtuṃ satpratikriyāṃ ।
kriyatāṃ sahasāsmākam iti vijñāpanāṃ śṛṇu ।। iti vijñāpitaṃ sarvais taiḥ śrutvā sa narādhipaḥ । sarvāns tān samupāmaṃtrya pura evaṃ samādiśat ।। alpotsukā bhavanto atra bhavate mā viṣīdata ।
bhaviṣyāmo atra kālajñāś caratu sa yathechayā ।। iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te abhyanumoditāḥ । tad vivādabhayātaṃkaṃ tyaktvā sarve prasedire ।। tadā sa supriyas tatra dṛṣṭvā tān abhimānikān ।
teṣāṃ mānavighātārthaṃ manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। ayaṃ rājapi gāṃdharvavidyābhimāniko bhavet । tad anena sahātrāhaṃ vādaṃ kuryāṃ sabhāśraye ।। ity evaṃ niścayaṃ kṛtvā supriyaḥ so abhimānikaḥ ।
nṛpatiṃ tam upālabdhuṃ tat sabhāṃ samupācarat ।। tatra sa nṛpatir dṛṣṭvā supriyaṃ tam upāgataṃ । prajñapyāsanam āmaṃtrya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।। svāgataṃ te bhavann atra tiṣṭhāsane prasīda me ।
kim arthe atra samāyāsi tad ādeṣṭuṃ hi me arhasi ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā supriyaḥ sa sabhāsthitaḥ । nṛpatiṃ taṃ samālokya pura evam abhāṣata ।। śṛṇu rājan mayākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ yat te yaśo mahat ।
tad guṇān bhavato draṣṭum ihāhaṃ samupācare ।। tan me darśaya rājendra gāndharvaguṇām ātmanaḥ । kas te sāstā gurur vāsti taṃ cāpi me pradarśaya ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājā pratibhāṇavān ।
supriyaṃ taṃ samālokya tathety evam abhāṣata ।। sādhu paśya mahābhāga darśayisyāmi taṃ guruṃ । yo me śāstā mahābhijñaḥ sarvavidyāguṇādhipaḥ ।। sa me śāstādhunehaiva sarvasatvahitārthataḥ ।
jetāraṇye mahodyāne nivaśati vṛṣaṃ diśan ।। sādhu paśya mahābhāga taṃ guruṃ me hitārthadaṃ । tad ehi saha yāsyāma śāstāraṃ darśayāmi taṃ ।। iti tena narendreṇa samākhyātaṃ sa supriyaḥ ।
śrutvā tatheti pramodya gantum abhāṣata ।। sādhu rājan samichāmi śāstāraṃ tat pradarśaya । tena saha vivādāni kuryāṃ tatra nayāśu māṃ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ sa tatheti hi ।
supriyaṃ taṃ samādāya vihāre gantum aichata ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatis tena supriyeṇābhimāninā । taiś ca paṃcaśatair anyair gāndharvikaiḥ sahācarat ।। tasminn avasare buddho bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
loke satvān samuddhartuṃ kṛpayā samapaśyata ।। tadā tena nareśena sārddham evam upāgataṃ । supriyaṃ taṃ sa ālokya manasaiva vyacintayat ।। aho vata sudhīr yā sā gandharvādhipanandanaḥ ।
pañcaśikho abhidho vīṇām ādāyehopasaṃkramet ।। iti tena munīndreṇa manasā paricintitaṃ । matvā pañcaśikhaḥ so api tathāgantuṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa saptagaṃdharvasahasreṇa sahānvitaḥ ।
vaiḍūryadaṇḍavīṇāṃ saṃprādāya sahasācaran ।। tathā sa saṃkramaṃs tatra vihāre samupāviśan । dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā tāṃ vīṇāṃ samupānayat ।। tataḥ sa sugataṃ bhaktyā samabhyarcya prasannadhīḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tat sabhāyām upāśrayat ।। tadā sa supriyo apy enaṃ dṛṣṭvā mānābhigarvitaḥ । tāṃ vīṇāṃ kvanayann agre anuśrāvituṃ samārabhat ।। tatprakvāṇāt svarā sapta ekai viṃśati mūrchanāḥ ।
samutthitāḥ sarvalokacetānsi paryamohayan ।। tadā sarve api te lokāḥ śrutvā tat prakvaṇān mudā । nṛpatipramukhāś cāpi paraṃ vismayam āyajuḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃś cāpi tasya mānābhighātane ।
vaiḍūryadaṇḍavīṇāṃ tām anuśrāvitum ārabhat ।। ekaikasyāṃ hi tat taṃtryā naikasvaraviśeṣitāḥ । mūrchanāś ca tathā nānāvidhā niścāritās tathā ।। tataḥ śabdāt samuccerur gāthā evaṃ pracodināḥ ।
tadyatheha bhave sarvaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ ।। idaṃ kāyaṃ ca vīṇāvad indriyāṇi svarānī ca । mūrchanā iva cittāni jñātvā bodhau samācara ।। etadgāthām anuśrutvā sarve lokā nṛpādayaḥ ।
satyam etad iti jñātvā bodhicittaṃ pralehire ।। tadā sa supriyo apy evaṃ śrutvā matvānumoditaḥ । paritatyāja gāṃdharvavidyāmadābhimānatāṃ ।। tato niryātya vīṇāṃ sa gandhakuṭyāṃ virāgitaḥ ।
bhagavacchāsane tatra pravrajituṃ samaichata ।। tadā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā supriyaḥ so anumoditaḥ । kṛtāñjaliḥ puraḥ sthitvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। vaṃde te caraṇau śāsta bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।
tan me atrānugrahaṃ kṛtvā pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । dṛṣṭvā tad āśayaṃ śuddhaṃ gaṃdharvaṃ taṃ tathāvadat ।। gaṃdharva saugate dharme pravrajituṃ yadīchasi ।
pitror ājñāṃ samāsādya prehi dāsyāmi te vrataṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa supriyo mudā । tatheti taṃ muniṃ natvā sahasarddhyā gṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa sahasā prāpto natvā tau pitarau mudā ।
sāñjaliḥ purataḥ sthitvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। śṛṇu me vāñchitaṃ tāta yadi te kṛpayā mayi । tan mamānugrahaṃ kṛtvā saddharme māṃ niyojaya ।। ahaṃ hi saugataṃ dharmaṃ dṛṣṭvā vāñchāmi tad vrataṃ ।
tat pravrajyāṃ samāsādya prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ tad atrāpi na me ratiḥ । avaśyaṃ hi bhaven mṛtyuḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām api ।। evaṃ dṛṣṭvātra saṃsāre bhogyaṃ nechāmi niḥspṛhaḥ ।
tat pravrajyāvrataṃ dhṛtvā prāptum iche sunirvṛtiṃ ।। api cāsau munīndro hi sadātraiva na tiṣṭhati । buddhakāryaṃ samāpyaiva nirvṛtiṃ sarvathā vrajet ।। kiṃ cātra sarvadā naivam utpatsyate munīśvaraḥ ।
kadā cid evam utpanno loke bodhiṃ samādiśet ।। tathā ca durlabhaṃ janma sadgatau ca kṣaṇaṃ tathā । tatkṣaṇe alabhyamāne atra kathaṃ dharmānulapsyate ।। dharmaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ sāraṃ sukhino api hi ।
kṣaṇadhvansi śarīraṃ hi jīvitaṃ ca tṛṇāmbuvat ।। dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ yāyāt saṃbodhim api prāpnuyāt । tat pravrajyācariṃ dhṛtvā prāptum iche atra nirvṛtiṃ ।। tad ātra yadi vāṃ tāta kṛpāsti svātmaje mayi ।
sarvathānugrahaṃ kṛtvā tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa gandharvādhipaḥ sudhīḥ । suciraṃ taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā snehād evam abhaṣata ।। satyam evaṃ sutākhyātaṃ tathāpi me vacaḥ śṛṇu ।
pravrajyā duṣkarīcaryyā tat kathaṃ tvaṃ samācareḥ ।। tvaṃ hi yuvā pramatto asi madanākrāṃtamānasaḥ । kāmabhogyasukhāraktas tat kathaṃ tad vrataṃ careḥ ।। pravrajito viraktātmā saṃsārabhogyanispṛhaḥ ।
sarvān parigrahāns tyaktvā sadaikāntī vane vase ।। sukule duḥkule cāpi yācitvā viraśāsanaṃ । bhuṃjīthās tat kathaṃ bhuktvā samādhiṃ saṃpradhāsyasi ।। ity evaṃ duṣkaraṃ jñatvā pravrajyāvratasādhane ।
sahasā mā kṛthāś cittaṃ nivāraya samāhitaḥ ।। yady ativāṃchase putra pravrajyāgrahaṇe tathā । vṛddhatve samupāśritya triratnaṃ tad vrataṃ cara ।। tat tvaṃ yāvad yuvā gehe saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yathepsitaṃ ।
vṛddhatve tad vrataṃ dhṛtvā triratnāni sadā bhaja ।। tathā cet te bhavej janma sāphalyaṃ bhavacāraṇe । sukhaṃ bhuktvā vrataṃ dhṛtvā nirvṛtiṃ vā samāpnuyāḥ ।। iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā matvaivaṃ tat prabodhitaḥ ।
tāvad gṛhe sukhaṃ bhuktvā smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ vasa ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā supriyaḥ so abhiśaṃkitaḥ । punas taṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā bodhayann evam abravīt ।। satyam evaṃ bhave tāta tathāpi vakṣyate mayā ।
tac chrutvāpi tvayā parijñāya vibudhyatāṃ ।। satkule durlabhaṃ janma tatrāpi durlabhaṃ kṣaṇaṃ । durlabhaṃ sugatotpādaṃ durlabhaṃ tadvrataṃ bhave ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre kleśamānamadākule ।
avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāptum iche atra nirvṛtiṃ ।। tad atra kṛpayā mahyam anujñāṃ dātum arhasi । yūyaṃ cāpi hi tad dharmabhāṇaiḥ sadgatim āpsyatha ।। iti hetoḥ pita tatra vilambaṃma kṛthā ciraṃ ।
sahasānugrahaṃ kṛtvā tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa gaṃdharvādhipaś cirāt । snehaduḥkhāgnisaṃtapto galadaśrumukho avadat ।। ayi supriya putra tvaṃ snehān mayā nivāryasa ।
yady ativāṃchase prāptuṃ nirvṛtiṃ tan samācara ।। saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dadhat । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā supriyaḥ so abhimoditaḥ । pitroḥ pādān praṇatvaiva sahasā niryayau gṛhāt ।।
tataḥ sa sahasā gatvā vihāraṃ samupācarat । tatra prāpto munīndraṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvaiva samupāviśat ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ nātvā prāñjaliḥ pura āśrayan । suprasannamukhāṃbhojaḥ prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
sarvajña bhagavāñ chāstar ādiṣṭaṃ bhavatāyathā । tathānujñāṃ pituḥ prāpya prāgatāham ihādhunā ।। tad atra bhavatāṃ śāstaḥ śaraṇaṃ samupāgataḥ । brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyāmi tat pravrajyāṃ pradehi me ।।
iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । dṛṣṭvā tasyāśayaṃ śuddhaṃ punar eva samādiśat ।। ehi supriya bhikṣo atra cara brahmacariṃ śivāṃ । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā samādhiṃ samupāśrayat ।।
tato dṛṣṭvā ca saṃsāraṃ kleśasaṃghasamākulaṃ । paṃcagaṃḍamayaṃ dehaṃ jīvitaṃ ca trināmvuvat ।। samādhisaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā saṃbodhisādhanodyataḥ । sarvakleśaripuñ jitvā sākṣād arhatpadaṃ yayau ।।
tataḥ supriyo bhikṣuḥ prāptābhijñaḥ kṛtī sudhīḥ । bhindan sarvam avidyāṅgaṃ nirvikalpo abhavad yatiḥ ।। samaloṣṭasuvarṇaś ca pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ । vāsīcaṃdanakalpo abhūd ākāśasamamānasaḥ ।।
saṃsārabhogyasatkāramānyalābhaparāṅmukhaḥ । niḥkleśaḥ pariṣuddhātmā brahmacārī niraṃjanaḥ ।। sadevāsuralokānāṃ sarvabhuvanavāsināṃ । vaṃdyaḥ pūjyo abhinaṃdyaś ca mānanīyo bhavan babhau ।।
tadaivaṃbhūtam arhantaṃ supriyaṃ tam śubhendriyaṃ । prālokya vismitāḥ sarve tatsabhāsthāḥ prasedire ।। tadā sarve api te lokā devā daityāś ca kinnarāḥ । yakṣāḥ siddhāś ca gaṃdharvā nāgāś ca rākṣasā api ।।
garuḍāś ca tathānye api vidyādharāś ca sāpsarāḥ । sarve lokādhipāś cāpi triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। saṃbuddhaśāsane tatra sāṃghikānāṃ samantataḥ । rakṣāvaraṇasaṃguptiṃ kṛtvābhajan samudyatāḥ ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā tāni pañcāpi gāṃdharvikaśatāni ca । anumodya prasannāni saṃmīlyaivaṃ vabhāṣire ।। ete sarve vayaṃ nīce karmaṇi parivarttikāḥ । sukhānabhijñaduḥkhārttāḥ kleśinaḥ kṛchravṛttayaḥ ।।
yad asmābhiḥ purā puṇyaṃ kiṃ cid vāpi na sādhitaṃ । tenāsyātra vayaṃ sarve duḥkhino nīcavṛttayaḥ ।। tad asmābhir ayam śāstā munīśvaraḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । satkṛtya bhojanair vāpi pūjanīyo yathāvidhiḥ ।।
nūnam etadvipākena bhavemahi subhāginaḥ । tataḥ puṇyānusāreṇa bodhimārge caremahi ।। tataḥ krameṇa saṃprāpya bodhicaryyāṃ śubhāṃ carīṃ । carantas tadvipākaiś ca nirvṛtiṃ saṃlabhemahi ।। iti matvā vayaṃ sarve vijñapya nṛpatiṃ tathā ।
sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ bhojyair arhāmahe samarcituṃ ।। tatheti saṃmataṃ kṛtvā sarve te abhyanumoditāḥ । nṛpater vijñāpanāṃ kartuṃ sahasā samupācaran ।। tatra te samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā taṃ nṛpatiṃ mudā ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt ।। jaya deva mahārāja lokān dharmeṇa pālaya । kiñcid vijñāpanāṃ karttuṃ vayam upāgatāḥ ।। vijānīyād bhavān hy etat tathāpi prārthayāmahe ।
śrutvā no anugrahaṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā tat prasīdatu ।। yad vayaṃ deva sarve atra nīcakarmānucāriṇaḥ । tat sasaṃghaṃ muniṃ bhojyaiḥ samichāmaḥ samarcituṃ ।। tad anujñāṃ pradatvā naḥ kṛpayoddhartum arhasi ।
etad vijñāpanāṃ kurmas tat prasīda nṛpādhipa ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ so anumoditaḥ । tān sarvān samupāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samādiśat ।। sādhu bhavatu sarveṣāṃ yuṣmākaṃ satsamīhitaṃ ।
tat tathā kriyatāṃ buddhe satkāraṃ śraddhayādarāt ।। saṃbuddhe yat kṛtaṃ karma tat phalaṃ kṣiṇuyān na hi । kramād bodhicariṃ pūrya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāt ।। tad atra sarvathā yūyaṃ sasaṃghaṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ ।
yathārhabhojanaṃ bhaktyā pūjayadhvaṃ samādarāt ।। ity ādiṣṭam ḥ - ndreṇa śrutvā sarve api te mudā । tatheti pratinaṃditvā nṛpaṃ natvā tato acaran ।। tatas te saṃmataṃ kṛtvā vihāre sahasā gatāḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt ।। bhagavaṃs tad vijānīyād yad arthaṃ samupāgatāḥ । tathāpi prārthayeyaivam anugrahītum arhati ।। yad vayaṃ bhavatāṃ sarvasāṃghikānāṃ yathāvidhiṃ ।
pūjayituṃ samichāmo satkartuṃ bhojanair api ।। tad bhavāṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā kṛtvāsmākaṃ anugrahaṃ । pure śvaḥ sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vijayituṃ samarhasi ।। iti taiḥ prārthite sarvair bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
teṣāṃ dharmapravṛddhyarthaṃ tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tatas sarve api te matvā bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ । bhūyas taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā svaṃ puraṃ sahasā yayuḥ ।। tatra sarve api te bhūmiṃ śodhayitvā samantataḥ ।
prajñapya svāsanāny evaṃ sāmagriṃ samasādhayan ।। tataḥ pūjopahārāṇi bhojyāṅgāni rasāni ca । peyāni supraṇītāni sādhayitvā pramoditāḥ ।। tatra taṃ sugataṃ sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ cāmaṃtrituṃ yayuḥ ।
vihāre samupasṛtya śrīghanaṃ saṃpraṇemire ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā sarve te samupasthitāḥ । saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ prārthayann evam ādarāt ।। sarvajña bhagavaṃ chāstaḥ samayo varttate adhunā ।
tad bhavān saṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vijayituṃ samarhati ।। iti taiḥ prārthite dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ । pātracīvaram ādaya pratasthe saṃprabhāsayan ।। tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra prātihāryaṃ pradarśayan ।
sarveṣāṃ śubhatāṃ kṛtvā tat pure samupāviśat ।। pradakṣiṇakrameṇaivaṃ caraṃs tatra samaṃtataḥ । bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kurvan tatpradeśe samācaran ।। tatra pādyārgham ādāya krameṇa saha sāṃghikaṃ ।
svāsane samupāviśya tasthau bhānur ivojvalan ।। tadā taṃ śrīghanaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ ca svāsane sthitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sarve api te harṣāt pūjayituṃ samārabhan ।। tathā krameṇa saṃpūjya taṃ buddhapramukhaṃ gaṇaṃ ।
yathārhabhojanaiḥ sarvaṃ saṃtṛptaṃ samatoṣayan ।। tatas te bhojanāṃte tatpātrāṇi vyapanīya ca । karādīñ chodhayitvā tad bhūmiṃ ca paryaśodhayan ।। tataḥ pūgādikaṃ datvā punaḥ sarve api te mudā ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā samupatasthire punaḥ ।। te ca gāṃdharvikāḥ sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । bodhipraṇidhim ādhāya prabhejire samāhitāḥ ।। veṇuvīṇāmṛdaṃgādi tūryasaṃgītivādanaiḥ ।
upasthitya sasaṃghaṃ taṃ śrīghanaṃ samatoṣayat ।। tada sa bhagavāṃ dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ bhaktiprasādinīṃ । sarveṣāṃ śuddhacittāni vyamuñcat smitam uddhavāt ।। tat saṃsmitasahotpannāḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ śubhāṃśavaḥ ।
sarvatra bhuvane gatvā pracerur amṛtāṃśuvat ।। teṣāṃ ke cid adhogatvā narakeṣu samantataḥ । avabhāsya parispṛṣṭvā sarvatrāpi sukhaṃ daduḥ ।। tadā te nārakīyās tat prabhāspṛṣṭāḥ sukhānvitāḥ ।
kim etad iti saṃdigdhāḥ saṃmīlyaivaṃ vabhāṣire ।। aho nu jāyate saukhyam asmākaṃ sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ । vatānyatra gatāḥ smo adya kasya puṇyānubhāvataḥ ।। iti saṃdigdhacittānāṃ teṣāṃ manaḥ prabodhane ।
bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ saṃpreṣayan samaṃtataḥ ।। tatrā taṃ saugataṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te narakasthitāḥ । vismitāḥ samupāsṛtya vavandire prasāditāḥ ।। namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya ca namas sadā ।
iti proktvā praṇatvā taccharaṇaṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarve te narakotthitāḥ । sahasā svargatiṃ yātāḥ saddharme samudācaran ।। evaṃ tān sarvasatvāṃś ca samuddhṛtya samantataḥ ।
sarve te apy aṃśavo bhūyas saṃbuddhāntikam upācaran ।। ke cid ūrddhvagatā yāvad akaniṣṭhaṃ samantataḥ । avabhāsya samudghuṣya tatraivaṃ samacodayan ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ ।
iti satyaṃ parijñāya triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yūjyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane । dhunīta mārasainyāś ca naḍāgāraṃ yathā karī ।। yo apy asmin saugate dharme hy apramattaś caret sadā ।
sa tyaktvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। iti saṃcodayantas tāṃ sārvān devāṃś ca sarvataḥ । te sarve apy aṃśavo bhāyaḥ sugatāntikam āyayuḥ ।। tatas te apy aṃśavaḥ sarve saṃmīlya saṃgatā muneḥ ।
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā tasyorṇāyāṃ samāviśan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhālokā vismayoddhatamānasāḥ । kim etad iti saṃcintya sarve tasthuḥ śakautukāḥ ।। athānaṃdaḥ samālokya tān sarvān vismayoddhavān ।
utthāya sāñjalir natvā śāstāraṃ taṃ samabravīt ।। bhagavans te mukhād bhāsiḥ paṃcavarṇā vinirgatā । avabhāsya diśaḥ sarvā ūrṇāyāṃ ca viśanti tāḥ ।। etad dṛṣṭvā sabhālokāḥ sarve apīme savismayāḥ ।
taddhetuṃ śrotum ichanti tad upādeṣṭum arhati ।। nāhetu hi smitaṃ buddhā darśayanti kadā cana । yad dhetau bhavatā śāstur hasitaṃ tat samādiśa ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ śiṣyena sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tam ānaṃdaiḥ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। paśyānaṃda yad etair hi sarvai gāndharvikair api । mama sasāṃghikasyaivaṃ satkāraṃ prakṛtaṃ mudā ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sarve apīme bhavāntare ।
kramād bodhicarīṃ prāptā niḥkleśā vimalāśayāḥ ।। māracaryāvinirmuktāḥ pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ । varṇasvarābhidhāḥ sarve pratyekasugatā jināḥ ।। prāntāśayyāsānāsīnā hīnadīnānukampakāḥ ।
dakṣiṇīyā mahāsatvā bhaviṣyanti śubhaṃkarāḥ ।। evam etāt samālokya yūyaṃ yadi samichatha । tathātra śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt ।। ye triratnaṃ sadā bhaktyā satkṛtyaivaṃ bhajanti te ।
vihāya durgatiṃ nityaṃ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre yeṣāṃ vāṃchā sukhe śive । te satkṛtya triratneṣu śraddhayā bhajatāniśaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve ca te janāḥ ।
satyam evaṃ pratijñāya triratnaṃ sarvadābhajan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayoddhatamānasāḥ । kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā paprachus taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। yad evaṃ bhagavann ebhiḥ satkāraṃ prakṛtaṃ mahat ।
tat te kena supuṇyena samyag ādeṣṭum arhati ।। evaṃ tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa jineśvaraḥ । sarvāns tāñ chrāvakān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ puṇyaṃ yan mayā prakṛtaṃ purā ।
tad atra kathitaṃ śrutvā śraddhayābhyanumodata ।। purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ prabodhanābhidho jinaḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। sarvavidyādhipo nāthas tathāgato vināyakaḥ ।
mārajil lokavid bharttā subhadro arhan hitaṃkaraḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān buddho janapadeṣu cārikāṃ । carann anyāṃ rājadhānīm anuprāptaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tatra tasya narendrasya krīḍodyāne taror adhaḥ ।
praviśya svāsanāsīnas tasthau vahnir ivojvalan ।। tadaikasmin dine tatra rājā kāntāpravādinaiḥ । saṃgītaiḥ saha saṃrakto ramituṃ samupāviśat ।। tatrasthaṃ taṃ samāsīnaṃ sugataṃ suprabhojvalaṃ ।
dṛṣṭvaiva sahasopetya natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ ।। samādhisthaṃ tam ālokya taṣṭhau ciram upāśrayan । tatas tanmukhapadmotthasaddharmāmṛtalipsayā ।। vādyamānaiḥ satair vādyair muniṃ prābodhayan nṛpaḥ ।
tataḥ sa sugato buddho samādheḥ śīghram utthitaḥ ।। sāntaḥpuraṃ nareṃdraṃ taṃ prādrākṣīt samupasthitaṃ । tadā taṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa saṃbuddhaḥ prabodhanaḥ ।। saddharmmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।
ehi rājan mahāvāho svāgataṃ te mahīpate ।। saddharmaṃ samupāśritya bodhicaryāṃ samācara । sadā dānaṃ pradatvātra śīlaṃ dhṛtvā samāhitaḥ ।। kṣāntyā prasādayal lokān dharmavīryaṃ prasādhaya ।
bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya prajñāratnam upārjaya ।। tadratnānubhāvena saṃbodhimārgam āpnuyāḥ । tatas te maṅgalaṃ nityam ihāmutre sadā bhavet ।। sarvasatvahitaṃ kurvan sadgatim eva prāpnuyāḥ ।
iti matvā mahārāja saddharmaṃ samupāśrayan ।। triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā satkṛtya bhaja sarvadā । triratneṣu kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana ।। sarvadā satphalāny eva sūte bodhiṃ samarpayet ।
iti matvā mahārāja triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā cara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ । tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sa bhūpatiḥ ।। śrutvā tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ । tataḥ sa mudito rājā taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।। yathāvidhi samabhyarcya bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।
tataś ca bhojanānte sa nṛpatiḥ sāñjalir mudā । taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ hṛdo vyadhāt ।। anena kuśalenāhaṃ loke andhe apariṇāyake । samyag bodhiṃ samāgamya bhaveyaṃ sugato jinaḥ ।।
etat tena narendreṇa praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā । matvā sa sugatas tasya tathāśīrvacanaṃ dadau ।। jayo astu te sadā rājaṃ dharmeṇa pālaya prajāḥ । praṇidhānaṃ yathā bodhau tathā te siddhyatu dhruvaṃ ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tena śrutvā sa bhūpatiḥ । muditaḥ sāñjalir natvā taṃ munīndraṃ samabravīt ।। adyārabhya sadā śāstas triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । saṃbodhisaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣyāmi samāhitaḥ ।।
tad bhavān kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā sadā māṃ draṣṭum arhati । sarvadā bhavatām eva śaraṇe asmi samāsthitaḥ ।। iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā rājā sa sajano mudā । bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya sānaṃdaḥ svapuraṃ yayau ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā samutthāya sasāṃghikaḥ । sarvatra bhadratāṃ kṛtvā svāśrame samupāyayau ।। manyatāṃ bhikṣavo yo asau rājā saṃbuddhasevakaḥ । aham eva tadābhūvan nānyo draṣṭavya eva saḥ ।।
yan mayā śraddhayā tasya prabodhanasya tāyinaḥ । pūjākāri mahotsāhais tūryasaṃgītivādanaiḥ ।। tena puṇyavipākena mamātraiva mahotsavaiḥ । etair gāndharvikair evaṃ satkāraḥ prakṛtādhunā ।।
evaṃ matvā mahatpuṇyaṃ saṃbuddhabhajanodbhavaṃ । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajanīyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ ।। yūyaṃ cāpi sadā nityaṃ śāstāraṃ sadguruṃ jinaṃ । saṃbuddhaṃ samupāśritya viharadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te bhikṣavo mudā । sarve tatheti vijñapya triratnāni sadābhajan ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā narādhipa । tathādhunā samākhyātaṃ tava puṇyapravṛddhaye ।।
evaṃ rājaṃs tvayāpy evaṃ triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā cara dharmaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। prajāś cāpi tathā rājaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । saṃbodhisādhane dharme yojanīyās tvayādarāt ।।
tathā cet te sadā bhadraṃ bhaven nūnaṃ samantataḥ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti śāstrā samādeṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti pratimoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
gāṃdharvikānām avadānam etac chrutvānumodanti narā mudā ye । te sarva enaḥparimuktacittā bhuktvā sukhāny eva labhanti bodhiṃ । athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhasi ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa yatiḥ sugatātmajaḥ । aśokaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam upādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvāpy evaṃ pramodaya ।। purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ । vihāre jetakāraṇye vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra sarve bhikṣugaṇā api ।
śrāvakāś cailakāś caiva sarva upāsakā api ।। sarve api bhikṣuṇīsaṃghā upāsikāgaṇā api । bodhisatvagaṇāś cāpi saddharmasādhanodyatāḥ ।। sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ jagadguruṃ ।
upatasthuḥ puraskṛtya parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।। tadā tasya munīndrasya mukhāmbhojavinirgataṃ । bhadradharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ ।। śakrādayaḥ surendrāś ca brahmādayo maharddhikāḥ ।
lokapālā mahāvīrāḥ sasainyaparivārakāḥ ।। yogino yatayaś cāpi maharṣayas tapaśvinaḥ । brāhmaṇāś ca mahāvijñāḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ ।। rājāno rājaputrāś ca vaiśyā maṃtrijanā api ।
amātyāḥ śreṣṭhino bhaṭṭāḥ paurikāś ca gṛhādhipāḥ ।। sainyādhipāś ca yodhāraḥ sārthavahā mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api ।। evam anye api lokāś ca saddharmaguṇavāñchinaḥ ।
sarve dharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ vihāre samupāgatāḥ ।। tatra prāptāḥ sabhāmadhye samāsīnaṃ munīśvaraṃ । śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvā samupācaran ।। tatra te samupāsṛtya sarve taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ ।
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samabhyarcya praṇemire ।। tataḥ sarve api te lokāḥ parivṛtya samantataḥ । sāñjalayaḥ prasannāsyā upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān samupasthitān ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇam āryadharmam upādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te tridaśādayaḥ । lokā dharmaviśeṣatvaṃ vijñāya prāṇanandire ।। tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāṃ pauriko gṛhī । śreṣṭhī mahājanaḥ śrimāñ chrāddho bhadrāśayābhavat ।।
sa ekasmiṃ dine svasmin bhāṇḍālakoṣṭhake viśan । svasaṃpannicayaṃ dṛṣṭvā manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। aho me jāyate saṃpad dīyatī saṃpravarddhitā । tathāpi varddhyate tṛṣṇā yataḥ saukhyaṃ na kiṃ cana ।।
yad ime caṃcalā bhogā jalacaṃdranibhā mama । anityā asthirāḥ padmapatrasthitajalopamā ।। tad atra kiṃ mano adyāpi tṛṣṇayākṛṣyate mama । yena carāmy ahaṃ loke duḥkhī bhavikalāśayaḥ ।।
tat kiṃ me saṃpadā sāraṃ yataḥ saukhyaṃ na vidyate । dharmārthe gocaraṃ naiva kevalaṃ madavṛddhaye ।। madena varddhate mānaṃ mānāl loke pramādatā । pramādād dīpyate cerṣyā kopāgnir dīpyate tataḥ ।।
kopāt krūrāśayaś caṇḍo nirdayo duritāśayaḥ । pāpātmā hiṃsako duṣṭo daśākuśalasādhakaḥ ।। svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayati durāśayaḥ । tato atipāpasaṃrakto durācaro atidurmanāḥ ।।
tato atidurmatir drohī saṃvṛttidharmaniṃdakaḥ । triratnāni pratikṣipya mahāpātakam ācaret ।। tato atipāpasaṃkliṣṭāḥ pramūḍho narakaṃ vrajet । narakeṣu bhraman nityaṃ duḥkhāny eva sadāśnuyāt ।।
yad vātrāpi ca saṃsāre jīvitam adhruvaṃ khalu । kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca sārveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। tad atrāham asārebhyo bhogebhyaḥ sāram uttamaṃ । saddharmaṃ samupādātuṃ yatnaṃ kuryāṃ samādarāt ।।
saddharmaṃ saugataṃ dharmam ity ākhyātaṃ purāvidaiḥ । tad atra saugate kṣetre dānaṃ kurvīya sāṃprataṃ ।। bauddhakṣetre kṛtaṃ dānaṃ bodhivījaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ । etad evātra saṃsāre sādhanīyaṃ śubhāptaye ।।
dānena śuddhyate cittaṃ sucittaḥ sumatiṃ labhet । subuddhiḥ sadguṇāraktaḥ saṃvṛttiśīlabhṛt kṛtī ।। suśīlaḥ kṣāntimān dhīraḥ parātmasamabhāvikaḥ । sudhīro vīryavān sarvasatvārthasādhanodyataḥ ।।
apradhṛṣyo mahāsatvaḥ kleśāridamako bhavet । tataḥ supariśuddhātmā samādhisusthito bhavet ।। tat samādhivalādhānaiḥ prajñābdhipāram āgataḥ । bodhiratnaṃ samāsādya bodhisatvo adhipo bhavet ।।
etad ratnānubhāvena bhadraṃkalā samantataḥ । sarvamārān vinirjitya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। ity arhadbhir mahābhijñaiḥ samākhyātaṃ mayā śrutaṃ । tat saṃbuddhapadāṃ praptuṃ buddhaṃ bhajeya sāṃprataṃ ।। nūnaṃ buddhānubhāvena bhāvitaṃ setsyate dhruvaṃ ।
tad buddhapramukhaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ pūjeya sādaraṃ ।। iti niścitya sa śrīmān gṛhasthaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghan taṃ pūjayituṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa sajanaḥ śreṣṭhī triratnabhajanotsukaḥ ।
vihāre jetakāraṇye prayayau saṃpraharṣitaḥ ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa gṛhasthaḥ pramoditaḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samarcayad yathāvidhiḥ ।। tataḥ sa sajano natvā sāñjaliḥ saṃpramoditaḥ ।
munīndraṃ taṃ samālokya puraḥ sthitvaivam abravīt ।। sarvajña bhagavaṃ chāstar bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tato abhilaṣite kārye prasīdatu jagadguro ।। bhagavaṃ bhavataḥ śāstuḥ sasaṃghasya jagadguroḥ ।
pūjayituṃ samichāmi tad anujñāṃ dadātu me ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tathāstv iti pratijñāya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛn matvā bhagavatādhyuvāsa taṃ ।
sāñjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā muditaḥ svagṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa svajanaiḥ svasmiṃ gṛhe margeṣu sarvataḥ । pariśodhya sugaṃdhaiś ca pariṣiṃcyābhyaśobhayat ।। tatrāsanāni prajñapya vitānāni vitatya ca ।
muktapuṣpaiḥ samākīrya surabhiṃ samadhūpayat ।। tataḥ sa bhojyasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvā svavaṃdhubhiḥ । tathopahārasāmagrīṃ pariśuddhām asādhayat ।। tato anye dyur gṛhasthaḥ sa snātvā śuddhāṃvarāvṛtaḥ ।
saṃbuddhāmaṃtraṇaṃ kartuṃ vihāre sajano yayau ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ sa purogataḥ । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo vartate adhunā ।
tat sasaṃgho mamāvāse bhāvān āgantum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ । pātracīvaram ādāya saṃpratasthe prabhāsayan ।। tatra sa bhagavān mārge kṛtvā bhadraṃ prabhāsayan ।
bhikṣusaṃghagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ śrāvastīṃ samupāviśan ।। tadābhūn nagare tatra sarvatrāpi sumaṅgalaṃ । upadravāṇi sarvāṇi sahasā vilayaṃ yayuḥ ।। andhā rūpāṇi paśyantaḥ śṛṇvanto vadhirā ravān ।
hīnendriyāś ca ye te api pratilabdhendriyā vavuḥ ।। ksutpipāsāhatā ye ca te abhavan parituṣṭitāḥ । rogiṇo nīrujā āsan kuvelā rucirāmvarāḥ ।। mūkā āsan pravaktāro jaḍāś cāpi suvāgminaḥ ।
ciravairābhisaṃnaddhās te apy āsan maitrabhāvitāḥ ।। ye ca caṇḍāśāyāḥ krūrās te apy abhūvan dayālavaḥ । ye ca duṣṭā durācārās te santas samyamodyatāḥ ।। daridrā dhaninaḥ proḍhyā dūrvalā valino abhavan ।
ye śaṭhā vaṃcakāś cauras te āryāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।। evaṃ ye duḥkhinaḥ satvās te sarve sukhino abhavan । evaṃ sa bhagavāṃs tatra kṛtvā bhadraṃ samantataḥ ।। pradakṣiṇakrameṇaivaṃ sasaṃghaṃ tadgṛhe viśan ।
tatra tasya munīndrasya sa gṛhastho yathākramaṃ । pādyaṃ dadau sasaṃghasya sadārāḥ śucināmbunā ।। tataḥ sa suprāsannātmā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । prajñapte svāsane tatra yathākramaṃ nyaveśayat ।।
tatra te sāṃghikāḥ sarve saṃbuddhapramukhāḥ kramāt । svasvāsane samāviśya samātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tataḥ svasvāsanāsīnān saṃbuddhapramukhān yatīn । tān sarvān sa gṛhī dṛṣṭvā yathāvidhi samarcayat ।।
tataḥ sa sajanaḥ śreṣṭhī svahastena sasāṃghikaṃ । taṃ munīndraṃ sudhākalpair bhojanaiḥ samatarpayet ।। tataḥ saṃtṛptitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । apanīya sa pātrāṇi tad dhastādīn vyaśodhayat ।।
tataḥ sa sāñjalir natvā tān buddhapramukhān yatīn । puro nīcāsanāsīno dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ gṛhaṣṭhaṃ subhāvinaṃ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dharmām ādeṣṭum abravīt ।।
ārogyam astu te nityaṃ gṛhapate sadā śivaṃ । bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya cara dharmaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। dharmeṇa jīyate pāpaṃ niṣpāpaḥ sadgatiṃ vrajet । sadgatau satsukhāny eva bhuktvā saṃcarate sadā ।।
dharmeṇa puruṣo vidvān sarvavidyākalādhipaḥ । sudhiro guṇavān vijño bhavec chrīmān maharddhikaḥ ।। dharmeṇa suciraṃ jīved ārogyaṃ ca sadā tanau । sarvatrāpi bhaven nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।।
dharmo na naśyate kvapi hriyate nāpi kena cit । kenāpi naśyate naiva cālayituṃ kadā cana ।। nāgnibhir dahyate dharmaḥ klidyate nāpi codakaiḥ । vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate naiva kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu ।।
dharmeṇa bhūḥ sthirībhūtā dharmeṇa dīpyate analaḥ । dharmeṇa calate vāyur dharmeṇa vahate jalaḥ ।। dharmeṇa dīpyate bhānur dharmeṇaivaṃ sudhākaraḥ । meghā dharmeṇa varṣāṇā bhūmiḥ śaṣyauṣadhībharāḥ ।। dharmeṇaivaṃ tathā sarve lokapālā maharddhikāḥ ।
sarvaduṣṭān vinirjitya pālayanti jagattraye ।। dharmo na śīyate kvāpi dharmo na paribhūyate । sarvatra jayate dharmo dharmo hi śobhate sadā ।। dharmahīnā na śobhante śrimanto guṇino api ca ।
dharmmiṣṭhā eva śobhante daridrā nirguṇā api ।। dharmeṇa rakṣitā vīrāḥ saṃgrāme vijitārayaḥ । yaśomānyamahatsaṃpatsukhāni te labhanti ca ।। tathā vīrā vaṇiksārthā dharmeṇaivābhirakṣitāḥ ।
mahāmbudhiṃ samuttīrya ratnāny api labhanti ca ।। dharmavanto narā dhīrā buddhimanto vicakṣaṇāḥ । sarvavidyākalāvijñā jayante paravādinaḥ ।। tathā dharmānubhāvena śilpavidyākalāvidaḥ ।
yaśomānyaprasādaśrīsatsukhāni labhanti ca ।। tathā ca maṃtriṇo amātyā dharmavanto vicakṣaṇāḥ । rājyakāryāṇi sarvāṇi sādhayanto jayanty arīn ।। rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś caivaṃ dharmanītivicakṣaṇāḥ ।
sarvaduṣṭān vinirjitya virājante nārādhipāḥ ।। tathā dharmeṇa rājendraś cakravarttī mahīśvaraḥ । saptaratnasamāyuktaḥ sarvaśāstā virājate ।। tathā dharmadharā eva yatayo yogino api ca ।
sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā labhanti paramaṃ padaṃ ।। tatharṣayo mahābhijñā dharmabhṛto maharddhikāḥ । yathābhilaṣitāṃ siddhiṃ prāpya mokṣaṃ vrajanti ca ।। tathā dharmānusāreṇa maṃtravidyārthasādhakāḥ ।
siddhisamṛddhisaṃprāptāḥ sādhayanti yathehitaṃ ।। tathā ca mānavāḥ sarve lokā dharmānusārataḥ । nihīnamadhyamotkṛṣṭāḥ prabhavanti mahītale ।। tathā dharmānusāreṇa lokā daityādayo api ca ।
nihīnamadhyamotkṛṣṭā pracaranti rasātale ।। tathā svargeṣu devāś ca svasvadharmānubhāvataḥ । sukhāni suciraṃ bhuktvā pravasanti pramoditāḥ ।। evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu svasvadharmānubhāvataḥ ।
sarve satvāḥ sukhaprāptāḥ pracaranti yathechayā ।। evaṃ traidhātukotpannāḥ satvāḥ sarve surādayaḥ । svasvadharmānusāreṇa bhramanti ṣaḍgatiṣv api ।। kim atra vahunoktena dharma eva jagatprabhuḥ ।
dharmeṇaiva sadā nityaṃ rakṣitaḥ pracarec chubhe ।। ṣubhena siddhyate cittaṃ śuddhacittaḥ sudhīr bhavet । subuddhiḥ sadguṇādhāraṃ sadguruṃ samupāśrayet ।। tadguror upadeśena caran nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।
bodhicittaṃ samādhāya triratnāni sadā bhajet ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena saddharmasādhanodyataḥ । bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bodhicaryāṃ vrataṃ caret ।। tato māragaṇāñ jitvā pūrya pāramitāḥ kramāt । trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।।
evaṃ dharmavaraṃ matvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । saddharmaṃ samupaśritya cara bodhipadāptaye ।। mṛtyukāle vipattau ca dharmma evānugas suhṛt । tadā sarve tyajanty āśu ko api naiva sahānugaḥ ।।
dharma eva tadā trātā sarvatrāpy anugaḥ suhṛt । tasmād dharmo mahāratnaṃ sādhanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। evaṃ sa bhagavāñ chāstā dharmasyābhyanubhāvatāṃ । samādiśya kṣaṇaṃ tasthau tūṣṇībhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।।
tatas tasya munīndrasya pādau sa mudito gṛhī । praṇatvā manasā caivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ sāmadadhe ।। anena kuśalenāhaṃ sarvakleśavivarjitaḥ । pratyekāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāt ।।
tataḥ sa suprasannāsyo gṛhasthaḥ sajano mudā । bhagavataṃ tam ālokya puras tasthau samāhitaḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavāṃs tasya śrīmato hṛdaye sthitaṃ । praṇidhānaṃ parijñāya susaṃsmitaṃ vyamuñcata ।।
tatas tasya munīndrasya mukhapadmāt surasmayaḥ । paṃcavarṇā vinirgatya sarvatra samudācaran ।। tāsāṃ yā raśmayo yātā adholoke samantataḥ । tāḥ sarvanarakeṣv evam avabhyāsya samāsarat ।।
tadā tābhiḥ parispṛṣṭāḥ sarve te narakasthitāḥ । mahatsaukhyaṃ samāsādya vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। tatra sarve api te satvāḥ parasparasamāgatāḥ । sarvaduḥkhavinirmuktāḥ saṃmīlyaivaṃ samabruvan ।।
aho citraṃ kim adyaivaṃ mahat saukhyaṃ prajāyate । kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanto asmāc cyutā anyatra cāgatāḥ ।। yad asmākaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ tat sarvaṃ śāmyate adhunā । saṃjāyate mahāsaukhyaṃ tad adbhutaṃ na manyate ।।
nūnam atrādhunā ko api bodhisatvaḥ samāgataḥ । yasmād iyaṃ mahāraśmir avabhāsya prasaryati ।। iti ciṃtābhidagdhānaṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane । bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ sarvatra tatra preṣayet ।।
tadā taṃ saugatiṃ mūrttiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve api te mudā । aho citram iti proktvā vismitāś caivam abruvan ।। nehaivetaś cyutāḥ sarve nāpy anyatra gatā vayaṃ । ihaiva saṃsthitāḥ sarve narake pravasāmahe ।।
api tv ayaṃ mahān satvo apūrvadarśana āgataḥ । nūnam asyānubhāvena saṃjāyante sukhāni naḥ ।। tad asmiṃ sugatākare vayaṃ sarve prasāditāḥ । upetya praṇatiṃ kṛtvā sarvathā saṃbhajemahi ।।
iti saṃbhāṣya sarve te nārakīyāḥ pramoditāḥ । upetya taṃ mahāsatvaṃ sāñjalayo abhinemire ।। namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāye ca namaḥ sadā । ity uktvā ca triratnānāṃ saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। iti te nirmite tasmiṃ cittaṃ prasādya nirmalāḥ ।
sarvanirmuktakarmāṇaḥ sahasā sadgatiṃ yayuḥ ।। tathā corddhagatā yās tāḥ kramāc cāturmahādhipān । samārabhya trayastriṃśān sarvāṃś cāpi surālayāt ।। yāvad bhavāgraparyantam avabhāsya prasāritāḥ ।।
tathā cāpi samodghuṣya sarvān devān anodayan । anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkham śūnyam anātmakaṃ । iti matvā śubhe nityaṃ caritavyaṃ sadāpi ca ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane ।
dhunīta mṛtyusainyāni naḍāgāraṃ karī yathā ।। yo hy asmiṃ dharmavinaye hy apramattaś cariṣyati । tyaktvā janmātra saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। iti matvātra saṃbodhipadaṃ yadi samichatha ।
tac chraddhayā triratnāni bhajadhvaṃ sarvadādarāt ।। etac chabdaṃ samākarṇya sarve devāḥ prabodhitāḥ । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire sadādṛtāḥ ।। evaṃ tā raśmayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvāṃl lokāṃc chubhe vṛṣe ।
bodhayitvā pratisthāpya pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ ।। tatra tā raśmayaḥ sarvāḥ piṇḍitās tasya tāyinaḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā sūrṇāyāṃ nyaviśat punaḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve lokās te samitisthitāḥ ।
kiṃ dharmam ādiśed buddha iti saṃciṃtya tasthire ।। athānando mahābhijñaḥ samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ । puraḥ sthito munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvā prārthayat tathā ।। bhagavān nānāvidhā raśmir bhavanmukhābjanirgatāḥ ।
avabhāsya jagallokaṃ bhavadūrṇāṃ niveśitā ।। mārajin nirmalasvānto nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ । nāhetvapratyayaṃ buddhā nirdainyā nirmadoddhavāḥ । smitaṃ caṃdrakarāhāsaṃ darśayanti kadācana ।।
tad yad arthaṃ bhavān smitaṃ darśayati munīśvara । tad arthaṃ śrotum icchaṃti sarve lokā ime adhunā ।। tad bhavāṃ yat samādeṣṭum ichati sāṃprataṃ mune । tad dharmaṃ samupādiśya prasādayatv imāṃ sabhāṃ ।।
iti tena vaśiṣyeṇa prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ । tam āyuṣmantam ānandaṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। evam etat sadānaṃda nāhetvapratyayaṃ smitaṃ । saṃbuddhā api te sarve darśayanti kadā cana ।।
yad arthe smitam ānaṃda darśitaṃ sāṃprataṃ mayā । tad arthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tac chṛṇudhvaṃ samāhitāḥ ।। paśyasi tvaṃ tadānaṃda śreṣṭhinānena yan mama । evaṃvidhaṃ sasaṃghasya satkāraṃ śraddhayā kṛtaṃ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena mayi cittaprasādataḥ ।
ayaṃ śrīmān mahāsatvo bodhisatvo bhavet sudhīḥ ।। tataḥ kleśavimuktātmā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ । sūkṣmatvag iti vikhyātaḥ pratyekabuddha ātmavit ।। bhaviṣyati mahābhijñaḥ saṃvṛtiparamārthavit ।।
evam etat mahatpuṇyavījam ārādhitaṃ mama । sāsane śrīmatānena śraddhayā bodhicetasā ।। buddhakṣetre kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana । saṃbodhisatphalaṃ dadyān nānyad dharmaphalaṃ khalu ।।
evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ buddhakṣetreṣu satkṛtaṃ । matvā taccharaṇaṃ kṛtvā triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt ।। ye buddaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajanti sarvadādarāt । te sadā sadgatiṃ yātāś caraṃti bodhisaṃvaraṃ ।।
ye dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā śrutvā bhajanti sādaraṃ । sarve te akleśino bhadrāḥ saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ ।। ye saṃghe śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajanti śraddhayā sadā । na te gacchanti duḥkhatvaṃ sadā yānti sukhāvatīṃ ।।
iti matvā tathā yūyaṃ sadā nityaṃ samāhitāḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajadhvaṃ śraddhayādarāt ।। tena puṇyavipākena yūyaṃ sarve api sarvathā । trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyatha ।।
iti śāstrā munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate । sarve api sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokāś ca saṃpramoditāḥ ।। tatheti pratisaṃśrutya triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhejire samāhitāḥ ।।
so api śreṣṭhī tathā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ tadātmanaṃ । vyākaraṇaṃ samākarṇya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ ।। tataḥ prabhṛti sa śrīmāṃs triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ sadā bheje pramoditaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā sasāṃghikaḥ samutthitaḥ । tathā sarvatra bhadrāṇi prakurvan svāśramaṃ yayau ।। ity evaṃ guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā mayātra kathyate । tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja śrutvā dharmaṃ śubhe cara ।।
prajāś cāpi tathā dharmaṃ śrāvayitvā prabodhayan । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya śubhe abhyava sadādarāt ।। tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ । bhaven nūnaṃ mahārāja satyam etat prabudhyatāṃ ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena daśapāramitā api । paripūryya krameṇaivaṃ saṃbodhim api cāpsyai ।। evaṃ satyaṃ parijñāya triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhaja bodhiṃ yadīchasi ।।
iti tenārhatā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya saḥ । nṛpas tatheti saṃśrutya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। sūkṣmatvaco avadānaṃ yat tad idaṃ ye narā mudā । satkṛtya śraddhayā bhaktyā śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti ca ।।
te sarve sadgatiṃ yātā bhuktvā saukhyāni sarvadā । saddharmaṃ samupāśritya saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ ।। athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar eva samabravīt ।।
bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhasi ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena rājñā sa yatir ātmavit । tam aśokaṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru ।। purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।।
bhikṣubiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ cailakair bhikṣuṇīgaṇaiḥ । upāsakair mahāśrāddhais tathā copāsikāgaṇaiḥ ।। bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi saddharmasādhanodyataiḥ । kṛtakṛtyair mahābhijñaiś caturbrahmavihārakaiḥ ।।
rājagṛhe puropānte veṇuvane śubhāṅkite । karaṇḍakanivāpākhye mahodyāne jināśrame ।। vihṛtya sarvasatvānāṃ hitārthena sabhāśritaḥ । ādimadhyāntākalyāṇaṃ dharmam ādeṣṭum ārabhat ।।
tadā sarve api devendrāḥ sadevāḥ kamalāsanaḥ । sarve lokādhipāś cāpi yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।। siddhā vidyādharāḥ sādhyā rākṣasā dānavādhipāḥ । nāgeṃdrā garuḍāś cāpi sajanaparivārakāḥ ।।
ṛṣayo brahmaṇāś cāpi yatayo yogino api ca । rājāno rājaputrāś ca maṃtriṇo api ca ।। amātyāḥ sainyalokāś ca sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā janāḥ ।।
grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi kārpaṭikāś ca nairgamāḥ । tathānye api samāyātāḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ ।। tatra sarve api te lokā vihāre samupāgatāḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ samāsīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā natvā pramoditāḥ ।।
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ । natvā sāñjalayaḥ sarve parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ suprasannamukhāmbujaṃ । śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya samātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā lokāḥ sarve api te mudā । saṃbodhisādhanotsāhāḥ pracerire pramoditāḥ ।। tasminn avasare tatra rājagṛhāntike vane ।
veṇuvanāntike paṃcapretaśatāni cerire ।। nagnāny atikṛtāṅgāni dagdhasthūṇākṛtīni vai । romavastrāṇi rukṣāṇi śailopamodarāṇi ca ।। sūcīchidramukhāny asthiyaṃtravad ucchṛtāny api ।
kṣutpipāsābhidagdhāni hīnadīnasvarāṇy api ।। tīvraduḥkhāni taptāni pralapanti vihāyasi । vibhramanti sadā kvāpi kiñci sthitiṃ na lebhire ।। tadaikasmin dine tatra maudgalyāyana ātmavit ।
āyuṣmān saugato bhikṣur mahābhijño dayānvitaḥ ।। pūrvāhne pātram ādāya kāṣāyacīvarāvṛtaḥ । rājagṛhe pure piṇḍaṃ yācituṃ samupācaran ।। tatra yatiḥ sa tāṃ pretāṃ sarvān vibhramato amvare ।
dṛṣṭvene ka iti dhyātvā paśyañ janair upācaran ।। te sarve pretakāś cāpi dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhikṣum āgataṃ । sahasopetya natvāgre rudanta etad abruvan ।। bhadanta bhavatāṃ pādau vandāmahe samānatāḥ ।
tad asmākaṃ hitaṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā trātum arhati ।। vayaṃ rājagṛhe jātāḥ paurāḥ paṃcaśatāny api । svakarmaparibhuṃjānaḥ pretībhūtāś carāmahe ।। tadā vayam ime sarve gṛhasthāḥ śreṣṭhino narāḥ ।
mahādhanā mahābhogās tīrthikā dharmasevakāḥ ।। yad vayaṃ matsārākrāntamānasāḥ kuṭukuñcakāḥ । āgṛhītapariṣkārāḥ kevalārjanasādhakāḥ ।। naiva kiñ cit tadā dānam adadmahi kadā cana ।
arthinam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā prākuṣyāmahi roṣitāḥ ।। paradattāny api śrutvā dṛṣṭvā cāpi praroṣitāḥ । dīyamāneṣu vighnāni prākurmahi prayatnataḥ ।। saugatā api cārhantaḥ pretā iveyam āgatāḥ ।
ity asmābhiḥ pramohāndhaiḥ paribhāṣyābhininditāḥ ।। tata ete vayaṃ sarve kālaṃ kṛtvā ca sāṃprataṃ । evaṃ pretālayotpannā duḥkhārditāś carāmahe ।। iti bhadanta vijñāya gatvā rājagṛhe bhavān ।
kṛpayāsmatpravṛttāṃtaṃ jñātīnāṃ purato vadan ।। chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā buddhādiṃ sarvasāṃghikaṃ । asmannāmnā samabhyarcya bhojayituṃ samarhati ।। saṃbuddhapramukhebhyaś ca saṃghebhyo bhavatādarāt ।
asmannāmnā prakarttavyaṃ praṇāmam api sadguro ।। dakṣiṇādeśanāpy asmannāmnā buddhādisāṃghikaiḥ । bhavatā kārayitavyā ity asmāsu kṛpāṃ kuru ।। yathāsmākam itaḥ pretalokā muktir bhaved dhruvaṃ । tathāsmāsu bhavāmc chāstā kṛpayā kartum arhāti ।।
iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ sarvaiḥ sa maudgalyāyanaḥ sudhīḥ । śrutvā tatheti saṃśrutya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tatas tān pretikān sarvān sa maudgalyāyano yatiḥ । samālokya samāśvāsya punar etat samabravīt ।।
tatra yūyaṃ ca sarva śvaḥ pravṛtte saṃghabhojane । sasaṃghaṃ śrīghanaṃ draṣṭuṃ samāyāta samādarāt ।। iti tenārhātādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te pretakā api । tatheti hi pratijñāya praṇatvā taṃ vane yayuḥ ।।
tataḥ sa saugato bhikṣur maudgalyo yatir ātmavit । gatvā rājagṛhe teṣāṃ jñātīnāṃ samupācaran ।। tatra sarvatra teṣāṃ tat jñātīnāṃ bhavaneṣu sa । gatvā teṣāṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ sarvam evaṃ nyavedayat ।।
tataḥ sa tatra sarvāṃs tāṃ jñātīn āhūya sādaraṃ । teṣāṃ pretagater muktihetor evaṃ samabravīt ।। śṛṇuta bho mahābhāgya yūyaṃ sarve samāhitāḥ । yuṣmākaṃ jñātivargāṇāṃ muktihetuṃ pravakṣyate ।।
yato yuṣmatsagotrās te matsariṇo durāśayāḥ । āgṛhītapariṣkārā daśākuśalasaṃcarāḥ ।। nāpi dānaṃ pradattaṃ taiḥ kasmai ci kvāpi kiṃ cana । paradattāny api śrutvā dṛṣṭvā vā paryabhāṣyata ।।
arhanto bhikṣavo vā tair yācakāś ca gṛhāgatāḥ । paribhāṣyābhisaṃtarjya niṣkāsitā gṛhād valāt ।। pretā iva sadā bhikṣāṃ yācitveme abhibhuṃjate । ity arhato yatī cāpi dṛṣṭvaiva te abhyanindayan ।।
etatkarmavipākais te pretībhūtā vane adhunā । kṣutpipāsāhatā nityaṃ vibhramyante abhiduḥkhitāḥ ।। tat tesāṃ tan mahatpāpamuktihetor ihādhunā । saṃbuddhaśāsane dānaṃ kartum ichāmy ahaṃ khalu ।।
mayaitad dakṣiṇādeśās tan nāmnā kārayiṣyate । tadā tat pāpamuktās te sarve yāyur divaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। tad atra śraddhayā yūyaṃ yathāśakti mayārthitāḥ । saṃghabhojanasāmagriṃ sarve pradātum arhaya ।।
saṃghabhojye pravṛtte atra sarve te pretikā api । draṣṭuṃ samāgamiṣyanti yūyaṃ cāgaṃtum arhatha ।। ity uktvā prārthite tena maudgalyena dayālunā । śrutvā taj jātayaḥ sarve vismayāṃ samupāyayuḥ ।।
tatas te vismitāḥ sarve tat pretagatimuktaye । tat bhojyasāmagrīṃ śraddhayā dātum icchire ।। ke cit tasmai suvarṇāni ke cid ratnāni saṃdaduḥ । ke cid ropyādi dhātūṃś ca dravyāni vividhāni cā ।। taṇḍulāni daduḥ ke cid dadur dhānyāni ke cana ।
ke cid daduḥ kalāyāṃś ca godhūmāṃś ca yavān api ।। kulmāṣān masurāṃś cāpi māṣacanakasarṣapān । mudgāṃś cāpi tathānyāṃś ca sarvān vrīhin daduḥ pare ।। tilapriyaṃgusiddhārthān bhaṃgāś ca rājikā api ।
mūlaśākakadamvāṃś ca patrapuṣpāṃkurāṇi ca ।। śṛṅgaverātipakvāni phalāni vividhāni ca । surasāni supathyāni pradaduś cāpare mudā ।। tiktāmlalavaṇādīni rasāni vividhāni ca ।
śunṭhīś ca pippirīś cāpi maricāni dadur mudā ।। hiṅguṃ ca jīrakāṃś cānye viḍarkasaiṃdhavādi ca । anye ghṛtāni tailāni pradaduḥ śraddhayā mudā ।। śaktūṃś ca piṣṭakāṃś cānyamodakāṃś ca dadur mudā ।
tathā dadhīni dugdhāni madhuni ca guḍāni ca ।। tathānye sarkarāś cāpi pradaduḥ śraddhayā mudā । tathauṣadhāni pathyāni pācakāni daduḥ pare ।। lāṅgalīpūgatāmbūlaravaṃgādīni saṃdaduḥ ।
sarvapeyāni bhojyāni vividhāny api । sarve te jñātayas teṣāṃ saṃghabhokṣyāya saṃdaduḥ ।। evaṃ te sarvavastūni datvā sarve pramoditāḥ । sāṃjalayaḥ praṇatvā taṃ maudgalyaṃ yatim ūcire ।।
bhadanto anugrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ bhavān । sarvasaṃghaṃ samabhyarcya bhojayatu pratoṣayan ।। vayam apy āgamiṣyāmaḥ pravṛtte saṃghabhojane । tān pretān samupāyātān sarvān draṣṭuṃ sabāndhavāḥ ।।
iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā tatheti sa prabodhayan । tāni dravyāni sarvāṇi gṛhītvā svāśrame yayau ।। tataḥ sa bhikṣur āyuṣmān vihāre samupācaran । dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā sāñjaliḥ samupāśrayan ।।
tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ maudgalyam upasthitaṃ । prahasan suprasannāsyaḥ samāmaṃtryaitad abravīt ।। kaṃ cit te kuśalaṃ vatsa kuto atrāsi samāgataḥ । lokeṣu kiṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ tan pracakṣva mahāmate ।।
ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sa maudgalyāyanaḥ sudhīḥ । bhagavantaṃ tam ānatvā sāñjalir etad abravīt ।। bhagavan kṛpayā śāstaḥ sarvatra kauśalaṃ mama । rājagṛhe pure piṃḍaṃ yācituṃ samupācaran ।।
tatra mārge vanopānte paṃca pretaśatāny api । dṛṣṭvā māṃ samupasṛtya praṇatvaitad vadanti vai ।। bhadanta tad vijānīyā yad vayaṃ pretikā ime । sarve rājagṛhe jātā gṛhasthāḥ paurikāḥ khalu ।।
tadā vayaṃ svayaṃ naṣṭā daśākuśalacāriṇaḥ । ete svadaivayogena pretībhūtāś carāmahe ।। tad bhavān kṛpayāsmākaṃ pretagativimuktaye । jñātīnām api sarveṣāṃ karmaplotiṃ nivedya hi ।।
chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ kṛtvāpy asmannāmnā sasāṃghikaṃ । bhagavantaṃ samabhyarcya bhojayituṃ samarhati ।। asmannāmnāya saṃbuddhaṃ sasaṃghaṃ namatāṃ bhavān । dakṣiṇādeśanāś cāsmannāmnā deśayatum arhasi ।।
tato nūnaṃ vayaṃ sarve pretagativimocitāḥ । nirmuktapāpakāḥ śuddhāḥ prāpnuyāma surālayaṃ ।। ity asmatprārthanāṃ kṛtvā kṛpayāsmān samuddharan । bodhimārge pratisthāpya pātum arhati sarvadā ।।
iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā tathā rājagṛhe gataḥ । tad jñātīnāṃ puras teṣāṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedya ca ।। chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ tebhyo yācitvāham ihācare । tathārcayitum ichāmi bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।।
iti me prārthanāṃ kṛtvā bhavāṃ chāstā jagadguruḥ । tad adhivāsanāṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā tān samuddhara ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tatheti saṃpratiśrutya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।।
tato matvā sa maudgalyo bhagavato adhivāsitaṃ । sahasā bhojyasāmagrīṃ sapauraiḥ samasādhayat ।। tato anye dyuḥ prabhātāyāṃ sarvasādhitasiddhite । sāñjalis taṃ munīndraṃ ca praṇatvaitat samabravīt ।।
bhagavan sarvasāmagrīṃ saṃsādhitaṃ susiddhyate । tat sarvasāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ sahasāgaṃtum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavāṃ sa munīśvaraḥ । bhikṣuṃ prāha samāhūya gaṇḍīm ākoṭyatām iti ।।
tadādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā bhikṣus tatheti saḥ । āśrutya sahasādāya gaṇḍīm ākoṭayat tadā ।। tad gaṇḍīśabdam ākarṇya sarve te sāṃghikā api । vihāre sahasāgatya bhagavantaṃ praṇemire ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra svāsane samupāviśat । sarve te sāṃghikāś cāpi kramāt svasvāsane aviśan ।। tatas tad jñātayaḥ sarve tatrānye paurikā api । tān pretān draṣṭum āyātā upatasthuḥ sakautukāḥ ।।
tadā te pretikāḥ sarve prakṣiptāḥ karmavāyubhiḥ । bahulokāntare dure yātās tasthur vimohitāḥ ।। tadā sa yatir ālokya sarvasaṃghān samāsthitān । tadjñātibandhuvargāṃś ca pretān draṣṭuṃ samācarat ।।
tatra pretān adṛṣṭvā sa maudgalyo vismitāśayaḥ । kiṃ te atra nāgatā veti samantato vyalokayat ।। vilokayan sa sarvatra nādrakṣīt tāṃ samaṃtataḥ । sa saṃdigdhaḥ punas tatra samyagdṛṣṭyā vyalokayat ।।
sarvatrāpi sa tāṃ pretān adṛṣṭvā vismayānvitaḥ । sarvatra magadhe apaśyat samyagdṛśā samāhitaḥ ।। tatrāpi ca sa sarvatra naiva kaṃ cid apaśyate । tato ativismito anyatra divyadṛśābhyalokayat ।।
aṃgavaṃgakaliṃgeṣu saurāṣṭramagadheṣu ca । tatrāpi tān adṛṣṭvā sa narakeṣu samantataḥ । divyena cakṣuṣā paśyan na ca tatrāpy apaśyata ।। tataś caturmahārājabhuvaneṣu samantataḥ ।
sa divyacakṣuṣā paśyaṃs tatrāpi nābhyapaśyata ।। tatrāpi tān adṛṣṭvā sa maudgalyo vismayānvitaḥ । devālayeṣu sarvatra krameṇa samalokayat ।। tatrāpi tāṃ samanteṣu sa maudgalyo ativismitaḥ ।
tān adṛṣṭvātisaṃdigdho bhagavatāntike acarat ।। tatra sa purato gatvā śāstāraṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā paprachaitat pravṛttitāṃ ।। bhagavan sarvalokeṣu paśyatā divyacakṣusā ।
