mayā na dṛśyate kaś cit te pretāḥ kvādhunā gatāḥ ।। teṣāṃ nāmnā bhavatpūjāṃ karttum etat prasādhitaṃ । yad atra nāgatāḥ kecit tat te pretā gatāḥ kuha ।। dṛśyante na mayā kvāpi sarvatrāpi samīkṣyate ।
eko api nāgato hy atra kva gatās te adhunā khalu ।। tan me cittaṃ prasaṃdigdhaṃ dṛṣṭvā śāstā bhavān sudṛk । teṣāṃ gatiṃ samākhyāya saṃbodhayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena maudgalyena sa sarvavit ।
bhagavāṃs taṃ samālokya maudgalyam etad abravīt ।। maudgalya mā kṛthā yatnaṃ khedam evābhipatsyase । gatās te pretikāḥ sarve sudūrabhuvane adhunā ।। sarve te yatidevarṣipratyekasugatair api ।
adṛśye viṣaye yātāḥ preritāḥ karmavāyubhiḥ ।। yadi sarvāṃ ca tāṃ draṣṭuṃ vāṃchasi tvam ihāśritaḥ । sarvāṃs tāṃ darśayiṣyāmi paśya buddhānubhāvatāṃ ।। tad atra tvaṃ samādāya gaṇḍīm ākoṭaya drutaṃ ।
oṃ namo bhagavate aparimitāyurjñānasuviniścitatejorājāya tathāgatāyārhate samyakambuddhāya ।। oṃ puṇye puṇye mahāpuṇye aparimitapuṇye aparimitapuṇyajñānasaṃbhāropacite । oṃ sarvasaṃskārapariśuddhe dharmate gagaṇasamudgate svabhāvaviśuddhe mahānayaparivāre svāhā । aṣṭottaraśatākṣaryyānayāsaṃlabdhacetanāḥ ।।
sarve te atrāgamiṣyanti gaṇḍīśabdābhināditāḥ । iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa pratibodhitaḥ ।। sahasā tat sabhāmadhye gaṇḍīm ākoṭayat tathā । tad gaṇḍīśabdam ākarṇya sarve te pretikā api । pariśuddhāśayā draṣṭuṃ vihāre samupācaran ।। tatra sarve api te pretā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā ।
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāñjalayaḥ praṇemire ।। kramāt tāṃ sarvasaṃghāṃś ca praṇatvā te pramoditāḥ । sarve apy ekāntam āśritya paśyanta upatasthire ।। tatra tad jñātayaḥ sarve paurikāś cāpare api ca ।
tān pretān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā tasthuḥ sakautukāḥ ।। evaṃ sarve api te pretāḥ svasvajñātīn upasthitān । bhātrādīn bandhuvargāṃś ca dṛṣṭvaivam upatasthire ।। tataḥ so arhan mahābhijño maudgalyas tān upasthitān ।
pretān sarvān samālokya natvāhaivaṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña te pretāḥ sarva āgatāḥ । tad eṣāṃ bhagavāṃ cchāstānugrahaṃ karttum arhati ।। nivedyeti sa maudgalyaḥ saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ kramāt ।
sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ samabhyarcya bhojayan samatoṣayat ।। tataḥ sa sarvasaṃghaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃtṛptikaṃ mudā । apanīyāśu pātrāṇi hastādīn samaśodhayat ।। tataḥ khapurasūkṣmailātāmbūlādi rasāyanaṃ ।
datvā kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā prārthayat sa munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavāṃ chāstā sasāṃghikaḥ । dakṣiṇādeśanām ebhyaḥ pretebhyaḥ kartum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te pretikā mudā ।
sasaṃghaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā sādaram upatasthire ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghas tān upasthitān । dakṣiṇādeśanāṃ tebhyaḥ sarvebhyo vidadhe śubhāṃ ।। ito dānād dhi yat puṇyaṃ tat pretān anugachatu ।
uttiṣṭhantaḥ prayānty ete sarve pretāḥ surālayaṃ ।। ity ādiśya punas tatra bhagavāṃ sa munīśvaraḥ । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhyāparimitāyuṣas tadā ।। dhāraṇyā guṇamāhātmyaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
saṃsāre mānuṣe janma durlabhaṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ । mānuṣye labhyamāne api kṣaṇasaṃpat sudurlabhā ।। mānuṣye alabhyamāne hi jantūnāṃ sukhatā kutaḥ । duḥkhāny eva bhave nityaṃ puṇye matiḥ kathaṃ caret ।।
vinā puṇyamatiṃ jantuḥ saddharme katham ācaret । vinā saddharmabhāvena sadgatiṃ katham āpnuyāt ।। preteṣu sarvadā nityaṃ kṣutpipāsāvidāhitaḥ । tiryakṣu narakeṣv eva bhraman duḥkhāny avāpnuyāt ।।
tad atra mānuṣe janmaprāptair yatnena mānavaiḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ śrotavyaṃ sadvṛṣaṃ mudā ।। saddharmaśrutamātreṇa mahatpuṇyam avāpnuyāt । etat puṇyavipākena sadgurau sarvadā bhajet ।।
sadguror upadeśena saddharmeṣv eva sadācaret । etatpuṇyavipākena sadgatiṃ sarvadā vrajet ।। tatra sukhāni saṃbhuktvā saṃcareta śubhe sadā ।। etad dharmānubhāvena mahatsamṛddhim āpnuyāt ।
mahatsamṛddhisaṃpatsu karttavyaṃ dānam arthiṣu ।। dānena varddhyate lakṣmīr lakṣmīmāṃ cchobhate pumān । sadbuddhiḥ sadguṇādhāro yaśobhāgyasukhānvitaḥ ।। tataḥ saugatadharmāṇi śrutvā nityaṃ prabodhitaḥ ।
triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajed bhaktyā sadādarāt ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhicittaṃ samāpnuyāt । bodhicitte hi labdhe hi bodhisatvo bhavet kṛtī ।। tataḥ sa bodhicittena daśapāramitāḥ kramāt ।
paripūrya mahāsatvas trividhāṃ bodhim āpnuyāt ।। tato māragaṇāṃ jitvā pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalaḥ । qsākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāt ।। evaṃ vijñāya martyena karttavyaṃ dānam arthine ।
dānena sadgatiṃ yāyād adātā durgatiṃ vrajet ।। durgatiṣu sadā bhuktvā duḥkhāni vividhāṃ sa । sarvadā duḥkhasaṃkliṣṭaḥ pāpeṣv evārataś caret ।। etatpāpavipākena daśasv akuśaleṣv api ।
nirato hy aviśaṃkena saṃcareta pramādataḥ ।। tataḥ so hy atipāpiṣṭhaḥ saddharmanindakaḥ kudhīḥ । svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayen nāstikaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।। tato atipāpasaṃkliṣṭaḥ pratikṣipya jinān api ।
ghoreṣu narakeṣv eva gatvā bhraman sadā vaset ।। sadāpi narakeṣv evaṃ bhramatas tasya duḥkhinaḥ । kaścin naiva samuddhartuṃ śaknuyāt saugatād ṛte ।। yāvan na smarate buddhaṃ tāvat sa narake vaset ।
yad eva smarate buddhaṃ tadā syāc chuddhitāśayaḥ ।। tadā taṃ kṛpayā buddho dṛṣṭvā bauddhena cakṣuṣā । puṇyakareṇa saṃspṛṣṭvā samuddhared araṃ tataḥ ।। tatas taṃ pāpinaṃ bauddhā dharmāmbubhir viśodhya ca ।
krameṇa bodhimārgeṣu niyojayet prabodhayan ।। tataḥ sa pariśuddhātmā saṃbuddhaśāsane rataḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saddharma eva prācaret ।। tataḥ satvahitārthe sa bodhicaryāsamudyataḥ ।
kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvā pūrayituṃ samudyamet ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ pūrayitvā samāhitaḥ । bodhisatvo mahāsatvo buddhātmajo bhaved api ।। tataḥ kleśagaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ ।
trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāt ।। evaṃ matvā sadā nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । saddharmaṃ samupāśritya caradhvaṃ mānavā mudā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te brāhmaṇādayaḥ । sarve lokā parijñāya dṛṣṭasatyās tathācaran ।।
tathā sarve api te pretāḥ śrutvā tad dharmadeśanāṃ । mudā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā śuddhātmānas tato acaran ।। tatas tad jñātayaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā śrutvā sakautukāḥ । sasaṃghaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā svasvālayaṃ yayur mudā ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān buddhaḥ samutthāya saṣāṃghikaḥ । dhyānālayaṃ samāśritya tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। sa maudgalyāyanaś cāpi kṛtakṛtyaḥ pramoditaḥ । śāstāraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ svam āśramaṃ samāśrayat ।।
tadā sarve api te pretāḥ saṃbuddhe abhiprasāditāḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tataś cyutā divaṃ yayuḥ ।। tatrotpannā hi te sarve mahatsaukhyasamanvitāḥ । pariśuddhasubhadrāṅgā vismitā etad abruvan ।।
aho asmākaṃ mahatsaukhyaṃ kim evaṃ jāyate adhunā । kutaś cyutāḥ kuhāyāmaḥ karmaṇā kena vā vayaṃ ।। atha buddhānubhāvena sarve te pretapūrvakāḥ । devaputrā anusmṛtvā prabodhitāḥ samabruvan ।।
bhavanto yad vayaṃ sarve pretā buddhānubhāvataḥ । maudgalyasyārhato bhikṣoḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprayatnataḥ ।। saṃbuddhadarśanaprāptās triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । etat puṇyaparispṛṣṭāḥ pariśuddhatrikāyikāḥ ।।
tataḥ pretagateś cyutvā svargaloke samāgatāḥ । mahaddivyasukhāny evam atra labhāmahe adhunā ।। etat satyaṃ parijñāya tasya śāstur jagadguroḥ । punaḥ sarve vayaṃ gatvā satkṛtya prabhajemahi ।।
iti saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā sarve te pretapūrvakāḥ । devaputrāḥ śubhāmbhobhiḥ snātvā divyāmvarāvṛtāḥ ।। divyasugaṃdhaliptāṅgā divyālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ । divyapūjopacārāṇi gṛhītvā mahadutsavaiḥ ।
sarvaṃ veṇuvanaṃ bhābhir avabhāsya samantataḥ ।। vihāre samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praharṣitā upācaran ।। tatra divyopacārais taiḥ pūjāṃgais taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।
sarve api te samabhyarcya satkṛtya śraddhayābhajan ।। tatra caikāntam āśritya saddharmmaśravaṇotsukāḥ । kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। atha sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān ।
āryasatyaṃ samārabhaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te pretapūrvakāḥ । devaputrāś ca dharmāṇāṃ viśeṣatvaṃ pralebhire ।। tatas te muditāḥ sarve saṃbodhipadavāṃchinaḥ ।
śāstāraṃ taṃ punar natvā samālokyaitad abruvan ।। bhagavan yad vayaṃ sarve vimuktakarmabaṃdhanāḥ । pretalokāt paricyutvā svarge yātāḥ sma sāṃprataṃ ।। divyasukhāni sāmbhuktvā devaiḥ saha pramoditāḥ । saddharmaguṇam ākarṇya carāmahe sadādhunā ।।
tat kṛpālo yatas tasya maudgalyasya mahāmateḥ । kṛpadṛṣṭiprasādena nūnaṃ manyāmahe vayaṃ ।। tad bhavaddarśanaṃ prāpya pītvā dharmāmṛtāny api । muditāḥ śraddhayā bhaktyā triratnaṃ saṃbhajāmahe ।।
etatpuṇyaiḥ parītāṅgāḥ pariśuddhāśayā mudā । bhavatāṃ darśanaṃ kartuṃ bhūyaḥ prāyāmahe vayaṃ ।। tathā ca bhavatāṃ śāstaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । āryadharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā saṃtuṣṭiṃ na labhāmahe ।।
tad vayaṃ bhavatām evaṃ sarvadā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya samupāsṛtya bhaktum ichāmahe punaḥ ।। tad bhavān kṛpayāsmā kaṃ kṛtvānugraham ābhavaṃ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sarvadā trātum arhati ।।
bhavatāṃ kṛpayāsmābhi duḥkhābdhiḥ parilaṃghitaḥ । satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ ca jñānavajreṇa bhidyate ।। jñānacakṣuś ca saṃprāptaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ māyāmayaṃ bhavaṃ । āryamārgaś ca saṃprāptaḥ prāptā ca nirvṛtiśrutiḥ ।।
dhanyā ime vayaṃ sarve yad bhavaccharaṇaṃ gatāḥ । āryadharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mahānandaṃ labhāmahe ।। dhanyās te puruṣāḥ sarve ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । sadā dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā kārāṃ kurvanti śāsane ।।
evaṃ bhavāṃ jagacchāstā sarvasatvānukampayā । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya tiṣṭhatu sarvadā sukhaṃ ।। iti prabhākhya sarve te devaputrāḥ pramoditāḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvā ca suprasannā divaṃ yayuḥ ।।
tatra sarve api te devās triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । prabhejire sadā smṛtvā saṃbodhipadavāṃchinaḥ ।। tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya bhagavān so anumoditaḥ । taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ śiṣyaṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।।
sādhu maudgalya saṃvṛttaṃ saphalaṃ te kṛpāmate । yat tvayā prakṛtaṃ kāyaṃ vaiyāvṛttaṃ suśobhitaṃ ।। yannāmnā bhikṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā buddhapūjā kṛtā tvayā । te sarve devalokeṣu samutpannāḥ pratisthitāḥ ।।
te sarve adya niśāyāṃ matsakāśaṃ samupagatāḥ । teṣāṃ bhadrāśayaṃ dṛṣṭvā saddharmo deśito mayā ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā te sarve api pramoditāḥ । dṛṣṭasatyāḥ prakrāntāś ca gachanti tridaśālaye ।।
tatra svarge api te sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । prabhajanti sadā nityaṃ saṃbodhiguṇavāṃchinaḥ ।। yannāmnā yat kṛtaṃ karma tat phalaṃ te prabhuṃjate । evaṃ lokahitaṃ kartuṃ karttavyaṃ puṇyasādhanaṃ ।। evaṃ lokahitaṃ kṛtvā prakurvanti śubhāni ye ।
te pumāṃso mahāsatvā bodhisatvā jinātmajāḥ ।। evaṃ vijñāya lokānāṃ hitaṃ kartuṃ samudyataḥ । saddharmasādhaneṣv eva caritavyaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā so arhaṃ mahāmatiḥ ।
satyam iti pratijñāya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ ।। tataḥ so arhan mahābhijñas tac chāstrādiṣṭam ādarāt । tad jñātīnāṃ purogatvā sarvam evaṃ nyavedayat ।। te api ca jñātayaḥ sarve tenārhatā niveditaṃ ।
śrutvā satyam iti jñātvā prāmodyaṃ pratilebhire ।। tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhejire samādarāt ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā narādhipa ।
lokaprabodhanārthena tava prītyā prakathyate ।। evaṃ vijñāya rājendra pretānāṃ śubhasādhanaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ lokaiḥ kārayituṃ tvam arhasi ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bhaven nūnaṃ samaṃtataḥ ।
sarvasatvahitodbhutaṃ mahatpuṇyaṃ hi satphalaṃ ।। iti matvā mahārāja lokān sarvān prabodhayan । pratiṣṭhāpya śubhe dharme pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ ।
tatheti pratimoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। pretāvadānaṃ manujā idaṃ ye śṛṇvanti ye cāpi niśāmayanti । te sarva evaṃ pratilabdhapuṇyā bhuktvā sukhāni pracaranti loke ।। athāśoko mahārājaḥ pramoditaḥ ।
upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evaṃ abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ ।
upagupto nareṃdrāṃ taṃ samalokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cāpy anumodaya ।। puraikasamaye buddhaḥ sākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ ।
sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ sāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। śrāvastyā nikaṭe araṇye jetāśrame śubhālaye । vihāre śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣubhiś cailakair api ।। bhikṣuṇībhiḥ suśilābhir upāsikāgaṇair api ।
upāsakais tathānyaiś ca triratnaśaraṇāgataiḥ ।। bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi satvoddharaṇatatparaiḥ । vijahāra jagallokaṃ dharmāṃśubhiḥ prabhāsayan ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ ।
śakrādayaḥ suparvāṇabrahmādi lokapālakāḥ ।। daityā nāgāś ca gaṃdharvā yakṣakinnararākṣasāḥ । garuḍā vidyādharāś cāpi sarve te saṃpracerire ।। tataḥ sarve api te tatra puraskṛtya samantataḥ ।
parivṛtya sasaṃghaṃ tam upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ ।
dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya prābhyanandañ chūbhāśayāḥ ।। tasminn avasare tatra vṛddhārāmodakārthinī । kacaṅgalābhidhā kumbhaṃ dhṛtvā kūpāntike acarat ।। tatra tāṃ bhagavān dṛṣṭvā matvā janmāntaraprasūṃ ।
ānaṃdaṃ samupāmaṃtrya pura evam abhāṣata ।। gachānaṃda tvam etasyāṃ vṛddhāyāṃ prārthayāmṛtaṃ । bhagavāṃs tṛṣito mātas tad ambu dīyatām iti ।। etad bhagavatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvānaṃdas tatheti saḥ ।
sahasā samupāśritya tāṃ vṛddhām evam abravīt ।। mātar me bhagavāñ chāstā tṛṣito ayam ihādhunā । tat pānīyaṃ pradatvā me mahaddharmam avāpnuhi ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sā sthavirā satī ।
tam ānandaṃ samālokya muditaivam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta sādhu tatrāham amṛtapūritaṃ ghaṭaṃ । svayam eva samānīya dāsyāmi vrajatāṃ bhavān ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa ānaṃdaḥ prabodhitaḥ ।
upetyaivaṃ samākhyāya śāstuḥ pura upāśrayat ।। tadā sā sahasā kṛtvā ghaṭaṃ śuddhāmbupūritaṃ । svayam eva samādāya tatrābhisaṃmukhācarat ।। tatra sā samupāśritya prādrākṣīt taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṇḍitaṃ ।। vyāmaprabhābhibhāsvaṃtaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ । jaṃgamam iva ratnābhaṃ saumyaṃ samantabhadrakaṃ ।। saha taddarśaṇāt tatra putrasnehasamudbhavāḥ ।
stanābhyāṃ praśrutās tasyāḥ kṣīradhārā niraṃtaraṃ ।। tato dharmānubhāvena smṛtvā pūrvabhavātmajaṃ । putra putreti soktvā taṃ pariṣvektum upācarat ।। tadā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve evaṃ tāṃ samupadrutāṃ ।
dṛṣṭvaiva sahasotthāya pradhārayitum ārabhan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā bhagavāṃ chastā sarvāṃs tāṃ sāṃghikān api । sahasā samupāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samādiśat ।। mā bhikṣava imāṃ vṛddhāṃ dhārāyatātra muñcata ।
paṃcajanmaśatāny eṣā mātā me bhūyataḥ purā ।। tatpūrvajanmamāteyaṃ putrasnehānubhāvinī । samāliṃgatum īchantī mama gātre pradhāvati ।। yady atraiṣā nivāryyete gātra me śleṣmaṇād api ।
idānīṃ rudhiraṃ hy uṣṇaṃ kamṭhād asyāḥ kṣaret kṣaṇāt ।। kṛtajñatām anusmṛtvā dṛṣṭvemāṃ putralālasāṃ । kāruṇyād gātrasaṃśleṣaṃ dadāmy atrānukaṃpayā ।। iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ ।
tāṃ śāstuḥ pūrvaprasūṃ matvā vyavatasthuḥ savismayāḥ ।। tatkṣaṇād urddhavāhuḥ sā samīkṣya taṃ munīśvaraṃ । sahasā saṃpradhāvitvā samāliṃgya namac ciraṃ ।। tataś cirāt samutthāya sā vṛddhā sāñjalir mudā ।
śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya puras tasthau samāhitā ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ puraḥ samupāsthitāṃ । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sa vṛddhāpi kacaṃgalā ।
pariśuddhāśayā bhadrā bodhicaryā prabodhitā ।। satkāyadṛṣṭibhūmīdhraṃ viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ । nirbhidya jñānavajreṇa dṛṣṭasatyaprabodhitā ।। saṃprāpya śrotaāpattiphalaṃ sākṣat kṛtodyamā ।
sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā gāthā imā abhāṣata ।। yat karttavyaṃ svaputreṇa mātur duṣkarakāriṇā । tat kṛtaṃ bhavatā me atra cittaṃ mokṣaparāyaṇaṃ ।। durgatibhyaḥ samuddhṛtya svarge mokṣaṃ ca sāṃprataṃ ।
sthāpito ahaṃ prayatnena viśeṣasaṃprabodhane ।। tathā me anugrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃbodhipadasādhanaṃ । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dātum arhati sāṃprataṃ bhavān ।। bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā triratnabhajanodyatā ।
pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣye brahmacārikāṃ ।। ity arthitaṃ tayā śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tasyāś cittaviśuddhatvaṃ matvaivaṃ samupādiśat ।। yadi śraddhāsti te mātaḥ pravrajyāsadhane khalu ।
bharttur anujñāṃ samāsādya prāgacha cara saṃvaraṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā saṃpramoditā । tathā hīti pratijñāya muniṃ natvā tato acarat ।। tatra sā sahasā gehe gatvā taṃ svāminaṃ mudā ।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā puraḥ sthitvaivam abravīt ।। svāmi cchṛṇv adbhutaṃ vakṣye yad adyāhaṃ jalārthinī । ghaṭaṃ dhṛtvā vahir deśe kūpāntikam upācare ।। tatra māṃ samupāyātāṃ dṛṣṭvānando mahāyatiḥ ।
sahasā samupāśritya bhagavate ambu yācate ।। tato ahaṃ sahasā śuddhaiḥ pūrayitvā jalair ghaṭaṃ । dhṛtvā svayaṃ pradātuṃ tat sabhāyām upasaṃcare ।। tatra tam śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā cittaṃ me snehamohitaṃ ।
kṣāradhārā stanābhyāṃ ca saṃpraśrutā niraṃtaraṃ ।। tatrāhaṃ sneharāgāṃdhā svātmajam iva taṃ muniṃ । ūrddhavāhuḥ pariṣvaktuṃ pradhāvāmi bhavāntare ।। evaṃ mām abhidhāvantīṃ dṛṣṭvā te sāṃghikā api ।
sarve pradhātum ichantaḥ pradhāvanti samutthitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān evam utthitān । sahasā samupāmaṃtrya pura evaṃ samādiśat ।। mā imāṃ sarvathā yūyaṃ nivārayitum arhatha ।
yan mameyaṃ puṇyaṃ ca śatajanmaprasū kila ।। tad atra māṃ samālokya svātmajasneharāgiṇī । pariṣvaktuṃ samīchantī pradhāvatīyam unmukhī ।। yady atreṣātra dhāryyeta purato me vimūrchitā ।
uṣṇaṃ rudhiram utsṛjya mṛtyuṃ yāyān na saṃśayaḥ ।। etac chāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te sāṃghikās tathā । prabodhitāḥ praṇatvā māṃ svasvāsane samāśritāḥ ।। evaṃ tena munīndreṇa samākhyātaṃ niśamya tat ।
sarvaṃ prabudhyamānāhaṃ purāvṛttaṃ smarāmi hi ।। tato ahaṃ vismayākrāṃtahṛdayātyabhinaṃditā । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatiṣṭhāmi sādaraṃ ।। tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mām evaṃ samupasthitāṃ । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya samādiśati sadvṛṣaṃ ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mano me atipramodite । bhūyo api tad rasāsvādatṛṣitaṃ pātum ichate ।। sarve te sāṃghikās tatra saddharmāmṛtatṛptitāḥ । śuddhātmānaḥ subhadrāṃgāḥ pariśuddhās trimaṃḍalāḥ ।।
śuddhaśīlāḥ śubhācārā dayākāruṇyabhāvinaḥ । sarvasattvahitādhānāḥ saṃsāralābhanispṛhāḥ ।। samādhidhāraṇīvidyā ghaṭamānāḥ samāhitāḥ । sākṣād arhatpadaprāptā nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ ।।
saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbodhisādhanodyatāḥ । vihāre samupāsīnāḥ pradṛśyante mayā prabho ।। tat sabhāgaṃ cariṃ prāptuṃ pravrajyāvratam ichyate । tad atra kṛpayā bharttas tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।।
iti bhāryāsamākhyātaṃ śrutvā so atidaridritaḥ । sāścaryastambhitas tasthau paśyaṃs tām eva niścalaḥ ।। tataḥ sa suciraṃ bhāryāṃ tām evam abhilokayan । viyogaśaṃkayā trastaḥ śanair evam abhāṣata ।।
are nāri pramūdhāsi kim evaṃ tvaṃ prabhāṣase । katham evaṃ tvayākhyātaṃ ko atra satyaṃ pratīṣyati ।। yad asau bhagavān buddhaś cakravarttinṛpātmajaḥ । sarvatraidhātukādhīśo dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।।
jagacchāstā jagannāthaḥ sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ । munīndro mārajid arhan ṣaḍabhijñas tathāgataḥ ।। bodhisatvo mahāsatvaḥ samaṃtabhadrarūpakaḥ । daśabalo maheśākhyo brahmacārī jitendriyaḥ ।।
subrahmāmaradaityādilokānāṃ sarvadehināṃ । śaraṇyo mānanīyo hi vandyaḥ pūjyo bhavaty api ।। tvam evaṃ durbhagā nārī daridratātiduḥkhinī । dāsī paravatī preṣyā kṛpaṇā duḥkṛtākṛtiḥ ।।
katham evaṃvidhāyās te garbhe jāto apy asau mahān । bodhicittaṃ samāsādya prācarad bodhicārikāṃ ।। yataḥ puṇyavipākena pūrya pāramitāḥ kramāt । adhunā bodhim āsādya saṃbuddho ayaṃ bhavaty api ।।
etatpuṇyavibhāgena kathaṃ te īdṛśī gatiḥ । adyāpīdṛgavasthā hi kiṃ cit saukhyaṃ na vidyate ।। tad atra mā vadaivaṃ ca tathoktvā naiva śobhase । kas tavaitad vacaḥ śrutvā supratītaḥ pramāṇayet ।।
dhik pravādāgnidagdhāṅgā mahatkaṣṭābhikhedītā । vamitvā rudhiraṃ hy uṣṇaṃ tvaṃ nūnaṃ maraṇaṃ vrajeḥ ।। mithyāvādābhisaṃkalpād api hi narake vrajet । tvam api ca tathā nūnaṃ narake na vrajeḥ kathaṃ ।।
narakeṣu sadā nityaṃ duḥkhāni vividhāni vai । bhuktvātivedanākrāntā suciraṃ sthāsyase dhruvaṃ ।। iti bharttroditaṃ śrutvā sā vṛddhā strī kacaṃgalā । vibhinnahṛdayā tasthau tan nirāśābhimohitā ।।
tadā sā sucireṇaiva saṃprāpya cetanāṃ tataḥ । bharttāraṃ taṃ punar dṛṣṭvā bodhayitum abhāṣata ।। svāminn atra prasīda tvaṃ mām evaṃ vada sarvathā । satyam etan mayā proktaṃ na mithyeti prakalpaya ।।
yadi mithyāvacaḥ syān me tenāhaṃ narake vraje । atha me vacanaṃ satyam atrāhaṃ sadgatiṃ vraje ।। tenātrobhayathāpy eva viyogaṃ nau bhavet khalu । sarveṣām api jaṃtūnām avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ bhave ।।
kim evaṃ jīvitenāpi kevalaṃ duḥkhabhāginā । yatra na vidyate dharmmaṃ tatra kiṃ sukhatāpi ca ।। dharmārtham eva saṃsāre janmadehārthasādhanaṃ । dharmaṃ vinā kim etair naḥ kevalaṃ duḥkhatāptaye ।।
iti matvā mahānto api śrīmanto api vicakṣaṇāḥ । sarvān parigrahān tyaktvā pravrajanti jināśrame ।। tathātrāhaṃ parijñāya saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatā । saddharmasādhanaṃ karttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ prabho ।।
tat pravrajyāvratānujñāṃ pradātuṃ me samarhasi । etatpuṇyavibhāgena tvaṃ cāpi sadgatiṃ vrajeḥ ।। yadi na dīyate anujñā pravrajyāvratasādhane । akasmāt mṛtyunāghrāte tadā kathaṃ nivāraye ।।
kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyaṃ vṛddhāhaṃ jirṇitendriyā । iti matvātra māṃ naivaṃ nivārayitum arhasi ।। kiṃ cāhaṃ jaratī vṛddhā tat te kiṃ snehatā mayi । vṛddhayā durbalāṅgātra kārye kiṃ nu prayojanaṃ ।।
tvaṃ cāpi jarayākrānto vṛddho asi durbalendriyaḥ । tat kiṃ te sneharāgeṇa vṛddhāyā mayi sāṃprataṃ ।। adyāpi kiṃ sukhāśā nau jarākrāntaśarīrayoḥ । avaśyaṃ mṛtyur atrāvāṃ samākramya grasiṣyati ।।
tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tvaṃ cāpi kiṃ kariṣyasi । śocitveva niṣatsyāmi tvam apy evaṃ niṣatsyasi ।। avaśyam atra saṃsāre bhāvi bhāvā phalanty api । kasyāpi bhūyate nātra bhāvi bhāvānyathā kvacit ।।
svakṛtakarma evātra gṛhītvā sarvajaṃtavaḥ । yātā yānti ca yāsyaṃti dehaṃ tyaktvā yamālayaṃ ।। tatra yamājñayā sarve svakṛtakarmabhāginaḥ । dharmiṇaḥ sadgatiṃ yātāḥ pāpino durgatiṃ gatāḥ ।।
evaṃ sarve ime satvāḥ svadaivaphalabhoginaḥ । sasukhāni ca duḥkhāni bhuktvā bhramanti sarvadā ।। evaṃ svāmin parijñāya sarvadā sukhavāṃchibhiḥ । dharmam evātra saṃsāre karttavyaṃ yatnataḥ sadā ।।
dharman tu pravaraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ saugatasaṃvarodbhavaṃ । iti buddhaiḥ samākhyātaṃ tvayāpy etac chrutaṃ na kiṃ ।। tasmād ahaṃ munīndrasya śāsane śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dharttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ prabho ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ । sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāṃ ।। etad dharmavibhāgena tvaṃ cāpi sadgatiṃ vrajeḥ । iti matvā tathā svāmiṃs tad anujñāṃ dadātu me ।।
tvam atra svagṛhe sthitvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । yāvaj jīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā śubhe cara sadādarāt ।। etatpuṇyavipākena tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ sudhīr bhaveḥ । tatas te saugate dharme vāṃchā jāyeta cetasi ।।
tatas tvaṃ śraddhayā gatvā saṃbuddhaśāsane svayaṃ । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ prāpya sākṣād arhatvam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti matvā bhavān svāmin saddharmaṃ yadi vāñchati । tat pravrajyāvratānujñāṃ mahyaṃ pradātum arhati ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa daridraḥ prabodhitaḥ । tāṃ bhāryāṃ suciraṃ dṛṣṭvā śanair evam abhāṣata ।। hā priye katham eva tvaṃ māṃ vihātuṃ samichasi । kim atrāhaṃ vadiṣyāmi tvayaivaṃ pratibhāṣate ।।
yadi te asti mano dhairyyaṃ kṛtvā śraddhānvitāśrayā । pravraja saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cara satyasamāhitā ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā sā vṛddhāpi kacaṃgalā । bharttāraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ tato acarat pramoditā ।।
tataḥ sā sahasā gatvā tatrāśrame upāgatā । śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya purataḥ samupācarat ।। tatra tat purato gatvā sāñjaliḥ sā pramoditā । munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tad bhavāṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā mahyaṃ pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati ।। tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । savyena pāṇinā tasyā vṛddhāyāḥ śirasi spṛśan ।।
ehi mataś cara brahmacārikāṃ tvaṃ samāhitā । ity uktvā tāṃ samāgṛhya sāṃghike punar abravīt ।। gacha māta prajāpatyā gautamyāḥ śaraṇaṃ vraja । sārhantī bhikṣuṇīmātā pravrajyāṃ te pradāsyati ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā pratinaṃditā । tathety āśrutya śāstāraṃ taṃ praṇatvā tato acarat ।। tatra sā samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā tāṃ gautamīṃ mudā । upetya sāṃjalir natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। mātar atra samāyāmi bhavatyāḥ śaraṇaṃ mudā ।
tad bhavantī jaganmātā pravrajyāṃ pradadātu me ।। tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā gautamī sānumoditā । hastena śirasi spṛṣṭvā sāṃghikatāṃ samagrahīt ।। tatra sāśu prajāpatyāṃ pravrajitā yathāvidhiḥ ।
muṇḍitā khikkhirīpātrahastā kākhāyacīvarā ।। saumyendriyā subhadraṃgā vṛddhāpi sā kacaṃgalā । bhikṣuṇīgaṇamadhyasthā śāntarūpātyaśobhata ।। tataḥ sā bhikṣuṇī śāstu gautamyāś ca prasādataḥ ।
samādhidhāraṇīvidyādhyayanābhisamudyatā ।। hitvāvidyāgaṇaṃ prāptavidyābhijñāviśāradā । pratisaṃvidguṇādyāgu pariśuddhākṛtir vabhau ।। atha sā parivijñāya bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ ।
viditvā saṃskāragatīś cābhivighātinīs tataḥ ।। sarvakleśagaṇāṃ jitvā pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalā । sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya vabhūva brahmacāriṇī ।। tadā sā nirjitakleśā nirvikalpā niraṃjanā ।
caṃdanakalpasaurabhyā samaloṣṭhasuvarṇikā ।। saṃsārabhogasatkāraniṣpṛhākāśasannibhā । sarvasatvahitādhānā sarvasūtrāṃtapāragā ।। sadevāsuralokānāṃ tridhātukanivāsināṃ ।
vaṃdyā pūjyābhimānyā ca vabhūva sā subhāṣiṇī ।। yadā sa bhagavañ chāstā bhikṣuṇīnāṃ subhāṣitaṃ । saṃkṣepeṇa samuddiśya dhyānāgāre samāśrayat ।। tadā sā bhikṣuṇī tatra kacaṃgalā subhāṣiṇī ।
bhikṣuṇīnāṃ sabhāmadhye sutrāntaṃ samupādiśat ।। tac chrutvā bhagavāṃs tatra tayā sūtrāṃtadeśite । sarvāns tān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। eṣo agrā bhikṣavo mātā bhikṣuṇīnāṃ mamāśrame ।
sūtrāntabhāgakartṝṇāṃ yad uteyaṃ kacaṃgalā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve api sāṃghikāḥ । savismayā munīndraṃ taṃ paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavann anayā karmaṃ kiṃ prakṛtaṃ purākṛtaṃ ।
imān sarvān sabhāsīnān prabodhayitum arhati ।। yeneyam śāsane bauddhe vṛddhā pravrajitādhunā । sākṣād arhatvam āsādya bhavati brahmacāriṇī ।। kiṃ vānayā purākarma kṛtaṃ kutra kadā kathaṃ ।
sūtrāntabhāgakartṝṇāṃ yenāgreyaṃ bhavaty api ।। kiṃcāpi prakṛtaṃ karmaṃ purānayā kadā kathaṃ । yenātra paścime garbhāvāse na dhārito bhavān ।। etat sarvaiḥ parijñāya bhagavānn asyāḥ purākṛtaṃ ।
imān sarvān sabhāsīnān prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvāṃs tān sāṃghikān dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad yat kṛtaṃ purānayā ।
tat tat sarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ cittabodhane ।। purā me bodhisatvasya bodhicaryānucāriṇaḥ । paṃcajanmaśatāny eṣā janany āsīn niraṃtaraṃ ।। tadā me dadato dānam antarāyaḥ kṛto anayā ।
tenādyāpi daridreyaṃ durbhagā ca bhavaty api ।। pravrajyāyai tadai caiṣā vahudhā prārthitā mayā । naivānujñāṃ dadau mahyaṃ vighnam eva vyadhād dhaṭhāt ।। etatkarmavipākena vṛddhaiṣā duḥkhinī satī ।
pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ prāptā carati mama śāsane ।। yadi naiṣā tadā dānaṃ vighnā mamākariṣyati । naiṣādhunā daridrātra bhavati hi kadā cana ।। pravrajyāyāṃ ca me vighnaṃ yadi naiṣākariṣyata ।
acariṣyad vrataṃ vālye na tu vṛddhātra sāṃprataṃ ।। yan mamaivaṃ kṛtaṃ vighnaṃ dāne vrate tadānayā । tenādhunā daridraiṣā vṛddhā vrataṃ caraty api ।। yat tadā sukṛtaṃ kiṃ cit prakṛtaṃ nānayā purā ।
tenāhaṃ paścime garbhāvāse adhunā na dhāritaḥ ।। yat sā māyā mahādevī mahāpuṇyārthasādhinī । tenāhaṃ paścime garbhāvāse tayātra dhāritaḥ ।। bhūyo apy eṣā purā tatra vāraṇasyāṃ dvijātmajāḥ ।
kleśāgniparidagdhāṃgā daridrā kṛpaṇābhavat ।। tadā tatra munīndrasya kāśyapasya jagadguroḥ । śāsane śaraṇaṃ gatvā pravrajitācarad vrataṃ ।। tatra sa sarvaśāstrārthakovidātivicakṣaṇā ।
sarvasūtrāntasaddharmaṃ bhikṣuṇīnām upādiśat ।। tadā sā bhikṣuṇī tatra kiñcit kāryārtharoṣitāḥ । sarvās tā bhikṣuṇīr dāsīvādena paryabhāṣata ।। etatkarmavipākena saiṣādhunātiduḥkhitā ।
parasevākarā dāsī bhavati durbhagākṛtiḥ ।। yac cānayā tadā tatra vidyābhyāsīkṛtaṃ mudā । tenaiṣā sahasārhantī bhavati brahmacāriṇī ।। yac cāpy esā tadā tatra sūtrāntaṃ samupādiśat ।
tena sūtrāntavaktānām agrā bhavati sāṃprataṃ ।। evaṃ hi bhikṣavaḥ sarve manyadhvaṃ karmasaṃbhavaṃ । sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca saṃsāre bhramatāṃ sarvadehināṃ ।। yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaivaṃ bhujyate phalaṃ ।
abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karmaṃ kvāpi kadā cana ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ klidyate nodakair api । vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate naiva kṣīyate na ca bhūmiṣu ।। ahyathāpi bhaven naiva vipāke karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ ।
yad uptaṃ bhūtale bījaṃ tad eva sūyate phalaṃ ।। anyathā na bhavet kvāpi kṛtaṃ karmaṃ phalaṃ bhave । śubhasya karmaṇaḥ pāke śubhataiva sadā bhave ।। kṛṣṇasya kṛṣṇataiva syā miśritasyāpi miśritaṃ ।
evaṃ vijñāya kṛṣṇāni vihāya miśritāni ca ।। śubha eva sadāpy atra caritavyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ । śubhena sadgatiṃ yāyāt kṛṣṇena durgatiṃ sadā ।। miśritena tathohe ca gatīr yāyād bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
iti matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāñchibhiḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। ye bhajanti sadā buddhaṃ na te gacchanti durgatiṃ । sarvadā sadgatau bhadraṃ kṛtvā yānti jinālayaṃ ।।
ye śṛṇvanti sadā dharmmaṃ na yānti te api durgatiṃ । sarvadā bhadrasaukhyāni bhuktvā yānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। dānaṃ dadanti ye saṃghe te api na yānti durgatiṃ । sarvadā śubhasaukhyāni bhuktvā yānti jināśrayaṃ ।।
evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajadhvaṃ samupāsthitāḥ ।। triratneṣu kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tadvipāke mahatphalaṃ । aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhipadasādhanaṃ ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhisatvāḥ sadā bhave । sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā pracaranti yathechayā ।। nānārūpadharāḥ sarve satvārthasādhanodyatāḥ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya pālayanti jagattrayaṃ ।।
kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya śubhānvitāḥ । sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ ।। jitvā māragaṇāñ cāpi prāpya saṃbodhim uttamāṃ । sarvatra dharmasotkṛtvā tato nirvṛtim āyayuḥ ।।
ye atītā jinās te api triratnabhajanodyamāt । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtipadam āgatāḥ ।। varttamānā jinās te api triratnabhajanodbhavaiḥ । puṇyair bodhiṃ samāsādya gacheyur nirvṛtiṃ tathā ।।
anāgatā jinās te api triratnabhajanodbhavaiḥ । puṇyair evaṃ kramād bodhiṃ prāpya yāsyanti nirvṛtiṃ ।। ahaṃ cāpi tathā nūnaṃ triratnabhajanodyamī । etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhiṃ prāpnomi sāṃprataṃ ।।
tathāham api sarvatra kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat । sarvān bodhau niyojyaivaṃ yāsyāmi nirvṛtiṃ dhruvaṃ ।। evaṃ ye ye bhajanty atra triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । te te sarve api saṃbodhiṃ prāpya nirvṛtim āyayuḥ ।।
iti matvātra saṃsāre nirvṛtipadavāṃchinaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracaradhvaṃ śubhe sadā ।। tathā kṛtvātra saddharmaṃbhuktvaiva satsukhāny api । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpsyatha ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve api te janāḥ । sāṃghikāś ca tathety uktvā prābhyanaṃdat prabodhitāḥ ।। tadā tatra janāḥ sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhejire anumoditāḥ ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvais tu tadā samaṃtataḥ । sarvadā maṃgalotsāhaṃ babhuva nirupadravaṃ ।। iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । śrutvā rājans tvam apy evaṃ triratnaṃ bhaja sarvadā ।।
prajāś cāpi tathā dharmaṃ śrāvayitvā prabodhayan । triratnabhajanaṃ nityaṃ kārayituṃ sadārhasi ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramāt pāramitā pūrya bodhiṃ cāpi samāpsyasi ।।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandan sapārṣadaḥ ।। kacaṃgalāyā avadānam etac chṛṇvanti ye śrāvayatīha yaś ca । vihāya pāpaṃ khalu te api sarve bhuktvā sukhāny eva sugatiṃ vrajanti ।।
athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evaṃ samabravīt ।। bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan sudhīr yatiḥ । upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu rājan samādhāya yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tava puṇyapravṛddhaye ।।
puraikasamaye sa śrīśākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhiś ca cailakaiḥ । upāsakai mahāśrāddhair upāsikāgaṇair api ।।
bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi mahāsatvaiḥ śubhārthibhiḥ । sarvasatvahitārthāya bodhicaryāṃ prakāśibhiḥ ।। vṛjiṣu puri vaiśālyāṃ markaṭākhyahradāntike । kūṭāgāraguhāvāse vijahāra prabhāsayan ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatra sarve samāgatāḥ । brahmaśakrādidevendrā lokapālā digāsthitāḥ ।। grahāḥ siddhagaṇāḥ sādhyā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । garuḍā nāgarājāś ca vidyādharāś ca dānavāḥ ।।
rākṣasāḥ sagaṇāś caiva ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇaḥ । brahmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā bhūpā rājāno api narādhipāḥ ।। tathā rājakumārāś ca vaiśyā maṃtrijanā api । gṛhasthāḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ paurāḥ sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ ।।
vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi tathānye api śubhārthinaḥ । grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathā kārpaṭikā api ।। evam anye api lokāś ca saddharmāmṛtavāṃchinaḥ । sarve te samupāyātās tatrādrākṣus tam īśvaraṃ ।।
sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ sarvasaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ । śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya sarve te samupāśritāḥ ।। natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ । punaḥ sāñjalayo natvā parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇīṃ bodhicaryāṃ samādiśat ।। tadāryadharmam ākarṇya sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ ।
tadā te dharmavaiśeṣyaṃ matvā pratinanaṃdire ।। tadā tatra mahāpūryyāṃ vaiśālyāṃ pauriko mahān । gṛhastho dhaniko nāma śrīmān sarvaguṇī sudhīḥ ।। śrāddho bhadrāśayo dātā śuddhaśīlo vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
sarvasatvahitādhānād āsīt satpuruṣottamaḥ ।। patnī dharmasakhī tasya śīlavatyabhidhābhavat । tanayaś ca vaṃdānyākhyaḥ satyavatyabhidhā snuṣā ।। tadā tatra dvijā sarve bhaktimanto jagadguroḥ ।
pūjānimaṃtraṇe cakruḥ samayaṃ saṃmatās tathā ।। bhavanto yan munīndro ayam atrāsmākaṃ hitechayā । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sasaṃghaḥ samupāgataḥ ।। tad asmābhir munīndro ayaṃ pūjanīyaṃ samādarāt ।
ato nimaṃtraṇīyo atra sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya nānyathā ।। ekaś cet kurute dravyamadād asya nimaṃtraṇaṃ । sarvair nirvāsanīyo asau yato anyadharmavighnakṛt ।। tadā sa dhaniko ajñātvā samayaṃ tais tathā kṛtaṃ ।
svayam eva munīndraṃ taṃ pūjayituṃ samichata ।। tataḥ sa dhanikaḥ śrīmān divyasaṃpatsamṛddhimān । svayaṃ nimaṃtraṇaṃ karttuṃ sasaṃghasya muner yayau ।। tatra sa samupāsṛtya natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā ।
sasaṃghaṃ tat puraḥ sthitvā prārthayad eva sāṃjaliḥ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । pūjayituṃ samichāmi paśyan me anugrahaṃ kuru ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tathā hīti pratiśrutvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tadā te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve saṃbhūya samupāgatāḥ । bhagavataś caraṇau natvā cakrur bhojyanimaṃtraṇaṃ ।। tac chrutvā bhagavān prāha tān dṛṣṭvā bhaktimānasān ।
pūrvam eva sasaṃghāham anenodya nimaṃtritaḥ ।। etad ākarṇya sarve te brāhmaṇā bheditāśayāḥ । paraṃ pratīkṣyamānāś ca śanaiḥ svasvagṛhaṃ yayuḥ ।। tataḥ sa dhaniko matvā munīndreṇādhyuvāsitaṃ ।
muditas taṃ muniṃ natvā sahasā svagṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa svagṛhe gatvā vāṃdhaveṣṭajanais saha । tadarhabhojyasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhyayat ।। tato bhojyasthalaṃ tatra śodhayitvā samantataḥ ।
ratnadhvajair vitānaiś ca sa patākair amaṇḍayat ।। tato yathākramaṃ tatra divyaratnamayāni ca । svāsanāni samāstīryya sugaṃdhīḥ samadhūpayat ।। tataḥ sa prātar utthāya snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ ।
pūjāpādyārghasāmagrīṃ pratiṣṭhāpya pramoditaḥ ।। savāṃdhaveṣṭajanas tatra kūṭāgāre samācarat । sāñjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate adhunā ।
tat sasaṃgho mamāvāse vijayituṃ samarhasi ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ । khikkhirīpātram ādāya pratasthe cīvarāvṛtaḥ ।। tatra sa bhagavān mārge kṛtvā bhadraṃ samantataḥ ।
prabhāsayan krameṇaivaṃ vaiśālyāṃ samupaviśat ।। tathāyātaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ śrīghanaṃ sāṃghikānvitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā vaiśālikāḥ lokāḥ sarve api samapūjayan ।। evam abhyarcyamāno abhivaṃdyamāno abhinaṃditaḥ ।
bhāsayan bhadratāṃ kṛtvā saṃghaiḥ saha samācarat ।। tatra tasya gṛhe gatvā sasaṃghaḥ sa munīśvaraḥ । tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svāsane samupāśrayat ।। tatas te sāṃghikāś cāpi sarve tatra yathākramaṃ ।
tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svasvāsane samāśrayan ।। tataḥ sa dhaniko dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । svasvāsane samāsīnaṃ pūjāṅgaiḥ samapūjayat ।। tato divyopacārais taṃ bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।
supraṇītai rasopetair bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। tadbhojyaṃ surasaṃ bhuktvā bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ । amṛtair iva saṃtuṣṭas tṛptiṃ yayau pramoditaḥ ।। asaṃghaiḥ taṃ muniṃ tṛptaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dhaniko mudā ।
tato apanīya pātrāṇi taddhastādīny aśodhayat ।। tataḥ śuddhauṣadhīpūgatāmvūlādi rasāyanaṃ । buddhapramukhasaṃghebhyo muditaḥ sa svayaṃ dadau ।। tataḥ sa harṣito natvā taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।
purataḥ sāñjaliḥ sthitvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । bhaktyaiva bhajanaṃ kurve tat kṣamasvāparādhatāṃ ।। sadaivaṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭya paśyan bhavān sasāṃghikaḥ ।
mamānugraham ādhāya trātum arhati sarvathā ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā sasāṃghiko anumoditaḥ । dhanikaṃ taṃ samālokya naṃdayann evam ādiśat ।। gṛhapate sadā nityam ārogyam astu vo dhruvaṃ ।
bodhipraṇidhisiddhiś ca bhūyād bhadraṃ ca sarvadā ।। tatas tasya priyā bhāryā śīlavaty anumoditā । sāñjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā prārthayat taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña śvaś cātra bhavatām ahaṃ । pūjāṃ kartuṃ samicche tad anugrahītum arhati ।।
tayeti prārthite dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa tad āśayaṃ । śraddhānvitaṃ pratijñāya tuṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā samutthāya sasāṃghikaḥ । bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kṛtvā svāśrame ca samāśrayat ।।
tataḥ paradine prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāṃvarāvṛtā । sādhitvā sarvasāmagrīṃ sā dūtaṃ preṣayan munau ।। sa dūtaḥ sahasā gatvā vihare taṃ munīśvaraṃ । sasaṃghaṃ sāṃjalir natvā punar evaṃ nyavedayat ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate adhunā । tat sasaṃgho bhavāṃs tatra sahasāgantum arhati ।। tataḥ sa bhagavānn evaṃ bhadraṃ kṛtvā sasāṃghikaḥ । dhanikasya gṛhe gatvā pādyaṃ gṛhyāsane aviśat ।।
tatrāsane samāsīnaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । dṛṣṭvā śīlavatī sātha yathāvidhi samarcayat ।। tataś ca sā muditā sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ buddhādikaṃ tathā । divyopacārasaṃyuktair bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।।
tataḥ saṃtarppitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śodhayitvā karādikaṃ । datvā tāmvurapūgādiṃ natvā sā samupāśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān tasmai datvāśiṣaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ । samutthāya tataś caivaṃ svavihāre samāśrayat ।।
tathā sarve tadānyo api dhanikasyātmajaḥ sudhīḥ । tat paredyu vihāraṃ taṃ gatvā natvā nyamaṃtrayat ।। bhagavānn api tasyaivaṃ dṛṣṭvā śraddhānvitaṃ manaḥ । tatheti pratimoditvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa ca ।।
tataḥ sas taṃ muniṃ natvā svagṛhaṃ sahasāgataḥ । bāṃdhavaiḥ sarvasāmagrīṃ muditaḥ samasādhayat ।। tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya snātvā śuddhāmvārāvṛtaḥ । vihāre samupāsṛtya natvaivaṃ munim abravīt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate adhunā । tat saṃgho bhavān gehe mamāgantuṃ samarhati ।। tataḥ sasaṃgha utthāya bhagavān sa tathācarat । tadgṛhe pādyam ādāya tatrāsane samāśrayat ।।
tataḥ sa mudito buddhapramukbaṃ sarvasāṃghikaṃ । samabhyarcya tathā divyabhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। tato apanīya pātrāṇi śodhayitvā karādikaṃ । datvā pūgādikaṃ natvā purataḥ samupāśrayat ।।
punaḥ sa sāṃjalir natvā prakṛtvā ca kṣamārthanāṃ । sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ tam saṃdṛṣṭvaivaṃ samupāśrayat ।। tadā tasya snuṣā cāpi satyavatī pramoditā । bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyamaṃtrayat ।।
bhagavānn api tasyāś ca dṛṣṭva śraddhānvitaṃ manaḥ । tatheti pratimoditvā tuṣṇībhūtvā radhāṃ vyadhāt ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasmai datvāśiṣaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ । tathā kṛtvā śubhaṃ loke gatvāśrame samāśrayat ।।
tataḥ sāpi tathā prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtā । dūtenāpi munīndraṃ taṃ sasaṃghaṃ samacodayat ।। tathā sa bhagavāṃś cāpi sasāṃghikaḥ samutthitaḥ । pracaran bhadratāṃ kṛtvā tasyā gehe samāviśat ।।
tatra pādyārgham ādāya bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ । śubhāsane samāsīnas tasthau tatra prabhāsayan ।। tathāsthitaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃpramoditā । yathāvidhi samabhyarcya tathā bhojyair atoṣayat ।।
tātas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ samīkṣya sā । tatrāpanīya pātrāṇi hastādīṃ paryaśodhayat ।। tataḥ pūgādikaṃ datvā prārthayitvā kṣamāṃ tathā । sasaṃghaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā sā sāñjalir upāśrayat ।।
tathā sa bhagavāṃs tasyai datvāśīṣaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ । tato vihāyasā gatvā svāśrame ca samāśrayat ।। tathā sa dhaniko bhaktyā bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । divyādbhutarddhisaṃbhāraiḥ punar evaṃ nyamaṃtrayat ।।
tatputreṇa tṛtīye ahni caturthe snuṣayā tathā । sasaṃgho bhagavānn evaṃ divyabhogair nimaṃtritaḥ ।। tac chrutvā tad dvijāḥ sarve vaiśālikāḥ prajā api । alabdhāvasarāḥ śāstuḥ pūjāyāṃ praticukruśuḥ ।।
tatas te saṃmataṃ kṛtvā sarve viprāḥ sapaurikāḥ । dhanikāya puraṃ kruddhāś cakrur nikāsanodyamaṃ ।। evaṃ tat samataṃ jñātvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । dhanikaṃ taṃ samāhūya pura evam upādiśat ।।
sādho gṛhapate sarve ime vaiśālikā dvijāḥ । kruddhās te saṃghabhojye atra hy alabdhāvasarā mama ।। tad atra tvaṃ kṣamāṃ kṛtvā dvijān sarvān prabodhaya । kṛtvātra vinayaṃ dharme prasādayitum arhasi ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa dhanikas tathā । ity āśrutya dvijān sarvān samupetyaivam abravīt ।। bhavanto na mayā jñātaṃ bhavatāṃ kopakāraṇaṃ । tad atra me samākhyāta yad arthe kupyate adhunā ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te brāhmaṇā । kopāgniparidagdhāsyā dhanikaṃ taṃ ninindire ।। tatraiko brāhmaṇaḥ sādhur dayāluḥ sukṛtārthavit । dhanikaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya bodhayituṃ samabravīt ।।
sādho gṛhapate asmābhir yathātra samataṃ kṛtaṃ । tathā tat te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā tat pratibudhyatāṃ ।। bhavanto yan munīndro ayam atrāsmākaṃ hitechayā । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sasāṃghikaḥ samāgataḥ ।। tad asmābhir munīndro ayaṃ pūjanīyaḥ samādaraiḥ ।
ato nimaṃtraṇīyo atra sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya nānyathā ।। ekaś cet kurute vittamadād asya nimaṃtraṇaṃ । sarvair nirvāsanīyo asau yato anyadharmavighnakṛt ।। ity asmābhiḥ kṛtaṃ sādho samayaṃ sarvasaṃmataṃ ।
tad vilaṃghya tvayaikena śāstuḥ pūjā kṛtā sadā ।। etad dheto ime sārve brāhmaṇā ruṣitās tathā । niṣkāsayitum ichanti tvām anyadharmavādhakaṃ ।। kiṃ cāpi bhagavān atra sarvadā sthāsyate na hi ।
tat sarve bhagavatpūjāṃ kartuṃ vāṃchanti sāṃprataṃ ।। yac cāyaṃ bhagavāñ chāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ । sarvasatvahitārthāya samutpanna ihā adhunā ।। tathātra sarvasatvānaṃ hitaṃ kartum upācaran ।
saddharmaṃ samupādiśya caraty ayaṃ samaṃtataḥ ।। tathātrāpi hitaṃ kartum asmākaṃ samupāgataḥ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijayate sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tad atra sarvalokānāṃ triratnabhajanotsavaṃ ।
dātum arhasi sarveṣām api puṇyapravṛddhaye ।। eka eva tvaṃ evaṃ tu mā kṛthā bhajanaṃ sadā । sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya te sāstuḥ karttavyaṃ bhajanaṃ sadā ।। iti tenoditam śrutvā dhanikaḥ sa vivodhitaḥ ।
brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।। mayā na jñāyate hy evaṃ bhavadbhiḥ samayaṃ kṛtaṃ । tad atra me aparādhatvaṃ kṣantum arhanti sarvathā ।। yadi vo vidyate śraddhā triratnabhajane sadā ।
kurudhvaṃ sarvadāpy atra saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ khalu ।। yadā na vidyate pūjā saṃbuddhe asmin sasāṃghike । tadaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmi saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ khalu ।। iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sarve api te dvijāḥ ।
satyam iti parijñāya vabhūvus tat prasāditāḥ ।। tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve saṃbhūya saha paurikaiḥ । bhagavataḥ sasaṃghasya nimaṃtritum upāsaran ।। tatra te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve sametya saha paurikaiḥ ।
sāñjalayo munīndraṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña trimāsyaṃ bhavatāṃ sadā । satkāraṃ kartum ichāma tvadanujñāṃ dadātu naḥ ।। iti taiḥ prārthite sarvair dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān muniḥ ।
teṣām āśayaśuddhatvaṃ tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ । matvā sapaurikā natvā taṃ muṇiṃ svapure acaran ।। tatra te paurikā viprāḥ śodhayitvā samamṭataḥ ।
bhojyakṣatre dhvajair uccair vitānaiḥ paryaśobhayan ।। tatrāsanāni prajñapya sarvasāmagrasādhanaṃ । kṛtvā sarve api te lokā mahotsāhaṃ pracakrire ।। tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtāḥ ।
tatrāśrame sametyaivaṃ natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate adhunā । tat sasaṃgho bhavāṃs tatra pure āgantum arhati ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān buddhaḥ sasaṃghaś cīvarāvṛtaḥ ।
khikkhiripātram ādāya saṃpratasthe prabhāsayan ।। tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ । bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kṛtvā pracaraṃs tatpure aviśat ।। tatra sa bhagavān kṣetre suśodhite sasāṃghikaḥ ।
tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svāsane samupāśrayat ।। saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ te samatoṣayat । tatas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ saṃghaṃ cāpi vilokyate ।। tat pātrāṇy upanītvā tad dhastādīkaṃ vyaśodhayat ।
tataḥ sa pūgatāmbūramahauṣadhyarasāya naṃ ।। datvā kṣamārthanaṃ kṛtvā taṃ sasaṃghaṃ praṇemire । tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve paurāś cāpi pramoditāḥ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātim upātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।।
tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān samupasthitān । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tato bhadrāśiṣaṃ datvā bhagavān saha saṃghikaiḥ । bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kurvan gatvā svāśramam āśrayat ।।
evaṃ vaiśālikā lokās te traimāsyaṃ niraṃtaraṃ । yathārhabhojanaiḥ śāstuḥ sasaṃghasya prabhejire ।। tato ante dhanikaś cāpi patnī putraḥ snuṣāpi ca । saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ divyabhogyaiḥ samārcayat ।।
bhagavānn api tathā tebhyo datvā śubhāśiṣaṃ tataḥ । samutthāya sasaṃghaś ca gatvāśrame samāśrayat ।। tataḥ sa dhanikaḥ patnīputrasnuṣāsamanvitaḥ । dṛṣṭasatyaḥ sadā ratnatrayasevārato abhavat ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvena bhūyo atiśrīsamṛddhimān । sarvalokahitaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śubhe sadā ।। tad dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve bhikṣavaḥ samupāśritāḥ । bhagavantaṃ praṇatvaivaṃ paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।।
bhagavan kiṃ purānena dhanikena vṛṣaṃ kṛtaṃ । kutra kathaṃ kadaitan naḥ sarvam ākhyātum arhati ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvāns tāṃ saṃghikān dṛṣṭvā tadaivaṃ samupādiśat ।।
śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anena vṛṣaṃ kṛtaṃ । tat patnyā ca putreṇa snuṣayā ca tad ucyate ।। varāṇasyām abhūt pūrvaṃ mālikaḥ kamalābhidhaḥ । durbhikṣakṣapite kāle parāṃ durgatim āgataḥ ।।
patnī patnavikā nāma putraḥ kuvaliyābhidhaḥ । pāṭalokhyā snuṣā ceti vabhūvus tasya saṃmatāḥ ।। tadaikasmin dine tasya gṛhāntike prapuṣpite । udyāne sāyam āgatya pratyekabuddha āśrayet ।।
te sarve ekavastrā hi paryyāyena nṛpālaye । datvā puṣpāṇi prāyātāḥ svabhavane niṣīdire ।। tadā sa ca gṛhasthās te tatrodāne jvalat prabhāṃ । dṛṣṭvā kiṃ mahojvālam udyāne iti vismitāḥ ।।
sahasā te samutthāya tatrodyāne nirīkṣituṃ । sarvagatāḥ samīkṣantaḥ dadṛśus taṃ prabhāsayaṃ ।। tatra te samupāśritya dṛṣṭvā taṃ dhyānasaṃsthitaṃ । sāñjalayaḥ praṇatvaiva muditā svagṛhaṃ yayuḥ ।।
tatra te svagṛhāsīnāḥ prātas tatpūjanotsukāḥ । nirddhanās tad vyathāṃ prāpu lūnapakṣāḥ khagā iva ।। tadā sa mālikas tasmai pūjāṃ kartuṃ samutsukaḥ । tad dravyaṃ svagṛhe samyag anviṣya samalokayat ।।
tatra gṛhe sa sarvatra samanviṣya samaṃtataḥ । kañci mātram api dravyam alabdhaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। aho mayā purā pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ kiṃ yato adhunā । akiṃcanyo daridro asmi kim atra jīvitena me ।।
yato na vidyate dravyaṃ kiṃ cid api gṛhe mama । tat kena kariṣyāmi pūjām asya mahātmanaḥ ।। atrāyaṃ svayam āgatya mamodyāne samāśritaḥ । pratyekabuddha ātmajo dhyātvā tiṣṭhati bhāsayan ।।
tad asya sugatasyātra karttavyā satkṛtir mayā । kadāyaṃ puri ramyatra samāgachet svayaṃ punaḥ ।। tat prātaḥ śūnyapātreṇa gached ito mamātmavit । tan mamātra bhave śūnyam iva janmāpi nisphalaṃ ।।
yato mānyo abhipūjyo yaṃ pūjyate na kathaṃ cana । tatra kiṃ jāyate bhadraṃ puṇyaṃ vāsya kathaṃ kutaḥ ।। puṇyaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ sāraṃ janma nisphalaṃ । bhuktvāpi kiṃ sukhāny atra suciraṃ jīvite nanu ।।
puṇyārthe jīvitaṃ janma tad atra yadi naśyati । kim eva jīvitenāpi janmanā pāpasādhinā ।। tan mṛtyur me varaṃ hy atra na mithyācirajīvitaṃ । avaśyam eva saṃsāre sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
kim evaṃ dehapuṣṭena bhuktvā duḥkhāṃ sarvadā । tat kenāpi pradānena pūjayeyam imaṃ jinaṃ ।। puṇyena sadgatiṃ yāyāṃ pāpena durgatiṃ sadā । tat pāpaṃ parityaktuṃ puṇyaṃ prāptu yateya hi ।।
yady atra pūjyate nāyaṃ drakṣyate ca kadā kuha । buddhapūjāṃ vinā bhadre puṇyaṃ ca lapsyate kutaḥ ।। yāvan na prāpyate puṇyaṃ tāvad durgaticāraṇaṃ । tasmāt puṇyaṃ prayatnena karttavyaṃ sukhatāptaye ।।
tad atra śraddhayā kiṃcin mātreṇāpi svavastunā । satkṛtyainaṃ mahābhijñaṃ bhajeyaṃ samupasthitaḥ ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya mālikaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । bhāryāṃ putraṃ snuṣāṃ cāpi samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।।
aye priye snuṣe putra yūyaṃ śṛṇuta madvacaḥ । yad atra kartum ichāmi tatra yūyaṃ prasādataḥ ।। yad atrāyaṃ mahābhijñaḥ svayam eva samāgataḥ । asmākaṃ gṛhe dravyaṃ kiñcit mātraṃ na vidyate ।।
tat kenātra kariṣyāmaḥ pūjām asya mahātmanaḥ ।। yadi na pūjyate asmābhiḥ sugato ayaṃ munir yatiḥ । tadā puṇyaṃ vayaṃ kutra lapsyāmahe kadā kathaṃ ।। puṇyaṃ vinātra saṃsāre nisphalaṃ janma jīvitaṃ ।
tad vayaṃ puṇyato prāptuṃ yatema sarvathā vayaṃ ।। puṇyena sadgatiṃ prāpya pāpena durgatiṃ sadā । tat sadgatisukhaprāptyai puṇyaṃ kurvīmahi dhruvaṃ ।। caturṇāṃ vidyate asmākam ekaṃ sarvasvam amvaraṃ ।
anenāpy enam āchādya prabhajamahi sāṃprataṃ ।। nādyarājakule nagnā gachāmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati । etat me vacanaṃ śrutvābhyanumoditum arhatha ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā patnī putraḥ snuṣāpi te ।
sarve apy abhyanumoditvā tathā kurv iti procire ।। ity etat samayaṃ kṛtvā sarve te śraddhayānvitāḥ । gatvā tenaikavastreṇa taṃ prāchādya samārcayan ।। tatas te muditāḥ sarve kṛtāñjalipuṭā muneḥ ।
tasya pādau praṇatvaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ pracakrire ।। anena vastradānena vayaṃ sarve śubhāśayāḥ । bhaveyaṃ sadgatiṃ yātā divyasaṃpattihāninaḥ ।। śāstāraṃ sugataṃ buddhaṃ samārādhya sadā bhave ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā bhavema bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। iti tair muditaiḥ sarvaiḥ praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tathā । viditvā sa mahāvijñas tathāstv iti samādiśat ।। tatas tesāṃ manoharṣaṃ kṛtvā sa sugato muniḥ ।
tata uḍḍīya pakṣīva bhāsayan svāśrame yayau ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te nanditāḥ sarve buddhadharmānuśaṃsinaḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracerire sukhaṃ sadā ।। tatpuṇyapraṇidhānena dhaniko ayaṃ sa mālikaḥ । jāto divyaprabhāvarddhiḥ patnīputrasnuṣānvitaḥ ।।
manaḥśuddhividhānena dānenātiglaghīyasā । bhavanty alaghvyāḥ saṃkalpaiḥ saṃpadaḥ satvaśālināṃ ।। buddhakṣetreṣu yat karma sukṛtaṃ duḥkṛtaṃ tathā । mahattaratvam āsādya phalaty eva sadā bhave ।।
iti matvātra saṃsāre karttavyaṃ sukṛtaṃ sadā । bauddhe satkṛtapuṇyena labhanti bodhisaṃpadaḥ ।। iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve api sāṃghikāḥ । menire cittavaimalyamūlaṃ dānaphalaśriyaṃ ।।
tac chrutvā brāhmaṇās te api tatpuṇyavismitā mudā । bhagavaṃtaṃ sadā smṛtvā prabhejire anumoditāḥ ।। tathā te brāhmaṇāś cāpi sarve api paurikās tathā । tatpuṇyapariśuddhāṃśā vabhuvuḥ kuśalodyatāḥ ।।
helārpitaṃ ratnadhanaṃ tṛṇāgraṃ śraddhāvatīrṇaṃ tṛṇam apy anarghaṃ । anekaśobhānubhavaṃ hi cittaṃ cittaṃ nimittaṃ śubhasaṃbhavānāṃ ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । śrutvāpy evaṃ mahārāja karttavyaṃ sukṛtaṃ sadā ।।
prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
idaṃ narā ye dhanikāvadānaṃ śṛṇvanti ye cāpi niśāmayanti । sukhāni bhuktvā sa śubhe sadā te sarve api śamyānti jinālayan te । athāśoko narendraḥ sa kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭum ca me arhati ।। iti sāṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhaṃ mahāmatiḥ । upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvaivaṃ paribudhyatāṃ ।। krauryeṇa dvirasanāḥ śuciveṣṭitānāṃ mithyāpavādaviṣamaṃ viṣam utsṛjanti । te pāpaśāpaparitāpaparaṃparārttās tīvravyalīkatimiravivaraṃ viśanti ।। tadyathābhūt purā bhikṣuḥ kāsmīre patitāśrame ।
raivatakābhidho bauddhaḥ sarvabhūtadayāśrayaḥ ।। sa kadācid dhanoddeśe vivikte sughaṭāntare । tarutvacaḥ kaṣāyena cakre cīvararaṃjanaṃ ।। tasminn avasare tatra piśunākhyadvijanmanaḥ ।
dhenuvatsā vane naṣṭā vabhūvur yūthanirgatāḥ ।। tadā sa brāhmaṇo dṛṣṭvā taṃ duṣṭāśitaśaṃkitaḥ । sarvatrāpi samanviṣṭā tatrāpy anveṣituṃ yayau ।। tatra taccīvarakvāthavāke vahnisamudgataṃ ।
dhūmaṃ sa dvija ālokya vatsapākam amanyata ।। tataḥ sa brāhmaṇaḥ sārddhaṃ svajanaiḥ śastrapāṇibhiḥ । tad draṣṭuṃ śailam āruhya sahasāgāt tadantike ।। tatra taṃ raivataṃ bhikṣuṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dvija ādarāt ।
upetya cūḍika-iḍyāhataṃ kumbham apaśyat ।। tad dṛṣṭvā śaṃkitaś cāsau vinayān samupāsaran । kim etat kriyate bhikṣor iti taṃ paryapṛchata ।। iti pṛṣṭe dvijenāsau raivato bhikṣur ādarāt ।
tatra cīvararāgo ayam iti taṃ dvijam abravīt ।। asminn avasare tasyā pūrvakarmavipākataḥ । gomāṃsaraktapāṇīyaḥ sapākaḥ samapadyata ।। sukhaṃ duḥkhatvam ānāti śuklam apy eti kālatāṃ ।
vidhau vidhuratāṃ yāte dharmo apy āyāty adharmatāṃ ।। mithyāpāpaprakaṭatā janakopaḥ padacyutiḥ । apuṇyaparipākānām etat pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ ।। doṣaḥ samunmiṣati yāty aguṇaḥ prakāśaṃ kāryaṃ viparyayam upeti viśīryate dhīḥ ।।puṃsāṃ purāvihitaḥ duḥkṛtapākakāle ke ke na nāma nipatanti mahābhighātāḥ ।। tataḥ sa brāhmaṇo apy atra kumbhe kim iti śaṃkitaḥ ।
paśyāmīti viniścitya nirīkṣitum upācarat ।। viruddhāmiṣagaṃdhena rudhireṇa ca śaṃkitaḥ । apaśyan sa dvijaḥ kumbhe māṃsapiṇḍaṃ supakvitaiḥ ।। pratyakṣadoṣam ālokya dvijaḥ krodhito ruṣā ।
tam abhāṣata nirbhatsya tīvravaiśaśakaṃpitaḥ ।। aho vata sadācāraḥ sthito ayaṃ vijane vane । yasyedṛśāni karmāṇi na kasyacid iha paśyati ।। pravrajyāraṃjitaḥ kāyaḥ kriyā mlechajanocitā ।
jānāti channapāpānāṃ kaḥ kūṭavrataśāntitāṃ ।। ity ukte tena sākṣepaṃ sa raivato apy aciṃtayat । doṣe pratyakṣalakṣyasmin kiṃ bravīmi niruttaraḥ ।। mama daivāya ghāto ayam ity ukte ko anumanyate ।
hāsyāyatanatām eti pratyakṣyāpahnavī janaḥ ।। upasthitaṃ sahe sarvaṃ maunam ālambya kevalaṃ । ayaṃ me niḥpratīkāraḥ salilād agnidutthitaḥ ।। doṣe guṇātiśayam āśu guṇe api doṣaṃ paiyūṣadhāmni viṣam apy amṛtaṃ viṣe ca ।।
saṃdarśayaty aniśam adbhutarūpam eva kālendrajālikāvadhūr bhavitavyeyaṃ ।। ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā raivataḥ sa mahāmatiḥ । svadaivasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau yogasamāhitaḥ ।। iti dhyānaṃ samālambya sthitaṃ taṃ raivataṃ muniṃ ।
dṛṣṭvātiruṣitaś cāsau saṃtaryya paryabhāṣata ।। are re durmate bhikṣo kiṃ atra durjane vane । sthitvevaṃ dāruṇaṃ pāpaṃ sādhayitvā niṣīdasi ।। are pāpiṣṭha bhāṣasva yad arthe vālakāṃ vṛṣaṃ ।
hatvātra pacyate māṃsa tvayātmano pareṇa vā ।। pareṇāpi hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tat pāpaiḥ parilipyase । tat tvayā vṛṣabhī hatvā kathaṃ pāpair na dahyase ।। dhig dhik tvām atra rebhikṣo saṃbuddhaśāsane yataḥ ।
pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā nirjane vana āśrayan ।। mahadduḥkarakarmāṇi kṛtvaivaṃ tapase adhunā । are re śrūyate kiṃ na tvayā saṃbuddhabhāṣitaṃ ।। atha śrutvāpi te tatra śraddhā na vidyate khalu ।
kim evaṃ pātakaṃ kṛtvā pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ caran ।। kevalaṃ pāpakāny eva sādhayitvātra tiṣṭhase । pravrajito viraktātmā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ ।। sarvasatvadayādṛṣṭiś caren nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।
adattaṃ kasya cid dravyaṃ gṛhīyān na kathaṃ cana । dayākaruṇyayuktātmā na kuryāt prāṇipīḍinaṃ ।। kāmabhogam adharmeṇa naiva bhuṃjyāt kadā cana । mṛṣāvādaṃ kadāpy atra naiva brūyāt kathaṃ cana ।। pāruṣyavacanaṃ cāpi naiva brūyāt kathaṃ cana ।
paiśunyavacanaṃ vāpi vaden na kasya cit puraḥ ।। saṃbhinnapralāpaṃ ca na pravadet kasya cid api । vyāpādaṃ kasya cic cāpi bhāvayen na kathaṃ cana ।। abhidhyāṃ ca tathā naiva ciṃtayet kasya cid api ।।
mithyādṛṣṭiṃ sadā kvāpi bhāvayen na kadā cana । etāni daśapāpānāṃ mūlāni sarvathā tyajet ।। etāni ye samālabhya pracaranti pramādataḥ । te sarve kleśasaṃtaptā bhramanti duḥkhino bhave ।।
tataḥ kleśāgnisaṃtaptāḥ pāpeṣv eva samāhitāḥ । duḥkhāny eva sadā bhuktvā narakeṣu bhramanti te ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre tyaktvaitāni daśāpi hi । santo nityam śubheṣv eva pracaranti samāhitāḥ ।।
śubhena sadgatiṃ yānti papina durgatiṃ sadā । ity ākhyātaṃ jinaiḥ sarvaiḥ kiṃ naitac chrūyate tvayā ।। katham etad avajñāya pravrajitas tvam ācareḥ । dhik te cittaṃ yad evaṃ me govatsaṃ bhoktum ichati ।।
pravrajito hi śuddhātmā pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalaḥ । sarvasatvadayācittaś caren nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā brahmacaryaṃ samāhitaḥ । bhikṣānnamātrasaṃkṛṣṭaḥ suniḥspṛhaś carec chubhe ।।
samādhinirato yogī dhāraṇīparamārthabhṛt । sarvakleśān vinirjitvā sarvamāragāṇān api ।। sarvān parigrahān tyaktvā nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ । sākṣād arhatvam āsādya brahmacaryaṃ samācaret ।।
evaṃ pravrajito bhikṣuś caran nityaṃ suśīlabhṛt । śivāṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāt ।। tvaṃ tu pravrajito apy evaṃ mahaddāruṇapātakaṃ । kṛtvātra nirjane bhuktvā carase mlechacārikāṃ ।।
hā vatātra vinaṣṭo asi yad etat pātakānvitaḥ । sahasā narake gatvā ciraṃ duḥkhāni bhokṣyasi ।। kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ purā janmāntare kathaṃ । yad atra saugate dharmaṃ prāpto apy evaṃ durāśayaḥ ।।
tac carasva samādhāya prāyaścittavrataṃ punaḥ । etatpāpābhisaṃśuddhyai punar vratasamāptaye ।। tathā te śuddhite kāye maṃgalaṃ ca bhavet kramāt । pariśuddhas trikāyaś ca pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ cara ।।
tadā tvaṃ sarvathā jitvā kleśān māragaṇānn api । sākṣād arhatvam āsādya brahmacārī bhaviṣyati ।। tadā tvaṃ pariśuddhātmā nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ । śivāṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā raivataḥ sa prabodhitaḥ । tathāpi maunam ādhāya tathau daivābhyanusmaran ।। evaṃ sthitaṃ tam ālokya brāhmaṇaḥ sa ruṣānvitaḥ । evaṃ dvidhā tridhāpy enaṃ paribhāṣyābhyanindayat ।।
evaṃ dvidhā tridhāpy ukte brāhmaṇena sa raivataḥ । svadaivam abhyanusmṛtvā maunenaiva nyaṣīdata ।। svadaivacintayas tasya maunāt sa brāhmaṇo ruṣā । raivataṃ tāṃ katākṣeṇa dṛṣṭvainaṃ paryabhāṣata ।।
are re durmate bhikṣo kim evaṃ tiṣṭhase adhunā । uttiṣṭhātra pravaṃdhitva nayāmi tvāṃ nṛpāntike ।। evaṃ tenodite apy eva sthitaḥ sa raivato yatiḥ । kiṃ cin naivāvaden maunam evālambya nyaṣīdata ।।
tataḥ sa brāhmaṇas tasya maunād atiprakopitaḥ । murddhni pāpam iva sthūlaṃ laguḍaṃ marpayātayat ।। tathābhighātyamāno api raivataḥ sa samāhitaḥ । daivam evābhyanusmṛtvā tasthau niḥkaṃpitāśayaḥ ।।
tathāsthitaṃ taṃ munim ātmavidyaṃ daivaṃ smaraṃtaṃ hy akṛtāparādhaṃ । nināya paścātkṛtavāhudaṃḍaṃ sadas tadā naṃdanabhūmibhartuḥ ।। tathāsthitaṃ tam ālokya sa dvijaḥ pratiroṣitaḥ । raktākṣaṃ raivataṃ vaddhvā sahasānayan nṛpāntike ।।
tatra sa brāhmaṇo nītvā taṃ rājñaḥ sthitaḥ । tadvatsapiśitaṃ pakvam upasthāpya abhyadarśayat ।। tataḥ sa brāhmaṇaḥ krūras tasya bhikṣo savistaraṃ । sarvavṛttāṃtam ākhyāya taṃ nṛpaṃ paryakopayat ।।
tad vatsamāṃsam ālokya nṛpatiḥ sa prakopitaḥ । raivataṃ taṃ yatiṃ vaddhvā cakre kārāgṛhātithiṃ ।। nirdoṣaḥ kleśam āśnāti tambhate guptapātakaḥ । jānāti kasya kaḥ śuddhiṃ citrākāreṣv asākṣiṣu ।।
tatra sa vaṃdhanāgāre vaṃdhito api sa sanmatiḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau daivānucintayan ।। tatraivaṃ vaṃdhanāgāre tasmin bhikṣau nivandhite । kāle na visnito rājā tad vicāre api nāsmarat ।।
tadānyasmin dine tatra te vatsāḥ sarva āgatāḥ । mātṛbhiḥ saha saṃsaktās tṛṇaṃ bhuktvā niṣedire ।। tān vatsān mātṛsaṃsaktān sarvān ālokya sa dvijaḥ । vismitaḥ punar ālokya paśyann evaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
aho vatsā ime sarve kutra gatvādhunāgatāḥ । sarvatrānviṣyamānā hi kutrāpi nābhyadṛśyate ।। hā mamātra mahatpāpo jāyate sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ । yan mayā sahasā bhikṣor asamīkṣyāparādhyate ।। yathā bhikṣor ghaṭe mānsaṃ dṛṣṭvaiṣām iti cintayat ।
caurāyam iti taṃ bhikṣuṃ paryabhāṣaṃ ruṣābhṛtaṃ ।। aparādhaṃ vinārhaṃtam api bhikṣuṃ pratāḍayat । vaddhvā taṃ sahasā rājñaḥ puro atra samupānayaṃ ।। rājāpi mama vākyena sahasaiva nimaṃtrayan ।
vaddhvāśu vaṃdhanāgāre prasthāpayati sāṃprataṃ ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi vatsāḥ sarve ihāgatāḥ । aparādhā yater neti vadeya sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ ।। yady avakṣyaṃ tathā rājā tadā me kupito nṛpaḥ ।
sarvasvam apahṛtvāpi prāhariṣyate mām iha ।। atha yadi bhayād rājño nāvadiṣyaṃs tathā kvacit । nūnaṃ taṃ yatim arhantam api rājā haniṣyate ।। tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tadghorapātakānalaiḥ ।
pacyamānas sadāvīcau tiṣṭheyam atiduḥkhitaḥ ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yatropāyaṃ na vidyate । sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo asmi vrajeya śaraṇaṃ kuha ।। yad imaṃ saugataṃ bhikṣum arhantaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ ।
anaparādhinaṃ hatvā kathaṃ pāpair na lepsyate ।। etair hi pātakair ghorair ahaṃ rājā janā ime । sarve vatsyāmahe avīcau bhuktvā duḥkhāni sarvadā ।। hā me daivād yateś cāpi nirjane vasato api yat ।
ghaṭe abhidṛśyate vatsamānsībhūtaṃ hi cīvaraṃ ।। avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavanty eva na cānyathā । tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi bhikṣur vā kiṃ kariṣyati ।। tasyaiva karmadoṣeṇa māṃsībhūtaṃ hi cīvaraṃ ।
atha mamaiva daivena tad iti manyate na hi ।। tad atra kiṃ vadeyāhaṃ daivaṃ hi sarvakarmakṛti । iti mamārho apy asya dūṣaṇaṃ nātra vidyate ।। tathapy etat pravṛttir na vaktavyaṃ kasya cid api ।
na gaṃtavyaṃ vahiḥ kvāpi sthātavyaṃ svagṛhe sadā ।। kadā cit skhalitā buddhir vāṇī ca vismṛtasya me । etad dhi pātakaṃ ghoraṃ samācakṣata kutra cit ।। tadāhaṃ niṃdyamāno atra sarvalokair itas tataḥ ।
bhratsyamānaḥ kathaṃ loke cariṣye duṣṭajaṃtuvat ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya brāhmaṇaḥ sa viṣāditaḥ । kasyāpy etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ noce daurjanyalajjayā ।। tat pātakāgnisaṃtaptaḥ smṛtvārhantaṃ tam eva saḥ ।
prāyaścittavrataṃ kurvann iva tasthau gṛhāśritaḥ ।। evaṃ dvādaśavarṣāṇi nṛpeṇāpi sa vismṛtaḥ । raivato vaṃdhanāgāre tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। atha dvādaśavarṣānte tac chiṣyāḥ sarva āgatāḥ । tat pravṛttiṃ samākarṇya vismitās te abhavaṃs tadā ।।
tataḥ sarve api te śiṣyāḥ saṃmīlya nṛpateḥ puraḥ । upetyaitat pravṛttāṃtaṃ samākhyāya nyavedayan ।। ārogyam astu te rājan lokān dharmeṇa pālaya । yadarthe vayam āyāmas tatra bhavān prasīdatu ।।
yad asmākaṃ gurur bhikṣur aparādhaṃ vinā kathaṃ । bhavatā vaṃdhanāgāre sthāpitas tad vicāraya ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvais tac chiṣyaiḥ prārthite tadā । vyomavāṇī tathākhyāya narendraṃ taṃ vyabodhayat ।।
tat khavāṇiṃ samākarṇya nṛpaḥ sa paribodhitaḥ । tac chiṣyaiḥ sārito bhikṣuṃ taṃ mumocāśu vaṃdhanāt ।। aho grāvāgralikhitā niścalā karmasaṃtatiḥ । prāptabhijño api yat prāpa krūrakleśadaśāṃ tathā ।।
taṃ yatiṃ nirgataṃ dṛṣṭvā sa rājābhyānutāpitaḥ । ninindā mandapuṇyatvaṃ pramādād dhatam ātmanaḥ ।। tadā sa nṛpati rājā sahasā tasya pādayoḥ । sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā samutthāyaivam abravīt ।।
bhadanto vicāryaiva pramadā yad bhavān mayā । sthāpito vaṃdhane tan me aparādhaṃ kṣaṃtum arhati ।। vismṛtā me sahāyāṃ ca parijñātā na kena cit । daṇḍaḥ patati śuddheṣu prāptaḥ pāpe mahīpatau ।।
ity uktaḥ kṣitipālena kṣāntiprakṣālitāśayaḥ । raivataḥ sa nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। rājan na te aparādhatvaṃ mamaitat karmajaṃ phalaṃ । tad atra mā kṛthāḥ kheṭaṃ saugata ātmavidyutaṃ ।।
tatas taṃ yatim arhantaṃ sa rājā sahasādarāt । cīvareṇa samāchādya piṃḍakena samārcayat ।। tadaitad vṛttim ākarṇya brāhmaṇaḥ sa tvarānvitaḥ । āgatya tat sabhāmadhye dattāśīḥ samupācarat ।।
tatra sa samupāsṛtya rājñe datvā jayāśiṣāṃ । taṃ yatiṃ sāñjalir natvā prārthayan vinayāt kṣamāṃ ।। bhadanta bhavatām evam aparādham akārayan । tan me aparādhatāṃ kṣaṃtum arhati sarvathā bhavān ।।
ity ukte tena vipreṇa raivataḥ sa viśuddhadhīḥ । brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ viṣaṇṇāsyaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। na manyur vidyate vipra na tvayāpakṛtaṃ mayi । mamaiva daivayā kena māṃsībhūtaṃ hi cīvaraṃ ।।
tatrāhaṃ maunam ālambya sthito daivābhyanusmaran । tenātra kiṃ vadiṣyāmi daivā hi valavān bhave ।। na tvayāpākṛtaṃ kiñcid vipulakleśapātitaḥ । tan mamopanataṃ pāke svakarmasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ ।। yat sautkaṇṭhatayaiva sarvavipadaḥ kurvanti kaṇṭhagrahaṃ sarvāṅgaprasabhopabhogasubhagāḥ kliśyanti yat saṃpadaḥ ।
yat svāchaṃdyasukhāspadaṃ viharaṇaṃ dīrghaṃ ca yad vaṃdhanaṃ tat puṃsāṃ nijakarmapākaśavalaṃ saṃsāravallīphalaṃ ।। iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvā naṃdaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । vismitaḥ kautukāc caivaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ yatim abravīt ।। tavāpi sumate kasya phalam etat kukarmaṇaḥ ।
kiṃ purā prakṛtaṃ karman tat samākhyātum arhati ।। iti pṛṣṭe narendreṇa raivataḥ sa sudhir yatiḥ । taṃ nareṃdraṃ samālokya bodhayituṃ tathāvadat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yan mayā prakṛtaṃ purā ।
tad atrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvalokaprabodhane ।। vārāṇasyāṃ purā krūracarito abhūt kuthābhidhaḥ । gocauraḥ kutsikācāro gomāṃsavihitāśanaḥ ।। kadā cit sa vane gatvā hatvā govatsam ātmanā ।
tad vatsamāṃsam ādāya sahasā tato viniryayau ।। tatra gorakṣiṇo vatsanaṣṭam anviṣya sarvataḥ । dṛṣṭvā taṃ māṃsabhārārttaṃ kopāt samabhidudruvuḥ ।। tatra sa kutha ālokya tān sarvān samupadrutān ।
sahasopadruto araṇye pradudrāva vanāṃtare ।। tatra pratyekabuddhasya dhyānalīnasya so agrataḥ । upanikṣipya tan māṃsaṃ tatraikānte nyalīyata ।। te api gorakṣiṇaḥ sarve sānucarām abhidrutāḥ ।
tatra pratyekabuddhaṃ tam ālokya samupācaran ।। tatra sa kutha āgatya teṣāṃ gorakṣiṇāṃ puraḥ । gomāṃsaṃ darśayitvā taṃ caurāyam ity adarśayat ।। tatra te gobhṛtaḥ sarve gomāṃsaṃ tan muneḥ puraḥ ।
dṛṣṭvaiva sahasā kopāt taṃ munim abhyaghātayat ।। vadhyo ayam iti taṃ vadhvā gopālās te prakopitāḥ । ākruśya sahasānītvā kārāgāre nyavaṃdhayat ।। tataḥ sa kutha ākarṇya taṃ yatiṃ vaṃdhane dhṛtaṃ ।
paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptas tahīty evaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। hā mayā pāpināpy evaṃ sādhyate pātakāni ca । avaśyaṃ vahnināvīcau kuṃhbhyāṃ pakṣye rataṃś ciraṃ ।। yad ayaṃ nirjane dhyāto pratyekabuddha ātmavit ।
caurāyam iti saṃdarśya vaṃdhane sthāpitomayā ।। etatpāpavipāke hi sarvadā narake sthitaḥ । tīvraduḥkhāgnisaṃtapta ante māṃ svakṛte phalaṃ ।। hā mayaivaṃ mahāghoraṃ pātakaṃ durdhiyā kṛtaṃ ।
kadā tat pātakān mukto vrajeyaṃ sadgatiṃ kathaṃ ।। hā sarvajña namas tubhyaṃ paśya mām atipāpinaṃ । bhavānn eva jagattrātā tan me api trātum arhati ।। mayā mūḍhena duṣṭena mahāpātakam ācitaṃ ।
tad vimuktyām upāyaṃ me kṛpayā dātum arhati ।। iti kuthaḥ sa cāṇḍālaḥ smṛtvā saṃbuddham ādarāt । paścāttāpābhisaṃtaptas tasthau gehe pramohitaḥ ।। tataḥ sa cetanaṃ prāpya saṃbuddhasyānubhāvataḥ ।
sahasā tata utthāya tadantike upācarat ।। tatra sa samupāsṛtya tesāṃ gorakṣiṇaṃ puraḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā yācitvābhayam abravīt ।। bhavanto atra mayā pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ tat pratidekṣyate ।
tad bhavaṃtaḥ samākarṇya kṣaṃtum arhaṃti sarvathā ।। asya pratyekabuddhasya hy aparādho na vidyate । tatra mayātiduṣṭena cauro ayam iti darśitaḥ ।। tad atra mucyatām eṣa pratyekasugato muniḥ ।
satkṛtyābhyarcya piṃḍena mānanīyo hi sarvadā ।। atraitat pātakaṃ nāsya mamaiva mastake pacet । tad aham eva vadhyo atra tad ayaṃ mucyatāṃ yatiḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve gorakṣiṇo api te ।
ruṣṭās taṃ sahasā vaddhvā paryyākhyāyātyatāḍayat ।। tat tāḍanaravaṃ śrutvā sa pratyekajinaḥ sudhīḥ । gopālāṃs tān samāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samādiśat ।। bhavanto mucyatām eṣa māparādhe api hanyatāṃ ।
kṣamā hi paramaṃ dharmaṃ tat kurvantu kṣamām iha ।। tantāsādyāgano yogaṃ kartum arhanti sarvathā । kiṃ daivaṃ nihataṃ hatvā yuṣmākaṃ setsyate phalaṃ ।। mayaitad vaṃdhanaṃ prāptaṃ mamaiva daivayogataḥ ।
tad asyāpy aparādho atra nāstīty eṣa vimucyatāṃ ।। iti pratyekabuddhena tenādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate । tatheti pratibuddhitvā tat kopaṃ mumucus tadā ।। atha te gobhṛtaḥ sarve śrutvā tasya muner vacaḥ ।
sahasā vinatiṃ kṛtvā vaṃdhanāt taṃ vyamuṃcayat ।। tatas te gobhṛtaḥ sarve taṃ pratyekamuniṃ mudā । cīvareṇa samāchādya samabhyarcyātyatoṣayan ।। tatra taṃ samupāśritya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natāḥ ।
tad aparādhasaṃtaptāḥ prārthayann evam ādarāt ।। bhagavañ jñāyate asmābhir bhavato nāparādhatā । tenāsmākaṃ kṣamāṃ kartum arhaty atra bhavān api ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa pratyekajinaḥ ।
tān sarvān gobhṛto dṛṣṭvā samāśvāsyaivam abravīt ।। bhavanto mā viṣīdantu dūṣaṇaṃ vā na vidyate । etad vṛttiṃ vijānāmi saugatā hi bhavārthavit ।। ity ādiśya sa sarvajñaḥ pratyekabuddha utthitaḥ ।
tata ākāśa utplutya svāśramaṃ gate āśrayan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te janāḥ sarve gopālāḥ prativismitāḥ । tam eva sugataṃ smṛtvā saddharme sarvadācaran ।। yo asau kuthābhidho goghnaḥ praduṣṭo ahaṃ tadābhavat ।
tatpāpair narakeṣv evaṃ ciraṃ duḥkhāni bhuktavān ।। asmiñ janmany api prāptakleśadvādaśavārṣikaṃ । tad asyātrāparādhaṃ na mamaitad daivayogataḥ ।। iti mahārāja śubhāśubhaṃ svadaivataḥ ।
saṃsāre atra sadā puṇyaṃ karttavyaṃ satsukhārthibhiḥ ।। puṇyam evātra saṃsāre sārasarvārthasiddhidaṃ । puṇyaṃ vinā na siddhyante kṛtakarmāṇi sarvathā ।। puṇyena jāyate svarge puṇyena yānti sadgatiṃ ।
puṇyena sarvadā bhadraṃ kṛtvā yāṃti jinālayaṃ ।। daṃḍena mucyate vadhyaḥ puṇyasyaivānubhāvataḥ । daṃḍārho api prahāreṇa prahārārho api roṣataḥ ।। roṣārhā romaharṣanena mucyate puṇyato nṛpa ।
yāvantaḥ sūkhinaḥ sarvasaṃpatsamanvitāḥ ।। sarve te puṇyakarttāra iti jñeyā narādhipa । puṇyena śuddhyate cittaṃ śuddhāśayo bhavet sudhīḥ ।। subuddhiḥ sarvadā nityaṃ śubheṣv eva samācaret ।
śubhācāro viśuddhāṃgaḥ satyavādī jitendriyaḥ ।। pariśuddhāśayo dhīro bhavet satvahitārthabhṛt । tathaitat puṇyayuktātmā sarvavidyākalārthavit ।। bhaved dharmārthavijñaś ca suguṇaśrīsamanvitaḥ ।
tato māheśvarīsaṃpatprāpto lokahitodyataḥ ।। dānaṃ kṛtvā sadā saukhyaṃ bhuktyā nityaṃ śubhe caret । etatpuṇyavipākena pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalaḥ ।। śubhraśīlo viśuddhātmā sadāryavratam ācaret ।
etatpuṇyānubhāvena kṣantidharmārthasādhakaḥ ।। svaparātmasamābhāvī caret maitrīsukhānvitaḥ । etatpuṇyavipākena dharmotsāhaguṇānvitaḥ ।। sarvaduṣṭagaṇāñ jitvā caret satvahite kṛtī ।
etatpuṇyaprabhāvaiś ca sarvakleśān vinirjayan । samādhidhāraṇīvijñaś cared dhyānaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākaiś ca sarvaśāstrābdhipāragaḥ । prajñāratnaṃ samāsādya mahābhijñapadaṃ labhet ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś cia sarvopāyavidhānavit । sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā śubhe nityaṃ samācaret ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś ca bodhipraṇidhimānasaḥ । sarveṣāṃ maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā bhadracaryāṃ samācaret ।।
etatpuṇyaprabhāvaiś ca daśabalasamanvitaḥ । sarvamārān vinirjitya cared bodhivrataṃ sadā ।। etat puṇyabalenaiva saṃbodhijñānam uttamaṃ । mahāratnaṃ samāsādya bhavet sarvavināyakaḥ ।। tataḥ sarvatra lokeṣu kṛtvā bhadrāṇi sarvadā ।
bodhisatvo mahāsatvaḥ saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś ca sarvāṃs traidhātukāsthitān । satvān bodhau pratisthāpya kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat ।। etatpuṇyavipākena dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।
nirvṛta ālayalīno mahābuddho bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। evaṃ matvā mahārāja nirvṛtipadalabdhaye । yadīchasi tathā puṇyam eva karttavyam ābhavaiḥ ।। puṇyam eva mahāratnaṃ sarvatrāpi mahānugaṃ ।
sarvārthasiddhidaṃ bhadraṃ saṃbuddhapadasādhanaṃ ।। iti vijñāya rājendra hitvā pāpānurāgatāṃ । puṇyāny evātra saṃsāre karttavyāni hi sarvadā ।। pāpena sarvadāpy evaṃ durgatīṣv eva saṃgatāḥ ।
mūḍhā kleśāgnisaṃtaptā bhramanti bhavacārake ।। yāvaṃto duḥkhito duṣṭā saṃsāre kleśatāpitāḥ । sarve te pāpakarttāra iti buddhaiḥ prakathyate ।। iti matvā mahārāja sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi ।
hitvā pāpānurāgatvaṃ saddharmaṃ cinu sādaraṃ ।। saddharmaṃ saugataṃ dharmaṃ yal lokaṃ hitasādhanaṃ । tenātra sarvadharmāṇāṃ pravaram agram ucyate ।। tad etaddharmasaṃprāptyai triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajasva samupasthitaḥ ।। triratne yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ tathā । tat phalam aprameyam asaṃkhyeya mahattaraṃ ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarve buddhā munīśvarāḥ ।
jagad dharmamayaṃ kṛtvā niḥkleśā parinirvṛtāḥ ।। evaṃ vijñāya bhūmīndra hitvā pāparatiṃ sadā । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara nityaṃ sadā śubhe ।। abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva kvāpi karma śubhāśubhaṃ ।
yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ dahyate deha eva hi । nodakaiḥ klidyate karmaṃ klidyate tanur eva ca ।। nānilaiḥ śuṣyate karmaṃ kāya evābhiśuṣyate ।
na kṣītau kṣīyate karmaṃ kṣīyate tanur eva hi ।। anyathāpi bhaven naiva vipāke karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ । yathaiva yat kṛtaṃ yena tenaiva bhujyate tathā ।। kṛṣṇasya karmaṇaḥ pāke duḥkhataiva sadā bhave ।
śubhasya sukhatā nityaṃ miśritasyobhayaṃ tathā ।। evaṃ karmavipākotthaṃ śubhāśubhaphalaṃ sadā । bhuktvā sarvatra saṃsāre bhramanti sarvajaṃtavaḥ ।। evaṃ matvā mahārāja kṛṣṇāni miśritāni ca ।
vihāyātra śobheṣv eva caritavyaṃ sadā bhave ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvānaṃdaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti prativijñapya sajanaḥ prābhya naṃdataḥ ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatir bhūyo raivataṃ taṃ mahāmatiṃ । sucīvaraiḥ samāchādya sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ vyadhāt ।।
punar utthāya bhūpālas tam arhantaṃ kṛtāṃjaliḥ । praṇatvā vinayaṃ kurvan kramāc ca prārthayat tathā ।। bhadantātra prasīdasva kṣamasva me aparādhatāṃ । sarvadā darśanaṃ datvānugrahaṃ kartum arhasi ।।
ity ukte anena bhūpena raivataḥ sa prasāditaḥ । haṃsarāja ivāplutya bhāsayan khe samāyayau ।। tatrākāśe samāsīnaḥ prātihāryaṃ pradarśayan । lokaiḥ saṃdṛśyamāno asau dhyātvā tasthau samujvalan ।।
tatas tair bhikṣubhiḥ śiṣyaiḥ samanvitaḥ prabhāsayan । tathākāśāś caraṃ gatvā svāśrame samupāśrayan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā sa nṛpo lokaiḥ sahātivismayānvitaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kurvan pracacāra sadā mudā ।।
evaṃ hy adoṣena viśeṣayuktyā pratyakṣaṇakṣyīkṛtalakṣaṇena । alaṃkṛtaḥ sādhujanaḥ khalena nighnīkṛto api na vikāram eti ।। evaṃ svadaivayogena jāyate hy aparādhatā । tan nānyasyāparādhatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ kena cit kva cit ।।
iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathātra kathyate mayā । iti matvā mahārāja sadā dharme samācara ।। prajāś cāpi tathā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva sadādarāt ।।
tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvaṃ cāpi bhavet sadā । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti satyaṃ parijñāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajasvātra samāhitaḥ ।।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathā hīti pratijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। satkṛtyedaṃ narā ye kalimatidaraṇaṃ raivatasyāvadanaṃ śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanaso bhaktiśraddhāprasannāḥ । te sarve apy evam atra vimalasumanasaḥ sarvadā satsukhāni bhuktvā kṛtvā subhadraṃ jinavaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodāṃ ।।
atha sa pārthivo asokaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan mahāmatiḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi sarve lokaprabodhane ।।
tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। ṣaḍabhijño jagannātho mārajit tu tathāgataḥ । puraikasamaye sārddhaṃ bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ saha ।।
cailakair bhikṣuṇībhiś caivam upāsikāgaṇair api । upāsākais tathānyaiś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ ।। bodhisatvair mahāsatvair brahmendrādisurādhipaiḥ । sarve lokādhipaiś cāpi dānavendraiḥ śubhārthibhiḥ ।।
nāgendrair garuḍendraiś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnaraiḥ । grahai vidyādharaiś cāpi tathānyaiś ca vṛṣārthibhiḥ ।। stūya mānārcyamānaś ca vaṃdyamāno abhinaṃditaḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena janapadeṣu sarvataḥ ।।
saddharmaṃ samupādiśya pracacāra sasāṃghikaḥ । tathā ca kośale rāṣṭre varaṃ dharmam upādiśat ।। tato anyatrāpi saddharmam upadeṣṭuṃ tato acarat । tatrānyasmin vane prāpto bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ ।।
sarvatra maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śanaiḥ kramāt । tatrārāṇye mahān yūtho mahiṣīṇāṃ samācarat ।। tatraiko mahiṣaś caṇḍo valavīryasamanvitaḥ । mahāśṛṃgo mahākāyaḥ pratyavasan madotkaṭaḥ ।।
tatrāsan paṃcamātrāṇi mahiṣapālaśatāni ca । sarve tan mahiṣīyūtham anurakṣyādhyuvāsata ।। tadaikasmin dine tatra bhagavān sa sasaṃghikaḥ । pracaraṃs tatpradeśe taṃ mahiṣīyutham aikṣata ।।
tadā te mahiṣīpālā taṃ munīṃdraṃ sasaṃghikaṃ । samupāyātam ālokya dūrād evam aghoṣayan ।। bhagavān mātra samāyāhi pathānyena vrajādhunā । asty atra mahiṣo duṣṭas tat sahasā carānyata ।।
iti taiḥ śabditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । sasaṃghaḥ samupāśritya tāṃ dṛṣṭvaivam ahhāṣata ।। alpotsukābhavatv atra bhagavantaḥ kiṃ kuto bhayaṃ । kālajño ahaṃ jinendro asmi tadarthe atra samācare ।।
tadā sa mahiṣo duṣṭas taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । dūrād dṛṣṭvā samutthāya pradudrāva tadantike ।। tatra tadgaṃdham āghrāya dṛṣṭvā taṃ raktacīvaraṃ । ruṣā lāṃgūlam unnāmya saṃmukhaḥ prābhyadhāvata ।।
tatra tena jinendreṇa pañcasiṃhā mahoddhatāḥ । abhinirmāya tatpṛṣṭhe sthāpitā bhīmarūpiṇaḥ ।। tathā nirmāya tatrāgniskaṃdhau dvāv atiprojvalau । ubhayoḥ pārśvayos tasya sthāpito bhīmanisvanau ।।
tathātra kūṭasaṃkāśo nirmāya mahatī śilā । upariṣṭāt pratiṣṭhāpya darśitā tasya bhītaye ।। tatra sa mahiṣo adrākṣīt tān siṃhān pṛṣṭhasaṃsthitān । pārśvayor ubhayor agniskaṃdhaur uparitāṃ śilāṃ ।।
evaṃ sa mahiṣo duṣṭo mahābhayam upasthitaṃ । samantataḥ samālokya pravikheṭābhimohitaḥ ।। tatra sa trasito dṛṣṭvā parāyituṃ caturdiśaḥ । samantato bhayād vignas tasthau trāṇanirāśrayaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa cakitas tasya munīndrasyābhisaṃmukhaṃ । upetya caraṇau natvā śaraṇaṃ samupāyayau ।। tatra tadbhayabhinnāsyaḥ parikhinnāśayo rudan । bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ālokya tasthau atrāṇāśrayo puraḥ ।।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mahiṣyaṃ tam upasthitaṃ । śaraṇāgatam ālokya dharmam evam upādiśat ।। bhadramukheti saṃskārāḥ sarve anityā bhave dhruvāḥ । sarvadharmā anātmanaḥ śāntaṃ nirvāṇam eva hi ।।
iti dharmaravam śrutvā sa tat puṇyānubhāvataḥ । pūrvajanmapravṛttāṃtaṃ smṛtvā prarurodānutāpitaḥ ।। evaṃ taṃ ruditaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa munīśvara । bodhayituṃ samāśvāsya punar gāthe abhyabhāṣata ।।
idānīṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tiryagyonigatasya te । akṣaṇapratipannasya kiṃ rodiṣi nirarthakaṃ ।। sādhu prasādyatāṃ cittaṃ mayi kāruṇike jine । tiryagyoniṃ virāgyeha tataḥ svargaṃ gamiṣyasi ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa mahiṣas tadā । sarvaṃ smṛtvā purāvṛttaṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। hā mayā durdhiyājñena tyaktvā saddharmasaṃyamaṃ । krodhāgninā svayaṃ dagdhā saṃtāpare api tāpitā ।।
yenāhaṃ hā paribhraṣṭaḥ saddharmamaṇinā adhunā । viṣarāgāgnisaṃtaptaḥ kṛṣṇāhir iva durmatiḥ ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi tiryakjātir ihādhunā । kiṃ mamānena kāyena duḥkhe pāpānusādhinā ।।
yatra puṇyaṃ sukhaṃ nāsti tatra kiṃ jīvitena me । varam evādya me mṛtyur na tv evaṃ cirajīvitaṃ ।। avaśyaṃ mṛtyum āpnuyāṃ sarveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ । tad atra me śarīre kā snehatā jīvite api vā ।।
dhik kāyaṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi yena puṇyaṃ na sādhyate । puṇyam eva bhave sāraṃ sarvatra satsukhapradaṃ ।। puṇyaṃ vinātrā saṃsare kiṃ śrīsaṃpatsukhānvite । sarvaṃ vihāya gaṃtavyaṃ puṇyām ekaṃ tadānugaḥ ।।
puṇyam eva jaganmitraṃ puṇyam eva sadānugaḥ । puṇyam eva mahatsāraṃ puṇyam eva hitārthadaṃ ।। tasmāt puṇyaṃ prayatnena sādhanīyaṃ bhave sadā । sarvatra sukhatāhetu puṇyam eveti kathyate ।।
tat puṇyaratnasaṃprāptyai buddhasya śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । sarvathā smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajeyeha samāhitaḥ ।। ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā mahiṣaḥ sa prabodhitaḥ । taṃ buddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ natvānusmṛtvābhajān mudā ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāns tasya dṛṣṭvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sasaṃghaḥ svāśrame yayau ।। tatrāśrame samāsīno bhagavān sasasāṃghikaḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbodhidharmam ādiśat ।।
taddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ । brahmaśakrādayo devā lokapālāś ca dānavāḥ ।। grahā vidyādharāḥ siddhā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । garuḍā nāgarājāś ca rākṣasāś ca śubhārthinaḥ ।।
ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāś cāpi nṛpā rājakumārakāḥ । vaiśyāc ca maṃtriṇo amātyā gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ ।। vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpinaḥ paurikā api । grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tīrthyāḥ kārpaṭikā api ।।
evam anye api lokāś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃ chinaḥ । sarve te samupāgatya tatrāśrame samāviśat ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samānarcur yathākramaṃ ।।
tatas te praṇatiṃ kṛtvā parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitāṃ । ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃprabodhitāḥ । dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya triratnaṃ sarvadābhajan ।। tatra sa mahiṣaḥ pūrvajanmavṛttim anusmaran । tadā taddeham utsraṣṭuṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
hā duṣṭena mayā pūrvam ācitaṃ ghorapātakaṃ । tenāhaṃ mahiṣo duṣṭo bhavāmy atra yathoditaṃ ।। tad atra kiṃ prakurvīya paśus tat pāpaśodhaṇaṃ । tat triratnam anusmṛtvā careyāham upoṣadhaṃ ।। datvātrāham imaṃ kāyaṃ satvebhyaḥ śraddhayā adhunā ।
manasā sugataṃ dhyātvā martuṃ tiṣṭheya sāṃprataṃ ।। tad imaṃ deham utkṛtya tvagmānsarudhirādikaṃ । asthimajjādi sarvaṃ ca bhujantu prāṇino mudā ।। ye ye satvā imaṃ dehaṃ bhujanti surasaṃ mudā ।
te te sarve sadā dharmaṃ kṛtvā yāntu surālāyaṃ ।। tathaitat puṇyapākena muktvāsmān pāpakāśrayāt । āsādya sadgatau janma bhajeyaṃ sugataṃ sadā ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya mahiṣaḥ sa prasannadhīḥ ।
tyaktvāhāraṃ tapaśvīva buddhaṃ smṛtvācarat tapaḥ ।। tathā sa mahiṣo dhyātvā triratnaṃ cābhyanusmaran । dehaṃ tyaktvā viśuddhātmā surālayaṃ samāyayau ।। tatra svarge sa utpanno mahāsukhasamanvitaḥ ।
vismitābhiprasannātmā tadaivaṃ samaciṃtayat ।। aho hi jāyate saukhyaṃ kutaś cyutvā kuhācare । kasya puṇyavipākena mamaivaṃ jāyate śubhaṃ ।। iti ciṃtayatas tasya mahiṣapūrviṇas tathā ।
vismayākrāṃtacittasya samutpannābhavan matiḥ ।। aho tiryaggateś cyutvā devaloka ihāsare । saṃbuddhasmṛtipuṇyena devo bhavāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। tad ahaṃ tasya munīndrasya draṣṭuṃ gacheya sāṃprataṃ ।
śraddhayā samupāśritya saddharmaṃ śṛṇuyāṃ punaḥ ।। iti mahiṣapūrvī sa devaputraḥ pramoditaḥ । tatra tasya munīndrasya darśane gaṃtum aichata ।। tataḥ sa muditaḥ snātvā śuddhadivyāṃvarāvṛtaḥ ।
divyagaṃdhānuliptāṃgo divyālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।। divyapūjopahārāṇi gṛhītvā devagaṇaiḥ saha । tasyāṃ rātrau munīndrasya bhāsayann āśrame yayau ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā muditaḥ samupāsaran ।
natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samānarcca yathāvidhiḥ ।। tatas tasya munīndrasya sāṃjaliḥ sa praṇamya ca । saddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ purataḥ samupāśrayat ।। tathā te tat sahāyāś ca devaputrāḥ prasāditāḥ ।
bhagavaṃtaṃ sāṃjalayaḥ upāśrayan ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān । āryyasatyasamārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā saha devaiḥ pramoditaḥ ।
devo mahiṣapūrvi sa dharmaviśeṣam āptavān ।। satkāyaduṣṭibhūmīndhraṃ viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ । nirbhidya jñānavajreṇa śrotaāpattim āyayau ।। tātaḥ sa dṛṣṭasatyas taṃ bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ ।
kṛtāṃjaliḥ puṭo natvā trir udānam udānayat ।। bhagavann idam asmākaṃ kṛtaṃ na janakena hi । na mātrā na ca rājñāpi nānyena kena cit khalu ।। bhavataiva yad asmākaṃ kṛtapāpaviśodhanaṃ ।
tenābhiśoṣitāśeṣarudhirāśrusāritpariḥ ।। laṃghitā asthiśailāś ca pihitā pāpapaddhatiḥ । vivṛtāḥ svargamārgāś ca mokṣamārgaś ca darśitaḥ ।। mayāptaṃ vimalaṃ cakṣuḥ śāntam āryapadaṃ tathā ।
duḥkhārṇavaḥ samuttīrṇo bodhimārgo api dṛśyate ।। tad bhavatāṃ kṛpādṛṣṭeḥ prasādān mama sāṃprataṃ । saṃsārajanma sāphalyaṃ buddhaputrāsmy ahaṃ yataḥ ।। adyārabhya sadā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya cariṣyāmi śubhāṃ cariṃ ।। tad atrānugrahaṃ kṛtvā bhavāñ chāstā jagaguruḥ । kṛpayā sarvadā paśyann evaṃ māṃ trātum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena suparvaṇā niśamya saḥ ।
śāstā tasyāśayaṃ śuddhaṃ samalokyaivam ādiśat ।। sadho śṛṇu hitaṃ vakṣye sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt ।। ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajaṃti śraddhayā sadā ।
māracaryābhimuktās te saṃprayāṃti jinālayaṃ ।। ye dharmaṃ saugataṃ nityaṃ śṛṇvanti śraddhayā mudā । sarvapāpābhimuktās te saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। ye ca saṃghe prakurvanti satkāraṃ śraddhayādarāt ।
