te sarve durgater muktvā saṃprayānti surālayaṃ ।। triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ye bhajanti sadādarāt । durgatiṃ te na gachaṃti sadā gachaṃti sadgatiṃ ।। sadgatau te sadā sthitvā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
kṛtvā lokahitaṃ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā ramanti sarvadā ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ । trividhāṃ bodhim āsadya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।। iti nirvāṇasatsaukhyaḥ prāptuṃ yadi samichasi ।
triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena pariśuddhas trimaṃḍalaḥ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa paribodhitāḥ ।
tathety abhyanumoditvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। adya me saphalaṃ saṃpūritaṃ manorathaṃ । bodhiratnābhisaṃpanno buddhaputro asmi sāṃprataṃ ।। sarvadā bhavatām eva śaraṇe ahaṃ samāsthitaḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kurvañ cariṣye bodhisaṃvaraṃ ।। iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā devaputraḥ sa moditaḥ । śrīghanaṃ taiḥ punar natvā sasahāyo divaṃ yayau ।। tatra svarge sa saṃprāpto devaiḥ saha samāśritaḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kurvan saukhyaṃ bhuktvā samācarat ।।
tasyāṃ rātrau mahatkāntiṃ prabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā savismayāḥ । sarve te mahiṣīpālā vabhūvuḥ śaṃkitāśayāḥ ।। tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya sarve te kautukānvitāḥ । saṃmīlya sahasā tatra buddhāśrame upācaran ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te pratimoditāḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā samupatasthur ādarāt ।। tadā sa bhagāvān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te pratibodhitāḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ punar natvā paprachur evam ādarāt ।। bhagavann adya rātrau ka ihāśrame prabhāsayan । bhavatāṃ samupāyātas tat samādeṣṭum arhati ।।
iti tair mahiṣīpālaiḥ paripṛṣṭe sa sarvavit । bhagavāṃs tān samālokya purāvṛttim upādiśat ।। yo atrāsau mahiṣo duṣṭo dṛṣṭvāsmān samupadrutaḥ । samantato bhayaṃ dṛṣṭvā trasto me śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
tadā maddharmam ākarṇya pūrvajātim anusmaran । mayi cittaṃ prasādyaiva tyaktvāhārā tyajan tanuṃ ।। tato asmatsmṛtipuṇyena pāpamukto viśuddhadhīḥ । svargaloke samutpanno devo bhavati sāṃprataṃ ।।
sa eṣa devaputro adya niśāyām atra bhāsayan । devalokaiḥ sahāyāto darśanāya mamālāye ।। matsaddharmaṃ samākarṇya dṛṣṭasatyaḥ sa harṣitaḥ । devasaṃghaiḥ saha svarge svālaye pragatas tathā ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvātivismayoddhatāḥ । sarve te mahiṣīpālā mitha evaṃ samabruvan ।। aho citra hi yan nāma tiryyagyonigato api saḥ । buddhaṃ sadgurum āsādya dharmaṃ śrutvābhavat sudhīḥ ।।
sadgurau sugate cittaṃ prasādya viratāśanaḥ । trirātnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prāṇaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau ।। tato apīha samāgatya saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । abhyarcya dharmam ākarṇya dṛṣṭasatyo divaṃ yayau ।।
svarge api tat tathā nityaṃ sadguroḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । śraddhayā bhajanaṃ kurvaṃ chubhe acarat samāhitaḥ ।। dhanyo ayaṃ sugataḥ śāstā sarvasatvaśubhaṃkaraḥ । yatra cittaṃ prasādyaiva paśur api divaṃ gataḥ ।।
vayaṃ tu mānavāḥ sarve katham enaṃ munīśvaraṃ । sadguruṃ samupāsādya śraddhayā na bhajemahi ।। tathā saddharmam ākarṇya prasādād asya sadguroḥ । atkṛtya sarvadā bhadraṃ na lābhema kathaṃ vayaṃ ।।
viśeṣadharmam ājñāya dṛṣṭasatyāḥ samāhitāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā nūnaṃ gachema sadgatiṃ ।। tad atra sadguror asya munīndrasyādhunā vayaṃ । sarve api śraddhayābhyarcya bhajemahi samādarāt ।।
tat sāddharmaṃ samākarṇya śraddhayā samupasthitāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caremahi śubhe sadā ।। tadādau sugatasyāsya sasaṃghasyā adhunā vayaṃ । yathārhabhojanenātra pūjayema prapuṣṭaye ।।
iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te pratimoditāḥ । tatheti saṃmataṃ kṛtvā tatra buddhāśrame yayuḥ ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ pramoditāḥ । sarvasāṃjalayo natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghikaṃ । pūjayituṃ samichāmas tann atrānugrahaṃ kuru ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । teṣāṃ puṇyābhisaṃvṛddhyai tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।।
tathādhyuvāsitaṃ matvā sarve te pariharṣitāḥ । pādau tasya munīndrasya natvā nijālayaṃ yayuḥ ।। tatra te muditāḥ sarve dadhikṣīrodanādikaṃ । yathārhabhojyasāmagriṃ sahasā samasādhayan ।।
tatas te samaye gatvā tatra buddhāśrame mudā । sasāṃghikaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate adhunā । tat saṃgha bhagavān pūjāṃ pratigrahitum arhati ।।
iti taiḥ prārthite sarve bhagavān sasasāṃghikaḥ । utthāya bhojanakṣetre upācarān prabhāsayan ।। tatra pādyaṃ samādāya saṃbuddhapramukhāḥ kramāt । sarve te sāṃghikās tatra svasvāsane samāśrayan ।।
tāṃ buddhapramukhān sarvān sāṃghikān svāsanāśritān । dṛṣṭvā te muditā sarve sāmānarcur yathākramaṃ ।। tatas te surasair bhojyaiḥ kṣīrodanaiḥ savyaṃjanaiḥ । praṇītair bhagavaṃtaṃ taṃ sasaṃghaṃ samatoṣayan ।।
tatas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ samīkṣya te । tat pātrāṇy apanīyāśu tad dhastādi samaśodhayan ।। tataḥ sapūgatāmburāmahauṣadharasāyanaṃ । saṃbuddhapramukhebhyas te saṃghebhyaḥ pradadur mudā ।।
tatas te mahiṣīpālāḥ kṛtāṃjalipūṭā mudā । śrīghanaṃ taṃ sasaṃghaṃ ca natvā samupatasthire ।। tathā tan samupāsīnān sarvān dṛṣṭvā sa sarvavit । āryadharmaṃ samādiśya bodhimārge abhyayojayat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te abhyanumoditāḥ ।
saṃbuddhaśāsane tatra pravrajituṃ samīkṣire ।। tatās te mahiṣīpālāḥ sarve kṛtvābhisaṃmataṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭā natvā prārthayan taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhāgavaṃ nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śāsane vayaṃ ।
pravrajituṃ samichāmas tan no anvāhartum arhati ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tān viśuddhāśayān sarvān samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। mātāpitror vinānujñāṃ pravrajyāṃ na dadāmy ahaṃ ।
tad anujñāṃ samādāya preta dāsyāmi vas tadā ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sarve te pratinaṃditāḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvāśu svasvagehaṃ yayur mudā ।। tatra te sahasā gatvā samātāpitṛvāṃdhavān ।
paribodhya prayatnena prāpyānujñāṃ samācaraṃ ।। tatra te sahasā gatvā bhagavata upāsṛtāḥ । pādau sāṃjalayor natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan sarvavit pitṛprāptānujñāḥ samāgatāḥ ।
tatrānugraham ādhāya pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati ।। iti taiḥ prārthite śāstā bhagavān savyapāṇinā । teṣāṃ śiras susaṃspṛṣṭvā samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sameta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yūyaṃ śraddhāsamaṃgitāḥ ।
pravrajyāvratam ādhāya carata brahmacārikāṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sarve te muṇḍitā vabhuḥ । khikkhirīpātradharttāraḥ kākhāyacīvarāvṛtāḥ ।। tataḥ śastuḥ prasādena sarve te vimalāśayāḥ ।
pralabdhabodhisaccittāḥ śuddhaśīlā jiteṃdriyāḥ ।। bhitvāvidyāguṇāḥ samyak prāptavidyāviśāradāḥ । pratisaṃvitsusaṃprāptāḥ satyamārgasamanvitāḥ ।। samādhidhāraṇīvidyā ghaṭamānāḥ samāhitāḥ ।
kṣamānvitāḥ śubhātmāno yogino bhikṣavo abhavan ।। tatas te sarvasaṃsāraṃ matvānityaṃ cālācalaṃ । dṛṣṭvā ca sarvasaṃskāragatīr ahivighātinīḥ ।। sarvakleśagaṇān hitvā jitvā māragaṇān api ।
sākṣād arhatvam āsādya pracerur brahmacārikāḥ ।। tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalāḥ । vītasaṃgā mahābhijñā nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ ।। samaloṣṭakasauvarṇāḥ satkāralābhanispṛhāḥ ।
akāśasamacittāṅgā bhave lābhaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। devāsurādi lokānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ । pūjyā mānyāś ca vaṃdyāś ca babhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayoddhatamānasāḥ ।
bhagavaṃtaṃ muniṃ natvā papracbus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavan kāni karmāṇi tena mahiṣapūrviṇā । kṛtāni devaputreṇa yair asau mahiṣo abhavat ।। ebhiś ca mahiṣīpālaiḥ kiṃ karma prakṛtaiḥ purā ।
yenārhatvaṃ samāsādya bhavaṃti brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। etat sarvaṃ samādiśya bhavāñ chāstātra sāṃprataṃ । asmākaṃ api cetāṃsi prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tān sarvān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve tena mahiṣapūrviṇā । purā kṛtāni karmāṇi tāni vakṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। ebhiś ca mahiṣipālaiḥ purā yāni kṛtāny api ।
tāni sarvāṇi karmāṇi vakṣyāmi ca tathā adhunā ।। tadyathābhūt purā buddhaḥ kāśyapo arhans tathāgataḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyākaḥ ।। bhagavān sa tadā pūryyāṃ varāṇasyā upāśrame ।
mṛgadāve samāśritya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tadā tasya munīndrasya śāsane tripiṭo yatiḥ । bhikṣur eko mahāvijño niścayārthaviśāradaḥ ।। tadaikasamaye bhikṣupaṃcaśataiḥ puraskṛtaḥ ।
sa sabhāyāṃ samāsīnaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tasya te bhikṣavaḥ śikṣāḥ śaikṣāś ca saṃścayānvitāḥ । tripiṭārthaṃ parijñātuṃ paprachus taṃ guruṃ muhuḥ ।। evaṃ tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe sa guruḥ pratiroṣitaḥ ।
tān sarvāñ chrāvakāñ chiṣyāñ chaikṣāṃś ca paryabhāṣata ।। tatas te śrāvakāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ ruṣitaṃ guruṃ । praṇatvā vinayaṃ kṛtvā punar evam abhāsire ।। bhavanta mā kṛthā roṣaṃ prasīdasva kṛpānidhe ।
vyākhyātaṃ bhavatā samyak tad asmābhi na budhyate ।। tad bhūyo api bhavān etadarthaṃ samyak suvistaraṃ । asmac cetaṃ prabodhārthaṃ samupādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti taiḥ prārthite bhūyas tripiṭaḥ so atiroṣitaḥ ।
tathā tāñ chrāvakān sarvān paribhāṣyaivam abravīt ।। are re mahiṣā yūyaṃ tat kiṃ jānītha madvacaḥ । tad bhūyaḥ kiṃ pravakṣyāmi yac chrutvāpi na budhyate ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te pariroṣitāḥ ।
taṃ guruṃ yatim arhantam api pratyavadas tathā ।। yad vayaṃ mahiṣāḥ sarve tad bhavān mahiṣādhipaḥ । yad asmākaṃ yathā śāsta tathā bhavatu pālakaḥ ।। iti taiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sarvaiḥ śikṣaiḥ śaikṣaṃ ca roṣitaiḥ ।
sadguror antike kopād yat khalaṃ pratibhāṣitaṃ ।। etat pāpābhiśaṃkārttāḥ paścāttāpābhitāpinaḥ । tam arhantaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evaṃ vabhāṣire ।। aho mūḍhā vayaṃ sarve yat kopāt sadguror api । pratyākhyāya vayo asmābhiḥ pratyuttaraṃ pradīyate ।।
tad etat pātakaṃ ghoraṃ kathaṃ vayaṃ śahemahi । tad bhavān kṛpayāsmākaṃ kṣaṃtum arhati sarvathā ।। tathā janmāṃtare cāpi bhavantam eva sadguruṃ । kalyāṇamitram āsādya prāpnuyāma susaṃvaraṃ ।।
iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā sarve te bhikṣavas tathā । tasya guror upāśritya dharmaṃ śrutvābhajan sadā ।। tatas te samaye sarve śrāvakās tripiṭo api saḥ । kālaṃ gatāḥ punar janma lehire durgatau tataḥ ।।
khalavākkarmapākena paṃcajanmaśatāny api । sa tripiṭapatiḥ śāstā mahiṣo ayaṃ sabhābhavat ।। sarve te śrāvakāś cāpi yathā vākkarmadoṣataḥ । tatheme mahiṣīpalā vabhūvuḥ sarvadā bhave ।।
atrāpi mahiṣo duṣṭas tripiṭo asau bhavaty api । ime api mahiṣīpālā bhavanti bhikṣavo api te ।। yac cāyaṃ mahiṣo apy atra kāśyapakṛtapuṇyataḥ । dṛṣṭvā māṃ suprasannātmā natvā me śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena devaputro bhavaty ayaṃ । āryasatyaṃ samāsādya dṛṣṭasatyo sudhīr api ।। ime api mahiṣīpālāḥ kāśyapapuṇyapākātaḥ । pravrajyārhatvam āsādya bhavanti brahmacāriṇaḥ ।।
evaṃ karmavipākair hi sarve api jantavo bhave । sukhaduḥkhāni bhuṃjānā bhramanti bhavacārake ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ vāyubhir vā na śuṣyate । klidyate nodakaiś cāpi kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu ।।
abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karmaṃ kvāpi kathaṃ cana । sarvatrāpi bhaven naiva karmaṇo gatir anyathā ।। śubhasya karmaṇaḥ pāke śubhataiva sadā bhave । tathā kṛṣṇasya pāke ca duḥkhataiva sadā bhave ।।
miśritānāṃ tathā pāke miśritāni phalāny api । evaṃ matvā śubheṣv eva caritavyaṃ sadā bhave ।। yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ । avaśyaṃ pariboktavyaṃ saṃsāre karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ ।।
na nasyaṃti hi karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api । sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajadhvaṃ sarvathādarāt ।।
ye bhajaṃti sadā nityaṃ triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । durgatiṃ te na gachaṃti yānty eva sadgatiṃ sadā ।। ity ādiṣṭaiḥ munīndreṇa śrutvā te saṃghikā mudā । sarve lokāś ca satkṛtya triratnaṃ sarvadābhajaṃ ।। etan me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā mayocyate adhunā ।
tvayāpy evaṃ mahārāja caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe ।। prajāś cāpi sadā dhārmaṃ śrāvāyitvā prabodhayan । bodhimārge pratisthāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। tathā te maṃgalam nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti abhyanumoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। idaṃ narā ye mahiṣāvādānaṃ śṛṇvaṃti ye capi niśāmayaṃti sukhāni bhuktvā khalu te atra sarve samyāṃti nūnaṃ sugatālayaṃ te ।।
athāśoko mahinātha upaguptaṃ yatiṃ guruṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadaṃta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tad yathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।।
saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhan sudhīr yatiḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaiyam abravīt ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru ।।
puraikasamaye buddho bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śastā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। sasaṃgho hāsayan tatra magadhe cārikāṃ caran । sarvatra bhadratāṃ kṛtvā gaṃgātīram upāśrayan ।।
tatra sa bhagavān sarvai bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ puraskṛtaḥ । sabhāmadhyāsanāsīno dharmam ādeṣṭum aichata ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarvalokās tadāgatāḥ । brahmaśakrādayo devā lokapālā gaṇādayaḥ ।।
daityeṃdro garuḍā nāgā yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnarāḥ । siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi rākṣasāś ca maharddhikāḥ ।। ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāś cāpi yogino yatayo api ca । rājānaḥ kṣatriyā bhūpā rājaputrāś ca tīrthikaḥ ।।
vaiśyāś cā maṃtriṇo amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ paurikāḥ prajāḥ । gṛhasthāḥ sādhavo bhadrāḥ sārthavāhamahājanāḥ ।। vaṇijāḥ śilpinaś cāpi grāmyā jānapadā api । tathānye api samāyātāḥ saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ ।।
tatra te samupāyātā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samānarcur yathākramaṃ ।। tataḥ sarve api te lokāḥ parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ । samāhitāḥ samudvīkṣya dharmaṃ śrotuṃ samāśrayan ।।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān । bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ । dharmāviśeṣam ājñāya triratnaṃ prābhajan sadā ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāl lokāñ chubhāśritān । tathānyatra śubhaṃ kartuṃ gaṃgātīram upācarat ।। sasaṃgho bhagāvaṃs tatra gaṃgātīra upāsṛtaḥ । navikān samupāhūya samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
nāvikā gantum ichāmi gaṃgāpāram ito adhunā । tan mām imāṃ nadīṃ gaṃgāṃ samuttārayata drutaṃ ।। iti tat prārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te nāvikā api ।। sasāṃghikaṃ munīndraṃ tan anādṛtyaivam abruvan ।
tarapaṇyaṃ vināsmābhiḥ kaści diśā na tāritaḥ ।। yadīchati bhavāns tarttuṃ tarapaṇyaṃ prayachatu । iti tair bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।। tān sarvān nāvikān dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।
aham api bhavaṃto atra nāviko asmi ti manyatāṃ ।। mayā hi tārito naṃdo mahārāganadīkṛtaḥ purā । dveṣābdhipatito duṣṭo aṅgulimālo api tāritaḥ ।। mānavo mānakūpārapatitas tārito mayā ।
mohodadhinimagnaś coruvilvīkāśyapas tathā ।। evam anye api lokāś ca kleśābdhe tāritā mayā । kasya cid api satvasya tarapaṇyaṃ na kiṃ cana ।। gṛhyate yācyate nāpi mayā kvāpi kadā cana ।
tathā yūyam apīhāsmān sarvān bhikṣūn nimāṃdakī ।। agāḍhāṃ sahasā tārya pāre nayatum arhatha । evaṃ tena munīndreṇa prārthite api na ke cana ।। nāvikās te munīndraṃ taṃ tārayituṃ samīchire ।
atra kaścit sudhīḥ sādhur nāvikas taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। mahābhijñaṃ parijñāya natvovāca kṛtāṃjaliḥ । bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavantaṃ sarvasāṃghikān ।। apy ahaṃ tārayiṣyāmi tat prasīdatu me sadā ।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।। sarvāns tān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat । bhikṣavo nāvam āruhya yūyaṃ sarve samāhitāḥ ।। imāṃ gaṃgāṃ samuttīrya tiṣṭhata tīram āśritāḥ ।
ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sarve te bhikṣusaṃghikāḥ ।। sahasā nāvam āruhya saṃniṣeduḥ samāhitāḥ । tadā sa nāviko dṛṣṭvā sarvān naukāsamāśritān ।। tāṃ nāvaṃ sahasā gaṃgāmadhye saṃprāpayan kramāt ।
tadā sa bhagavānn ṛddhyā vihāyasā svayaṃ caran ।। tad agrataḥ samuttīrya tīrabhūmau samāśrayan । tad dṛṣṭvā nāvikā sarve te salokāḥ savismayāḥ । paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptāḥ paśyanta eva tasthire ।।
so api ca nāvīko dṛṣṭvā taṃ munīndraṃ vihāyasā । sahasā tīram āsadya sthitaṃ paśyan nyaṣīdat ।। tataḥ sā niścarā naukā stambhitaiva jalāśritā । tad dṛṣṭvā nāvikaḥ so ativismayākulato abhavat ।।
tatas taiḥ śrīghanaṃ tīrasamāsīnaṃ sa nāvikaḥ । dṛṣṭvā tat smṛtim ādhāya praṇanāma kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। tataḥ sāsaṃcarā naukā vāyusaṃpreritā drutaṃ । sahasā tīram āsādya tasthau tatra suniścarā ।। tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve samuttīrya vahitrataḥ ।
sahasā tīram āgatya saṃbuddhāntikam āyayuḥ ।। tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān samupāgatān । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ tasthau sabhāsanāśritaḥ ।। tataḥ sa nāvikaś cāpi dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ ।
bhikṣusaṃghasabhāsīnaṃ praṇatuṃ samupācaran ।। tatra sa sāñjalir natvā sarvān tan sāṃghikān kramāt । pādāmbujau munīndrasya praṇanāma pramoditaḥ ।। tatra te nāvikāś cāpi sarve te vismayānvitāḥ ।
tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ muditāḥ samupācaran ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ saṃpramoditāḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samupatasthur ādarāt ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān ।
āryyasatyasamārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat addharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā nāvikaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । vijñāya dharmavaiśeṣyaṃ saddharmābhirato bhavet ।। tataḥ satkāyabhūmīndhraṃ viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ ।
nirbhidya jñānavajreṇa dharmadṛṣṭi samāptavān ।। tataḥ sa śrotaāpattiphalaprāptaḥ prasannadhīḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ samālokya trir udānam udānayat ।। bhagavan yat mayā prāptaṃ dharmacakṣuḥ sunirmalaṃ ।
śāntaṃ padam āryakāntaṃ tīrṇaś cāpi bhavārṇavaḥ ।। satkāyadṛṣṭiśailāś ca laṃghitāḥ sāṃprataṃ mayā । pihito pāpamārgo me svargamārgaḥ prakāśitaḥ ।। mokṣamārgo api saṃprāpto bhavatāṃ kṛpayā adhunā ।
tathā bhavān sadā nityaṃ māṃ paritrātum arhati ।। evaṃ hi na kṛtaṃ mātrā nāpi pitrā kṛtaṃ mama । na suhṛdiṣṭamitraiś ca vāṃdhavaiḥ svajanair api ।। śramaṇair brāhmaṇaiś cāpi gurubhiś ca na vā nṛpaiḥ ।
tathānyaiś ca mahāvijñair na kṛtam āryadeśanāṃ ।। bhavataiva kṛtaṃ nātha satyamārgopadeśanāṃ । tadāryasatyasaṃprāpta āryamārgaṃ labhāmy ahaṃ ।। adya me saphalaṃ janma buddhaputro asmi sāṃprataṃ ।
ity uktvā sa munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvā prābhyanaṃdata ।। tataḥ sa nāvikas tatra triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । satkṛtya samupāśritya prābhajan sarvadā mudā ।। tat samīkṣya paraś cāpi nāviko atyanutāpitaḥ । tatra tasya munīndrasya satkāraṃ kartum aichata ।।
tataḥ sa nāvikas tatra samutthāyānumoditaḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ praṇatvaiva saṃprabodhayat kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। bhagavan yan mayā lobhapraluptadharmacetasā । tarapaṇyaṃ vinā gaṃgāṃ tārito na bhavān api ।।
tan mahān aparādho me bhavaty atrāhi jāyate । tat kṣamatāṃ jagannātha kṣamāratnākaro bhavān ।। yac cātra bhavatāṃ pūjāṃ kartum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ । tān mamānugrahaṃ kṛtvā pratigrahītum arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sa bhagavān muniḥ । tatheti pratimoditvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tathādhivāśitaṃ śāstrā nāvikaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । sa pūjābhojyasāmāgrīm sahasā samasādhaya ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavaṃtaṃ taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ yathākramaṃ । abhyarcya surasaiḥ śuddhair bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve saṃbuddhapramukhā api । tad bhojyaṃ surasaṃ bhuktvā samātṛptiṃ samāyayuḥ ।।
tataḥ sa nāviko dṛṣṭvā tṛptaṃ muniṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । apanīyāśu pātrāṇi tad dhastādi vyaśodhayat ।। tataḥ pūgādi tāṃbūlamahauṣadharasāyanaṃ । datvā sa nāvikas tatra sāṃjaliḥ prārthayat kṣamāṃ ।।
tataḥ sa sāṃjalir natvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । bodhicittaṃ samālamvya tat puraḥ samupāśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya nāvikasya manogataṃ । bodhyabhilāṣam ālokya tadā smitaṃ vyamuṃcata ।।
tatas tasya munīṃdrasya nānāvarṇā marīcayaḥ । mukhapadmād viniryātāḥ praserur bhuvanatraye ।। yā adhastād gatās tatra narakeṣu samaṃtataḥ । tāḥ saumyā raśmayaḥ sarvāḥ prasṛtya samahāsayan ।।
tatra tābhiḥ parispṛṣṭāḥ sarve te narakāśritāḥ । mahat saukhyaṃ samāsādya vismitā evam abruvan ।। aho citraṃ mahat saukhyam adhunā jāyate kathaṃ । kutaś ceyaṃ prabhā jātā kasya ceha samāgatāḥ ।।
yat prabhābhiḥ parispṛṣṭā vayaṃ saukhyasamanvitāḥ । sarve duḥkhābhinirmuktās tad idaṃ mahad adbhutaṃ ।। kiṃ nu cyutā ito aho svid anyatropagatā vayaṃ । yan no duḥkhāni śāṃyaṃte jāyaṃte sasukhāny api ।।
iti ciṃtāsamākrāntahṛdayās te savismayāḥ । ṣarve apy ekatra saṃmīlya bhāṣaṃta upatasthire ।। evaṃ sarve api te satvāḥ sarvatra narakeṣv api । nirduḥkhā sukhasaṃpannā upatasthuḥ savismayāḥ ।।
tadā teṣāṃ prabodhārthaṃ nirmāya bhagavān muniṃ । pratyekaṃ narākeṣv evaṃ sarvatrāpi vyasarjayat ।। taṃ buddhaṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sārve te narakāśritāḥ । bhūyo ativismayākrāṃtahṛdayāś caivaṃ abruvan ।। na hy evetac cyutās sarve nāpy ānyatra gatā vayaṃ ।
ihaiva narake sthāne sthitāḥ sarve vayaṃ khalu ।। yad ihāyaṃ samāyātaḥ puruṣo pūrvadarśanaḥ । nūnaṃ asya prabhākāntir iyam atrābhiprasṛtā ।। tad asmākaṃ hi duḥkhāni praśāntāṃ samaṃtataḥ ।
mahatsaukhyāni jayante nūnam asyānūbhāvataḥ ।। ayaṃ hi sugato buddhaḥ sarvasatvānukaṃpakaḥ । sarvān no duḥkhitān dṛṣṭvā samuddhartum ihāgataḥ ।। tad asya śaraṇaṃ gatvā vayaṃ sarve samādarāt ।
satkṛtya śraddhayā natvā yathāśakti bhajemahi ।। iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve nārakīyās tathā mudā । sahasā taṃ purogatvā praṇatvaivaṃ vabhāṣire ।। namas te bhagavan nātha śaraṇaṃ te vrajāmahe ।
evam asmān sadā dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā trātum arhasi ।। iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā sarve te pratimoditāḥ । tasyaiva śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire samāhitāḥ ।। etatpuṇyaparītās te sarve vimuktapāpakāḥ ।
narakebhyaḥ samutthāya sahasā sadgatiṃ yayuḥ ।। evaṃ tā rasmayaḥ sarvā narakebhyaḥ samaṃtataḥ । sarvān satvān saṃuddhṛtya pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ ।। yāś cāpy urddhagatābhāsaprasṛtāḥ tāḥ samaṃtataḥ ।
avabhāsya diśaḥ sarvān samahārājikālayāḥ ।। sarvān devālayān yāvad akaniṣṭhaṃ bhavālayaṃ । avabhāsyamarān sarvān gāthābhiḥ samacodayat ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāre sarvaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ ।
iti matvātra saṃsāre carata sarvadā śubhe ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane । dhunīta mṛtyusainyāni naḍāgāram iva dvipaḥ ।। yo hy asmin saugate dharme cariṣyati samāhitaḥ ।
sa hitvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। iti tac chabdam ākarṇya sarve devāḥ prabodhitāḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire samāhitāḥ ।। evaṃ tā rasmayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvān devān samaṃtataḥ ।
codayitvā tatas tatra pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ ।। tatra tā rasmayaḥ sarvā ekībhūtā supiṇḍitāḥ । muneḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhrumadhye antarhito abhavat ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokāś cānye api vismitāḥ ।
śāstā kim ādiśed dhārmam iti dhyātvā niṣedire ।। tadānaṃdaḥ samutthāya śāstāraṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā paprachaivaṃ puraḥ sthitaḥ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavadvaktrāt sudhākarāt ।
nānā varṇāḥ prabhāḥ kāṃtā viniḥsṛtya prasāritāḥ ।। sarvāṃs traidhātukānn avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ । punaḥ pratyāgātāḥ sarvā ekībhūtā supiṃḍitā ।। tava pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhrumadhye pravisaṃti tāḥ ।
nāhetupratyaye buddhā darśayanti smitaṃ kvacit ।। tad bhavān hetunā kena smitaṃ muṃcasi sāṃprataṃ । yad dṛṣṭvā sāṃghikaḥ sarve ime lokāś ca vismitāḥ ।। śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti saṃdigdhamānasāḥ ।
kutūhalasamākrāṃtahṛdayāḥ sadguṇārthinaḥ ।। tvatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum ichanti tṛṣitā iva । yadarthe atra bhavān smitaṃ darśayati sarasmikaṃ ।। tadarthaṃ samupādiśya sarvāl lokān prabodhaya ।
ity ānaṃdavaca śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tam ānaṃdaṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। evam etat tathānaṃda nāhetupratyayaṃ kvacit । saṃbuddhāḥ sugatāḥ sarve pravikurvanti saṃsmitaṃ ।।
yadarthe aham ihānaṃda smitaṃ muṃcāmi sāṃprataṃ । tadarthaṃ samupākhyāmi śṛṇuta yūyam ādarāt ।। yad anena satānaṃda nāvikena prasādinā । sasaṃgho ahaṃ samabhyarcya vaṃdito bodhicetāsā ।।
anena kuśalenāyaṃ nāviko api bhaviṣyati । saṃsārottaraṇo nāma pratyekabuddha ātmavit ।। evaṃ matvā mahatpuṇyaṃ triratnaṃ satkṛtodbhavaṃ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt ।।
triratneṣu kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana । vratapuṇyavipākena saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā triratnaṃ sarvadābhajet ।।
evaṃ śāstrā munīndreṇa vyākṛtam ātmanas tadā । śrutvā sa nāviko buddhaḥ prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ ।। tadārabhya sadā nityaṃ nāvikaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā satkṛtya śraddhayābhajat ।।
sarve lokāś ca tad dṛṣṭvā saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ prābhajan mudā ।। tataś ca sa jagacchāstā bhagavān saha sāṃghikaiḥ । tathānyatra śubhaṃ kartuṃ pratasthe sāṃprabhāsayan ।।
iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ mayā pracakṣyate tava । tathātra tvaṃ mahārāja triratnaṃ sarvadā bhaja ।। prajāś cāpi tathā dharme bodhayitvā prasādayan । bodhimārge pratisthāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā ye prasannāḥ ।
te sarve śuddhabhāvā jinaguṇarūcano bodhicaryā carante । bhuktvā saukhyāni nityaṃ munivaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodaṃ ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā prārthayac caivam ādarāt ।।
bhadaṃta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhan sudhīr yatiḥ । tam aśokam mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me gurubhāṣitaṃ । tathāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tava puṇyavivṛddhaye ।। puraikasmin dine tatra rājagṛhe sasāṃghikaḥ । bhagavān sa jagannāthaḥ piṇḍārthaṃ samupāviśat ।।
tadā rājagṛhe tatra gṛhapateḥ suto mahān । tasyaikā dāsikā bhadrā satyadharmānucāriṇī ।। sā svāmyaṅgānulepārthaṃ lohitacaṃdanaṃ tadā । surabhigaṇasaṃyuktaṃ pipeṣa prastare mudā ।।
tasminn eva kṣaṇe tatra sa saṃbuddhaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । bhāsayaṃ maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā tad gṛhaṃ nikaṣācarat ।। tathāyātaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ śrutvā sā dārikā mudā । sahasā nirgatā gehāt tatra draṣṭum upācaran ।।
tatra sā samupāgatya prādrākṣīt taṃ munīśvaraṃ । dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaparibhūṣitaṃ ।। śatasūryādhikābhāsaṃ śatacaṃdrāmṛtaprabhaṃ । vyāmaprabhāsamujvālaṃ ratnāṃgam iva jaṃgamaṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā sā dāsikā tatra muditā vismayānvitā । suciraṃ taṃ samālokya tasthau niścalamānasī ।। tatra sā suciraṃ dṛṣṭvā dāsikābhipramoditā । satkāraṃ karttum ichantī śāstur evaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
aho bhāgyaṃ munīndro ayaṃ dṛśyate yan mayādhunā । tad asya kiṃ bhajiṣyāmi daridrā preṣikā hy ahaṃ ।। kutra vā drakṣyate bhūyo munīndro ayaṃ jagadguruḥ । dhig me janmāpi yenātra kiṃ cit puṇyaṃ na sādhyate ।।
kiṃ mamānena dehena yenedṛśaṃ munīśvaraṃ । prāpya kiṃ cit pradatvāpi puṇyaṃ prāptuṃ na śakyate ।। anena jīvitenāpi kiṃ mamātra prayojanaṃ । yena duḥkhāni bhuktvaiva kiṃ cit puṇyaṃ na sādhyate ।।
puṇyaṃ vinātra saṃsāre saukhyaṃ prāptuṃ kathaṃ kuha । tat puṇyaṃ prāpyate kena vinā dānavrataḥ kvacit ।। kiṃ cātra dāsyate dānaṃ kiṃ cid dravyaṃ na me gṛhe । vrataṃ vā kiṃ kariṣyāmi parādhīnā hi dāsikā ।।
tad atra kiṃ sukhaṃ lapsye kiṃ cid dānaṃ vrataṃ vinā । sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭā syāṃ ko māṃ rakṣed bhavāntare ।। puṇyena sadgatiṃ yāyāṃ pāpena durgatiṃ sadā । iti hetoḥ prakarttavyaṃ dānaṃ kiṃ cid api vrataṃ ।।
tarhy etad vidyate haste lohitacaṃdanaṃ mama । etenāpi munīndrasya bhajeyaṃ caraṇāmbujau ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya darikā sā prasāditā । sahasā svagṛhaṃ gatvā tac caṃdanaṃ samāgrahīt ।।
tac caṃdanaṃ samādāya dāsikā sā vyacintayat । yad idaṃ svāmino dravyaṃ tad anujñāṃ vinā kathaṃ ।। yadi svāmi vijānāti tadā me kupito ruṣā । nirbhatsya tāḍayitvā māṃ gṛhān niṣkāsayed apl ।।
tadātra kiṃ cariṣyāmi dāsikāham nirāśrayā । avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavanti mahatām api ।। yadi me kupitaḥ svāmī paratra kiṃ kariṣyati । prasanno yadi vā svāmī kalyāṇaṃ syād ihāpi me ।।
kupito va prasanno vā bhavatv atraiva me prabhuḥ । svāmī bharttānuśāstaiva paratra kiṃ kariṣyati ।। buddhas tu jagatāṃ svāmī bharttā nātho anukaṃpakaḥ । prabhu dharmānuśāstā me paratrehāpy avet sadā ।।
tad atra kiṃ mamānena svāmināpi kariṣyate । tad etac caṃdanenāpi bhajeyaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya dāsikā sā pramoditā । lohitacaṃdanenobhau pāṇau pralipya setvayā ।।
gṛhād vahir vinirgatvā bhagavate anta upāgatā । pādayor ubhayos tena caṃdanena lilepa sā ।। tataḥ sā dārikā nārī kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । pādau tasya muner natvā purataḥ samupāśrayat ।।
tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasyā bhaktirataṃ manaḥ । tac caṃdanasaurabhyais tat puraṃ samapūrayat ।। tatas tad gaṃdham āghrāya sarve paurāḥ savismayāḥ । kasyedaṃ gaṃdham āyātam iti proktvā pracerire ।।
tatas tad vṛttim ājñāya sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ । tad draṣṭuṃ sahasā tatra bhagavato antikam upāyayuḥ ।। tatra sarve api te lokā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samupatasthur ādarāt ।।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tad dhārmadeśanāṃ śrutvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitaḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā sadā bhajitum īchire ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā dāsikā sā prabodhitā । sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tathā ।। etatpuṇyavipākena saṃsāre atra punarbhave । pratyekāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvāṇapadam āpnuyāṃ ।। evaṃ buddhapadaṃ prāptyai praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tayā ।
dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāṃs tatra smitaṃ prādurvyadhāt tadā ।। tatas tasya muner vaktrān nānāvarṇāḥ surasmayaḥ । vinirgatā diśaḥ sarvā bhāsayantaḥ praserire ।। yā adhastād gatābhāsāḥ sarvatra narakeṣv api ।
avabhāsya śubhaṃ kṛtvā sarvatra saṃprasaṃsire ।। tatra satvān parispṛśya kṛtvā sarvān sukhānvitān । saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ datvā saṃpreṣayan surālāyaṃ ।। yāś cāpy urddhaṃ gatābhāsatāḥ sarvāṃś ca surālayan ।
avabhāsyāmarān sarvān samudghuṣyābhyacodayan ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ sarvaṃ śūnyaṃ nirātmakaṃ । iti matvātra karttavyaṃ saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ sadā ।। niṣkrāmata rabhadhvaṃ tat saddharmaṃ buddhaśāsane ।
māracaryāṃ parityajya carata bhadracārikāṃ ।। yo apramattaś caraty atra saṃbuddhaśāsane vrataṃ । sa vihāya punarjātiṃ duḥkhasyāṃtaṃ kariṣyati ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ ।
triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajadhvaṃ śraddhayā sadā ।। etad ghoṣaṃ samākarṇya sarve devāḥ pramoditāḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prācaran sarvadā śubhe ।। tatas te raśmayaḥ sarve bhāsayantaḥ samaṃtataḥ ।
pratyāgatā munīndrasya purataḥ samupāśrayan ।। tatra te raśmayaḥ sarve apy ekībhūtāḥ supiṇḍitāḥ । śāstuḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhruvo antare tirodadhau ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhāsīnāḥ sarve lokāḥ savismayāḥ ।
śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti dhyātvā samāśrayan ।। tatrānaṃdaḥ samālokya sarvāṃl lokān savismayān । sāṃjalis taṃ jagannāthaṃ praṇatvaivaṃ samabravīt ।। bhagavan hetunā kena smitaṃ muṃcati sāṃprataṃ ।
nāhetupratyayaṃ buddhāḥ smitaṃ muṃcaṃti sarvadā ।। yad bhavataḥ smite vaktrān nānāvarṇāḥ suraśmayaḥ । nirgatāḥ sarvalokeṣu prasṛtā avabhāsyata ।। ime sarvatra bhadrāṇi kṛtvā satvāṃś ca bhadritān ।
pratyāgatā bhavadurṇāmadhye cāntardadhanti hi ।। etad adbhutam ālokya sarve lokā ime adhunā । śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti dhyātvā samāsthitāḥ ।। bhavaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve saddharmavāṃchinaḥ ।
bhavantam eva saṃvīkṣya saṃtiṣṭhante samāhitāḥ ।। bhagavaṃs tad yad arthe tvaṃ smitaṃ muṃcasi sāṃprataṃ । tad arthaṃ samupādiśya sarvāl lokān prabodhaya ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīścaraḥ ।
tam ānaṃdaṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। evam etan mahānaṃda sarve api sugatā jināḥ । nāhetupratyayaṃ kvāpi smitaṃ muṃcaṃti sarvadā ।। yadarthe aham ihānaṃda smitaṃ muṃcāmi sāṃprataṃ ।
tadarthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarve śṛṇvaṃtu sādaraṃ ।। paśyānaṃdānayā nāryyā dārikayā mama padoḥ । lohitacaṃdanenaivaṃ pralipya satkṛtiḥ kṛtā ।। etatpuṇyavipākena dārikeyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
pratyekasugato gandhamādano nāma sarvavit ।। yatheyaṃ mayi saṃbuddhacittaṃ prasādya moditā । praṇidhānaṃ karoty evaṃ pratyekabodhim āpsyati ।। evaṃ matvā mahatpuṇyaṃ saṃbuddhabhajanodbhavaṃ ।
satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ bhajam ādarāt ।। triratnabhajanodbhūtaṃ puṇyamahattaraṃ bahu । yathechābodhisaṃbhārapūraṇaṃ nirvṛtiṃ pradaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve anumoditāḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kartuṃ prābhyanandan sadāpi te ।। tadā sā dāsikāpy evaṃ śāstrā vyākṛtam ātmanaḥ । śrutvābhinaṃditā bhūyo nanāma taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। tataḥ sā svāminā dattaṃ dravyam ādāya satvarā ।
tad arhabhojanaiḥ pūrṇaṃ pātraṃ kṛtvā mudācarat ।। tatra sā muditā tasmai munīndrāya pradāpayat । sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā svagehaṃ samupācarat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān pṛṣṭe piṇḍapātraṃ tayārcitaṃ ।
sasaṃghaṃ svāśrame gatvā vyaharad dharmam ādiśat ।। tatra sā dāsikā bhadrā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prābhajan sarvadā mudā ।। evaṃ me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayātra kathyate ।
tathā tvam api rājeṃdra triratnaṃ sarvadā bhaja ।। tathā rājaṃ prajāś cāpi bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। tathā taṃ maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। idaṃ narā ye ci ca gaṃdhamādanāvadānam atra prathitaṃ prasāditāḥ । śṛṇvanti ye cāpi niśāmayanti sarve sukhāḍhyāḥ pracaranti sadgatau ।
athāśoko mahārājaḥ sāṃjaliḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhaṃ mahāmatiḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taiḥ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā buddhānumodaya ।।
purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhiś ca cailakaiḥ । upāsakaiḥ śubhācārair upāsikāgaṇair api ।।
bodhisatvair mahāsatvaiḥ saṃbodhicārikodyamaiḥ । tathānyais tīrthikaiś cāpi saṃbuddhaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ ।। rājagṛhapuropānte veṇuvane manorame । jināśrame mahodyāne karaṃdakanivāpake ।।
sarvasatvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan । saddharmadeśanāṃ kurvan vijahāra virocayan ।। tat saddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ tatra sarve samāgatāḥ । devā daityāś ca nāgendrā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।।
grahā vidyādharāḥ siddhā lokapālagaṇā api । ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāś cāpi rājānaḥ kṣatriyātmajāḥ ।। vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo amātyā gṛhādhipā mahājanāḥ । paurikāḥ sārthavāhāś ca vaṇijaḥ śilpino api ca ।।
grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathā kārpaṭikādayaḥ । sarve te samupāyātās tatrāśrame upāviśan ।। tatra sabhāsanāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । vyāmaprabhāvirocaṃ taṃ bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ puraskṛtaṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā te muditāḥ sarve praṇatvā samupāgatāḥ । kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāny enaṃ samānarcu yathākramaṃ ।। tatas sarve api te lokāḥ parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupāśṛtān । āryyasatyaṃ samārgāṃgaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśan ।। tāt saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃprabodhitāḥ । dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya bodhicaryāṃ samīchire ।। tadaikasmin dine bhikṣur āyuṣmān nāradābhidhaḥ ।
bhikṣārthaṃ pātram ādāya rājagṛhapure yayau ।। tatra sa nārado bhikṣuḥ piṃḍārthaṃ samupācaran । gṛhasthena samālokya nītvā gehe mudāsane ।। pratisthāpya samabhyarcya supraṇītarasānvitaiḥ ।
tīlodanaiḥ sudhākalpaiḥ pānaiś ca pratipūjitaḥ ।। tad bhuktvā sa yatis tuṣṭo datvā tasmai śubhāśiṣaṃ । samutthāya tato araṇye viharttuṃ nirjane acarat ।। tatra sa nārado yogī gṛdhrakūṭanagāntike ।
dadarśa pretikām ekāṃ rākṣasīm iva bhīṣaṇāṃ ।। vṛkṣamūle sthitāṃ raktavinduvyāptāmvarāvṛtāṃ । asthiśakalasaṃkīrṇe pretālaye nivāsinīṃ ।। svātmajān api bhakṣantīṃ kṣutpipāsāgnidāhināṃ ।
kṛśāṅgīṃ vikṛtākārāṃ karvuramuktakeśinīṃ ।। dṛṣṭvā sa nāradas tatra samupāsṛtya tat puraḥ । pretikāṃ tāṃ samālokya paprachaivaṃ purākṛtaṃ ।। kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ ghoraṃ pātakaṃ pūrvajanmasu ।
yenaivaṃ duḥsaham anubhavasi sāṃprataṃ ।। iti tenārhatā pṛṣṭe pretikā sā rudanty api । nāradaṃ taṃ yatiṃ dṛṣṭvā śanair evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta kiṃ mayā hy atra vakṣyate yat purākṛtaṃ ।
divārātrau paṃcaputrān prasūtā me prabhakṣitā ।। tenāpi na saṃtuṣṭā bubhukṣitā pravarddhate । tad bhavāṃs taṃ jagadvijñaṃ pṛchatā matpurākṛtaṃ ।। sa munīndro jagacchāstādiśet te asmatpurākṛtaṃ ।
āditye hi samudyāte dīpena kiṃ prayojanaṃ ।। tathāsmatprakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutvānyena narādayaḥ । satvāḥ saṃtrasitā evaṃ kuryu na ke cana ।। sarve te api diśet pāpān viramya śīlasaṃvṛtāḥ ।
triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhajeyuḥ sadādritāḥ ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā nāradaḥ sa prabodhitaḥ । tatheti sahasā gatvā tatra veṇuvane asarat ।। tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra dhyānālayāt samutthitaḥ ।
sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tasminn avasare tatra nāradaḥ satvarānvitaḥ । dūrāt taṃ śrīghanaṃ paśyan sahasā samupācaran ।। tam eva samupāyātaṃ nāradaṃ sa munīśvaraḥ ।
dṛṣṭvārāt samupāmaṃtrya punar evam abhāṣata ।। ehi te svāgataṃ bhikṣo kutas tvaṃ samupāgataḥ । kim artham iha yenaivaṃ prāyāsi tad vadasva me ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa nāradaḥ sa kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।
samupetya munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat ।। bhagavan bhavatāṃ pādau draṣṭum iha samācare । adyāhaṃ nirjane araṇye vihartuṃ samupācare ।। tatrāhaṃ pretikām ekāṃ rākṣasīm iva bhīṣaṇāṃ ।
kṛśāṅgīṃ vikṛtākārāṃ raktavindu'nvitāṃvarāṃ ।। anekā asthiṣaṃkīrṇe pretālaye iva sthitāṃ । paśyāmi tām upāsṛtya paripṛchāmi tat kṛtaṃ ।। kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ pūrvajanmasu dāruṇaṃ ।
yenedṛg mahāduḥkham anubhavasi sāṃprataṃ ।। iti pṛṣṭe mayāthāsau pretikā duḥkhatāpinī । rudantī māṃ samālokya śanair evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta kiṃ vadiṣyāmi yan mayā pātakaṃ kṛtaṃ ।
yenedṛśaṃ mahāduḥkham anubhavāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। paṃcaputrān ahaṃ rātrau divā paṃca tathāparān । prasūya tāṃ prabhakṣyāmi nāsti tṛptis tathāpi me ।। evaṃ kṣutpipāsāgnitīvratāpābhidāhitā ।
divārātriṃ mahadduḥkhaṃ bhuktvā tiṣṭhāmi jaṃgale ।। tat purā kiṃ kṛtaṃ ghoraṃ pātakam atidāruṇaṃ । mayāpi jñāyate nātra paripṛcha munīśvaraṃ ।। sarvajñas trijagacchāstā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat sarvam samupāviśet ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā tatheti paribodhitaḥ । bhavantam atra saṃpraṣṭuṃ samāgachāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। kiṃ tayā prakṛtaṃ ghoraṃ pātakam atidāruṇaṃ ।
yenaivaṃ duḥsahaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhuktvā carati sādhunā ।। tat sarvaṃ samupādiśya prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । nāradaṃ taṃ mahābhijñaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśet ।।
nārada pretikā sātitīvrapātakasādhinī । yadīcches tat kṛtaṃ śroṭuṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te adhunā ।। tadyathābhūt purā puryyāṃ vārāṇasyāṃ mahājanaḥ । śreṣṭhī prāḍhyo mahacchrīmāc chrīdopamo dhanādhipaḥ ।।
sa kuladharmiṇīṃ bhāryām upayeme yathāvidhiṃ । tataḥ sa kāṃtayā sārddhaṃ tayā reme pramodayan ।। tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya krīḍataḥ sucirād api । tasyām eko api putro vā putrī vā nābhyajāyata ।।
tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī santatidarśanotsukaḥ । tan nirāśābhisaṃtaptamūrchito abhūd yathāturaḥ ।। kapolaṃ svabhuje sthāpya śokāgāre vyavasthitaḥ । saṃpaccintāviṣaṇṇāsyo manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
hā daiva kiṃ mayā pāpaṃ sukṛtaṃ duḥkṛtaṃ purā । yan mamaivaṃ vidhaṃ duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ cātra prajāyate ।। anekadravyasaṃpattisamuditaṃ gṛhaṃ mama । tatra bhoktā tu naiko api putro asti duhitāpi na ।। tat sarvaṃ svāpateyaṃ hi mamātyayān narādhipaḥ ।
aputrakam iti kṛtvā sarvasvaṃ sarvathā haret ।। yan mayānekayatnena sādhitaṃ rakṣitaṃ ca tat । sarvam eva nirarthena vinaṣṭaṃ me bhaviṣyati ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yasyopāyaṃ na manyate ।
sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo asmi ko māṃ rakṣed ihādhunā ।। evaṃ cintāviṣaṇṇāsyaṃ svāminaṃ taṃ gṛhādhipaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sā ramaṇī bhāryā samālokyaivam abravīt ।। svāminn atra kim eva tvaṃ tiṣṭhase duḥkhacintayā ।
kiṃ tava jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad vadasva mamāgrataḥ ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhastho viniśvasan । taṃ bhāryāṃ ramaṇīkāntāṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। priye atra kiṃ vadiṣyāmi yasyopāyaṃ na manyate ।
yan me asti mahatī saṃpad asyā bhoktā na vidyate ।। nūnaṃ madatyayād rājā mamaitāḥ sarvasaṃpadaḥ । aputrasya nṛpādhīnā iti kṛtvā hariṣyati ।। yan mamaitā mahāyatnaiḥ sādhitā vanditā api ।
tat sarvaṃ hi nirarthena vinakṣyati niratyayāt ।। etan me jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad atra kiṃ vadeya hi । ko mamaitan mahac chalyaṃ hṛdaye atra samuddharet ।। iti cintāviṣaṇṇātra hṛdayaṃ dahyate mama ।
tenaivam atra tiṣṭhāmi viṣadagdho yathāturaḥ ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryā ramaṇī priyā । svāminaṃ taṃ samālokya bodhayituṃ samabravīt ।। etadarthe viṣādatvaṃ mā kṛthāḥ sarvathā priye ।
upāyāṃ kuru tat prāptyai yadi saṃtatim ichasi ।। upāyam api siddhyeta devatānāṃ prasādataḥ । tad devatāḥ samārādhya yācasva santatiṃ mudā ।। tadā devaprasādena jayen nau santatiḥ khalu ।
putro vā yadi vā putrī jātā syāt saphalaṃ bhave ।। iti me vacanam śrutvā kulasthitiṃ yadīchasi । devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā bhajasva saṃtatīchayā ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ prabodhitaḥ ।
tathety abhyanumoditvā tathā karttuṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī bhāryayā saha moditaḥ । svakuleśaṃ samabhyarcya santānaṃ samayāca tat ।। tathāpi śreṣṭhinas tasya bhāryābhūn naiva garbhiṇī ।
tataḥ sa parikhinnātmā tasthāv evaṃ nirāśayā ।। tataḥ sā ramaṇī bhāryā nirāśākhinnamānasaṃ । svāminaṃ taṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।। svāmin mātra viṣādatvaṃ kṛthā dhairyaṃ samāśraya ।
viṣādo klīyate cittaṃ kṣīṇadtto na vīryabhāk ।। vīryaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ cit kāryaṃ na siddhyate । tasmād vīryaṃ samālambya bhaja devān samāhitaḥ ।। yadi putro na jātāḥ syāt putrī vāpi na jāyate ।
puṇyaṃ tu varddhyate nūnaṃ devatārādhanād api ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre sadā saukhyaṃ yadīchasi । sarvān devān samabhyarcya bhajasvā śraddhayādarāt ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā bharttā śreṣṭhī sa bodhitaḥ ।
tatheti pratibhāṣitvā devān arcitum aichata ।। tathā santānam ichen sa gṛhastho bharyyayā mudā । vidhiṃ sraṣṭāram ārādhya saṃtatiṃ samayācata ।। tathāpi tasya bhāryā sā garbhiṇī no abhavac ciraṃ ।
tataś ca sa vibhagnāśas tasthau śokaviṣāditaḥ ।। taṭo api bhāryayā bhūyaḥ preryyamāṇaḥ sa bodhitaḥ । viśvaṃbharaṃ samabhyarcya yayāca saṃtatiṃ tathā ।। tathāpi sābhavan naiva dohadalakṣaṇāṅkitā ।
tataś cāsau gṛhastho abhūn nirāśāparikheditaḥ ।। tathā sa bhāryayā bhūyaḥ preritaḥ paribodhitaḥ । maheśvaraṃ samabhyarcya saṃtatiṃ samayācata ।। tathendraṃ ca samārādhya prārthayat saṃtatiṃ mudā ।
evaṃ lokādhipān sarvān grahān sarvān ahūr api । samārādhya samabhyarcya prārthayat santatiṃ tathā ।। tataś caivaṃ mahākālaṃ kumāraṃ ca gaṇādhipaṃ । bhairavaṃ mātṛkāś cāpi prārthayad vaṃśam arcayan ।।
evam anyān api devān vihāramaṇḍapāśrayān । maṭhasatrāśramārāmaśṛṃgāṭakapratiṣṭhitān ।। udyānaparvatāraṇyākṣatrasīmādisaṃsthitān । sarvajalāśrayasthāṃś ca sarvān nāgādhipān api ।।
rathyācatvaramārgādipratisthitān samutsukaḥ । sarvān devān samārādhya yayācaivaṃ sa saṃtatiṃ ।। tathāpi śreṣṭhinas tasya bhāryāyāṃ sucīrād api । tasyāṃ naivābhavat kiṃ cid dohadotpattilakṣaṇaṃ ।।
tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī dṛṣṭvā vaṃśanirantaraṃ । nirāśāpratikhinnātmā tasthāv evaṃ yathāturaḥ ।। etad duḥkhavibhinnāsyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā ramaṇī priyā । svāminaṃ taṃ samīkṣantī punar evam abhāṣata ।।
svāminn atra viṣādena kiṃ cit kāryaṃ na siddhyate । iti matvā yathākāmaṃ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā samācara ।। yad āvābhyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat phalaṃ bhujyate adhunā । tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo daivaṃ hi valavān bhave ।।
yad abhāvi bhaven naiva bhāvi cen nānyathā kvacit । avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavanti sarvathā bhave ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre bhuktvā saukhyaṃ yathechayā । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara satyaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।
tehaiva sarvadā bhadram ihāmutrāpi sarvataḥ । kramād bodhipadaṃ prāpya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpsyati ।। iti bhāryāsamākhyātaṃ śrutvā śreṣṭhī sa bodhitaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā kañcit kālaṃ vyalaṃghayat ।।
tatas tasya suhṛn mitram upāgatya puraḥ sthitaḥ । tat saṃtānasamutpatyai tan mitram evam abravīt ।। bho mitra śṛṇu me vākyaṃ yat te hitaṃ mayocyate । sarvathāsyāṃ priyāyāṃ te saṃtānaṃ vidyate na hi ।।
tad upāyaṃ tu karttavyaṃ saṃtatiṃ pratipattaye । nirvaṃśasya hi saṃsāre nirarthaṃ sarvasādhanaṃ ।। tat saṃtānasamutpatyai dvitīyaṃ putrabhāvinīṃ । aparāṃ yuvatīṃ bhāryāṃ vivaha vidhinā punaḥ ।।
kadā cit tava bhāgyena sā putraṃ janayed api । tadā te saphalaṃ janmaḥ kulasthitir bhaved api ।। iti mitroditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ prabodhitaḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya taṃ mitram abhyamānayat ।।
tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī nirīkṣya putrabhāvinīṃ । aparāṃ yuvatīṃ kāṃtām upayeme yathāvidhiḥ ।। tataḥ sa kulikaḥ śreṣṭhī tayā sārddhaṃ pramoditaḥ । yathākāmaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā rarāma paricārayan ।।
tatas tasya gṛhasthasya yathākāmaṃ prabhuṃjataḥ । samaye sā priyā bhāryā vabhūva garbhiṇī acirāt ।। tataḥ kramāt pravṛddho abhūd garbhas tasyā dine dine । tadā sā garbhasaṃjātaṃ parijñāyābhyanandata ।।
tataḥ sā bhadrikā kāntā svāminaṃ taṃ pramoditā । rahasi samupāmaṃtrya samālokyaivam abravīt ।। diṣṭyāryyaputra vṛddho asi garbhe me jāyate śiśuḥ । dakṣiṇapārśvasaṃsthāyat tad ayaṃ dārako bhavet ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhastho abhinaṃditaḥ । savyavāhuṃ samutsārya mudaivaṃ samudāharat ।। hā me abhilaṣitaṃ siddhyet paśyeyaṃ saṃtater mukhaṃ । sāṃprataṃ nāvajāto asmi kulasthitir bhaved api ।।
kṛtyāni me prakurvīta vibhṛyāc ca bhṛtaḥ prati । dāyādyaṃ pratipadyeta vaṃśo pi syāc cirasthitaḥ ।। yan mayā prakṛtaṃ dānaṃ yac ca puṇyaṃ prasādhitaṃ । etad vipākakauśalyam etayor anugachatu ।।
evaṃ sa muditaḥ śreṣṭhī tāṃ bhāryāṃ bhadrikāṃ priyāṃ । supathyopacārasaṃyuktair āhāraiḥ samapoṣayat ।। dūṣyaiś cīnāṃśukaiḥ paṭṭaiḥ komalais saurabhānvitaiḥ । nānāratnābhyalaṃkārair maṇḍayitvābhyamodayat ।।
evaṃ tāṃ bhadrikāṃ kāntāṃ pathyopacārabhūṣaṇaiḥ । poṣitāṃ maṇḍitāṃ kṛtvā prāmāṇayat prasādayan ।। evaṃ tāṃ garbhiṇīṃ bhartur bahumānābhinaṃditāṃ । dṛṣṭvā sā prathamā bhāryā bhūya evaṃ vyaciṃtāyat ।।
yady eṣā yuvatī kāṃtā janayed atisaṃtatiṃ । tad etat sarvasaṃpattir adhīnāsyā bhaved api ।। eṣaiva hi pradhānā syāt sarvalokapramāṇikā । ko api pramāṇayen naiva jaratīṃ mām aputritāṃ ।।
tad atrāsyāḥ sapatnyā me yathā syād garbhaśātanaṃ । tathopāyaṃ prakarttavyaṃ suguptena mayādhunā ।। kāmarāgāgnitaptasya nāsti kiṃ cid dhi pātakaṃ । sarvam api prakarttavyaṃ bhoktavyaṃ sarvato api ca ।।
tataḥ sā pramadā duṣṭā tasyā garbhābhiśātanaṃ । drayaṃ pānābhisaṃyuktaṃ dadau viśrambhavādinī ।। tat sapatnyārpitaṃ pānaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā bhadrikārjavā । hastābhyāṃ sahasādāya papau tṛṣṇārditā yathā ।।
tad etat pītamātreṇa tasyā garbho vighūrṇitaḥ । sahasābhidravībhūtaḥ prasaśrāvābhyaśoṣataḥ ।। tataḥ sā bhadrikā nārī bharttāraṃ taṃ sabāṃdhavaṃ । sahasā samupāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ nyavedayat ।।
svāmiṃs tavānayā patnyā priyayā garbhaśātanaṃ । pānam auṣadhasaṃyuktaṃ sādaraṃ me pradīyate ।। tat tad dattaṃ saviśvāsaṃ gṛhītvā pīyate mayā । tatpānapītamātreṇa garbho me srasyate adhunā ।।
tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yato me naśyate śiśuḥ । yad arthaṃ prakṛtaṃ dānaṃ tat sarvaṃ nisphalaṃ tava ।। ity ākhyātaṃ tayā patnyā śrutvā śreṣṭhī sa roṣitaḥ । tāṃ sahasāhūya paribhāṣyaivam ālapat ।।
hā re re durmate duṣṭe ghorapātakasādhinī । evam api mahāghoraṃ pātakaṃ prakṛtaṃ tvayā ।। yadarthe devatāḥ sarvās samārādhyābhiyācitāḥ । nānāvidhānayatnāni prakṛtāni mamāniśaṃ ।।
sarvāṇy etāni yatnāni tvayā vyarthīkṛtāni hi । tad atra kiṃ tvayā patnyā pāpiṣṭhayā vrajādhunā ।। mayā tvaṃ pāpinī tyaktā mā tiṣṭheha gṛhe mama । ity uktaṃ svāminā tena śrutvā sā duritāśayā ।
sajñāteḥ svāminas tasya purar evam abhāṣata ।। kim evaṃ vadase svāmin na mayedaṃ kṛtaṃ khalu । mayā na manyate nūnaṃ tad idaṃ tvaṃ vicāraya ।। yadi dattaṃ mayā dravyam asyā garbhābhiśātanaṃ ।
pretībhūtātmajān putrāñ jātāṃ jātān divāniśaṃ ।। prabhuktvaivaṃ mahadduḥkhe cireyu durgatau sadā । ity evaṃ śapathaṃ kṛtvā svāminaṃ tam abodhayat ।। iti proktaṃ tayā patnyā śrutvā śreṣṭhī sa bodhitaḥ । cirāśāparimuktātmā mṛtā pretālaye yāyau ।।
eṣaiva pretikā śreṣṭhibhāryā durāśayā । svakṛtakarmabhogyāni bhuktvaivaṃ bhramate adhunā ।। yad īrṣyayā tayā tasyāḥ prakṛtaṃ garbhaśātanaṃ । tena sā duṣkṛtākārā pretībhūtā caraty api ।।
yac ca tayā mṛṣāvācā śapathaḥ prakṛtā yathā । tathā tatkarmapākena durgatau bhramate sadā ।। paṃcaputrān divārātriṃ prasūya sā kṣudhānvitā । sarvāṃs tāṃ svātmajān vālān api bhuktvā na tṛpyate ।।
evaṃ sā pāpinī pretī jātāṃ jatāṃs tathātmajān । bhuktvā kṣudhāgnisaṃdagadhā bhramet pretālaye sadā ।। evaṃ nārada vijñāya viramya pātakāt sadā । mṛṣāvādāc ca saddharme caritavyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ ।।
saddharmasya vipāke hi sarvadā maṃgalaṃ bhave । pātakasya sadā duḥkhaṃ viśrite sya tathobhayaṃ ।। iti matvā sadā yūyaṃ triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhajadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ ।।
ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajanti śraddhayā mudā । te sarve durgatiṃ hitvā saṃprayānti jinālaye ।। ye ca śṛṇvanti saddharmaṃ mānayanti ca sādaraṃ । te api kleśān vinirjitya saṃyāṃti saugatālaye ।।
ye saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā satkṛtya prabhajanti te । sarve api durgater muktvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāṃchibhiḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīṃdreṇa śrutvā sa nāradaḥ sudhīḥ । sasaṃghaḥ sarvadā lokāś ca tatheti pratyapadyata ।। tataḥ sa nārado bhikṣuḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ purogataḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ praṇatvā ca papracha tad viśodhanaṃ ।।
bhagavan sā pāpinī pretī tataḥ pretālayāt kadā । tadghorapātakān muktā saṃyāyāt sadgatau kathaṃ ।। tad upāyaṃ jagacchāsta samupādeṣṭum arhati । yenāsau durgāter muktā sahasā sadgatiṃ vrajet ।।
iti saṃprārthite tena nāradena sa sarvavit । bhagavāṃs taṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu nārada tasyās tat pātakapariśodhanaṃ । upāyaṃ samayaṃ cāpi pravakṣyāmy adhunā tathā ।।
yadā lokeśvaro nāthaḥ sarvasatvānukaṃpakaḥ । bodhisatvo mahāsatvas traidhātukādhipeśvaraḥ ।। sukhāvatyā vinirgatya sarvāl lokān prabhāsayan । sarvān satvān samuddhartuṃ pretaloke samācaret ।।
tadā tatprabhayā spṛṣṭā sātisaukhyasamanvitā । kim adya me mahatsaukhyam iti proktvābhyaciṃtayat ।। aho saukhyaṃ samutpannaṃ prabhāveyaṃ prasāritā । nūnam atra mahāsatvaḥ satvān uddhartum āgatāḥ ।।
yasyedṛk satkṛpādṛṣṭiḥ satveṣv evaṃ prasaryyati । tasyaiva śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajeyaṃ sarvadādarāt ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya sā pretī prativismitā । tasyaivā smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhe dṛṣṭaṃ samutsukā ।।
tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra lokanāthaḥ kṛpāmayaḥ । pretalokān samūddhartum upācaret prābhāsayaḥ ।। taṃ prabhāsaṃtam āyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve api pretakāḥ । sahasā samupetyaivaṃ prārthayeyuḥ samādarāt ।।
svāgataṃ bhagavan nātha prasīda parameśvara । kṛpayāsmān samālokya pretalokān samuddhara ।। sarvadā bhavatām eva śaraṇaṃ saṃvrajāmahe । tat kṛtvā pariśuddhān naḥ sarvā preraya sadgatau ।।
iti tat prārthite sarve lokanāthaḥ kṛpānidhiḥ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya punar evam upādiśet ।। yadīchatha sadā saukhyaṃ yūyaṃ sarve samāhitāḥ । triratnaṃ smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajata śraddhayā mudā ।।
tadaitat pātakair muktās sarve yūyaṃ pavitritāḥ । sahasā sadgatiṃ prāptā bhaveta bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ jagacchāstrā lokanāthena tena te । sarve api pretikāḥ śrutvā tathā kartuṃ samīchire ।।
tadā te pretikāḥ sarve pariśuddhāśayā mudā । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā smṛtvā bhajeyur ānatāḥ ।। tadā tatsmṛtipuṇyena sarve te pretikās tataḥ । pretalokāt samutthāya saṃyāsyanti sukhāvatīṃ ।।
tatrāmitābhanāthasya sarve te śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । bhajanto dharmam ākarṇya cariṣyaṃti śubhācariṃ ।। tataḥ sarve api te satvā bodhisatvāḥ śubhaṃkarāḥ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।।
tadā sā pāpinī pretī sarvapāpavimocitā । pretalokāt samutthāya sadgatiṃ samavāpsyati ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sadgatiṃ sukhavāṃchibhiḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe ।।
triratnabhajanodbhūtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇuyāt kvacit । sarvakleśān vinirdahya prāpayet saugataṃ padaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa nārado yatiḥ । sasāṃghikasabhālokas tatheti prābhyanaṃdata ।।
iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ mayātra vakṣyate । matvā rājaṃs tvam apy evaṃ triratnaṃ bhaja sarvadā ।। prajāś cāpi tathā dharmaṃ śrāvāyitvā prabodhayan । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।।
tatas te sarvadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ śivāṃ prāpya saṃbuddhapadaṃ āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśoko narādhipaḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
ye cedaṃ pretikāyāḥ sugatakathitam idaṃ śraddhayā ye avadānaṃ śṛṇvaṃti śrāvayanti pramuditamanasas te narāḥ sarva evaṃ । kṛtvā ratnatrayasya prabhajanam aniśaṃ bodhicittaṃ samāpya kṛtvā lokeṣu bhadraṃ sakalaguṇabharā bauddhaloke prayānti । athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayac ca tathādarāt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā me samupādiśa ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhaṃ sudhīr yatiḥ । nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ saṃpaśyann evam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tava dharmapravṛddhaye ।। tadyathā bhagavāñ chāstā śrīghanaḥ sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugato nātho dharmarāja vināyakaḥ ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhiś ca cailakaiḥ ।
upāsakaiḥ śubhācārair upāsikāgaṇair api ।। bodhisatvair mahāsatvais tathānyair bodhivāṃchibhiḥ । brahmadevāsurendraiś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnaraiḥ ।। siddhair vidyādharaiś cāpi nāgendrai garuḍair api ।
sarvai lokādhipaiś cāpi tathānyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।। brāhmaṇai rājabhi rājakumāraiś ca śubhārthibhiḥ । vaiśyai maṃtrigaṇaiś cāpi tathāmātyagaṇair api ।। śreṣṭhibhiḥ paurikaiś capi gṛhasthaiś ca mahājanaiḥ ।
vaṇigbhiḥ sārthavāhaiś ca tathā śilpigaṇair api ।। grāmyai jānapadaiś cāpi kārpaṭikaiḥ satīrthikaiḥ । tathānyaiḥ sujanai vijñaiḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ ।। sevitābhyarcitas tatra veṇuvane manorame ।
karaṃdakanivāpākhye vihāre saugatāśrame ।। saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra prabhāsayan । sarvasatvahitārthena ratnarāśim ivojvalan ।। tadaiva samaye tatra rājagṛhe purottame ।
āsīd gṛhapate śreṣṭhī mahājano mahādhanaḥ ।। śrimāṃ śrīdopamaḥ sarvadravyasaṃpatsamānvitaḥ । sa sadṛśāt kulā bhāryāṃ svakuladharmacāriṇīṃ ।। subhadrāṃgāṃ samānīya vidhinodavahan mudā ।
tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛt kantā bhāryayā kāṃtayā tathā ।। yathākāmaṃ ratiṃ bhuktvā cakrīḍa paricārayan । tatas tasya gṛhasthasya yathākāmaṃ prabhuṃjataḥ ।। samaye sā priyā bhāryā babhūva garbhadhāriṇī ।।
tataḥ sā samaye asūta dārakaṃ suṃdarāṃśikaṃ । tac chrutvā sa pitā śreṣṭhī mudā draṣṭum upācaran ।। tatra sa samupetyāśu dārakaṃ taṃ śubhāṃśikaṃ । dṛṣṭvā saṃmuditaḥ paśyann eva tasthāv atṛptitaḥ ।।
tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ śiśoḥ । asya nāmaprasiddhena kriyatām ity abhāṣata ।। tac chrutvā jñātayaḥ sarve te kṛtvā samataṃ tathā । taṃ śreṣṭhinaṃ samāhūya pura evaṃ samabruvan ।।
yad ayaṃ dārako jāto nakṣatra uttarābhidhe । tenottara iti khyāto bhavatu bhavadātmajaḥ ।। iti tair jñātibhiḥ khyātaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhabhṛt tathā । tenaiva nāmadheyena prākhyāpayat tam ātmajaṃ ।।
tataḥ sa dārako aṣṭābhi dhātribhiḥ pratipālitaḥ । dine dine pravṛddho abhū hradastham ambujaṃ yathā ।। tataḥ pravarddhamānaḥ sa gurubhiḥ śikṣitaḥ kramāt । lipyādi sarvavidyānāṃ drutaṃ pāraṃ samāyayau ।।
tadā sa uttaro vijñaḥ savayobhiḥ sahānvitaḥ । caramānaḥ pure tatra lokamanoharo vabhau ।। yadā sa uttaraḥ prauḍhayauvanamadanāśrayaḥ । tadā tasya pitā śreṣṭhī daivāt kālaṃ samāyayau ।।
tatas tasya gṛhe tatra sa uttaras tadātmajaḥ । svāmī saṃpattisaṃprāpto gṛhi lokādhipo abhavat ।। tataḥ sa kulavṛttistho vyavahāravicakṣaṇaḥ । krayavikrayakāryāṇi kṛtvā dravyaṃ samarjayat ।।
sa ekasmin dine tatra veṇuvane jināśrame । saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ draṣṭuṃ dharmārthī samupācarat ।। tatra sa samupāsṛtyādrākṣīt tam śrīghanaṃ muniṃ । dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṃḍitaṃ ।।
vyāmaprabhāvirocaṃtaṃ samaṃtabhadrarūpiṇaṃ । ratnarāśim ivojvālaṃ ratnādrim iva jaṃgamaṃ ।। sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ । dharmāmṛtapravarṣantaṃ sarvalokair namaskṛtaṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā sa muditas tatra sāṃjaliḥ purato vrajan । pādau tasya munīndrasya praṇatvaikānta āśrayan ।। tatra tasyāśayaṃ śuddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāṃs tathā । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sa uttaraḥ pramoditaḥ । punaḥ pādau muner natvā pratyāyayau svam ālayaṃ ।। evaṃ sa uttaro vijñaḥ pratidinaṃ jagadguroḥ । draṣṭuṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ vāpi pātum nityam upācarat ।।
tathā tasya munīndrasya pītvā dharmāmṛtaṃ tadā । saṃbuddhaśāsane tatra pravrajituṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa uttaras tasya munīndrasya purogataḥ । pādābjau sāṃjalir natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।
tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ mahyaṃ dātum arhati sāṃprataṃ ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān munīśvaraḥ । uttarākhyaṃ kumāraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। kumāra śāsane bauddhe pravrajituṃ yadīchasi ।
anujñāṃ mātur āsādya prāgacha dāsyate tadā ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sa uttaraḥ prabodhitaḥ । tatheti caraṇau tasya muner natvā gṛhaṃ yayau ।। tatra gṛhe samāsādya sa uttaraḥ pramoditaḥ ।
jananyāś caraṇau natvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। mātar adya vihāre ahaṃ gachāmi saugatāśrame । tatra śāstu mukhābjottham āryadharmāmṛtaṃ pibe ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā tṛṣṇā me varddhyate punaḥ ।
tat saddharmaṃ samālabdhum ichāmi parituṣṭaye ।। dhanyās te hi śubhātmānaḥ pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalāḥ । saṃbuddhaśāsane sthitvā sadā dharmaṃ pibanti ye ।। aham api sadā tatra saṃbuddhaśāsane caran ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ labdhum ichāmi jananī dhruvaṃ ।। tat pravrajyāvrataṃ dhṛtvā carituṃ saugatāśrame । ichāmi sāṃprataṃ mātas tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। iti putrāditaṃ śrutvā matā sā prahatāśayā ।
ciraṃ tam ātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā rudantyaivam abhāṣata ।। kim eva vadase putra maivaṃ me purato vadaḥ । kim arthaṃ svagṛhaṃ tyaktvā pravrajitu tvam ichasi ।। kiṃ te duḥkhaṃ kuto jātaṃ mayā kiṃ cin na dṛśyate ।
tvayā tu dṛśyate yat tad vaktavyaṃ purato mama ।। adyāpi tava tātasya śokādhiḥ śāmyate na me । tathāpi māṃ kathaṃ tyaktum ichasi sāṃprataṃ sute ।। iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā sa uttaraḥ kumārakaḥ ।
mātaraṃ taṃ samālokya bodhayituṃ samabravīt ।। mātas tvatkṛpayā me atra kiṃ cid duḥkhaṃ na vidyate । gṛhe api mahatī saṃpad asti bhogyaṃ yathechayā ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīrakaṃ ।
anityaṃ jīvitaṃ vidyutsaṃpātam iva na dhruvaṃ ।। saṃpac cāpi sthirā naivaṃ kasya śrī sarvadā sthirā । sarveṣām api jaṃtūnāṃ sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। sarve api prāṇinaḥ kāle tyaktvā sarvān parigrahān ।
jñātivaṃdhusuhṛtmitrānn api yāṃti yamālayaiḥ ।। eko api vidyate naiva mṛtyuprāpte sahānugaḥ । dharma eva tadaikaḥ syāt trātānugo yamālaye ।। dharmeṇa rakṣyate tatra yamadūtair adhiṣṭhite ।
tad atra sarvathā nityaṃ karttavyaṃ dharmam eva hi ।। dharmavānn atra saṃsāre bhramann api sadā sukhī । sarvatra satsukhāny eva prabhuktvā yāti sadgatiṃ ।। tatrāpi sarvadā saukhyaṃ bhuktvā kṛtvā ca maṃgalaṃ ।
sarvasatvahitārthena saddharmāṇy eva sādhayet ।। etatpuṇyavipākaiḥ sa sadguruṃ samupāśrayet । sadguros tu prasādena bodhicittaṃ labhet tadā ।। tato bodhicarīṃ prāpya bodhisatvo bhavet sudhīḥ ।
tataḥ satvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ samācaret ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ । trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarvajñena hitārthinā ।
śrutaṃ mayā parijñāya tathā caritum ichyate ।। etatpuṇyavibhāgatvam api prāptuṃ yadīchasi । tad anujñāṃ pradatvā me cittaṃ mātaḥ pratoṣaya ।। iti putroditaṃ śrutvā mātā sā vihatāśayā ।
viyogaduḥkhasaṃkārttā vilapanty evam abravīt ।। hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihātuṃ tvam ichasi । nānyo me vidyate putras tvam evaiko asti naṃdanaḥ ।। pitāpi tava māṃ tyajya daivād yāto yamālayaṃ ।
tvam api māṃ parityaktvā kutra gaṃtuṃ tathechasi ।। hā putra katham ajño asi kenātra tvaṃ pravaṃcyase । kiṃ paśyan hetunā kena pravrajituṃ tvam ichasi ।। hā putra kena mūḍho asi yad etā dravyasaṃpadaḥ ।
tyaktvā paragṛhe bhikṣāṃ yācitvā bhoktum ichasi ।। hā putra tvaṃ kumāro asi tat pravrajyāṃ careḥ kathaṃ । pravrajito gṛhaṃ tyaktvā bahir deśe sadāśrayeḥ ।। tat kathaṃ tyaktvā bahir deśe samāśrayeḥ ।
śāṇakaṃṭāvṛto muṃdo mṛtvātra dhareśvaraḥ ।। śītavātātapākrānte kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ saheḥ suta । kṣutpipāsāgnisaṃtaptaḥ duḥkhaṃ kas te abhiśāmayet ।। śmaśāneṣu śavāny asyan katham ekaś careḥ suta ।
jaṃgale nirjane araṇye ekākī nivaseḥ kathaṃ ।। tathā bhūtālaye śūnyageheva nivaseḥ kathaṃ । tathāmitreṣu deśeṣu katham ekor iva ccare ।। jvarādi rogasaṃtapte kas tava paricārayet ।
ko vā te kṛpayā dadyāt pathyam āhāram auṣadhaṃ ।। yadi daivād vipattiḥ syāt tadā kaḥ pariśodhayet । iti samīkṣya mā putra pravrajyāvrata utsaha । mamātra vacanaṃ śrutvā sukhaṃ bhuktvā gṛhe vasa ।। iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā sa putraś caivam abravīt । daivabhāvā bhavanty eva sarvatrāpi jagatsv api ।।
eko api vidyate nātra suhṛnmitrasahānugaḥ । dharma eva sahāyaḥ syāt sarvatra maraṇe dhruvaṃ ।। iti saddharmasaṃprāptyai pravrajyāvratam uttamaṃ । caritavyaṃ bhaved vijñair nirvṛtipadavāṃchibhiḥ ।।
iti tena munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate । māta tasmā tathātraitad vrataṃ caritum ichyate ।। tad atra saugate dharme māṃ niyoktuṃ yadīchasi । tad anujñāṃ pradānaṃ me kṛpayā dātum arhati ।।
iti putrārthitaṃ śrutvā mātā sā gadgadasvarā । snehaduḥkhāgnisaṃtaptā dṛṣṭvaivaṃ sutam abravīt ।। hā putra katham eva tvaṃ nirdayāsy atiniṣṭhuraḥ । yad vṛddhāṃ jananīṃ dṛṣṭvā kāruṇyaṃ nāsti te hṛdi ।।
tad atra yadi te putra dayāsti mayi mātari । yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ tāvad gṛhe vasa mayā saha ।। yāvac caitan mahat saṃpat svagṛhe sthirā tava । tāvad yathepsitaṃ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā ramaṃ samācara ।।
avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ yāyāṃ kasya mṛtyur bhave na hi । tadā mayi mṛtāyāṃ tu pravrajasva yathechayā ।। saṃpac cāpi bhavet kṣīṇā kasya saṃpat sadā sthirā । tadā saṃpat parikṣīṇe bhikṣānnādo vrataṃ cara ।।
yady evaṃ prārthite api tvaṃ vilaṃghya vacanaṃ mama । nirdayāniṣṭhurasvāntaḥ pravrajasi haṭhād api ।। tadāhaṃ te purogatvā saugataśāsane api hi । tyaktvāhāraṃ viṣaṃ bhuktvā yāsyāmi maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
iti me vacanaṃ satyaṃ vijñāyeha tvam ātmaja । mayā saha gṛhe saukhyaṃ bhukṣva kutrāpi mā vraja ।। iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā yathākāmaṃ sukhaṃ gṛhe । bhuktvā nityaṃ sadotsāhaiś caraṃ rama svam ātmaja ।।
iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā sa uttaro abhiśaṃkitaḥ । tatheti pratibuddhitvā tasthau gehe nirāśitaḥ ।। tataś caikadine prātaḥ samutthāya sa uttaraḥ । saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ muniṃ draṣṭuṃ vihāre samupācarat ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa uttaraḥ pramoditaḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāṃjalis samupāśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃc chāstā dṛṣṭvā tasya manogataṃ । bodhayituṃ samālokya tam evaṃ samupālapat ।।
kumāra kiṃ viṣaṇṇo asi yan mano antargataṃ tava । tan mamāgre samākhyāhi pūrayāmi yadīhitaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sa uttaraḥ samutthitaḥ । pādau tasya muner natvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।।
sarvajña bhagavañ chāstar vijānīyād bhavān mama । yan mano antargataṃ sarvaṃ yathāpy ahaṃ nivedaye ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña na me mātā prabodhitā । tad anujñāṃ na me dātum ichati prārthitāpi sā ।।
tad bhavān me yathā yogyaṃ vrataṃ saṃbodhisādhanaṃ । anyathāpi pradatvātra prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । taṃ viśuddhāśayaṃ dṛṣṭvā samāśvāsyaivam ādiśat ।।
mā kumāra viṣādatvaṃ kṛthā dhairyaṃ samāśraya । avaśyaṃ samaye prāpte brahmacārī bhaviṣyasi ।। tāvad gṛhe sadā dānaṃ kṛtvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā śubhe cara samāhitaḥ ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena samaye samupāgate । pravrajyāvratam āsādya nirvāṇapadam āpsyasi ।। iti matvā kumārātra yāvaj jīvati sā prasūḥ । tāvad gṛhe sadā dānaṃ kṛtvā śubhe caran vasa ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa uttaraḥ sudhīḥ । tatheti prativijñapya prasasāda prabodhitaḥ ।। tataḥ sa uttaro natvā sāṃjalis taṃ munīśvaraṃ । suprasannamukhāmbhojas tan manāḥ svagṛhaṃ yayau ।।
tatra sa svagṛhe sthitvā svakulavṛttisādhanaiḥ । pratisāryāpaṇaṃ tatra cakāra krayavikrayaṃ ।। tatra mulādhikaṃ lābhaṃ yal labdhaṃ gaṇavandhanaṃ । tat sarvaṃ sa sutas tasyā mātur haste samarpayat ।।
tataḥ sa uttaraḥ putro mātaraṃ tāṃ prasādayan । tal labdhaṃ sakalaṃ dravyaṃ datvaivaṃ pratyabodhayat ।। śṛṇu mātar mamānena dravyena svajanāṃ janān । arthinaḥ kṛpaṇān viprān mānayitvābhitoṣaya ।।
iti putroditaṃ śrutvā mātā sā atikuṃcikā । lubdhā matsarākrāṃtahṛdayaivam abhāṣata ।। putra pitrā prayatnena saṃpadas te samarjitāḥ । tvam etāḥ saṃpadaḥ sarvā datvārthibhyo vyayiṣyasi ।।
yāvat pitrārjitaṃ dravyaṃ tāvan mayā na dāsyate । tāvat mātraṃ tavādhīnaṃ yāvat tvayā samarjitaṃ ।। yāvaj jivāmy ahaṃ tāta na te dāsyāmi kiṃ cana । mṛtāyāṃ mayi tat sarvaṃ tavādhīnaṃ bhavet tadā ।।
ity uktvā sā prasūs tasya mātsaryyakaluṣāśayā । sarvadravyaṃ prayatnena guptīkṛtyātyarakṣata ।। kiṃ cid arthibhyo sā kudhī dadau । guptīkṛtya prayatnena tad dravyaṃ samagopayat ।।
dṛṣṭvā ca sārthinaḥ sarvān svagṛhaṃ samupāgatān । sahasā samupāśritya paribhāṣyābhyanindayat ।। are māyā na gehe asmiṃ yūyaṃ pretā ivāgatāḥ । nityaṃ paragṛhe piṃḍaṃ bhoktuṃ bhramatha bhūtavat ।।
evaṃ tān arthinaḥ sarvān sā nārī duritāśayā । naikadhā vipralāpena paribhāṣyābhyaniṃdayat ।। evaṃ mātrā pratikruṣya vipralāpābhiniṃditān । śrutvā sa uttaraḥ putro mātaraṃ tām abhāṣata ।।
are māta kim eva tvam arthinaḥ paribhāṣase । dhik tvāṃ dharmaparibhraṣṭāṃ kathaṃ na narake pateḥ ।। yadi tvaṃ vāṃchase saukhyam ihāmutrāpi sarvadā । kṛpaṇān arthinaḥ sarvān saṃpradānaiḥ pramodaya ।।
yady evaṃ kriyate mātaḥ saṃgatiḥ sarvadāvayoḥ । anyathā cet tato nau syād vibhinnabhojanāśrayaḥ ।। yady asti te mayā sārddhaṃ sarvadā bhojane ratiḥ । yathepsitaṃ sadārthibhyo datvā cara śubhe vṛṣe ।।
iti tenātmajenāpi pratyākhyataṃ niśamya sā । mātā lajjāvibhinnāsyā tam ātmajam abhāṣata ।। yady evaṃ nandanārthibhyaḥ sarvasvam api ditsasi । tat svadravyāṇi sarvāṇi dāsyāmi tad yathepsitaṃ ।।
ity uktvā sā prasū nārī tam ātmajaṃ mṛṣāgirā । bodhayitvā gṛhe tāni dravyāṇi samagopayet ।। tataḥ sā pramadā duṣṭā mithyāvācā tam ātmajaṃ । adya yato arthino bhikṣūns toṣayāmīty abodhayat ।।
evaṃ mithyayā vācā bodhayantī tam ātmajaṃ । svayam eva prabhuktvā ca tad dravyaṃ sarvaṃ gopayat ।। kasmai cid arthine kiṃ cid api sā na dadau kudhīḥ । sā kebhyo api valiṃ dātuṃ naivotsehe kadā cana ।।
evaṃ sā durmatir lubdhā matsarākrāntacetasā । paribhāṣyārthinaḥ sarvān niṃdayanty aśubhe acarat ।। evaṃ kevalapāpāni prācitvā sā durāśayā । kāle nirāśayā duḥkhārttā mṛtā pretālaye yayau ।।
tatra pretagatiprāptā pretībhūtā durākṛtiḥ । svakeśapratichannāṃgā śūcīmukhā kṛśāṃgikā ।। asthiyaṃtravad ucchrāyā parvatasaṃnibhodarā । kṣutpipāsāgnisaṃtaptā dagdhasthūṇāsamāṃgikā ।।
ārttasvarā virāvantī kraṃdantī sā samaṃtataḥ । annapāna hi mārgantī paryabhramad itas tataḥ ।। tataḥ sa uttaro mātuḥ kṛtvāgnisaṃskṛtiṃ tadā । snānaśaucādi karmāṃ kurvañ chokaṃ vyanodayat ।।
tataḥ sa uttaro vijo mātṛśokaṃ vyanodayat । arthibhyo vāṃchitaṃ datvā bahupuṇyāṇy upārjayat ।। tataḥ kāmaviraktaḥ sa saṃsārabhoganispṛhaḥ । nirvṛtipadasaṃprātyai pravrajituṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa mudito gatvā veṇuvane jināśrame ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā sāṃjaliḥ samupācarat ।। tatra pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । praṇatvā purataḥ sthitvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña vijānīyād bhavān api ।
yan me sā jananī vighnā sāṃprataṃ pralayaṃ gatā ।। tad atra bhagavac chāstar bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tan me anugraham ādhāya pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati ।। iti saṃprarthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
savyakareṇa tanmūrddhni saṃspṛśyaivaṃ samādiśat ।। ehi cara kumārātra brahmacaryaṃ samāhitaḥ । ity uktvā bhagavāṃ chāstā sāṃghike taṃ samagrahīt ।। ehīty ukte munīndreṇa muṃḍito abhūt sa uttaraḥ ।
khikkhirīpātrabhṛc chuddhakāṣāyacīvarāvṛtaḥ ।। tataḥ śāstuḥ prasādāt sa pariśuddhas trimaṃḍalaḥ । niḥkleśayaviśuddhātmā saṃsāraviratotsavaḥ ।। samādhidhāraṇīvidyāghaṭamāno vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
hitvāvidyāgaṇaṃ sarvavidyāguṇāntam āptavān ।। viditvā sarvasaṃsāragatiṃ vidyutkṣaṇasthitiṃ । matvā ca sarvasaṃskāragatir anekavighātiniṃ ।। sarvakleśagaṇāṃ jitvā sarvān māragaṇān api ।
sākṣād arhatvam āsādya śrāvakabodhim āptavān ।। tataḥ sa suviśuddhātmā vītarāgo jiteṃdriyaḥ । ākāśanirmalasvāntaḥ sarvaloṣṭakakāṃcanaḥ ।। vāsīcaṃdanakalpāṃśo nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ ।
sarvasatvahitādhānaḥ saṃbuddhaguṇasādhakaḥ ।। sadevāsuralokānāṃ sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām api । vaṃdyaḥ pūjyo abhimānyaś ca brahmacārī babhūva saḥ ।। tataḥ so arhan mahābhijño gaṃgātire śubhasthale ।
parṇakuṭyāṃ samāśritya tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। tatraikasmin dine tasya mātā sā pretikā satī । nagna svaromasaṃchannā daghasthūṇāvivarṇitā ।। sūcīmukhāsthiyaṃtreva parvatasannibhodarā ।
kṣutpipāsāgnidagdhāṃgā pānāhāragaveṣinī ।। ārtasvaraṃ virāvantī kraṃdantī samupāgatā । āyuṣmantaṃ tam arhantaṃ paśyantī samupāśrayat ।। evaṃ tāṃ samupāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa uttaro yatiḥ ।
kā tvam evaṃvidhāyātā vadasvety anvapṛchata ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sā pretī purataḥ sthitā । uttaraṃ taṃ yatiṃ putraṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। ahaṃ te jananī snigdhā yayāsi janitaḥ sutaḥ ।
annapānaviviktāsmi pretībhūtā adhunā care ।। paṃcaviṃśati varsāṇi yāṃti kālagatā hy ahaṃ । nābhijānāmi pāṇīyaṃ kuto bhaktasya darśanaṃ ।। saphalāṃ puṣpitāṃ vṛkṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā gachāmi dūrataḥ । sarve api niṣphalā śuṣkā vipuṣpāś ca bhavanti te ।।
sarāṃsi cāmbupūrṇāṇi dṛṣṭvā gachāmi dūrataḥ । tāni sarvāṇi śuṣkāni bhavanti tat kṣaṇād api ।। bhedaṃ tasya mahāsaukhyaṃ vṛkṣamūlaśritasya te । vidyate sarvadāpy atra kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ śubhaṃ ।।
tad atra kṛpayā paśyan kāruṇyaṃ janayan suta । mātre tṛṣārditāyai me śītāmbu dātum arhasi ।। iti tayārthitam śrutvā sa uttaraḥ savismayaḥ । tāṃ pretīṃ suciraṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṃkitaś caivam abravīt ।।
mātas tarhi kṣaṇaṃ prāpte tvayā pāruṣyabhūtayā । dānāni na kṛtāny eva puṇyāni vā citāni na ।। anyakṛtāni dānāni puṇyāni bhāṣitāni ca । dṛṣṭvā śrutvāpi te citte krodhāgnir jvalitas tadā ।।
kiṃ cin nāpi śubhaṃ karma kṛtvāpuṇyaṃ tvayārjitaṃ । pareṇāpi kṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvāpi nānumoditaṃ ।। etatkarmavipākena jananī tvaṃ mṛtādhunā । pretībhūtānnapānena viyuktā bhramase bhave ।।
idāniṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tvaṃ cātra kiṃ kariṣyasi । tadā sarvāhitaṃ proktaṃ tvayā tatra śrutaṃ na tat ।। iti tenātmajenoktaṃ śrutvā sā pratibodhitā । vigaladaśrurukṣākṣā taṃ putram evam abravīt ।।
na mayā hi kṛtaṃ dānaṃ puṇyaṃ na cābhisādhitaṃ । dṛṣṭvānumoditaṃ nāpi mātsaryaparibhūtayā ।। yad yad dravyaṃ tvayā putra mama haste samarpitaṃ । tat tat sarvaṃ mayā vaṃdhikhadāyāṃ parigopitaṃ ।।
tad idāniṃ samuddhṛtya jñātihaste samarpaya । tena taṃ sugataṃ buddhaṃ sasaṃghaṃ bhojayātmaja ।। dakṣiṇādeśanāṃ cāpi mama nāmnābhikāraya । tadā pretagater muktā yāyām ahaṃ surālayaṃ ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa uttaro anubodhitaḥ । evam astv iti saṃśrutya punas tām evam abravīt ।। sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ tena bhojayiṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ । kiṃ tu tvayāmva tatrāpi sthātavyaṃ sugatāṃtike ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sā pretī lajjayānvitā । tam arhantaṃ samālokya pura evam abhāṣata ।। yad ahaṃ putra nagnāsmi pretī vibhransitākṛtī । tat kathaṃ samupāśritya sthāsyāmi śrīghanāṃtike ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa uttaro mahāmatiḥ । tāṃ pretīṃ samupālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।। kriyamāne yadā pāpe lajjā nāsti tadā tava । phalabhojanakāle atra kim evaṃ lajjase adhunā ।।
iti tad vacanaṃ śrutvā sā pretī pratibodhitā । tathā gamiṣyāmīti proktva tvaritaṃ vijñālayaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sa uttaro gatvā jñātīn āhūya tad vṛtiṃ । yathāmātroditaṃ khyāya sarvam eva nyavedayat ।। tac chrutvā jñātivargās te sarva ativismayānvitāḥ ।
tathā tad dravyam ādāya sarvaṃ tasyān upāharan ।। tad dravyaṃ sarvam ālokya sa uttaraḥ pramoditaḥ । sarveṣām api gotrāṇāṃ punar evaṃ samabravīt ।। bhavanto jñātayaḥ sarve dravyenaitena sāṃprataṃ ।
sasāṃghikaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ bhojayiṣyāmi pūjayan ।। tad etat sarvam ādāya yadā prakaṃpitāśayāḥ । saṃghabhojyārhasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvā pradatta me ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayas tathā ।
saṃghabhojyārhasāmagrīṃ sarvadravyair asādhayat ।। tad dṛṣṭvā muditaḥ so arhan uttaraḥ saṃprasannadhīḥ । śāstur nimaṃtraṇaṃ kartuṃ vihāre samupācarat ।। tatra sa samupāśritya taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaiḥ ।
praṇatvā sāñjalis tatra puraḥ sthitvā nyamaṃtrayat ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । pūjayituṃ samichāmi śvo anugṛhītum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tam uttaraṃ samālokya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa uttaro matvā bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ । taṃ munīndraṃ punar natvā jñātīnāṃ purato yayau ।। tatra sa uttaras teṣāṃ ca nimaṃtraṇaṃ ।
kṛtvā tatra punas teṣāṃ pura evam abhāṣata ।। saṃghabhojye pravṛtte atra yūyaṃ sarve samāgatāḥ । pretībhūtāṃ mamāmbāṃ tām avalokitum arhatha ।। ity uktvā svāśramaṃ gatvā sa uttaraḥ prasāditaḥ ।
dhyānāgārasamāsīnas tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya jñātīnāṃ purato gataḥ । pūjopacārasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat ।। tataḥ sa uttaraḥ prāhne vihāre samupāsaran ।
bhagavaṃtaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।। bhagavan sarvavic chāstaḥ samayo varttate adhunā । tat sasaṃgho bhavān atra vijayituṃ samarhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena gaṃḍīm ākoṭayan muniḥ ।
tac chabdacoditās tatra sa ca saṃghā upāsaran ।। tatra te jñātayaḥ sarve lokā anye api harṣitāḥ । tatra pretāṃ samāyātāṃ tāṃ draṣṭuṃ samupāgatāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra sasāṃghikaḥ samāgatāḥ ।
tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya śuddhāsane samāśrayat ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā jñātayaḥ sarve lokā anye api kheṭitāḥ । hā pāpam iti bhāṣante tasthuḥ saddharmavāṃchayā ।। tadā te jñātayaḥ sarve bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।
yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve saṃbuddhapramukhā api । tat praṇītarasaṃ bhojyaṃ bhuktvā tṛptiṃ samāyayuḥ ।। tato apanīya pātrāṇi śodhayitvā bhujādikaṃ ।
teṣāṃ pūgādi tāmbūlagaṇaṃ te pradadur mudā ।। tatra sa uttaro bhikṣur jñātibhis tai sahānvitaḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ praṇatvā samupāśrayat ।। tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tam uttaram upāśritaṃ ।
dākṣiṇādeśanāṃ tasyāḥ pretyā nāmnā samādiśat ।। ito dānād dhi yat puṇyaṃ tat pretīm upagachatu । uttiṣṭhatām iyaṃ pretī pretalokāt tato drutaṃ ।। iti śubhāśiṣaṃ datvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ ca samādiśat ।। tad āryyadharmam ākarṇya sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ । dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya babhūvuḥ satyadarśinaḥ ।। sāpi pretī samānīya tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ mudā ।
suprasannāśayā smṛtvā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sā bhūtaloke abhūj jātā bhūtamaharddhikā । tatrāpi sābhavad duṣṭā mātsaryyarukṣitāśayā ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasmāt sasāṃghikaḥ prabhāsayan ।
gatvā svāśramam āśritya tasthau dharmam upādiśan ।। tataḥ sa buddhimān vijña āyuṣmān yatir uttaraḥ । kutrāsau jāyate mātādhuneti samapaśyata ।। evaṃ sa uttaro vijñaḥ samabhīkṣya samaṃtataḥ ।
dadarśa tāṃ saṃprajātāṃ bhūtamaharddhikālaye ।। dṛṣṭvā sa uttaraḥ putro mātaraṃ tāṃ ca bhautikāṃ । sahasā samupāśritya samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। kim ambāsti tvayā śaktir api dāneṣu sāṃprataṃ ।
yadīchasi sadā bhadraṃ kuru dānam ihādhunā ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sā ca bhūtamaharddhikā । uttaraṃ taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। nādyāpi vidyate dāne abhilāṣaṃ mama naṃdana ।
tat kiṃ cid api vā dravyaṃ pradātuṃ nāham utsahe ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvāyuṣmān sa uttaro yatiḥ । dṛṣṭvā tāṃ mātaraṃ bhūtamaharddhikām abhāṣata ।। adyāpi te tiṣṭhati tac charīraṃ vivṛddhanirmānsatvagasthicarmā lobhāṃdhakārāvṛtalocanāyā nivartitaṃ yat tava pretaloke । dhik tvāṃ praduṣṭām iha kiṃ vadeyam adyāpi yat tvaṃ duritāśayāsi । kenātra te pāpanimagnacittaṃ saṃśodhitaṃ puṇyakaroddhṛtaṃ syāt ।।
sadāpi caivaṃ narake nivāsā bhavet kadā tvaṃ parimokṣyase ataḥ । aho hi durbuddhidurāśayānāṃ mano na kenāpi viśuddhyate vai ।। evaṃ bahuprakāreṇa paribhāṣyottaraḥ sa tāṃ । tadaṅgāt yamalīm ekām ākṛṣyāpaharad valāt ।।
tatas tāṃ yamalīṃ so arhaṃ saṃghāya samakalpayat । tatra mūlyena tāṃ krītvā bhikṣumānavake nyaset ।। tatrāpi niśi sā gatvā yamalīṃ tām upāharat । tathāpahṛtāṃ bhikṣur uttarāya nyavedayat ।।
tac chrutvā cottaro gatvā paribhāṣya valena tāṃ । apahṛtya punas tasmai bhikṣave samakalpayat ।। bhūyo api niśi sā gatvā yamalīṃ tām upāharat । tathā sa uttaraś cāpi tasyāś ca tām apāharat ।।
evaṃ tridhā niśāyāṃ sā tatra gatvāharac ca tāṃ । uttaraś cāpahṛtyaiva tāṃ tasmai bhikṣave dadau ।। tenāpi bhikṣuṇādāya catudiksāṃghikāya sā । pādyalepānikāyāṃ saṃsīvitvā pratipāditā ।।
tatra tāṃ sīvitāṃ dṛṣṭvā sā ca bhūtamaharddhitā । apahṛtavibhagnāśā rudantī svālayaṃ yayau ।। taccittāgniprataptā sā smṛtvā taṃ sutam uttaraṃ । kālaṃ gatā tato anyatra yakṣaloke alabhaj januḥ ।।
evaṃ matvā mahatpāpamūlaṃ mātsaryyam eva hi । tat mātsaryaṃ parityajya karttavyaṃ dānam ādarāt ।। dānena śuddhyate cittaḥ śuddhacittaḥ sudhīkṛtiḥ । kramād bodhicariṃ dhṛtvā saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।।
evaṃ vijñāya sarvatra yadīchanti sadā śubhaṃ । mātsaryaṃ viṣavat tyaktvā caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe ।। iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ tathā mayocyate । tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ parijñāya caritavyam śubhe sadā ।।
prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayituṃ sadārhasi ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti pratibhāṣitvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। idaṃ narā ye muditāś ca bhūtamaharddhikāyānuvadānam atra । mudā niśamya pratimodayante prayāṃti te śrīghanasaṃnivāse ।।
athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam avocat ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan mahāmatiḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me gurubhāṣitaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cātrānumodaya ।।
tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śrīghanaḥ sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhiś ca celakaiḥ । upāsakagaṇaiś cāpi tathā copāsikāgaṇaiḥ ।।
rājagṛhapuropānte gṛddhakūṭe nagottame । veṇuvane mahodyāne karaṃdakanivāpake ।। sarvasatvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra prabhāsayan ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokā upāgatāḥ । devā daityāś ca nāgāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।। grahā vidyādharāḥ siddhā rākṣasā garuḍā api । lokapālagaṇāś cāpi tīrthikāś ca maharṣayaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā bhūpā vaiśyāś ca māṃtriṇo api ca । amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaś cāpi gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ ।। vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpinaḥ paurikās tathā । grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathā kārpaṭikā api ।।
tathānye api janāś caivaṃ sarve tatra samāgatāḥ । dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ ।। kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve parivṛtyopatasthire । tataḥ sa bhagavāṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tāṃ samupasthitān ।
ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ । dharmavaiśeṣam ājñāya babhūvur bodhisādhinaḥ ।। evaṃ sa bhagavāṃs tatra nityaṃ saddharmam ādiśan ।
varṣāsu vyaharal lokahitaṃ kṛtvā sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tasmiṃs tu samaye tatra śrāvastyāṃ puri sattamaḥ । anāthapiṃḍadaḥ śreṣṭhī gṛhapatir mahājanaḥ ।। triratnabhaktimān dātā saṃbuddhadarśanotsukaḥ ।
prasenajin mahīpālaṃ praṇatvā prārthayat tathā ।। jaya deva mahāraja jānīyāt tad bhavān api । yad asmābhi munīndro asau suciraṃ nābhidṛśyate ।। tat tasmātra munīndrasya darśane tṛṣitā vayaṃ । bhagavaṃtaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ draṣṭum ichāmahe adhunā ।।
tad bhavān samupāmaṃtrya bhagavaṃtaṃ jagadguruṃ । atra lokahitārthāya vijayituṃ samarhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena gṛhādhipatinā sadā । śrutvā sa bhūpatī rājā taṃ gṛhapatim abravīt ।।
kiṃ tvayā śrūyate sādho bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । etarhi tiṣṭhate kutra varṣāsu saha sāṃghikaiḥ ।। iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā so anāthapiṇḍado gṛhī । taṃ nareṃdraṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।।
śrutaṃ mayā mahārāja bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaṃ । rājagṛhe adhunā prāvṛtsamaye apy avatiṣṭhate ।। iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatis tataḥ । dūtam ekaṃ samāhūya pura evam upālapat ।।
ehi tvaṃ bho mahāsādho śrutvā me vacanaṃ drutaṃ । tatra rājagṛhe gatvā bhagavata upācara ।। asmākaṃ vacanais tasya śāstuḥ pādāmbuje namaḥ । natvā dehādi sarvatra kauśalyaṃ paripṛcha ca ।।
evaṃ cāpi munes tasya puro vijñāpayādarāt । kauśalye nṛpatī rājā bhagavaṃtaṃ draṣṭum ichati ।। tathā sarve api lokāś ca śrāvastyāyāś ca paurikāḥ । triratnadarśanaṃ kartum abhivāṃchanti sāṃprataṃ ।।
bhavaddharmāmṛtaṃ cāpi pātum ichaṃti sarvavit । tat sasaṃgho bhavāṃs tatra kṛpayāgaṃtum arhati ।। iti rajñoditaṃ śrutvā tatheti pratimoditaḥ । taṃ nṛpaṃ sāṃjalir natvā drutaṃ rājagṛhaṃ yayau ।।
tatra rājagṛhe gatvā sa dūtaḥ pratinaṃditaḥ । vilokya suprasannātmā gṛdhrakūṭe upācarat ।। tatra sa dūrato dṛṣṭvā bhagavaṃtaṃ pramoditaḥ । upetya sāṃjalir natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña vaṃde te caraṇāmbuje । yadarthe aham ihāyāmi taj jānīyād bhavāṃ jinaḥ ।। tathāpy ahaṃ jagacchāstuḥ puro vijñāpayāmi tat । bhagava sarvavid rājā prasenajit sukauśalaḥ ।।
bhavatāṃ vaṃdate pādau kuśalaṃ cāpi pṛchate । tathā ca bhagavan sarve śrāvastyeyāś ca paurikāḥ ।। vaṃdaṃte bhavatāṃ pādau pṛchaṃte cāpi kauśalaṃ । nṛpādi sarvalokāś ca bhavatāṃ darśanotsukāḥ ।।
triratnaṃ draṣṭum ichāma ity evaṃ pravadanti te । bhavaddharmāmṛtaṃ cāpi pātum ichaṃti te adhunā ।। nṛpatipramukhāḥ sarve tṛṣṇārditā ivāmṛtaṃ । tat sādhu bhagavāṃs tatra śrāvastyāṃ puri sāṃprataṃ । anukampām upādāya vijayatāṃ sasāṃghikaḥ ।। ity ukte tena dūtena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
taṃ dūtaṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtryevam ādiśat ।। bho puruṣa mahārājo bimbisāro nṛpādhipaḥ । yady anujñāṃ dadāty atra tadā yāsyāmy ahaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। tat sādhu nṛpates tasya bimbisārasya bhūbhṛtaḥ ।
anujñāprārthanāṃ kṛtvā gachāyāsyāmy ahaṃ tadā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa dūta ādarāt । tatheti taṃ muniṃ natvā rājño antikam upācarat ।। tatra sa samupāśritya bimbisāraṃ narādhipaṃ ।
sāṃjaliḥ purato gatvā praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat ।। jaya deva mahārāja prasīdānugrahaṃ kuru । prasenajinmahībhartur dūto ahaṃ samupāgataḥ ।। mahārāja mahīpāla prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ ।
bhagavato munīndrasya darśanam abhivāṃchati ।। tathā sarve api lokāś ca śrāvastryeyāḥ sapaurikāḥ । triratnasya jagadbhartuḥ praṣṭum ichanti sāṃprataṃ ।। tad asya trijagacchāstur bhagavato bhavān prabho ।
tatrānugamane anujñāṃ kṛpayā dātum arhati ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bimbisāraḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । taṃ dūtaṃ samupālokya cireṇaivam abhāṣata ।। sadho sa bhagavāns tatra yadi gaṃtuṃ samichati ।
tad atra kiṃ vadiṣyāmi yatrechet tatra gachatu ।। iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā dūtaḥ sa moditaḥ । bimbisāraṃ nareṃdraṃ taṃ natvā yayau jināntike ।। tatra sa sahasā gatvā śrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavaṃs tena bhūpena hy anujñāto asi sāṃprataṃ । tat sasaṃgho bhagavāṃs tatra vijayituṃ samarhati ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
enaṃ dūtaṃ samālokya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān varṣātrimāsānta sasāṃghikaḥ । sarvatra maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā pratasthe saṃprabhāsayan ।। tadā sa puruṣo dūtas tadvihārād vinirgataḥ ।
sahasā ratham āruhya saṃpratasthe puraḥ pathi ।। tatra sa bhagavaṃtaṃ padbhyāṃ saṃprasthitaṃ pathi । dṛṣṭvaiva sahasā tasmād rathāt svayam avātarat ।। tatra sa sahasopetya bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ ।
sāṃjaliḥ purato gatvā praṇatvaivam avocata ।। prasīdatu jagannātha mamānukampayā bhavān । idaṃ rathaṃ samāruhya vijayatāṃ sasāṃghikaḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ ।
