taṃ dūtaṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraivaṃ samupādiśat ।। ṛddhipādarathenāhaṃ samyagvyāyāmavarttinā । pracarāmi mahīṃ kṛtsnām akṣataḥ kleśakaṣṭakaiḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sa dūtaḥ pratibodhitaḥ । bhūyo api sāṃjalir natvā prārthayat taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।।
yady api bhagavān ṛddhiyānayāyī tathāpi tu । mamānugraham ādhātuṃ gṛhyatām anukampayā ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sasāṃghikaḥ । ṛddhyā rathopari sthitvā saṃpratasthe prabhāsayan ।।
tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra bhagavān sasāṃghikaḥ । bhāsayan maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā śrāvastīpuram āyayau ।। tatra sa puruṣo dūtaḥ sahasā pracaran puraḥ । prasenajinnarendrasya gatvaivaṃ saṃnyavedayat ।।
jaya deva mahārāja diṣṭyā varddhasva sāṃprataṃ । yad asau bhagavāṃc chāstā sasaṃgho atra samāgataḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā prasenajit sa bhūpatiḥ । tatra sarvatra mārgeṣu śodhayitvābhyaśodhayat ।।
chatradhvajavitānaiś ca samaṃtato abhyamaṃḍayat । tataḥ sa nṛpati rājā tūryasaṃgītivādanaiḥ । sajano bhagavantaṃ taṃ pratyudyayau mahotsavaiḥ ।। tatra samudito rājā samaṃtrijanapaurikaḥ ।
dūrāt taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā padbhyāṃ carann upācarat ।। tatropetya sa bhūpālaḥ sasaṃghan taṃ munīśvaraṃ । praṇatvā sāṃjaliḥ sthitvā puro dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt ।। bhagavan nātha sārvajña kaccic ca kuśalaṃ tanau ।
bhavatāṃ viṣaye hy atra viharasva sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tathā sarve api lokāś ca samaṃtrijanapaurikāḥ । sāṃjalayaḥ praṇatvaivaṃ prārthayaṃs taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। svāgataṃ bhagavaṃc chāsta vijayasva kṛpānidhe ।
sadātra svāśrame sthitvā viharasvānukampayā ।। ity uktvā sarvalokās te nṛpatipramukhā mudā । pūjādi maṃgalotsāhaiḥ prāveśayaṃs tataḥ pure ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān saṃpramoditān ।
nṛpatipramukhān datvā bhadrāśiṣaṃ samācarat ।। tatra sa bhagavāṃs tasyāḥ śrāvastyā gopurāntike । avatīrya yathā padbhyāṃ pracakrāma sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tatra sa śrīghano nāthaḥ prabhāsayan samaṃtataḥ ।
sarveṣāṃ bhadratāṃ kurvan praviveśa sasāṃghikaḥ ।। praviṣṭe nagare tatra saṃbuddhe sugate jine । tatpuṇyasuprabhāvyāpte sarvatrāpy abhavac chubhaṃ ।। aṃdhā rūpāṇi prādrākṣur vadhirāḥ śuśruvu ravaṃ ।
ye ca hīneṃdriyās te api sarve pūrṇendriyā vabhuḥ ।। kṣudhāgniparitaptāṃgās te abhavan paritṛptitāḥ । pipāsāparidagdhāṃgās te apy āsan saṃpratarpitāḥ ।। kucelā durbhagāṃśā ye śuddhāṃśukāḥ śubhāṃśikāḥ । cirarogāturā yena nīrogā valino abhavan ।।
unmattāḥ smṛtimaṃtaś ca daridrā dhanino abhavan । ciravairānuvaddhā ye te apy āsan maitrabhāvinaḥ ।। caṃḍālāś ca dayāvantaḥ krodhinaḥ kṣāntibhāvinaḥ । labdhāś ca niḥspṛhā āsan īrṣyālavaś ca sādhavaḥ ।।
matsariṇaś ca dātāraḥ kṛpaṇāḥ saṃtoṣitāśayāḥ । adharmakāmasaṃraktās te dharmakāmasādhinaḥ ।। mṛṣāvādaratā ye ca te apy āsan satyabhāṣiṇaḥ । paiśunyābhiratā ye ca te api viśrambhabhojanāḥ ।।
saṃbhinnalāpino duṣṭās te api saṃtaḥ samārjavāḥ । pāruṣyaṃvādinaḥ krūrās te āsan priyavādinaḥ ।। ye abhidhyālavas te api sajjanā kīrtimāninaḥ । vyāpādaniratā ye ca te api satvahitārthinaḥ ।।
mithyādṛṣṭicarā ye ca te dharmasatyadṛṣṭayaḥ । bodhicaryāsamutsāhāḥ sarve puṇyārthino abhavan ।। evam anye api ye satvā duḥkhinaḥ pāpasaṃratāḥ । sarve te sukhinaḥ saṃtaḥ saddharmavāṃchino abhavan ।।
sugaṃdhinaḥ sukhasparśāḥ śītalā vāyavo vavuḥ । prasedire diśaḥ sarvāḥ puṣpāṇi vavṛṣur ghanāḥ ।। suraduṃdubhayo neduḥ prasasāra mahodadhiḥ । pracacāra mahī ṣaḍdhā prajujvaluḥ śubhāgnayaḥ ।।
babhūvuḥ pādapāḥ sarve phalapuṣpābharānattāḥ । aṣṭāṃgaguṇayuktāmbuparipūrṇajalāśrayāḥ ।। anekadhāturatnādi nidhayaḥ pracakāsire । nispannaśasyasaṃpannā bahhūva vasudhā tadā ।।
bahukṣīrapradā gāva auṣadhayo guṇānvitāḥ । rasāś ca suguṇā āsan phalāni surasāni ca ।। evaṃ tatra subhadrāṇi sarvatrāpy abhavaṃs tadā । upadravāś ca sarve api sarvatra vilayaṃ gatāḥ ।।
sarve vighnagaṇā duṣṭā te apy atra vilayaṃ yayuḥ । sarve satvāḥ sukhāḍhyāś ca pracerire praharṣitāḥ ।। evaṃ tadā munīndrasya prabhāvena samaṃtataḥ । saddharmamaṃgalotsāhaṃ babhūva nirupadravaṃ ।।
evaṃ sa bhagavāṃs tatra kṛtvā bhadraṃ prabhāsayan । pradakṣiṇakrameṇaivaṃ pracakrāma nṛpālaye ।। tatra śodhāntare ramye prāsāde pariśodhite । chatradhvajavitānaiś ca maṇḍite visṛtāsane ।।
praviśya pādyam ādāya nṛpadattaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ । bhagavān bhāsayaṃs tatra śuddhāsane samāśrayan ।। tathā te sāṃghikāś cāpi sarve dattaṃ mahībhujā । svayaṃ samādāya svasvāsane samāśrayat ।।
evaṃ tatra samāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । nṛpatipramukhāḥ sarve lokā dṛṣṭvā pramoditāḥ ।। sarvapūjopahārāṃgaiḥ samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ । yathārhabhojanaiś cāpi praṇītaiḥ samatoṣayan ।।
tatas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ sasamahaṃ sa narādhipaḥ । dṛṣṭvāpanīya pātrāṇi tad dhastādīn aśodhayat ।। tataḥ kramukatāmbūlamahauṣaddhirasāyanaṃ । datvā kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā nanāma taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।।
tatra samudito rājā tasya śāstur jagadguroḥ । puro nīcāsanāsīno tasthau śrotuṃ vṛṣaṃ mudā ।। tathā maṃtrijanādyāś ca sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ । natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ tatra dharmam śrotum upāśrayan ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān samupāśritān । nṛpatiṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga sarvadārogyam astu vaḥ । sarve satvāś ca saddharmaniratā santu sarvadā ।।
evaṃ tvaṃ bho mahārāja sādhayitvā prayatnataḥ । sarvāṃ satvāṃ śubhe dharme yojayitvābhipālaya ।। evaṃ loke śubhaṃ kṛtvā bodhicaryāṃ samāhitaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cinu dharmaṃ samādarāt ।।
anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīrakaṃ । jīvitaṃ ca kṣaṇasthāyi dharma eva sahānugaḥ ।। iti matvā mahārāja kleśān durjayān valaiḥ । jitvā satvāṃc chubhe sthāpya pālaya sadvṛṣaṃ cinuḥ ।।
dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ yāyāḥ sadgatau sarvadā sukhaṃ । bhuktvā bodhicariṃ dhṛtvā caraṃ bodhim avāpnuyāḥ ।। evaṃ vijñāya rājeṃdra svayaṃ dharme samāhitaḥ । sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā cara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।
ity ādiśya nareṃdrāya salokāya śubhāśiṣaṃ । sasaṃgho bhagavān buddhaḥ svāśrame gaṃtum utthitaḥ ।। bhāsayaṃ sakalāṃl lokāṃ bhadraṃ kṛtvā samaṃtataḥ । svāśramābhimukhas tasmāt pratasthe kramataḥ purāt ।।
tatra sarve api lokā nṛpatipramukhā api । śāstus tasya sasaṃghasya prānuyayuḥ sahotsavaiḥ ।। tathā sa bhagavān gatvā sasāṃghiko nṛpādibhiḥ । lokaiḥ saha mahotsāhaiḥ svāśramaṃ samupāyayau ।।
tatra jetavanodyāne vihāre samupāśritaḥ । sasāṃghikaḥ sabhāsīnaḥ sa śāstā dharmam ādiśat ।। tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrutvā tatraiva te nṛpādayaḥ । sarve lokāḥ pramodanto rātrau nyūṣuḥ sahotsavaiḥ ।।
tasyām eva niśāyāṃ sa dūto alpāyūr jvarānvitaḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kurvan dehaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau ।। tatra svarge samutpannaḥ sa dūto vismayānvitaḥ । kutaś cyutaḥ kuhotpannaḥ katham iti vyaciṃtayat ।।
tadā sa manasādrākṣīn manuṣyebhyaś cyutāsmy ahaṃ । iha svarge samutpannaḥ saṃbuddhabhajanād iti ।। atha sa dūtapūrvī sa devaputraḥ prasāditaḥ । saṃbuddhasya guṇān smṛtvā punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
aho hy ahaṃ munīndrasya prasādād divi sāṃprataṃ । jāto asmi tan munīndrasya kuryāṃ saṃdarśanaṃ punaḥ ।। iti hi dūtapurvī sa devaputro viciṃtayan । snātvā sugaṃdhiliptāṃgaṃ śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ ।।
maulikuṇḍalamālādi divyālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ । divyapūjopacārāṃ dhṛtvā devaṃ sahācarat ।। tasyām eva niśāyāṃ sa devaputraḥ suraiḥ saha । avabhāsya prabhās tasmij jetāraṇye upācarat ।।
tatrodyāne vihāre taṃ bhagavaṃtaṃ munīśvaraṃ । ālokya sāṃjalir natvā purataḥ samupācarat ।। tatas taṃ śrīghanaṃ nāthaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāṃjaliḥ samupāśrayat ।।
atha sa bhagavāṃs tasya dṛṣṭvā cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tad āryyadharmam ākarṇya devaputraḥ sa bodhitaḥ । dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya dṛṣṭasatyo abhavaṃs tataḥ ।।
satkāyadṛṣṭibhūmīndhraṃ viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ । prabhitvā jñānavajreṇa saddharmaṃ sādhanotsukaḥ ।। pariśuddhāśayaḥ śrotaāpattiphalam āptavān । śāstus tasya padau natvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।।
bhagavann idam asmākaṃ gurubhir na kṛtaṃ khalu । na mātrā nāpi pitrā vā na jñātimitravāṃdhavaiḥ ।। na ceṣṭair brāhmaṇair vāpi na cāpi pūrvapretakaiḥ । na rājñā śramaṇaiś cānyair devair api kṛtaṃ khalu ।।
yad asmākaṃ kṛtaṃ bhadraṃ bhavatāsthiśiroccayāḥ । laṃghitā rudhirā cābdhir uchoṣitāś ca sāṃprataṃ ।। pihito pāpamārgaś ca svargamārgaś ca vaivṛtaḥ । darśito mokṣamārgo api tīrṇo duḥkhārṇavāpi ca ।।
prasādād bhavatām adya prāptaṃ śuddheṃdriyaṃ mayā । śāntam āryapadaṃ kāṃtaṃ saṃbodhiguṇasādhanaṃ ।। adya me saphalaṃ janma bhavatāṃ darśanād iha । saddharmaśravaṇād adya buddhaputro asmi sāṃprataṃ ।।
ity uktvā dūtapurvī sa devaputraḥ pramoditaḥ । tasya śāstur jagadvaṃdhoḥ pādau natvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhinaṃditāśayaḥ । tato anujñāṃ samāsādya suraiḥ saha divaṃ yayau ।।
tatra svarge sa samyātaḥ suramye svālaye sthitaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvāramaṃ devaiḥ sahāvasat ।। tatra dṛṣṭvāvabhāsaṃ taṃ prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ । vismitaḥ prātar utthāya vihāre samupācarat ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatiḥ sa pramoditaḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāṃjaliḥ samupāśritaḥ ।। tataḥ sa nṛpa utthāya sūttarāsaṅgam udvahan । jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitvā prārthayat taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।।
bhagavann atra niśāyāṃ ko bhavatāṃ samupāgataḥ । tad bhavatāṃ samupādiśyā māṃ bodhayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
anyo na hi sa rājeṃdra yo adya rātrāv ihāgātaḥ । api tu tāvako dūto devabhūtaḥ sa āgataḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa nṛpatiḥ sa savismayaḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ punar natvā tat karma paryapṛchataḥ ।।
bhavan kiṃ kadā tena dūtena sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ । yenāsau divi saṃjāto dṛṣṭasatyo bhavaty api ।। tad bhavān bhagavaṃc chāsta yat tena sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ । tat sarvaṃ samupākhyāya bodhayitum anāśayaṃ ।।
iti saṃprārthite rājñā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । kauśalaṃ taṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga tena devena yat kṛtaṃ । tad atra saṃpravakṣyāmi tava cittaprabodhane ।।
yat tvayā preṣito dūto mayi rājagṛhe sthite । yena saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā tathā hy ahaṃ samāgataḥ ।। sa sādhus tāvako dūto mayā sārddham ihāgataḥ । saddharmadeśanāṃ śrutvā śraddhābhaktisamanvitaḥ ।।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācarac chāsane mama । ālpāyuṣko hy asau bhadrī vihāre atra nivāsitaḥ ।। kāladharmābhisaṃyukte tyaktvā dehaṃ divaṃ yayau ।। sa hy asau tāvako dūto rātrāv adyeha bhāsayan ।
mama saṃdarśanaṃ kartuṃ devalokaiḥ sahāgataḥ ।। mama pūjāṃ vidhāyāsau kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇāṃ । natvā sādaram āśritya saddharmaṃ śraddhayāśṛṇot ।। matsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā dṛṣṭasatyaḥ pramoditaḥ ।
natvā māṃ sa punaḥ svarge devalokaiḥ sahācarat ।। tatra sa svālaye ramye sthitvā devaiḥ sahāraman । triratnabhajanaṃ kurvan prācaraṃ vasate sukhaṃ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena dūtaḥ sa tāvakaḥ kṛtī ।
svarge saukhyaṃ ciraṃ bhuktvā kramād bodhim avāpsyati ।। evaṃ vijñāya rājeṃdra saṃsāre atra mahatsukhaṃ । yadīchasi sadā bhadre caritavyaṃ tvayādarāt ।। bhadraṃ tu jāyate śīghraṃ triratnabhajanodyamāt ।
tat triratnam upāśritya bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। triratne yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tan naiva kṣiṇuyā kvacit । yāvad bodhipadaṃ dadyā evaṃ mahattaraṃ vṛṣaṃ ।। ye triratnaṃ bhajanty atra na te gachanti durgatiṃ ।
sadaiva sadgatiṃ yānti bodhiṃ ca samavāpnuyuḥ ।। tisro hīmāḥ samākhyātā agrāḥ prajñaptayo nṛpa । yatra kiṃ cit kṛtaṃ karma tadvipāko mahān smṛtāḥ ।। tadyathā katamās tisro agrāḥ prajñaptayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
triratne prakṛtā yās tā agrāḥ prajñaptayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tadyathā sarvasatvānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ । buddha eva mahān agro jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭho varottamaḥ ।। ye buddhaśraddhayā bhaktyā prabhajaṃti prasāditāḥ ।
sarve atyagraprasannās te jyeṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhā varottamāḥ ।। tadagrābhiprasannānāṃ vipāko apy agra uttamaḥ । tathā dharmāś ca ye sarve saṃskṛtā vāpy asaṃkṛtāḥ ।। teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ buddhadharmāgra ucyate ।
tatra dharme prasannā ye te agre hi saṃprasannitāḥ । tad agrābhiprasannānāṃ vipāko apy agra ucyate ।। ye ca saṃghā gaṇās teṣāṃ buddhasaṃgho agra ucyate । tatra saṃghe prasannā ye te agre abhisaṃprasādinaḥ ।।
teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipāko apy agra ucyate । etāḥ prajñaptayas tisro hy agrāḥ khyāto munīśvaraiḥ ।। tad atra śraddhayā rāja triratne saṃprasannadhīḥ । satkāraiḥ samupāśritya bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt ।।
etatpuṇyam asaṃkhyeyam aprameyaṃ mahattaraṃ । sarvasatvamahāsaukhyaguṇasaṃpattidāyakaṃ ।। evaṃ matvā mahatpuṇyaṃ sarvān satvān prabodhayat । triratnabhajanotsāhaiś cārayasva śubhe nṛpa ।।
evaṃ te sarvadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa nṛpatir mudā । tatheti hi pratijñāya prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpa utthāya natvā taṃ jagadīśvaraṃ । mahānaṃdamahotsāhaiḥ svapuraṃ sajano yayau ।। tatra sa nṛpatī rājā prāsādatalam āśritaḥ । sa maṃtripaurikān sarvān samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।।
maṃtriṇaḥ paurikāḥ sarve śṛṇudhvaṃ vacanaṃ mama । yadi vāṃchāsti vo bhadre triratnaṃ bhajatādarat ।। yavad ayaṃ jagacchāstā viharaty atra sāṃghikaḥ । tāvad asya munīndrasya bhajata sarvadotsavaiḥ ।। vihāre sarvadā gatvā śraddhayā samupāśritāḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mudā carata sadvṛtau ।। sarvāṃś ca saugatān bhikṣūn sarvopakaraṇair api । satkṛtya śraddhayāmaṃtrya mānayadhvaṃ sadādarāt ।। etan me vacanaṃ śrutvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
saṃbodhipraṇidhānena carata bodhicārikāṃ ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya labhata saugatiṃ gatiṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te maṃtriṇo janāḥ ।
sarve vīrādayo lokās tatheti pratiśuśruvuḥ ।। tadā sarve api te lokāḥ saddharmasādhanodyatāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracerire samoditāḥ ।। tadārabhya sadā tatra maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।
sarvatra sarvadāpy āsīt triratnasyānubhāvataḥ ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā te kathyate mayā । tvam apy evaṃ sadā rājan triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। saddharmaṃ samupāśritya cara nityaṃ sadā śubhe ।
lokāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । triratnaśaraṇe sthāpya pālanīyāḥ sadā tvayā ।। evaṃ te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। dūtāvadānaṃ yad idaṃ mudā ye śṛṇvaṃti ye cāpi niśāmayanti । te sarva evaṃ tridive vrajanti saṃbuddhaloke api saranti cānte ।।
athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ tam arhantaṃ praṇatvaivam abravīt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā sa sugatātmajaḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathātrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru ।।
tadyathā bhagavāṃc chāstā śrīghano arhan munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ tathā sarvaiś ca sāṃghikaiḥ । tatraiva jetakodyāne vihāre vyaharat purā ।।
tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokaiḥ samāgataiḥ । devadānavagaṃdharvair yakṣakinnararākṣasaiḥ ।। siddhair vidyādharaiś cāpi nāgendrair garuḍair api । lokapālaiḥ sasainyaiś ca brāhmaṇaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।।
yogibhir yatibhiś cāpi nirgranthibhiś ca tāpasaiḥ । rājabhiḥ kṣatriyaiś cāpi tathā rājakumārakaiḥ ।। vaiśyaiś ca maṃtribhiḥ śreṣṭhair gṛhasthaiś ca mahājanaiḥ । vaṇigbhiḥ sārthavāhaiś ca śilpibhiḥ paurikair api ।।
grāmyair jānapadaiś cāpi kārpaṭikais tathāparaiḥ । triratnadarśanotsāhaiḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ ।। satkṛto mānito nityaṃ pūjyamāno abhivaṃditaḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena varṣaṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ sadā ।।
tadā tatra pure rājā prasenajin nṛpādhipaḥ । saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā triratnam abhajan mudā ।। tad dṛṣṭvā tīrthikāḥ sarve īrṣyāroṣāhatāśayāḥ । saṃmīlya saugataṃ dharmaṃ pratikṣipyaivam abruvan ।।
bhavanto yad ayaṃ buddhaḥ sarvajña ṛddhimān kṛtī । tatsarvān imāṃ lokān svaṃ dharme saṃniyojayet ।। tadāsmadvacanaṃ śrotum apīchen nātra kaścana । sarve naḥ śrāvakāś cāpi bhajeyuḥ sugataṃ jinaṃ ।।
tadā sarve vayaṃ lokai niṃdyamānaḥ samaṃtataḥ । katham atra cariṣyāmas tad anyatra caremahi ।। iti sarvair api prokte tīrthikopāsako dvijaḥ । sarvāns tāns tīrthikaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।।
bhavaṃto ma viṣīdatvaṃ kartuṃ arhati sarvathā । tad upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yenānyatra carej jinaḥ ।। iti tāns tīrthikān sarvān bodhayitvā sa durmatiḥ । nṛpater antike gatvā sādaram evam abravīt ।।
śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yad dhitaṃ te tad ucyate । tathā tvayā samādhāya caritavyaṃ sadādarāt ।। yad ayaṃ muṇḍito bhikṣuḥ kuladharmavināśakṛt । jātidharmaparibhraṣṭaḥ saṃsāravṛttiniṃdakaḥ ।।
māyāvī kutsitācāro duḥśīlo lokavaṃcakaḥ । svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayitum ihāgataḥ ।। tad asya darśanaṃ rājaṃ karttavyaṃ na kadā cana । grahītavyaṃ na nāmāpi śrotavyaṃ nāpi tad vacaḥ ।।
satkāraṃ na ca karttavyaṃ dātavyaṃ nāpi kiṃ cana । āśrame api na gantavyaṃ sthātavyaṃ na tadantike ।। darśanaṃ ye prakurvanti tasya bhikṣor durātmanaḥ । te sarve narake yāyuḥ sadgatiṃ na kadā cana ।।
ye ca śṛṇvanti tad vākyaṃ sarve te nilayaṃ gatāḥ । tīvraduḥkhābhisaṃtaptā vaseyur anutāpitāḥ ।। satkāraṃ ye ca kurvaṃti sarve te vilayaṃ gatāḥ । daridrā durgatiṃ gatvā bhrameyur nihatāśayāḥ ।।
ye ca dānaṃ prakurvanti tatrāśirluhitāśayāḥ । te api ca narake yātā duḥkhāny evam avāpnuyuḥ ।। tadāśrame ca gachaṃti sarve te duritāṅkitāḥ । kuṣṭhādi rogasaṃtaptā yāyuś ca niraye acirāt ।।
ye ca taiḥ saha tiṣṭhanti te sarve pāpasaṃgitāḥ । tīvraduḥkhāgnisaṃdagdhā careyu niraye sadā ।। gṛhnanti ye ca mannāma teṣāṃ geheṣu sarvadā । lakṣmīr maiva śrayet tatra nairṛtir eva saṃśrayet ।।
ye buddhaṃ bhajanty atra te te sarve apy adharmiṇaḥ । kadāpi sadgatiṃ naiva yāṃti dūragatim eva hi ।। iti matvā mahārāja sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi । satkāraṃ darśanaṃ tasya karttavyaṃ naiva ke cana ।।
kiṃ dharmaṃ saugataṃ dharmaṃ yan mithyā parikalpitaṃ । tat tasya duryater dharmaṃ śrotavyaṃ naiva kena cit ।। yasya dharmo hi sarvatra vedaśāstre na gaṇyate । sa kiṃ dharmātmako buddhas tat tatra maṃgalaṃ na hi ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa paribodhitaḥ । triratnabhajanotsāhaśaithilyakṣubhito abhavat ।। tatas tasya vacaḥ śrutvā tīrthikopāsakasya saḥ । nṛpatis tairthike dharme abhilalāṣa prasāditaḥ ।।
tatraiko gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī saṃbuddhopāsakaḥ sudhīḥ । taṃ tīrthyopāsakaṃ dṛṣṭvā bodhayitum abhāṣata ।। kim evaṃ durmate buddho dharmarājo api niṃdyate । mā maivaṃ vadatām atra tvam eva narakaṃ vrajeḥ ।।
yo loke samutpannaḥ sarvakleśān vinirjayan । jitvā māragaṇān sarvān saṃbodhijñānam āptavān ।। sarvai brahmādibhir lokaiḥ saṃstuto vaṃdito arcitaḥ । mānitaḥ satkṛto buddhas tvayaiva niṃdyate kathaṃ ।।
yenaiva trijagallokāṃ putravat pratipālitaṃ । pūjanīyaḥ kathaṃ nāthaṃ dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। buddha eva jagannātho dayāluḥ sadguṇākaraḥ । sarvasatvahitādhāno advayavādī vināyakaḥ ।।
sarvajñaḥ sugato bhadrarūpaḥ sarvahitārthabhṛt । sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ ।। nirjitakleśa ātmajñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño jagadguruḥ । saṃbuddho arhañ jinas trāyī dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavānn eva sarvatraidhātukeṣv api । agraḥ śreṣṭho mahāñ jeṣṭho nānyaḥ kaścid ato adhikaḥ ।। tasmād asya munīndrasya satkāraṃ śraddhayā sadā । śaraṇagamanaṃ kṛtvā śrotavyaṃ dharmam ādarāt ।।
ye buddhe śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ । sarvadā sadgatau saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yānti jinālaye ।। śṛṇvanti ye ca tad dharmaṃ te api no yānti durgatiṃ । sadā svarge sukhaṃ bhuktvā yāyuś cānte sunirvṛtiṃ ।।
bhajanti ye ca saṃgheṣu te api na yānti durgatiṃ । sadā dharmaratāḥ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yānti sukhāvatiṃ ।। evaṃ ye ye triratnānāṃ sarvadā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajanti bodhimānasāḥ ।।
sarve te sadguṇādhārāḥ sarvasatvahitārthinaḥ । kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।। tenāyaṃ bhagavānn eva jagannātho jagadguruḥ । dharmarājo jagadbharttā jagattrāyī vināyakaḥ ।।
tenāsya sadguroḥ śāstuḥ śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । saddharmaṃ sarvadā śrutvā kartum arhati satkṛtiṃ ।। ye cāpy asya munīndrasya pratikṣipanti śāsanaṃ । sadgatiṃ naiva te yānti durgatim eva sarvadā ।।
iti matvā na karttavyā buddhe niṃdā kathaṃ cana । triratnabhajanāny eva karttavyāni śubhārthibhiḥ ।। ye triratnaṃ bhajanty atra sarve te bodhibhāginaḥ । bodhisatvā mahāsatvā bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ ।।
tena te api mahāsatvās triratnopāsakā api । śraddhayā praṇatiṃ tesāṃ karttum arhanti sarvadā ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikopāsakaś ca saḥ । taṃ buddhopāsakaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। ā kim evaṃ tvayā proktaṃ kiṃ buddho atāpasā ayatiḥ ।
pūraṇo brahmavijñas tapasvī saṃyamī sudhīḥ ।। tat tasya pūraṇasyāgre buddhaḥ kiṃ vaktum utsahet । bālakān eva vañcitvā hy asaddharmme yunakti saḥ ।। pūraṇa eva sarveṣāṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ ।
ṛddhimatāṃ mahān agro mātraikaś cit tato adhikaḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa buddhopāsakas tataḥ । tīrthikopāsikaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar eva tam abravīt ।। are kiṃ jñāyate tasya saṃbuddhasya guṇas tvayā ।
yenaiva kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā pālitaṃ putravaj jagat ।। yasya loke dayā nāsti tena kiṃ pālyate jagat । kevalalobhasatkāraṃ hetunādombhiko hi saḥ ।। tapasvī yogavit prājña ṛddhimān siddhimān api ।
yasya nāsti dayā satve sa kim śāstā jagadguruḥ ।। yo dṛṣṭvā sakalān satvān kṛpayā saṃprabodhayan । saddharme yojayaty atra sa eva jagatāṃ guruḥ ।। tasmād atra jagacchāstā sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt ।
buddha eva jagannātho jagattrāyī jagadguruḥ ।। nāsti buddhasamaḥ kaś cit sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ । tena brahmādidevaiḥ sa vaṃdanīyo munīśvaraḥ ।। yato ayaṃ śrīghanaḥ trāyī ṣaḍabhijño vināyakaḥ ।
munīndro arhaṃ subhadrāṃśas tena tasyādhiko hi kaḥ ।। tenāyaṃ sugato buddho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā sarve bhajanīyaḥ śubhechubhiḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikopāsako atha saḥ ।
roṣāgniparidagdhāsyas taṃ bauddham evam abravīt ।। ā evam ucyate ko atra pūraṇāt para uttamaḥ । yatīr vijño mahābhijñaḥ sa eva trijagadguruḥ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā saṃbuddhopāsako api saḥ ।
sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā bhūmāv evaṃ tam abravīt ।। buddhād anyo viśiṣṭaḥ kas traidhātubhuvaneṣv api । bahudhā kiṃ pravādena buddha eva jagatprabhuḥ ।। tenety ukte sa ruṣṭātmā tīrthikopāsakas tadā ।
kopāgniparidagdhāṃgas taṃ buddham evam abravīt ।। yadi buddho viśiṣṭaḥ syāt pūraṇād arhato yateḥ । sarvasvaṃ me tavādhīnaṃ dāsaś cāpi bhavāmy ahaṃ ।। yadi buddhād viśiṣṭo hi pūraṇo arhaṃ mahāmatiḥ ।
sarvasvaṃ te mamādhīnaṃ dāsaś cāpi bhaveḥ khalu ।। iti tenodite tatra saṃbuddhopāsako api saḥ । tatheti vaṃdhanikṣepaṃ kṛtvā svīkaraṇaṃ vyadhāt ।। tayor etat pravādatvaṃ prasenajin narādhipaḥ । matvāmātyān samāhūya purar evam abhāṣata ।।
gachadhvaṃ maṃtriṇaḥ sarve buddhatairthikayor api । nirṇayitvā vivādatve mimāṃsā kriyatām iha ।। iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te maṃtriṇo janāḥ । sahasā taj janān sarvān samāhūyaivam ādiśat ।।
bhavanto nṛpater evam ājñāṃ śrutvā samāhitāḥ । sarvatra vijite ghaṇṭānādaiś codaya tad drutaṃ ।। iti tair maṃtribhiḥ proktaiḥ śrutvā te sajanās tathā । ghaṇṭāvaghoṣanaṃ kṛtvā sarvatraivaṃ ghoṣayan ।।
śṛṇvantu paurikāḥ sarve ito ahni saptame ahani । bauddhatairthikasaṃvāde mimāṃsātra bhaviṣyati ।। ye ye atra draṣṭum ichanti sarve te samupāgatāḥ । buddhasya tīrthikasyāpi prabhāvaṃ draṣṭum arhata ।।
evaṃ te vijite tatra sarvatra viṣayeṣv api । ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā maṃtriṇāṃ pura āyayuḥ ।। tatas te sajanāḥ sarve rājño antikam upāgatāḥ । praṇatvaitat pravṛttāṃtaṃ purataḥ saṃnyavedayan ।।
tato ahni saptame prāpte sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ । vistīrṇe bhūtale ramye tad draṣṭum upatasthire ।। tathā devā aneke ca taddarśanakutūhalāḥ । antarīkṣe samāśritya saṃtasthuḥ pratimoditāḥ ।।
evaṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu nṛpamaṃtrijanādiṣu । naikaśatasahasreṣu sannipāteṣu sarvataḥ ।। tīrthikopāsakas tatra sa gomaye praleṣite । maṃḍale gaṃdhapuṣpādipūjāṃgaiḥ samapūjayat ।।
tataḥ sa sāṃjalir natvā jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ । udvahann uttarāsaṃgaṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। yena satyena ṣaḍvijñāḥ śāstāraḥ pūraṇādayaḥ । bhagavaṃto mahābhijñā arhanto brahmacāriṇaḥ ।।
anena satyabhāvena sarvān etān yatīśvarān । etatpūjopahārāṇi prānugaṃchaṃtu saṃmukhaṃ ।। evaṃ saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā tīrthikopāsako mudā । tāni paṃcopahārāṇi prādāya gagaṇe akṣipat ।।
tena kṣiprakṣiptamātrāṇi tāni sarvāṇi bhūtale । patitāny astaṃgatāny eva sahasādarśane yayuḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā sasurā lokāḥ sarve te bhūmipādayaḥ । uccair nādair hasantas taṃ tairthikam eva menire ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā dhikpravādaṃ ca śrutvā sa tairthiko apatat । tataś cirāt samutthāya lajjābhinnamukhāśayaḥ ।। trasito adhomukhodraṣṭo niṣprabhaḥ parikaṃpitaḥ । bhrastaskaṃdhaḥ kare kaṇḍaṃ sthāpya tasthau vimurchitaḥ ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā sa prasannātmā buddhopāsako mudā । prakṛtvā maṇḍalaṃ tatra gomayapratilepite ।। paṃcopahārapūjaṃgaiḥ samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ । udvahann uttarāsaṅgaṃ jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ ।।
sāṃjaliḥ purataḥ sthitvā saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । smṛtvā natvā tathā satyaṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। yato ayaṃ bhagavān buddhaḥ sarvalokavināyakaḥ । tena satyena sarvāṇi puṣpāṇīmāni sūdakaṃ ।।
idaṃ saurabhyadhūpaṃ ca bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ । saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ nāthaṃ prābhiyāntu vihāyasā ।। iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā sa buddhopāsako mudā । tāni sarvopahārāṇi prādāya gagaṇe akṣipat ।।
tāni tena prakṣiptāni sarvāṇi gagaṇe asaran । tāni sarvāṇi puṣpāṇi chatrībhūtvācaran kramāt ।। dhūpo meghavad ambho api vaiḍūryyavat tadācarat । tad dṛṣṭvā janatā sarvā mahāścaryyaṃ pralehire ।।
krameṇa tāni sarvāṇi pracaranti vihāyasā । jhaṭiti jetakāraṇye vihāre saṃmukhaṃ yayuḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā sajanakāyo api pratihāryaṃ tad adbhutaṃ । jayaśabdaṃ prakurvantaḥ paśyanto anuyayur mudā ।।
tatra sarvāṇi puṣpāṇi chatrībhūtvā jagadguroḥ । saṃbuddhasya jagacchāstur upari samupāśrayan ।। tad dhūpam agratas tasya tasthau kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ । padāmbujaṃ tad ambho api papāta viyataḥ sarat ।।
tat samālokya sarve te dvijādi paurikā janāḥ । prasāditā munīndrasya sabhāyāṃ samupācaran ।। sarve pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṛtāṃjalipuṭā mudā । bhagāvantaṃ muniṃ natvā sarve te samupāśrayan ।।
sa buddhopāsakaś cāpi natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthau kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। tīrthikopāsakaḥ so api tad dṛṣṭvā vismayānvitāḥ । mahad buddhānubhāvatvaṃ matvā draṣṭum upāśrayat ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān । āryasatyam upādiśya punar evam upādiśat ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ sādhavaḥ sarve āryadharmaṃ samucyate । yat triratnaṃ samākhyātaṃ tat trilokye mahattaraṃ ।।
tadyathā sarvalokānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ । sarveṣām api bhadrārthaṃ saddharmaṃ saṃprakāśaye ।। sa saṃbuddho jagacchāstā sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ । jagannātho jagattrātā buddharatnam idaṃ varaṃ ।।
atra yaiḥ śraddhayā karmaṃ dānādi sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ । teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipākaiḥ phalam uttamaṃ ।। aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhipadadāyakaṃ । evaṃ matvātra saṃbuddhaṃ bhajata sarvadā mudā ।। yāvataś cātra saṃsāre saṃskṛtā vāpy asaṃskṛtāḥ ।
dharmās teṣāṃ mahān agro virāgo dharmaṃ uttamaḥ ।। dharmaratnam idaṃ ye atra prabhajanti prasāditāḥ । teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipāke phalam uttamaṃ ।। aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhijñānadāyakaṃ ।
tad etat saugataṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā bhajaṃti saṃvaraṃ ।। yāvantaś cātra trailokye saṃghāḥ pūgā gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ । teṣām agro mahān khyāto buddhasaṃgho jagadvaraḥ ।। saṃgharatnam idaṃ ye atra bhajanti śraddhayā mudā ।
teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipāke phalam uttamaṃ ।। aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhimārgacālakaṃ । tad atra saugate saṃghe bhajata śraddhayādarāt ।। idaṃ ratnatrayaṃ khyātaṃ sarvasatvaśubhaṃkaraṃ ।
vāñchitārthapradaṃ siddhaṃ saṃbodhijñānadāyakaṃ ।। tad etat tritayaṃ ratnaṃ saṃbodhipadavāṃchibhiḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ pūjanīyaṃ samādarāt ।। ye triratnaṃ sadā nityaṃ pūjayanti prasāditāḥ ।
na te māravaśaṃ yātā bhavaṃti bodhilābhinaḥ ।। iti matvā triratnaṃ tad dṛṣṭvā kṛtvānumodanāṃ । sāñjalipraṇatiṃ kṛtvā dūrād vanditum arhatha ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te brāhmaṇādayaḥ ।
sarve lokāḥ prasīdantas triratnaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। tatra ke cij janā bhadrāḥ saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । śikṣāpadaṃ samādāya prācarat saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। ke cid bhadrāśayā vijñā saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
pravrajyāvratam ādāya prācarad brahmacārikāṃ ।। tataḥ kleśān vinirjitya saṃsārabhogyanispṛhāḥ । sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya babhūva brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। etat sarvaṃ samālokya tīrthikopāsako api saḥ ।
vismitaḥ suprasannātmā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sa tairthikas tasya munīndrasya padāmbuje । sāñjalipraṇataś caivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ vyadhān mudā ।। adyārabhya sadāpy asya munīndrasya jagadguroḥ ।
saddharmaṃ samupāśritya triratnopāsako bhave ।। etatpuṇyavipākena loke andhe aparināyake । saṃbodhijñānam āsādya bhaveyaṃ sugato jinaḥ ।। atīrṇāṃ tārayiṣyāmi mocayiṣyāmy amocitān ।
sarvān āśvāsayiṣyāmi hy anāśvastān suduḥkhinaḥ ।। satvān nirvāpayiṣyāmi bhavālayād anirvṛtān । kariṣyāmi sadā bhadraṃ traidhātubhuvaneṣv api ।। iti tena kṛtaṃ bodhipraṇidhānaṃ svacetasā ।
matvā sa bhagavān smitaṃ visasarja saraśmikaṃ ।। tadā tā raśmayaḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ sarvāḥ samaṃtataḥ । lokeṣu prasṛtā bhadraṃ saukhyaṃ kṛtvā praserire ।। yā adhastād gatābhāso sarvatra narakeṣu tāḥ ।
prasṛtā avabhāsyaivaṃ bhadrasaukhyaṃ pracakrire ।। tatprabhābhiḥ parispṛṣṭā sarve te narakāśritāḥ । nirduḥkhā saukhyam āsādya vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। tatas te nārakāḥ satvāḥ sarve te narake sthitāḥ ।
ekaikanarakeṣv evaṃ saṃmīlya saṃvabhāṣire ।। aho citraṃ kim adyaivaṃ mahat saukhyaṃ prajāyate । itaś cyutāḥ kim anyatra samutpannā vayaṃ khalu ।। iti saṃvādināṃ tesāṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃprabodhane ।
bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ prerayan narake prati ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā nārakāḥ sarve vismitāḥ saṃprasāditāḥ । bhūya ekatra saṃmīlya mitha evaṃ vabhāṣire ।। aho vayam itaś cyutvā naivānyatra gatāḥ khalu ।
kiṃ tv asyāpūrvarūpasya prabhāvān naḥ śubhāyate ।। nūnam ayaṃ jagannātho buddho asmān duḥkhapīḍitān । samīkṣya kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā samuddharttum ihāgataḥ ।। tad asyātra vayaṃ sarve satkṛtya śraddhayādarāt ।
sarvadā śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktum arhāmahe adhunā ।। iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te saṃprasāditāḥ । asyaiva śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇatvā saṃprabhejire ।। tatas te nārakāḥ sarve tatpāpaparimocitāḥ ।
pariśuddhāḥ śubhātmānaḥ sadgatiṃ sahasā yayuḥ ।। evaṃ tān nārakān sarvāḥ samuddhṛtya prabhāś ca tāḥ । sarvāḥ pratyāgatās tatra saṃbuddhasya puro asaran ।। evam ūrddhaṃ gatāyāś ca raśmayas tāḥ samaṃtataḥ ।
sarvān devālayāṃ lokān avabhāsya praserire ।। yāvad bhavāgraparyantam avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ । prasāritāḥ tato gāthā nisṛtāḥ samacodayan ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ ।
puṇyam eva jagatsāraṃ tat puṇyaṃ cinutādarāt ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane । dhunīta mṛtyusainyāni carata saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। yo hy asmin saugate dharme cariṣyati samāhitaḥ ।
sa hitvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। tat triratnaṃ sadā yūyaṃ saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajata bodhiprāptaye ।। evaṃ tad ghoṣam ākarṇya sarvadevāḥ prabodhitāḥ ।
triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire sadādarāt ।। evaṃ tā raśmayo devāñ codayitvā samaṃtataḥ । punaḥ pratyāgatās tatra buddhāntikam upāyayuḥ ।। tatra tā raśmayaḥ sarvā ekībhūtvābhipiṇḍitāḥ ।
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sūṣṇīṣe antardadhur muneḥ ।। taddṛṣṭvā sasabhālokāḥ sarve te vismayānvitāḥ । śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti dhyātvā niṣedire ।। athāyuṣmān mahānando matvā tal lokaciṃtitaṃ ।
utthāya sāṃjālir natvā papracha taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। vigatoddhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ । nākāraṇe śaṃkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadeśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ ।। tat kālaṃ svayam evam adhigamya dhīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jineṃdra kāṅkṣitānāṃ dhīrabhir ।
munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ ।। nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ । yasyārthe smitam upadarśayaṃti dhīrās taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti janoghāḥ ।। tad bhavān sarvasatvānāṃ cittābhiparibodhane ।
yad abhilaṣitaṃ kāryaṃ tad upadeṣṭum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । āyuṣmantaṃ tam ānaṃdaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। evam etan mahānaṃda nāhetupratyayaṃ jināḥ ।
saṃbuddhāḥ sugatāḥ sarve darśayanti smitaṃ kvacit ।। śṛṇv ānaṃda yadarthe ahaṃ smitaṃ muñcāmi sāṃprataṃ । tadarthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvasatvaprabodhane ।। paśyasi yad ayaṃ śreṣṭhī tīrthikopāsako mudā ।
mamātra śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇidhānaṃ karoti hi ।। etatpuṇyavipākena trikalpāntam anātmavit । kramād bodhicārīḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya bhavet sudhīḥ ।। tataḥ kleśagaṇāñ jitvā sarvān māragaṇān api ।
bodhiṃ prāpyācalo nāma tathāgato bhaviṣyati ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdādi bhikṣavaḥ । sarve te suprasannāsyāḥ prābhyanandan savismayāḥ ।। tathā tena munīndreṇa vyākhyātaṃ sa tairthikaḥ ।
śrutvānumodanāṃ kṛtvā prābhyanandan savismayaḥ ।। tataḥ sa sarvadā nityaṃ satkṛtya śraddhayā mudā । triratnabhajānaṃ kṛtvā prācarat saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate ।
tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja triratnasevako bhava ।। prajāś cāpi tathā rājaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । triratnabhajanotsāhe saṃcārayitum arhasi ।। tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । satyam iti pratijñāya prābhyanāndat sa pārthikaḥ ।। śṛṇvantīdaṃ narā ye munivarakathitaṃ tairthikasyāvadānaṃ ye cāpi śrāvayanti pramuditamānasaḥ śraddhayā bhaktiyuktāḥ । te sarve bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇabharā bhadracaryā caranto bhuktvā satsaukhyabhadraṃ jinavaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodāḥ ।।
athāśoko mahīnāthaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ tam arhantaṃ praṇatvā prārthayat punaḥ ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ tvaṃ arhati ।।
iti tena narendreṇa prārthitaṃ sa yatīśvaraḥ । upagupto narendran taṃ samālokyaivaṃ ādiśat ।। śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ tat pravakṣyāmi tava puṇyavivṛddhaye ।।
tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। ekasmin samaye tatra śrāvastyā upakaṇṭhike । jetāraṇye mahodyāne vihāre śrāvakaiḥ saha ।।
bhikṣubhiś cailakaiś cāpi bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ । upāsikābhir anyaiś ca bodhisatvagaṇair api ।। sarvasatvahitārthena bodhicaryaṃ prakāśayan । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra prabhāsayan ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ । śakrādayo api devendrā brahmādilokapālakāḥ ।। daityeṃdrā garuḍā nāgā yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnarāḥ । siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi rākṣasāś ca maharddhikāḥ ।।
ṛṣayo brāhmaṇā cāpi kṣatriyāś ca narādhipāḥ । vaiśyā rājakumārāś ca maṃtriṇo amātyakā janāḥ ।। gṛhasthāḥ sārthavāhāś ca vaṇijaḥ śilpino api ca । paurā jānapadā grāmyā anye kārpaṭikā api ।।
sarve te samupāgatya tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ । dṛṣṭvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇatvā samupācaran ।। yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya natvā sāṃjalayo mudā । parivṛtya puraskṛtya sarve te samupāśrayan ।।
tān sarvān samupāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān muniḥ । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tad dharmaṃ samupākarṇya sarve te saṃprabodhitāḥ । dharmavaiśeṣam ājñāya babhuvur bodhivāṃchitāḥ ।।
tadā tatra pure rājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ । yadā na sugatas tatra tadā tīrthikabhāg abhūt ।। yadā tu sugatas tatra sasāṃghikaḥ samāgataḥ । tadā sa nṛpatir nityaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ sadābhajat ।।
tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra kaścid ārāmiko vanāt । navaṃ padmaiḥ samādāya rājñe dātuṃ pure aviśat ।। tatraikapathi taṃ dṛṣṭvā tīrthikopāsiko mudā । sahasā tasya puro gatvā prārthayat taṃ saroruhaṃ ।। bho mālinn idaṃ padmaṃ yadi vikretum ichasi ।
ucitaṃ mūlyam ādāya mahyaṃ dātuṃ tvam arhasi ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā mālikaḥ lubhitāśayaḥ । yadīchati bhavān dadyām iti taṃ dātum aichata ।। tasminn eva kṣaṇe tatra gṛhastho anāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।
puṣpārthī samupāyāto mālikaṃ tam apṛchata ।। bho mālinn idaṃ padmaṃ yadi vikretum ichati । dviguṇaṃ mūlyam ādāya bhavān me dātum arhati ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikopāsako api saḥ ।
taddviguṇena mūlyena tad padmaṃ samayācata ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa cāpy anāthapiṇḍadaḥ । taddvaiguṇyena mūlyena kamalaṃ tam ayācata ।। tac chrutvā tairthikaḥ so api madadarpābhimāninaḥ ।
tattriguṇamūlyena gṛhītuṃ taṃ samaichata ।। tad dṛṣṭvā sa gṛhastheṇānāthapiṇḍadotsahī । caturguṇena mūlyena padmaṃ tam abhyayācata ।। evaṃ tau gṛhapatī so tha yāvac chatasaharsrakaiḥ ।
mūlya taṃ padmam ādāya mālinaṃ taṃ yayācatuḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvārāmikaḥ sa api pravarddhayan parasparaṃ । tayor dvayor adatvaiva manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। ayaṃ gṛhapatiḥ śreṣṭho hy anāthapiṇḍadaḥ sudhīḥ ।
acapalo mahādhīraḥ sthirasatvo vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। kasyārthe nv idaṃ padmam iyan mūlyena yācate । nūnam atra mahaddhetur bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। tad etat paripṛchāva dāsyāmi sadguṇārthine ।।
iti dhyātvā svacittena sa ārāmika utsukaḥ । tairthikaṃ taṃ samālokya paprachaivaṃ samādarāt ।। bho puruṣa bhavān kasya kāryasyārthe idaṃ kajaṃ । iyanmūlyena vikretum ichati tad vadasva me ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa tairthikaḥ pramoditaḥ । ārāmikaṃ tam ālokya prabodhayitum abravīt ।। yaḥ śrīpatir jagadbharttā nārāyano janārdanaḥ । tasya pūjāṃ kariṣyāmi tad idaṃ dehi me ambujaṃ ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvārāmiko sānubodhitaḥ । anāthapiṇḍadaṃ taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kāryam apṛchata ।। bho sādho bhavaṃś cāpi kim artham idam ambujaṃ । bahumūlyaiva samāharttum ichati tad vadasva me ।।
iti tad vacanaṃ śrutvā so anāthapiṇḍadaḥ sudhīḥ । ārāmikaṃ tam ālokya prabodhayitum abravīt ।। sādhu sādhu mahābhāga yad idaṃ te saroruhaṃ । bahumūlyena vāṃchāmi tad arthaṃ kathyate śṛṇu ।।
yo atra śauddhodanī rājā cakravarttī nṛpādhipaḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbodhisādhanodyataḥ ।। sarvatra bhuvane loke kleśākulāsamāhite । bodhicaryāvihīne atra mlechadharmapravarttate ।।
bodhicaryāṃ svayaṃ dhṛtvā prakāśayitum udyataḥ । sarvarājyaṃ parityajya sarvāṃś cāpi parigrahān ।। vairāgyadharmam āśritya saṃsārabhoganispṛhaḥ । gayāśīrṣe nage gatvā kṛtvā tapaḥ suduṣkaraṃ ।।
tato loke hitaṃ kartuṃ samutthāya samāhitaḥ । bodhivṛkṣatalāsīnas tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। tatra māragaṇān sarvāñ jitvā kleśagaṇān api । saṃbodhijñānaṃ āsādya buddho bhavati sāṃprataṃ ।।
so ayaṃ buddho jagacchāstā jagannātho jagadguruḥ । jagadbharttā jagattrāyī dharmarājā munīśvaraḥ ।। sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śrimān ṣaḍabhijño vināyakaḥ । satyavādī mahādhīraḥ satyadharmaśubhārthabhṛt ।।
samantabhadrarūpāṃśaḥ saumyarūpo jiteṃdriyaḥ । dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṃḍitaḥ ।। bhagavāñ chrīghano brahmavihāriko guṇākaraḥ । sarvatraidhātukādhīśaḥsarvaduṣṭapraśāntakṛt ।।
sarvamāravijetārhaṃ saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ । vāñchitārthapradātāraś ciṃtāmaṇiguṇādhikaḥ ।। śuddhaśīlaḥ śubhācāraḥ kṣāntivratadharaḥ sudhīḥ । sarvasatvahitodyogī niḥkleśaḥ sarvajit kṛtī ।।
samādhidhyānasaṃraktaḥ saṃbodhidharmabhāskaraḥ । prajñānidhir mahāvijñaḥ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ ।। sarvopāyavidhānajñaḥ praṇidhipāratārakaḥ । trailokavijayī vīraḥ saṃbodhikāryapūrakaḥ ।।
vijñānormisamādhisthaḥ saṃbodhijñānaratnabhṛt । sarvasatvaśubhaṃkārī sarvākārasvarūpikaḥ ।। śākyamunir mahābuddho jineśvaras tathāgataḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena sarvatra samupācaran ।।
bhāsayan sakalān lokān bhadraṃ kṛtvā samaṃtataḥ । ihāpi sarvasatvānāṃ bhadraṃ kartuṃ samāgataḥ ।। sāṃprataṃ jetakārāme vihāre saha sāṃghikaiḥ । saddharmam ādiśan nityaṃ viharati prabhāsayan ।।
tasya pūjām ahaṃ kartum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ khalu । tadarthe bahumūlyena yācāmīdaṃ saroruhaṃ ।। tad bhavān mūlyam ādāya dehi me idam ambujaṃ । yathābhilaṣitaṃ dravyaṃ dāsyāmi te prasāṇayan ।।
śraddhayedaṃ pradattaṃ cet tvayāhaṃ saṃpramoditaḥ । etatpuṇyavipākena bodhicittam avāpsyasi ।। sarvadā sadgatiṃ yāyād durgatiṃ na kadā cana । kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya saṃbodhim api prāpnuyāḥ ।।
evaṃ matvā bhavān sādho yadi saṃbodhim ichati । yathābhilaṣitaṃ dravyam ādāyedaṃ pradehi me ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa mālikaḥ pramoditaḥ । taṃ gṛhastham anāthānāṃ bharttāram evam abravīt ।।
aho buddho mahābhijño dṛśyate na kadā cana । īdṛg mahad guṇaṃ cāpi śruyate na kvacin mayā ।। tad ahaṃ taṃ jagannāthaṃ draṣṭum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ vāṃchā me jāyate khalu ।।
tasmāt tatra svayaṃ gatvā saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । anena puṇḍarīkena pūjayiṣye aham ādarāt ।। tad bhavān kṛpayā sādho saṃbuddhasya jagadguroḥ । nītvā mām āśrame tatra saddharme yoktum arhati ।।
iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā so anāthapiṇḍado mudā । mālikaṃ taṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।। sādhu sādhu mahābhāga kuruṣvevaṃ yadīchasi । prāgacha tvaṃ mayā sārddhaṃ pūjaye taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।।
ity uktvā mālikaṃ taṃ sa gṛhapatiḥ prasādayan । ādāya jetakārāme vihāre samudācarat ।। tatra tena sahāyebhya so anāthapiṇḍado gṛhī । sāṃjalis taṃ jagannāthaṃ natvaikānte samāśrayat ।।
tataḥ sa māliko drākṣīc chrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraiḥ । sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ ।। dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyāṃjanapratimaṇḍitaṃ । ratnarāśim ivojvālaṃ vyomaprabhābhyalaṃkṛtaṃ ।।
samaṃtabhadrarūpāṃśaṃ saumyarūpaṃ śubhendriyaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sa mudito natvā kṛtvā tridhā pradakṣiṇaṃ ।। tat padmaṃ purataḥ kṣiptvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ puro mudā । natvā pādau munes tasya tatraikānte samāśrayat ।।
kṣiptamātraṃ ca tatpadmaṃ sahasākāśaṃ saṃsaran । chatrībhūtvā mune mūrddhnar uparisthaṃ vyarājata ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhālokaḥ sarve te vismayānvitāḥ । aho buddhasya māhātmyam iti proktvā prasedire ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā mālikaḥ sa ativismayānaṃditāśayaḥ । utthāya sahasā śastuḥ pādayo nyapatan nataḥ ।। tataḥ sa sāṃjalir natvā pādābjavor jagadguroḥ । saṃbuddhapadalābhāya praṇidhānaṃ vyadhād dhṛdo ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena loke andhe aparināyake । kleśākule vinaṣṭe ahaṃ bhūyāsaṃ sugato jinaḥ ।। svayaṃ tarttum aśaktānaṃ tārayitā bhavodadhiṃ । tathā kleśābdhimagnānāṃ samuddharttā vimocākāḥ ।।
dharme anāśvasitānaṃ ca sādāśvāsayitāpi vai । adṛṣṭabodhimārgānāṃ darśayitā bhaveya hi ।। iti tena kṛtaṃ matvā praṇidhānam sa sarvavit । bhagavān muditaḥ prāvirakārṣīt sa smitaṃ tadā ।।
tatra smite munīndrasya mukhapadmād vinirgatāḥ । suraśmayaḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ prasesrus trijagatsv api ।। yā adhastād gatābhāsas tā sarvanarakeṣv api । avabhāsya śubhaṃ kṛtvā pracakru duḥkhanāśaṇaṃ ।।
tatprabhābhiḥ parispṛṣṭvā sarve te narakāśritāḥ । duḥkhamuktā sukhaspṛṣṭā vismitā evam abruvan ।। aho kiṃ nu mahāsaukhyam asmākaṃ jāyate adhunā । itaś cyutāḥ kuhānyatra samutpannā vayaṃ nu kiṃ ।।
iti cintāparitānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane । bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ preṣayat prati nairayaṃ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā narakasthās te sarve ativismayānvitāḥ । parasparaṃ samālokya punar evaṃ vabhāṣire ।।
bhavanto no itaś cyutvā nānyatra saṃgatā vayaṃ । ihaiva narake sthāḥ sma kutrāpi calitā na hi ।। kiṃ tv ayaṃ samupāyātā hy apūrvadarśanaḥ pumān । nūnam asyānubhāvena jāyate śubhatā adhunā ।।
nūnam ayaṃ mahāsatvo dṛṣṭvāsmān duḥkhapīḍitān । kṛpayā sarvathoddharttuṃ narake atra samāgataḥ ।। tad asya samupāśritya prakṛtvā śaraṇaṃ sadā । praṇatvā śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajemahi samādarāt ।।
iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve nārakīyāḥ prabodhitāḥ । taṃ buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇatvā prābhajan mudā ।। tadbhajanodbhavaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sarve te narakotthitāḥ । sahasā sadgatiṃ yātā babhūvur dharmabhājanāḥ ।।
evaṃ tā raśmayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvāṃs tān narakāśritān । samuddhṛtya punas tatra jagacchāstur upāyayuḥ ।। yā cāpy ūrddhvaṃ gatābhāsas tāvabhāsya diśo aṣṭa ca । yāvad bhavāgraparyantam avabhāsyābhiprāsaran ।।
gāthābhiś ca surān sarvān divyakāyasukhāratān । samantato mahacchabdaṃ ruccair evam acodayan ।। anityaṃ sarvasaṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ । iti matvā śubhe dharmaṃ sarvadā caratādarāt ।।
niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajadhvaṃ sarvadādarāt ।। yo hy asmiṃ saugate dharme cariṣyati samāhitaḥ । sa hitvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।।
etac chabdaṃ samākarṇya sarve devāḥ prabodhitāḥ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire samāhitāḥ ।। evaṃ tāḥ raśmayaḥ paṃcaḥ sarvāṃl lokān surān api । triratnaśaraṇe sthāpya punar muner upāyayuḥ ।।
tatra tā raśmayaḥ sarvā ekībhūtā ca piṇḍitāḥ । jinaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tad uṣṇīṣe viśet punaḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhālokāḥ sarve te vismayānvitāḥ । kim ādeśen munīndro ayam iti dhyātvā niṣedire ।। athā yuṣmān sa ānando matvā teṣāṃ vitarkitaṃ ।
utthāya sāṃjalir natvā bhagavantaṃ tam abravīt ।। bhagavan bhavatā kena hetunā sṛjyate smitaṃ । nāhetu sugatāḥ sarve vihasanti kadā cana ।। yadarthe hetunā smitaṃ bhavān muṃcati sāṃprataṃ ।
tadarthaṃ śrotum ichanti sarve lokā ime khalu ।। yadarthena bhavān smitaṃ prakaroti jagadguro । tadarthaṃ samupādiśya sarvān lokān prabodhaya ।। ity ānandoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
sarvān lokān samālokya tam ānaṃdaṃ cābravīt ।। evam etan mahānaṃda nāhetupratyayaṃ kvacit । sarvabuddhāḥ pramuṃcanti smitaṃ kiṃcit kadā cana ।। paśya tvaṃ yad ayaṃ sādhu ārāmikaḥ prasāditaḥ ।
mamaivaṃ śraddhayā pūjāṃ karoti śraddhayā mudā ।। etatpuṇyavipākena māliko ayaṃ subuddhimān । bodhicittaṃ samāsādya bodhicaryāṃ caran kramāt ।। sarvāḥ pāramitāḥ pūryya sarvān māragaṇān vinijayan ।
samyakṣaṃbodhim āsādya niḥkleśo arhan munīśvaraḥ ।। daśabalo jagannāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt । padmottamo abhidho buddhas tathāgato bhaviṣyati ।। yad ayaṃ mama saddharmasādhane abhiprasāditaḥ ।
saṃbodhipraṇidhiṃ dhṛtvā karoti śraddhayārcanāṃ ।। evaṃ ye śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । bhajanti te janāḥ sarve bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ ।। tatas te sarvasatvānāṃ hitārtheṣu samudyatāḥ ।
bodhisatvā mahāsatvā bhaviṣyaṃti guṇākarāḥ ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ । tataḥ saṃbodhim āsādya bhaveyuḥ sugatā api ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre saṃbodhijñānavāṃchibhiḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdādayo api te । bhikṣavaḥ sāṃghikāḥ sarve prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।। sarve lokāś ca te sarve śrutvaivaṃ śrīghanoditaṃ ।
triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire anumoditāḥ ।। evaṃ śāstrā munīndreṇa vyākṛtaṃ svayam ātmanaḥ । śrutvā sabhāntikaś cāpi prābhyanandat pramoditaḥ ।। tadārabhya sadā nityaṃ mālikaḥ so anumoditaḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācarad bodhicārikāṃ ।। tataḥ sānāthapiṇḍo api tena saha pramoditaḥ । sāṃjalis taṃ jagannāthaṃ natvā sve nilaye yayau ।। tatra sa māliko gehe bhāryayā saha moditaḥ ।
triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prācarat sarvadā śubhaṃ ।। tatas taṃ saugate dharme anucarantaṃ niśamya saḥ । tīrthikopāsiko ruṣṭo upetya paryabhāṣata ।। are re durmate pāpin kim evaṃ carase aśubhe ।
sarvathā tvaṃ paribhraṣṭo narake duḥkham āpsyasi ।। yad apātre durācāre mithyādharmābhibhāṣinī । upetya bhajanaṃ kṛtvā vinoṣi kilviṣaṃ mahat ।। bhajante ye narā buddhaṃ na te gachanti sadgatiṃ ।
durgatim eva te yātāś caranty aśubhe sadā ।। kadā cid api tad gehe bhadraṃ na jāyate kvacit । lakṣmīś cāpi vasen naiva yato dharmo vinaśyate ।। kiṃ cin nāsti śubhācāraṃ tasya bhikṣāśino ayateḥ ।
kim evaṃ śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajase sadguror iva ।। kṛpaṇo yaḥ svayaṃ bhraṣṭaḥ parāṃś ca bhraṃśayed iha । adharme ye api saddharmam ity ākhyāyābhivaṃcate ।। sa kiṃ śāstā sudhīr vijño dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।
sadbhir na pūjanīyo asau niṃdanīyo hi durgatiḥ ।। iti satyaṃ mayākhyātaṃ hitārthaṃ te śubhārthinaḥ । yadi dharme asti te vāṃchā śrutvāsmadvacanaṃ cara ।। tad buddhasaṃgatiṃ tyaktvā tīrthe snātvā samāhitaḥ ।
brahmaṇaṃ viṣṇum īśānaṃ bhaja nityaṃ yathāvidhiṃ ।। brāhmaṇaṃ ye bhajaṃty atra sarve te brahmacāriṇaḥ । pariśuddhāśayā bhadrā saṃprayānti surālayaṃ ।। ye bhajanti sadā viṣṇuṃ na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ ।
sadgatiṃ sarvadā yātā bhavanti manujādhipāḥ ।। ye bhajanti mahārudraṃ na te gachanti nārake । sarvasaukhyāni saṃbhuktvā yānti cānte śivālayaṃ ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre yadi saukhyaṃ sadechasi ।
tad etāṇ trijagannāthān bhaja nityaṃ prapūjayan ।। etan me vacanaiḥ śrutvā bhaja tān sadgurūn yatīn । teṣāṃ saddharmam ākarṇya cara nityaṃ śubhe vrate ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvadātra bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
ante pāpavinirmuktāḥ prayānti tridaśālayaṃ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā mālikaḥ sa viroṣitaḥ । tairthikaṃ taṃ samārabhya paribhāṣyaivam abravīt ।। ā kim evaṃ vadasy atra mā maivaṃ vadathāḥ punaḥ ।
tvam eva narakaṃ yāyā nindase yan munīśvaraṃ ।। śṛṇv atrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃbuddhe guṇam alpakaṃ । vistareṇa kathaṃ vaktuṃ śakyate alpaśiyā mayā ।। tathāpi kathyate alpatvāt tavābhibodhane mayā । śrutvā tvayā vicāryaiva sad asac ca parīkṣyatāṃ ।।
saṃbuddha eva bhagavān suguṇī na viṣṇuḥ saṃśasyate na hiraṇyagarbhaḥ । teṣāṃ subhadracaritātiśayaprabhāvāñ chrutvā vicārayata ko guṇavān na veti ।। rudro vibhūtyajakayoladharaḥ pramattaḥ । kaṃ pūjayemahi suśāntam aśāntarūpaṃ ।।
duryodhanādi nṛpanāśakaraḥ sa cakrī haras tripūranāśakaḥ pinākī । krauṃcaṃ guho api dṛḍhaśakti hate cakāra buddhastokavalamayas tu jagatāṃ hiteṣī ।। pīḍyāmamāyamayam eva tu rakṣaṇīyo vadhyo yam ity api surottamanītir eṣā । niḥśreyasātyudayasaukhyahitaikabuddhir buddhasya naivaridavonahivaṃ ।।
rāgādi doṣajanitāni vacānsi viṣṇor unmattaceṣṭitakarāṇi ca yāni śambhoḥ । niḥśeṣadoṣaśamakāritatathāgatasya vaṃdyatvam arhati ca ko atra vicārayadhvaṃ ।। yaś codyataḥ parivadhāya ghṛṇāṃ vihāya trāṇāya yaś ca jagataḥ kṛpayā pravṛttaḥ । rāgī ca yo bhavati yaś ca vimuktarāgaḥ pūjyaṃs tayoḥ ka iha taṃ vadatānucintya ।।
śakraṃ vajradharaṃ balaṃ haladharaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca cakrāyudhaṃ skaṃdaṃ śaktidharaṃ śmaśānavilayaṃ rudraṃ triśūlāyudhaṃ । etān duḥkhabhayāṅkitān gataghṛṇān bālān vicitrāyudhān nityaṃ prāṇivadhodyute praharaṇān kas tān namasyed budhaḥ ।। na yaḥ śūlaṃ dhatte na ca suratim aṅke suvadanāṃ na cakraṃ śaktiṃ vā na ca kuliśam ugraṃ rava halaṃ vinirmuktaṃ kleśaiḥ parahitavidhānādyatadhiyaṃ । śaraṇyaṃ lokānaṃ tam ṛṣim upayātāsmi śaraṇaṃ ।।
rudro rāgavaśāt striyaṃ vahati yo hiṃsyā hriyā varjitā viṣṇuḥ krūrataraḥ kṛtaghnacaritaḥ skaṃdhaḥ svayaṃjñāti ha । krūrāsyā mahiṣāntakṛn naravaśā mānsāśinī pārvatī pānepsī ca vināyako daśabalo srasto hy adoṣaḥ suhṛt ।। vaṃdhur nabhe sa bhagavān na ripur na cānyaḥ śāstā trilokagurur ekatamo api dhīraḥ śrutvā vacaḥsucaritātiśayaprabhāvaṃ buddhaṃ guṇātiśayalobhatayāśritāḥ smaḥ ।। nāsmākaṃ sugataḥ pitā na ripavas tīrthyāṃdhanaṃ naiva te ।
dattaṃ tena tathāgatena ca hṛtaṃ kiṃcit kaṇādādibhiḥ । kiṃ tv ekāṃtajagaddhitaḥ sa bhagavān buddho yataś cāmalaṃ vākyaṃ sarvamalāpahārica yatas tad bhiktavaṃto vayaṃ ।। hiteṣī yo nityaṃ satatam upakārīva jagataḥ kṛtaṃ yena svāsthyaṃ bahuvidharujārttasya jagataḥ । gūḍhaṃ yaś ca jñe bhayaṃ karatalam ivāvaiti sakalaṃ prapadyadhvaṃ santas temṛṣivaradaraṃ bhaktimanasaḥ ।। asarvabhāvena yadṛcchayā vā parānuvṛtya vicikitsayā vā ।
ye taṃ namasyanti munīndracaṃdraṃ te apy āmarīsaṃpadam āpnuvaṃti ।। paurāṇīśrutineṣa lokamahito buddhaḥ kilāyaṃ harir dṛṣṭvā janmajarāvipattivaśagaṃ lokaṃ kṛpābhyudyataḥ । jātaḥ śākyakulenduracyutamatis trātā nṛṇāṃ gautamaḥ śāstāraṃ hitam eva kas tam adhunā nāvaiti mūḍho janaḥ ।। yadā rāgadveṣād asurasuradārāpaharaṇaṃ kṛtaṃ māyādvitvaṃ dharaṇiharaṇāśaktamatinā ।
tadā pūjyo vandyo harir aparimukto abudhatayā vinirmuktaṃ buddhaṃ na namati jano māhavahulaḥ ।। caturjaladhimekhalākuratambabhārālasāṃ mahīṃ mahatīṃ visṛjya harayevāpakaṣṭāṃ valiḥ । pradāya munaye tu pāṃśulavam apy aśoko nṛpaḥ kṣitiṃ sakalacaṃdramaṇḍalatarāñ ca saṃprāptavān ।। yakṣapāto na me buddhena dveṣaṭakapilādiṣu ।
muktimac ca vaco yasya kāryas tasya parigrahaḥ ।। avaśyam eṣāṃ katamo api sarvavit jagarddhitaikāntaviśālasāraḥ । sa eva mṛgyo hy atisūkṣmacetasā janena śeṣaiḥ kim anarthapaṇḍitaiḥ ।। yasyāpi kiñcin na hi doṣaleśaṃ śaradguṇāḥ santi jagaddhitārthe ।
brahmāpi viṣṇutiriṇo harir vā samehi śāstā śubhakārimitraṃ ।। yasya na vidyate doṣo vidyante sakalā guṇāḥ । sarvajñaḥ sa jagacchāstā tam ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। yo asmin sudṛṣṭyāt saṃrakṣyati jagacchubhe ।
tasyāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajāmi satataṃ mudā ।। yaṃ dṛṣṭvā suprasannās te bhavanti nirmalāśayāḥ । tam eva sugataṃ nāthaṃ bhajāmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। yenaiva trijagallokaṃ putravat pratipālitaṃ ।
tam eva trijagannāthaṃ bhajāmi śaraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। yasmai suśraddhayā dattaṃ tat phalaṃ bodhisādhanaṃ । tam eva śrīghanaṃ bhaktyā bhajāmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। yasmād dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāḥ pramodinaḥ ।
tam eva saṃti sarve api duḥkhachedanasadguṇāḥ । tam eva śrīpradātāraṃ bhajāmi śraddhayādarāt ।। buddha eva jagacchāstā buddha eva jagadguruḥ । buddha eva jagannātho buddha eva munīśvaraḥ ।।
tad ahaṃ sarvabhāvena buddhasya śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । śraddhayā dharmam āsādya bhajāmi bodhiprāptaye ।। ye buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ । nirmuktapāpakāḥ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti jinālayaṃ ।।
śṛṇvanti saugataṃ vākyaṃ ye te na yānti durgatiṃ । samantabhadrasaukhyāni bhuktvā yāṃti sukhāvatiṃ ।। bhajanti lokanāthaṃ ye te api na yānti durgatiṃ । pāpamuktāḥ sukhāny eva bhuktvā yāṃti surālayaṃ ।।
etad ratnatrayaṃ loke utpannaṃ sadguṇākaraṃ । tad ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajāmi samupāsikaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sarvasatvahitārthakaḥ । kramād bodhicarāḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।।
tadāhaṃ sugato bhūtvā sarvasatvaśubhārthabhṛt । satvān bodhau pratiṣṭhāpya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāt ।। evaṃ vijñāya saddharmaṃ yadīchati bhavān api । triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sadā tvaṃ sadgatiṃ tataḥ । bodhiṃ cāpi samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa paribodhitaḥ । tairthyadharmaṃ pratikṣipya saṃbuddhaśrāvako abhavat ।।
tadārabhya sadā nityaṃ saddharmaśravaṇotsukaḥ । vihāre samupāśritya prābhajat taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ mahārāja triratnaṃ sarvadā bhaja ।।
prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sadā te maṃgalaṃ bhavet । kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ । tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। śṛṇvantīdaṃ mudā ye jinavarakathitaṃ mālikasyāvadānaṃ ye cāpi śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā bhadrakāmāḥ । te sarve lokanāthās trimalakalijitā bodhisatvā maheśā bhuktvā saukhyaṃ sadānte jinavaranilaye saṃprayānti prasannāḥ । athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā ।
upaguptaṃ guruṃ bhikṣuṃ natvaivaṃ punar abravīt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa upagupta ātmavit ।
tam aśokaṃ mahīpālaṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru ।। tadyathāsau jagacchāstā śākyasiṃhas tathāgataḥ ।
sarvajñaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājā munīśvaraḥ ।। ekasmin samaye tatra śrāvastyā bahir āśrame । vihāre jetakodyāne vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ puraskṛtaḥ ।
sabhāmadhyāsanāsīno dharmam ādeṣṭum ārabhat ।। tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ । devā daityāś ca nāgāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।। siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi garuḍā rākṣasā api ।
ṛṣayo brāhmaṇā vijñā rājānaḥ kṣatriyā api ।। vaiśyā rājakumārāś ca maṃtriṇaś ca mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca gṛhasthāḥ śilpino api ca ।। grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi kārpaṭikādayo api ca ।
tīrthikā api te sarve jetārāme upāgatāḥ ।। vihāre taṃ jagannāthaṃ dṛṣṭvā sāṃjalayo mudā । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ ।। tatas te muditāḥ sarve parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ patum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ ।
saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracerur bodhisaṃvaraṃ ।। tasminn avasare tatra paṃcāla uttarādhipaḥ । dakṣiṇādhipapaṃcālaṃ parājetum upākramat ।। tayoḥ paṃcālayo rājño viruddhāsy abhimāninoḥ ।
mahāyuddham abhūn nityaṃ parasparavighātanaṃ ।। pravarttite sadā yuddhe tayo rājño hi māninoḥ । durbhikṣam api tatrābhūd bahulokavighātanaṃ ।। tadā tau kṣatriyau krūrau parasparavighātinau ।
viruddhamānasau vīrau vairaśāmyaṃ na jagmataḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā nṛpatī rājā prasenajin sa kauśalaḥ । tad vairaśamanopāyaṃ ciraṃ dhyātvā vyaciṃtayat ।। yad etau nṛpatī vīrau nityaṃ yuddhābhikāṃkṣiṇau ।
saṃbodhisādhanaṃ dharmaṃ śrotuṃ naivābhivāṃchata ।। sarve api maṃtriṇo amātyāḥ sarve lokāś ca yodhinaḥ । saṃbuddhadarśane cāpi nātrāgachanti ke cana ।। evaṃ teṣāṃ sadā nityaṃ hiṃsākarmābhirāgiṇāṃ ।
saddharme śravaṇe vāpi gocaraṃ naiva vidyate ।। dharmaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ sāraṃ janma mānuṣe । parasparaṃ nihatyaiva yāsyaṃti narake dhruvaṃ ।। dhig janma mānuṣe teṣāṃ kevalaṃ pāpasādhanaṃ ।
ye kleśamānadarpyāndhā na paśyaṃti munīśvaraṃ ।। ye cātra saugataṃ dharmaṃ na śṛṇvanti kadā cana । kathaṃ te bhadracaryāyāṃ gocaraṃ samavāpnuyuḥ ।। sadā te māracaryāyāṃ sthitvā kleśābhimāninaḥ ।
bodhicaryāṃ pratikṣipya careyuḥ kāmacāriṇaḥ ।। tataḥ svayaṃ paribhraṣṭā bhraṃśayantaḥ parān api । yathechayā carantas te cinuyur bahupātakaṃ ।। tatas te kleśasaṃtaptāḥ svaparārthābhighātinaḥ ।
tīvraduḥkhāgnisaṃtaptāḥ pateyur narake dhruvaṃ ।। narakeṣu bhramantas te sadā duḥkhābhibhojinaḥ । paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptāś careyur ābhavaṃ tathā ।। tad eṣāṃ sarvalokānāṃ bhadrārthaṃ hitakāraṇaṃ ।
sarvathopāyam ādhātum arhāmi sāṃprataṃ drutaṃ ।। yāvad etau nṛpau vīrau viruddhau nopaśāmyataḥ । tāvad atra bhuvi kvāpi maṃgalaṃ na bhavet sadā ।। tad etau nṛpatī tāvad bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ ।
maitrasnehasaṃbaddhau kuryāṃ nirvairabhāvinau ।। etau hi kṣatriyau vīrau pāṃcālau mānagarvitau । anayor mitravaṃdhaṃ ko bodhayitvā kariṣyati ।। buddha eva jagacchāstā dharmarājaḥ prabodhayan ।
anayoś ciravairyāgniṃ śamayituṃ praśaknuyāt ।। tad atra sahasā gatvā prārthayeyaṃ munīśvaraṃ । nūnaṃ buddhānubhāvāt tau nṛpau mitratvam āpsyataḥ ।। iti niścitya rājā sa prasenajit samutthitaḥ ।
vihāre sahasā gatvā nanāma taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। tatra sa purato gatvā sāṃjaliḥ samupāśrayan । etat sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivam abhāṣata ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña vijānīyād bhavān api ।
yat tau pāṃcālabhūpālau viruddhau bhavato adhunā ।। yad etayor viruddhe ta sarve lokā virodhitāḥ । tad atra sarvadā yuddhaṃ pravarttate divāniśaṃ ।। tat tesāṃ sarvalokānāṃ saddharme gocaraṃ kadā ।
sadā yuddhābhisaktās te sādhayeyuḥ śubhaṃ kathaṃ ।। tad atra bhagavāñc chāstā bodhayaṃs tau narādhipau । saṃbodhimārgam ādiśya śubhe cārayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān muniḥ ।
tasya rājñe nareṃdrasya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā matvā śāstrādhivāsitaṃ । sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā muditaḥ svālayaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān pātram ādāya cīvarāvṛtaḥ ।
bhāsayan bhadratāṃ kurvan pratasthe saha sāṃghikaiḥ ।। evaṃ sarvatra mārgeṣu bhāsayaṃ sa munīśvaraḥ । kṛtvā bhadraṃ krameṇaivaṃ vārāṇasīm upācarat ।। tatra sa bhagavāṃ prāpto bhābhiḥ saṃbhāsayan kramāt ।
caraṃ kṛtvā subhadratvaṃ mṛgadāve upācarat ।। tatra sa bhagavān prātaḥ sasaṃghaḥ saugatāśrame । sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ ।
triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire samādarāt ।। tadā dakṣiṇapāṃcālanṛpatiḥ sa pramoditaḥ । saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ kartuṃ mṛgadāve upācarat ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatiḥ sa pramoditaḥ ।
sāṃjaliḥ purato gatvā natvaikānte upāśrayat ।। tasminn avasare tatra mṛgadāve samāśritaḥ । bhagavānn iti śuśrāva pāṃcālauttarādhipaḥ ।। sa uttarapāṃcālo nṛpatiḥ pratiroṣitaḥ ।
taṃ nṛpaṃ yāmyapāṃcālaṃ parājetum upācarat ।। tatra sa nṛpatir vīraś caturaṃgavalaiḥ saha । jayavādyamahotsāhaiḥ sahasā samupācarat ।। tatra sa yāmyapāṃcālarājā taṃ ripum āgataṃ ।
niśamya sahasotthāya natvā ha taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña sa me vairā ihāgataḥ । tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi tad anujñāṃ dadātu me ।। iti tena narendreṇa prārthite sa jineśvaraḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ yāmyapāṃcālaṃ samāśvāsyaivam ādiśat ।। nṛpate mā vibheṣī tvaṃ dhairyyam ālambya tiṣṭhata । tad upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yenāsau te vaśe caret ।। ity ādiśya sa sarvajñaś caturaṅgabalānvitaṃ ।
mahatsainyādhipaṃ vīraṃ nirmāya apreṣayat tataḥ ।। sa sainyādhipatir vīraś caturaṅgabalaiḥ saha । carann uttarapāṃcālam abhiyoddhum upācarat ।। tan mahatsainyaṃ āyātaṃ samālokyābhyupadrutaṃ ।
sarva uttarapāṃcālasainyā bhītāḥ parāyayuḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvottarapāṃcālanṛpatiś cāpi kheṭitaḥ । ekākī ratham āruhya bhagavatsaṃmukhe acarat ।। tatra sa dūrato dṛṣṭvā śrīghanaṃ taṃ sabhāśritaṃ ।
avatīrya rathāt tatra mṛgadāve upācarat ।। tatra sa nṛpati rājā samupetya kṛtāṃjaliḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya nanāma śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। tataś cirāt samutthāpya sa pāṃcalo narādhipaḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatraikānte samāśrayat ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā nṛpatiṃ taṃ samāśritaṃ । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tad āryasatyam ākarṇya nṛpatiḥ so abhibodhitaḥ ।
saṃsārasādhanaṃ dharmaṃ punaḥ śrotuṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ । praṇatvā bhagavaṃtaṃ taṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।
tan me atrānugrahaṃ kṛtvā samyag ādeṣṭum arhati ।। yad atra bhagavan satvāḥ pravarttanto bhavodadhau । sukhaduḥkhābhibhuṃjāno bhramaṃte ṣaḍgatau kathaṃ ।। karmaṇā kena devāḥ syur mānuṣāḥ kena karmaṇā ।
daityāś ca karmaṇā kena tat samyak samupādiśa ।। tiryañcaḥ karmaṇā kena pretāś ca kena karmaṇā । nārakāḥ karmaṇā kena tat sarvaṃ samupādiśa ।। tatrāpy anekarūpāś ca sarve bhinnāśayā api ।
nihīnamadhyamotkṛṣṭāḥ sukhaduḥkhānvitā api ।। etat sarvaṃ samākhyāya bhavāñ chāstā jagad guruḥ । saṃsāragatisaṃcāraṃ prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān sudhīḥ ।
taṃ viśuddhāśayaṃ bhūpaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samupādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja saṃsāragaticāraṇaṃ । samyag dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ paribodhane ।। kāyavāgmānasaṃ karmakṛtaṃ yac ca śubhāśubhaṃ ।
lokas tasya phalaṃ bhukte karttā nānyo asti kasya cit ।। iti sarve kṛpāviṣṭās trailokye guravo jināḥ । uktavantas tathā tad dhi karmaṇo yasya yat phalaṃ ।। karmaṃ kartuṃ vihātuṃ ca sadasadgatihetukaṃ ।
lobhamohabhayakrodhā ye narā naraghātinaḥ ।। saṃvaddhyānyāñ ca hi santi saṃjīvaṃ yānti te dhruvaṃ । saṃvatsarasahasrāṇi bahūny api hatāhatāḥ ।। saṃjīvanti yatas tatra tena saṃjīva ucyate ।।
mātāpitṛsuhṛdvaṃdhumitradrohakarāś ca ye । paiśunyānṛtavattāraḥ kālasūtrābhigāminaḥ ।। kālasūtreṇa saṃsūḍya pāṭyante dāruvad yataḥ । jvaladbhiḥ krakacais tatra kālasūtras tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
dāvādau dahanair dāhaṃ dehināṃ vidadhāti ye । sa tīvrajvalanair jantus tapyate tapane raṭan ।। tīvraṃ tapanasaṃtāpaṃ tanoty eva niraṃtaraṃ । yat tato anvartham āloke khyātas tapanasaṃjñayā ।।
dharmādharmaviparyāsaṃ nāstiko yaḥ prakāśayan । saṃtāpayati cānyāṃś ca tapyate sa pratāpane ।। pratāpayati tatrasthān satvāns tīvreṇa vahninā । tapanātiśayano asau proktas tasmāt pratāpanaḥ ।।
ajaiḍakaśṛgālāṃś ca śaśākhumṛgāsukarān । anyāṃś ca prāṇino ghnaṃti saṃghātaṃ yānti te narāḥ ।। saṃhatās tatra ghātyaṃte samyagvāhaiva vaṃyayaḥ । tasmāt saṃghāta ity evaṃ vikhyāto anvarthasaṃjñayā ।।
kāyavāgmānasaṃ tāpaṃ ye kurvantīha dehināṃ । kaṭukyapaṭikā ye ca rauravaṃ yānti te nārāḥ ।। tīvreṇa vahninā tatra dahyamānā niraṃtaraṃ । raudraṃ ravaṃ vimuṃcanti yatas tasmāt sa rauravaṃ ।।
devadvijaguror dravyaṃ hṛtaṃ yair duḥkhinām iha । te mahārauravaṃ yānti ye cānyasvāpahāriṇaḥ ।। raudratvād vahnidāhasya ravasya ca mahattayā । rauravo hi mahāṃs tasya mantva rauravād api ।।
kṛtvā guṇādhike tīvram apakāraṃ nihatya ca । mātāpitṛgurun kalpam avīcau pacyate dhruvaṃ ।। asthīny api viśīryyante raudrāgnau tatra dehināṃ । yato na vīciḥ saukhyasya nāvīcir udāhṛtaḥ ।।
mithodroharatā ye traṇe ghnantīva dehinaḥ । pāpād asinakhās te tu jāyante duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।। nakhā evāsayas teṣām āyasā jvalitāḥ kharāḥ । tair anyonyaṃ nikṛntanti yat tenāsinakhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
lohajvalitatīkṣṇāgrāḥ ṣoḍaśāṅgulakaṇṭakāḥ । balād ārohyata hraṃdan śālmalīḥ pāladārikaḥ ।। lohadamṣṭrā mahākāyā jvalitās tīvrabhairavāḥ । aśliṣya bhakṣayanty enaṃ paradāropahāriṇaṃ ।।
āraṭanto api khādyante śvagṛdhrolūkavāyasaiḥ । aśivaṃ kurvate chinnā viśvāsaghāṭino narāḥ ।। ayoguḍāni bhujyante prataptāni punaḥ punaḥ । yāpyante kvathitaṃ tāmraṃ ye parasvāpahāriṇaḥ ।।
krūraiḥ śvabhir ayodraṃṣṭraiḥ kṛtyante vivaśā bhṛśaṃ । varṣakoṭi raṭanto api ye narāḥ kheṭake ratāḥ ।। matsyādīñ jalajān hatvā jvalanty amradravodakāṃ । yāti vaitaraṇīṃ śaśvad vahninā dahyate naraḥ ।।
ye svārthalavasaṃmūḍho vyavahāram adhārmikaṃ । karoti narake kradan sa cakreṇābhipīḍyate ।। pīḍā vahubhir ākāraiḥ kṛtā yair duḥkhinām iha । pīḍyante te ciraṃ taptair yatra mudgaraparvataiḥ ।।
bhedakā dharmasetūnāṃ ye cāsan mārgavāhinaḥ । kṣuradhārācitaṃ mārgaṃ gatvā krāmanti te narāḥ ।। nakhaiḥ saṃcūrṇya yūkādīñ cūrṇyante meṣaparvatai । bhūyo bhūyo mahākāyāḥ krandantas te śaracchataṃ ।। vrataṃ yas tu samāśritya saṃpanno parirakṣati ।
śīryamānamānsāsthiḥ kukuṃle pacyate dhruvaṃ ।। aṇunāpi hi yaḥ kaścin mithyājīvena jīvati । bhakṣyate krimibhiś caṇḍaiḥ saṃmagno gūthamṛttike ।। dṛṣṭvāpi vrīhimadhyasthān prāṇinaś cūrṇayanti ye ।
āyasai mukhalais taptaiḥ kṣobhyante te punaḥ punaḥ ।। atyantakrodhanāḥ krūrāḥ śaṭhāḥ pāpābhikāṃkṣiṇaḥ । paravyasanakṛṣṭvā ca jāyante yamarākṣasāḥ ।। sarveṣām eva duḥkhānāṃ vījaṃ mṛd vābhibhedataḥ । kāyavāgmānasaṃ karma pāpaṃ yat tad aṇv api varttayet ।
haṃsapārāvatādīnaṃ kharāṇām api rāgiṇāṃ । yena rāgeṇa jāyante mūḍhāḥ kīṭādiyoniṣu ।। sarppāḥ krodhopanāhābhyāṃ mārastabdhā mṛgādhipāḥ । abhimānena jāyante gadāmāśvādiyoniṣu ।।
mātsaryerṣyādi doṣeṇa vānarāḥ pretadehinaḥ । jāyante mukharā dhṛṣṭāś capalātmānaś ca vāyasāḥ ।। vadhavaṃdhanamātsaryair gavāśvādiṣu dehinaḥ । jāyante krūrakarmāṇo lūtāḥ kharjjūravṛścikaḥ ।।
vyāghramārjāragomāyuṛkṣagṛdhravṛgādāyaḥ । jāyante pretamansādoḥ krodhanā matsarā narāḥ ।। dātāraḥ krodhanāḥ krūrā narā nāgamaharddhikāḥ । bhavāntatyāgino darppāt krodhāc ca garuḍeśvarāḥ ।।
kṛtaṃ yat pāpakaṃ karma svayaṃ vākkāyamānasaṃ । tiryañcas tena jāyante tan manogatim ākṛthāḥ ।। bhakṣyabhojyāpahartāro ye kṣudrā dānavarji । bhavanti kuṇapāhārāḥ pretās te kaṭapūtanāḥ ।।
viheṭhayanti ye bālā vaṃcayanty api tṛṣṇayā । te api garbhamalāhārā jāyante kaṭapūtanāḥ ।। hīnācārātidīnāś ca matsarā nityakāṃkṣiṇaḥ । jāyaṃte ye narāḥ pretā aṣṭās te galagaṇḍakāḥ ।।
dānaṃ nivārayaty eva na hi kiṃ tid dadāti yaḥ । kṣutkṣāmāsau mahākukṣiḥ pretaḥ śūcimukho bhavet ।। dhanaṃ rakṣati vaṃśārthe na bhuṃkte na dadāti yaḥ । dattādāyī tataḥ pretaḥ śrāddhabhoktā sa jāyate ।।
yaḥ parasvāpahārepsur datvā caivānutapyate । bhoktā viṭśleṣmavāntānāṃ pretya pretaḥ sa jāyate ।। apriyaṃ vakti yaḥ krodhād vākyaṃ marmavibhedataṃ । bbavanty ulkāmukhaḥ pretaḥ suciraṃ tena karmaṇā ।।
kurute kalahaṃ yas tu niṣkṛpaḥ krūramānasaḥ । krimikīṭapataṅgādeḥ prete asau jyotiko bhavet ।। grāmakūṭau dadāty eva yo janaṃ pīḍayanty api । kumbhāṇḍo vikṛtākāraḥ pūyāhāraś ca jāyate ।।
nirdayāḥ prāṇino ghnanti bhakṣyārthaṃ ye dadanty api । māṃsāhārāś ca te avaśyaṃ bhavanti pretarākṣasāḥ ।। gaṃdhamālāratā nityaṃ maṃdakrodhāḥ pradāyakāḥ । gaṃdharvāḥ pretya jāyante devānāṃ ratihetavaḥ ।।
krodhanāḥ piśunaḥ kiñcidarthārthaṃ yaḥ prayachati । sa piśācaṃ praduṣṭātmā jāyate vikṛtānanaḥ ।। nityapraduṣṭāś capalāḥ parapīḍākarā narāḥ । saṃpradānaratā nityaṃ bhūtāḥ pretya bhavanti te ।।
krūrāḥ krūddhāḥ pradātāraḥ priyā sarvasurā ca ye । jāyante pretya yakṣās tu krūrātmānaḥ surāpriyāḥ ।। mātāpitṛgurūn yānair ye nayanti yathepsitaṃ । vimānacāriṇo yakṣā jāyaṃte susukhānvitāḥ ।।
tṛṣṇāmātsaryadoṣeṇa pretā bhavanty amī sadā । yakṣādayaḥ śubhaiḥ kliṣṭair atas tān parivarjayet ।। devāsuramanuṣyeṣu dīrgham āyur ahiṃsayā । jāyate hinsayā svalpām ato hiṃsāṃ vivarjayet ।।
kuṣṭharogajvaronmādā ye cānye vyādhayo nṛṇāṃ । bhavanti bhūtaprayuktes te vadhavaṃdhanatāḍanaiḥ ।। yo na harttā parasvānāṃ na vañcavit prayachati । mahatāpi prayatnena sa dravyaṃ nādhigachati ।।
adattaṃ vittam ādāya dānāni ca dadāti yaḥ । sa pretya dravyavān bhūtvā bhūyo bhavati nirdhanaḥ ।। yo na harttā na dātā ca na cātikṛpaṇo naraḥ । kṛtsnena mahatā dravyaṃ sthiraṃ sa labhate dhruvaṃ ।।
na harttā yaḥ parasvānāṃ tyāgavān vītamatsaraḥ । ahāryaṃ vipulaṃ vittam iṣṭam ca labhate naraḥ ।। āyurvarṇavalopetaḥ śrīmān rogavivarjitaḥ । sukhī ca sa labhen nityaṃ yo dadātīha bhojanaṃ ।।
salajjo rūpavān bhogī suchāyaḥ prāṇināṃ priyaḥ । sa bhaved vastralābhī ca yo vāsānsi prayachati ।। āvāsaṃ yo dadātīha suprasannena cetasā । prāsādāḥ sarvakāmāś ca jāyante tasya dehinaḥ ।।
upānatsaṃkramādīni ye prayachanti mānavāḥ । bhavanti sukhino nityaṃ yānāni ca labhanti te ।। vāpīkūpataḍāgādīn kārayitvā jalāśrayān । sukhinas tyaktasaṃtāpā niḥpipāsā bhavanti te ।।
puṣpair abhyarcitaḥ śrīmān śaraṇyaḥ sarvadehināṃ । samṛddhitaḥ sa syād ārāmaṃ yaḥ prayachati ।। vidyādānena paṇḍityaṃ prajñābhyāsena cāpyate । bhaiṣajyābhayadānena rogamuktas tu jāyate ।।
dīpadānena cakṣuṣmān vādyadānena susvaraḥ । śayanāsanadānena sukhī bhavati mānavaḥ ।। gavādīnn yo dadātīha bhojyaṃ rasasamanvitaṃ । balavān varṇavān bhogī dīrghāyuḥ sa bhaven naraḥ ।।
kanyādānena samānyāṃ lābhī syāt parivāravān । dhanadhānyasamṛddhas tu bhūmidānena jāyate ।। patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyam abhayaṃ vacanaṃ priyaṃ । yad yad evepsitaṃ śaktyā dātavyaṃ tat tad arthinaḥ ।।
kleśayitvā dadātīha svakārthaṃ vā ha yena vā । yaśaḥsaukhyābhilākhād vā sa kliṣṭaṃ labhate phalaṃ ।। svakāryaṃ nirapekṣeṇa kṛpāviṣṭena cetasā । parārthaṃ yo dadātīha so akliṣṭaṃ phalam aśnute ।।
yat kiñcid dīyate anyasmai yathākālaṃ yathāvidhiṃ । tena tena prakāreṇa tat sarvam upatiṣṭhate ।। parān anvapahaty evaṃ sarvakālaṃ yathepsitaṃ । akleśayitvā dātavyaṃ hitaṃ dharmāvirodhiyat ।।
evaṃ hi dīyamānasya dānasyaiva phalādayaḥ । dānaṃ hi sarvasaukhyānām ananyat kāraṇaṃ mataṃ ।। virajaḥ paradārebhyo dārān iṣṭān avāpnuyāt । svebhyo apy adeśakālau ca varjayet puṃstvam archati ।।
paradāreṣu saṃsaktaṃ cittaṃ yo na niyachati । anaṃgeṣu cakṣyeta sa pumāṃ strītvam archati ।। strītvaṃ jugupsate yā tu suśīlamandarāgiṇī । puṃstvam ākāṃkṣate nityaṃ sā nārī naratāṃ vrajet ।।
yas tu samyagnirātaṅkaṃ brahmacaryaṃ niṣevate । tejasvī sadguṇaḥ śrīmān devair api sa lakṣyate ।। dṛḍhasmṛtir asaṃmūḍho maghavāno niṣevanāt । jāyate satyavādī ca yaśaḥsaukhyānvitaḥ pumān ।।
bhinnānām api satvānāṃ bhedaṃ naiva karoti yaḥ । abhedyaparivāro asau jāyate sthiramānasaḥ ।। yas tv ājñāṃ kurute nityaṃ gurūṇāṃ hṛṣṭamānasaḥ । hitāhitābhidhāyī ca sa syād ādeyavākkṛtī ।।
nīcāparāyamānena viparyāsena codgataḥ । bhavanti sukhinaḥ saukhyaṃ duḥkhaṃ datvā ca duḥkhinaḥ ।। paraprapañcābhiratāḥ śaṭhāś cānṛtavādinaḥ । kubjavāmanatāṃ yānti ye ca rūpābhimāninaḥ ।।
jaḍo vijñānamātsaryād bhaven mūkaḥ priyāpriyaḥ । vādhiryaṃ yāti mūḍhātmā hitavākyābhigūḍhakaḥ ।। duḥkham pāpasya puṇyasya sukhaṃ miśrasya miśritaṃ । sarvaṃ sādṛśyaniḥsyandam abhyuhyaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ ।।
śaṭhyena māyayā nityaṃ caraty akṛtakilbiṣaḥ । kalipriyaḥ pradātā ca sa bhaved asureśvaraḥ ।। nātmanā yaḥ sukhākāṃkṣī na ca kṛvyeta parigrahaṃ । grahāṇām agraṇī cāsau mahārājikatāṃ vrajet ।।
mātāpitṛkulajyeṣṭhapūjakasyāgavān kṛtī । hṛṣyame yo na kalahais tridaśeṣu sa jāyate ।। na vigrahe ratā naiva kalahe hṛṣṭamānasāḥ । ekāntakuśalodyuktā ye ca moyāpagās tu te ।।
bahuśrutā dharmadharāḥ suprajñā mokṣakāṃkṣiṇaḥ guṇair । ye parihṛṣṇāś ca narās te tuṣitopagāḥ ।। śīlapradānavinaye pravṛttā ye svayaṃ narāḥ । mahotsāhāś ca te avaśyaṃ nirmāṇaratigāminaḥ ।।
adīnasatvā me śreṣṭhāḥ pradāne damasaṃyamaiḥ । guṇādhikāś ca ye yānti paranirmitatāṃ dhruvaṃ ।। śīlena svargam āpnoti dhyānena ca viśeṣataḥ । yathābhūtaparijñānāt paryante vo punarbhavaḥ ।।
śubhāśubhaphalaṃ karma yad etat kathitaṃ sphuṭaṃ । śubhena labhyate saukhyaṃ duḥkhaṃ tv aśubhasaṃbhavaṃ ।। mṛtyur vyādhir jarā caiva cintanīyam idaṃ trayaṃ । viprayogā priyaiḥ sārddhaṃ karmaṇāṃ ca svakaṃ phalaṃ ।।
evaṃ virāgam āpnoti viviktaḥ puṇyam archati । pāpaṃ ca nārjayed evaṃ tac ca saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu ।। samyakparārthakaraṇaṃ parānarthavivarjanaṃ । puṇyaṃ viparyayāt pāpabhuktam eva munīśvaraiḥ ।।
evaṃ matvā mahārāja ṣaḍgatikārikāṃ bhave । saṃbodhidharmam ādhāya caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe ।। ye saṃbodhivrataṃ dhṛtvā pracaranti samāhitāḥ । sarvasatvahitārthena bodhisatvā bhavanti te ।।
evaṃ vijñāya rājendra sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sarvakleśan vinirjayan । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
iti tena munīndreṇa samākhyātaṃ niśamya saḥ । rājāpy uttarapāṃcālaḥ pravrajituṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ । bhagavantam ānatvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । saṃbodhivratam ādhāya prechāmi carituṃ sadā ।। yad bhavāñ jagatāṃ śāstā saṃbodhidharmadeśikaḥ । tan me anugrahatāṃ kṛtvā pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān sudhīḥ । tasya rājño manaḥśuddhaṃ vijñāyaivam upādiśat ।। sādhu rājan mahābhāga yadīchasi śubhāṃ gatiṃ । ehi cara samādhāya cara me śāsane vrataṃ ।।
ity ādiśya munīndro asau pāṇinā tac chiraḥ spṛśan । saṃbuddhe śāsane dharme taṃ nareṃdraṃ samagrahīt ।। ehīti tena śāstrokte nṛpatiḥ sa prabodhitaḥ । khikkhirīpātradharo bhikṣu abhūc cīvarāvṛtaḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhūpatiś cāpi virakto bhogyanispṛhaḥ ।
niḥkleśaḥ pariśuddhātmā babhūva vijiteṃdriyaḥ ।। sākṣād arhatvam āsādya brahmacārī niraṃjanaḥ । saṃbodhipadam āsādya saṃbuddhaḥ śrāvako abhavat ।। tataḥ sa brahmavid yogī traidhātuvāsinām api ।
sadevāsuralokānāṃ vandyo mānyo abhavad guruḥ ।। tato dakṣiṇapāṃcālarājā sa pratimoditaḥ । utthāya sāṃjalir natvā prārthyat taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña kṛpayā me prasīdatu ।
traimāsyaṃ bhaktum ichāmi tat kurutām anugrahaṃ ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । nṛpatiṃ taṃ samālokya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā bhagavatādhyuvāsitaṃ ।
viditvā sarvasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat ।। tataḥ sa rājā bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । yathārhabhojanair nityaṃ samabhyarcya abhyatoṣayat ।। vicitracīvaraiś cāpi śrīghanaṃ taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ ।
āchādya sāṃjalir natvā praṇidhānaṃ mudā vyadhāt ।। etatpuṇyavipākena loke aṃdhe aparināyake । saddharmabhāskaraḥ śāstā saṃbuddho arhaṃ bhaveya hi ।। evaṃ tena narendreṇa praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā ।
matvā sa bhagavān smitaṃ prāmuñcac chubharociṣaṃ ।। tat smitasamutpannāḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ suraśmayaḥ । prasāritās trilokeṣu bhāsayantyaḥ pracerire ।। tadrasmisaṃparispṛṣṭāḥ sarve api nārakāśritāḥ ।
nirmuktavedanākhedā mahatsaukhyaṃ pralebhire ।। tadā te vismitāḥ sarve nārakīyāḥ pramoditāḥ । kim evaṃ jāyate saukhyam iti dhyātvā niṣedire ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs teṣāṃ vismayākrāṃtacetasāṃ ।
manāṃsi paribodhārthaṃ praiṣayat tatra nairmitaṃ ।। tadā te nārakāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ mudā । upetya praṇatiṃ kṛtvā prābhajañ charaṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। tatas tat puṇyaliptās te sarve vimuktapāpakāḥ ।
pariśuddhāḥ śubhātmānaḥ sadgatiṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। tatas tā raśmayaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ । akaniṣṭhālayaṃ yāvat prasṛtāḥ samabhāsayan ।। gāthāghoṣaiś ca sarvatra sarvān devān pramodinaḥ ।
bodhayitvā śubhe dharme pratiṣṭhāpya pacerire ।। tatas tā raśmayaḥ sarvā piṇḍībhūtā muneḥ puraḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā mahoṣṇīṣe samāviśat ।। tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhālokāḥ sarve ativismayoddhatāḥ । śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti dhyātvā niṣedire ।।
iti teṣāṃ manastarkaṃ matvānaṃdaḥ samutthitaḥ । upetya sāṃjalir natvā prārthayet taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan hetunā kena smitaṃ muṃcati sāṃprataṃ । nāhetvapratyayaṃ smitaṃ na muṃcaṃti munīśvarāḥ ।।
tad yadarthe bhavān smitaṃ muṃcatīme sabhājanāḥ । śrotum ichaṃti sarve tad artham ādeṣṭum arhati ।। ity ānaṃdoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । sarvāṃl lokān samālokya tam ānaṃdaṃ samabravīt ।।
evam eva sadānaṃda sarve buddhā munīśvarāḥ । nāhetupratyayaṃ smitaṃ vimuṃcanti kadā cana ।। paśyatām ayam ānaṃda rājātisaṃprasāditaḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayāsmākaṃ traimāsyaṃ bhajate mudā ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena rājāyaṃ sadguṇākaraḥ । kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya balānvitaḥ ।। sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā mārāñ cāpi vinirjayan । bodhim āsādya sarvajñas tathāgato munīśvaraḥ ।।
sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ । vijayo nāma saṃbuddho bhaviṣyati bhavāntare ।। evam ānaṃda vijñāya buddhakṣetraśubhaṃkṛtaṃ । tadvipāke mahatsaukhyaṃ bhadraṃ saṃbodhisādhanaṃ ।।
triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā satkāraiḥ śraddhayā sadā । saṃbodhivāñchibhir lokaiś caritavyaṃ śubhe mudā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdādayo api te । sarve lokās tathety uktvā prābhyanandan prasāditāḥ ।।
so api dakṣiṇapāṃcālo rājā śrutvā pramoditaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śubhe sadā ।। tadārabhya sadā tatra maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ । samaṃtato mahotsāhaṃ kṛtayuga ivābhavat ।।
iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathā adhunā । kathyate atra tvayāpy evaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālanīyāḥ sadā tvayā ।।
tathā te sarvadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
rājño pāñcālayor yan munikathitam idaṃ tat prasiddhāvadānaṃ । śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā ye prasannāḥ । sarve te bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇadharāḥ sarvasaṃpatsukhāḍhyāḥ । kṛtvā lokeṣu bhaddraṃ munivaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodāḥ ।।
athāśoko mahīpālaḥ samupetya kṛtāṃjaliḥ । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathākhyātuṃ ca me arhati ।।
iti saṃprarthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan mahāmatiḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu maharāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cāpy anumodaya ।।
tadyathā bhagavān buddhā śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। ekasmin samaye mātur māyādevyā hitechayā । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ prācarat tridaśālaye ।।
tatra sa bhagavān gatvā suramye naṃdane vane । pārijātatale pāṇḍusacchilāyām upāśrayat ।। tatra śakrādayo devāḥ sarve taṃ sadguṇākaraṃ । śākyamuniṃ samālokya muditāḥ samupācaran ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve devāḥ pramoditāḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāñjalayaḥ praṇemire ।। tato devādhipaḥ śakro divyaratnamayāsanaṃ । saṃbuddhasya jagacchāstuḥ prājñāpayac chubhojjvalaṃ ।।
tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā divyaratnamahojvale । āruhya samupāśritya samātasthau prabhāsayan ।। tadā sā jananī mātā māyādevī samāgatā । tam ātmajaṃ jagannāthaṃ saṃdṛṣṭvā samupācarat ।।
tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mātaraṃ tāṃ samāgatāṃ । utthāya samupāsṛtya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।। svāgataṃ kuśalaṃ mātar ārogyam astu te sadā । tvatmukhaṃ draṣṭum āyāmi tat prasāditum arhasi ।।
atrāsane samāśritya niṣīdaikāgramānasā । upadikṣyāmi saddharmaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva samāhitā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā jananī satī । māyādevī samālokya tam ātmajaṃ samavrāvīt ।।
prāyāmi te mukhaṃ draṣṭuṃ kuśalaṃ te sadātmaja । tan mamānugrahārthena dharmam ādeṣṭum arhasi ।। ity uktvā sā satī māyādevī mātā jagadguroḥ । upāsanaṃ samāśritya nisasāda samāhitā ।।
tataḥ śakrādayo devāḥ sarve te saṃpraharṣitāḥ । pūjāṃgais taṃ jagannāthaṃ māyādevīṃ ca prārcayan ।। tataḥ pādāns tayor natvā kṛtvā ca tripradakṣiṇaṃ । parivṛtya puraskṛtvā dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayan ।। tatas ta bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān devān samupasthitān ।
āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tataś ca bhagavāṃs teṣāṃ devānāṃ sukhamāninaṃ । saṃbodhisādhanaṃ punar evam upādiśat ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāre duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ ।
kāme kiṃcit sukhaṃ nātra kleśasaṃghe samākule ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre sadā saukhyaṃ yadīchatha । bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcaradhvaṃ sadā śubhaṃ ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane ।
māracaryyāṃ parityajya caradhvaṃ bodhicārikāṃ ।। yaḥ satvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ cariṣyati । sa samyag bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyati ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarve yūyaṃ samāhitāḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caradhvaṃ bodhisaṃvaraṃ ।। ye triratnaṃ bhajanty atra na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ । sadā sadgatisaṃyātāḥ kramād bodhim avāpnuyuḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve api te amarāḥ ।
satyam eva parijñāya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।। tataḥ śakraḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña sarvadeha surālaye ।
saddharmaṃ naḥ samādiśya bhavan vihartum arhati ।। vayaṃ sarve surā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । saddharmaṃ sarvadākarṇya cariṣyāmaḥ śubhāṃ cariṃ ।। tataḥ sāpi mahāmāyādevi mātā samutthitā ।
upetya sāṃjalir natvā bhagavantaṃ tam abravīt ।। dhanyo asi yat tvayā putra pratijñātaṃ yathāpurā । tathā tvaṃ pūryate sarvaṃ sarvārthasiddhir astu te ।। sadātra devalokānāṃ hitārthe ca prabodhayan ।
saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vihara saṃprabhāsayan ।। iti mātrārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । jananīṃ tāṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। mātar naikahitārthenabodhicaryāṃ dadhāmi hi ।
sarveṣām api satvānāṃ hitārthe ahaṃ jino bhave ।। tad atra sarvadā naivaṃ tiṣṭheyaṃ tridaśaiḥ saha । varṣā māsatrayaṃ sthātum ichāmi dharmam ādiśan ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā jananī mudā ।
tathāstv iti prabhāṣitvā prābhyanaṃdat prabodhitā ।। tathā sa bhagavāns tatra bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya tasthau māsatrayaṃ divi ।। sarvaśakrādayo devās triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā prabhejire ।। tadā tatra sadā svarge maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ । saddharmasādhanotsāhaṃ prāvarttate samaṃtataḥ ।। tasmiṃś cā samaye tatra srāvastyā vahir āśrame ।
jetodyāne vihāre sa maudgalyāyana āśrayat ।। tadā te sāṃghikāḥ sarve taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ yatiṃ । vihāre saṃsthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā dharmaṃ śrotuṃ samīchire ।। tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokāś cānye api sajjanāḥ ।
tat saddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ muditāḥ samupācaran ।। tatra sarve api te lokās taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ guruṃ । samabhyarcya samānamya dharmaṃ śrotu]m upāśrayan ।। tān dṛṣṭvā samupāsīnān sa maudgalyo jinātmajaḥ ।
ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāś ca sāṃghikāḥ । saddharmmasādhanodyuktā vabhūvuḥ paribodhitāḥ ।। atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve kṛtāṃjaliḥ puṭo mudā ।
taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ natvā paprachur evam ādarāt ।। bhadanta bhagavaṃ chāstā kutredānīṃ samāśritaḥ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya viharati na manyate ।। tad asmākaṃ manānsy atra bhagavāñ chāstā yataḥ sthitaḥ ।
tat satyaṃ samupādiśya prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa maudgalyāyanaḥ sudhīḥ । sarvāns tān saṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam abravīt ।। śrutaṃ mayā bhavanto asau bhagavāñ chāstā adhunā divi ।
tato mātuḥ surāṇāṃ cā tiṣṭhate dharmam ādiśat ।। tato varṣātrimāsānte bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । atra lokahitaṃ kartum avataret svayaṃ khalu ।। iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvā te sāṃghikā janāḥ ।
sarve apy abhyanumodantaḥ svasvālayaṃ samācaran ।। sadā te sāṃghikās tasya maudgalyasya mahāmateḥ । saddharmaṃ sarvadākarṇya bhajantaḥ samupāśrayan ।। tato varṣātrimāsānte sarve te sāṃghikā janāḥ ।
api taṃ maudgalyam ānatvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। bhavantātra bhavāñ chāstā vijānīyāj jagadguroḥ । draṣṭum ichāmahe śāstuḥ saddharmaṃ tṛṣitā vayaṃ ।। ciradṛṣṭo yad asmābhir bhagavāṃ sa munīśvaraḥ ।
