tad asyāgramunīndrasya darśanaṃ dātum arhati ।। tad asmadanukampārthaṃ bhavan ṛddhiprabhāvataḥ । gatvā svarge munīndrasya sahasā samupakramet ।। tatra gatvā bhavāc chāstur munīndrasya jagadguroḥ ।
asmākaṃ vacanaiś cāpi vaṃdatāṃ caraṇāmbujau ।। dehe ca kauśalaṃ saukhyaṃ pṛchatāṃ vacanaiś ca naḥ । evaṃ cāpi puraḥ śāstur nivedituṃ samarhati ।। bhagavaṃ nātha sarvajña te jāmbūdvīpikā narāḥ ।
bhavantaṃ draṣṭum ichanti saddharmāmṛtalālasāḥ ।। yad bhavān sarvasatvānāṃ hitaṃ kartuṃ samudyataḥ । tad bhagavān manuṣyāṇāṃ dharmam ādeṣṭum arhati ।। narāḥ svarge samāgaṃtuṃ śaknuvanti na ke cana ।
devās tu sarvalokeṣu pracaranti yathechayā ।। tad bhagavān manuṣyāṇāṃ hitārthāyānukampayā । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ jambudvīpam avātaret ।। vayaṃ sarve sadā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
satkṛtya śraddhayā dharmmaṃ śrutvā saṃprabhajemahi ।। evaṃ śāstar mahāvijña gatvā tatra surālaye । bhagavaṃtaṃ jagannāthaṃ saṃprārthyeha samānaya ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaiḥ śrutvā sa maudgalyo mahārddhimān ।
evam iti pratijñāya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। atha te sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokāś cāpi mahātmanā । tenādhivāsitaṃ matvā muditāḥ svasvālayaṃ yayuḥ ।। atha so arhaṃ mahābhijño maudgalyana ātmavit ।
svarge gaṃtuṃ samādhāya samādhiṃ vidadhe kṣaṇaṃ ।। tataḥ sa ṛddhivīryeṇa suparṇa iva khe agamat । bhāsayan sahasā gatvā divi śāstur upācarat ।। tatra taṃ samupāyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān mudā ।
svāgataṃ prehi maudgalya niṣīdeti samabravīt ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sa maudgalyaḥ pramoditaḥ । sāñjaliḥ pādayoḥ śāstuḥ praṇatvaivaṃ samabravīt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña prāgato ahaṃ mudā divi ।
bhavatāṃ darśanaṃ kartuṃ tat prasīda dayānidhe ।। kaccit te kuśalaṃ śāstaḥ kiñcid vādhāpi naiva hi । yātrā sukhaṃ valaṃ vīryaṃ kaccit kāye na cānyathā ।। bhavān api vijānīyād yadarthe aham ihāgataḥ ।
tathāpi bhagavann atra vijñāpayeya sarvathā ।। bhavatāṃ sāṃghikaiḥ sarvair lokaiś cāpi mahājanaiḥ । bhavantaṃ draṣṭum ichadbhiḥ preṣito aham ihāgataḥ ।। te sarve sāṃghikā lokā bhavatāṃ caraṇāmbuje ।
vandanti kauśalaṃ kāye paripṛchanti cādarāt ।। evaṃ cāpi vadante te sarve lokāś ca sāṃghikāḥ । saddharmaśravaṇotsāharahitā vikalāśayāḥ ।। bhagavān sarvasatvānāṃ hitārthe bodhim āptavān ।
tat tathātra manuṣyāṇāṃ dharmam ādeṣṭum arhati ।। tataḥ svarge samāgaṃtuṃ śaknuvanti na ke cana । devās tu sarvalokeṣu pracaranti yathechayā ।। tad bhagavān manuṣyānāṃ hitārthāyānukampayā । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ jambūdvīpam avātaret ।।
vayaṃ sarve sadā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkṛtya śraddhayā dharmaṃ śrutvā saṃprabhajemahi ।। evam asmadvacobhis tvaṃ gatvā tatra surālaye । bhagavaṃtaṃ jagannāthaṃ saṃprārthyeha samānaya ।।
iti taiḥ prārthyamāne ahaṃ tatheti pratibodhitaḥ । bhavatāṃ vijñāpanāṃ kartuṃ sahasā samupācare ।। tad bhagavan manuṣyāṇāṃ hitānukampayādhunā । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ bhuvy eva tarttum arhati ।।
iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ dṛṣṭvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra sarve śakrādayo amarāḥ । saddharmam śravaṇotsāhāḥ samāgātāḥ samaṃtataḥ ।।
kṛtvā pūjāṃ munīndrasya praṇatvā caraṇāmbuje । parivṛtya puraskṛtya dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayan ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvan samupāśritān । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve śakrādayo api te । devāḥ saṃharṣitā bodhicaryābhivāñchito abhavan ।। tat samīkṣya sa maudgalyaḥ kiñcid vihasito mudā । bhagavaṃtaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samaciṃtayat ।।
ihāpi bhagavānn evaṃ samākīrṇasabhāśritaḥ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya viharati yathābhuvi ।। atha sa bhagavāṃs tasya maudgalyasya mahāmateḥ । manaścintitam ājñāya taṃ maudgalyaṃ samabravīt ।।
na me maudgalya satkāravaṃdhitaṃ bhavate manaḥ । api tv ahaṃ yathechāmi tathā sarvaṃ samṛddhyati ।। āyāntv ihāmarāḥ sarve iti mayā yadecchyate । tadā sarva ime devā āgachaṃti samaṃtataḥ ।।
gachantu ca surāḥ sarve iti mayā yadehyate । tadā sarva ime devā gachaṃti ca svam ālayaṃ ।। evaṃ me sarvakāryeṣu mano abhilaṣitaṃ yathā । tathātra sarvakāryāṇi siddhyaṃte hi sadā tadā ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā maudgalya ātmavit । śāstuḥ pādāmbujau natvā sāṃjaliḥ samupāśrayat ।। tataḥ sabhāṃ surāṃ kīrṇāṃ sa maudgalyāyano yatiḥ । tāra sarvāṃ saṃnirīkṣyaivaṃ bhagavantam abhāṣata ।।
vicitrā bhagavan devāparṣad iyaṃ virājate । nūnam ime surāḥ sarve saṃbuddhapadalābhinaḥ ।। santi hy asyāṃ sabhāyāṃ ye saṃbuddhe saṃprasāditāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।।
santi dharme prasannā ye āryaśīlaiḥ samanvitāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।। santi saṃghe prasannā ye āryadharmānucāriṇaḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।।
iti maudgalyasaṃproktaṃ śrutvā sa bhagavāṃs tathā । taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ dṛṣṭvānuvarṇayan sāmādiśat ।। evam etad dhi maudgalya vicitreyaṃ mahāsabhā । surendrapramukhā devā yatra santi pramoditāḥ ।।
santi buddhe prasannā ye saṃbodhisādhanotsahāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te saṃbodhipadonmukhāḥ ।। santi dharme prasannā ye āryaśīlasamācarāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhigāminaḥ ।।
saṃti saṃghe prasannā ye āryasatyasamanvitāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।। evaṃ śāstrā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā devādhipo api saḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ samālokya maudgalyaṃ ca tathābravīt ।।
vicitrā bhagavan devaparṣad iyaṃ virājate । yatra santi mahāsatvāḥ saṃbodhisādhanodyatāḥ ।। santi buddhe prasannā ye śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te saṃbuddhapadalābhinaḥ ।।
saṃti dharme prasannā ye śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te saṃbuddhapadalābhinaḥ ।। santi dharme prasannā ye śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।।
saṃti saṃghe prasannā ye śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । kāyabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।। iti devādhipākhyātaṃ śrutvānyāpi surātmajaḥ । maudgalyaṃ śrīghanaṃ cāpi śakraṃ caikṣyaivam abravīt ।।
vicitreyaṃ mahāsatva devasabhā virājate । santi yatra mahātmānaḥ saṃbodhisādhodyatāḥ ।। santi saṃghe prasannā ye satkṛtya prabhajanti te । dehabhedād ihotpannā bhavaṃti bodhilābhinaḥ ।।
santi dharme prasannā ye bhajanti śraddhayā mudā । dehabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।। santi buddhe prasannā ye bhajaṃti śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । dehabhedād ihotpannās te api saṃbodhilābhinaḥ ।।
evam etat samākhyātaṃ maudgalyena mahātmanā । munīndraśakradevaiś ca śrutvā sarve surā mudā ।। prabodhitāḥ parijñāya saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ । tatra sarve api te devās triratnabhajanodyatāḥ ।।
tatpuṇyaiḥ śrotaāpattiphalaṃ sākṣāt samāyayuḥ ।। tatas tāṃ śrīghanaṃ nātvā maudgalyaṃ ca prasāditāḥ । te śakrādayo devāḥ sarve svasvālayāṃ yayuḥ ।। atha so arhan mahābhijño maudgalyāyana ātmavit ।
bhagavantaṃ tam ānamya sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatkāryyaṃ prasiddhyati । atra sarve surā bhadraiś caranti bodhimānasāḥ ।। tat tatrāpi manuṣyāṇāṃ hitāya bhagavān api । jambudvīpe adhunā śāstaḥ samavatarttum arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthite tena maudgalyena mahātmanā । bhagavāṃs taṃ mahāsatvaṃ maudgalyam evam ādiśat ।। sādhu gachādhunā tatra jambudvīpe nijāśrame । gatvā lokasabhāmadhye sthitvaivaṃ saṃprabodhaya ।।
avatarej jagadvandhur ito ahni saptame divaḥ । sāṃkāśe nagare hy āpajjure vana udumvare ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā maudgalya ātmavit । tatheti prativijñapya tathā kartuṃ samaichata ।।
atha sa ṛddhimān yogī maudgalyāyana ātmavit । sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā samādhiṃ vidadhe tadā ।। tataḥ so arhaṃ mahābhijño maudgalyo antarhito divi । kṣaṇāt pakṣī yathākāśāj jambudvīpam avātarat ।।
tatra jetāśrame so arhann avatārya nijāśrame । śubhāsanasamāsīnaḥ prabhāsayan nyaṣīdata ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvāsana āsīnaṃ maudgalyaṃ samupāgataṃ । matvā te sāṃghikāḥ sarve muditāḥ samupācaran ।।
tac chrutvā muditāḥ sarve lokāś cāpi nṛpādayaḥ । vihāre jetakārāme sahasā samupācaran ।। tatrāsanasamāsīnaṃ maudgalyaṃ taṃ maharddhikaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sarve api te natvā parivṛtyopatasthire ।।
tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve maudgalyaṃ taṃ maharddhikaṃ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭā natvā paprachur evam ādarāt ।। bhadanta kuśalaṃ kaccid bhavato api jagadguroḥ । kutra sa bhagavān dharmam ādiśaṃs tiṣṭhate divi ।।
kadā sa bhagavāṃc chāstā svargād iha samācaret । kathaṃ cāpi samākhyāti tat sarvaṃ samupādiśa ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa maudgalyāyano yatiḥ । tāṃ sarvān saṃghikāl lokāṃś cāpi dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt ।।
bhavantaḥ kuśalaṃ śāstu munīndrasya mamāpi ca । yuṣmākam api nāmno aham avandaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। parijātam upāśritya sendradevaiḥ samarcitaḥ । mātuḥ sa bhagavān dharmam ādiśaṃs tiṣṭhate divi ।।
yathā yuṣmābhir ākhyātaṃ tathā niveditaṃ mayā । śrutvā sa bhagavāṃc chāstā mamaivaṃ samupādiśat ।। ito ahni saptame svargād avatareya bhūtale । sāṃkāśanagaropāpajjure vane udumvare ।।
ity ādiśya munīndreṇa preṣito aham ihācare । etad yūyaṃ parijñāya prābhyanandata sāṃprataṃ ।। iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvā te saṃghikā mudā । sevaṃ nṛpādi lokāś ca prābhyanandan pramoditāḥ ।।
tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokā bhūpādayo api ca । sāṃkāśanagaropāpajjure vane upācaran ।। tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra svarge sendrān surān api । mātaraṃ samupāmaṃtrya pura evam upādiśat ।।
mātaḥ sendrādi devāś ca yūyaṃ sarve samādarāt । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracaradhvaṃ sadā śubhe ।। gacheyaṃ sāṃprataṃ dharmam upadeṣṭuṃ mahītale । nṛṇām api hitārthena gantum ichāmi nānyathā ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve sendrāḥ surā api । mātāpi sāṃjalir natvā prārthayat taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña ko asmākaṃ dharmam ādiśet । tad atra kṛpayā dharmam ādeṣṭuṃ sthātum arhati ।।
iti taiḥ prārthite bhūyo bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । mātaraṃ tān surān sarvān dṛṣṭvaivaṃ ca samādiśat ।। mātar nāhaṃ sadaikatra tiṣṭheyaṃ dharmam ādiśan । sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbuddho asmi jagadguruḥ ।।
tan mātar aham ālokya martyānāṃ hitakāmpayā । saddharmāmṛtasaṃdānaṃ dātuṃ gachāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā mātā surā api । sendrāḥ sarve api te śāstuḥ pādāmbuje praṇemire ।।
tatas te tridaśāḥ sarve mātāpi tasya tāyinaḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya natvā svasvālayaṃ yayuḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra devālaye samāhitaḥ । tat samādhiṃ samādhāya kṣaṇād antarhito acarat ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra jambudvīpe prabhāsayan । sāṃkāśanagaropāpajjure dāve udumvare ।। avatīrya kṣaṇāt tatra śuddhāsane surāstṛte । samādhāya samāsīnas tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā svāsanāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ samupāgataṃ । sarve te sāṃghikā lokā bhūpādayo apy upācaran ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcyopatasthire ।।
brahmaśakrādi devāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । daityā vidyādharā nāgā garuḍāḥ siddhādayo api ca ।। śrīghanaṃ samāyātaṃ draṣṭuṃ sarve samāgatāḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcyopatasthire ।।
tatropapāduko bhikṣur bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । devādi sarvalokāṃś ca bhojayituṃ nyamaṃtrayat ।। bhagavān api devādi lokāḥ sarve prasāditāḥ । tasyānugraham ādhātuṃ tatheti pratyamodayan ।।
atha sa bhagavāṃs tatra bhojanasamayāgate । saṃghamelāpane gaṇḍīm ākoṭayan pranādinīṃ ।। tadgaṇḍīdeśanākāle tasya bhikṣor yathehitaṃ । tathāsanāṃ vastrāṇi divyāni rucirāni ca ।।
pūjāṅgāny api divyāni bhojyapānāmṛtāny api । sarvāṇy upacāravastūni punaḥ prādurbabhūvire ।। tadā sa bhikṣur ālokya sarvasāmagrasaṃyutaṃ । bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।।
bhagavan bhojanasyātra samayo varttate adhunā । tat sasaṃgho bhavān atra svasvāsane niṣīdatu ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra pādyaṃ gṛhya sasāṃghikaḥ । svasvāsane samāruhya samāśrayad yathākramaṃ ।।
tathā devādi lokāś ca sarvasvasvāsaneṣu tat । yathākramaṃ samāśritya saṃniṣeduḥ prasāditāḥ ।। tān buddhapramukhān sarvān svasvāsanasamāśritān । dṛṣṭvā sa mudito bhikṣur yathāvidhiṃ samarcayat ।।
tato divyopacārais tair bhojyapānāmṛtādibhiḥ । tān buddhapramukhān sarvan yathechaiḥ samatoṣayat ।। saṃbuddhapramukhāḥ sarve saṃghā lokāḥ surādayaḥ । tad divyabhojanaṃ bhuktvā vismitās tṛptim āyayuḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhikṣur ālokya sarvāns tān saṃpratoṣitān । tatpātrāṇy apanītvā taddhastādīn samaśodhayat ।। tataḥ sa bhikṣur oṣadhyatāmbūlādi rasāyanaiḥ । tān buddhapramukhān sarvān saṃmoditān akārayat ।।
tatropapāduko bhikṣuḥ sāṃjaliḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । sasāṃghikaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ natvā tatpura āśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya bhikṣor matvā śubhāśayaṃ । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।।
taddharmadeśanāṃ śrutvā sa upapāduko yatiḥ । bhitvā avidyāgaṇaṃ prāptavidyābhijñāpado bhavan ।। paṃcagaṇḍamayaṃ dehaṃ saṃsāram aticañcalaṃ । viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatīś cāpi vighātinīḥ ।।
kleśān māragaṇāñ cāpi jitvārhatvam avāptavān । tataḥ so arhaṃ mahābhijñaḥ pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ ।। jiteṃdriyo viśuddhātmā nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ । saṃsāralābhasatkāranispṛhas trijagatsv api ।।
vaṃdyaḥ pūjyo abhimānyo abhūd brahmacārī jinātmajaḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayākulitāśayaḥ । bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavan kiṃ purānena bhikṣuṇā sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ ।
yenopapāduko arhaṃ ca bhavaty ayaṃ mahāsudhīḥ ।। yac cāpy asya yater bhikṣoḥ prārthitaṃ tat samṛdhyati । etat sarvaṃ samākhyāya sarvān asmān prabodhaya ।। evaṃ tair bhikṣubhiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tān sarvān sāṃghikāl lokān samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavānena bhikṣuṇā yat purākṛtaṃ । tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yuṣmaccittaprabodhane ।। purāsīn bhagavān buddho vipaścī nāma sarvavit ।
dharmarājo jagacchāstā tathāgato munīśvaraḥ ।। sa saṃbuddho jagannātho vandhumato mahīpateḥ । vandhumatyā mahāpūryyā rājadhānyā upāśraye ।। jināśrame mahodyāne sarvasatvahitechayā ।
saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tasya vipaścinaḥ śāstuḥ sāṃghikāḥ paṃcabhikṣavaḥ । anyasmin mahodyāne varṣāsu vyaharans tadā ।। tatraikabhikṣuṇā teṣāṃ caturṇāṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ ।
vaiyāvṛtyakṛtaṃ karma suprasannānucāriṇā ।। tatas te bhikṣavas sarve catvāras tatprasādhanāt । sarvavidyāsamudyuktāḥ samādhisādhanodyatāḥ ।। klesān māragaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ ।
sākṣād arhattvasaṃprāptā babhūvu brahmavittamāḥ ।। tān arhato mahābhijñān dṛṣṭvā sa paṃcamo yatiḥ । muditas taccaraṇān natvā praṇidhānaṃ tathā vyadhāt ।। yad etebhir mamāgamya sākṣād arhattvam āgataṃ ।
etaddharmavipākena pravrajyārhattvam āpnuyāṃ ।। sarvopakaraṇair dravyair avaikalyaṃ yathehitaṃ । tat tathā sarvam apy eva sarvatrāpi samṛddhyatu ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sa bhikṣuḥ paṃcamaḥ sudhīḥ ।
ayam eva mahābhijño bhavati hīti manyatāṃ ।। punar api bhavaty atra yenāyam upapādukaḥ । tat karmaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta yūyam ādarāt ।। purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo nāma sarvavit ।
arhan nātho jagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। sa saṃbuddho mahāpūryā vārāṇasyā upāśrame । mṛgadāve adiśad dharmaṃ vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra vārāṇasyaṃ gṛhādhipaḥ ।
āsīt tasya priyā bhāryyā garbhiṇī garbhapīḍitā ।। prasūtisamaye akrandad ārttasvarā vilāpitā । tasyā ārttaravaṃ śrutvā sa bharttā karuṇārditaḥ । śokālaye samudvignaḥ niśrityaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
hā duḥkhaṃ garbbhapīḍāsyā jāyate kiṃ kariṣyate । evaṃ duḥkhaṃ hi saṃsāre rogiṇāṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ ।। mātur evaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ garbbhasthasya śiśor na kiṃ । etad duḥkham ahaṃ soḍhuṃ na śaknuyāṃ kathaṃ cana ।।
tad atra kāśyapasyāhaṃ śāsane śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā careyaṃ saṃvṛtiṃ sadā ।। iti niścitya sa śreṣṭhī gatvā kāśyapaśāsane । pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cacāra saṃvṛtiṃ sadā ।।
tataḥ kāle samāghrāte śreṣṭhī sa parikheditaḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tadā ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadātra punarbhave । mātur garbhe hy ajāyeyaṃ bhaveyam upapādukaḥ ।। etena praṇidhānena kāśyapaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
triratnabhajanaiḥ kṛtvā pracacāra samāhitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sārthavāhaḥ sa sanmatiḥ । bhavaty ayaṃ mahābhijñaḥ sāṃpratam upapādukaḥ ।। yathānena tadā tatra praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā ।
tathātra śāsane bauddhe pravrajyārhattvam āpyate ।। evaṃ hi manyatāṃ sarve saṃsāre karma yat kṛtaṃ । tat phalaṃ bhujyate nūnaṃ yathehitaṃ tathā dhruvaṃ ।। yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ ।
abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva kṛtakarmaphalaṃ kvacit ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ kriyate nāpi codakaiḥ । vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate nāpi kṣīyate naiva bhūmiṣu ।। anyāthāpi bhaven naiva yat kṛtaṃ tat phalaṃ khalu ।
sarvatra bhujyate sarvair jantubhir bhavacāribhiḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya karmaṇaḥ pāke duḥkhataiva sadā bhave । śubhasya sukhatā nityaṃ miśritasyāpi miśritaṃ ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā sukhavāṃchibhiḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te bhikṣavas tathā । satyam iti parijñāya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।। so api bhikṣuḥ parijñāya śrutvaivaṃ sugatoditaṃ ।
prabodhitaḥ prasannātmā prācaran sarvadā śubhe ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । śrutvā rājans tvayāpy evaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ ।
prerayitvā śubhe dharme pālanīyās tvayādarāt ।। evaṃ te sarvadā rājan sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet । krameṇa bodhim āsadya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ ।
tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। yadāvadānaṃ hy upapādukasya śṛṇvaṃti ye cāpi niśāmayaṃti । sarve api te kleśavimuktadehā bhuktvā sukhaṃ yānti jinālayaṃ te ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ purogataḥ ।
upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhaṃ sudhīr yatiḥ ।
upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja tava puṇyapravṛddhaye । yāthā me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā mayā pravakṣyate ।। tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho mahāmuniḥ ।
ekasmin samaye tatra śrāvastyā bahir āśrame ।। jetodyāne manoramye vihāre maṇimaṇḍite । sarvalokahitārthena vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tatra sa bhagavāṃc chāstā sabhāsthitaḥ prabhāsayan ।
tāṃ sarvān sāṃghikān dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। anityā bhikṣavaḥ sarve saṃskārā adhruvāḥ kṣaṇāḥ । vipariṇāmadharmāṇo asthirā nāsvāsikā api ।। yāvanto bhikṣavaḥ satvāś caturyonisamudbhavāḥ ।
bhautikāḥ prāṇinaḥ sarve jaṃgamā acalā api ।। ete api prāṇinaḥ sarve saṃskārabhavacāriṇaḥ । svakṛtakarmabhuṃjāno bhramanti ṣaḍgatiṣv api ।। yāvantaḥ prāṇinaḥ satvāḥ sarveṣu narakeṣv api ।
svakṛtakarmabhuṃjāno bhramaṃti duḥkhapīḍitāḥ ।। te sarve api svadaivāṃtte kāle mṛtyuṃ vrajanty api । kṛtakarmānusāreṇa punarbhave bhramaṃti te ।। kasya na janma mṛtyuś ca maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।
yāvaṃtaḥ pretikāḥ satvāḥ sarve pretālayeṣv api ।। svakṛtakarmabhuṃjāno bhramaṃti duḥkhapīḍitāḥ । te ca sarve api karmāṃte kāle mṛtyuṃ prayāṃty api ।। kṛtakarmānusāreṇa punarjanma labhaṃti te ।
sarveṣām api jantūnāṃ saṃskāragaticāriṇāṃ ।। kasya na janma mṛtyuś ca maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ । tiryaggatiṣu yāvaṃtas tiryañcuḥ prāṇinaś ca te ।। sarve api karmabhuṃjāno bhramaṃti svakṛtānugāḥ ।
te ca sarve api karmānte kāle mṛtyuṃ vrajaṃty api ।। te ca karmānusāreṇa punarjanma labhanty api । sarveṣām api jaṃtūnāṃ saṃskāragaticāriṇāṃ ।। kasya na janma mṛtyuś ca maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ । yāvanto manujāḥ satvā martyalokeṣu bhūmiṣu ।
svakṛtakarmabhuṃjānā bhramaṃti sukhaduḥkhitāḥ ।। te ca sarve api karmānte kāle mṛtyuṃ prayāṃty api । te ca karmānusāreṇa punarjanma labhaṃty api ।। ye cāpi brāhmaṇā dhīrāḥ sarve śāstravicakṣaṇāḥ ।
ṣaṭkarmaniratā vijñāś caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ ।। te api sarve svakarmānubhuṃjāno bhavacāriṇaḥ । prayāṃti samaye mṛtyuṃ kasya mṛtyur bhave na hi ।। yāvanto ṛṣayo dhīrāḥ paṃcābhijñāguṇābdhayaḥ ।
te sarve samaye mṛtyuṃ prayāṃti bhavacāriṇaḥ ।। ye cāpi tīrthikā dhīrā mahatkaṣṭatapodharāḥ । te api ca samaye mṛtyuṃ gachaṃti bhavagāminaḥ ।। ye dhīrā yoginaś cāpi yogadhyānasamāhitāḥ ।
te api sarve prayāṃty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpy upāsakā dhīrāḥ śuddhaśīlā vrataṃdharāḥ । te cāpi samaye sarve prayāṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi kṣatriyā vīrā rājāno lokapālakāḥ ।
te api sarve prayāṃty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi maṃtriṇo vijñā hitārthaṃ maṃtradeśakāḥ । te api sarve prayāṃty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpy evaṃ mahāmātyā rājyapālanatatparāḥ ।
te sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye ca bhaṭṭā mahāvīrā duṣṭamardanatatparāḥ । te api sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi dhaninaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ sādhavo bhadrakārakāḥ ।
te api sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi vaṇijo dhīrāḥ sārthavāhā dhanādhipāḥ । te api sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi śilpino vijñā hitārthaṃ guṇasādhakāḥ ।
te api sarve pragachaṃti samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi kṛṣikarttāraḥ prāṇahitārthasādhakāḥ । te api sarve vrajanty eva maraṇaṃ samaye dhruvaṃ ।। ye ca vaiśyāḥ prajānāthāḥ sarvadravyahitaṃkarāḥ ।
te api sarve vrajanty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi sadguṇādhānā daivajñā vidhivittamāḥ । te cāpi samaye sarve prayāṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye ca vaidyā mahāvijñāḥ sarvarogaśamaṃkarāḥ ।
te api sarve vrajanty eva maraṇaṃ samaye dhruvaṃ ।। ye capi bhautikā vijñāḥ sarvabhūtapraśāṃtakāḥ । te api sarve visaṃyogād vrajaṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। ye cāpi maṃtriṇo vīrāḥ sarve karmārthasādhakāḥ । te api sarve visaṃyogāt prayāṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
evam anye api lokāś ca nihīnamadhyamottamāḥ । sarve mṛtyuṃ prayānty eva kasya mṛtyur vaśe khalu ।। gaṃdharvāś ca mahāvīrā devādhikā maharddhikāḥ । te api sarve vrajanty eva nissārā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
kumbhāṇḍāś ca mahāvīrā mahābhīmā mahāvalāḥ । te api kāle prayānty eva sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। nāgāś cāpi mahābhimā garuḍāś cā maharddhikāḥ । te api sarve prayānty eva kāle mṛtyuṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ ।।
yakṣāś cāpi mahāvīrā devāsuramaharddhikāḥ । te api sarve prayānty eva kāle mṛtyuṃ nirudyamāḥ ।। kinnarāś ca mahāvīrāḥ khagāmino maharddhikāḥ । te api sarve nirutsāhāḥ kāle yānti yamālayaṃ ।।
siddhāś cāpi mahāvīrāḥ sarvakāryārthasādhakāḥ । te api sarve vrajanty eva kāle mṛtyuṃ nirudyamāḥ ।। sādhyāś cāpi mahādhīraḥ sarvahitārthasādhakāḥ । te api sarve prayānty eva maraṇaṃ sarvadā dhruvaṃ ।।
rākṣasāś ca mahābhīmā mahāvīryaparākramāḥ । te api sarve prayānty eva nivīryā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। evam anye api satvāś ca siṃhavyāghrādi jaṃtavaḥ । paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaś cāpi krimikīṭādayo api ca ।।
aṇḍajāḥ svedajāś caiva sarve api prāṇino api te । kāle daivānubhoktāro vrajanti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। daityāś cāpi mahāvīrā māhāvīryā maharddhikāḥ । te api sarve prayāṃty evaṃ samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
śakrādayo api devendrāḥ sārve devāḥ sudhāṃśinaḥ । te api kāle divaś cyutvā bhramaṃti ṣaḍgatiṣv api ।। apsaraso api divyāṃgā yathākāma sukhaṃcarāḥ । tāś cāpi samaye sarvāś cyutvā yāṃti yamālayaṃ ।।
vidyādharā mahābhijñā yathechā sukhacāriṇaḥ । te api sarve nirutsāhāḥ kāle yāṃti yamāntike ।। evam anye api lokāś ca janmino bhavacāriṇaḥ । sarve api karmabhuṃjānaḥ kāle mṛtyuṃ vrajanty api ।।
rasātalacarā ye svakṛtakarmabhojinaḥ । teṣāṃ api ca sarveṣāṃ maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।। kāmadhātucarā ye ca svakṛte karmacāriṇaḥ । teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।।
rūpadhātugatā ye cā dhyānabhogasamāhitāḥ । teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।। ye cāpy ārūpiṇo devā nirālokyā niraṃjanāḥ । teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।।
ye cāpi bhikṣavo arhanto vītakleśā jiteṃdriyāḥ । māracaryāvinirmuktā nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ ।। teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ । kasya mṛtyur bhave nāsti janmino maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। pratyekasugatā ye ca niḥkleśā vijiteṃdriyāḥ ।
nirvikalpā nirāsaṃgā ekāṃtadhyānacāriṇaḥ ।। teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ । kasya nāsti bhave mṛtyur jātasya maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkarāḥ ।
mahābhijñā mahādhīrāś caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ ।। daśabhūmīśvarā nāthā daśapāramitāratāḥ । satvārthavaśitāprāptā dhāraṇībalasaṃyutāḥ ।। teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ ।
kasya nāsti bhave mṛtyur janmino maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। tathāgatāś ca saṃbuddhāḥ sarvajñāḥ sugatā jināḥ । mārajito jagannāthāḥ ṣaḍabhijñā munīśvarāḥ ।। dharmarājāḥ suśāstāro daśavalā vināyakāḥ ।
samaṃtabhadrakarttāraś caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ ।। te sarve bhagavanto api traidhātubhuvaneṣv api । bodhicaryāṃ kṛtvā samādiśya saddharmaṃ ca samaṃtataḥ ।। sarvatra maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat ।
bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya sarvasatvāñ chubhānvitān ।। sarvasaṃbuddhakāryāṇi samāpya parinivṛtāḥ । supariśuddhanirvāṇaṃ samaye saṃvrajanty api ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।
sarvān saṃskārajān duḥkhāns tyaktuṃ prārabhatodyamaṃ ।। anityā vata saṃskārā avidyākalpanodbhavāḥ । kleśāśrayā mahāduḥkhamūlā vidhvaṃsino aśubhāḥ ।। tasmāt saṃsāraduḥkhāni tyaktum ichaṃti ye narāḥ ।
te māyāsaṃratiṃ tyaktvā caraṃtu buddhaśāsane ।। ye buddhaśāsane bhaktyā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । saṃbodhisaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā saṃcaraṃte samāhitāḥ ।। te sarve śubhātmāno niḥkleśā vimalāśayāḥ ।
bodhicaryāṃ samāsādya kuryus satvahitaṃ sadā ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ । samyakṣaṃbodhim āsādya bhaveyuḥ sugatā jināḥ ।। tataḥ sarvatra lokeṣu kṛtvā loke subhadratāṃ ।
bodhimārge jagallokaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya prayatnataḥ ।। tato nirvāṇam āsādya nirviśeraṃ jinālaye । tadā te vimalātmāno nilīnāḥ syu nijālaye ।। evaṃ matvā nijānaṃdaṃ prāptuṃ saṃbodhisādhane ।
trikāye vīryam utthāpya carantu buddhaśāsane ।। kiṃ kāyena vinā dharmaṃ vācāpi kiṃ vinā guṇaṃ । manaso kiṃ vinā vīryyaṃ kiṃ vīryaṃ saṃvaraṃ vinā ।। yathā puṣpaṃ tathā dehaṃ yathā pakvaphalaṃ tanuḥ ।
kṣaṇāc cyutvāyate bhumau tathā kiṃ śobhate tanuḥ ।। kumbhakārakṛtaṃ yadvan mṛnmayaṃ māmabhājanaṃ । tadvad dehaṃ kṣaṇadhvaṃsi matvā carantu saṃvaraṃ ।। kadalīstambhasaṃkāśaṃ nissāraṃ bhedano sahaṃ ।
matvā dehaṃ samutthāya carantu saugataṃ vṛsaṃ ।। phenapiṇḍopamaṃ kāyaṃ nirguṇaṃ kṣaṇabhaṃguraṃ । matvā vīryamahotsāhaṃ dhṛtvā caraṃtu saṃvaraṃ ।। āyurdehe sthiraṃ naiva tṛṇaṃ patragatāmbuvat ।
matvā saṃbodhisaṃprāptyai carantu saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। ye saugatavrataṃ dhṛtvā caraṃti bodhilabdhaye । durgatiṃ na gachaṃti gachaṃti sadgatiṃ sadā ।। tasmād ichaṃti ye bhadraṃ saṃsāre bodhisādhanaṃ ।
te triratnaṃ sadā bhaktyā bhajaṃtu śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। triratnabhajanotpannaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇute kvacit । etatpuṇyabalenaiva jīyate sarvapātakaṃ ।। puṇyam eva jaganmitraṃ pāpa eva jagadripuḥ ।
tat puṇyamitram ārādhya jayaṃtu pāpakaṃ ripuṃ ।। puṇyavān puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvatra jagate sadā । yathābhilaṣitaṃ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti sukhāvatiṃ ।। ity evaṃ bhagavān āha śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ ।
satyam iti paribuddhvā praceruḥ saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। etan me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā tatra mayocyate । tvayāpy evaṃ mahārāja caritavyaṃ śubhe vṛṣe ।। prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ ।
śubhe dharme pratiṣṭhāpya pālanīyāḥ sadādarāt ।। tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet sadā । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ ।
tathety uktvā praṇatvā ca prābhyanadat sapārṣadaḥ ।। anityatāsūtram idaṃ subhāṣyaṃ śṛṇvanti ye cāpi narāḥ prasannāḥ । sukhāni bhuktvā śubhadharmaraktāḥ samyāṃti cānte sugatālaye te ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ puraḥsthitaḥ ।
upaguptaṃ tam ānamya mudaivaṃ punar abravīt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa yatīśaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।
tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru ।। tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ ।
sarvajño arhañ jagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। puraikasamaye tatra śrāvastyā bahir āśrame । jetavane mahodyāne vihāre maṇimaṃḍite ।। sarvasatvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan ।
saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tatra te bhikṣavo arhantaḥ sāṃghikāś cailakā api । bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ sarvasatvahitārthinaḥ ।। bhikṣuṇyaḥ śuddhaśīlāś ca vratinaś ca śubhāśayāḥ ।
triratnasevakāḥ śrāddhā upāsakā upāsikāḥ ।। sarve api sāṃghikās tatra saddharmaṃ śrotum āgatāḥ । kramāt taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā kṛtvā tridhā pradakṣiṇāṃ ।। tat sabhāyāṃ krameṇaiva puraskṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭo dṛṣṭvā samupatasthur ādarāt ।। tadā tatra sureṃdrāś ca saśakrojamaheśvaraḥ । sarve api lokapālāś ca sasainyabalavāhanaḥ ।। asurendrāḥ sasainyāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnarāḥ ।
rākṣasā garuḍā nāgāḥ siddhā vidyādharādayaḥ ।। evam anye api lokāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca maharṣayaḥ । yatayo yoginaś cāpi tīrthikāś ca tapaśvinaḥ ।। rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi nṛpo rājakumārakāḥ ।
vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ śreṣṭhā amātyāś ca mahājanāḥ ।। senānyaḥ sabalāś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā janāḥ । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca dhaninaḥ śilpino api ca ।। anye jānapadāś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api ।
evam anye api lokāś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ ।। sarve tatra samāyātā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya kramān mudā ।। tataḥ sarve api te natvā puraskṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ । saṃbodhisādhanotsāhaṃ labdhvā saṃmumudur bhṛśaṃ ।।
tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śrāvastye yo gṛhādhipaḥ । āḍhyo mahādhanaḥ śrāddhaḥ śrīmāñc chrīdopamaḥ kṛtī ।। sa tadā tatra saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । draṣṭuṃ jetāśrame ramye vihāre samupācarat ।।
tatra sabhāsamāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । dṛṣṭvā sa muditaḥ śreṣṭhī praṇatvā samupācarat ।। tatra pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praṇatvā sāṃjalir mudā । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ purataḥ samupāśrayat ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā samupāsīnaṃ bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । matvā tasyāśayaṃ śuddham āryasatyam upādiśat ।। tadāryasatyam ākarṇya sa śreṣṭhī pratibodhitaḥ । saṃsāraviratas tatra pravrajituṃ samaichata ।।
tatra sa suprasannātmā śreṣṭhī mudā samutthitaḥ । sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ mahyaṃ kṛpayā dātum arhati ।।
iti saṃprārthite tena dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān muniḥ । tasyāśayaṃ viśuddhatvaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। yadi śrāddhāsti te vatsa saugataśāsane vrate । ehi cara samādhāya brahmacaryaṃ vratottamaṃ ।।
ity uktvā sa jagacchāstā savyahastena tac chiraḥ । saṃspṛṣṭvā śāsane bauddhe śreṣṭhinaṃ taṃ samagrahīt ।। tatra pravrajitas tena munīndreṇa sa muṇḍitaḥ । khikkhirīpātradhṛg bhikṣu rarāja cīvarāvṛtaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhikṣur ātmajño lābhī lokābhipūjitaḥ । āgṛhītapariṣkārā labdhadravyaṃ samācinot ।। tallabdhaṃ saṃcitaṃ dravyaṃ sa saha brahmacāribhiḥ । saṃvibhāgaṃ guroḥ kiṃcid apy akarot kadā cana ।।
tathā sa matsarākrāntahṛdayo duritāśayaḥ । svayam eva prabhuṃjānaḥ kiṃcin naiva dadau kvacit ।। tataḥ sa samaye kāladharmayukto rujāturaḥ । tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ smṛtvā nitaḥ pretālayaṃ yayau ।।
pretībhūto api sa smṛtvā tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ punaḥ । svakoṣṭhālaya āgatya tasthau svāsana āśrayan ।। tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve tatkoṣṭhe taṃ mṛtakaṃ yatiṃ । dṛṣṭvā gaṇḍīṃ parāhatya saṃskārtuṃ vidhi cārcayan ।।
tato nītvā bahirdeśe saṃskṛtya vahnināpitaṃ । tataḥ pratyāgatāḥ sarve tat koṣṭhadvāram āyayuḥ ।। tatas tal layanadvāraṃ vimucya pātracīvaraṃ । pratyaveksitum ālabdhās taṃ pretaṃ samapaśyata ।।
taṃ pretaṃ vikṛtaṃ pātraṃ dhṛtaṃ cīvaraprāvṛtaṃ । dṛṣṭvā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve samudvignā vicerire ।। tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve bhagavataḥ purogatāḥ । etat sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ praṇatvā saṃnyavedayat ।।
tac chrutvā bhagavāṃs tasya pretasyānugrahārthataḥ । sa lokodvejanārthaṃ ca tad deśaṃ samupācarat ।। tatrāsau preta ārāt taṃ bhagavaṃtam upāgataṃ । dvātriṃsallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṇḍitaṃ ।।
śatasūryyādhikodbhāsaṃ vyāmābhāsam alaṃkṛtaṃ । ratnāṃgam iva bhadrāṃśaṃ dadarśa śrīghanaṃ muniṃ ।। tatra sa preta ālokya lajjāvibheditāśayaḥ । prarudan sāṃjalir natvā tasthau prasāditāśayaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ pretaṃ saṃprasāditaṃ । brahmagambhīranirghoṣavacasā paryabhāṣata ।। bhadramukha tvayaivaitad ātmavadhāya durdhiyā । pātracīvaram ādhāya caritaṃ saṃvaraṃ vṛthā ।।
yenāpāyasamutpannaḥ pretībhūto durākṛtiḥ । kim idānīṃ ruditvātra svakṛtaṃ paribhuktavān ।। sādhv atra sāṃprataṃ cittaṃ prasādaya mamāntike । asmāc cāpi pariṣkāradravyāc cittaṃ virāgaya ।।
mā haivetaḥ punaḥ kālaṃ kṛtvā yāsyasi nairaye । tat saṃghe śaraṇaṃ gaccha tena tvaṃ sadgatiṃ vraje ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa preta utthitaḥ । sa pātracīvaraṃ dravyaṃ saṃghebhyo nirayātayat ।।
tataḥ saṃghān praṇatvaiva bhagavatpādayo pure । nipatya svakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ dideśa sāṃjalir mudā ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña yat pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ mayā । mātsaryākrāntacittena mahāmūḍhena durdhiyā ।।
tat sarvaṃ sāṃprataṃ śāstar darśayāmi bhavatpuraḥ । tat kṣamasvāparādhaṃ me prasīdatu bhavān guruḥ ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa kṛpānvitaḥ । tat pretaṃ sudṛśālokya samapaśyac ciraṃ mudā ।।
tataś ca bhagavāṃs tasya tadupāyavimuktaye । sadgatipreraṇārthena dakṣiṇām evam ādiśat ।। etaddānād dhi yat puṇyaṃ tat puṇyaṃ tvam avāpnuyāḥ । uttiṣṭha kṣipram etasmāt pretalokāt sudāruṇāt ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā pretaḥ sa moditaḥ । tatheti pratinaṃditvā natvānumodito abhavat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya pretasya śubhasādhanaṃ । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sasaṃghaḥ svāśraye yathā ।।
tathā sa preta ākarṇya saddharmaṃ taj jinoditaṃ । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bheje nityaṃ prabodhitaḥ ।। tataḥ kāle samāghrātaḥ ca preto jvaradāhitaḥ । triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā mṛto yayau yamālayaṃ ।। tataḥ pretaḥ sa satpuṇyais triratnasmaraṇodbhavaṃ ।
yamena preritas tasmāt pretamaharddhike yāyau ।। tatrāpi sa samutpanne vismitas taṃ munīśvaraṃ । smṛtvā nityaṃ sadā bheje śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। tataḥ so cintayed evaṃ kutaḥ kutrāham āgataḥ ।
kena puṇyānubhāvena mahatsaukhyaṃ labhe nv iti ।। iti ciṃtāhate tasya cittapuṇyānubhāvataḥ । triratnasmaraṇāt puṇyād iti mene sa puṇyabhāk ।। tataś cāsau parijñāya triratnabhajanotsukaḥ ।
saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ karttuṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। aho mayā sukhaṃ labdhaṃ tat saṃbuddhaprasādataḥ । tad idāniṃ munīṃdraṃ taṃ draṣṭum arhāmi sarvathā ।। ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā so api pretamaharddhikaḥ ।
snātva śuddhāmvaro divyaratnālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।। paṃcagaṃdhaviliptāṃgaṃ pariśuddhāśayaḥ śuciḥ । pūjāpaṃcopahārāṇi dhṛtvā jetāśrame asarat ।। tatra jetāśrame bhābhir avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ ।
vihāre śrīghanaṃ draṣṭuṃ muditaḥ samudācarat ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvānaṃditaḥ sa kṛtāṃjaliḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya purataḥ samupācarat ।। tatas taṃ sugataṃ nāthaṃ samabhyarcya pramoditaḥ ।
natvā sa sāṃjalir dharmaṃ śrotum ekāṃta āśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya dṛṣṭvā cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ । bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya saddharmam evam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu sādho atra saṃsāre sukhaduḥkhārthakāraṇaṃ ।
vakṣyāmy etat parijñāya samādhāya śubhe cara ।। yaḥ pumān atra saṃsāre satsaukhyaṃ sarvadechati । sa ādau śraddhayā bhaktyā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena dānaṃ dadyād yathepsitaṃ ।
etatpuṇyavipākaṃ saṃbodhau me pariṇāmayet ।। itthaṃ kṛtaṃ pradānaṃ yat tad vipāke mahat phalaṃ । kramād vṛddhitaraṃ yāyān na kṣiṇuyāt kadā cana ।। etat puṇyaparītātmā cakravarttī narādhipaḥ ।
śāstā dharmādhipo rājā bodhisatvaḥ sudhīr bhavet ।। tadāpi sa mahādātā sarvasatvahitechayā । triratnabhajaṇaṃ kṛtvā dadyād dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sa viśuddhāśayaḥ sudhīḥ ।
suśīlasaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā triratnaṃ sarvadā bhajan ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sa bhavet tridaśādhipaḥ । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ sarvadā bhajan ।। sarvasatvahitārthena śīlapāramitā caran ।
tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai manasā pariṇāmayet ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sa suyāmādhipo bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena kṣāṃtipāramitā caran । saṃbodhipadalābhāya tatpuṇyaṃ pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sa bhavet tuṣitādhipaḥ । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena vīryyapāramitodyataḥ । saṃbodhipadasaṃprāptyai tatpuṇyaṃ pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākaiḥ sa nirmāṇaratiyo bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyatat ।। sarvasatvahitārthena dhyānapāramitārataḥ । saṃbodhijñānasaṃprāptyai tatpuṇyaṃ pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākaiḥ sa vaśavartīśvaro bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajano rataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena prajñāpāramitārataḥ । tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai manasā pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sa brahmādhipatir bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnārāgaṇodyataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthāya samupāyavidhānadhṛk । tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai cetasā pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena mahābrahmādhipo bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnārādhanodyataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthāya praṇidhānasamāhitaḥ । tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai sarvathā pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sa maheśādhipo bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena balapāramitodyataḥ । tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai pradhyānaṃ pariṇāmayet ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena bodhisatvādhipo bhavet । tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnasaṃprasāditaḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthasya jñānapāramitārataḥ । tatpuṇyair bodhisaṃprāpto dharmarājo jino bhavet ।।
tataḥ sa sugataḥ śāstā jagannātho vināyakaḥ । sarvajño arhan mahābhijñas tathāgato munīśvaraḥ ।। tato māragaṇāñ jitvā bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan । sarvasatvāñ chubhe sthāpya nirvṛtaḥ saugatiṃ vrajet ।।
evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre ya ichati śivāṃ gatiṃ । sa evaṃ śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyataḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena karotu dānam ādarāt । tataḥ kramāt sa tatpuṇyaiḥ sarvāḥ pāramitā api ।।
paripūrya mahābhijñā prāpto bodhim avāpnuyāt । iti matvā śubhe nityaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ ।। śubhena sadgatiṃ yāyā pāpena durgatīṃ vrajet । pāpas tu jāyate lobhāt mātsaryamalināśrayāt ।।
vopakārāṃ sukhecho api na kiṃ cit sukham āpnuyāt । sarvadā durmatir duṣṭo durgatinirayāśrayaḥ ।। saddharmmanindako mūḍho pāpakarmarato bhavet । tasmāt mātsaryyam utsṛjya sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt ।
saṃbodhipraṇidhiṃ kṛtvā caren nityaṃ susaṃvare ।। etatpuṇyavipākena saṃsārasukhabhāk sadā । triratnabhajanotsāhī bodhicaryārato bhavet ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ ।
śivāṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। evaṃ tvaṃ vā parijñāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । bodhicittaṃ samādhāya cara nityaṃ susaṃvare ।। tathā te sarvadā bhadraṃ bhaven nityaṃ samantataḥ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa paribodhitaḥ । tatheti hi pratiśrutvā prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ ।। tataḥ sa taṃ jagannāthaṃ praṇatvā sāṃjalir mudā ।
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praṇatvā svālaye acarat ।। tatra prāptaḥ prasannātmā so api pretamaharddhikaḥ । triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracaran sarvadā mudā ।। tad rātrau tatprabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavo vismayānvitāḥ ।
sarve te prātar utthāya natvāpṛchan munīśvaraṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña ko adya rātrāv ihāgataḥ । etad vṛttaṃ samākhyāya sarvān naḥ paribodhaya ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tān sarvān sāṃghikān dṛṣṭvā bodhayitum upādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yo adya rātrāv ihāgataḥ । etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ pravakṣyāmi suvistaraṃ ।। yo asau śreṣṭhī mahāśrāddhaḥ saugate śāsane mudā ।
śraddhayā pravrajitvātra brahmacaryaṃ mudā caran ।। pravrajitaḥ sa mātsaryaparibhūto durāśayaḥ । labdhadravyaṃ na kasmai cid dadau kiñcit kadā cana ।। kevalaṃ saṃcayaṃ kṛtvā koṣṭhāgāre nidhāya tat ।
guptīkṛtvā prayatnena vyabhajan naiva kiṃ cana ।। tataḥ kāle samāghrāte dhyātvā tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ । mṛtaḥ pretālayotpannaḥ pretodbhavad bhayānakaḥ ।। tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ smṛtvā mātsaryākulitāśayaḥ ।
punaḥ pratyāgatas tatra svālaye saṃnyaṣīdata ।। tatra taṃ saṃsthitaṃ pretaṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ samupācaran । āryadharmam upādiśya prābodhayaṃ prasādayan ।। tataḥ sa suprasannātmā sasaṃghasya mamāṃtike ।
sa pātracīvaraṃ sarvaṃ taddravyaṃ nirayātayat ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । kāle tataḥ paricyutvā pretamaharddhiko abhavat ।। tatra sa suprasannātmā smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ mudā ।
matsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum iha rātrau samāgataḥ ।। sa saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mamāntike prasāditaḥ । saṃbodhisādhanotsāhī muditaḥ svālaye acarat ।। yo ayaṃ śreṣṭhī na cānyo hi rātrāv iha samāgataḥ ।
yat sa mṛto abhavat pretas mātsaryaduritāśrayāt ।। tasmāt mātsaryam uddhṛtya tyajantu śubhavāṃchinaḥ । mātsaryaṃ hi trilokeṣu pāpamūlaṃ nigadyate ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre duḥkhākaraṃ sukhāṃtakaṃ ।
mātsaryaṃ sumaduṣṭaṃ ripuṃ jayata sarvathā ।। mātsaryaṃ jīyate yair hi samuddhṛtya svamānasāt । te eva mānino vīrāḥ śūrāḥ prājñā vicakṣaṇāḥ ।। ye ca jetuṃ na mātsaryaṃ śaknuvaṃti kathaṃ cana ।
kiṃ te śūrā vijetāro virā na kleśabhojinaḥ ।। yeṣāṃ na jāyate citte mātsaryan duḥkṛtākaraṃ । te eva sukhino virā jayinaḥ kleśaghātakāḥ ।। yāvan na jīyate citte mātsaryaṃ duritāśayaṃ ।
tāvat kiṃ te suvīrā vā kṣaṇāt kleśānucāriṇaḥ ।। ye ca kleśavaśā vīrā na te dhīrā vicakṣaṇāḥ । kṣaṇāt kiṃ cin nimitteti careyur vikṛtāśayāḥ ।। tatas te kleśasaṃtaptā mūḍhā rāgāgnidāhitāḥ ।
duṣṭāḥ krodhāgnisaṃdagdhāḥ saṃpaśyeyur na kiṃ cana ।। tatas te andhā ivāloke careyur na ca satpathe । kumārga eva saṃraktāḥ pracareyuḥ pramāditāḥ ।। tato durjanasaṃraktā māracaryānucāriṇaḥ ।
asanmitropadeśena pracareyur mṛṣādṛśaḥ ।। tataḥ saddharmanindāṃ kṛtvā dānādi saṃcare । vighnaṃ kartuṃ samudyogaṃ kuryur nityaṃ samāhitāḥ ।। tatas te pāpino duṣṭā unmattā iva tāyinaḥ ।
svayaṃ naṣṭāḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayeyuḥ pravaṃcakāḥ ।। tatas te kleśasaṃtaptā mahopāyānurāgiṇaḥ । sughorāṇi pāpāni kuryāttiḥ śaṃkitāśayāḥ ।। tato bhakṣam apīchaṃtaṃ bhuktvāgamye api saṃratāḥ ।
viparītasamācārāḥ pracāreyur virodhitāḥ ।। tatas te pātakālīḍhā mahāduḥkhābhighātitāḥ । tīvrātivedanāghrātā mṛtā yāyur yamālayaṃ ।। tatra yamo mahārājā dṛṣṭvā taṃ duritāśayaṃ ।
sahasā karmaśāsibhyaḥ samarpya saṃpracodayan ।। tatra tair yamadūtās tāṃ gṛhītvā sahasā balāt । yathā karmānusāreṇa śāsayeyur yathāvidhiṃ ।। tatra te daivabhogyāṃ bhuktvā bhoktuṃ samaṃtataḥ ।
coditā yamadūtaiś ca bhrameyur narakeṣv api ।। tatra te daivabhogyāni bhuktvātitīvraduḥkhitāḥ । asahyavedanākrāṃtā niṣīdeyuḥ prakheṭitāḥ ।। evaṃ te daivabhogyāṃ bhuktvā tathā ciraṃ sadā । narakān narake gatvā duḥkhāny evāśnuyu vabha ।।
yadā te daivayogānte tīvrātivedanāhatāḥ । triratnasaṃsmṛtiṃ kṛtvā praṇameyuḥ samānatāḥ ।। tadā tān sugatān dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā saṃpracoditāḥ । dṛkprabhābhiḥ samuddhṛtya preṣayeyuḥ surālaye ।।
tatra te sukhasaṃpannāḥ smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ mudā । sarvadā śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracareyuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tathaitatpuṇyapākena saṃbuddhaśāsane gatāḥ । śraddhayā satkṛtiṃ kṛtvā śṛṇuyur dharmam ādarāt ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtāsvādaṃ labdhvā te parimoditāḥ । bodhicittaṃ samāsādya prakuryu dānam ādarāt ।। tatas tatpuṇyapākena suśīlāḥ saṃvarodyatāḥ । sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā sādhayeyuḥ śubhāṃ cariṃ ।।
tato vīryabalenaiva jitvā kleśagaṇān ripūn । tatas te vimalātmāno dhyātvā yogasamāhitāḥ ।। prajñābdhipāram āsādya jñānaratnam avāpnuyuḥ । tato māragaṇāṃ jitvā pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ ।।
samyakṣaṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre mātsaryaṃ mūlam enasāṃ । bodhicittāsinochitvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। tato vo maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bhaved bhave samaṃtataḥ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyatha ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sāṃghikā mudā । sarve api pratibuddhitvā prābhyanaṃdan prasāditāḥ ।। iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate ।
evaṃ tvaṃ nṛpa mātsaryyaṃ tyaktvā cara śubhe sadā ।। prajāś cāpi tvayā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhicaryāśayāḥ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpyāḥ śubhe sadā ।। evaṃ te sarvadā bhadraṃ bhaved bhave samaṃtataḥ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। pretībhūtāvadānaṃ duritahṛtamataiḥ śreṣṭhino lobhino ye śṛṇvaṃti śravayaṃti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayedaṃ manuṣyāḥ ।
mātsaryaṃ te vihāya trimaṇiśaraṇagāḥ sarvasatvānurāgā dānaṃ datvā prasannāḥ satataśubhacarā yānti buddhālayaṃ te ।। athāśoko maharājaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayec caivam ādarāt ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
tad yathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhan sudhīr yatiḥ । tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi tava dharmapravṛddhaye ।। tad yathaivaṃ puraikasmin samaye sa munīśvaraḥ । bhagavāṃ trijagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। sarvajñaḥ sākyasiṃho arhaṃ chrāvstyā bahir āśrame ।
jetodyāne vihāre asmin vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tadā tatra sabhāmadhye siṃhāsane sumaṃḍite । sarvasatvahitārthena dharmam ādeṣṭum āśrayat ।। tatra te bhikṣavaḥ sarve bhikṣuṇyo api samāgatāḥ ।
yatinaś cailakāś caivam upāsakā upāsikāḥ ।। vratino bodhisatvāś ca saṃbodhiguṇalālasāḥ । nirgranthās tīrthikāś cāpi tāpasāś ca maharṣayaḥ ।। brahmaśakrādayo devā lokapālā maharddhikāḥ ।
daityā yakṣāś ca gaṃdharvāḥ kinnarāś cāpi rākṣasāḥ ।। siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi nāgāś ca garuḍā api । sādhyā grahāḥ satārāś ca vasavaś cāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi nṛpā rājakumārakāḥ ।
vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaś ca mahājanāḥ ।। gṛhasthā vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca dhanino api ca । śilpinaḥ paurikāś cāpi jānapadāś ca nairgamāḥ ।। grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikāś cāpi saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ ।
sarve te samupāgatya vihāre samupāviśan ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te saṃprasāditāḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya purataḥ samupācaran ।। tatra sarve api te lokāḥ samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ ।
taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvaiva dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayan ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupāśritān । bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te tridaśādayaḥ ।
lokāḥ satyam iti jñātvā prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।। tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāḥ pauriko gṛhī । āsīn mahādhanaḥ śrīmāñ chṛdopamo mahājanaḥ ।। sa svakulasamārāmāṃ svakuladharmacāriṇīṃ ।
kāṃtāṃ bhāryyāṃ samānīya samyakvyūhe yathāvidhiḥ ।। tataḥ sa kāmasaṃraktaḥ sukāminyā tayā saha । yathechayā sukhaṃ bhuktvā reme nityaṃ pracoditaḥ ।। tatas tasya gṛhasthasya yathākāmaṃ prabhuṃjataḥ ।
samaye sā satī bhārya garbhitābhūt kṛśāṃgikā ।। tataḥ sā samaye asūta dārakaṃ durbhagākṛtiṃ । durvarṇaṃ duritākāraṃ virūpaṃ vikṛtāśrayaṃ ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ mātā bhinnāśayā viṣeditāḥ ।
kiṃ īdṛg ātmajenāpi dhig mām iti vyaciṃtayat ।। tataḥ sa janakaḥ śrutvā taṃ jātaṃ vikṛtāśrayaṃ । virūpaṃ durbhagākāram ity evaṃ samaciṃtayat ।। aho kiṃ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ janmāṃtare purā mayā ।
yenāyaṃ durbhagākāro virūpo jāyate sutaḥ ।। tad atra kiṃ mayopāyaṃ karttavyaṃ nāpi manyate । dhig māṃ yena sute jāte lajjayā me sukhaṃ hṛtaṃ ।। tathāpi kiṃ kariṣyāmi daivāt me jāyate hy ayaṃ ।
tad virūpo api putro ayaṃ pālanīyo mayātmajaḥ ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryyāpy evam abravīt । yad ābhyāṃ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatphalaṃ bhujyate khalu ।। yad abhāvi na tad bhogyaṃ bhāvi cen na tad anyathā ।
sarvatra bhāvino bhogyaṃ bhuṃjate sarvajaṃtavaḥ ।। tad atrāham imaṃ bālaṃ pālayeyaṃ prayatnataḥ । ity uktvā sā vibhinnāsyā nārī tasthau pralajjitā ।। taṃ virūpaṃ sutaṃ jātaṃ vīkṣya sa janako api ca ।
lajjāvidīrṇacitto abhūn nirutsāhaviṣāditaḥ ।। hā mayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ manyate na bhavāṃtare । yato ayaṃ dārako jāto virūpo durbhagākṛtiḥ ।। tathāpi kiṃ kariṣyāmi daivān no jāyate hy ayaṃ ।
daivabhogyaṃ prabhoktavyaṃ sarvair api hi jaṃtubhiḥ ।। avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhavanti sarvadehināṃ । tad ayaṃ svātmajo bālaḥ pālanīyotmayā mayā ।। iti dhyātvā pitā so athadṛṣṭvā tasya śiśor mukhaṃ ।
lajjayā pratibhinnāsyas tasthau daivānucintayan ।। tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ sa ca । pitāsya nāma vikhyāte kuruteti samabravīt ।। tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve saṃkṛtvā samataṃ tathā ।
tad gṛhasthaṃ samāmaṃtrya pura evam upādiśan ।। gṛhapate virūpo ayaṃ putro yat tava jāyate । tasmād bhavatun āmnāyaṃ prasiddho bālako bhuvi ।। tataḥ snehād virūpo asau mātrā yatnena pālitaḥ ।
krāmāt puṣṭo vivṛddhābhūd hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ ।। tadā yadā kumāratvaṃ prāptaḥ sa vikṛtāśrayaṃ । svarūpaṃ darppaṇe dṛṣṭvā virūpo lajjito abhavat ।। tato jehrīyamāno asau virūpaḥ parimohitaḥ ।
pāpaciṃtāparitātmā manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। hā mayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenāhaṃ duritākṛtiḥ । kiṃ mamānena kāyena mṛtyuṃ me atra varaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। kiṃ kariṣye virūpo ahaṃ kva yāsyāmi durākṛtiḥ ।
kiṃ mamānena jīvena kevalaṃ duḥkhabhoginā ।। tad atrāhaṃ gṛhaṃ tyaktvā vanodyāne samāśrayan । saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ dhyātvā mṛtyuṃ gaccheya muktaye ।। avaśyam eva sarveṣāṃ jaṃtūnaṃ maraṇaṃ bhave ।
tan mamedṛg virūpo asmin śarīre jīvite spṛhā ।। yady atrāhaṃ ciraṃ jīvī nindito duḥkham āpnuyāṃ । tad buddhaṃ sugataṃ dhyātvā tiṣṭheyaṃ prāṇamuktaye ।। tat saṃbuddhaṃ jinaṃ dhyātvā mṛto ahaṃ yadi sāṃprataṃ ।
tat puṇyaḥ paritātmā sugatiṃ gacheya sarvathā ।। ye buddhaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā gachanti mṛtyum ātmanā । durgatiṃ te na gachanti samyānty eva sukhāvatīṃ ।। tasmāt te sudhiyaḥ santaḥ tyaktvā yāyāt kulaṃ gṛhaṃ ।
saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ dhyātvā tiṣṭhanti nirjane vane ।। tathāhaṃ tat samālokya saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । samādhāya sadā smṛtvā vaseyaṃ vijane vane ।। ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā virūpaḥ sa prasannadhīḥ ।
sa saṃpadaṃ gṛhaṃ tyaktvā jīrṇodyānaṃ samāśrayat ।। tatrodyāne vivikte sa parṇakuṭṭiṃ samāśrayan । bhagavantam anusmṛtvā tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavāñ chāstā taṃ tathā sthitaṃ ।
viśuddhāśayam ālokya samuddhartuṃ samudyataḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān nātho bhikṣusaṃghasamanvitaḥ । tatrodyāne virūpaṃ taṃ paśyan bhāsvān upācarat ।। tatprabhāparispṛṣṭo asau virūpaḥ satsukhānvitaḥ ।
vismitas taṃ samāyātaṃ sasāṃghikam apaśyata ।। taṃ munīṃdraṃ samālokya virūpaḥ sa vimohitaḥ । jehrīyamāna utthāya parāyituṃ tato acarat ।। tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā virūpaṃ taṃ parāyitaṃ ।
sahasarddhyā diśo mārge nirudhyābhyatiṣṭhata ।। tathā nirudhyamānaḥ sa virūpas tena śāsinā । parāyituṃ prayatnena na śaśāka kathaṃ cana ।। sa parikhinnātmā virūpo lajjitāśayaḥ ।
parṇakuṭṭisamāsīnaṃs tasthau bhīto divāndhavat ।। tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā nilīnaṃ lajjayāsane । saṃnirodhasamāpattiṃ samādhiṃ vidadhe tadā ।। tataḥ sa bhagavañ chāstā tat samādheḥ samutthitaḥ । svayaṃ virūpam ātmānaṃ nirmāya vikṛtāśrayaṃ ।।
bhojanapūrṇam ādāya śarāvaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tataḥ । śanais tasya virūpasya parṇakuṭṭyantike acarat ।। tatra taṃ samupāyātaṃ virūpaṃ vikṛtāśrayaṃ । sa virūpaḥ samālokya harṣita evam abravīt ।।
svāgataṃ bho sahāye hi kutra gantum ihāgataḥ । tiṣṭhātrāvāṃ sadāvāse vatsyāvahe sukhānvitā ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa virūpadhṛk । tvāṃ draṣṭum ihāyāmi proktveti samupāśrayet ।।
tatra sthitaḥ kathāṃ kṛtvā bhagavān sa virūpadhṛk । dadau tasmai virūpāya surasāmṛtabhojanaṃ ।। tat pradattaṃ prabhuktvānnaṃ sa virūpaḥ sa moditaḥ । tatkṣaṇāt paripuṣṭāṅgo babhūva prīṇitendriyaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā dṛṣṭvā taṃ saṃpramoditaṃ । svarūpeṇa sthitas tatra vyarājat saṃprabhāsayan ।। taṃ saumyabhadrarūpāṅgaṃ śrīghanaṃ śubhiteṃdriyaṃ । sa virūpaḥ samālokya vismitaś caivam abravīt ।।
aho kathaṃ bhavaty evam abhirūpataro bhavān । kasya puṇyavipākān tad vaktum arhati me puraḥ ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । bodhayituṃ virūpaṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
mahāvidyāsti me sādho saṃbodhisādhanottamā । cittaprasādasaṃjātajananyākhyā mahebalaḥ ।। tasyā eva prabhāvena bhavāmy ahaṃ śubheṃdriyaḥ । samaṃtabhadrarūpāṅgaḥ sarvasatvamanoharaḥ ।।
ity ādiśya munīndraḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra śubhāsane । saddharmaṃ samupādestuṃ samāśrayat prabhāsayan ।। tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve saumyarūpāḥ śubheṃdriyāḥ । parivṛtya munīndraṃ taṃ puraskṛtyopatasthire ।।
tān sarvān samupāsīnān saumyarūpāñ chubhendriyān । dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ matvā babhūva vismayānvitaḥ ।। aho bhāgya mayā labdhaṃ mahatpuṇyam ihādhunā । yan mamārthe munīndro ayaṃ sasāṃghika upāgataḥ ।।
nūnam atra munīndro ayaṃ matkarmaparicoditaḥ । saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sasaṃghaḥ kṛpayāgataḥ ।। tad aham asya munīndrasya śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । satkṛtya saugataṃ dharmaṃ śrotum arhe samāhitaḥ ।।
ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā virūpaḥ sa pramoditaḥ । upetya sāṃjalir natvā taṃ munīndram upāśrayat ।। tadā tasya virūpasya buddhapuṇyānubhāvataḥ । lakṣmī prādurabhūt tatra divyabhogapradāyinī ।।
tadā so abhūd virūpo api divyābhirūpasundaraḥ । pariśuddhatrikāyo api sadguṇārtho śubhāṃśikaḥ ।। tataḥ so atiprasannātmā dṛṣṭvaitat mahad adbhutaṃ । mudā tasya muneḥ pādau vavande sa kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।।
tataḥ utthāya taṃ nāthaṃ bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । samālokya prasannātmā prārthayat sa samādarāt ।। bhagavan bhavatā śāstaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । prādurbhūtātra me lakṣmī bhavāmi yātisuṃdaraḥ ।।
tad etan mahad āścaryaṃ dṛṣṭvā me rocate manaḥ । bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitvā carituṃ saṃvaraṃ sadā ।। tad atra bhagavan nātha kṛpayā buddhaśāsane । anvāhṛtya śubhe dharme niyoktuṃ māṃ samarhati ।।
śraddhayāhaṃ jagannātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣye atra samāhitaḥ ।। iti tat saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tasya śuddhāśayam ālokya samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।।
yadi vāṃchāsti te vatsa carituṃ saugataṃ vrataṃ । pitur ājñāṃ samāsādya prāgacha dāsyate tadā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa pratiharṣitaḥ । mudā tasya muneḥ pādau praṇatvaiva tato acarat ।।
tatra sa svagṛhe gatvā pādau pituḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ । praṇatvā purataḥ sthitvā prāvadad evam ādarāt ।। tatodyāne virūpo aham iti lajjāviṣāditaḥ । parṇakuṭyāṃ samāsīno dhyatvā vasāmi yogavit ।।
tatra sa bhagavān buddhaḥ sasaṃghaḥ svayam āgataḥ । bodhayitvāmṛtaṃ bhogyaṃ dadāti samupāyavit ।। tad dattam amṛtaṃ bhuktvā bhavāmi suṃdarākṛtiḥ । lakṣmīś cāpi samudbhūtā mamaivaṃ jāyate śubhaṃ ।।
etat sarvaṃ munīndrasya kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । nānyathā hīti vijñāya prasīda sugate sadā ।। evam etat mahaccitraṃ dṛṣṭvā me saṃprasāditaṃ । mano adya śāsane bauddhe carituṃ rocate vrataṃ ।।
etatsaṃprārthanāṃ kartum ihāhaṃ prāgato mudā । tad atra kṛpayā tāta tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। etatpuṇyavibhāgena tvaṃ cāpi sugatīṃ vrajeḥ । tatra ca sarvadā saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāyāj jinālayaṃ ।।
iti matvā prasīdātra mā kuruṣva mano anyathā । śraddhayānugrahaṃ kṛtvā tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ savismayaḥ । pitā taṃ svātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā sucirād evam abravīt ।।
aho hi bhāgyavān putra puṇyavāñchābhi sāṃprataṃ । yato asau kṛpayopetya buddhat tvām abhirakṣati ।। tat te asti yadi vāñchati carituṃ saugataṃ vrataṃ । taṃ buddhaśaraṇaṃ gatvā vrataṃ cara samāhitaḥ ।।
iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sa virūpaḥ prasāditaḥ । pādau pitroḥ praṇatvaiva sahasā prācarad gṛhāt ।। tato jetāśrame gatvā sa virūpaḥ pramoditaḥ । pādau tasya muner natvā prārthayed evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña labdhānujñaḥ sāmāgatāḥ । tad bhavān kṛpayā mahyaṃ saṃvaraṃ dātum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavāṃs tasya mastake । savyahastena saṃspṛṣṭvā śāsane taṃ samagrahīt ।।
tatra sa vrājitaḥ sāstrā virūpo muṇḍito api saḥ । khikkhiripātrabhṛc cīvaraprāvṛto vabhau ।। tataḥ sa bhikṣur ātmajñaḥ saṃyamī vijiteṃdriyaḥ । matvā saṃsārasaṃskāragatīḥ kṣaṇavighātinīḥ ।।
bhitvāvidyāgaṇān bodhipakṣe dharmeṣu prodyataḥ ।। tataḥ sa dhāraṇīvidyāsamādhinirato yatiḥ । sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā sākṣād arhatvam āptavān ।। saṃsāralābhasatkāraniḥspṛho nirmalāśayaḥ ।
pariśuddhatrikāyaś ca nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ ।। sa devāsuralokānām api traidhātucāriṇāṃ । mānyaḥ pūjyo abhivandyo abhūd brahmacarī sa yogavit ।। tadā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ yatim uttamaṃ ।
vismitās taṃ muniṃ natvā paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavann arhatānena kiṃ karma prakṛtaṃ purā । yenāyaṃ duritākāro virūpo jāyate adhunā ।। yac cāyaṃ bhagavāc chāsta bhavatā saṃprasāditaḥ ।
lakṣmīvān abhirūpaś ca bhavati sadguṇārataḥ ।। yac cāyaṃ śāsane bauddhe śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । sahasā kleśasaṃghārīñ jitvārhattvaṃ samāptavān ।। tad asya sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ yad anena purākṛtaṃ ।
suvistaraṃ samākhyāya sarvān naḥ paribodhaya ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvāṃs tān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anena purākṛtaṃ ।
tat sarvaiḥ karma vakṣyāmi sarvalokaprabodhane ।। yathābhūt purā buddhaḥ puṣyābhidhas tathāgataḥ । sarvajño arhañ jagacchāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। sa bhagavāñ jagannāthaḥ kṛtvā bhadraṃ samaṃtataḥ ।
sarvatra saugataṃ dharmam upadeṣṭum upācarat ।। evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu sasāṃghikaḥ sa mārajit । pūrvottaradiśo bhāge rājadhānīm upāśrayat ।। tatra sa bhagavāñ chāstā sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇam āryadharmam upādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokaḥ prabodhitaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracerire śubhe sadā ।। tatra sa bhagavān puṣyo buddhadṛṣṭya samaṃtataḥ ।
loke paśyan hitaṃ kartuṃ dadarśa dvau jinātmajau ।। ekaḥ śākyamunir nāma maitreyaś cāparaḥ sudhīḥ । tasmin kāle ubhav etau bodhisatvau jinātmajau ।। maitreyasya subuddheḥ svasaṃtatiḥ paripākitā ।
tasya śāstuś ca vaineyāḥ satvā na paripācitāḥ ।। śākyamunes tu vaineyāḥ paripakvā na saṃtatiḥ । evaṃ sa sugataḥ puṣyo dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samaciṃtayat ।। aho śākyamuner na svasantatiḥ paripācitā ।
tatsvasantatipākārthaṃ careyāhaṃ tadantike ।। iti vicintya puṣyaḥ sa tathāgataḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । himavaṃtaṃ giriṃ gatvā pracakrāma prabhāsayan ।। tatra ratnaguhāyāṃ sa praviśya sa munīśvaraḥ ।
tejodhātusamāpanno dhyātvā tasthau śubhāsane ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śākyamuniḥ sa sanmatiḥ । phalamūlasamāhartuṃ tadantikam upācarat ।। tatra ratnaguhāyāṃ taṃ puṣyaṃ tathāgataṃ muniṃ ।
suparyaṅkasamāsīnaṃ dhyānalīnaṃ prabhāsitaṃ ।। dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ paribhūṣitaṃ । ratnāvalim ivojvālaṃ śatasūryyādhikaprabhaṃ ।। saumyaṃ divyātiriktābhaṃ samaṃtabhadrarūpiṇaṃ ।
suprasannamukhāmbhojaṃ dharmarājaṃ samaikṣata ।। tatra taṃ sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā śākyamuniḥ sa moditaḥ । sahasā sāṃjalir natvā pūjāṃgainārcayan mudā ।। tataḥ sa ekapādena sthitvā saptaniśāṃ mudā ।
sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā tuṣṭāva gāthayānayā ।। na divi bhuvi vā nāsmil loke na vaiśravaṇālaye । na marubhavane divye sthāne na dikṣu vidikṣu vā ।। caratu vasudhāṃ sphītāṃ kṛtsnāṃ saparvatakānanāṃ ।
puruṣavṛṣabhasya tulyānyo mahāśramaṇaḥ kutaḥ ।। etayo gāthayā stutvā taṃ puṣyaṃ sugataṃ muniṃ । sa śākyamunir utsāhāt saptarātriṃ mudā bhajan ।। tataḥ saptadinānte sa puṣyathāgato mudā ।
paristutas tam ālokya śākyamunim abhāṣata ।। sādhu sādhu mahāsatva tvam evaṃ yat samudyataḥ । anena balavīryeṇa saṃpannena dvijottama ।। navakalpāḥ parāvṛttāḥ saṃstutyādya tathāgataṃ ।
kramāt pāramitāḥ pūrya saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ ।। ity ādiśya munīndro asau puṣyo dharmādhipo jinaḥ । parivṛtto maheśākhyais tatra dhyānārato abhasat ।। so api śākyamunir bodhisatvo dvijottamaḥ sudhīḥ ।
tasya puṣyasya sadbhaktya śaraṇasthaḥ sadābhajat ।। tatra tasmin sthite buddhe devī guhānivāsinī । tadguhāyāṃ praveṣṭum asau na śaśāka kathaṃ cana ।। tataḥ sātivirūpākṣā vikṛtāṃśā durākṛtiḥ । bhūtvā taṃ sugataṃ puṣyaṃ dhyānālīnam abhīṣapat ।।
tathā sā sucireṇāpi bhīṣapītvāpi durmatiḥ । kiñcit tasya muneś cittaṃ cārayituṃ śaśāka na ।। tadā sā śaṃkitākhinnā vismayāhatamānasā । svarūpeṇaiva taṃ draṣṭuṃ praṇatā samupācarat ।।
tatra taṃ sugataṃ puṣyaṃ tathāgatam munīśvaraṃ । dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṇḍitaṃ ।। sarvātikrāṃtasaumyābhaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ । śāntarūpaṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ dhyānālīnam apaśyata ।।
dṛṣṭvaiva sā prasādantī puṇyātmāyaṃ susiddhimān । iti dhyātvā surūpeṇa tadantikam upācarat ।। tatra sā sāṃjalir natvā pādau tasya muneḥ puraḥ । sthitvā kṣamārthanāṃ karttuṃ prārthayad evam ānatā ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña yan mayā prakṛtaṃ tvayi । tat kṣamasva jagannātha kṣāntidharmādhipo asi hi ।। tad atrāhaṃ jagacchāstar bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā । sarvadā samupāśritya bhajeyaṃ śraddhayā mudā ।।
yad atra te sasaṃghasya yathāvidhi samarcituṃ । ichāmy ahaṃ jagannātha tad adhyuṣitum arhati ।। iti tenārthite puṣyo bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tāṃ viśuddhāśayāṃ dṛṣṭvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।।
tathādhivāsitaṃ śāstrā matvā sābhyanumoditā । āśu tadbhojyasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat ।। tataḥ sā muditopetya pūjāṃgais taṃ munīśvaraṃ । abhyarcya bhojanair divyaiḥ sasaṃghaṃ samatoṣayat ।।
tataḥ sā bhojanānte api praṇatvā sāñjalir mudā । bhūtvā kṣamāpayitvā ca prārthayad evam ānatā ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitā । sadopasthānam ādhāya bhajiṣyāmi samāhitā ।।
tat kṣamasva jagannātha yan mayāpakṛtaṃ vṛthā । prasīdatu bhavāñ chāstā saṃbuddho hi kṣamākaraḥ ।। iti tayārthitaṃ śrutvā puṣyaḥ sa bhagavān muniḥ । devatāṃ tāṃ samālokya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
śṛṇuṣva devate dharmam ihāmutra śubhāptaye । dharmeṇa rakṣitā loke sarvatrāpi sukhī bhavet ।। tad ādau śraddhayā dharmaṃ śrotavyaṃ saugataṃ varaṃ । tatas triratnam abhyarcya dātavyaṃ dānam arthine ।।
tataḥ śuddhatrikāyaḥ syāc chuddhaśīlaḥ śubhāśayaḥ । tataḥ satyasamādhānaḥ sarvasatvakṣamākaraḥ ।। saṃbodhisādhanodyogāt sarvakleśān vinirjayet । tato dhyānasamādhisthaḥ prajñāratnam avāpnuyāt ।।
tat suratnānubhāvena sarvamārān vinirjayan । sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāñchibhiḥ । dharmaṃ śrutvā sadā dānaṃ prakarttavyaṃ yathepsitaṃ ।।
tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ sadā saukhyaṃ yadīchasi śubhānvitaṃ । triratnaṃ bhajanaṃ kṛtvā kuru dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ ।। etat puṇyaṃ tu saṃbodhiprāptaye pariṇāmaya । etatpuṇyavipākena nūnaṃ bodhiṃ samāpnuyāḥ ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā devatā mudā । tathā hītipratijñāya prābhyanandat prabodhitā ।। tataḥ sa sugataḥ puṣyas tathāgataḥ sasāṃghikaḥ । prabhāsayan samutthāya svāśrame samupāśrayat ।।
eṣa hy ayaṃ virūpo asau devatā yā guhāśritā । yuṣmābhiḥ satyam eveti manyatāṃ nānyathā khalu ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā sukhavāñchibhiḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।।
śubhasya karmaṇaḥ pāke śubhataivaṃ sadā bhave । kṛṣṇasya duḥkhataivaṃ hi miśritasyāpi miśritaṃ ।। abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana । yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ ।।
nāgnibhir dahyate karma klidyate nāpi codakaiḥ । śuṣyate vāyubhir naiva kṣīyate ca na bhūmiṣu ।। nānyathāpi bhave naiva karma kvāpi kathaṃ cana । yad yathā prakṛtaṃ karmaṃ tat tathaiva kuled dhruvaṃ ।।
yad asau devatā tatra guhāśritā durāśayā । vikṛtāṅgā virūpākṣā bhūtvā puṣyaṃ vyabhīṣapat ।। etatpāpavipākena paṃcajanmaśatāny api । vikṛtāṅgo virūpākṣo babhūvāyaṃ bhave sadā ।।
etatpāpāvimukto ayaṃ virūpo vikṛtākṛtiḥ । vibhransyo durbhagākāro bhavaty atrāpi sāṃprataṃ ।। yac cāsau devatā paścāttāpasaṃtapitāśayā । tasya puṣyasya buddhasya prasannā śaraṇaṃ gatā ।।
śraddhayā bhojanair divyaiḥ satkṛtya prābhajan mudā । etatpuṇyavipākena lebhe anantaṃ sukhaṃ bhave ।। atrāpi śāsane bauddhe śraddhayā samupāgataḥ । pravrajyāsaṃvaraprāptaḥ sākṣād arhatvam āptavān ।।
iti yūyaṃ parijñāya caradhvaṃ sarvadā śubhe । tato bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve te sāṃghikā api । śrutvānumoditāḥ satyam ity uktvā parimenire ।।
iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ mayātra kathyate । tvayāpy evaṃ mahārāja caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। prajāś cāpi tathā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālanīyaḥ sadādarāt ।।
tena te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ ।। śāstrādiṣṭaṃ prasannā idam api manuja ye virūpāvadānaṃ śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanaso ye ca puṇyābhirāgāḥ ।
sarve te śrīsametāḥ sakalaguṇadharāḥ satsukhāni prabhuktvā saṃbuddhabhaktiraktāḥ sugatavaragṛhe saṃprayānti pramodaṃ ।। athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ puraḥ sthitaḥ । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ ।
tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ samarhasi ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhan sudhīr yatiḥ । aśokaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ tat pravakṣyāmi tava dharmavivṛddhaye ।। tadyathābhūt purā pūryyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ kauśalādhipaḥ । prasenajid iti khyāto mahārājā mahīpatiḥ ।। vārāṇasyāṃ tadācāro brahmadattābhidho nṛpaḥ ।
mahārājo mahīpālanṛpādhipas tadābhavat ।। tadā tayor mahībhoktroḥ parasparaviruddhayoḥ । mahāhavasamāraṃbhād babhūva kṣubhitāśayaṃ ।। tatra sa kṣatriyo rājā prasenajin narādhipaḥ ।
svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā sarvāntaḥpurikānvitaḥ ।। caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ mahotsāhaṃ praṇādayan । vaijayantīṃ samucchrāya kośalāviṣayāntataḥ ।। paryante sahasā gatvā vīryotsāhasamanvitaḥ ।
vadhvā kāṣṭapaṭaṃ tatra prāvatasthe pure yathā ।। tac chrutvā brahmadatto api kṣatriyo bhūpatir nṛpaḥ । svastyayanavidhiṃ dhṛtvā svāntaḥpurasamanvitaḥ ।। caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ jayotsāhaṃ ninādayan ।
vaijayantīṃ samucchrāya nadyā tīram upācarat ।। tatraiva samupāśritya vīryotsāhasamanvitaḥ । vadhvā kāṣṭapaṭaṃ tatra saṃtasthe nagare yathā ।। tatra sa bhūpatī rājā brahmadatto narādhipaḥ ।
agrarājñyā sahāraktaḥ saṃreme paricārayan ।। tadā sa mahiṣī rājñā saha krīḍāratā satī । svalpāhāraratā gaurā dohadalakṣaṇaṃ dadhau ।। tathā tasmin kṣaṇe so api prasenajin narādhipaḥ ।
mahiṣyā saha saṃraktaḥ prareme paricārayan ।। tadā sāpi mahārājñī svāmikrīḍānucāriṇī । svalpāhārotsahā gaurā dadhau dohadalakṣaṇaṃ ।। kramāt to api mahārājñyāṃ pravṛddhagarbhahārite ।
pīnastane haridrābhavarṇe abhūtāṃ kṛśāṅgike ।। tato agramahiṣī rājño brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । sā sūta samaye putraṃ divyāṃśam atisuṃdaraṃ ।। tac chrutvā sa bhūpālo brahmadattaḥ pramoditaḥ ।
sahasopetya taṃ putraṃ dṛṣṭvā na tṛptim āyayau ।। tasminn eva dine tasya prasenajin mahīpateḥ । bhāryāpi samaye sūta sutāṃ divyātisuṃdarīṃ ।। strīratnalakṣaṇopetaṃ subhadrāṃgīmanoharāṃ ।
ramopamaṃ śubhākārāṃ manāpāṃ ratisaṃnibhāṃ ।। tac chrutvā sa mahīpālaḥ prasenajit prasāditaḥ । sahasopetya tāṃ putrīṃ dadarsātipramoditaḥ ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa nareṃdro api me vabhūva samāgataḥ ।
tām eva suciraṃ paśyann avatasthe suniścalaḥ ।। tayor apy ubhayo rājñoḥ skaṃdhācārāḥ pravarttitāḥ । ye nityaṃ tatpravṛttāṃtaṃ svaprabhor upahārakāḥ ।। ye prasenajitaś cārā brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ ।
putro jāta iti śrutvā parijñāya prasedire ।। te prasenajito rājñaḥ sahasā samupāgatāḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā pura evaṃ nyavedayan ।। jaya deva mahārāja śṛṇu tatra pravarttitaṃ ।
brahmadattasya bhūpasya putro jāto adhunā khalu ।। sāṃprataṃ tatra rājendraśubhotsāhaṃ pravarttate । tat tvayā saha saṃvaṃdhaṃ kṛtvā sa svapuraṃ vrajet ।। tat prasīda mahārāja mā vibhaiṣīḥ śubhaṃ bhavet ।
tena saṃdhiṃ bhavān kṛtvā viharatāṃ yathāsukhaṃ ।। iti taiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā sa prasenajin narādhipaḥ । satyam etad iti jñātvā prasasāda aviśaṃkitaḥ ।। tathā ye brahmadattasya gūḍhacārāḥ pravarttitāḥ ।
te prasenajitaḥ putrī jāteti śuśruvus tadā ।। tatas te sahasā tatra brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । purataḥ samupāśritya praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan ।। jaya deva mahārāja śṛṇu tatra pravarttitaṃ ।
prasenajinmahīpasya putrī jātā adhunā khalu ।। dārikā sā subhadrāṃgī divyakāmā ramopamā । sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā suṃdarī ratisaṃnibhā ।। tena tatra śubhotsāhaṃ pravarttate adhunā prabho ।
tena sahātra saṃvaṃdhaṃ karttum arhati sarvathā ।। iti taiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā brahmadatto narādhipaḥ । bhadram iti parijñāya tatraivaṃ samaciṃtayat ।। aho citra mahotsāho bhadram ekasmin divase yataḥ ।
jāto me atra suto bhadras tasyāpi jāyate sutā ।। tat tāṃ bhadrāṃ ramākārāṃ taṃ prasenajitam ādarat । prārthayitvātra putrāya sandhiṃ kṛtvā carevahi ।। iti niścitya sa brahmadatto rājā prasāditaḥ । sujanaṃ dūtam āmaṃtrya pura evaṃ samabravīt ।।
gacha dūta mahīpālaṃ taṃ prasenajitam ādarāt । mamaivaṃ vacasopetya prārthayasva prabodhayan ।। brahmadatto mahīpālo vadaty evaṃ samādarāt । bhavatā saha saṃvaṃdhaṃ karttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ ।।
yad ekasmin dine jātau dārakāv āvayor api । sutā te bhadrikā khyātā mama putro api bhadrikaḥ ।। tad etayor hi saṃvaṃdhaṃ karttum arhāvahe dhruvaṃ । tad bhavān mama putrāya svātmajāṃ dātum arhati ।।
evaṃ kṛte api saṃvaṃdhe yāvajjīvaṃ sadāvayoḥ । vairotsargo bhaven nūnaṃ prītisaṃdhir na bhetsyati ।। tadāvayoḥ sadā bhadraṃ viṣayeṣu samaṃtataḥ । nirītikaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।।
iti me vacasā rājā prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ । prārthanīyas tvayā sādho gachāstu te sumaṃgalaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ narendreṇa śrutvā dūtaḥ sa bodhitaḥ । tathety uktvā nṛpaṃ natvā samutthāya tato acarat ।।
tatra sa sahasā gatvā taṃ prasenajitaṃ nṛpaṃ । upetya sāṃjalir natvā purastha evam abravīt ।। jaya deva mahārāja yadarthe aham ihāgataḥ । tadarthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi bhavāṃ śrotuṃ samarhati ।।
brahmadatto mahārājo bhavatāṃ kuśalaṃ mudā । pṛchati sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api ।। punar evaṃ sa bhūpālo brahmadatto bravīty api । bhavatā saha saṃvaṃdhaṃ kartum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ ।।
yad ekasmin dine jātau dārakāv āvayor iha । sutā te bhadrikā khyāto mama putro api bhadrikaḥ ।। tad etayor hi saṃvaṃdhaṃ kartum arhāmahe dhruvaṃ । tad bhavān mama putrāya svātmajāṃ dātum arhati ।।
evaṃ kṛte api saṃvaṃdhe yāvajjīvaṃ sadāvayoḥ । vairotsargo bhaven nūnaṃ prītisaṃdhir na bhetsyate ।। tadāvayoḥ sadā bhadraṃ viṣayeṣu samaṃtataḥ । nirītikaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ bhaved eva na saṃśayaḥ ।।
iti me vacasā rājā prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ । prārthanīyas tvayā sādho gachāstu tvaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। ity ādiśya narendreṇa brahmadattena bhūrbhujā । preṣito ahaṃ mahārāja bhavatām aṃtike khalu ।।
tat tena bhūpatīśena yathādiṣṭaṃ narādhipa । bhavān api tathā kartum arhaty edan na nānyathā ।। evaṃ hi bhavatāṃ bhadraṃ yāvājjīvaṃ sukhaiḥ sadā । sarvatra maṅgalotsāhaṃ bhaven nūnaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
tad bhavān api rājendra brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । putrāya svātmajāṃ bhadrāṃ saṃpradātum ihārhati ।। iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa kośalādhipaḥ । tuṣṇībhūtvā kṣaṇaṃ tatra manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayet ।।
aho me jāyate kṣemaṃ yad asau kṣatriyādhipaḥ । vairaṃ vihāya saṃvandhaṃ karttum ichati sāṃprataṃ ।। tad ahaṃ tena bhūpena yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā adhunā । datvaināṃ svātmajāṃ bhadrāṃ saṃdhiṃ kuryāṃ śubhāptaye ।।
evaṃ kṛte sadā kṣemaṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api । mama tasyāpi bhūpasya bhaven nūnaṃ na cānyathā ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ । taṃ dūtaṃ samupāmaṃtrya samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
sādho tena narendreṇa yathādiṣṭaṃ tathādarāt । ājñāṃ śirasā dhṛtivā kariṣyāmi sadāpy ahaṃ ।। evaṃ me vacasā sādho sarvam etat suvistaraṃ । samākhyāya narendraṃ taṃ prasādayitum arhasi ।।
iti tena narendreṇa samākhyātaṃ niśamya saḥ । dūtas tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandat prasāditaḥ ।। tataḥ sa dūtas taṃ bhūpaṃ kośalādhipatiṃ mudā । natvā dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtrya tato acarat pramoditaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa sahasā gatvā brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । upetya sāṃjaliḥ pādau praṇatvevam abhāṣata ।। jaya deva mahārāja diṣṭyā varddhasva sāṃprataṃ । yathābhilaṣitaṃ sarvaṃ tat siddham iti manyatāṃ ।।
tad yathā bhavatādiṣṭaṃ tathā vijñāpitaṃ mayā । tac chrutvānena bhūpena pramoditvādhyuvāsitaṃ ।। iti satyaṃ samādhāya pālayasva yathoditaṃ । sarvadā te bhaved bhadraṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā brahmadattaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । prabodhito anumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhūpatī rājā brahmadatto mahotsavaiḥ । caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ jayavādyaṃ pravādayan ।।
tataḥ saṃprasthito lokaiḥ stūyamānaḥ surair api । pracaran sahasā tatra svapuraṃ samupāyayau ।। tataḥ so api mahīpālaḥ prasenajit pramoditaḥ । caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ jayotsāhaṃ praṇādayan ।।
tataḥ pratyāgato lokai stūyamāno amarair api । pracaran sa nṛpo tatra śrāvastyāṃ samupācarat ।। tatra svanagare prāptaḥ prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ । svaprāsādatalāsīnaḥ sarvāntapurikānvitaḥ ।।
tāṃ bhadarikāṃ sutāṃ dṛṣṭvā suprasannāśayo mudā । aho kṣemaṃ prajātaṃ me ity evaṃ muhur abravīt ।। tatas tasyāḥ sutāyāḥ sa kṛtvā jātimahaṃ mudā । sarvañ jñātīn samāhūya pura evam upādiśat ।।
bhadantaḥ śrūyatām asyā bhadrāyā duhitur mama । yathāyuktaṃ nāmadheyaṃ sthāpayata prasiddhitaṃ ।। iti tena narendreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate । saṃpaśyañ jñātayas tatra saṃmīlyaivaṃ samabruvan ।।
yasmin dine prajāteyaṃ tasminn eva dine yataḥ । kṣemaṃ no jāyate tasmāt kṣemābhidhā bhavantv iyaṃ ।। iti te jñātayaḥ sarve kṛtvaivaṃ saṃmataṃ tataḥ । kauśalendraṃ tam āmaṃtrya praṇatvaivaṃ samabruvan ।।
śṛṇu rājan yad asmākam abhiprāyaṃ pracakṣyate । tad asyā nāmadheyaṃ karotu bhuvi viśrutaṃ ।। yasmin dine prajāteyaṃ kṣemaṃ bhavati sarvataḥ । tenāsyā kriyatāṃ nāma kṣemeti viśrutaṃ bhuvi ।।
tathā tair gaditaṃ śrutvā rājā sa janako mudā । tasyāḥ putryās tathā nāma kṣemeti prārthitaṃ vyadhāt ।। tataḥ sā dārikāṣṭābhir dhātribhiḥ pratipālitā । paripuṣṭā pravṛddhābhūd dhradastham iva paṃkajaṃ ।।
tathā sa brahmadatto api rājā svāntargṛhe gataḥ । taṃ putrāṃ muhur ālokya prābhyanaṃdat pramoditaḥ ।। tatra tasya śiśo rājā kṛtvā jātimahaṃ pitā । sarvāñ jñātīn samāhūya pura evam abhāṣata ।।
bhavaṃto dārakasyāsya putrasya me śubhākṛteḥ । kriyatāṃ nāmadheyan sanmaṃgalākṣarasaṃyutaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ narendreṇa śrutvā te jñātayo mudā । sarve apy ekatra saṃgamya mithar evaṃ samabruvan ।।
yad ayaṃ jātamātro api kṣemaṃ karoti sarvataḥ । tathāsya bhavatu kṣemaṃkara ity āhvayaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। iti te jñātayaḥ sarve brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । purataḥ samupāsṛtya praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan ।।
śṛṇu rājan yad asmābhir nāmāsya kriyate śiśoḥ । tan nāma kṣemasaṃpannaṃ prathayatu bhāvān bhuvi ।। yad ayaṃ jātamātro api kṣemaṃ karoti sarvataḥ । tena kṣemaṃkarākhyo ayaṃ bhavaṃtu lokanaṃdanaḥ ।।
etat taiḥ kathitam śrutvā brahmadattaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tad eva nāme putrasya tasyākarot pravisṛtaṃ ।। tataḥ sa dārako aṣṭābhi dhātribhiḥ pratipālitaḥ । paripuṣṭaḥ pravṛddho abhūd dhradasthaṃ kamalaṃ yathā ।।
tataḥ kramāt kumāratvam āptavān sa nṛpātmajaḥ । gurūṇāṃ samupāśritya lipī kramād aśikṣat ।। yathākramam adhītyevaṃ kṣemaṃkaraḥ sa buddhimān । sarvaśāstrakalāsv ādi vidyāparaṃ yayau laghu ।।
tataḥ sa daharaḥ kāntaḥ kumāro ratilālitaḥ । savayeḥsacivaiḥ sārddhaṃ reme pure paribhraman ।। tadā sa dārikā kṣemā prasenajitsutāpi ca । kramād abhūt kumārītvaprāptā kāntābhisuṃdarī ।। tataḥ sā bhadrikā kanyā sumatir guṇalālasāḥ ।
gurūṇāṃ samupāśritya kramāl lipir aśikṣata ।। yathākramam adhītyaivaṃ sā subuddhimatī satī । sarvaśāstrakalāvidyāpāraṃ yayau vicakṣaṇā ।। tadā sā bhāvinī kṣemā svasakhībhiḥ samanvitā ।
saṃbuddhabhāṣitaṃ dharmam anuśrutvā mudānamat ।। tadā sa brahmadattasya kumāro ativicakṣaṇaḥ । tāṃ kṣemāṃ suṃdarīṃ draṣṭuṃ samaichad ratilālasaḥ ।। tataḥ sa dūtam āhūya bodhayitvā prasādayan ।
datvā suratnamālāṃ taṃ kṣemāyāḥ preṣayet svayaṃ ।। tataḥ sa dūta ādāya tāṃ mālāṃ sahasā caran । śrāvastyāḥ puri saṃprāptaḥ kṣemāyāḥ sadane acarat ।। tatra sa dūta ālokya sakhīm ekām upāgatāṃ ।
tām upetya samāmaṃtrya suguptam evam abravīt ।। kṣemaṃkarakumāreṇa kṣemāye prahitām imāṃ । ratnamālāṃ tvam ādāya bhadre tasyai samarpaya ।। ity uktvā ratnamālāṃ tāṃ kṣemāsakhīkare rahaḥ ।
datvā sa dūta āmaṃtrya sahasā svapuraṃ yayau ।। tatra sāpi sakhī tasyāḥ kṣemāyāḥ purato gatā । prābhṛtaṃ tam upasthāpya rahasy evaṃ nyavedayat ।। ayi bhadram imaṃ paśya prahitaṃ svāminā tava ।
tad idaṃ tvaṃ samāśliṣya patim iva vibhāvaya ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā kṣemā lajjitāśayā । kāmaviṣāgnisaṃtrastā tasthau dinam adhomukhā ।। tataḥ sā kanyakā kṣemā tāṃ sakhīṃ purataḥ sthitāṃ ।
sucirāt samupārabhya hartsayanty evam abravīt ।। are re kiṃ vadasy evaṃ svāmī me kātra vidyate । nilajje vada tat kena prahitaṃ prābhṛtaṃ tava ।। ity uktaṃ sā sakhī śrutvā kṣemāyā durituḥ prabhoḥ ।
ājanme sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ vistareṇa nyavedayat ।। evaṃ sakhyā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā nṛpanaṃdinī । kṣemā saṃsārasaṃcārasamudvignāśayābhavat ।। tata utthāya sā kṣemā kanyāpi sahasā pituḥ ।
upetya caraṇau natvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। tāta kāmārthinī nāham api tu sadguṇārthinī । sadguṇāṃ sādhayiṣyāmi tad anujñāṃ dadātu me ।। yad ahaṃ śāsane bauddhe pravrajitvā samāhita ।
brahmacaryaṃ samādhāya prechāmi carituṃ prabho ।। tad bhavāṃ kṛpayā tāta saṃbodhivratasādhane । anujñāṃ saṃpradatv me sarvathānugrahaṃ kuru ।। ity arthitaṃ tayā putryā śrutvā sa kośalādhipaḥ ।
tāṃ kumārīṃ samālokya tasthau saṃdigdhamānasaḥ ।। tataḥ sa janako rājā tāṃ kṣemāṃ svātmajāṃ priyāṃ । bodhayituṃ samāmaṃtrya samālokyaivam abravīt ।। naivaṃ putri mayā kartuṃ śakyate tat kṣamasva me ।
yat te janmani me rāṣṭre kṣemam evaṃ prajāyate ।। tadāpi tvaṃ pratijñaya brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । kṣemaṃkarāya putrāya saṃkalpitā mayātmaje ।। tad yathā me pratijñātaṃ vacanaṃ pūrayātmaje ।
mā kṛthāḥ sarvathā kṣeme pravrajyāsādhane mama ।। yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ kariṣye na tad anyathā । matveti me vacaḥ śrutvā kuladharme carātmaje ।। evaṃ pitroditaṃ śrutvā sā kṣemā prahatāśayā ।
utthāya svālaye gatvā tūṣṇībhūtā nyaṣīdata ।। tadā sa janako rājā dūtam āhūya sādaraṃ । sarvam etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ samākhyāyaivam abravīt ।। gacha sādho narendrasya brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ ।
pura etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivaṃ prabodhaya ।। yad iyaṃ me sutā kṣemā pravrajituṃ samichati । tad imāṃ sahasāgatvā bhavān ādātum arhati ।। iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā puraḥ sa sādaraṃ ।
tatheti saṃpratijñāya praṇatvā taṃ tato acarat ।। tatra sa sahasā gatvā brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । upetya sāṃjalir natvā pura evaṃ nyavedayat ।। jaya eva yadarthe ahaṃ preṣito atra mahībhṛtā ।
kośalendreṇa tad bhavāṃ śṛṇotv evaṃ bravīti saḥ ।। yad iyaṃ me sutā kṣemā pravrajituṃ samichati । tad imāṃ sahasāgatvā bhavān āhartum arhati ।। yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ karttuṃ na śakyate anyathā ।
tad ahaṃ te kumārāya dāsyāmi svātmajām imāṃ ।। evaṃ tena nareṃdreṇa samākhyāya bhavatpuraḥ । preṣito aham iti jñātvā tat tatrāgaṃtum arhati ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā brahmadattaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ ।
taṃ dūtaṃ sahasāmaṃtrya pura evam abhāṣata ।। evaṃ ced āgamiṣyāmi saputraḥ saptame ahaṃ । yat tat kṛtyaṃ hi tat sarvaṃ karttavyam iti kathyatāṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ nareṃdreṇa brahmadattena sāṃjaliḥ ।
natvā tatheti vijñapya samutthāya tato acarat ।। tatra sa sahasā gatvā svapuraṃ samupācaran । nṛpatiṃ sāṃjalir natvā pura evaṃ nyavedayat ।। jaya deva yathādiṣṭaṃ brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ ।
tathā vijñāpitaṃ sarvaṃ tad uktaṃ yācyate śṛṇu ।। evaṃ ced āgamiṣyāmi saputraḥ saptame ahani । tad yat kṛtyaṃ hi tat sarvaṃ sādhayituṃ tvam arhasi ।। iti tena narendreṇa pratijñāya nideśitaṃ ।
iti satyaṃ parijñāya sarvaṃ kṛtyaṃ prakāraya ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā prasenajit sa bhūpatiḥ । tadarhasarvasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat ।। tadaitat sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ śrutvā cā dārikā sudhīḥ ।
udvignamānasā kṣemā manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। hā kiṃ mayātra karttavyaṃ vivāhāṃ me bhave yataḥ । kāmabhogaṃ parityajya vāṃchāmi saugatavrataṃ ।। kāmā hi garhyate sadbhi varṇyate saugataṃ vrataṃ ।
tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yan me na gocaraṃ vrate ।। dhig janma tasya saṃsāre yasya na gocaraṃ vrate । vrataṃ vinātra kiṃ sāraṃ kāmabhogyai guṇair api ।। tad atra kva gamiṣyāmi nimagnā kāmapaṃkile ।
ko me trātā bhaved atra saṃbuddhād aparaḥ kṛtī ।। tad atra taṃ jagannāthaṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvatāyinaṃ । saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatvā prārthaye sādhunādarāt ।। nūnaṃ buddho jagannātho jagacchāstā munīśvaraḥ ।
kṛpayā māṃ samālokya buddhavrate niyojayet ।। yadi me daivayogena vrataṃ naiva labheya hi । saṃbuddhaśaraṇodbhūtaṃ puṇyaṃ tu labhyate dhruvaṃ ।। saṃbuddhasmṛtijaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana ।
saṃbuddhasaṃvaraṃ dadyād iti prajñair nigadyate ।। tad ahaṃ taṃ jagannāthaṃ smṛtvātra maraṇaṃ varaṃ । na tu kāmaviṣaṃ bhokṣye bhojye puṇyāmṛtaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। iti niścitya sā kṣemā snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtā ।
śaraṇapṛṣṭham āruhya abhavad dinmukhā sthitā ।। jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitā kṛtāṃjalipuṭā mudā । bhagavantam anusmṛtvā natvaivaṃ prārthayat tridhā ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña sarvasatvānukaṃpaka ।
brahmacārin mahābhijña maharṣe duritāntakaḥ ।। praśamopāyavid vijña śānta citta mahāmune । tvam eva hi jagannātha tat te ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। tan māṃ bhavodadhau magnāṃ kṛpayoddhartum arhati ।
iti saṃprārthite satyo kanyayā kṣemayā tayā । bhagavān kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā dadarśa tāṃ śubhāśayāṃ ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ kṣemāṃ bodhibhāvinīṃ । ṛddhyākaśāt samāgatya tatra kṣemāntike yayau ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā kṣemā sahasotthitā । prajñapya svāsanaṃ natvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। bhagavan nātha saṃbuddha praviśātrāsane śubhe । prasīda kṛpayapāyān māṃ samuddhartuṃ arhasi ।।
iti tasyārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tāṃ kṣemāṃ bhadrikāṃ kanyāṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। mā bhaiṣi bhadrike kanye tvadīhitaṃ samṛdhyati । tathā me śaraṇaṃ gatvā cara śubhe samāhitā ।।
ity ādiśya punas tasyāḥ saṃbodhipadasādhanaṃ । āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tad āryyadharmam ākarṇya kṣemā paribodhitā । anāgāmiphalaṃ prāptā labdhābhijñābhavat tadā ।।
tataḥ sā muditā kanyā dṛṣṭasatyā prasāditā । sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā prārthayac caivam ādarāt ।। bhagavan sarvavin nātha sadaivaṃ kṛpayā bhavān । dṛṣṭvā māṃ saugate dharme niyojya trātum arhati ।।
ity arthitaṃ tayā śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya tathārddhyā cāśrame yayau ।। tadā sā kanyakā kṣemā saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatā । saṃsmṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prācaran muditā śubhe ।।
tadā sa brahmadatto api putrapurohitādibhiḥ । svajanaiḥ sahasotsāhaiḥ śrāvastyāṃ samupācarat ।। tadāgatam samākarṇya prasenajit sa bhūpatiḥ । sahasā maṃgalotsāhaiḥ pratyudyayau tam ādarāt ।।
tatra sa kośaleśas taṃ brahmadattaṃ narādhipaṃ । upetya kuśalaṃ dṛṣṭvā svapure saṃnyaveśayat ।। tatrānekāḥ samāyātā lokāḥ sarve pramoditāḥ । tadvivāhamahotsāhaṃ draṣṭuṃ samupatasthire ।।
tataḥ sa kauśalo rājā tadvivāhadine śubhe । sādhitasarvasāmagrīṃ hotuḥ samatyaḍhaukayat ।। tadā kṣemā kumārī sā sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitā । mātrā saha samāgatya tatrāsane samāśrayat ।।
kṣemaṃkarakumāro api sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ । pitrā saha samāgatya tatrāsane upāviśat ।। tataḥ sa vidhivid dhotā śuddhāsane samāśrayan । vidhināgniṃ samāvāhya sa havyaiḥ samatarpayat ।।
tataḥ purohito vipras tadvelā samupāgate । kṣemaṃkarāya tāṃ kṣemāṃ saṃkalpayitum ārabhat ।। yathāvidhi samārabhya brāhmaṇaḥ sa purohitaḥ । kṣemāyā hastam ādāya kumārasyāsya prāgrahīt ।।
tasminn eva kṣaṇe tatra sā kṣemā sahasodgatā । pakṣivat khaṃ samāśritya tasthau dhyātvā munīśvaraṃ ।। tātra sā bhāsayanty eva sthitā ciraṃ samāhitā । prātihāryāṇi citrāṇi vividhāny abhyadarśayat ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā kauśalo rājā prasenajit pitāpi saḥ । brahmadatto narendro api purohito dvijo api saḥ ।। kṣemaṃkaraḥ kumāro api sarve api brāhmaṇāś ca te । amātyā maṃtriṇaś cāpi sarve sainyagaṇā api ।।
paurāś cāpi striyo anye api dārakā dārikā api । sarve ativismayākrāṃtahṛdayā avatasthire ।। tatra kṣemaṃkaro rājakumāro brāhmaṇaiḥ saha । tāṃ kṣemāṃ sāṃjalir natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
namas te bhagini kṣeme yat te ahaṃ kāmalālasāḥ । pāṇiṃ grahītum ichāmi tat kṣamasva dayānidhe ।। yad evaṃ tvaṃ mahābhijñāpadaprāptā maharddhikā । yat kāmān paribhuṃjīthā ity asthānam eva hi ।।
tat kṣamasva tvam ākāśād avatīrya mahītale । sarvalokābhibodhārthaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśa ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena kumāreṇa niśamya sā । kṣemā prasannāsyā tatrākāśād avātarat ।।
