tatra sā samupāgatya janakāye sabhāsane । sthitvāryasatyam ārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ । satyam iti parijñāya prābhyanandan prasāditāḥ ।।
tataḥ kṣemaṃkaraḥ pitrā saha taṃ kośalādhipaṃ । āmaṃtrya tadguṇāhṛṣṭamanāḥ svaṃ nagaraṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sā kanyakā kṣemā sāñjaliḥ purato gatā । pituḥ pādāmbuje natvā prārthayed evam ādarāt ।।
nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta saṃbuddhaśaraṇārthinī । tad itaḥ śāsane bauddhe gantum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। tad yadi te mayi prītir asti dhārme api vā ruciḥ । tad atra kṛpayānujñāṃ dātum arhati me pita ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ putryā śrutvā sa kauśalādhipaḥ । tāṃ kṣemāṃ svātmajāṃ kanyāṃ ciraṃ dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt ।। kimetra vakṣyate putri yat tvaṃ saddharmavāṃchinī । kiṃ cāpy asi mahābhijñāvatī prajñāvatī sudhīḥ ।।
kiṃ tu tvaṃ dārikā kanyā śītavātātapāhatā । tat pravrajyāvrataṃ vālye carituṃ śaknuyāḥ kathaṃ ।। saddharma yadi te vāṃchā gṛhe sthitvā samāhitā । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā saddharmaṃ sādhayātmaje ।।
triratnabhajanodbhūtaṃ puṇyaṃ saddharmasādhanaṃ । tena saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। evaṃ matvā svagehe tvaṃ śuddhaśīlavratāvṛtā । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara nityaṃ śubhe sadā ।।
iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā śā kṣemā kāmaniḥspṛhā । pitaraṃ taṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।। na me tāta gṛhāvāse kleśamāragaṇākule । kṣaṇaṃ sthātuṃ manas tena vāṃchati saugataṃ vrataṃ ।।
sarve api saugataḥ santo vihāre sugatāśrame । sadā dharmāmṛtaṃ bhuktvā vasanti sadguṇodyatāḥ ।। ta eva sadguṇādhārā bodhisatvāḥ sukhānvitāḥ । yāvajjīvaṃ vrataṃ dhṛtvā yānti cānte jinālayaṃ ।।
iti dṛṣṭvāham ichāmi pravrajituṃ jināśrame । tad bhavān kṛpayānujñāṃ dātum arhati me prabho ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ putryā śrutvā sa bodhitaḥ pitā । tathānumodanāṃ kṛtvā tāṃ kṣemām evam abravīt ।।
kiṃ mayā vakṣyate vatse tvam evaṃ satsubhārthinī । tad vraja śāsane bauddhe vrataṃ cara samāhitā ।। iti pitrābhyanujñātaṃ śrutvā sā muditāśayā । kṣemā tasya pituḥ pādau natvaiva niryayau tataḥ ।।
tataḥ sā muditā kṣemā sahasā tatra jināśrame । gatā taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā muditā samupācarat ।। tatra sā sāñjalir natvā sāstāraṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ । purataḥ samupāsīnā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tat pravrajyāvrataṃ datvā sadā me anugrahaṃ kuru ।। ity arthitaṃ tayā śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tac chiro dakṣahastena pṛṣṭvā tām evam abravīt ।।
ehi vatse pragacha tvaṃ gautamyāḥ śaraṇaṃ vraja । sā mātā bhikṣuṇīśāstā pravrajyāṃ te pradāsyati ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā muditāśayā । kṣemā tasyā jaganmātur gautamyāḥ samupācarat ।।
tatra sā samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā tāṃ gautamīṃ mudā । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। jaganmātar ahaṃ kṣemā bhavatyāḥ śaraṇaṃ vraje । tan pravrajyāvrataṃ mahyaṃ bhavantī dātum arhati ।।
ity arthitaṃ tayā śrutvā gautāmī sā prasāditā । tac chiro dakṣahastena pṛṣṭvaivaṃ tām abhāṣata ।। ehi bhikṣuṇi vatse śāsane saugate śubhe । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā brahmacaryaṃ samācara ।।
ehīti samādiṣṭe gautamyāsya śubhāśayā । kṣemābhūn muṇḍitā pātradharā sucīvarāvṛtā ।। tataḥ sā bhikṣuṇī kṣemā saumyarūpā jitendriyā । bhitvā avidyāgaṇān duṣṭān prāptavidyāgaṇāñ chubhān ।।
samādhidhāraṇīvidyā ghaṭamānā samudyatā । mahābhijñāpadaprāptā saṃbodhipadasādhinī ।। tataḥ sā sumatīr matvā bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ । matvā ca sarvasaṃskāragatiś cāpi vighātinīḥ ।।
sarvakleśagaṇān hitvā jitvā māragaṇān api । sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya babhūva brahmacāriṇī ।। tataḥ sākāśasādṛśyā nirvikalpā niraṃjanā । vāsicaṃdanakalpāṃśā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalā ।।
saṃsāralābhasatkāraniḥspṛhā sarvadehināṃ । sa devāsuralokānāṃ vaṃdyā pūjyābhavat satī ।। tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā sarvajño arhan munīśvaraḥ । sarvāns tāṃ śrāvakāṃ bhikṣūn samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। eṣāgrā bhikṣavaḥ sarvabhikṣūṇīnāṃ mamāśrame ।
abhijñāpratibhāṇasatprajñānāṃ yad iyaṃ sudhīḥ ।। kṣemākhyā bhikṣuṇī satyavādinī brahmacāriṇī । saty advayaparijñātā saṃbodhipadagāminī ।। ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sarve te sāṃghikā api ।
vismitās taṃ muniṃ natvā paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavann anayā karma kiṃ purā sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ । yeneyaṃ bhadrikā kṣemā prajñāvatī maharddhikā ।। mahāprajñāvatīnāṃ ca sarvāsām api saddhiyāṃ ।
maharddhipratibhāṇānām agrā nirdiśyate tvayā ।। tad ime sāṃghikāḥ sarve śrotum ichaṃti sāṃprataṃ । tat sarvaṃ samupādiśya sarvāl lokān prabodhaya ।। iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ ।
sarvāns tān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve purā yad anayā kṛtaṃ । tad ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvalokābhibodhane ।। purābhūt kāśyapo nāma tathāgato munīśvaraḥ ।
sarvajño arhañ jagacchāstā sugato dharmādhipo jinaḥ ।। vārāṇasyām upāraṇye mṛgadāve jināśrame । saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tac chāsane tadā śreṣṭhiduhitā śaraṇaṃ gatā ।
pravrajyāvratam ādāya pracacāra samāhitā ।। sā tatra śāsane bauddhe dadau dānaṃ samādarāt । dvādaśābda sahasrāṇi brahmacaryaṃ cacāra ca ।। na kesmiṃ viguṇe abhyāsaṃ cakāra sā nirudyamā ।
kevalaṃ saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā triratnaṃ sarvadābhajat ।। tasyāyābhūd upādhyāyā bhikṣuṇī brahmacāriṇī । sā kāśyapena nirdiṣṭā prajñāvatīgaṇāgragā ।। tat samākarṇya sā sādhvī bhikṣuṇī cānumoditā ।
manasaivaṃ samādhāya praṇidhānaṃ vyadhān mudā ।। yathāyam uttaro vipro vyākṛtas tena tāyinā । kalau śākyamunir nāma tathāgato bhaved iṭi ।। tadā tasya munīndrasya śāsane śaraṇaṃ gatā ।
pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā careyaṃ brahmacārikāṃ ।। aham api tayā tatra prajñāvatīgaṇādhipā । bhaveya hi yathāpīyam upādhyāyā mamādhunā ।। sadaitatpraṇidhānena caraṃti sā śubhāśayā ।
triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā samaye maraṇaṃ yayau ।। yāsau śreṣṭhisutā hy eṣā kṣemā rājasutādhunā । yānmeti bhikṣavo yūyaṃ manyadhvaṃ vratam eva hi ।। yat tadā prakṛtaṃ dānaṃ kāśyapaśāsane anayā ।
etaddharmavipākena bhavatīyaṃ nṛpātmajā ।। yac cāpi hy anayā tatra brahmacaryaṃ supālitaṃ । etatpuṇyair ihārhantī bhavatīyaṃ kilā adhunā ।। yadyāpi hy anayā tatra praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ yathā ।
tatheyaṃ bhavati hy atra prajñāvatīgaṇādhipā ।। evaṃ hi yat kṛtaṃ yena tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ । abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana ।। nāgnibhir dahyate karma klidyate nodakair api ।
vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate naiva kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu ।। na praṇaśyaṃti karmāṇi janmakalpaśatair api । sāmāgrīṃ prāpya kāle hi phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu ।। anyathāpi bhaven naiva kṛtakarmaphalaṃ kvacit ।
kṛṣṇakarmavipāke hi duḥkhataiva sadā bhave ।। śubhakarmavipāke tu sukhataiva sadā bhavet । miśritakarmapākena miśritatā sadaiva hi ।। yathaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tathaiva tat phalaṃ dhruvaṃ ।
evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāṃchibhiḥ ।। triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ । tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।।
etan me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ mahārāja cara nityaṃ śubhe sadā ।। prajāś cāpi tathā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।।
tena te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet । kramād bodhiṃ ca saṃprāpya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā aśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
kṣemāvadānaṃ manujā idaṃ ye śṛṇvaṃti cāpi niśāmayanti । te sarva evaṃ satataṃ sukhāni bhuktvā prayānty eva jinālayan te ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ pramoditaḥ । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।।
bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuñ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan mahāmatiḥ । tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ । tathātrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi tava dharmapravṛddhaye ।। tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugato śāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।।
śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ । upāsikāgaṇaiś cāpi cailakaiś cāpi tīrthikaṃ ।। bodhisatvair mahāsatvaiḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkaraṃ । ṛṣibhir yogibhiś cāpi yatibhir brahmacāribhiḥ ।।
śrāvastyā bahir udyāne jetāraṇye jināśrame । vihāre vyaharal lokahitārthaṃ dharmam ādiśan ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve satvāḥ pramoditāḥ । śakrabrahmādayo devāḥ sarvalokādhipā api ।।
nagendrā asurendrāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । siddhā vidyādharāḥ sādhyā garuḍā rākṣasā api ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā bhūpā rājaputrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ । amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ paura gṛhādhipā mahājanāḥ ।।
vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpino api śubhārthinaḥ । grāmyā jānapadāś cānyalokāḥ kārpaṭikādayaḥ ।। sarve te samupāśritya vihāre taṃ munīśvaraṃ । dṛṣṭvā sāñjalayo natvā muditāḥ samunpāviśan ।।
tatra sarve api te nāthaṃ tam abhyarcya yathākramaṃ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇatvā samupāśrayan ।। tadā tān samupāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāñ jinaḥ । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītva sarve brahmādayo api te । lokāḥ satyam iti matvā prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।। tasminn avasare kaścit'sau atha āramikaḥ sudhīḥ । dantakāṣṭhaṃ samādāya śrāvastyāṃ samupāviśat ।।
tatra naimittiko dvāre avasthitas tam āgataṃ । dṛṣṭvā tad dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca samālokyaivam upāgamat ।। vataitad dantakāṣṭhaṃ yo bhakṣayiṣyati mānavaḥ । nūnam ṇataraṇaṃ bhogyaṃ prabhokṣyati sa bhāgyavān ।।
etat tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa āramika unmukhaḥ । tatraiva kṣaṇam āśritya manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। kasmāy etad ahaṃ dadyāṃ saṃmāno yena me bhavet । evaṃ dhyātvā punas tatra manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।।
yad ayaṃ bhagavān buddhaḥ sarvatraidhātukādhipaḥ । jagacchāstā jagannātho dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। yad asmai dīyate kiñcid api tat phalam uttamaṃ । aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ mahatkhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā ।।
tad asmai dharmarājāya buddhāya sarvatāyine । jagacchāstre munīndrāya dadyāṃ kāṣṭham idaṃ nv ahaṃ ।। iti dhyātvā viniścitya sa āramika ādarāt । dantakāṣṭhaṃ tad ādāya jetodyāne upācarat ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ । vihāre sa prasannāsyāḥ praviṣṭaḥ samupācarat ।। tatra tasya munīndrasya dantakāṣṭhaṃ tad ādarāt । upasthāpya praṇatvā sa sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña mamānugrahakāraṇāt । dantakāṣṭham imaṃ śāstā bhavān ādātum arhati ।। evaṃ saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । dṛṣṭvā tat kāṣṭham ādāya tasyāgrato vyasṛjata ।।
tadā tat kāṣṭham ādāya sa udyānapālako mudā । tatraiva saugatārāme nikhanya nidadhe bhuvi ।। tatra nihitamātraṃ tat kāṣṭhaṃ mūlapratiṣṭhitaṃ । mahacchākhāharitpatrapuṣpaphalasamṛddhitaḥ ।।
tatkṣaṇena mahān vṛkṣo nyagrodhaḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ । sarvasatvamanohārī mahāmegha ivābhavat ।। tatra sa bhagavān gatvā tacchāyāṃ samupāśrayan । sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaḥ saddhārmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
etad adbhutam ālokya sarve lokāḥ savismayāḥ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā prābhyanandan pramoditāḥ ।। tadā tatra mahātmā sa gṛhīśo anāthapiṇḍadaḥ । samāgatya munīndraṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।।
bhagavann aham adyeha bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । pūjayituṃ samichāmi tan mamānugrahaṃ kuru ।। iti tat prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । tatheti taṃ samālokya tūṣṇīṃ bhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।।
tad adhivāsitaṃ śāstra matvā so anāthapiṇḍadaḥ । tatrāsanāni prajñapya tat sāmagrīṃ samānayat ।। tadā sa bhagavāns tatra sasāṃghikaḥ samutthitaḥ । tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svasvāsane samāśrayat ।।
tatrāsanasamāsīnaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sa muditaḥ śreṣṭhī yathākramaṃ samarcayet ।। tataḥ śatarasai bhojyaiḥ supraṇītaiḥ sa dīnabhṛt । saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ taṃ samatarpayat ।। tataḥ sa śrīghanaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ ca parituṣṭitaṃ ।
matvā panīyapātrāṇi tad dhastādīṃ vyaśodhayat ।। tataḥ kramukatāmbūlagaṇauṣadhīrasāyanaṃ । datvā sa sāṃjalir natvā sasaṃghaṃ tam upāśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ gṛhastham upasthitaṃ ।
ādimadhyāmṭakalyāṇaṃ sāśiṣaṃ dharmam ādiśat ।। tad dṛṣṭva samahotsāham āramikaḥ sa mohitaḥ । naimittikasamākhyātaṃ satyaṃ matvābhyanaṃdata ।। tataḥ sa suprasannātmā ārāmikaḥ pramoditaḥ ।
samutthāya munīndrasya purataḥ samupācarat ।। tatra tasya munīndrasya pādayoḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ । praṇatvā manasā bodhipraṇidhānaṃ vyadhān mudā ।। yad asmai dharmarājāya jagacchāstrai jagadbhute ।
mayātra śraddhayā dattakāṣṭhamātraṃ samarppitaṃ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena caritvāhaṃ śubhe sadā । pratyekāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāṃ ।। iti tena sucittena praṇidhānam kṛtaṃ sadā ।
matvā sa bhagavān smitaṃ visasarja saraśmikaṃ ।। tatas te raśmayaḥ sarvā munimukhābjaniḥsṛtāḥ । nānā varṇāḥ samanteṣu bhuvaneṣu sa bhāsayan ।। ye cādho bhuvane yātāḥ sarvatra narakeṣu te ।
avabhāsya sukhīkṛtya nārakīyān pracerire ।। tadraśmisaṃparispṛṣṭāḥ sarve te narakasthitāḥ । nirduḥkhāḥ sukhasaṃpannā vismitā evam ūcire ।। aho citraṃ kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ prasrabdhaṃ jāyate sukhaṃ ।
itaś cyutāḥ kuhānyatra saṃprāptāḥ sāṃprataṃ vayaṃ ।। iti saṃdigdhacittānāṃ teṣāṃ narakavāsināṃ । bodhārthaṃ nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ bhagavān vyasṛjat tadā ।। tan nirmitaṃ muniṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te narakasthititāḥ ।
mahaccitrasamākrāntahṛdayāś caivam ūśire ।। naivānyatra gatā sarve ihaiva saṃsthitā vayaṃ । kintv ayaṃ puruṣo apūrvadarśanaḥ samupāgataḥ ।। nūnam ayaṃ mahāsattvaḥ samīkṣyāsmān suduḥkhinaḥ ।
kṛpayā coditaḥ sarvān samuddharttum ihāgataḥ ।। tad asya puruṣasyātra sarvair asmābhir ādarāt । śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā karttavyaṃ bhajanaṃ mudā ।। iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve nārakīyā prasāditāḥ ।
tasya nirmitabuddhasya prābhajañ charaṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। tadaitadbhajanotpannaiḥ puṇyais te narakotthitāḥ । nirmuktapātakāḥ sarve śuddhakāyā divaṃ yayuḥ ।। evaṃ te raśmayaḥ sarve sarvāns tān nirayāśṛtān ।
avabhāsya samuddhṛtya pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ ।। evam urddhagatā ye ca raśmayas te prasāritāḥ । avabhāsya diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃprasusruḥ surālayān ।। sarvān devālayāṃś caivam avabhāsya samantataḥ ।
gatvākaniṣṭhaparyantaṃ sarvān devān acodayan ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaśūnyam anātmakaṃ । puṇyam eva jagatsāraṃ matvā tac cinutādarāt ।। niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane ।
mārasainyān vinirjitya caradhvaṃ saṃvare sadā ।। yo apramatto munīndrasya śāsane saṃcariṣyate । sa hitvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati ।। ity udghoṣaiḥ surān sarvāñ codayitvā samantataḥ ।
sarve te raśmayas tatra puraḥ pratyāyayur muneḥ ।। tatra te raśmayaḥ sarve apy ekībhūtāś ca piṇḍitāḥ । muniṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tad ūrṇāyāṃ samāviśan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā sabhāsīnāḥ sarve lokāḥ savismayāḥ ।
kiṃ śāstehādiśed dharmam ity evaṃ samacintayat ।। athānaṃdaḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ savismayaḥ । bhagavantaṃ tam ānamya prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। nāhetupratyayaṃ śāstar hasanti sugatāḥ kvacit ।
tat kim arthañ jagannātha bhavān hasati sāṃprataṃ ।। yad bhavataḥ smitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve ime sabhājanāḥ । vismayasamupākrāntacittās tiṣṭhanti sarvavit ।। tad yad arthe bhavān smitaṃ muṃcati taj jagadguro ।
samupādiśya sarveṣāṃ saṃśayaṃ chetum arhati ।। ity ānandoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān munīśvaraḥ । tam ānandaṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। evam etat tathānaṃda yathākhyātaṃ tvayā kila ।
nāhetupratyayaṃ buddhā muñcaṃti hi smitaṃ kva cit ।। yadarthe aham ihānanda smitaṃ muñcāmi sāṃprataṃ । tat satyaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta yūyam ādarāt ।। yad ayaṃ śraddhayānanda sudhīr udyānapālakaḥ ।
dantakāṣṭham upasthāpya satkāraṃ kurute mama ।। etatpuṇyavipākena kalpāny api trayodaśa । vinipātam ayaṃ kvāpi gamiṣyati kadā cana ।। sarvadāyaṃ mahāsatvaḥ saddharmasādhanodyataḥ ।
sadguṇī sukhasaṃbhoktā bodhisatvo bhaviṣyati ।। tato ante ayaṃ mahābhijñaḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalaḥ । pratyekaṃ bodhim āsādya pratyekasugato jinaḥ ।। vimalo nāma satvānāṃ hitakarī śubhaṃkaraḥ । brahmacārī viśuddhātmā lokanātho bhaviṣyati ।।
evam ānaṃda vijñāya saṃbuddhaśāsane kvacit । kiñcid vāpi pradātavyaṃ tat phalaṃ syān mahattaraṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sāṃghikādayaḥ । sarve lokāḥ sabhāsīnāḥ prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ ।।
so api cārāmikaḥ śrutvā vyākṛtaṃ sugatena tat । triratnabhajanaṃ kartuṃ samaichan muditaḥ sadā ।। tac chrutvā sa mahādātā gṛhastho anāthapiṇḍadaḥ । sāñjalis taṃ jinaṃ natvā muditaḥ svagṛhaṃ yayau ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāṃc chāstā samutthāya sasāṃghikaḥ । svāsanasamupāsīnas tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ ।। tataḥ āramikaḥ so api sarvādā saṃpramoditaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kurvan prācarat samupasthitaḥ ।।
iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । tvayāpy evaṃ mahārāja bhaja ratnatrayaṃ sadā ।। lokāś cāpi tathā rājaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । triratnabhajanotsāhe yojanīyās tvayā sadā ।।
tena te maṅgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet sadā । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।।
āramikasyedam ihāvadānaṃ śṛṇvanti ye ye ca niśāmayanti । te sarvam evaṃ śubhasatsukhāni bhuktvā prayaāsyanti jinālayan te ।। athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayec caivam ādarāt ।।
bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathākhyātuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā so arhaṃ sudhīr yatiḥ । upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me gurubhāṣitaṃ । tathātra hi pravakṣyāmi tava cittābhibodhane ।। tadyathā bhagavāc chāstā śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajño arhañ jagannātho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।।
saṃbuddhaḥ sa tathā tatra pure kapilavastuni । nyagrodharucirārāme vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra pure kapilavastuni । śākya āsīn mahāsādhuḥ śrīmān yakṣādhipopamaḥ ।।
sarvalokapradhānākhyaḥ sarvadravyasamṛddhimān । tasya bhāryā surūpākhyā suṃdarī ratisaṃnibhā ।। subhāvinī ramā kāntā svakuladharmacāriṇī । tayā saha samāraktaḥ sa śrīmān paricārayan ।।
yathākāmaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā rarāma saṃpramoditaḥ । tataḥ svāpannasatvābhūt sā surūpā pragarbhitā । kramād vṛddhodarā pāṇḍuvarṇā svalpāśinī kṛśā ।। tataḥ sā samaye sūta dārakaṃ divyasuṃdaraṃ ।
darśanīyaṃ subhadrāṅgaṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ ।। tasya janmany anekāni mahāścaryakarāṇy api । prādurbhūtāni taiḥ sarvaṃ nagaraṃ pariśobhitaṃ ।। tam abhiśobhitaṃ jātam śrutvā sa janako mudā ।
sahasopetya saṃpaśyans tasthau citrānvitāśayaḥ ।। tataḥ sa mudito jñātīn āhūya saha vāṃdhavaiḥ । kṛtva jātimahaṃ tasya nāmā hi khyātum abravīt ।। bhavanto jñātayaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvāsya lakṣaṇaṃ yathā ।
tathā nāmaprasiddhena vyavasthāpitum arhatha ।। iti tenoditaiḥ śrutvā sarve te jñātayas tathā । tasya nimittam ālokya taṃ śākyam evam abruvan ।। sādho yaj jāyate ātmābhaiḥ śobhayati puraṃ tataḥ ।
śobhita iti nāmāsya bhavatu prathitaṃ bhuvi ।। iti tai jñātibhiḥ sarve samākhyātaṃ niśamya saḥ । tathā tenābhidhānena prākhyāpayat tam ātmajaṃ ।। tataḥ śobhito aṣṭābhir dhātrībhiḥ prātipālitaḥ ।
paripuṣṭo abhivṛddho abhū hradāruhāmbujaṃ yathā ।। yadā so dārakaḥ prauḍhaḥ kumāratvam avāptavān । tadā pitrā sa vidyārthī guruhaste samarppitaḥ ।। tataḥ sa guruṇā śāstrā kramāl lipir aśiṣyate ।
tathābhiśiṣyamāṇaḥ sa sarvavidyāntam āyayau ।। tataḥ sa śobhito dhīmān sarvavidyāṃ vicaksaṇaḥ । tīrthikavādasaṃrakto virakto abhūd gṛhāśrame ।। sadā sa tīrthikārāme gatvā sa tīrthikaiḥ saha ।
śāstrasaṃcodanotsāhai reme jayan pravādinaḥ ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra nyagrodharucirāśramaṃ । sa bhagavān sabhāsīno dharmam ādeṣṭum ārabhat ।। tadā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve bhikṣuṇyo api samāgatāḥ ।
vratinaś cailakāś cānye upāsakā upāsikāḥ ।। bodhisatvā mahāsatvās tathānye śrāvakā api । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve te samupācaran ।। tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।
puraskṛtya samālokya sarve te upatasthire ।। tadānye api samāyātā brahmaśakrādayaḥ surāḥ । catvāro lokapālāś ca sarve lokādhipā api ।। siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।
rakṣasā garuḍā nāgās tathānye api maharddhikāḥ ।। yatayo yoginaś cāpi nirgranthās tīrthikā api । ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāś cāpi tāpasā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। rājānaḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā amātyā maṃtriṇo janāḥ ।
śreṣṭhino dhaninaḥ paurāḥ sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ ।। vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi tathānyadeśavāśinaḥ । grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathā kārpaṭikā api ।। sarve te samupāgatya dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā ।
yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ ।। sāṃjalayaḥ punar natvā parivṛtyā samaṃtataḥ । tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tataḥ sa śobhitaś cāpi tac chrutvā kauṭukānvitaḥ ।
tatra tāṃ parṣadaṃ draṣṭuṃ sahasā samupācarat ।। tatra sa sahasopetya prādrakṣīt taṃ munīśvaraṃ । sarvalokasabhāmadhyasamāsīnaṃ prabhāsvaraṃ ।। dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaparibhūṣitaṃ ।
vyāmaprabhāsamudbhāsaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ । saumyaṃ śāntendriyaṃ kāntaṃ samaṃtabhadrarūpikaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sa suprasannātmā natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ ।। taddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ tatraikānte upāśrayat ।
tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sarvāṃ samupasthitān ।। āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat । tadāryadharmam ākarṇya sarve te sa surādayaḥ ।। lokā dharmaviśeṣatvam ājñāya pratibodhitāḥ ।
bodhicittaṃ samādhāya triratnabhajanodyatāḥ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena babhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ । tadā sa śobhitaś cāpi śrutvāryasatyam uttamaṃ ।। prabodhitaḥ prasannātmā saṃsāravirato bhavān ।
satkāyadṛṣṭibhūmīndhraṃ viṃsatiśikharodgamaṃ ।। hitvā jñānāsinā śrotaāpattiphalam āptavān ।। dṛṣṭasatyo viśuddhātmā saddharmaguṇalālasaḥ । saṃbuddhapadasaṃprāptyai pravrajituṃ samaichata ।।
tataḥ sa samupāśritya kṛtāṃjalipurogataḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ jagannāthaṃ svaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । pravrajituṃ samichāmi tatkṛpayā prasīdatu ।।
iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । śobhitaṃ taṃ samālokya samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। yadi tvaṃ śāsane bauddhe pravrajituṃ samichasi । pitur ājñāṃ samāsādya prehi dāsyāmi te vrataṃ ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa śobhito mudā । pādau tasya muner natvā sahasā niryayau tataḥ ।। tatra sa svagṛhe gatvā pādau natvā puraḥ sthitaḥ । pitror etat samākhyāya prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
tātāham adya gachāmi nyagrodharucire vane । tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ buddhaṃ paśyāmi parṣadāśritaṃ ।। dhanyās te śrāvakāḥ sarve bhikṣavo bhadrikāśikāḥ । śāṃteṃdriyāḥ samācārā arhanto brahmacāriṇaḥ ।।
teṣām eva hi saṃsāre sāphalyaṃ janma mānuṣe । ye bhajanti munīndrasya śāsane śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। teṣāṃ caivaṃ susāraṃ syān saṃsāre bhavacāraṇe । ye saddharmaṃ munīndrasya śrutvā caraṃti saṃvaraṃ ।।
teṣāṃ cāpi bhave sāraṃ janmadravyaguṇārjanaṃ । satkāraiḥ sāṃghike sevāṃ kṛtvā caranti ye vrataṃ ।। kiṃ teṣāṃ mānuṣe janma nisphalaṃ sarvasādhanaṃ । ye dhyātvāpi jinaṃ smṛtvā bhajaṃti na kadā cana ।।
teṣāṃ ca kiṃ bhave janma kevalaṃ pāpasādhanaṃ । ye na śṛṇvaṃti saddharmaṃ saṃbuddhabhāṣitaṃ kva cit ।। teṣāṃ ca nisphalaṃ janma mānuṣye duḥkhasādhanaṃ । ye na kurvanti satkāraṃ sāṃghikeṣu kadā cana ।।
evaṃ ye paśuvad gehe bhogyaṃ bhuktvā vasaṃti vai । teṣāṃ kiṃ janma saṃsāre pāpaduḥkhārtham eva hi ।। evaṃ te prāṇinaḥ sarve bhramaṃti bhavasāgare । yato yair dṛśyate kvāpi triratnaṃ na kadā cana ।।
tathāsmākam api cātra saṃsāre janma nisphalaṃ । saṃpado api nirarthā hi triratnabhajanaṃ vinā ।। dharmārthajanmasaṃsāre yadi dharmo na labhyate । kim evaṃ jīvitenāpi kevalāśubhasādhinā ।।
tad varaṃ mṛtyur adyevaṃ vinā dhārmārthasādhanaṃ । kiṃ tena jīvitenāpi yan mithyāduḥkhasādhanaṃ ।। na prāptaṃ bhagavatpūjā mahotsāhaṃ kadāpi yaiḥ । dharmo api na śrutaḥ kaścin na kārāḥ sāṃghike kṛtāḥ ।।
bhītebhyo nābhayaṃ dattaṃ daridrāśā na pūritā । duḥkhāya kevalaṃ mātur gatās te garbhaśalyatāṃ ।। dhanyās te sukhino loke subhadrāḥ śubhabhāvinaḥ । satpuruṣā mahātmānaḥ śrīmaṃtaḥ sadguṇāśrayāḥ ।।
ye buddhe śaraṇaṃ gatvā dhyātvā smṛtvā samāhitāḥ । saddharmāmṛtam āpīya carantaḥ saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। sarve satvahitārthaṃ ca dānaṃ datvā yathepsitaṃ । dayālavaḥ susaumyāṃśāḥ sarvasatvahitāśayāḥ ।।
saṃbodhisādhanotsāhasarvasatvahitodyatāḥ । niḥkleśā vimalātmānaḥ samādhiniścalāśayāḥ ।। prajñāvaṃto mahādhīrāḥ saṃbodhiratnalābhinaḥ । pravrajyāvratinārhanto nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ ।।
bhikṣāhārā nirātaṃkā niḥśaṃkā damiteṃdriyāḥ । niḥśeṣanirjitāvidyāḥ prāptavidyā viśāradāḥ ।। svachaṃdacāriṇaḥ santaḥ sarvasatvātmabhāvinaḥ । niḥspṛhā viratotsāhā nirdainyaḥ kṣubhitāśayāḥ ।।
nirmadā nirahaṃkārā āryā nirabhimāninaḥ । nirmāyā nirmamākhaḍgā niḥsaṃgā niḥparigrahāḥ ।। muṇḍitā khikkhirīpātradadhānāś cīvarāvṛtāḥ । yatinaḥ sugatākārās triyānamokṣadeśakāḥ ।।
svaparātmahitārthena saṃbodhimārgadeśakāḥ । vaṃdyāḥ pūjyāḥ pramānyāś ca caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ ।। te eva sugatiṃ yāṃti yāṃti cānte jinālaye । saṃbodhiṃ ca samāsādya bhaveyuḥ sugatā api ।।
iti satyaṃ munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya me । mano atra bhavasaṃcāre carituṃ nābhivāṃchati ।। triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaśāsane śubhe । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā caritum ichati sāṃprataṃ ।।
kiṃ ca me janmakāle yad idaṃ yuḥ śobhitāruṣā । saṃpado api pravarddhante divyābhisuṃdarāsmi ca ।। tat sarvaṃ me purā bhadrakarmadharmavipākataḥ । saṃpadyate adhunā nūnaṃ viddhi mā tv anyathā pita ।।
etan nūnam iti matvā bhūyo api me manas tathā । saddharmasādhanaṃ kartum ichati saugataṃ vrataṃ ।। etad dhetor ahaṃ tāta prārthayāmy evam ādarāt । tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me yadi vāṃchāsti vā śubhe ।।
etatpuṇyavibhāgena yūyam api surālayaṃ । gatvā divyasukhāny eva bhuktvā ciraṃ nivatsyatha ।। tataḥ kāle divaś cyutvā martyaloka ihāgatāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cariṣyatha śubhe sadā ।।
tac chubhapuṇyapākena śuddhāśayāḥ śubhāvinaḥ । saṃbuddhaśāsane gatvā saddharmaṃ śroṣyathādarāt ।। tatas tat puṇyapākena saṃghānāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । satkāraiḥ samupasthitvā bhajiṣyatha samādarāt ।।
tatas tat puṇyapākena bodhicittam avāpsyatha । tato lokahitārtheṣu bodhicaryāṃ cariṣyatha ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ । tato bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyatha ।।
evaṃ vijñāya saṃbuddhapadasaṃpratipattaye । tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me saṃbuddhapadavāṃchire ।। anityaṃ khalu samṣāraṃ jīvitaṃ kṣaṇabhaṃguraṃ । kṣaṇabhaṃgiśarīraṃ ca sarveṣāṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ ।।
saṃpado api sthirā naiva satkṣaṇaṃ ca sudurlabhaṃ । mānuṣye sarvadā janma labhyate na sudurllabhaṃ ।। tatrāpi durlabhā dharme matir jātāpi na sthirāḥ । dharmaṃ tu saugataiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ yat saṃbodhipadasādhanaṃ ।।
tat saṃbodhipadaprāptyai dharmaṃ ichāmi saugataṃ । tad anujñāṃ pradatvā me mano harṣayata drutaṃ ।। dharmaṃ vinātra kiṃ sāraṃ bhogyair arthair guṇair api । kiṃ kāmasukhaṃ bhuktvā sthitvā ca paśuvad gṛhe ।।
tad anujñāṃ na datyaśyen sthāsyāmi na gṛhe apy ahaṃ । sarvān parigrahāns tyaktvā gamiṣyāmi tapovanaṃ ।। tatra ko nirjane sthitvā caritvā duṣkaraṃ tapaḥ । anāhāro mariṣye ahaṃ sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।।
kasya mṛtyu bhave nāsti kutra mṛtyor bhayaṃ na hi । sarvalokān grasen mṛtyur eko api sa mahāvaliḥ ।। tad atra kiṃ viṣādena yad damopāyam atra na । avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavanti mahatām api ।।
mṛtyukāle sahāyo api ko api nāsti sahānugaḥ । dharma eva tadaiko hi sahāyaḥ syāt sahānugaḥ ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sthātuṃ nechanti sajjanāḥ । sarvān parigrahāns tyaktvā pravrajanti śubhārthinaḥ ।।
tathāham api tan mṛtyubhayaṃ dṛṣṭvābhiśaṃkitaḥ । saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatvā carituṃ vratam utsahe ।। iti dharme nidheddhaṃ mā kiṃ cid vā vaktum arhatha । suprasannādhiyānujñāṃ pradātum eva me arhati ।।
iti tenātmajenaivaṃ saṃprārthitaṃ niśamya tau । pitarau vismayākrāṃtacittau taṣṭhatur mūrchitau ।। tatas tau dhairyam ālambya tam eva svātmajaṃ cirāt । dṛṣṭvā viyogaduḥkhārttau taṣṭhatur likhitāv iva ।।
tataḥ sa janakaḥ śākyas taduktaparibodhitaḥ । galadaśrumukho dṛṣṭvā taṃ putram evam abravīt ।। hā putra kiṃ atrāhaṃ vadeya sāṃprataṃ khalu । yat tvam eva sudhīr vijñaḥ paṇḍito asi vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
yat tvaṃ śāsane bauddhe pravrajituṃ samichasi । tac chāstuḥ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ cara samāhitaḥ ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sa sobhitaḥ pramoditaḥ । pitroḥ pādān praṇatvaiva sahasā niryayau gṛhāt ।।
tataḥ sa sahasā gatvā nyagrodhatarumaṇḍite । vihāre sugatārame praviśya samupācarat ।। yatra sa purato gatvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । praṇatvā taṃ jagannāthaṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña prāpyānujñāṃ samāvraje । tad bhavān sāṃprataṃ mahyaṃ pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati ।। bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitvā pravrajya saugataṃvrataṃ । dhṛtvā sadā samādāya cariṣye bodhicārikāṃ ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । savyena pāṇinā tasya śiraḥ spṛṣṭvaivam ādiśat ।। ehi ca vatsa samādhāya vrataṃ carasva saugataṃ । ity uktvā sa munīndraḥ svasāṃghike taṃ samagrahīt ।।
ehīty ukte munīṃdreṇa śobhito abhūt sa muṇḍitaḥ । khikkhirīpātravibhrāṇaḥ kākhāyacīvarī yatiḥ ।। tataḥ sa sumatir bhikṣuḥ saṃsāragatinispṛhaḥ । bhitvāvidyāgaṇān sarvān prāptavidyā viśāradaḥ ।।
sarvakleśagaṇāṃ jitvā sākṣād arhatvam āptavān ।। tataḥ so arhan mahābhijñaḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalaḥ । nikleśaḥ suviśuddhātmā śuddhendriyo jināṃśabhṛt ।। nirvikalpaḥ samākāro brahmacārī niraṃjanaḥ ।
saṃsāralābhasatkāraniḥspṛhaḥ khasamāśayaḥ ।। sa devāsuralokānāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ । mānyaḥ pūjyo abhivaṃdyaś ca babhūva sa jinātmajaḥ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayoddhatamānasāḥ ।
bhavantaṃ praṇatvaivaṃ paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavan kiṃ purānena sukṛtaṃ prakṛtaṃ kuha । yenāyaṃ sukule jāto divyakalpātisuṃdaraḥ ।। janmani vāsya jātāni mahādbhutakarāṇy api ।
yair etan nagaraṃ sarvaṃ caṃdrābhair iva śobhitaṃ ।। bhavatāṃ śāsane cāpi triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā yatir arhan bhavaty api ।। etat sarvaṃ samākhyāya bhavāṃc chāstā jagadguruḥ ।
sarvān asmān sabhāṃś cāpi prabodhayitum arhati ।। iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvān yatīn sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anena purākṛtaṃ ।
tat sarvaṃ samāśakhye yuṣmākaṃ paribodhane ।। tadyathābhūt purā śāstā krakuchandas tathāgataḥ । sarvajño arhaṃ jagannātho dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। tadā sa bhagavān loke bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan ।
saddharmaṃ samupādiśya pracacāra samaṃtataḥ ।। evaṃ sa bhagavāṃ chāstā kṛtvā sarvatra maṃgalaṃ । śobhāvatyā mahāpūryyā rājadhānyā upāśrame ।। vihāre saugatāvāse samāśritya prabhāsayan ।
saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tatrāgatya samānīnaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । śrutvā śobho mahārājo draṣṭuṃ sa samupācarat ।। tatra sa nṛpatiḥ śobho dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ muniṃ ।
krakuchaṃdaṃ samāsīnaṃ bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ ।। muditaḥ samupāsṛtya kṛtāṃjaliḥ purogataḥ । praṇatvā suprasannāsyaḥ prārthayam evam ādarāt ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavāñ chāstā jagadguruḥ ।
tad asmākaṃ hitārthena dharmam ādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān api । taṃ śobhaṃ kṣitipāleṃdraṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan samādhāya satvānāṃ hitakāraṇaṃ ।
saṃbodhisādhanaṃ dharmaṃ vakṣyāmi te śubhārthataḥ ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāre sarvaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ । māyākleśasamudbhūtaṃ jagallokam aśāśvataṃ ।। tad atra kiṃ bhave sāraṃ nirarthaṃ duḥkhasādhanaṃ ।
iti vijñāya rājendra kleśāñ jitvā śubhe cara ।। śubhena sadgatiṃ yāyā sadgatau sarvadā sukhaṃ । sukhena sarvadā bhadre caritavyaṃ tathā bhavaṃ ।। śubhaṃ saṃjāyate puṇyāt sarvatrāpi sadā dhruvaṃ ।
puṇyaṃ saṃjāyate hy ādau saṃbuddhadarśanād api ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena saddharmaśravaṇaṃ labhet । tat saddharmarasāsvādasaṃsaktaś ca samutsahet ।। tadutsāhāt punaḥ śrotum abhilāṣaḥ samudbhavet ।
samudbhūtābhilāṣaś ca satkṛtya mānayen mudā ।। sadguruṃ samupāsṛtya saddharmaṃ śṛṇuyāt sadā । tat saddharmāmṛtasvādaguṇalabdhaḥ pramoditaḥ ।। saddharmacāraṇo bhikṣūn satkṛtya mānayen mudā ।
tatas tad dharmam ākarṇya saṃbodhidharmavāṃchitaḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā svaparārthahite caret ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sa kule śrīsamālaye । jāto lokahitārthena dānaṃ dadyād yathepsitaṃ ।।
tad dānapuṇyapākena sa dātā sadgatiṃ vrajet । sadgatisthaḥ sukhenaivaṃ suśīlaḥ saṃvaraṃ caret ।। tat suśīlavratotpannaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sa pariśuddhadhīḥ । sarvasatvahitārtheṣu dayālu maitravac caret ।।
tatas tat puṇyapākena sa sudhīro vicakṣaṇaḥ । svaparātmahitārthena sarvakāryāṇi sādhayet ।। etat puṇyaviśuddhātmā niḥkleśo vimalāśayaḥ । samādhidharaṇīvidyāsamādhānaḥ sudhīr bhavet ।।
tatas tat puṇyasaṃbhārasaṃbodhiguṇasārthabhṛt । prajñābdhipāram āsādya bodhicittamaṇiṃ labhet ।। tan maner anubhāvena sarvopāyavidhānavit । sarvasatvahito dhānaṃ bodhicaryāvrataṃ caret ।।
tatpuṇyaiḥ sa mahāsatvaḥ sarvasatvaśubhaṃkaraḥ । saṃbodhipraṇidhānena saddharmābhirato bhavet ।। tatas tad dharmapūtātmā duṣṭakleśān vinirjayan । sarvahitārthasaṃbhartā mahābhijñā valī bhave ।।
tato māragaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalaḥ । so arhan saṃbodhisaṃprāptaḥ saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। tataḥ sa sugataḥ śāstā kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya nirvṛtaḥ svālayaṃ vrajet ।।
tataḥ sa svālaye līno dharmadhātvīśvaro jinaḥ । viśvarūpā viśuddhābhajyotirūpo niraṃjanaḥ ।। evaṃ vijñāya rājendra saṃbuddhapadavāṃchibhiḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।।
tathā taṃ sarvadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyatha ।। iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā śobhaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathā hīti pravijñapya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ ।।
tadārabhya sa bhūmīndras triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā prācarat sarvadā śubhe ।। tadā tadviṣaye tatra sarvadābhūc chubhotsavaṃ । sarva lokāś ca saddharmāratotsāhāḥ pracerire ।।
evaṃ sa nṛpatiḥ śobhas taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । yathārhabhojanaiś cāpi trimāsyaṃ samasevita ।। tataḥ sa bhūmīrājo trimāsānte sasāṃghikaṃ । krakuchaṃdaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।।
bhagavan nātha sarvajña sarvadātra sasāṃghikaḥ । saddharmaṃ kṛpayāsmadbhyam ādeṣṭum sthātum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । tada śobhaṃ jagatīpālaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
nāhaṃ rājaṃs tavaikasya hitārthe sugato bhave । api tu sarvasatvānāṃ śubhahetau bhave jinaḥ ।। tad evaṃ sarvalokeṣu bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan । saddharmaṃ samupākhyātuṃ careyaṃ saha sāṃghikaiḥ ।।
yady asti te sadā rājaṃ bhaktiśraddhāmatir mayi । mannāmābhisamuddiśya stūpaṃ kṛtvā sadā bhaja ।। etasmiṃ yat kṛtaṃ karma tan mayi kṛtam eva hi । tiṣṭhato nirvṛtasyāpi tulyaṃ bhaktimatāṃ phalaṃ ।।
tadyathā mayi rājendra śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā carasvaivaṃ śubhe mudā ।। tathāsmin sarvadā stūpe śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā śubhe cara samāhitaḥ ।।
tathā te sarvadā kṣemaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। ity ādiśya sa saṃbuddhas tasmai śobhāya bhūrbhuje । svanakhakeśam utkṛtya dadau stūpārtham ādarāt ।।
taṃ munīndrapradattaṃ sa bhūpatiḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । praṇatvā samupāgṛhya sānaṃdaḥ svālayaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa nṛpatī rājā tan nakhakeśam ādarāt । garbhe nidhāya sadratnair mahastūpam akārayat ।।
tatas taṃ sa nṛpo rājā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhiḥ । mahotsavaiḥ sadā nityaṃ samabhyarcya bhajan mudā ।। tatraikasmin dine bhadre parvaṇi pratyupasthite । sametya goṣṭhikāḥ sarve taṃ stūpaṃ draṣṭum āgatāḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā te goṣṭhikāḥ sarve suprasannābhimoditāḥ । nānāpuṣpais tam abhyarcya mahotsavaiḥ sahābhajat ।। tatraiko goṣṭhiko dṛṣṭvā daridro aham iti bruvan । tatpūjāmahotsāhe lajjayā svagṛhaṃ yayau ।।
tatas tair goṣṭhikaiḥ sarvair dṛṣṭvā sa svagṛhe tataḥ । bahuśaḥ paribhāṣitvā goṣṭhimadhyād bahiṣkṛtaḥ ।। tataḥ sa lajjayākhinnaḥ paścāttāpāgnitāpitaḥ । hā maṃdaḥ katham eko ahaṃ tiṣṭheyam ity aciṃtayat ।।
tataḥ sa sugataṃ smṛtvā daridro api samaṃtataḥ । sarvapuṣpāṇi saṃgṛhya tais taṃ stūpaṃ samarcayat ।। tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāṃjaliḥ sa pramoditaḥ । tat pādayoḥ praṇatvaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ mudākarot ।।
yan mayātra munīndrasya stūpaḥ puṣpaiḥ samarcitaḥ । etatpuṇyavipākena bhaveyaṃ śrīsamṛddhimān ।। ity evaṃ praṇidhiṃ kṛtvā tat stūpaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । sa daridraḥ samabhyarcya prābhajan saṃpramoditaḥ ।।
manyatāṃ bhikṣavo yo asau daridro ayaṃ hi śobhitaḥ । yat stūpo arcitaḥ puṣpais tenāyaṃ śrīsamṛddhimān ।। anyad api yathānena sukṛtaṃ prakṛtaṃ purā । tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvan yūyam ādarāt ।।
tathāthābhūt purā pūryyāṃ vārāṇasyāṃ gṛhādhipaḥ । śreṣṭhī mahājanaḥ sādhur vyavahāravicakṣaṇaḥ ।। tadaikasmin dine tasya gṛhāntike śanaiś caran । pratyekasugato glāno bhikṣārthaṃ samupācaran ।। taṃ gṛhāntikam āyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa karuṇāhataḥ ।
sahasopetya natvainam āmaṃtrya svagṛhe nayet ।। tatra śreṣṭhī sa taṃ glānaṃ pratyekabuddham āsane । upasthāpya samabhyarcya paṭenāchādayan mudā ।। tasmai kṣīrodanaiḥ pūrṇaṃ pātraṃ paṃcāmṛtaiḥ saha ।
pradatvā sāṃjalir natvā manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। yad ayaṃ sugato glāno abhyarcito mayādarāt । etatpuṇyavipākena bhaveyaṃ kṣemavān sudhīḥ ।। ity evaṃ praṇidhānena sa śreṣṭhī pratimoditaḥ ।
satkṛtya sādaraṃ tatra svāśrame samacārayat ।। manyatāṃ bhikṣavo yo asau śreṣṭhī śrīmān mahājanaḥ । ayam eva mahābhijñaḥ śobhito arhan mahāmatiḥ ।। yad anena tadā glānapratyekabuddha ādarāt ।
paṭenāchādya piṃḍena pratipādya samarcitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena śobhito ayaṃ samṛddhimān । paṃcajanmaśatāny evaṃ babhūva sadguṇākaraḥ ।। bhūyo api yat purānena sukṛtaṃ sādhitaṃ yathā ।
tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ yūyam ādarāt ।। tadyathābhūt purā śāstā kāśyapo arhans tathāgataḥ । sarvajñaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ ।। vārāṇasyāṃ sa saṃbuddho mṛgadāve sasāṃghikaḥ ।
sarvasatvahitārthena vyaharad dharmam ādiśat ।। tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra vārāṇasyām abhūd gṛhī । saṃbuddhabhaktimān sādhur daridraḥ kāṣṭhahārikaḥ ।। sa ekasmin dine kāṣṭham āhartu parvaṭe vrajan ।
tatraikatra mahat stūpaṃ dadarśāchāditaṃ tṛṇaiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā sa samupāśritya tat tṛṇāni samaṃtataḥ । sarvāṇy api samutpāṭya saṃmṛjya samaśodhayat ।। tatas taṃ śobhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa śreṣṭhī saṃpramoditaḥ ।
natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। yad ayaṃ saugatastūpo mayā saṃmṛjya śodhitaḥ । etatpuṇyavipākena bhaveyaṃ divyasuṃdaraḥ ।। divyātiriktābhaiḥ śobhitaḥ syān samṛddhimān ।
anāgatāṃś ca saṃbuddhān ārāgayeyam ādarāt ।। tadā tacchāsane gatvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । pravrajyārhatpadaṃ prāpya vrajeyāhaṃ sunirvṛtiṃ ।। ity evaṃ praṇidhiṃ kṛtvā praṇatvā taṃ jinālayaṃ ।
satataḥ kāṣṭham ādāya svagṛhaṃ samudācarat ।। tataḥ sa sumatiḥ śrīmān abhūt tatpuṇyavān kṛtiḥ । sukhāni suciraṃ bhuktvā kāle mṛto divaṃ yayau ।। svarge sa divyabhogyāni bhuktvā reme suraiḥ saha ।
paṃcajanmaśatāny evaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā bhramed bhave ।। atrāpi yadeyaṃ śrīmāñ chāsane me samāgataḥ । pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā carann arhan bhavaty api ।। tat sarvaṃ hi vijānīta tatstūpasaṃmṛṣṭapuṇyataḥ ।
yathā ca ciṃtitaṃ tatra tathāsya siddhyate adhunā ।। daridrakāṣṭhahāro yo bhavet so ayaṃ hi śobhitaḥ । anya iti na manyantavyaṃ yuṣmābhir nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। evaṃ sarvatra saṃsāre sarveṣām api prāṇināṃ ।
yathaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tathaiva tat phalaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana । anyathāpi bhaven naiva karmaphalaṃ kathaṃ cana ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā sukhavāṃchibhiḥ ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ । sarve lokāś ca saṃbodhiprāptuṃ dharmārthino abhavan ।। iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate ।
tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja saddharmanirato bhava ।। prajāś cāpi mahāraja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge abhisaṃsthāpya pātum arhati sarvadā ।। evaṃ kṛte mahārāja sarvatra vaḥ śubhaṃ bhavet ।
kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ । tathā hīti pratijñapya prābhyanandat sa pārṣadaḥ ।। ye śraddhāḥ suprasannā idam api manujāḥ śobhitasyāvadānaṃ ।
śṛṇvanti śrāvayaṃti pramuditamanasā ye ca saṃbodhikāmāḥ । te sarve bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇabhṛto bodhicaryāṃ caranto । bhuktvā saukhyaṃ prakāmaṃ daśabalanilaye saṃprayānti pramuktvā ।। athāśoko mahīpālaḥ sāṃjaliḥ samupāśritaḥ ।
upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ । tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan sudhīr yatiḥ ।
tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me gurubhāṣitaṃ । tathātrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi tava cittaviśuddhaye ।। tadyathābhūn mahāpūryyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ śrīdasaṃnibhaḥ ।
śreṣṭhī mahādhanaḥ sādhuḥ puṣyābhidho mahājanaḥ ।। tasya bhāryā subhadrāṃgī rāmākhyā śrīsamānikā । kuladharmasamācarā svāmicaryānucāriṇī ।। yayā patnyā subhāvinyā sārddhaṃ puṣyaḥ sa sanmatiḥ ।
yathākāmaḥ sukhaṃ bhuktvā reme samupacārayan ।। tataḥ sā samaye kāṃtā garbhiṇī varddhitodarā । svalpāhāraratā pāṇḍuvarṇā kṛśābhavat kramāt ।। tataḥ sā samaye asūta dārikāṃ divyasuṃdarīṃ ।
śironivaddhamuktā srakkohitām abhirocinīṃ ।। tāṃ saṃjātāṃ śirovaddhamuktāmālāṃ praśobhitāṃ । dārikāṃ sā prasū dṛṣṭvā sacitrānaṃdito abhavat ।। tac chrutvā sa pitā puṣyo vismayoddhatamānasaḥ ।
upetya tāṃ sutāṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthau paśyan savismayaḥ ।। tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve vaṃdhumitrasuhṛjjanāḥ । tāṃ saṃjātāṃ niśamyāśu draṣṭum ājagmur ādarāt ।। tatra tāṃ dārikāṃ kāṃtāṃ śiromuktāsraganvitāṃ ।
darśanīyāṃ subhadrāṃgīṃ prādrākṣus te ciraṃ mudā ।। ahosvid devakanyeyaṃ nūnaṃ mānyā na mānavī । yad iyaṃ jātamātrāpi bhābhiḥ śobhate puraṃ ।। iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve jñātivaṃdhū suhṛjjanāḥ ।
suciraṃ tāṃ samālokya vismitā niryayus tataḥ ।। tataḥ sa janakas tasyāḥ kṛtvā jatimahaṃ mudā । sarvāñ jñātīn samāmaṃtrya pura evam abhāṣata ।। bhavanto asyāḥ sutāyā me dṛṣṭvā saṃpannimittamāṃ ।
yathā loke prasiddhaṃ syāt tathā nāmābhidhīyatāṃ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātivāṃdhavāḥ । tan nimittaṃ samālokya taṃ puṣyam evam abruvan ।। sādho yat saṃprajāteyaṃ muktāmālāśiroruhā ।
tad asyā nāma mukteti prasiddhaṃ bhavatu dhruvaṃ ।। evaṃ taiḥ jñātibhiḥ sarvaiḥ samākhyātaṃ niśamya saḥ । puṣyas tasyāḥ sutāyās tan nāmaprasiddham acārayat ।। tataḥ sā dārikā muktā dhātrībhiḥ pratipālitā ।
aṣṭābhir abhipuṣyāṃgā pravṛddhābhūd hradābjavat ।। tataḥ sā dārikā kāntā pravṛddhābhūt kumārikā । guruṇāṃ samupāśritya kramād vidyā aśikṣate ।। tatra sā sumatīr muktā lipipāraṃ gatā kramāt ।
sarvaśāstrakalāvidyāpāraṃ yayau vicakṣaṇā ।। tataḥ sā dānasaṃraktā sarvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । saddharmapraṇidhānena dadau nityaṃ prasāditā ।। sarve api yācakās tasyā gṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvā samāgatāḥ ।
tad dattaṃ dravyam ādāya prayayuḥ saṃpramoditāḥ ।। tadaiko brāhmaṇas tasyā muktāmālāṃ śiroruhāṃ । dṛṣṭvā lobhākulātmā sa gṛhaṃ gatvā samāśrayat ।। tatra sa brāhmaṇo dṛṣṭvā tāṃ kanyāṃ saṃpradāyanīṃ ।
upetyāśīrvacoddatvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। jayo astu te sadā bhadre ciraṃ jivyāḥ sukhānvitā । yathā te vāṃchate cittaṃ tathā sarvaṃ prasiddhyatu ।। bhadre ahaṃ te guṇāc chrutvā dūrato yad ihāvraje ।
tad arthaṃ śṛṇu te vakṣye tac chrutvā me prasīdatu ।। yad iyaṃ te śirobaddhā muktāmālā praśobhitā । tad imāṃ me pradatvātra mano mama vinodaya ।। iti saṃprārthite tena sā muktā saṃpradānikā ।
tāṃ pradātuṃ samichantī taṃ vipram evam abravīt ।। sādhu vipra kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭha mā vrajasvānyataḥ kvacit । pitror ājñāṃ samāyācya dāsyāmi te imām api ।। ity uktvā sa samāśvāsya brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ pralobhitaṃ ।
sahasā purato gatvā pitror evam abhāṣata ।। pitar amba gṛhe asmākaṃ brāhmaṇo arthī samāgataḥ । sa mamemāṃ śirorūḍhāṃ muktāmālāṃ prayācate ।। tad imāṃ dātum ichāmi tasmai viprāya sādhave ।
tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me yady asti vāṃ dayām api ।। iti putryoditaṃ śrutvā sa pitā vismayāhataḥ । tāṃ putrīṃ suciraṃ dṛṣṭvā paribhāṣyaivam abravīt ।। bho vatsa kiṃ samīkṣyaivaṃ svamastaka samudbhavāṃ ।
netravat katham utkṛtya pradadyād arthine sute ।। yadi dātuṃ samichā te brāhmaṇāyārthine sute । tad anyatprārthitaṃ dravyaṃ pradadasva yathepsitaṃ ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sā muktā duhitā sudhīḥ ।
janakaṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvā caivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu tāta yad arthe ahaṃ svaśiraḥsaṃbhavām api । muktāmālaṃ samuddhṛtya ditsāmi tat pravakṣyate ।। anityaṃ khalu saṃsāre mānuṣye janma durlabhaṃ ।
kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca jīvitaṃ ca tṛṇāmbuvat ।। tatrāpi bahavo rogāḥ saṃpado apy aticaṃcalaḥ । durlabhā kṣaṇasaṃpac ca dharmamatiś ca durlabhā ।। kiṃ nityam atra saṃsāre ko hi nityasthito bhave ।
ity anityām imāṃ muktāmālāṃ ditsāmy ahaṃ pita ।। ko anyatra mānuṣā dehād dānaṃ kartuṃ praśaknuyāt । ity āpy ahaṃ samīkṣyātra dātum iche kajām api ।। kasyātra vigrahe mṛtyor viśvāsaṃ vidyate khalu ।
iti matvāpi tātemāṃ ditsāmi muktakāsrajaṃ ।। kasyātra jīvitaṃ kāye svechayā samavasthitaṃ । evaṃ vijñāya tātemaṃ mālāṃ ditsāmi puṣpavat ।। ko nātra pīḍyate rogaiḥ sakleśair devasaṃbhavaiḥ ।
ity evaṃ samīkṣyaimāṃ dātum ichāmi muktikāṃ ।। kasya saṃpat sthirā gehe astāś capi sthitir na hi । evaṃ vijñāya tatemaṃ ditsāmi kusumākṛtiṃ ।। kasya cātra śubhe dṛṣṭir jāyāt tiṣṭhec ca sarvadā ।
evaṃ vāpi parijñāya ditsāmīmāṃ kajām api ।। sadā na jāyate naivaṃ dharme matiḥ kathaṃ cana । iti dṛṣṭvāpi me cittam imāṃ ditsati puṣpavat ।। imāṃ me daivasaṃjātāṃ śiraḥsthāṃ keśasādṛśīṃ ।
dātum ichāmy ahaṃ tāta saddharmaratnalabdhaye ।। kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyaṃ sarveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ । yāvad jīvitamuktāyām iyaṃ muktāpi nakṣyati ।। yad iyaṃ me śirojāpi prāṇena saha nakṣyati ।
tad dattā vāpy adattāpi sarvathāpi vinakṣyati ।। etad devaṃ samīkṣye māṃ muktāṃ puṣpasrajaṃ yathā । kajām api samuddhṛtya dātum ichāmy ahaṃ pita ।। tad atra mā kṛthā vighnaṃ mama saddharmasādhane ।
tad anujñāṃ pradatvā me prārthitaṃ saphalaṃ kuru ।। yadi na dīyate anujñāṃ dānavighnaphalaṃ lābheḥ । tato te duṣkṛtir jāyāt tato hi durgatiṃ vrajeḥ ।। yady anujñāṃ pradānena satyaṃ pūrayase mama ।
tatas te sukṛtir jāyāt tena yāyād dhi sadgatiṃ ।। sadgatau sarvadā saukhyaṃ bhuktvā careḥ śubheṣv api । tataḥ krameṇa saṃbodhiṃ prāpya buddhatvam āpnuyāḥ ।। evaṃ vījñāya tātātra vārayituṃ na me arhati ।
tad anujñapya me satyaṃ saṃpūrayitum arhati ।। iti putryā tayākhyātaṃ śrutvā pitā sa bodhitaḥ । tāṃ muktāṃ sumātiḥ putrīṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। yat tvayaivaṃ samākhyātaṃ tat sarvaṃ satyam eva hi । yadi śraddhāsti te dātuṃ pradehi kiṃ nivāraye ।।
iti pitrābhyanujñāte sā muktā parimoditā । tāṃ śiraḥsadbhavāṃ muktāṃ mālām utkartum aichata ।। tadā sā jananī dṛṣṭvā tāṃ muktāṃ svātmajāṃ priyāṃ । śirojām api tāṃ muktāṃ mālām utkartu vāṃchinīṃ ।।
sahasā gāḍham āliṃgya vārayituṃ samudyatā । galadaśruviliptākṣā vilapaṃtyaivam abravīt ।। hā priye svātmaje putrī katham ajñāsi sāṃprataṃ । indriyavat tanūdbhūtām api dātuṃ yadīchasi ।।
yac chirojāṃ samutkṛtya muktāmālāṃ svadaivajāṃ । kim anyad iha paśyanti viprāya dātum ichasi ।। yadi dāne ativāṃchā te pradehi tad yad ipsitaṃ । imām eva śirojatāṃ mā dāḥ kasmai cid arthine ।।
dam iyaṃ svatanūdbhūtā sahajā jīvitendraiḥ । tad iyaṃ katham utkṛtya dātavyeti vicāraya ।। yadīmaṃ svaśirorūḍhāṃ balenotkṛtya dāsyasi । tadeyaṃ nakṣyate nūnaṃ jīvitena saha dhruvaṃ ।।
vinaṣṭe jīvite kāye ko dharmaṃ sādhayet punaḥ । dharmaṃ vinātra saṃsāre nirarthaṃ sarvasādhanaṃ ।। dharmamūlaṃ hi saṃsāre satkāyajīvitaṃ kila । taj jīvitāśrayaḥ kāyo rakṣitavyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
yat kāyaprāṇarakṣārthaṃ saṃsāre dharmasādhanaṃ । kāyaprāṇaṃ vinā ko arthaḥ saṃsāre dharmasādhane ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣādi sādhanaṃ sukhakāraṇaṃ । abhāve jīvite kāye kasyārthe sukhasādhanaṃ ।।
yat svajīve na pakṣyaivaṃ kim arthe dātum ichasi । svakāyajīvarakṣārthaṃ dānādi puṇyasādhanaṃ ।। svakāyajīvitaṃ tyaktvā kim arthe puṇyasādhanaṃ । svakāyajīva bhadrārthe guṇadravyavṛṣārjanaṃ ।।
iti satyaṃ mayākhyātaṃ hitārthaṃ te priyātmaje । śrutvemaṃ netravad rakṣyā mā dāḥ kasmai cid arthine ।। yadi te asti vṛṣe vāṃchā datveto anyad yathepsitaṃ । gṛhe vrataṃ caraty evaṃ sukhena puṇyam arjaya ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sarvatra te śubhaṃ bhavet । sarvadā durgatiṃ naiva yāyāt sadā tu sadgatiṃ ।। evaṃ matvātmaje śrutvā saddharmaṃ saugatoditaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā gṛhe vrataṃ sukhaṃ cara ।।
etatpuṇyaviśuddhā tvaṃ sarvadā śubhabhāvinī । kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti mātrā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā muktātmajāpi sā । utthāyāśruvirukṣā yayau śokālaye śanaiḥ ।।
tatra śayyātalāsīnā muktādānacintayā । saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau dhyānasamāhitā ।। tatra taddhyānasaṃmūḍhā nidrāsuptendriyāpi sā । tam eva śrīghanaṃ smṛtvā tasthau niścaritāśayāḥ ।।
tām evāṃ saṃsthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ । svapna iva samābhāṣya muktām evaṃ vyabodhayat ।। vatse mātra viṣīda tvaṃ pradeyeyaṃ kajāpi te । pradīyatāṃ samuddhṛtya punaḥ prādurbhaviṣyati ।।
iti saṃbhāṣitaṃ śrutvā svapne iva samutthitā । sā muktā vismayākrāntacittā tasthau suniśalā ।। tataḥ sā taṃ jagannāthaṃ smṛtvā taccintayākulā । kim etat satyam evaṃ syād iti jñātuṃ samaichata ।।
tataḥ sā svayam uddhṛtya svaśiraḥsthāṃ svapāṇinā । muktāmālāṃ mudālokya tāṃ śāstre samakalpayat ।। tato anaṃtaram evaṃ sā muktāmālābhiśobhitā । tasyāḥ śirasamubhūtā rarāja tatsamānikā ।।
tāṃ samālokya sā muktā kanyātivismayānvitā । sahasā purato gatvā mātur evaṃ nyavedayat ।। mātar adya munīndrasya kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ pūryyeta me tathā dhruvaṃ ।।
ity uktvā sā mudā muktā samuddhṛtāṃ śiroruhāṃ । ye ubhe darśayitvāgre mātur evam abhāṣata ।। mātar ahaṃ vipannāśā śayyā talasamāśritā । saṃbuddhaṃ manasā dhyātvā tiṣṭhāmi dānaciṃtayā ।।
yadā me dhyānasuptāyā hṛdi nidropasarpate । tadaivaṃ sarvanāthena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā ।। pradeyeyaṃ śirojātā muktāmālā tvayā mudā । punaḥ prādurbhaved bhūyo apy etatsamānikā dhruvaṃ ।।
iti śrutvā prabuddhāhaṃ kim etat sūnṛtaṃ bhavet । iti kṛtvā samuddhṛtya paśyāmīmāṃ pramoditā ।। tato anaṃtaram evaṃ me śirasyaitatsamānikā । muktāmālā samudbhūtā dṛśyatām iyam ambike ।।
ity uktvā sā sutā muktā tasyā mātuḥ puro mudā । muktāṃ mālāṃ upasthāpya darśayanty evam āha ca ।। imāṃ mātur jagacchāstre mudā saṃkalpayāmy ahaṃ । tad enāṃ trijagacchāstre saṃpradātuṃ vrajeya hi ।।
iti putryā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā jananī mudā । tāṃ muktāsrajam ālokya tac chirojāṃ ca harṣitā ।। muhur muhuḥ samīkṣantī tāṃ sutām evam abravīt । dhanyāsi bhadrikā putri tvayā yathā samīhitaṃ ।।
tathā te siddhyate nūnaṃ saṃbuddhasyānubhāvātaḥ । tad imāṃ tvaṃ samādāyā yathā saṃkalpitaṃ tvayā ।। tathā tasmai munīndrāya prābhyarcya dātum arhasi । tathā te aṅgīkṛtaṃ putri tat satyaṃ setsyate dhruvaṃ ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś ca sarvadā sadgatiṃ vrajeḥ । iti matvā jagacchāstur upahṛtya bhajādarāt ।। tathā cāsmai dvijāyaivam ādāya dātum arhati । tathā te aṅgī kṛte siddhe sarvatra maṃgalaṃ bhavet ।।
saphalaṃ mānuṣe janma sadā ca sadgatau sthitiḥ ।। iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā pratisaṃmoditāśayā । sā tatheti pratiśrutya tathā kartuṃ samaichata ।। tathā saitatpravṛttāṃtaṃ bharttur agre nyavedayat ।
śrutvā bharttāpi puṣyaḥ samuditābhyanvamodata ।। tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāṃ jetakāśrame । vihāre bhagavān so arhan vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tatra sa trijagacchāstā bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan ।
sarvasatvasahitārthena dharmam ādeṣṭum ārabhat ।। tadā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve śrāvakāś cailakādayaḥ । bhikṣuṇyo vratinaś cāpi bodhisatvagaṇā api ।। upāsakagaṇāś cāpi tathā copāsikā api ।
sarve te samupāśritya samātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tathā śakrādayo devā brahmādyā brahmacāriṇaḥ । dānavā lokapālāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।। rākṣasā garuḍā nāgāḥ siddhavidyādharādayaḥ ।
yatayo yoginaś cāpi nirgranthās tīrthikā api ।। ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāś cāpi tapaśvino maharddhikāḥ । rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyā rājakumārakāḥ ।। śreṣṭhino maṃtriṇo amātyā gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ ।
vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca paurikāḥ śilpino api ca ।। grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathānyaddeśavāsinaḥ । sarve te samupāgatya dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā ।। natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ । tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।।
tat saddharmaṃ samākarṇya sarve lokāḥ [prabodhikāh] prabodhitāḥ । sarvasatvahitārtheṣu babhūvuḥ bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। tadā sā kanyakā muktā sakhībhiḥ saha moditā[ḥ] । muktāmālāṃ samādāya dharmaṃ śrotum upācarat ।।
tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā natvā sā sāṃjalir mudā । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tasya śāstuḥ purogatā ।। tatrāgre tām upasthapya muktāmālāṃ kṛtāṃjaliḥ । pādau natvā prasannāsyā dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayat ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasyā dṛṣṭvāśayaṃ viśuddhitaṃ । āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat ।। tat saddharmaṃ samākarṇya sā muktā paribodhitā । dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya babhūva bodhivāñchinī ।।
tatra sā kanyakā muktā satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ । hitvā jñānāsinā śrotaāpattiphalam āyayau ।। tataḥ sā bhadrikā muktā dṛṣṭasatyā pramoditā । sāṃjaliś caraṇau śāstur natvā svagṛham āyayau ।।
tataḥ sā ca samādāya muktāmālaṃ svamūrddhajaṃ । suprasannāśayā tasmai dvijāya pradadau mudā ।। tāṃ muktāsrajam ādāya brāhmaṇaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ । tasyai bhadrāśiṣaṃ datvā sahasā svagṛhe avrajat ।।
tathā sā muditā gatvā sarvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā śubhadharme samācarat ।। tadā tasyā guṇāñ chrutvā bahavaḥ kāmarāgiṇaḥ । saratnaprābhṛtaṃ datvā tāṃ prārthayitum īchire ।।
kumārā bhurbhujā tasyāḥ pitaraṃ puṣyam ādarāt । svasvadūtaiḥ saratnāni datvā saṃprārthayan mudā ।। tathā dvijakumārāś ca maṃtriputrāś ca kāminaḥ । vaiśyaputrās tathānye na dhanino vaṇigātmajāḥ ।।
sārthavāhasutāś cāpi tathā śilpisutā api । mahājanasutāś caivam anye api kāmamohitāḥ ।। sarve te tāṃ subhadrāṃgīṃ muktāṃ muktābhyalaṃkṛtāṃ । dṛṣṭvā rāgāgnisaṃtaptās tanmukhāmṛtavāṃchinaḥ ।।
savastrālaṃkāraratnāni datva dūtaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak । tasyās taṃ janakaṃ puṣyaṃ prārthayann evam ādarāt ।। tathā taiḥ prārthyamāno asau puṣyo dūtaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak । tad dattaṃ prābhṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthau taṃ kṣubhitāśayaḥ ।।
tata utthāya puṣyaḥ sa śokāgāre viṣaṇṇadhīḥ । gatvā śayyātalāsīno manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। hāre duḥkhaṃ prajātaṃ me kiṃ kariṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ । ekaiva duhitā me asti yācakā bahavo api me ।।
yady ekasmai pradāsyāmi sarve anye syur mama dviṣaḥ । atrāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi yad upāyaṃ na manyate ।। iti cintāviṣaṇṇāsyas tasthau mohaviṣārditaḥ ।। tatraivaṃ saṃsthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā janakaṃ taṃ samohitaṃ ।
sametya sātmajā muktā natvaivaṃ paryapṛchata ।। tāta kiṃ te mano duḥkhaṃ yad evaṃ tiṣṭhase adhumā । tat satyaṃ samupākhyā prabodhayātmajām imāṃ ।। iti saṃprārthite putryā tayā sa janakaḥ sudhīḥ ।
taṃ muktāṃ svātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā sucirād evam abravīt ।। ayi putri subhadrāṃgī kim atrāhaṃ vadeya hi । yat tvam ekā sutā me asti yācakā bahavās tava ।। yady ekasmai pradāsyāmi tvām ekaṃ divyasuṃdarīṃ ।
te sarve anye bhaveyur me śatravo hy apakāriṇaḥ ।। iti cintāvidagdhātmā tiṣṭhāmy evaṃ hi nānyathā । tad upāyaṃ na paśyāmi yato me jāyate bhayaṃ ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sā muktā duhitā punaḥ ।
janakaṃ taṃ samālokya bodhayanty evam abravīt ।। nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta saṃbuddhaśāsane gatā । pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣyāmi śubhāṃ cariṃ ।। iti me niścitaṃ cittam anyathā na karomi hi ।
tad atra mā viṣīda tvaṃ tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।। iti putryā tathākhyātaṃ sa puṣyo janakaḥ sudhīḥ । svātmajāṃ tāṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।। ayi putri kathaṃ tāvat pravrajyāṃ carituṃ saheḥ ।
tvaṃ hi bālā subhadrāṅgī kumārī sukhamedhinī ।। tasmād yāvat kumārī tvaṃ tāvad gehe samāśritā । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caropāsakasaṃvaraṃ ।। iti pitryoditaṃ śrutvā sā muktā duhitā sudhīḥ ।
tathā hīti pratiśrutya prabodhitānvamoditaḥ ।। tathā sā bhadrikā muktā śuddhaśīlā subhāvinī । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cere upāsikāvrataṃ ।। yadā sā yauvanī kāṃtā muktā muktātiśobhitā ।
tadā kaniṣṭhaputreṇa dṛṣṭānāthānnasaṃstṛtaḥ ।। tataḥ so anāthabhṛtputraḥ supriyākhyo abhimoditaḥ । kāmarāgāgnisaṃtapto rogī vābhūd viṣaṇṇadhīḥ ।। taṃ putraṃ kāmarāgārttaṃ dṛṣṭvā so anāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।
tan nimittaṃ samālokya samāśvāsyaivam abravīt ।। bho putraivaṃ kim arthe tvaṃ rogīva tiṣṭhase adhunā । tad vadasva mamāgre api yad ichati manas tava ।। iti pitroditam śrutvā supriyaḥ sa viniḥśvasan ।
pitaraṃ taṃ samālokya śanair evam abhāṣata ।। tāta yo asau subhadrāṅgī muktā muktātiśobhitā । dṛṣṭvā mayānurūpeti mano me harate api sā ।। tadabhilāṣarāgāgnidāhasaṃtoṣitaṃ manaḥ ।
tad rāgāgniśamopāyaṃ kartum arhati me adhunā ।। iti putroditaṃ śrutvā so anāthapiṇḍadaḥ pitā । putrasya prāṇarakṣārthaṃ yācituṃ tāṃ samaihata ।। tataḥ sa dūtam āhūya pura evam abhāṣata ।
sādho gacha gṛhasthasya puṣyasyaiva paro vada ।। sādho tad duhitā bhadrā tad dīyatāṃ sutāya me । evaṃ kṛte api saṃbaṃdhaṃ yāvajjīvaṃ sukhāya nau ।। ity uktvā tasya puṣyasya tāṃ muktākhyāṃ subhāvinīṃ ।
prārthayitvā sutāyāsmai dātuṃ me arhati sarvathā ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tatheti pratibhāṣya saḥ । dūtaḥ prābhṛtam ādāya puṣyasya samupācarat ।। tatra tasya puraḥ sthāpya prābhṛtaṃ saṃvinodayan ।
yathānāthabhṛtādiṣṭaṃ tathā sarvaṃ nyavedayat ।। tad uktaṃ sarvam ākarṇya sa puṣyaḥ paribodhitaḥ । muktāṃ tāṃ svātmajāṃ putrīṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। ayi priyātmaje putri tvam anāthabhṛtā satā ।
supriyāya svaputrāya prārthitā tvaṃ prasīda tat ।। iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā muktā sā duhitā satī । pitaraṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata ।। nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatā ।
pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣyāmi śubhāṃ carīṃ ।। iti putryoditaṃ śrutvā sa puṣyo abhihatāśayaḥ । duhitāṃ tāṃ ciraṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। he sute katham eva tvaṃ vadethāḥ kiṃ na manyase ।
yad asau gṛhabhṛn nāthas tad vacaḥ śrūyate na kaiḥ ।। tad yāvad yauvanī bhūtā tāvad bharttā sahānugāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara vrataṃ gṛhe sukhaṃ ।। yadā vṛddhā vyavasthāsyai tadā tvaṃ saugatāśrame ।
pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā pracarasva śubhāṃ carīṃ ।। iti pitrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sā duhitā sudhīḥ । pitro vākyaṃ kathaṃ laṃghyam iti matvaivam abravīt ।। nāhaṃ kāmarthinī tāta saddharmasādhanārthinī ।
tathāpi tvadvaco alaṃghyam iti śroṣyāmi te vacaḥ ।। yadi me samayaṃ dhṛtvā satyavākyaṃ dadāti me । vṛṇuyāṃ taṃ patiṃ nanum iti me vacanaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। iti putryoditaṃ śrutva sa puṣyaḥ paribodhitaḥ ।
etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ dūtasyāgre nyavedayat ।। dūtāpi tat pravṛttāṃtaṃ śrutvā tatheti satvarāḥ । anāthapiṇḍadasyāgre vistareṇa nyavedayat ।। so anāthapiṇḍadaś cāpi śrutvā sa pratimoditaḥ ।
sarvam etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ putrasyāgre nyavedayat ।। etat pitrā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa supriyaḥ sudhīḥ । tathā hīti pratijñāya dūtasyāgre nyavedayat ।। dūtaś ca tadvacaḥ śrutvā puṣyasya purato gataḥ ।
sarvam etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ vistareṇa nyavedayat ।। puṣyo api tat samākhyātaṃ śrutvā patnyāḥ puro avadat । sāpi taj jananī śrutvā putryā agre nyavedayat ।। tan mātrā samupādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sā duhitā satī ।
tathā hīti pratiśrutya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat ।। tataḥ sa janakaḥ puṣyo matvā putryādhivāsitaṃ । tasyā vivāhasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat ।। tataḥ sa janakaḥ puṣyo apy anāthapiṇḍadātmajaṃ ।
supriyaṃ taṃ samānīya satkṛtya samamānayat ।। tatas tām ātmajāṃ muktāṃ supriyāya subhāvine । saṃkalpya pradadau puṣyo janakaḥ sa yathāvidhiḥ ।। tataḥ sa supriyo bharttā tāṃmuktāṃ ramaṇīṃ priyāṃ ।
bhāryāṃ svagṛhe ānīya reme bhuktvā yathāsukhaṃ ।। evaṃ sā bhāvinī muktā kāñcit kālaṃ gṛhe mudā । bharttrā saha yathākāmaṃ bhuktvā reme pramoditā ।। tatas tau daṃpatī dehe vṛddhatva samupākrame । pitroḥ pādān praṇatvaivaṃ prārthayataṃ samādarāt ।।
pitarau yat kṛtaṃ satyam āvābhyāṃ tat susiddhaye । pūrayituṃ samichāvas tad ājñāṃ dātum arhatha ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tābhyāṃ śrutvā pitā sa sā prasūḥ । dṛṣṭvā tau daṃpatī śrāddhāyuktāv evaṃ samūcatuḥ ।।
yadi vāṃ vidyate vāṃchā carituṃ saugataṃ vrataṃ । tat satyapūraye tasmāt pracarata samāhitau ।। iti tābhyām anujñāte daṃpatī tau pramoditau । pitroḥ pādān praṇatvaiva pratasthuḥ sahasā gṛhāt ।।
tatas tau jetakodyāne vihāre samupāgatau । bhagavantaṃ tam ānamya pravrajyāṃ samayācatāṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña vijānāti yad āvayoḥ । satyaṃ tat pūrayiṣyāvas tat pravrajyāṃ dadātu vāṃ ।।
iti saṃprārthite tābhyaṃ bhagavāṃ dakṣapāṇinā । spṛṣṭvā tac chirasor dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। evaṃ caratam ādāya pravrajyāvratam uttamaṃ । svaparātmahitārtheṣu brahmacaryaṃ samāhitau ।।
ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa tāv ubhāv api muṃḍitau । khikkhirīpātravibhrāṇau ca bhartuś cīvarāvṛtau ।। tato avidyāgaṇaṃ bhitvā prāptavidyāviśāradau । sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā sākṣād arhatvam āvatuḥ ।।
tatas tau vimalātmānau priśuddhatrimaṇḍalau । jitendriyāū samācārau nirvikalpau niraṃjanau ।। sarveṣām api lokānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ । pūjyau mānyau ca vaṃdyau tāv abhūtaṃ brahmacāriṇau ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayoddhatamānasā । bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ ।। bhagavan kiṃ kṛtaṃ karma purābhyāṃ sukṛtaṃ kuha । tat sarvaṃ samupādiśya sarvān naḥ paribodhaya ।।
iti saṃprārthite sarvair bhikṣubhiḥ sa munīśvaraḥ । sarvāṃs tāṃ śrāvakān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ karma yad ābhyāṃ prakṛtaṃ purā । tat sarvaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cābhyanumodata ।।
tad yathābhūt purā śāstā kāśyapākhyamunīśvaraḥ । sarvajño arhaṃ jagannātho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। bhagavān sa mṛgāraṇye vārāṇasyāṃ jinārame । sarvasatvahitārthena vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।।
tadā tatra mahān sādhuḥ śrīmāñ chrīdopamaḥ sudhīḥ । sadā tasya munīndrasya saddharmaśrāvako abhajat ।। tataḥ sa buddhimān dātā sarvalokahitārthataḥ । chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ tatra yācitvā paṃcavārṣikaṃ ।।
kāśyapasya munīndrasya sasaṃghaya niraṃtaraṃ । sapūjābhojanair nityam upasthātuṃ samaichata ।। tataḥ sa nṛpater ājñāṃ samāsādya pramoditaḥ । hastiskandhe samāruhya ghaṇṭāvādyaṃ pravādayan ।।
sarvatra viṣaye tatra vārāṇasyāḥ samaṃtataḥ । chaṃdakabhikṣaṇaṃ sārddhaṃ yācituṃ prācaraj janaiḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā sārthavāhasya bhāryā bhadrā subhāvinī । sā tasyai śiraso mucya muktāhāraṃ dadau mudā ।।
tatas tasyāḥ śiraskaṃ tanmuktāhāravyapohitaṃ । dṣṭvā sa vismito hāryyaṃ tām eva paryapṛchata ।। kvāsau bhadre śirasthas te muktāhāro na vidyate । kasyai dattas tvayā kena hṛto vā tad vadasva me ।।
iti bhartrābhipṛṣṭe sā muditā racitāṃjaliḥ । bharttāraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ vinodayitum abravīt ।। āryaputra prasīdātra mā kṛthā roṣatām iha । yan mayā śraddhayā dattaś chaṃdakabhikṣaṇe apy asau ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhas tataś caran । niṣkrīya bahumūlyena tasyai patnyai dadau punaḥ ।। taṃ muktāhāram ālokya sārthabhṛtaḥ priyāpi sā । saṃpradattaṃ mayā śāstu iti taṃ nāgrahīd api ।।
tataḥ sa sārthabhṛt svāmī tāṃ bhāryāṃ ramaṇīṃ priyāṃ । snehārdacakṣuṣā dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bahumūlyena bhadre yaṃ mayā krītas tu dīyate । tat kasmān nechasīdaṃ mad grahītuṃ katham eva hi ।।
iti bhartroditam śrutvā sā dattaṃ svāminā punaḥ । taṃ muktāhāram ādāya bharttuś cittaṃ vyanodayat ।। tataḥ sā viṣayāraktā saddharmaguṇavāṃchinī । taṃ saṃpūjāṃgam ādāya yayau śāstur mudāśrame ।।
tatraitad gandhakuṭyāṃ sā kṛtvā sugaṃdhilepanaṃ । supuṣpaiś ca samākīryya natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ ।। tataḥ sā muditā tasya kāśyapasya jagadguroḥ । muktāhāraṃ puraḥ kṣiptvā praṇanāma kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।।
tato buddhānubhavena muktāhāraḥ sa tat kṣaṇaṃ । tasya śāstuḥ śiraḥ saṃstho rarāja saṃprabhāsayan ।। tad dṛṣṭvā sā suprasannāsyāḥ saṃbodhiguṇalālasāḥ । śāstuḥ pādau praṇatvaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ vyadhān mudā ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena śāstāram īdṛśaṃ jinaṃ । ārāgyedṛgguṇānāṃ ca lābhī syāṃ sarvathā bhave ।। evaṃ sā bhāvinī kāṃtā tasya śāstu jagadguroḥ । praṇidhānaṃ sadā kṛtvā prabheje saṃprasāditā ।।
yo asau sārthapater bhāryā mukteyaṃ sā subhāvinī । manyatām iti yuṣmābhir nānyathā tu hi bhikṣavaḥ ।। yad anayā tadā tasya kāśyapasya jagadguroḥ । pūjāṅgaiḥ śraddhayābhyarcya muktāhāraḥ praḍhokitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena jāteyaṃ sukule adhunā ।
śirasy asyāś ca saṃrūḍho muktāmālā sahodbhavā ।। yathānayā kṛtaṃ tatra praṇidhānaṃ tathā adhunā । māṃ śāstāram āgamya sākṣād arhatvam āpyate ।। evaṃ hi yat kṛtaṃ yena tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ ।
abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma na cānyathā kvacit ।। evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāṃchibhiḥ । saddharmaṃ samupāśritya caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। śubhe caranti ye nityaṃ na te gachaṃti durgatīṃ ।
sadgatim eva saṃyānti bodhiṃ ca samavāpnuyuḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sāṃghikā api । sarve tatheti vijñapya prābhyanaṃdan prabodhitāḥ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ hi me śāstrā śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate ।
śrutvāpy evaṃ tathā rājaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā ।। prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratisthāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। tathā hi te sadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
kramād bodhiṃ ca saṃprāpya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathā hīti pratijñapya prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। muktāvadānaṃ manujā idaṃ ye śṛṇvaṃti ye cāpi niśāmayanti ।
te sarva evaṃ sukhitā śubhāni kṛtvā prayānti sugatālayan te ।। athāśoko mahīndro asau kṛtāṃjaliḥ pramoditaḥ । upaguptaṃ tam arhantaṃ natvaivaṃ punar abravīt ।। bhadanta ye mahāsatvā bodhisatvā yathepsitaṃ ।
sarvārthibhyaḥ pradatvaivaṃ dānaṃ kurvanti sarvadā ।। teṣām evaṃ pradatte api tad dravyaṃ kṣīyate na hi । punarvṛddhitamaṃ yāti tat kathaṃ me samādiśa ।। katamadvratapuṇyasya prabhāvāc chrīḥ pravarddhate ।
tad vrataṃ me bhavāñ chāstā samyag ādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so arhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ । upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi loke dharmābhivṛddhaye ।। ye satyasamādhānāḥ śuddhaśīlāḥ śubhārthinaḥ । vasudhārāmahādevyāś caranti vratam uttamaṃ ।। teṣāṃ na kṣīyate dravyaṃ pradatte api sadā gṛhe ।
pravṛddhitaram eva syād vasudhārānubhāvataḥ ।। tadyathāsīt purā buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ । sarvajño arhañ jagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ ।। bhagavānn ekadā tatra vārāṇasyāḥ purāntike ।
mṛgadave jināvāse vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।। tadā tad dharmapīyūṣaṃ pātuṃ śakrādayo amarāḥ । brahmādi brāhmaṇāś cāpi sarve lokādhipā api ।। siddhā vidyādharā daityā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ ।
rākṣasā garuḍā nāgās tathānye api samāgatāḥ ।। yatayo yoginaś cāpi tīrthikāś ca tapaśvinaḥ । nirgranthā vītarāgāś ca munayo brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। evam anye api lokāḥ saṃbuddhadharmavāṃchinaḥ ।
tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ mudā tatra samāgatāḥ ।। tatpurādhipatī rājā viśvabhadrābhidho mahān । tasya bhāryā priyādevī ratnamālābhidhā satī ।। tadātmajakumārāṃśaḥ sūryaprabhābhidhaḥ kṛtī ।
tadātmajā ramākārā kumārī vimalābhidhā ।। anye apy antarjanāś cāpi sa jñātimitravāṃdhavāḥ । purohitādayaś cāpi vedavijñā dvijātayaḥ ।। vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo amātyā gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ ।
vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpinaś cāpi paurikāḥ ।। grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathā kārpaṭikā api । evam anye api lokāś ca sarve te samupāgatāḥ ।। tatretya taṃ sabhāsīnaṃ sarvasaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ । saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā muditāḥ samupācaran ।।
tatra sarve api te lokāḥ samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ । tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praṇatvā taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ । puraskṛtya samādhāya samupatasthur ādritā ।।
atha sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān । bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ ।। tat saddharmaṃ samākarṇya sarvalokāḥ prabodhitāḥ । bodhicittaṃ samāsādya bhavaṃti bodhicāriṇaḥ ।।
āsīt tat samaye tatra vārāṇasyāṃ gṛhādhipaḥ । dharmadhvajābhidhaḥ śreṣṭhī dātā sādhur mahājanaḥ ।। tasya bhāryā priyā kāntā śāntamatīti viśrutā । putrāś ca bahavas tasya sutāś cāpy abhavaṃs tathā ।।
pautrāḥ karmakarāḥ preśyā dāsī dāsajanā api । aneke parivārāś ca vaṃdhumitrasuhṛjjanāḥ ।। sarve te poṣitās tena saṃbhṛtya paripālitāḥ । poṣaṇīyā gṛhasthasya sarve hi samupāśritāḥ ।।
arthino api sadā tasya gṛhe anekasamāgatā । śubhāśīrvacanair nityaṃ mahotsāhaṃ pracakrire ।। so api dharmadhvajo dātā tān sarvān arthino janān । yathābhilaṣitair dravyais toṣayitvābhyamodayat ।।
evaṃ pradadatas tasya kramāt saṃpat kṣayaṃ gatā । tad dṛṣṭvā sa gṛhī dānavighnaśaṃkārdito abhavat ।। tataḥ śokālaye sthitvā tat saṃpatkṣīyaciṃtayā । viniśvasan viṣaṇṇātmā tasthau bhogyanirutsahaḥ ।।
tatas tasya priyā bhāryā śāntamatī vicakṣaṇā । bharttāraṃ taṃ viṣaṇṇāsyaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ paryapṛchata ।। svāminn evaṃ kim ālokya tiṣṭhase duḥkhaciṃtayā । yat te atra jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad vadasva manogataṃ ।।
iṭi bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa bharttābhiviniśvasan । tāṃ bhāryāṃ supriyāṃ kāṃtāṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। ayi priye mahad duḥkhaṃ hṛdi me jāyate adhunā । yat saṃpadaḥ parikṣīṇā āyā me atra na vidyate ।।
putrapautrādayo aneke bahayo me kuṭumbinaḥ । karmakarādayo bhṛtyā dāsīdāsādayo janāḥ ।। anye api bahavaḥ preṣyāḥ pālanīyā divāniśaṃ । arthino yācakāś ca bahavo nityam āgatāḥ ।
kathaṃ tāns toṣayiṣyāmi kramāt kṣīṇā hi saṃpadaḥ ।। nūnaṃ me yācakāḥ sarve śūnyahastā gṛhād ataḥ । parikhinnavibhinnāsyā vrajiṣyanti nirāśayāḥ ।। iti cintāviṣaṇṇe me hṛdi duḥkhaṃ prajāyate ।
tad duḥkhānalasaṃtaptas tiṣṭhāmy evaṃ vimohitaḥ ।। kiṃ hi dānamahotsāhaṃ vinā gehe sukhaṃ bhavet । paśuvat kevalaṃ bhuktvā kiṃ sāraṃ satsukhaṃ vinā ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā sātha śāntamatī satī ।
bharttāraṃ taṃ samāśvāsya bodhayanty evam abravīt ।। āryaputra kim atrāpi jātā te hṛdi duḥkhatā । kiṃ viṣādenā siddhyeta kevalaṃ dahyate manaḥ ।। avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavanti mahatām api ।
tad viṣādaṃ parityajya cara śubhe samāhitaḥ ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa bharttābhiviniḥśvasan । tāṃ bhāryāṃ supriyāṃ kāṃtāṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। ayi priye śubhaṃ kāryyaṃ nābhijānāmi sanmate ।
tad upāyaṃ samākhyāya māṃ bodhayitum arhati ।। iti bharttroditam śrutvā sā ca śāṃtamatī satī । bharttāraṃ taṃ samāśvāsya prabodhayitum abravīt ।। āryaputra mahāsādho tad upāyaṃ prakathyate ।
kauśāṃvyāṃ ghoṣirārāme śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ ।। sarvajñaḥ sugato buddho hīnadīnānukaṃpakaḥ । sarvavidyākalābhijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। mārajil lokavin nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṇḍitaḥ ।। vyāma prabhābhibhāsvaṃtaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ । jaṃgamam iva ratnābhaṃ saumyaṃ samaṃtabhadrakaṃ ।। sarvasatvahitārthena vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।
tatra gatvā praṇatvā tat taṃ buddhaṃ śṛṇutādarāt ।। tadā sa bhagavān buddhas tad upāyaṃ samādiśet ।। iti bhāryāsamādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā dharmadhvajo api saḥ । tatheti paribhāṣitvā sa bharttā saṃpramoditaḥ ।।
tadā sa dharmadhvajo bhāryaṃ velām ādāya prācarat । tato vihāre gatvā sa bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ । dūrataḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā ekasthāne samāśrayat ।। tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ dharmadhvajaduḥkhitaṃ ।
jānann apy āgataṃ kāmaṃ dharmadhvaje samabravīt ।। sādho kasmād ihāgatya tiṣṭhase tat samādiśa । iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā dharmadhvajo api saḥ ।। kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā bhagavaṃtam evam abravīt ।
bhagavan yad vijānīyā nānya gacchāmi me vibho । tvayi mama kāryyam eka pṛchāmīti vyacintayat ।। tadyathā me mahāsaṃpat kṣīṇaṃ yāti daridratāṃ । punar vṛddhigataṃ dravyaṃ tat kathaṃ me samādiśa ।।
katamad vratapuṇyasya prabhāvāc chrī pravarddhate । tad vrataṃ me bhavāñ chāstā samyag ādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sa bhagavān mudā । dharmadhvajaṃ tam āmaṃtrya saṃpaśyann evam abravīt ।।
sādhu śṛṇu samādhāya tad vidhiṃ saṃpravakṣyate । tac chrutvā te prabodhitvā samācara vidhānataḥ ।। vasudhārāvrataṃ samyak yathā śrutaṃ mayā purā । vajradharābdhigaṃbhīranirghoṣeṇopadeśitaṃ ।।
tathāthā prathamaṃ tāvac chuddhabhūmau parigrahaṃ । kṛtvā mṛdgomayāmbhobhiḥ saṃlipya paryaśobhayet ।। tataḥ sadgurum ārādhya natvā kṛtāṃjalir mudā । satkṛtya prārthayed evaṃ vasudhārāvrataṃ varaṃ ।।
tataḥ sa guruṇā sārddhaṃ snātvā tīrthe viśuddhadhīḥ । śuddhavastrāvṛtāḥ śuddhacitto brahmavihārikaḥ ।। māse bhādrapade kṛṣṇapakṣe māghe api vā punaḥ । tṛtīyāyāṃ tithau devīṃ samāvāhya vrataṃ caret ।।
pūrvasmin divase vighnān kīlayet sarvadiksthitān । tatra subhūtale sūtraṃ pātayitvā yathāvidhi ।। varttayen maṃḍalaṃ devyāḥ sagaṇapratimaṇḍitaṃ ।। evaṃ tan maṃḍalaṃ kṛtvā saptavrīhisuveṣṭitaṃ ।
tato aṣṭayakṣaṇīcihnaṃ śobhitaiḥ kalaśair vṛtaṃ ।। sapatākadhvajachatravitānaiḥ parimaṇḍitaṃ । kṛtvā tan maṇḍalaṃ vajrī pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi ।। vicitrapuṣpamālābhiḥ pradīpaiḥ saṃprabhojvalaiḥ ।
saurabhyadhūpanaiś cāpi samabhyarcyābhiśobhayet ।। tatas tan maṇḍale devī sagaṇāṃ parisaṃsmaran । dhyātvā jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tad rātrīṃ vyatilaṃghayet ।। tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya tīrthe snātvā suśuddhadhīḥ ।
śucivastrāvṛte paṃcagavyaiḥ svāṃgaṃ vyaśodhayet ।। tataḥ sa sadguruṃ natvā tadājñāṃ śirasāvahan । uttarābhimukhaḥ śuddha āsane samupāśrayet ।। tatas tāvad guruṃ natvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
maṃḍale sagaṇāṃ devīṃ dhyātvāvāhya samarcayet ।। tato arahaṃ saṃpradatvāgre praṇatvā sāṃjalir mudā । japastotrādikaṃ kṛtvā kuryāc ca pāpadeśanāṃ ।। puṇyānumodanāṃ kṛtvā prārthayed bodhisaṃvaraṃ ।।
tataḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvā natvāstāṃgaiś ca sāṃjaliḥ । tataḥ pītamayaṃ sūtram ṣoḍaśabhedavarttitaṃ । śuddhaṃ gurur maṃtreṇa śodhayet ।। tatas tad vratasūtraṃ sa sagurur dhāraṇīṃ pathan ।
tasmai śiṣyāya rakṣyārthaṃ datvābhiṣekam arppayet ।। tad vrataṃ sūtram ādāya vaṃdhitvā svakare vratī । yāvad vratasamāptaṃ na tāvat tat sūtram ādharet ।। tataḥ vratī yathāśakti gurave dānadakṣiṇaṃ । datvāṣṭāṅgapraṇāmeṇa natvā samabhitoṣayet ।।
tataḥ paṃcāmṛtair yuktaṃ baliṃ kṣīrodanābharaṃ । sa yakṣayakṣaṇīlokapālebhyaḥ saṃpradāpayet ।। tataḥ kṣamārthanaṃ kṛtvā guruṇā saha pālanaṃ । tṛtīyapraharāgre ahneḥ kuryāt sa yavapūrakaiḥ ।।
pālanāṃte punaḥ snātvā tāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ smaran । paṭhañ chrīdhāraṇīm rātrī pūjayec ca yathāvidhi ।। evaṃ nityaṃ catuḥsaṃdhyaṃ pūjayec chrīvasuṃdharāṃ । yāvajjīvaṃ yathāsaktau varṣaikaṃ vā tathā caret ।।
ṣaṇmāsaṃ māsam ekaṃ ca yathāśakti vrataṃ caret । navasaptadināny evaṃ paṃcatrīṇi dināny api ।। aho rātraṃ tathaikaṃ vā vāram ekaṃ vrataṃ caret । tatpare dyur dine prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāśayo vratī ।
tathā tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīṃ samarcayed yathāvidhi ।। tataś ca guruve abhyarcya vastrālaṃkārabhūgṛhaṃ । sadakṣiṇāṃ pradatvaivaṃ svātmānaṃ ca samarppayet ।। tataḥ sa gurur ādāya tasmai śiṣyāya sāśiṣaṃ ।
datvā kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā tan maṇḍalaṃ visarjayet ।। tatas tad raja ādāya bhaṇḍāgāre abhigopitaṃ । saṃnidhāya sadā nityam abhyarcya sādaraṃ bhajet ।। tad rajaḥśeṣanirmālyaṃ nadyāṃ nāgān yathāvidhi ।
samabhyarcya samarppitvā sarvaṃ jale pravāhayet ।। tatas taj jalam ādāya gṛhe gatvā mahotsavaiḥ । taj jalair maṇḍalāgārakoṣṭhe sarvatra siṃcayet ।। tatas tad vratapūrṇārthaṃ rātrau devīṃ kumārikāṃ ।
yathāvidhi samāvāhya samabhyarcyābhyatoṣayet ।। satgurupramukhān sarvān yogino yoginīr api । samabhyarcya yathākāmaṃ bhojanaiḥ saṃpratoṣayet ।। tatas taṃ sagaṇaṃ cakraṃ natvā vratī sa sāṃjaliḥ ।
kṣamāpya vinayaṃ kṛtvā prārthayec chrīsamṛddhitāṃ ।। tatas tat sagaṇaṃ cakraṃ tadbhaktyā saṃpratoṣitaṃ । tasmai vratine dadyāt susaṃpattisubhāṣitaṃ ।। tatas tasya gṛhe devī vasudhārā samāśritā ।
sarvadravyābhisaṃpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhet sadā sthirā ।। tatas tad dravyam ādāya sarvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । saṃpradatvā yathākāmaṃ bhuktvā bhavaṃ sukhaṃ caret ।। evaṃ gṛhapate matvā vasudhārāvrataṃ mahat ।
yathāvidhi samādāya gṛhe cara samādarāt ।। tatas te sarvadā gehe maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ । bhavet sāpi mahādevī sagaṇā nivaset sthirā ।। tatas te sarvasaṃpattiḥ pravarddhitā śubhānvitā ।
bhavane saṃbhavanty eva na kadācit kṣayaṃ vrajet ।। tatas tvaṃ sarvadā saukhyaṃ bhuktvā datvā yathepsitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā śubhe cara samāhitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sadā tvaṃ sadgatiṃ tataḥ । bodhicaryāṃ caran bodhiṃ prāpya buddhapadaṃ labheḥ ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā dharmadhvajo gṛhī । sa mudā suprasannātmā vrataṃ caritum aichata ।। tataḥ sa mudito natvā sāṃjalis taṃ jagadguruṃ । bhagavantaṃ jagannāthaṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt ।।
bhagavan sarvavic chāstar bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । bhavadājñāṃ śiro dhṛtvā cariṣye aham idaṃ vrataṃ ।। tad bhavāṃ kṛpayā śāstas tad anujñāṃ dadātu me । bhavatātra yathādiṣṭaṃ cariṣye tat tathā khalu ।।
iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ । tasmai devyā mahāvidyāṃ dhāraṇīṃ saṃpaṭhan dadau ।। so api dharmadhvajo natvā sāñjalis taṃ munīśvaraṃ । dhāraṇīṃ tāṃ samādāya saṃpapāṭha pramoditaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa suprasannātmā dharmadhvajaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ jagannāthaṃ praṇatvā svagṛhaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sa svagṛhaprāptaḥ suprasannamukhāmbujaḥ । tāṃ śāṃtamatāṃ bhāryāṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।।
priye dhanyāsi kalyāṇī yat tvayāhaṃ prabodhitaḥ । saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ ratnam āptavān aham āgataḥ ।। tadyathā samupādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇānuśāsinā । tathāvāṃ tad vrataṃ devyāś carevahi samādarāt ।।
iti bhartrā samuddiṣṭe sāpi śāntamatī mudā । bharttāraṃ taṃ samālokya sudṛṣṭyaivam abhāṣata ।। ayi svāmin kathaṃ śāstra samādiṣṭaṃ vadasva me । yathādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tatha carevahi dhruvaṃ ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā bharttā dharmadhvajo atha saḥ । mudā śāṃtamatīṃ bhāryāṃ tāṃ samīkṣyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu bhadre yathādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tathā khalu । yad vrataṃ vasudhārāyās tad vidhiṃ te pravakṣyate ।।
ity ukte svāminā tena sā ca śāntamatī priyā । bharttāraṃ taṃ samālokya muditaivam abhāṣata ।। svāmins tena munīndreṇa yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā bhavān । suvistaraṃ samākhyāya mano me saṃvinodata ।।
ity ukte bhāryayā sātha dharmadhvajaḥ suvistaraṃ । yathādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tathā sarvaṃ nyavedayat ।। tac chrutvā sā prabodhantī śāṃtamaty anumoditā । tathā tasyā mahādevyā vrataṃ caritum aichata ।।
tatas taṃ svāminaṃ natvā sā ca śāntamatī satī । tadvratārambhasāmagrīṃ sādhitum evam abravīt ।। svāmin vrataṃ cariṣyāvo vasulakṣmyā yathāvidhi । sāmagrīṃ sādhayeyāsya tad anujñāṃ pradehi me ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā dharmadhvajaḥ sa moditaḥ । sādhyatāṃ sarvasāmāgrīm iti tāṃ sāṃvyanodayat ।। tataḥ sā muditāḥ sarve sāmagrīṃ sādhayanty api । bharttāraṃ tam upāmaṃtrya darśayanty evam abravīt ।।
sarvaṃ me sādhitaṃ siddhaṃ svāminn atra prasīdatu । tat sadguruṃ samāmaṃtrya vratam ālabdhum arhati ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa dharmadhvaja ādarāt । sadguruṃ samupārādhya natvevaṃ prārthayan mudā ।।
bhadanta śrīvasudhārādevyā vrataṃ carevahi । tasmāt devīṃ samārādhya vratopadeśam ādiśa ।। iti saṃprārthite tena tatheti hi sa sadguruḥ । pratiśrutya yathādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tathācarat ।।
tathā bhādrapade māse kṛṣṇapakṣe sa sadguruḥ । dvitīyāyaṃ tithau tīrthe snātvā suvāsasā sudhīḥ ।। yathāvidhiṃ samārabhya maṃḍalaṃ samavarttayat । tatra tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīṃ pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayat ।।
tat paredyus tritīyāyāṃ susnātaṃ śubhāmbaraṃ । dharmadhvajaṃ sadāraṃ taṃ paṃcagavyair vyaśodhayat ।। tatas tau daṃpatī śāstrā yathādiṣṭaṃ samāhitau । śrutvā tathā samādhāya pracaratu vrataṃ mudā ।।
yathā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ tathā kṛtvā vrataṃ mudā । gaṇacakrādikaṃ sarvaṃ samāpya tau nanandatuḥ ।। tatas tasya gṛhe devīṃ vasudhārā samāśritā । sarvadravyaṃ samāpūryya tasthau sadā prasāditā ।।
tatas tasya gṛhe saṃpad dine pravarddhitā । saratnadhātusadvastraśasyādi dravyajātayaḥ ।। tā evaṃ varddhitā dṛṣṭvā sadāraḥ sa gṛhādhipaḥ । sa vismayo muditotphullavaktrāmbujo abhyanaṃdata ।।
tataḥ sa sarvadārthibhyo datvā dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ bhuktvā śubhe acarat ।। tad dṛṣṭvā tasya gehasya samīpastho dvijottamaḥ । viṣṇudāsābhidho vijño vismayoddhatamānasaḥ ।।
dhīmatīṃ ramaṇīṃ bhāryāṃ suviśuddhāśayāṃ satīṃ । niḥśvasans tāṃ samāmaṃtrya punar evam abhāṣata ।। paśya bhadrasya mitrasya gṛhe saṃpat samṛddhitā । kim anena kṛtaṃ dharmaṃ yenaivaṃ śrīḥ pravarddhitā ।।
kim āvābhyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenaivaṃ no vipat sadā । kim atrāvāṃ kariṣyāvo yena saṃpat pravarddhitā ।। tad upāyaṃ na jānāmi ko me upadiśed dhitaṃ । dhanyās te dhanavaṃtā ye yathākāma sukhāśinaḥ ।।
kiṃ te sadguṇavaṃto api kṛpaṇā ye daridritā । varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ na tv evaṃ jīvitaṃ bhave ।। kiṃ teṣāṃ sadguṇaiś cāpi yeṣāṃ saṃpad gṛhe na hi । dhanavān puruṣo dhīraḥ kulīno nirguṇo api ca । sarve hi dhanināṃ vaśyā paṃḍitāḥ suguṇā api ।। dhanavān nirguṇaś cāpi mānyate guruvaj janaiḥ ।
dhanahīnā na pūjyaṃte paṃḍitā brahmaṇā api ।। dhig me jīvitam evaṃ hi brāhmaṇasyāpi duḥkhinaḥ । varam evādyetan mṛtyur na tv eva cirajīvituṃ ।। kim anenāpi jīvena kevaladuḥkhabhoginā ।
tad atra marttum ichāmi naiva jīveya duḥkhabhāk ।। sarveṣām api jaṃtūnām avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ bhave । tad atra vidyamāno ahaṃ kathaṃ loke careya hi ।। ity evaṃ vilapaṃ vipro viṣṇudāsaḥ sa mohitaḥ ।
galadaśruvirukṣākṣas tasthau muhur viniḥśvasan ।। ity evaṃ vilapantan taṃ dṛṣṭvā sā dhīmatī priyā । bodhayituṃ samāśvāsya bharttāram evam abravīt ।। mā viṣādaṃ kṛthāḥ svāmin dhairyyam ālambya tiṣṭhatu ।
kiṃ kariṣyāvahe hy atra daivāt saṃpan na tau gṛhe ।। tathāpi dhairyyam ālambya yatnaṃ kuru samāhitaḥ । yatnena siddhyate sarvaṃ guṇadravyādi sādhanaṃ ।। tad atrāhaṃ vadiṣyāmi hitārthaṃ te śṛṇu prabho ।
bhāryā hi svāmino bharttur hitārtham abhyanudeśinī ।। yad ayaṃ gṛhabhṛd bharttā dharmadhvajas tava priyaḥ । suhṛn mitraṃ mahāsādhus tad ādarāt sa pṛchyatāṃ ।। yathā tena samādiṣṭaṃ tathaiva krīyatāṃ prabho ।
tatas tasya yathā saṃpat tathāsmākaṃ bhaved api ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā viṣṇudāsaḥ sa tairthikaḥ । bauddhavākye viruddhatvād anichann evam abravīt ।। vayaṃ hi brāhmaṇā bhadre buddhadevī vasuṃdharā ।
tad vidhiṃ vedaśāstreṣu kathitaṃ na kvacid api ।। tat kathaṃ svakulācāraṃ tyaktvānyacharaṇaṃ gatāḥ । bauddhopadeśam āsādya lakṣmyā vrataṃ caremahi ।। ye tyaktvā svakulācāram anyatra śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
vrataṃ caraṃti saṃpattilābhilābhākulāśayāḥ ।। te svadharmaparibhraṣṭā ihāpi kliṣṭabhoginaḥ । rogiṇo duhitātmāno mṛtā yāsyaṃti durgatīṃ ।। iti bhadre na me vāṃchā bauddhadevyā vrate aśubhe ।
varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ nānyadvrataṃ caremahi ।। asmākam api yā devī mahālakṣmī kuleśvarī । tasyā vrataṃ samādhāya caremahi sadādarāt ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī gṛhe aśmākaṃ samāśritā ।
yathābhivāṃchitaṃ dravyaṃ sarvaṃ dadyāt prasāditā ।। iti tasyā mahālakṣmyā vrataṃ carāvahe vayaṃ । tat tad vratasya sāmagrīṃ sādhaya sarvam ādarāt ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sā pramoditā । tathety abhyanumodantī tat sāmagrīm asādhayat ।।
tatra sā dhīmatī tasyāḥ śāṃtamatyāḥ puro gatā । tad vṛttāntaṃ sāmākhyāya sāmagrīṃ samayācata ।। sāpi śāṃtamatī tasyai dhīmatyai saṃpramoditā । yad yat saṃprārthitaṃ dravyaṃ tat tat sarvaṃ dadau mudā ।।
tad dravyaṃ sā samādāya bharttur agre samāgatā । tat sarvaṃ samupasthāpya vinodyaivam abhāṣata ।। svāmin tvayā yathādiṣṭaṃ tat sarvaṃ sādhitaṃ mayā । tathā tasyā mahālakṣmyā vratam ārabha sāṃprataṃ ।।
iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā viṣṇudāsaḥ sa moditaḥ । yathāvidhi mahālakṣmīvrataṃ caritum ārabhat ।। māse bhādrapade kṛṣṇapakṣe aṣṭamyāṃ yathāvidhi । maṇḍalādīn pratisthāpya śuddhaśīlaḥ samāhitaḥ ।।
sadāras tāṃ mahālakṣmīṃ samāvāhya samarcayan । vidhinā tad vrataṃ kṛtvā saṃpattiṃ prārthayan mudā ।। tataḥ sa brāhmaṇaḥ kṛtvā tad vrataṃ susamāptitaṃ । sabhāryaḥ suprasannātmā prācarat tāṃ śriyaṃ smaran ।।
tathā tasya gṛhe saṃpat samudbhūtābhyajāyata । dṛṣṭvā tau daṃpatī tatra mahānaṃdam avāpatuḥ ।। tataḥ sa brāhmaṇo lubdho dṛṣṭvā tān saṃpadaṃ mudā । sarvān gupte nidhāyaiva na kiṃ cit tad vyayaṃ vyadhāt ।।
bhūyas tṛṣṇābhisaṃtapto mātsaryābhihatāśayaḥ । kasmai cid api tad dravyaṃ kiṃ cid dānaṃ dadau kvacit ।। tathā saṃrakṣya tad dravyaṃ nidhāya tu viyatnataḥ । gopayitvā svayaṃ bhoktum api naivābhyavāṃchata ।।
tathāpi sa pralubdhātmā nityaṃ kṛpaṇo arthivat । dhanināṃ samupāśritya yācitvā dhanam ārjayat ।। tathārjanaḥ kṛtas tasya gṛhe dravyaṃ na varddhitaṃ । dine dine nihīnatvaṃ gatvā kṣayaṃ kramād yayau ।।
tataḥ sa brāhmaṇo lubdho dhaninām arthino gṛhe । dṛṣṭvātiruṣitaḥ sarvān paribhāṣyābhyaniṃdayat ।। tatpāpatāvipākena gṛhe yad gopitaṃ dhanaṃ । tat sarvaṃ nihṛtaṃ caurair nidagdhaṃ cāpi vahninā ।।
