tataḥ sa brāhmaṇas tīvrakleśāgniparitāpitaḥ । daridritāvibhagnāśaḥ sabhāryo nyavasad gṛhe ।। tasminn avasare tasyā dhīmatyāḥ sa pitā dvijaḥ । hariśarmābhidho gehe yajñaṃ karttuṃ sadārabhat ।।
tadā sa vāṃdhavān sārvāñ jñātīn mitrasuhṛjjanān । bhaginībhāgineyāṃś ca jāmātrīṃś tatsutān api ।। duhitṝr api sarvāś ca nyamaṃtrayat samādarāt ।। tatra te vāṃdhavā sarve jñātimitrasuhṛjjanāḥ ।
bhaginyā bhāgineyāś ca jāmātaro api tatsutāḥ ।। duhitaras tathā pautrāḥ pautryādayo api cāpare । sarve te samupāgatya samupatasthur ādritāḥ ।। tatra sā kṛpaṇībhūtā durbhageti pitāpi saḥ ।
tatra yajñamahotsāhe tām ekāṃ na nyamaṃtrayat ।। tadā sā dhīmatī śrutvā pitur yajñamahotsavaṃ । kathaṃ me vismṛtaṃ pitrā mātrāpi vāṃdhavair api ।। iti ciṃtāviṣāghrātahṛdayā parimūrchitā ।
bhojane api nirutsāhā tasthau lajjānvitā gṛhe ।। tathā sa viṣṇudāso api sasurasya gṛhe tadā । śrutvā yajñamahotsāhaṃ tāṃ bhāryām evam abravīt ।। kathaṃ te janakenāvāṃ vismṛtau kena hetunā ।
naiva nimaṃtritau bhadre yathā sarve nimaṃtritā ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sātilajjitā । bharttāraṃ viṣṇudāsaṃ taṃ bodhayanty evam abravīt ।। kim atrāhaṃ vadiṣyāmi yan nau saṃpad gṛhe asti na ।
tena nau lajjayāmbāpi nimaṃtrituṃ na vāṃchate ।। iti sā dhīmatī lajjāsaṃkuṃcitāśayānanā । bhartrā saha vilapyaiva tasthau gṛhe nirāśitā ।। tadā tajjanaṃ smṛtvā dhīmatīṃ tām anāgatāṃ ।
kāñ cit paṭhigatāṃ ceṭīṃ samāhūyaivam abravīt ।। ayi sakhi sutā me sā dhīmatā yadi dṛśyate । madvācasā sametyāsau vaktavyaivaṃ laghu tvayā ।। pitus te mandire yajñamahotsāhaṃ pravarttate ।
tat kathaṃ na samāyāsi sabharttāgantum arhasi ।। iti saṃdiśya te mātrā preṣitāhaṃ tvadantike । tan mātur vacanaṃ śrutvāgacheti tat puro vada ।। tat saṃdiṣṭaṃ tayā śrutvā tatheti pratibhāṣya sā ।
ceṭī tato abhigachantī dhīmatyā bhavane yayau ।। tatra tāṃ dhīmatīṃ dṛṣṭvā sā ceṭī samupasthitā । yathā mātrā samādiṣṭaṃ tathā sarvaṃ nyavedayat ।। tat tayā kathitaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sāśrumocinī ।
viniḥśvasya prasūṃ smṛtvā vilapantyaivam abravīt ।। hā mātaḥ katham adyāhaṃ saṃsmṛtā sāṃprataṃ tvayā । kim āgacheya te putrī pāpinī duḥkhabhāginī ।। tasminn eva kṣaṇe bharttā viṣṇudāsa upācarat ।
tāṃ ceṭīṃ samupālokya kim artham ity apṛchata ।। iti tenābhisaṃpṛṣṭe sā ceṭī racitāṃjaliḥ । brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ praṇamyaitat sarvaṃ vṛtāṃtam abravīt ।। tathā tat kathitaṃ śrutvā viṣṇudāso api sa dvijaḥ ।
galadaśruvirukṣākṣas tāṃ bhāryām evam abravīt ।। kiṃ vadiṣyāvahe bhārye daivān nau jāyate vipat । tathāpi dhairyyam ālamvya gacha draṣṭuṃ pitur manaḥ ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sā kuvāsinī । nirmaṇḍanāt sutān putrīḥ samādāya śanair yayau ।।
tato mātur gṛhe prāptā dṛṣṭvā tau pitarau puraḥ । gatvā sā dhīmatī natvā tasthau lajjāhatāśayā ।। pitarau tāṃ sutāṃ dṛṣṭvā vichandāṃ lajjitāśayaṃ । kiṃ cid dṛṣṭvāgatāsīti kathitvaiva niṣedatuḥ ।।
tataḥ sā dhīmatī sarvāñ jñātīn bhrātrīṃś ca vāṃdhavān । bhaginīḥ suhṛdo jeṣṭhān praṇanāma yathākramaṃ ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā jñātayaḥ sarve bhrātaro vāṃdhavā api । bhaginyāpi suhṛdaś cāpi dṛṣṭvopahasya jalpire ।।
tathā prahasitaṃ sarve sā dṛṣṭvātitrapānvitā । svadaivasmṛtim ādhāya niḥśvasyaikānta āśrayat ।। tataḥ sa hariśarmā sa purohito yathāvidhi । yajñakarmasamārabhya yathākāmaṃ samāpayat ।।
tatas tān vāṃdhavāñ jñātīn suhṛnmitrajanān api । satkṛtyātyabhisaṃtuṣṭān sādareṇa vyasarjayat ।। tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve vaṃdhumitrasuhṛjjanāḥ । naṃditās taṃ praśaṃsitvā svasvālayaṃ mudā yayuḥ ।।
tatas te susthitāḥ sarve jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanāḥ । nānākathābhisaṃlāpaṃ kurvantaḥ saṃniṣedire ।। tataḥ sā dhīmatī paścād bhuktvaikānte nirādritā । putraputrī samādāya śivasya bhavane acarat ।।
tatra sā stṛṇam āstīrya putraputrīsamanvitā । dāridryaduḥkhacintānuniḥśvasantī nyaṣīdata ।। tatra sa viṣṇudāso api paścād bhuktvā nirādritaḥ । śivālaye sthitāṃ śrutvā saha sthātum upācarat ।।
bharttāraṃ tam upāyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā dhīmatī tadā । galadaśruvirukṣākṣā vilapanty evam abravīt ।। dhig me jīvaṃ daridrāyāḥ kim evaṃ jīvitena hi । pitror api dayāsnehadṛṣṭir na vidyate mayi ।।
yat pitroḥ samāḥ sarvā bhaginyaḥ svātmajā api । tathāhaṃ mānitā naiva mānitās tā yathādarāt ।। dhig jīvitaṃ daridrāyā janmāpi dhik ca mānuṣe । kiṃ rūpaiḥ suguṇaiḥ vāpi vidyābhiḥ kiṃ dhanaṃ vinā ।।
hā daiva kiṃ mayā pāpaṃ dāruṇaṃ prakṛtaṃ purā । yan me na vidyate saṃpat pitro dadhāpi dayā mayi ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yāsyāmi śaraṇaṃ kuha । kā māṃ rakṣet svadaivotthadaridryaduḥkhatāpinīṃ ।।
kim evaṃ jīvitenāpi varaṃ mṛtyur hi sāṃpratāṃ । avaśyam eva marttavyaṃ sarveṣām api janmināṃ ।। evaṃ nānāpralāpena vilapantī sutam sutāṃ । bharttāraṃ ca muhur dṛṣṭvā kāruṇyārttā ruroda sā ।। evaṃ vilāpaṃ kurvantīṃ rudantīṃ tāṃ vilokya saḥ ।
viṣṇudāso viniḥśvasya samāśvāsyaivam abravīt ।। priye atra mā rudihi tvaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāvahe adhunā । yad āvābhyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhoktavyam eva tat phalaṃ ।। tad atra dhairyyam ālamvya tiṣṭha kiṃ vakṣyate bahu ।
avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavaṃti mahatām api ।। śivo api sa virūpākṣo nīlakaṇṭho digaṃvaraḥ । unmatto bhasmaliptāṃgaḥ kapālayo api rasthidhṛk ।। viṣṇur vīro api saṃsāre bhramitaḥ sa janārdanaḥ ।
so api dāso validvāsthaś cauro vyādheṣuṇāhataḥ ।। brahmā lokādhipaḥ so api kāmārtto agamyakarmakṛt । niyujyo nighnito vairisevakaś chinnamastaka ।। cicheda brahmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ rudraḥ krodhātta paṃcamaṃ ।
tac chiro dustyajaṃ gṛhṇan brahmāṇḍaṃ parivabhrame ।। śaṃkhatīrthe gato rudras tac chiraḥ parimuktavān । kapālamocanas tīrtho dvitīyāvarttasaṃsthitaḥ ।। iti utkalakhaṇḍakṣetramāhātmye uktam āste ।
evam anye api lokāś ca munayas tāpasā api ।। kopāgnidahitātmāno vrajanti narakeṣv api । evaṃ sarve api lokāś ca svasvadaivānubhāvinaḥ ।। sukhino duḥkhino bhūtā bhramaṃti bhavasāgare ।
kṣaṇāl labhanti saṃpattiṃ bhavanti ca daridritāḥ ।। sarve devādayo lokāḥ svakṛtakarmabhoginaḥ । evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ svadaivajaṃ ।। mā kṛthās tad viṣāda tvaṃ dhairyaṃ dhṛtvā samācara ।
svakuleśam anusmṛtvā samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ । śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samāhitā ।। tatas tatpuṇyapākena pāpaṃ no vilayaṃ vrajet । tataḥ saṃpat samṛddhiḥ syāt tadā lapsyāvahe sukhaṃ ।।
iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā dhairyyam ālamvya sāṃprataṃ । putraputrīṃ samādāya praihi gṛhe vrajāmahe ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sābhibodhitā । putraṃ putrīṃ purodhāya śanair bhartrā sahācarat ।।
tatra sā svagṛhe gatvā kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā nirutsahā । tataḥ śāntamatīṃ draṣṭuṃ samutthāya śanair yayau ।। tatra sā dhīmatī tasyāḥ śāṃtamatyāḥ purogatā । galadaśruviliptāsyā niḥśvasaṃty evam abravīt ।।
śāṃtamate pitur yajñamahotsāhapravarttitaṃ । tat saṃdraṣṭu gatā tatra mahālajjānvitā caraṃ ।। yan māṃ dṛṣṭvā bhaginyo api jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanāḥ । api sarve mitho dṛṣṭvā prajalpitābhyupāhasan ।।
bhāgineyāś ca sarve api māṃ dṛṣṭvā ruṣitāśayāḥ । putraputrīṃ ca me dṛṣṭvā phutkṛtya pratyātāḍayan ।। pitṛbhyāṃ mānitāḥ sarvāḥ bhaginyas tā yathādarāt । tathāhaṃ mānitā naiva draṣṭum api na caiṣyate ।।
rātrāv api gṛhe vāsaṃ na me dattaṃ nirādarāt । śivālaye niṣaṇṇā tan niśāṃ kṛcchrād vyalaṃghayaṃ ।। evam ahaṃ mahallajjāduḥkhāgnipatitāpitā । marttum api tad icchāmi kim evaṃ jīvitenapi ।।
yadi te asti kṛpā bhadre duḥkhinyāṃ mayi vidyate । tad dravyopārjanopāyaṃ samupadeṣṭum arhati ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā śāntamatīr dayārditaḥ । dhīmatīṃ tāṃ samālokya samāśvāsyaivam abravīt ।।
dhīmatī śrīmahāsaṃpatsādhanopāyam asti me । yady atrāpy asti te vāṃchā pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva tat ।। yadi śraddhāsti te devyā vasulakṣmyā vrataṃ cara । tatas te śrīvasundhārā mahādevī vased gṛhe ।।
tatas tasyā mahādevyāḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ । saṃpattis te samudbhūtā pravarddhitā bhaved gṛhe ।। tadā tvaṃ śraddhayārthibhyo dānaṃ datvā yathepsitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā śubhe cara sukhāśinī ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadā sadgatiṃ gatā । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। evaṃ matvāsti te vāṃchā saṃbuddhapada sādhane । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā samādhāya vrataṃ cara ।।
iti tayā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutva sā dhīmatī mudā । tāṃ śāṃtamatīm ānamya sāṃjalīr evam abravīt ।। sādhu bhadre vrataṃ dhṛtvā śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatā । triratnabhajanam kṛtvā cariṣyāmi śubhe sadā ।।
tad bhavaṃtī kṛpādṛṣṭyā tad upadeśam ādiśa । yāvajjīvaṃ cariṣyāmi śrīdevyā vratam ādarāt ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā śāntamatiḥ samādarāt । dhīmatīṃ tāṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।।
yadi bhadre asti te satyaṃ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtā । prehi taṃ śrīghanaṃ nāthaṃ saṃsmṛtvā prārthayāvahe ।। tayeti samupādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sā dhīmatī mudā । sahasā svagṛhe gatvā snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtā ।।
sa lājākṣatapuṣpāṇi gṛhitvā sahasā mudā । tasyāḥ śāṃtamater agre prayātevam abhāṣata ।। bhadre tvayā yathādiṣṭaṃ tathāhaṃ samupāgatā । taṃ munīndram anusmṛtvā prārthayeha samāgamaṃ ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā śāntamatir ādarāt । tāṃ dhīmatīṃ samāmaṃtrya prāsādāntaṃ yayau mudā ।। tatra śāntamatiḥ sāṭṭe dhīmatyā saha saṃsthitā । jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitvā bhagavatsthitadigmukhā ।। saṃbhavanty uttarāsaṅgaṃ saha lājākṣatādibhiḥ ।
sāmbupuṣpāñjaliṃ dhṛtvā natvaivaṃ prārthayan muniṃ ।। bhagavan nātha sarvajña vijānīte bhavān api । yad iyaṃ dhīmatī sādhvī bhagavaccharaṇam āgatā ।। yad iyaṃ sāṃprataṃ śāstur upadeśād yathāvidhi ।
śrīvasudhāmahādevyā vrataṃ caritum ichati ।। tad atra samupāgatya kṛpayāsmai dayānidhe । śrīsādhanaṃ vrataṃ śreṣṭhaṃ samupadeṣṭum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthya sā śāntamatis taṃ trijagadguruṃ ।
anusmṛtvā tridhā nātvā prākṣipat tajjalādikaṃ ।। prakṣiptāni tayā tāni sāmbulājākṣatāṇy api । sadūrvākuṇḍapuṣpāṇi sarvāṇi gagaṇe śaran ।। tatas tāni pragacchanti vihāyasā vihaṅgavat ।
kośāmvyāṃ ghoṣirārāme vihāre samupāyayuḥ ।। tatrasthasya munīndrasya murddhā pari vihāyasi । saṃsthitāni prabhāsanti virejus tāni chatravat ।। tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve sāṃghikās te savismayāḥ ।
kuto nimaṃtraṇam āyātam iti dhyātvābhitasthire ।। tatrānandaḥ samutthāya sāṃjaliḥ purato gataḥ । taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvaivaṃ papracha vismayānvitaḥ ।। bhagavan kuta etāni sāmbulājākṣatāny api ।
puṣpāṇi samupāyānti tat samādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavāṃ sa munīśvaraḥ । tam ānaṃdaṃ samāmaṃtrya samālokyaivam abravīt ।। yaḥ kāśīpure vipro viṣṇudāso daridritaḥ ।
dharmadhvajo dhanī śrīmān gṛhastho dhanadopamaḥ ।। tayor bhārya ubhe sādhvau śāntamatī ramopamā । dhīmatī brāhmaṇī bhadrā daridritā suduḥkhinī ।। tābhyāṃ śrīvasudhārāyā vrataṃ caritum ichyate ।
tad idaṃ nimaṃtraṇārthaṃ me upahāraṃ samāgataṃ ।। tasmāc chrīvasudhārāyā vratavidhiṃ tvam ātmanā । upadeṣṭuṃ tayor gehe kāśyāṃ gaṃtuṃ samarhasi ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdas tatheti saḥ ।
śāstur ājñāṃ śirodhṛtvā kāśyāṃ vihāyasā yayau ।। tatrākāśān sa ānaṃdaḥ śāṃtamater gṛhe puraḥ । avatīrya sudhāraśmir iva tasthau prabhāsayan ।। tatrasthaṃ taṃ samālokya śāntamatiḥ sa dhīmatī ।
muditā sahasā tasya praṇaṃtuṃ samupācarat ।। tatra sā samupāsṛtya śāṃtamatiḥ sadhīmatī। tam ānaṃdaṃ samālokya natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।। bhadanta caraṇau vaṃde bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā । tad atra kṛpayāsmākam anugṛhya prasīdatu ।।
yad asmākaṃ bhavāñ chāstā tad gṛhe samupāśrayan । vasudhārāmahādevyā vratavidhiṃ samādiśa ।। yad iyaṃ dhīmatī bhadrā bhavatām upadeśataḥ । vasulakṣmyā mahādevyā vrataṃ caritum ichati ।। tad asyai śrīmahādevyā vratavidhiṃ yathākramaṃ ।
vistaraṃ samupādeṣṭum arhati kṛpayā bhavān ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ śāntamatyā tayā niśamya saḥ । ānaṃdas te ubhe dṛṣṭvā tatheti pratyabhāṣata ।। tataḥ sā dhīmatī natvā sāṃjalis taṃ jinātmajaṃ ।
ānaṃdaṃ suprasannāsyā dṛṣṭvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā ।। bhadaṃto ahaṃ svadaivena pāpinī duḥkhabhāginī । tad bhavaccharaṇaṃ gatvā samiche vasudhāvrataṃ ।। tad bhavān kṛpayā śāstar gṛhe me samupāgataḥ ।
yathāvidhi samādiśya vrataṃ me dātum arhati ।। tayaivaṃ prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa ānaṃdo jinātmajaḥ । tatra utthāya dhīmatyās tasyā gṛhe upācarat ।। tatra sā dhīmatī sādhvī śāntamatyā samanvitā ।
sahasā svagṛhe gatvā prastārayat tadāsanaṃ ।। tataḥ sā dhīmatī tasya śāstuḥ śuddhāmbunā mudā । pādaprakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā praṇatvaiva ca prārthayat ।। bhadaṃtārhan mahābhijña mamānugrahakāraṇaṃ ।
atrāsane samāśritya dharmam ādeṣṭum arhati ।। tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa ānaṃdaḥ prasannadhīḥ । tad dattāsana āśritya tasthau dhyātvā prabhāsayan ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇaḥ so api viṣṇudāsaḥ prasāditaḥ ।
sahasā sāṃjalir natvā tatraikāṃta upāśrayan ।। tataḥ sā dhīmatī sādhvī sāṃtamatīsamanvitā । tam ānaṃdaṃ samabhyarcya bhojanenābhyatoṣayat ।। tataḥ sā praṇatiṃ kṛtvā nīcāsanasamāśritā ।
tam ānaṃdaṃ mahābhijñaṃ sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। bhadanta bhavatām ājñāṃ dhṛtvāhaṃ śirasā mudā । śrīdevyā vasudhārāyāś cariṣyāmi vrataṃ dhruvaṃ ।। tad bhadanta bhavāñ chāstā tad vidhiṃ me yathākramaṃ ।
kṛpānugraham ādhāya samupādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tena viṣṇudāsena saddhiyā । śrutvānaṃdaḥ sa saṃpaśyans taṃ dvijam evam abravīt ।। śṛṇu vipra munīndreṇa yāthādiṣṭaṃ mayā śrutaṃ ।
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrīvratasya vidhiṃ kramāt ।। bhādrapade aśite pakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ tithau tathā । māghe vāpi śite pakṣe śuklapakṣe api vā sadā ।। tīrthe devālaye śuddhabhūpradeśe gṛheṣu vā ।
samyag bhūśodhanaṃ kuryād gomayena mṛdāmbunā ।। prātar utthāya tīrtheṣu snātvā śucisamācaraḥ । tridhācamyāmṛtaṃ kāyaṃ paṃcagavyena śodhayet ।। śuddhaśīlasamādhānaḥ pariśuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ । saṃbodhicittam ādhāya sadguror upadeśa dhṛk ।।
subhūmau maṇḍalaṃ samyag varttayitvā yathāvidhi । dhvajachatrapatākābhi vitānaiś cābhimaṃḍayet ।। maṃḍalasya vahis tasya jvālāvalyā vahiḥ punaḥ । paṃcavalyāvalībhiś ca sa lājākṣatasaṃyutaiḥ ।।
veṣṭayitvā tato vāhye kramān saṃsthāpayed ghaṭān । tīrthāmbupūritān pītavastrāvṛtān saciṃhnitān ।। tātra śrīvasudhāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ vidhinā kramāt । samāvāhya samabhyarcya pratiṣṭhāpyādhivāsayet ।।
tṛtīyāyāṃ tathā prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ । madhyāhne svāsanāsīna uttarādigmukhasthitaḥ ।। ādau guruṃ samabhyarcya ratnatrayaṃ samarcayet । tato dhyātvā mahādevīṃ vasudhārāṃ śubhakarīṃ ।।
sagaṇāṃ tāṃ samāvāhya datvā pādārgham ādarāt । pītamayopahāreṇa samabhyarcya yathāvidhi ।। sarvopakaraṇāny agre nivesya samaḍhokayat । tatas taddhāraṇīṃ samyak paṭhen maṃtrāṇi ca kramāt ।।
tataḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ stutvā kuryāś ca pāpadeśanāṃ । puṇyānumodanāṃ cāpi kuryāc ca praṇatiṃ smaran ।। kuryāt pradakṣiṇāny evam aṣṭāṅgaiḥ praṇamet punaḥ । bodhicittaṃ samādhāya saṃprārthayed abhīpsitaṃ ।।
tato valiṃ pradatvā ca sa bhūtān paritoṣayet । tataḥ kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā vratasūtraṃ ca prārthayet ।। ṣoḍaśabheditaṃ sūtram ṣoḍaśagraṃthisaṃyutaṃ । vratasūtraṃ samādāya rakṣārthaṃ vaṃdhayet kare ।।
tato guruṃ samārādhya deyād dānaṃ samichitaṃ । sadakṣiṇaṃ susatkāraiḥ satkṛtya samatoṣayet ।। tatas tṛtīyā yāme ahneḥ prāśnuyād yavapūrakān । paṃcāmṛtaphalaskaṃdamūlapatrādikān api ।।
pālanānte punaḥ snātvā tāṃ śrīdevīm anusmaran । taddhāraṇīṃ paṭhan rātrau pūjayec ca samāhitaḥ ।। evaṃ nityaṃ catuḥ saṃdhyaṃ pūjayec chrīvasuṃdharāṃ । tat paredyus tathābhyarcya tan maṃḍalaṃ visarjayet ।।
tad rajāṃsi samādāya saṃnidhāya śubhe ghaṭe । bhaṃḍāgāre pratisthāpya sadārān bhajen namet ।। śeṣarajaḥ sa nirmālyaṃ nadyāṃ nāgān yathāvidhi । samabhyarcya samarppitvā sarvaṃ jale pravāhayet ।।
tatas taj jalam ādāya gṛhe gatvā samantataḥ । prokṣya tan maṃḍalasthāne kumārīṃ vidhinārcayet ।। tatas tan sagaṇaṃ cakraṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi । bhojanaiḥ saṃparitoṣya prārthayed yat samīchitaṃ ।।
tathā tat sagaṇaṃ cakraṃ kṛtvā kṣamārthanāṃ tataḥ । sāṃjaliś ca kramān natvā visarjayet prasādayan ।। tadā śrīvasudhā devī svayam āgatya tadgṛhe । samāśritya sadā sarvadravyaiḥ saṃpūrayed dhruvaṃ ।।
tatas tatra gṛhe nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ । dānapuṇyamahotsāhapravarttitaṃ bhavet sadā ।। evaṃ tasyā mahādevyā vasulakṣmyā vratodbhavaṃ । puṇyaṃ mahad asaṃkhyeyam aprameyaṃ vidur jināḥ ।।
evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ vijñāya dvija tat tathā । śraddhaye tadvrataṃ kuryā yadi saṃpattim ichasi ।। yaś ca tāṃ śrīmahādevīṃ vasudhārām anusmaran । yat kāryyam ārabhet tasya tat sarvaṃ hi samṛddhyati ।।
ratnārthī labhate ratnaṃ dhanārthī labhate dhanaṃ । bhogyārthī labhate bhogyaṃ yaso arthī labhate yaśaḥ ।। dravyārthī labhate dravyān guṇārthī labhate guṇān । vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ śubhārthī labhate śubhaṃ ।।
mānyārthī labhate mānyaṃ jayārthī labhate jayaṃ । dharmārthī labhate dharmān sukhārthī labhate sukhaṃ ।। rājyārthī labhate rājyaṃ gṛhārthī labhate gṛhaṃ । kṣetrārthī labhate kṣetrān rasārthī labhate rasān ।।
bhāryārthī labhate bhāryāṃ sutārthī labhate sutāṃ । putrārthī labhate putrān pautrārthī pautram āpnuyāt ।। jñānārthī labhate jñānaṃ mokṣārthī mokṣam āpnuyāt । evam anyāni vastūni sarvopakaraṇāny api ।।
sarvāṇi dravyajātāni vastrādi bhūṣaṇāny api । samāpnuyāt samṛddhāni vasulakṣmyāḥ prasādataḥ ।। tato dānāni dadyāt sa śuddhaśīlaḥ samācaret । kṣāntiṃ ca bhāvayen nityaṃ dharmavīryyaṃ samārabhet ।।
tathā dhyānaṃ samādhāya prajñābdhiṃ saṃtared drutaṃ । sarvopāyavidhānajño bodhipraṇidhimānasaḥ ।। sadbuddhibalavān dhīraḥ sa bodhijñānam āpnuyāt । sarvamāragaṇāñ jitvā niḥkleśo arhañ jitendriyaḥ ।
saṃbuddhapadam āsādya nirvṛtapadam āpnuyāt ।। evaṃ brāhmaṇa vijñāya saddharmmaṃ yadi vāṃchasi । tāṃ śrīdevīṃ mahālakṣmīṃ vasudhārāṃ sadā bhaja ।। tathā te sarvadā gehe maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।
sarvatreha paratrāpi bhaven nūnaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। tathā dānāni datvā tvaṃ svayaṃ tadvrataṃ saṃcaran । sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ cara ।। tataḥ kleśavimuktātmā saṃbodhipraṇidhānadhṛk ।
bodhicaryāvratāraktā bodhisatvo bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। sarve api sugatā bodhisatvāś cāpi jinātmajāḥ । vasudhārāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃvibhrati jagattrayaṃ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa brāhmaṇo mudā । tathā śrīvasudhārāyā vrataṃ caritum aichata ।।
tataḥ sa viṣṇudāso api bhāryāṃ tāṃ dhīmatīṃ mudā । suprasannamukhāmbhojaḥ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। priye dhanyāsi kalyāṇī yad ahaṃ tvatprayatnataḥ । śrīdevyā vrataṃ ratnaṃ prāpnomi sāṃprataṃ khalu ।।
tad yathānena śāstrātra samādiṣṭaṃ tathā khalu । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā vāṃchāmi carituṃ vrataṃ ।। tat tvam api samādhāya mayā sārddhaṃ tathādarāt । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caritum arhati ।।
iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sānumoditā । bharttāraṃ taṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata ।। tathā satyaṃ samādhāya śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatau । śrīdevyā vratam atrāvāṃ samādarāc carāvahe ।।
ity uktvā sā satī bhadrā dhīmatī sahasādarāt । vratopacārasāmagrīṃ muditā samasādhayat ।। tatas taṃ gurum ānaṃdaṃ natvā sā sāṃjalir mudā । tad vratārambham ādhātuṃ prārthayed evam ādarāt ।।
bhadanta śrīmahādevyā vratadina upāsthitaḥ । tad yathāvidhim ādiśya saṃcārayatāṃ vrataṃ ।। tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa ānaṃdo jinātmajaḥ । sarvavidhiṃ samādiśya vratāraṃbhaṃ samākramat ।।
tatra bhūśodhanaṃ kṛtvā sa ānaṃdo yathāvidhi । maṃḍalaṃ varttayitvā tat pratisthāpyādhyavāsayat ।। tathā tau daṃpatī tīrthe snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtau । yathā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvopatasthatuḥ ।।
tatas tau daṃpatī tasya śāstur ādeśataḥ kramāt । śuddhāsanasamāsīnāv uttarābhimukhasthitau ।। gavyaiḥ kāmādi vastūni sarvāṇi śuddhitāny api । kṛtvā śāstrā yathādiṣṭaṃ tathāraṃbhaṃ pracakratuḥ ।।
ādau guruṃ samabhyarcya tato ratnatrayaṃ mudā । abhyarcya śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇatvā vidhinādarāt ।। tatas tanmaṇḍale devīṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । dhyātvā tathā samāvāhya datvā pādārgham ādarāt ।।
tatas tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīṃ samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ । sarvapūjopacāraiś ca paṭhitvā dhāraṇīṃ tataḥ ।। sahṛdvījādimaṃtrāṇi yathākramaṃ jajalpatuḥ । tato aṣṭāṅgapraṇāmaiś ca natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ ।।
guṇābhivādanai stotrai stutvā natau vavaṃdatuḥ ।। tatas tau sāṃjalī sthitvā prakṣitvā pāpadeśanāṃ । puṇyānumodanāṃ cāpi saṃprārthya śrīsamṛddhyatāṃ ।। salokapālabhūtebhyo baliṃ paṃcāmṛtānvitaṃ । yathāvidhi praḍhaukitvā prārthayatāṃ susaṃpadaṃ ।।
tato dānaṃ pradatvaivaṃ gurave api sudakṣiṇāṃ । tataḥ kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā samāptaṃ cakratur vrataṃ ।। tato gurus tayoḥ śāstā vratasūtraṃ samarppayat । saṃpattisasamṛddhāśīrvādaṃ dadau prasāditaḥ ।।
tato guruṃ puraskṛtya yathoktaṃ vratapālanaṃ । kṛtvā tataḥ punaḥ snātvā devīṃ dhyātvā niṣedituḥ ।। tato rātrau samādhāya sagaṇāṃ vasuṃdharāṃ । devīṃ dhyātvā samabhyarcya dharmmaṃ śrutvā niṣedatuḥ ।।
tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtau । tathā tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīm āvāhyānarcatuḥ kramāt ।। tatas tad vratasaṃpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā dānaṃ sadakṣiṇaṃ । pradatvā gurave natvā tan maṇḍalaṃ vyasarjatāṃ ।।
tatas tad rajam ādāya bhaṃḍāgāre yathoditaṃ । nidhāya tat sa nirmālyaṃ śeṣaṃ nadyāṃ yathāvidhiṃ ।। gurur nāgān samabhyarcya samarpya prākṣipaj jale । tatas taj jalam ādāya mahotsāhair gṛhaṃ yayau ।।
tata gṛhe tad ambhobhir abhiṣiṃcya samantataḥ । kumārīṃ vidhinārādhya gaṇacakraṃ samarcayat ।। tatas tau daṃpatī natvā sāṃjali sādaraṃ mudā । saṃpattiprārthanāṃ kṛtvā kṣamāpya tad vyasarjatāṃ ।।
tatas tasyā gṛhe devī vasundhārā svayaṃ sthitā । sarvadravyasamāpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau prasāditā ।। sarvadravyābhisaṃpūrṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā tau daṃpatī gṛhaṃ । vismayānaṃdasaṃpannau mitha evaṃ samūcatuḥ ।।
aho satyaṃ jagacchāstur yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā khalu । tathāvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā devyā vrataṃ carevahi ।। ity uktvā tau prasīdaṃtau śaraṇaṃ gatvā samāhitau । tasyāḥ śrīmahādevyāḥ sadā vrataṃ praceratuḥ ।।
tadārabhyaḥ sadārthibhyo datvā dānaṃ yathārthitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā praceratuḥ śubhe sadā ।। tato asau yatir ānaṃdas tau samāmaṃtrya daṃpatī । pakṣivat sahasākāśāt kauśāṃvyāṃ samupācarat ।।
tatra sa taṃ jagannāthaṃ praṇatvā sāṃjaliḥ punaḥ । etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaikāntam āśrayat ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tam ānaṃdaṃ sabhāṃ ca tāṃ । dhīmatyāḥ śāṃtamatyāś ca prasāditvaivam ādiśat ।।
dhanyā sā dhīmatī śāntamatī cāpi subhāvinī । yat te śrīvasudhārāyā bhavetāṃ vratadhāriṇī ।। tan me ubhe mahatpuṇyalābhinyau śrīsamanvite । sarvasatvahitādhānabodhicaryāsamudyate ।। kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya buddhapadam avāpsyata ।।
ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ । tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ smṛtvā nityaṃ prabhejire ।। tadā tasyāḥ pitā viprā dhīmatyā duhitur gṛhe । samudbhūtā mahāsaṃpad ity aśroṣīj janoditaṃ ।।
tataḥ sa brāhmaṇo bhāryāṃ dhīmatyā mātaraṃ mudā । sahasā samupāmaṃtrya pura evam abhāṣata ।। kiṃ tvayānuśrutaṃ bhārye dhīmatyā yad gṛhe adhunā । mahāsaṃpat samudbhūtā mayeti śrūyate khalu ।।
iti bhartrā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā vismayānvitā । katham etad bhavet satyam iti taṃ patim abravīt ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā hariśarmāpi sa dvijaḥ । savismayenākhyātaṃ śrutvā caivam abhāṣata ।।
priye śrutaṃ mayā satyaṃ dhīmatyā yad gṛhe adhunā । mahāsaṃpatsamudbhūtā vasundhārāprasādataḥ ।। yadi naitat pratīto api janaiḥ sā dhīmatī sutā । svagṛhe atra samāhūya tvam evaṃ paripṛchyatāṃ ।।
kathaṃ saṃjāyate saṃpan mahatī te gṛhe adhunā । etat satyaṃ tvayā putrī puro me kathyatām iti ।। evaṃ bhartrā samākhyātaṃ śrutva sā dhīmatīprasūḥ । tatheti prativijñāya svasakhīm evam abravīt ।।
śṛṇu sakhi sutāyā me dhīmatyā yad gṛhe adhunā । saṃbhūtā mahatī saṃpad vasuṃdhārā prasādataḥ ।। iti śrutaṃ mayā satyaṃ draṣṭum ichāmi tat khalu । tat tāṃ sutāṃ samāhūya samādarād ihānaya ।।
iti tayā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā supriyā sakhī । tatheti prativijñapya dhīmatyā bhavane yayau ।। tatra sā samupāsṛtya dhīmatīṃ tāṃ subhadrikāṃ । dṛṣṭvā savismayānaṃdayuktā natvaivam abravīt ।।
bhadre ahaṃ preṣitā mātrā tvadāhvānaṃ pratīha tat । sahasā tvaṃ samāgaṃtum arhasi svātmajānvitā ।। iti tayā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā dhīmatī mudā । hasantī tāṃ sakhīṃ mātuḥ samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
ayi māṃ smarate mātā kim arthaṃ sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ । tadāhaṃ na smṛtā mātrā dāridriyaduḥkhinī yadā ।। tathāpy ahaṃ mukhaṃ mātur draṣṭum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ । tathāham āgamiṣyāmi yathā mātuḥ samīhitaṃ ।।
ity uktvā dhīmatī sātha putraṃ ca bhūṣaṇaṃ । bhūṣayitvā suvastraiś ca prāvārya samamaṇḍayat ।। svayaṃ ca sā prasādhitvā duṣyapaṭṭāmvarāvṛtā । śrīmad ratnāmvalaṃkārair maṇḍitāṃgābhiśobhitā ।।
tataḥ sakhyā tayā sārddhaṃ putraputrīsamanvitā । saṃprasthitā janaiś cāpi saha mātur gṛhe yayau ।। tatra sā jananī dṛṣṭvā dhīmatīṃ tāṃ samāgatāṃ । taṃ suputraṃ suputrīṃ ca paśyantī samupācaran ।।
tatra tāṃ jananīṃ dṛṣṭvā dhīmatī sātmajānvitā । sahasā samupāgatya natvāpṛchat sukauśalaṃ ।। jananī sāpi tāṃ putrīṃ putraputrīsamanvitāṃ । dhīmatīṃ sahasāliṃgya papracha kauśalaṃ mudā ।।
tataḥ sā dhīmatī putrī putraputrīsamanvitā । mātrā sahābhigachaṃtī pitur geham upāsarat ।। tatra sādhīmatīṃ putrīṃ putraputrīsahāgatāṃ । dṛṣṭvā sa janako apy evaṃ paśyan pratyudyayau mudā ।।
janakaṃ taṃ samālokya dhīmatī sātmajānvitā । saṃsmitā samupāsṛtya natvāpṛchat sukauśalaṃ ।। pitāpi sa samālokya dhīmatīṃ tāṃ śubhāṃśikāṃ । putraputryau ca saṃbhāṣya papracha kauśalaṃ mudā ।।
pitā sa jananī sāpi dhīmatīṃ tāṃ subhāvinīṃ । pautraṃ pautrīṃ ca saṃdhṛtvā svagṛhe jagmatur mudā ।। tatra sā jananī tasyāḥ pautryāḥ pautrasya cādarāt । pādān prakṣālayitvāśu svakam ānayat ।।
tad āsanaṃ samāstīrya tāṃ putrīṃ svayam ādarāt । pautraṃ pautrīṃ ca tān sarvān saṃdhṛtvā saṃnyaveśayat ।। tatrāsane samāśritya pārśvayor vāmadakṣayoḥ । putrīṃ putram upasthāpya tasthau sā dhīmatī smitā ।।
tām āgatāṃ samākarṇya sarve api jātayo mudā । sahasā draṣṭum āgatya sā daraṃ samupāyayuḥ ।। tathā te vāṃdhavāḥ sarve suhṛtminrajanā api । tāṃ tathā svagṛhāyātāṃ kuśalaṃ praṣṭum āyayuḥ ।।
tathā tāś ca bhaginyo api tāsāṃ sarve api cātmajāḥ । tāṃ dhīmatīṃ tathāyātāṃ śrutvā draṣṭu samā yayuḥ ।। evam anye api lokāś ca dhīmatīṃ tāṃ subhūṣaṇāṃ । svamātur gṛhamāyātāṃ śrutvā draṣṭum upāyayuḥ ।।
tatretaṃ dhīmatīṃ kāṃtāṃ suvastrabhūṣaṇāvṛtāṃ । te sajñātyādayaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā vismayam āyayuḥ ।। tato anujā bhaginyādi jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanāḥ । sarve tāṃ sādaraṃ natvā paprachuḥ kuśalaṃ mudā ।।
tathā sā dhīmatī cāpi jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanān । vandanīyāns tān natvāpṛchat sukauśalaṃ ।। tataḥ sā jananī tasyai dhīmatyai sādarān mudā । varṇagaṃdharasopetaṃ bhojanaṃ samupāharat ।।
tathā sautāya sautāyai bhojanaṃ surasānvitaṃ । sādaram upaḍhokitvā pura evam abhāṣata ।। gṛhṇāṇa surasaṃ bhogyaṃ bhukṣva hṛd dhīmati priye । yo sauta saute ca saudārdda procyutaṃ yadabhīpsitaṃ ।।
janako vitathya sarvo bhaginyo bhrātaro api ca । bhātṛjāyāṃ sukhāś cāpi tasyāś cakruḥ samādaraṃ ।। tathādarāṃ kṛtaṃ sarve śrutvā sā dhīmatī tadā । pūrvavṛttim anusmṛtvā manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।।
naivāhaṃ mānitā hy ebhir nāyaṃ putro api mānitaḥ । na ca yaṃ mānitā putri dhanam evātra manyate ।। yadā na me gṛhe saṃpad daridro ahaṃ ca duḥkhinī । tademe sarva ete api nāpi apaśyan mukhaṃ mama ।।
idānīṃ me gṛhe saṃpaj jātā tat sukhānvitāṃ । evaṃ mate api sarve māṃ mānayaṃti samādarāt ।। yad ahaṃ mānitā naiva dhanam evābhimānyate । tad yasya taiḥ kriyate mānyaṃ sa bhuṃjyād idam ādaraṃ ।।
iti sā manasā dhyātvā sarvāṇi bhūṣaṇāny api । svāni putrasya putryāś ca saṃnirīkṣya samādade ।। tataḥ sā dhīmatī kāṃśasthālyāṃ sarvāṇi tāny api । bhūṣaṇāni prasāryaivaṃ sādaraṃ pratyabhāṣata ।।
bho bho bhavanti sarvāṇi bhūṣaṇāni priyāṇi me । idaṃ saurasikaṃ bhojyaṃ prāśnuta svechayā sukhaṃ ।। saṃsāre mānanīyaṃ hi dhanam eva sadādarāt । dhanānurūpeṇa yal loke mānyate niṃdyate naraḥ ।।
dhanavān puruṣo loke nīco api mānyate aguṇaḥ । nirdhanā guṇavāṃś cāpi sujāto api na mānyate ।। dhanānurūpeṇa sarvatra vicāramānyabhojanaṃ । dhanaprasaṃgato mūrkho nīco api dhanyato bhavet ।।
yāvat saṃpad gṛhe tāval loke samādrito naraḥ । yadā saṃpad vihīne tu tadā sa bhūtavac caret ।। iti sābhilapanty eva sarvāṇi bhūṣaṇāny api । tāni punaḥ samādāya yathā sthānaṃ nyayojayat ।।
tatas tadbhojanaṃ kiṃcid bhaktvā sā svātmajānvitā । natvaiva pitarau bharttur gṛhe yayau prasāditā ।। tatra sā dhīmatī bharttur viṣṇudāsasya pādayoḥ । natvā sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ nyavedayat puraḥ sthitā ।।
etad bhāryāsamākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa brāhmaṇaḥ patiḥ । muditas tāṃ sukalyāṇīṃ bhāryaṃ dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt ।। dhanyo asi tvaṃ sukalyāṇī yat te samupādeśataḥ । śrīdevīvratam ādhāya samāpnomi susaṃpadaṃ ।।
priye tvām atra tadratnasaṃbhavakulasaṃbhavāṃ । śrīvasudhāmahādevīsamāṃ manye aham ātmanā ।। ity uktvā brāhmaṇo bharttā viṣṇudāsaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ । dhīmatīṃ taṃ sukalyāṇīṃ natvaivaṃ punar abravīt ।।
priye tava prasādena sāphalyaṃ janma me adhunā । yac chrīvasuṃdharādevyā upāsako vratī bhave ।। tan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat sarvaṃ kṣīyate adhunā । saṃpattiḥ saṃprajātā ca naiva kṣīṇā bhave dhi naḥ ।।
tathā vayaṃ sadāpy asyāḥ śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । yathāvidhi vrataṃ dhṛtvā caremahi śubhe adhunā ।। triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā datvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । yāvajjīvaṃ śubhaṃ kṛtvā bhuktvā saukhyaṃ caremahi ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadā sadgatīṃ gatāḥ । kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya buddhapadaṃ labhemahi ।। iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sānumoditā । tathā sadā vasuṃdhārāvrataṃ dhṛtvā śubhe acarat ।।
tataḥ sā dhīmatī tasyāḥ śāṃtamateḥ purogatā । sarvam etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivam abhāṣata ।। priye sakhi mahābhāge bhavatkṛpāprasādataḥ । pāpaṃ me kṣīyate sarvaṃ taj janma saphalaṃ bhave ।।
saṃpattiḥ saṃprajātā me naiva kṣīṇā bhaved api । tad yāvajjīvitaṃ devyāḥ śaraṇastho bhajāni hi ।। tvam eva śāstā na cānyā hi saddharmopadeśinī । tan me puṇyānubhāvena saṃbuddhapadam āpnuhi ।।
ity udite tam āśrutvā śāṃtamatiś ca sā mudā । dhīmatīṃ tāṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣāta ।। bhadre dhīmati saṃbuddhaśaraṇasthā sadādarāt । śrīdevyāvratam ādhāya śubhe cara samāhitā ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadā sadgatīṃ gatā । kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti matvātra saṃsāre śubhaṃ dharmārthasādhanaṃ । dharmo lokahitārthāya tal lokārthe dharmam ācareḥ ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sā prabodhitā । tatheti pratinaṃditvā muditā svagṛhe yayau ।। tataḥ prabhṛti sā sādhvī dhīmatī sarvadā gṛhe । śrīdevyā bhajanaṃ kṛtvā datvā dānaṃ śubhe acarat ।।
tathā tasyā gṛhe saṃpad dine dine pravarddhitā । sarvasatvopabhogyārthaṃ babhūva dharmasādhinī ।। tathā sā dhīmatī dṛṣṭvā sarvasaṃpatpravarddhitāṃ । mudā lokahitaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śubhe sadā ।।
iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate । tathā tvam api rājendra vasudhārāvrataṃ cara ।। prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇe sthāpya vrataṃ cāraya sarvadā ।। tathā te sarvadā kṣemaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।
kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।। iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। dhīmatyā ye avadānaṃ śubhaphaladam idaṃ suprasannāḥ śṛṇvanti ।
śrāvayanti pramuditamanasā bodhicaryānurāgāḥ । sarve te bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇadharāḥ sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhāḥ । śrīmanto lokaśreṣṭhā jinanilayagatāḥ saṃvasaṃti sukhāḍhyāḥ ।। athāśoko maharājaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā ।
upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata ।। bhadanta śrotum ichāmi vasudhārāvrataṃ kadā । kena kuha kathaṃ martyaloke pracāritaṃ purā ।। tad atra no bhavāñ cchāstar yathā pravarttitaṃ purā ।
tathā sarvaṃ samākhyātuṃ vistareṇa samarhati ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so arhan mahāmatiḥ । aśokaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu rājan yathākhyātaṃ guruṇā me srutaṃ mayā ।
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi vasudhārāvratodbhavaṃ ।। tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyamunis tathāgataḥ । sarvajño arhaṃ jagacchāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ ।। sa ekasamaye tatra kauśānvyā upakaṇṭhike ।ms ekaḥ samaye vihāre ghoṣirārāme vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ ।।
tadā śakrādayo devā brahmādi brāhmaṇā api । daityendrā lokapālāś ca saddharmaśravaṇotsukāḥ ।। rākṣasā garuḍā nāgā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ । siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi tathā cāpy apsarogaṇāḥ ।।
yogino yatayas tīrthā ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇaḥ । rājāno rājaputrāś ca vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo janāḥ ।। amātyāḥ sainikāś cāpi gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ । vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpinaḥ paurikā api ।।
grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathānyadeśavāsinaḥ । evam anye api lokāś ca saddharmāmṛtavāṃchinaḥ ।। sarve te tatra kauśāṃvyā ghoṣilārāma āgatāḥ । sabhāsanasamāsīnaṃ prādrākṣus taṃ munīśvaraṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā te muditāḥ sarve praṇatvā samupāsṛtāḥ । yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya kṛtvā tritvaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ ।। tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tatra te tatsabhāsīnā bhikṣavaḥ śrāvakā api ।
bhikṣuṇyaś cailakāś caivam upāsakā upāsikāḥ ।। bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ saṃbodhivratacāriṇaḥ । vasuṃdharāvratotpattiṃ śrotuṃ sarve samīchire ।। tatrānaṃdaḥ parijñāya teṣāṃ manaḥsamīhitaṃ ।
sāṃjaliḥ purataḥ sthitvā natvaivaṃ prārthayan muniṃ ।। bhagavan sarvavic chāstān ime sarve sabhājanāḥ । vasulakṣmīvratotpattiṃ śrotum ichanti āsṛtāḥ ।। tad bhavāṃs trijagacchāstā sarvasatvābhibodhane ।
vasulakṣmīvratotpattiṃ samupādeṣṭum arhati ।। ity ānaṃdena bhadreṇa prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ । tān sabhāsaṃsthitān sarvān samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇv ānanda pravakṣyāmi munīndreṇa yathoditaṃ ।
vajradharābdhigambhīranirghoṣeṇa śrutaṃ mayā ।। tadyathābhūt purā rājā sūryodayābhidho nṛpaḥ । śrīpure nagare ramye cakravarttī nṛpādhipaḥ ।। daśākuśalasaṃraktaḥ pramadājanavaśyagaḥ ।
tadā tatra narāḥ sarve apy asanmitropadeśataḥ । daśākusalamūleṣu karmasu saṃpracerire ।। tadā tatpāpadoṣeṇa mahetayaḥ pravarttitāḥ । tad ītisamupākrāntā saṃkṣobhitābhavan mahī ।।
tataḥ sarvatra deśeṣu durbhikṣam abhavad bhuvi । tadā te manujāḥ sarve daridrā abhavan kramāt ।। tatas te nirdhanāḥ sarve kṣutpipāsāhatāturāḥ । lobhitā nirdayāḥ krūrāḥ praduṣṭā duritāratāḥ ।
svakuladharmamaryādaṃ vilaṃghyāpy aśubhe acaran ।। tataḥ sarve api te lokā andhā iva kumārgagāḥ । asatsaṃgānusaṃraktāḥ pracerur narakāmukhāḥ ।। tadā tatpāpasaṃghṛṣṭaduḥkhāgniparitāpitā ।
śoṣitevābhavad bhūmī nirguṇā nīrasā kharā ।। tadā sarve api satvāś ca kṣuttṛṣṇāgnyahidāhitāḥ । nirāśā mṛtyum ichanto niṣeduḥ parimohitāḥ ।। tadaikasmin dine tatra tuṣitabhuvane sthitāḥ ।
śrīdevīpramukhā devyo vasundharyyāḥ sahāyikāḥ ।। sarvās tā militā martyaloke gaṃtuṃ samipsavaḥ । kim idānīṃ manuṣyāṇām avastheti samīkṣire ।। tatas tān manujān sarvān daridrān pāpacāriṇaḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā tāḥ sakalā devyā dayārttā evam abruvan ।। aho duḥkhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ yat pāpe niratā narāḥ । daridrā nirdayāḥ krūrā bhavanti narakāmukhāḥ ।। tat tatra martyaloke api daridryaduḥkhaśāntaye ।
yatnāc chrīvasudhārāyā vrataṃ cārayemahi ।। tatas te manujāḥ sarve śrutvā dṛṣṭvānumoditāḥ । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā careyur vratam ādarāt ।। tadā tatpuṇyasaṃpūtāḥ sarve te mānavā api ।
śrīmantaḥ sukhino bhadre careyuḥ sarvadādarāt ।। tatas te manujāḥ sarve daśakuśalasaṃratāḥ । parasparahitaṃ kṛtvā careyur bodhisaṃvaraṃ ।। tatas te bhadritātmānaḥ sarvasatvahitodyatāḥ ।
bodhisatvā mahāsatvā bhaveyur bodhicāriṇaḥ ।। tatas te sadguṇādhānās triratnabhajanāratāḥ । kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।। iti hetor vayaṃ sarvāḥ śrīdevyāḥ purato gatāḥ ।
etat sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ vijñāpayema sāṃprataṃ ।। ity evaṃ saṃmataṃ kṛtvā sarvā devvyo api tās tataḥ । śrīvasudhāmahādevyā ālaye samupācaran ।। tatra tāḥ sakalā devyaḥ sāṃjalaya upāsṛtāḥ ।
tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan ।। bhagavati mahādevi vijānīyād bhavaṃty api । yan manuṣyā daridrās te bhavanti pāpacāriṇaḥ ।। tad bhavatī prayatnena manujāns tān suduḥkhitān ।
kṛpayā sahasālokya sarvānn uddharttum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite tābhir devībhiḥ sā vasundharā । tā devī sakalā dṛṣṭvā prasannāsyaivam abravīt ।। aho duḥkhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ yatra śāstā na sadguruḥ ।
tena te akuśalācārāḥ sarve narā daridratāḥ ।। pāpābhis saṃratā duṣṭā kṣuttṛṣṇāgnyabhidāhitāḥ । durbhagā nirdayāḥ krūrāḥ pateyur narake dhruvaṃ ।। iti hetor ahaṃ tesāṃ martyānāṃ duḥkhaśāṃtaye ।
saṃvare tānn upasthāpya bodhau niyojayemahi ।। iti niścitya sā devī vasulakṣmī kṛpārditā । tatra samādhim ādhāya trimurttiṃ sā samādadhau ।। tadyathaikā vasuṃdharyyā mahālakṣmī dvitīyakā ।
tṛtīyikā kumāryyāś ca trimūrttir iti sā dadhe ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī gaṃtuṃ martyālaye svayaṃ । naṃdīmukhāśvaghoṣau dvau samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। naṃdīmukhāśvaghoṣau yan mayā saṃprārthitaṃ yathā ।
tathā tan me mahatkāryaṃ harttum arhatha sarvathā ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ tayā devyā niśamya tau kṛtāṃjaliḥ । nandimukhāśvaghoṣau tāṃ devīṃ natvaivam ūcatuḥ ।। devi kiṃ te mahat kāryaṃ tadā jñāpayatu dhruvaṃ ।
yathādiṣṭaṃ bhavaty āśu kariṣyāvas tathā khalu ।। iti tābhyāṃ samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā śrīvasuṃdharā । mahādevī prasannāsyā tau dṛṣṭvaivam abhāṣata ।। śṛṇuta bhadramukhau yan me kāryaṃ vāṃ tan mayocyate ।
tathā yuvāṃ samādhāya karttum arhatha sāṃprataṃ ।। yan narā bhūtale sarve daridrā atiduḥkhitā । pāpābhiniratā duṣṭā bhavanti narakāmukhāḥ ।। tat tān sarvān samuddharttum ichāmi sarvathā adhunā ।
tridhā mūrttim ahaṃ dhṛtvā gacheyaṃ tan mahītale ।। tayo rājā mahīpālaḥ sarvalokādhipaḥ prabhuḥ । taṃ evaṃ prathamaṃ dharme vinīya yojayemahi ।। yatra rājā svayaṃ dharme sthitvā caret samāhitaḥ ।
tatra sarve anugā rājño dharme careyur ādarāt ।। yatrābhinirato rājā carate apy aśubhe śubhe । tatra sarve api lokās te pracareyur hi sādaraṃ ।। ity ādau nṛpati dharme yojanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ । tataḥ sa nṛpatiḥ sārvāl lokān dharme niyojayet ।।
tataḥ sarve api lokās te daśākuśalavaimukhāḥ । saddharme hi ratā bhadre pracareyuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। tataḥ sarve api te lokāḥ parasparahitonmukhāḥ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā careyuḥ saṃvare sadā ।।
tatas te sarvadā śreyaḥ kṛtvā yāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ । tatrāpi saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā pracareyuḥ sukhānvitāḥ ।। tataḥ kramāt samādhāya sarvapāramitāsv api । carantaḥ sarvasatvānāṃ hitaṃ kuryuḥ sadādarāt ।।
tatas te bodhisatvāḥ syuḥ saddharmaguṇaratninaḥ । śuddhātmāno mahāsatvā bhaviṣyanti jinātmajāḥ ।। tataḥ sarve api te dhīrāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ । triyānabodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।।
iti hetor ahaṃ teṣāṃ satvānāṃ vinayārthataḥ । trimūrttirūpam ādhāya gachāmi bhūtale adhunā ।। tad yuvāṃ me vaco dhṛtvā gantum arhatha bhūtale । tatra gatvā prayatnena sarvathāhara taṃ nṛpaṃ ।।
tato ahaṃ taṃ vaśīkṛtya bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । saddharmacāriṇaṃ kṛtvā cārayiṣyāmi me vrataṃ ।। iti tayā mahādevyā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya tau । nandimukhāśvaghoṣau tāṃ devīṃ natvaivam ūcatuḥ ।।
bhadre devi tavādeśaṃ dhṛtvāvāṃ śirasā tathā । gatvā nṛpaṃ samāhṛtya prāṇayiṣyāvahe puraḥ ।। ity uktvā tau prasannāsyau kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । pādau devyāḥ praṇatvaivaṃ prajagmatus tato bhuvi ।।
trimūrttirūpam ādhāya vasulakṣmīr api svayaṃ । śrīdevyādisakhīyuktā gaṃgātīram upāgatāḥ ।। tatra tau bhūtale gatvā prāpaśyataṃ samaṃtataḥ । ramaṇīyaṃ mahodyāne puṣkariṇīpraśobhitaṃ ।।
dṛṣṭvā tāv ubhau tatra kṣaṇaṃ viśramya saṃsthitau । tato mithasamāsīnau dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samabhāṣatāṃ ।। aho ramyaṃ mahīlokaṃ taḍāgodyānamaṇḍitaṃ । tat katham iha rājānam apaharttuṃ carevahi ।।
tatra nandīmukhaḥ prāha divyastrīsuṃdaraṃ vapuḥ । dhṛtvāvāṃ surasaṃgītaṃ gāyantau prācarevahi ।। nūnaṃ sa nṛpatī rājā dṛṣṭvā nau divyasuṃdaraṃ । vapuḥ kāmāgnisaṃtaptaḥ samāharttum upācaret ।।
tadāvāṃ sahasāhṛtya nṛpatiṃ taṃ prayatnataḥ । mohayitvā vaśīkṛtya devyā upānayevahi ।। iti saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā vidhāya ca susaṃmataṃ । nandimukhāśvaghoṣau tau strīrūpaṃ dadhatus tathā ।।
tatas te divyarāmāṃśe manābhirāmaniḥsvanaiḥ । gāyaṃtyau surasaṃgītaṃ durgāsthane niṣedatuḥ ।। tayos tat surasaṃgītaṃ śrutvā tatpuravāsinaḥ । janāḥ kautūhalākrāntacittā draṣṭum upāsaran ।। dṛṣṭvā te divyarūpāṃśe sarve te vismayānvitāḥ ।
devakanye ime nūnam iti proktvā samīkṣire ।। divyāṃśe te samālokya sarve te vismayoddhatāḥ । aho citram iti proktvā pratyāyayuś cirāt puraṃ ।। tatra te surakanyāṃśe naikasthāne niṣedatuḥ ।
pratidinaṃ caturddikṣu pragāyaṃtyau praceratuḥ ।। tathā te caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te paurikā api । atyadbhutasamākrāṃtacittā ceruḥ praśaṃkitāḥ ।। tatas te paurikā lokāḥ sādbhutaśaṃkitāśayāḥ ।
nṛpateḥ purato gatvā praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayet ।। jaya deva mahārāja vijānīyā bhavānn api । tathāpy atra mahac citraṃ vijñaptuṃ vayam āgatāḥ ।। tad atra surarāmāṃśe ubhe striyau sulakṣaṇau ।
gāyantyau surasaṃgītaṃ durgāsthāne samāśrite ।। pratidinaṃ caturdikṣu tathā te devakanyake । gāyaṃtyo surasaṃgītaṃ bhramitvā carato mudā ।। tan nimittaṃ kathaṃ rājaṃ cchubhaṃ vā syād athāśubhaṃ ।
iti praṣṭuṃ samāyāmo vayaṃ sarve api nānyathā ।। iti taiḥ paurikaiḥ sarvair niveditaṃ niśamya saḥ । mahīpatiḥ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā tato dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt ।। strībhir ālāpitaṃ gītaṃ śubhāya na bhavet kvacit ।
ity uktvā sa viṣaṇṇātmā manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। kṣemaṃ neme bhaven nūnaṃ yat te striyau na mānave । strīrūpā vahinirmāya preṣite kena māyayā ।। tad atra kiṃ bhaven nūnaṃ tan nimittaṃ śubhaṃ na hi ।
kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi na manye ko hitaṃ diśet ।। iti ciṃttā viṣaṇṇātmā nṛpatiḥ sa viniśvasan । śokālaye samāsīno vahi naivācaret kvacit ।। tathā sthitaṃ narendraṃ taṃ matvā vahir anirgataṃ ।
nandīmukho asvaghoṣaṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। aśvaghoṣa narendro asau tathāpi na vahiś caret । tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo yan nṛpo na vahiś caret ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutva so aśvaghoṣo vicintayan ।
taṃ nandimukham ālokya bodhayann evam abravīt ।। śṛṇu naṃdimukhopāyaṃ yena nṛpaḥ sa nicaret । tad ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tan nṛpāharaṇaṃ prati ।। yat tatra nṛpater gehe māyāgninābhidhakṣyate ।
tadā sa nṛpatis trastaḥ kopito niḥsared vahi ।। tadā taṃ nṛpatiṃ dūrāt samāhṛtya prayatnataḥ । sahasā purato devyā upaneṣyāvahe drutaṃ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā nandīmukhaḥ sa bodhitaḥ ।
tathā hīti pratiśrutya tathā kartuṃ samaichata ।। tatas tau saṃmataṃ kṛtvā tato apy antarhitau drutaṃ । gatvā māyāgninā tābhyāṃ pradāhitaṃ nṛpālayaṃ ।। tad dṛṣṭvā nṛpatis trastaḥ sahasā niścarans tataḥ ।
upāyais taj jvaladvahniṃ śamayām āsa satvaraṃ ।। tataḥ sa bhūpatī rājā taccintāparikheṭitaḥ । śokāgare viṣaṇṇātmā sthitaś caiva vyacintayat ।। aho sadyaphalaṃ hy etad yat strīgītanimittajaṃ ।
tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yenaitac chāmyate aśubhaṃ ।। bhūyo apy atra bhaved anyan mahotpātam amaṃgalaṃ । katham atra pratīkāraṃ kariṣyāmi na manyate ।। iti ciṃtāviṣaṇṇātmā nṛpatiḥ sa vimohitaḥ ।
śokāgāre samāsīno naiva vahir viniryayau ।। tathāpi svālayāsīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā vahir ayāyinaṃ । nandīmukhāśvaghoṣau tau punar evaṃ samūcatuḥ ।। tathāpi sa nṛpo rājā naiva vahir viniḥsaret ।
tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo yenāśu niścaren nṛpaḥ ।। tataś cāpi samālokya so aśvaghoṣo vicintayan । naṃdīmukhaṃ sahāyaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। bho sakhe sa mahārājas tathāpi nātra niścaret ।
tad atra kiṃ vilambena yatnena taṃ harevahi ।। varāharūpam ādhāya tasyodyāne manorame । sarvatrotpātanaṃ kastuṃ pracārevo adhunā drutaṃ ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā naṃdīmukhas tatheti sā ।
pratiśrutya sakhāyaṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। evam api kariṣyāvo devīkāryābhisiddhaye । iti tau saṃmataṃ kṛtvā tatrodyāne prajagmatuḥ ।। tatra tau samupālokya puṣkariṇīṃ manoramāṃ ।
nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇāṃ paśyaṃtau tasthatuś ciraṃ ।। tato nandīmukho dṛṣṭvā tam udyānaṃ manoramaṃ । puskariṇīṃ ca prāmodya gaṃdhāḍhyām evam abravīt ।। ahodyānaṃ manoramyaṃ suramyaṃ ca saro varaṃ ।
nedaṃ vidhvaṃsanīyaṃ hi kathaṃ vidhvaṃsayevahi ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā so aśvaghoṣo viciṃtayan । udyānaṃ tat saro dṛṣṭvācirād evam abhāṣata ।। yathābhilaṣitaṃ devyāḥ sādhayeva tathā drutaṃ ।
tan nṛpatim apāharttuṃ tad idaṃ dhvaṃsayāvahe ।। ity uktvā saumataṃ kṛtvā tāv ubhau mahadāśrayaṃ । varāharūpam āsthāya prajagmatus sarastaṭe ।। raktākṣau hṛṣṭaromāṇau nādāpuritadiṅmukhau ।
siṃhaśārdūlasadṛśau damṣṭravibhīṣaṇānanau ।। tatra tau prasarantau tad udyānaṃ tat saro api ca । vindhvaṃsitum upākramya praceratuḥ samaṃtataḥ ।। tau varāhau samālokya traste udyānapālakaḥ ।
sahasā sa vinirgatya tato rājakule yayau ।। tatra sa samupāsṛtya rājñaḥ pādau kṛtāṃjaliḥ । natvā trāsavibhinnāsyaḥ pura evaṃ nyavedayat ।। jaya deva vijānīyā yad udyāne sarovaraṃ ।
dvau varāhāv upākramya dhvaṃsituṃ caratā adhunā ।। tad atra sahasā deva sarvasainyajanānn api । samupāhūya tau haṃtuṃ preṣayasva drutaṃ vane ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājā parikopitaḥ ।
sahasā sainyam āhūya svayaṃ tau hantum udyayau ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samaṃtrīsainyapaurikāḥ । sahasā nādayan vādyāns tatrodyāne upācarat ।। tatra sa nṛpatir dṛṣṭvā samaṃtrisainyapaurikān ।
tān sarvān samupāmaṃtrya punar evam upādiśat ।। bho bhavanto janāḥ sarve sajjīkṛtya samāhitāḥ । atra dṛṣṭvopatiṣṭhantu parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।। ahaṃ prāgdiśi tiṣṭhāmi yāmye amātyāḥ samaṃtriṇaḥ ।
paścimādiśi sainānyaḥ paurās tiṣṭhantu cottare ।। evaṃ sarve apy amātyādyāḥ sarvadikṣu samāhitāḥ । sajjīkṛtyābhitiṣṭhantu parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ ।। yatra sthāne varāhau tau boddhuṃ naivābhiśaknutha ।
yataś cāsau parāyetāṃ taddiksthān daṇḍayeya hi ।। iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā sarve yūyaṃ samāhitāḥ । sajjīkṛtya samālokya parivṛtyānutiṣṭhata ।। iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve api te janāḥ ।
tatheti prativijñapya tathā sthātuṃ pracerire ।। tathā rājā sthitaḥ prācyāṃ yāmye amātyagaṇās tathā । senānyo paścimāyāṃ ca paurās tasthus tathottare ।। evaṃ te sanṛpā lokāḥ sāmātyasainyapaurikāḥ ।
sajjīkṛtya samālokya sarve tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। evaṃ te sarvato dikṣu nirudhya samavasthitāḥ । sarvavādyābhinirghoṣaṃ mahārāvair akheṭayan ।। tat savādyamahārāvaṃ śrutvā tau tān upasthitān ।
samaṃtataḥ samālokya mahāśabdaṃ vyamuṃcatāṃ ।। tatas tau sahasotpātamahāvāte pravarttataiḥ । kṛtvāndhakāraṇair lokya rājānam adhyadhāvatāṃ ।। tatra sa nṛpatis tābhyāṃ spṛśyamāno vimūrchitaḥ ।
saṃtrāsaparibhūyātmā kaṃpito nyapatad bhuvi ।। tataś cirāt samutthāya kutremāv iti lokya saḥ । sahasāśvaṃ samāruhya tad anuprāsaran yayau ।। tathā te maṃtriṇo amātyāḥ sainyalokāś ca paurikāḥ ।
sarve te apy anudhāvantaḥ pradudruvur nṛpānugāḥ ।। sa nṛpāśvasamārūḍhas tadvarāhānugaḥ śaraṃ । maurvīyuktaiḥ samādhāya vegād vanam upāviśat ।। tatra tau māyikau tyaktvā vārāhadeham āśu tau ।
niviśyāśvaṃ samāhṛtya prerayatāṃ vanāṃtare ।। tatra so aśvo mahāvegād vāyunā riva mahājavi । vilaṃghya nimnagāṃ chailāṃ pradudrāva mahāvane ।। tatas te maṃtriṇo amātyāḥ sainānyaḥ sainikāḥ prajāḥ ।
nṛpaṃ dūravanāviṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā pratyāyayuḥ śramāt ।। sena eko mahāvīraḥ svāmyamārgānusaṃcaran । asakteḥ asahas tūrṇaṃ kamaṇḍalukaras tadā ।। chāyeva sahago vegād vanāṃtare tathānvagāt ।।
tatrātivegato rājā vāyuhato samāhitaḥ । aśvavṛkṣatale so aśvād dhāvatā nyapatad bhuvi ।। tatra sa mūrchito rājā kṣaṇaṃ tasthāv acetanaḥ । tataḥ senaḥ prayatnena niḥśvasanrudatiṣṭhata ।।
tataḥ sena samāśvāsya dhṛtvā taṃ nṛpam ātmanā । saha tatrāsane sthāpya vyaśrāmayec chramānvitaṃ ।। tataḥ sa nṛpa ālokya tam aśvaṃ samupasthitaṃ । tṛṣārtto niḥśvasan senaṃ muhur dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt ।।
aho sena mahat kaṣṭaṃ jāyate nāv ihā adhunā । yat sudūre mahāraṇye majjāvahe sudustare ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo yat sarve nirvṛto janāḥ । sudūre nirjane araṇye ko atra mārgaṃ hi nirdiśet ।।
yad atrātitṛṣārtto ahaṃ tāpavātāhatāturaḥ । śramakleśāgnisaṃdagdho dhairyeṇāpi vimocitaḥ ।। tad atra sahasā sena mama jīvitarakṣaṇaṃ । yatas tato api vānviṣya śītalāmṛtam ānaya ।।
iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā sa seneḥ sahasotthitaḥ । svāminaṃ taṃ samāśvāsya paśyann evam abhāṣata ।। mā viṣīdāta rājendra yat kṣatriyo asi dhīravān । tad bhavān dhairyam ālambya muhurttaṃ sthātum arhati ।।
yatas tato api vānviṣya pāṇīyam amṛtopamaṃ । sahasā samupānīya dāsyāmi te narādhipa ।। tad yāvannātra pāṇīyaṃ dhṛtvāgachāmi sarvathā । tāvad dhairyaṃ samālambya tiṣṭhāśvena saha prabho ।।
iti vijñapya seno asau svāminaṃ taṃ narādhipaṃ । samāśvāsya supāṇīyam anveṣituṃ drutaṃ yayau ।। tatra sa samupālokya sarvatrāpy abhilokayan । supāṇīyam anasādya paśyan dūratare yayān ।।
tatra suranadīśabdaṃ śrutvā senaḥ sa satvaraḥ । tac chabdaṃ samanuśrutvā tatrābhyanusaran yayau ।। tatra tīraṃ samāsādya suranadyāḥ samāditaḥ । sahasā samupāśritya pānīyaṃ surasaṃ papau ।।
tatra sa parituṣṭātmā samaṃtato vilokayan । tatpāre śuddhite dvīpe prādrākṣīd apsarogaṇān ।। tān apsarogaṇān dṛṣṭvā sa seno vismayānvitaḥ । mudā vilokayann eva tasthau citrārppitā yathā ।।
tatrasthaṃtaṃ samālokya sarvā apsaraso api tāḥ । katham atrāgataḥ kas tvaṃ prehīti samakandayan ।। iti tābhiḥ samāhūtaṃ śrutvā sa sena ātmanā । suranadīṃ vilaṃghyāśu tatprabhāvād upāsarat ।।
tatra sa samupāśritya sarvāns tān apsarogaṇān । sāṃjaliḥ suprasannāsyaḥ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat ।। mahādevyā vijānīdhvaṃ yat trailokyeṣu viśrutaḥ । sūryodayo mahārājas tasyāhaṃ sevako anugaḥ ।।
yan nṛpasya varāhābhyāṃ udyānaṃ dhvaṃsitaṃ tataḥ । tau varāhau nihaṃtuṃ sa nṛpo anudhāvati drutaṃ ।। aśvenāpahṛto rājā sa mayaikena naujjhitaḥ । atyabhidhāvato araṇye patito aśvād ihā adhunā ।।
aśokavṛkṣa āśritya gharmavātā hato aturaḥ । śramatṛsārditas tatra sthito ambu pātum ichati ।। tad ambu sarvato anviṣya kutrāpi labhyate na hi । nadīśabdam ihākarṇya sahasāham upāsare ।।
atra me bhāgyayogena preṣito aham ihāgataḥ । labhāmi darśanaṃ devyo bhavāṃtīnam aho adhunā ।। ity uktvā sena ālokya sāṃjaliḥ purato gataḥ । tāḥ sarvā apsarā devīnatvaitaṃ samapṛchata ।।
bho devyo bhavantyo api kim artham iha tiṣṭhatha । vaktavyaṃ cet tad arthaṃ me samupādeṣṭum arhatha ।। iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena niśamyāyāpsaro adhipāḥ । sā taṃ senaṃ samāmaṃtrya purar evam upādiśat ।।
mānava tvaṃ na jānāsi yad idaṃ vratam uttamaṃ । śrīvasudhāmahādevyā vayaṃ sarvāś carāmahe ।। iti devyā tayākhyātaṃ śrutvā senaḥ sa moditaḥ । tad vrataṃ dharttum ichaṃs tāṃ devīṃ natvaivam abravīt ।।
prasīda me mahādevi yac chrīdevyā idaṃ vrataṃ । aham api samichāmi dhartuṃ tan me upādiśa ।। iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sā devī paritoṣitā । taṃ senaṃ sudhiyaṃ dhīraṃ matvaivam abravīt punaḥ ।।
mānava vadi te vāṃchāpy asti śrīvasudhāvrate । tat tāvad iha saṃpaśya samāpyetā adhunā vrataṃ ।। paścāt te ahaṃ samākhyāya śrīdevyā vratasādhanaṃ । vidhiṃ samupadekṣyāmi saṃbuddhena yathoditaṃ ।।
ity uktvā sāpsaro devī sarvās tā apsarogaṇāḥ । prāhūya tan nadītīre vratārambhaṃ tathākarot ।। tatra tāḥ samupāśritya sarvā devyā yathākramaṃ । yathāvidhi samārabhya vrataṃ pūrṇaṃ pracakrire ।।
tad vrataṃ samupālokya sa seno abhyanumoditaḥ । aṣṭāṃgapraṇatiṃ kṛtvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt ।। aho bhāgyena saṃprāptaṃ śridevīvratadarśanaṃ । tan metiḥ kṣīyate pāpam ātmāri śuddhyate adhunā ।।
prasīdata mahādevyaḥ sarvā me kṛpayā dṛśā । paśyantyo anugrahaṃ kṛtvā vrate pradātum arhataṃ ।। sarvadāhaṃ cariṣyāmi śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । tad vratavidhi saṃpūrṇaṃ samupādeṣṭum arhatha ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā devī pradhānikā । sā taṃ senaṃ viśuddhāṃśaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samupādiśat ।। śṛṇu sādho samādhāya vratavidhiṃ samucyate । vajradharābdhigaṃbhīranirghoṣeṇa yathoditaṃ ।।
bhādrapade asite pakṣe śuklapakṣe api vā tathā । māghe māse ca tadvac ca sarveṣv api ca māsu vā ।। dvitīyāyām upātīrthe snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ । śuddhabhūmī pradeśeṣu saṃśodhayet samaṃtataḥ ।।
mṛdgomayaśubhāmbhobhiḥ pralipya pariśodhayan । tatra ratnamayaraṅgai dhātucūrṇaiś ca paṃcabhiḥ ।। pauṣpikair vrīhicūrṇair vā tathā pāṣāṇacūrṇakaiḥ । yathāvidhi samārabhya sūtrayitvā yathākramaṃ ।।
guruḥ śiṣyaiḥ sahālakṣya varttayen maṇḍalaṃ kramāt । tatra devyādi cihnāni likhed yathāvidhi kramāt ।। saptavrīhyāvalībhiś ca saṃveṣṭayet samaṃtataḥ । tatas tīrthāmbusaṃpūrṇān pītavastrāvṛtān ghaṭān ।
ṣoḍaśadevatācihna lakṣitān pariśuddhitān ।। paṃcaratnāmṛtauṣadhyapallavapratisaṃyutān । suvarṇatilakachatradhvajapatākikānvitān ।। bahiḥ pītāmbujāvalyāṃ saṃsthāpya veṣṭayet kramāt ।
dhvajacāmarasaṃyuktavitānaiḥ parimaṃḍayet ।। vicitrapuṣpamālābhiḥ sugaṃdhibhiḥ samaṃtataḥ । saurabhyadhūpanai dīpai paṃktibhiś cābhiśobhayet ।। tatas tanmaṇḍale devīṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ ।
dhyātvāvāhya samabhyarcya pratiṣṭhāpyādhivāsayet ।। tato rātrau trisaṃdhyaṃ ca samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ । baliṃ paṃcāmṛtair yuktaṃ datvā devīṃ smaraṃś caret ।। tataḥ prātas tṛtīyāyāṃ tīrthe dravyaiḥ sugaṃdhibhiḥ ।
saha śuddhāmbubhiḥ snātvā śuddhapītāmvarāvṛtaḥ ।। paṃcagavyaiḥ svam ātmānaṃ pariṣiṃcya viśodhayet । maṇḍale sagaṇāṃ devīṃ dhyātvāvāhya samarcayet ।। vratīnāpi tathā snātvā śuddhapītāmvarāvṛtāḥ ।
paṃcagavyais tathā sarvār abhisiṃcya viśodhayet ।। tatas te vratinaḥ sarve ācāryyapramukhāḥ kramāt । madhyāhne yakṣarājasya digmukhāḥ svāsanāḥ śritāḥ ।। yathācāryasamādiṣṭaṃ tathādhārya samāhitāḥ ।
ādau vajradharaṃ natvā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। maṃtrale sagaṇāṃ devīṃ dhyātvārcaye yathākramaṃ ।। tadyathā gurur ācāryaḥ śūnye drīkārasaṃbhavaṃ । pītavarṇaṃ mahāpad maṃ tatrasthaṃ candramaṇḍalaṃ ।
tadutthaṃ śrībhavaṃ ratnaparvataṃ tasya copari । tvaṃja bhadraghaṭāsīnāṃ bhāvayec chrīvasuṃdharāṃ ।। pītām ekamukhāṃ kāṃtām ṣaḍbhujāṃ lalitāsanāṃ । savye varadasaṃbuddhaṃ praṇāmaratnamaṃjalīṃ ।।
vāme bhadraghaṭaprajñā pustakadhānyamaṃjaliṃ । dadhānaṃ ratnasaṃbuddhamakuṭinīṃ susuṃdarīṃ ।। pītapaṭṭāvṛtāṃ divyaratnālaṃkārabhūṣitaṃ । tad dvitīyapuṭe pṛṣṭhe pīto vajrāsano jināḥ ।।
vajradharābdhinirghoṣo varābhayapradānabhṛt ।। dakṣiṇe dvibhujārakto varadavajrahastakaḥ । lokeśvaro rājallīlāvajraparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ ।। vajrapāṇis tathā vāme varadavajrabhṛtkaraḥ ।
haritā rājasaṃlīlā vajraparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ ।। līlā devī puraḥ pītā satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitā । bhujadvayena sarvopakaraṇādhikṛtiṃ tadā ।। tad vāme varuṇaḥ śvetaḥ satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ ।
vījapūrakam utsaṅgasthitiṃ karadvayena bhṛt ।। nīlobhe dakṣiṇe bhadraḥ satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ । bījapūrakam ekena vibhrat kroḍaṃ tathāparaṃ ।। civikuṇḍalir āgneye iṣadraktas tathāsthitaḥ ।
bījapūrakam utsaṅge sthitiṃ dorbhyāṃ samā tathā ।। nairṛtye kelimālī ca śyāmavarṇas tathā sthitaḥ । bījapūrakam utsaṃgasthitaṃ dadhat karadvayaḥ ।। vāyavye ca mukhendrākhyaḥ pītavarṇas tathā sthitaḥ ।
bījapūrakam utsaṃgasthitiṃ dadhat karadvayaṃ ।। carendro gaurar iśāne satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ । bījapūrakam utsaṃgasthitiṃ dadhad bhujadvayaḥ ।। tat tṛtīyapuṭe pūrve guptā devī tathā sthitā ।
haridvarṇā bhujābhyāṃ sa cāmaraṃ vibhratī dharā ।। nairṛte vasuguptākhyā devī raktās tathā sthitā । bhujābhyāṃ vibhratī chatraṃ sarvaratnasamujvalaṃ ।। sarasvatī ca vāyavye devī pītā tathā sthitā ।
dhvajahastā subhadrāṃgī sarvavidyārthadāyinī ।। iśāne caṃdrakāṃtākhyā devī śvetā tathā sthitā । patākā vibhratī sarvaratnālaṃkārabhūṣitā ।। pūrvadvāre mahāyakṣo māṇibhadras tathā sthitaḥ ।
kuṃkumābhā dadhad dorbhyāṃ nakulībījapūrakau ।। dakṣiṇe pūrṇabhadrākhyo nīlavarṇas tathāsthitaḥ । karābhyāṃ vidadhad ratnastavakaṃ bījapūrakaṃ ।। paścime dhanado raktaḥ satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ ।
bhujadvayena vibhrāṇaḥ sughaṭabījapūrakau ।। uttare pītavarṇaś ca vaiśravaṇas tathā sthitaḥ । bhujābhyāṃ saṃdadhad ratnaprasavabījapūrakauḥ ।। ity etā devatā sarvāḥ śrīdevīpramukhān kramāt ।
dhyātvāvāhya tato datvā pādyācamanaprokṣaṇaṃ ।। tatas tā maṇḍale sarvāḥ pratiṣṭhāpya yathā kramaṃ । ṣoḍaśavidhipūjāṃgaiḥ samarcayed yathā vidhi ।। gaṃdhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ naivedyam eva ca ।
ete paṃcopacārās tu kaivalyaphaladāyinaḥ ।। pādyam arghyaṃ tathā snānaṃ madhuparkācanaṃ tathā । gaṃdhaṃ puṣpaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca dīpaṃ naivedyam eva ca । pūtanācamanīyaṃ ca daśaitān saṃpracakṣyate ।।
āsanaṃ svāgataṃ pādyam arghyam ācamanīyakaṃ । madhuparkācamanasnānaṃ vasanābharaṇāni ca ।। sugaṃdhasumano dhūpadīpanaivedyacaṃdanaṃ । prayojayed arcanāyām upacārās tu ṣoḍaśaḥ ।।
tato devyāḥ svahṛtmaṃtraṃ tathā upahṛdayaṃ japet । sarvāsām api maṃtrāṇi yāvac chatasahasradhā ।। tataḥ stotrādibhi stutvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāny evaṃ aṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇayet punaḥ ।।
tataś ca sāṃjaliḥ sthitvā prakuryāt pāpadeśanāṃ । puṇyānumodanāṃ capi saṃsthitiyācanām api ।। tataḥ kṣīrodanaiḥ śuddharasaiḥ paṃcāmṛtair yutaṃ । baliṃ gāthāḥ paṭhan dadyāt sarvabhūtā hi tuṣṭaye ।।
tathā te vratinaḥ sarve sarvaṃ dhṛtvā samāhitāḥ । yathā śāstrā samādiṣṭam anukuryu vrataṃ kramāt ।। tatas te vratinaḥ sarve dānaṃ dadyuḥ sa dakṣiṇaṃ । gurave devatābhyo api praṇameyuś ca sādaraṃ ।।
tataḥ kṣamārthanaṃ kṛtvā sūtraṃ ṣoḍaśabheditaṃ । ṣoḍaśagraṃthitaṃ pītaṃ vratibhyo gurur arpayet ।। tat sūtraṃ te samādāya sarve api vratino mudā । rakṣārthaṃ svakare vadhvā dadhyur vratasamāptitaḥ ।।
tatas te vratinaḥ sarve dhṛtvā saṃpattiprārthanāṃ । natvā kṣamārthanāṃ cāpi kṛtvā careyur utthitāḥ ।। tato dinatriyāmāgre yavagodhūmapiṣṭakaṃ । saha paṃcāmṛtaiḥ sarvaiḥ kuryus tadvratapālanāṃ ।।
tatas tevratinaḥ sarve snātvā cāpi samāhitāḥ । dīpamālāḥ samujvālya tiṣṭheyu niśi jāgritāḥ ।। tāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ smṛtvā paṭhanto dhāraṇīm api । japastotrādikaṃ kṛtvā toṣayeyur upasthitāḥ ।।
evaṃ te tan niśāṃ sarve vyatilaṃghya punas tathā । prātaḥ sugaṃdhibhis tīrthe snātva śuddhāmvarāvṛtāḥ ।। tāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ dhyātvā samāvāhya yathākramaṃ । sarvapūjopahāraiś ca prārcayeyus tathādarāt ।। japastotrādikaṃ kṛtvā ratvā sāṃjalayo mudā ।
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ cāpi kuryur aṣṭāṅgaprāṇatiṃ ।। tataś ca purataḥ sthitvā prakuryuḥ pāpadeśanāṃ । puṇyānumodanāṃ cāpi prārthayeyuḥ susaṃsthitiṃ ।। tataḥ saṃbodhicaryārthaṃ sarvasatvahitārthataḥ ।
sarvadravyasusaṃpattiḥ prārthayeyur yathechayā ।। tato guruṃ samabhyarcya datvā dānaṃ sadakṣiṇaṃ । śraddhayā praṇatiṃ kṛtvā toṣayeyuḥ samādarāt ।। tato bhūtavaliṃ datvā prārthayitvā yathepsitaṃ ।
kṛtvā kṣamārthanāṃ cāpi visarjayed yathāvidhi ।। tataḥ śāstā sa ācāryaḥ kṛtvā cāpi kṣamārthanāṃ । saṃpūrṇaṃ tad vrataṃ kṛtvā vratasūtraṃ samāharet ।। tato abhiṣekam ādāya vratināpy abhiṣiṃcayet ।
śubhāśiṣaṃ pradatvā ca tan maṇḍalaṃ visarjayet ।। tatas tad rajam ādāya koṣṭhāgāre suguptite । nikṣipya pratisaṃsthāpya nityaṃ namet sadādarāt ।। aparaṃ puṣpādikaṃ sarvaṃ nirmālyaṃ savid ambhasi ।
nāgān abhyarcya tat sarvaṃ samarppitvā pravāhayet ।। tan nadījalam ādāya gṛhe tataḥ samācaret । tatra sarvatra geheṣu tajjalair abhiṣiṃcayet ।। tatas tan maṇḍale sthāne samāvāhya yathāvidhi ।
śrīkumārīṃ mahādevīṃ samabhyarcya hi toṣayet ।। tatprasādaṃ samādāya gaṇacakraṃ yathāvidhi । samabhyarcya yathārheṇa bhojanenapi toṣayet ।। evaṃ tad vratasaṃpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā sarve pramoditāḥ ।
śrivasudhāṃ mahādevīṃ smṛtvā careyur ābhavaṃ ।। evam etad vidhānena śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । yathāvidhi samādhāya vrataṃ caret samādarāt ।। tasya gṛhe tad ārabhya śrīdevī śrīvasundharā ।
svayam āgatya sarvatra kṣemaṃ kṛtvā vaset sadā ।। tad ārābhya sadā tasya gṛhe sarvatra maṃgalaṃ । nirupadravam ānaṃdaṃ sarvadāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। tatas tasya gṛhe saṃpad dine dine pravarddhitā ।
sarvadravyābhisaṃpūrṇā śrīdasyeva samudbhavet ।। atha cāpi tathā śaktau yaḥ śrāddhaḥ puruṣaḥ sudhīḥ । snātvā śuddhāmvaro gehe śodhayitvā samaṃtataḥ ।। śrīdevyāḥ pratimāyaivaṃ paṭaṃ vāpi prasārya ca ।
yathāśakti samabhyarcya dhāraṇīṃ sarvadā paṭhet ।। tasyāpi ca gṛhe tiṣṭhec chrīdevī sagaṇānvitā । tathā tatra bhaved evaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।। tadā tasya gṛhe saṃpad dine dine hi varddhate ।
sarvadravyābhisaṃpūrṇā bhaven na kṣiṇuyāt kvacit ।। atha vā prāktane pītarajasā maṃḍalaṃ tathā । varttayitvātra tad rātrīṃ niyamenātināmayet ।। prātaḥ snātvā sugaṃdhena śuddhapītāmvarāvṛtaḥ ।
brahmacārī viśuddhātmā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ dhyātvāhya samāhitaḥ । yathāśakti samabhyarcya dhāraṇīṃ śraddhayā paṭhet ।। tasyāpi ca gṛhe bhadraṃ kṛtvā devī vaset sadā ।
tatas tathā kramāt saṃpat parivṛddhā bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। atha prātas tathā snātvā śuddhavastrāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ । brahmacārī samādhāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। śubhe sthāne paṭaṃ cāpi devyā mūrttiṃ prasārya ca ।
yāthāśakti samabhyarcya trivārān dhāraṇīṃ paṭhet ।। tasyāpi ca gṛhe bhadraṃ kṛtvā devī sadā vaset । tathā tatra mahāsaṃpad abhivṛddhā bhaved dhruvaṃ ।। atha vā ca tathā snātvā śuddhavastrāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ ।
brahmacārī viśuddhātmā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। śubhe sthāne gṛhe devyāś candanenāpi maṃḍalaṃ । varttayitvā tathā devīṃ dhyatvāvāhya samarcayet ।। saṃpaṭhed dhāraṇīṃ caivaṃ kuryāj japastavādikaṃ ।
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāny evaṃ natvā saṃprārthayen nidhiṃ ।। tasyāpi ca gṛhe devī maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ । kṛtvā svayaṃ samāśritya nivaset sarvadā dhruvaṃ ।। tatas tatra gṛhe saṃpatsarvadravyasamanvitā ।
abhivṛddhya bhaven nūnaṃ nidhiś cāpi samudbhavet ।। atha vā svagṛhe śuddhe kośakoṣṭhālaye api ca । tathā paragṛhe vāpi manoramye abhiśodhite ।। atha tathāgatasyāpi lokeśasyāpi cāgrataḥ ।
tathānyabodhisatvānāṃ devatānāṃ tathāgrataḥ ।। candanenāpi kṛtvaivaṃ śrīdevyā maṇḍalaṃ tathā । vidhivan manasā dhyātvā samāvāhya samarcayet ।। tathā tathāgatānaṃ ca trailokādhipater api ।
tathānyabodhisatvānāṃ yathāśakti samarcayet ।। tatas tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīṃ dhyātvā japet samāhitaḥ । saṃpaṭhed dhāraṇīṃ cāpi śraddhayā bhaktimānasaḥ ।। tatha caikam ahorātram avichinnaṃ paṃthen mudā ।
yāvat tripaṃcasaptāhorātrāṇi ca paṭhet tathā ।। ācāryaś ca tathā rātrau striḥ kṛtvā divasasya ca । sa lokapālabhūtebhyo baliṃ dadyād yathāvidhi ।। tato dānapatiḥ śāstre sarvopakaraṇādikaṃ ।
dāne sadakṣiṇaṃ dadyād anyebhyo api tathādarāt ।। tataś ca sāṃjalir natvā prārthayitvā kṣamām api । saṃbodhisādhanīṃ dravyasaṃpattiṃ prārthayen mudā ।। tataḥ sarvaṃ samāpyaivaiḥ kṛtvāpi tad visarjanaṃ ।
yathārhabhojanaiḥ sarvāñ chāstrādīn samatoṣayet ।। tan maṇḍale rajaḥ sarvaṃ samādāya sapuṣpakaṃ । koṣṭhakoṣṭhālayāgāre nikṣipya sthāpayet sadā ।। tad rajo yatra nikṣiptaṃ tatra saṃpat pravarddhitaḥ ।
sarvadravyābhisaṃpūrṇā bhaven na kṣiṇuyāt kvacit ।। nirmālyam aparaṃ sarvaṃ sanaivedyadhvajādikaṃ । nadyāṃ nāgān samabhyarya saṃprakṣipya pravāhayet ।। tatas tad dhāraṇīvidyā bhavet paṭhitasiddhitā ।
yatrāpi paṭhyate tatra saṃpat pravarddhitā bhavet ।। evaṃ satyaṃ samākhyātaṃ sarvair api munīśvaraṃ । śrīdevyāḥ sādhanaṃ kalyaṃ matvaivaṃ cara tad vrataṃ ।। ya evaṃ śrīmahādevyāḥ śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
yathāvidhi samādhāya carate vratam ādarāt ।। tasya māragaṇāḥ sarve satvopadravakārakāḥ । viheṭhanāṃ sadā kvāpi karttu maivābhiśaknuyuḥ ।। sarvaśakrādayo devāḥ sarvadaityādhipā api ।
grahās tārāś ca siddhāś ca sādhyā vidyādharā api ।। lokapālāś ca sarve api gaṃdharvāḥ kiṃnarā api । yakṣāś ca rākṣasāḥ sarve nāgāś ca garuḍā api ।। mātṛkā bhairavāḥ sarve sakumāravināyakāḥ ।
mahākālāś ca ḍākinyaḥ śākinyo api tathāparāḥ ।। yoginyo api tathā sarve vīrā yamāntakādayaḥ । rakṣanti sarvadā nityaṃ śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇāśritaṃ ।। dhāraṇīpāṭhakaṃ yo api sādhakaṃ vratacāriṇaṃ ।
tathā bhūtagaṇāḥ sarve piśācāś ca durāśayāḥ ।। sarve jvarādayo rogā apasmārādayo api ca ।। unmādā piṭakāś cāpi sarve kuṣṭhāś ca kachavaḥ । śrīdevīvratino dehe na spṛśaṃti kadācana ।।
ītayaś ca tathā sarvā mahopadravakārakāḥ । tasya deśe gṛhe dehe na viśanti kadā cana ।। vasuṃdharyā vrate yatra dhāraṇī ca pravarttate । tatra māragaṇā duṣṭā upasargā viśanti na ।।
nṛpāgnyudakā caurādi duṣṭāḥ śaṭhāś ca vaṃcakāḥ । śrīdevīvratinaḥ kiṃcid apakartuṃ na śaknuyuḥ ।। yaś ca śrīvasudhārāyā bhaktimāñ charaṇaṃ gataḥ । sarvadā smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajate saṃcarad vrataṃ ।।
yaś ca tasyā mahādevyā dhāraṇīṃ muditaḥ smaran । paṭhate sarvadāpy evaṃ parebhyo api samādiśet ।। yaś caitad dhāraṇīṃ samyag alikhel likhāyayed api । likhitāṃ samādāya saṃsthāpya bhajate gṛhe ।।
yaś cāpi hṛdayaṃ devyā likhitvā bhūrjapatrake । mūrddhni kaṇṭhe bhuje vāhau dadhāti nityam ādarāt ।। teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ māravighnopasargikāḥ । sarve api sarvadā kvāpi hy apakarttuṃ na śaknuyuḥ ।। sarve api bodhisatvās te traidhātukanivāsinaḥ ।
etadvidyānubhāvena dānapāramitāśritāḥ ।। sarvopakaraṇaiḥ sarvān satvān saṃtarppayanty api । tathā dānaṃ sadā kṛtvā bodhimārge caranti ye ।। te sarve krameṇaivaṃ pūrya pāramitā daśaḥ ।
sarvān māragāṇāṃ jitvā prāpnuyu bodhisaṃpadaṃ ।। sarvabhūpāś ca rājānaś cakravarttyādayo nṛpāḥ । pālayanti prajā lokān dharmair lakṣmīvratodbhavaiḥ ।। evam anye api lokāś ca ye ye saṃpatsamṛddhitāḥ ।
mahādhanā mahābhogāḥ sarvadravyasamanvitāḥ ।। datvā dānaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā yāvajjīvaṃ śubhe sadā । pracaranty api sarve te jñeyā lakṣmīprasādataḥ ।। ye śrīdevyā vrataṃ dhṛtvā sarvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ ।
dadāti te mahāsatvāḥ śrīmantaḥ sadguṇānvitāḥ ।। yaśaḥsaṃpatsamāpannāḥ sarvavidyākalāspadāḥ । dharmātmāno maheśākhyaḥ sudhiyaḥ satyavādinaḥ ।। suśīlāḥ subhagā bhadrāḥ kṣāntisaurabhyavāsinaḥ ।
saumyendriyā viśuddhāṃgāḥ karuṇārdraśubhāśayāḥ ।। balavīryamahotsāhā niḥkleśāḥ susamāhitāḥ । jitendriyā mahādhīrāḥ prajñāvanto vicakṣaṇāḥ ।। upāyavidhivijñāś ca sarvasatvahitārthinaḥ ।
supraṇidhisamādhānā balino brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। jñānavijñānavidvānsaḥ sarvasatvaśubhaṃkarāḥ । bodhisatvā jagannāthā buddhātmajā bhavaṃty api ।। yatibhir nā atītās te varttamānā anāgatāḥ ।
te api sarve mahādevyā vratapuṇyānubhāvataḥ ।। kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya samāhitāḥ । bodhilabdhā bhavaṃty evaṃ lapsyaṃti nānyathā khalu ।। evaṃ matvā mahāvidyaṃ śrīdevīṃ dhāraṇīṃ parāṃ ।
samādhāya paṭhan nityaṃ vrataṃ cara samādarāt ।। eṣā mahaiśvarī devī bodhilakṣmīr jineśvaśrī । jananī sarvabuddhānāṃ dhātrī mātānupālinī ।। adhṛṣyā sarvaduṣṭānāṃ sarvavighnavināśinī ।
mahāvidyeśvarī bhadrā sarvāriṣṭhanisūdanī ।। yasyāḥ śaraṇamātreṇa vrataṃ caraṃti mānavāḥ । dāridryaduḥkhaśokāgnau na pataṃti kadāpi te ।। acintitāni ratnādi dhanadravyaguṇāni ca ।
yaśodharmārthakāmādi sukhāni samavāpnuyuḥ ।। etatpuṇyam asaṃkhyeyam aprameyaṃ mahattaraṃ । sarvair api munīndrair hi saṃkhyātuṃ nāpi śakyate ।। sarve vratajapuṇyānāni saṃkhyātum abhiśakyate ।
tad etadvratapuṇyānāṃ saṃkhyātuṃ kena śakyate ।। yad etadvratasādṛśyaṃ kutrāpi no hi vidyate । tad adhikaṃ kuto loke sarvatrāpi na dṛśyate ।। īdṛk puṇyamahāratnaṃ trailokyeṣv api durllabhaṃ ।
triratnabhajanād eva labhyate bhuvi mānavaṃ ।। tad evaṃ tvaṃ parijñāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । śrīdevīṃ vidhināvāhya vrataṃ cara samāhitaḥ ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarvadā sadgatīṃ gataḥ ।
śrīsaṃpattisamāpannaḥ pradātā sukhabhṛd bhavet ।। trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।। iti hetor mahādevyāḥ svayaṃ tvaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । vrataṃ caraṃs tathā loke pracāraya samaṃtataḥ ।।
iti tayā mahādevyāḥ samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya saḥ । senaḥ kṛtāṃjalir natvā tāṃ devīm evam abravīt ।। evaṃ devi kariṣyāmi bhavatyājñāṃ śiro vahan । tat prasīda mahādevyā dhāraṇīṃ saṃpradehi me ।।
iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sā saṃprasāditā । devī taṃ senam ālokya samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu sena gṛhāṇa tvaṃ devyāyā dhāraṇīṃ varāṃ । svayaṃ paṭhaṃ parebhyo api deśayasva yathāvidhi ।।
ity ādiśyāpsarorūpā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । tasmai senāsu tāṃ devyā dhāraṇīṃ saṃpaṭhan dadau ।। sa senas tāṃ mahādevīṃ praṇatvā sāṃjalir mudā । śrīdevyā dhāraṇīṃ vidyāṃ praṇatvā śraddhayādade ।।
tataḥ sā cāpsaro devī tasmai senāya sādaraṃ । sa paṃcāmṛtagodhūmai piṣṭakaṃ pālane dadau ।। tad dattaṃ piṣṭataṃ taṃ sa seno dṛṣṭvā pramoditaḥ । praṇatvādāya taṃ bhūpaṃ smṛtvā na bubhuje svayaṃ ।।
tadā divyapsarorūpaṃ tyaktvā sākṣāt trimūrttidhṛk । caṃdramaṇḍalamadhyasthabhadraghaṭoparisthitā ।। darśayām āsa rūpaṃ svaṃ prabhāmaṇḍalavarttitaṃ । anyā devyo api rūpaṃ svaṃ dhṛtvā devīṃ vasuṃdharāṃ ।।
parivṛtya puro dhāya patākādhvajacāmaraiḥ । vījayaṃtyaḥ sarvadikṣu tasthu saṃproktarūpavat ।। tataḥ sa sena utthāya tāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ mudā । muhurmuhur vaddhagala aṣṭāṅgaiḥ praṇatiṃ vyadhāt ।।
tataḥ sa sena ādhāya sapaṃcāmṛtapiṣṭakaṃ । taṃ jalaṃ ca samādhāya sahasā nṛpāṃtike yayau ।। tatra sa sena ālokya nṛpaṃ durād upāgataṃ । tad amṛtādikaṃ sarvam upasthāpyāpy adhaukayat ।।
tataḥ sa sena ālokya taṃ nṛpaṃ sāṃjalir mudā । praṇatvā suprasannāsyaḥ purataḥ samupāśrayat ।। tam amṛtādikaṃ sarvaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa vismito nṛpaḥ । kiṃ vilaṃvaṃ kṛtaś caitad ity evaṃ tam apṛchata ।।
iti pṛṣṭe narendreṇa sa senaḥ samupāśritaḥ । taṃ narendraṃ samālokya vinayann evam abravīt ।। kṣamasva bho mahārāja yad arthe me vilaṃvitaṃ । tat sarvaṃ samupākhyāya bhavantaṃ bodhayāny api ।।
idaṃ tāvan mahārāja suranadyamṛtaṃ pivā । idaṃ paṃcāmṛtaṃ cāpi bhukṣvedaṃ ca supiṣṭakaṃ ।। ity uktvā sa samādāya kamaṇḍaluṃ samarppayat । bhogyaṃ paṃcāmṛtaṃ cāpi piṣṭakaṃ cāgrataḥ prabhoḥ ।।
tad amṛtādikaṃ sarvaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa mudito nṛpaḥ । kamaṇḍaluṃ samādāya papau tat surasāmṛtaṃ ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatis tuṣṭo nistṛṣṇāhlāditāśayaḥ । taṃ ca paṃcāmṛtaṃ bhogyaṃ bubhuje piṣṭakāny api ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpatis tuṣṭo mahānaṃdapramoditaḥ । taṃ senaṃ sumatiṃ dhīraṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। tvam apīdaṃ sudhākalpam amṛtaṃ piva sanmate । bhukṣva pacāmṛtaṃ bhogyaṃ piṣṭakaṃ cedam uttamaṃ ।।
iti rājñā samādiṣṭe sa senaḥ pratimaṃḍitaḥ । tad amṛtādikaṃ sarvam ādāya bubhuje svayaṃ ।। tatas tac cheṣam ādāya sa senaḥ paritoṣitaḥ । aśvāya samupasthāpya sarvaṃ dadau vinodayan ।।
so api cāśvaḥ samālokya tat sarvam amṛtādikaṃ । āśvādya paribhuṃjāno mahānaṃdaṃ samāyayau ।। tataḥ sa nṛpati rājā pariśuddhāśayo mudā । taṃ senaṃ tam upāmaṃtrya punar evam apṛchata ।।
aho sena tvam ānītaṃ yad etad amṛtādikaṃ । kutaḥ kathaṃ samāsādya tat satyaṃ vaktum arhasi ।। ity evaṃ prārthite rājñā sa senaḥ sāṃjalir mudā । svāminaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ natvā samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
śṛṇu rājan samādhāya yad etad amṛtādikaṃ । mayāsādya samānītaṃ tat saṃnivedayāni te ।। yad atra tvaṃ tṛṣārtto asi tadarthe ahaṃ sasaṃbhramaḥ । jalam anveṣituṃ tatra vane paśyan bhramāmy ahaṃ ।।
kutrāpi dṛśyate nātra pānīyaṃ nirjane vane । tato dūrataraṃ gatvā jalam anveṣituṃ bhrame ।। tatrāpi dṛśyate naiva jalaṃ kvāpi samaṃtataḥ । tato atidūrato nadyāḥ śabdaṃ śṛṇvann anuvraje ।।
tacchabdānusaran gatvā paśyāmi suranimnagāṃ । tatra devīgaṇāś cāpi paśyāmi vratacārikāḥ ।। tatra tāsāṃ samālokya samākraṃdaṃti sādaraṃ । tato ahaṃ tatprabhāvena tāṃ nadīṃ laṃghayan vraje ।।
tatra māṃ samupāhūya sarvā tā apsarogaṇāḥ । kutaḥ katham ihāyāsi tvaṃ vadeti babhāṣire ।। tato ahaṃ samupāsṛtya tāḥ sarvā apsarogaṇāḥ । sāṃjaliḥ sādaraṃ natvā pura evaṃ nivedaya ।।
sūryodayo mahārājo mahīpālo narādhipaḥ । tasyodyāne varāhau dvau prakurvāta upadravaṃ ।। tan niśamya sa bhūpālaḥ samaṃtrisainyapaurikaḥ । saha bhogyaṃ samāruhya varāhau haṃtuṃ udyayau ।।
tatrodyāne caturdikṣu parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ । hāhākāraṃ prakurvantas tiṣṭhanti te nṛpādayaḥ ।। tatas tau dvau mahāghorau varāhau saha sāgataḥ । udyānān nirgatau vegān nṛpāntikāt parāgatau ।।
tatra sa nṛpatiḥ kopāt tau varāhāv anudrutaḥ । aśvam āruhya vegena praviṣṭo bhramate vane ।। tatra sa nṛpatir aśvād vegāt pradhāvato apatat । śramatāpapipāsārtto tarutale niṣīdati ।।
tasya rājñas tṛṣārttasya jalam anveṣituṃ bhraman । kutrāpi nirjane araṇye jalaṃ paśyāmy ahaṃ na hi ।। tato dūrataraṃ gatvā jalam anviṣya sarvataḥ । bhraman dūrān nadīśabdaṃ śrutvāhaṃ samupāsare ।।
etad artham ahaṃ devyo dūrataḥ sahasāgataḥ । tad bhavantyaḥ prasīdaṃtu dṛśyaṃte bhāgyato mayā ।। bhavantyo api kim arthe atra viharanti samāśritāḥ । iti pṛṣṭe mayā tāś ca devyaḥ sarvāḥ prasāditāḥ ।।
ādarān māṃ samāmaṃtrya pura evaṃ babhāṣire । mānava tvaṃ na jānīṣe yad iheva mamāśritā । tad arthaṃ samupākhyāyas tat saṃśṛṇu samāhitaḥ ।। yā śrībhagavatī devī māheśvarī vasuṃdharā ।
tasyā vrataṃ vayaṃ sarvā caritum iha saṃsthitāḥ ।। tad atra no vrataṃ paśyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭha samāhitaḥ । etaddṛṣṭe api te puṇyaṃ saṃprajāyen mahattaraṃ ।। iti tābhiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāhaṃ saṃpramoditaḥ ।
tatheti prativijñapya tad vrataṃ draṣṭum āśrame ।। tatas tā apsarodevyaḥ sarvās tatra yathākramaṃ । svasvāsane samāśritya prārabhanti yathākramāt ।। tatra tā maṃḍale devīṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṇ ।
yathāvidhiṃ samāvāhya pūjayaṃti samādarāt ।। japastotrādikaṃ kṛtvā sarvāḥ sāṃjalayaś ca tāḥ । natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya prārthayaṃti susaṃpadaṃ ।। tatas tā apsarodevyaḥ sarvāḥ samāptite vrate ।
sa paṃcāmṛtaiḥ pūpaiḥ kurvaṃti vratapālanāṃ ।। mahyam api tathā dattaṃ tābhiḥ sarvābhir ādarāt । idaṃ paṃcāṃṛtaṃ bhojyaṃ godhūmapiṣṭakaṃ varaṃ ।। smṛtvā bhavaṃtam ādāya tābhir dattaṃ samādarāt ।
tathā pātre pratiṣṭhāpya gopayāmi tavārthataḥ ।। tato ahaṃ sāṃjalir natvā tā devīḥ sakalā api । tathā caritum ālocya prārthayāmi vidhiṃ vrate ।। mayā saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā yā tad devī gaṇādhipā । sā tad vratavidhiṃ samyak samādiśati me kramāt ।।
tat sarvaṃ samupādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāhaṃ saṃpramoditaḥ । tathā tad vratam ārādhya prechāmi carituṃ sadā ।। pratyakṣadarśanaṃ labdhvā aṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇato asmy ahaṃ ।। tatas tāḥ sakalā devīḥ prārthayitvā samādārāt ।
idaṃ divyāmṛtaṃ bhojyaṃ prādāya sahasā care ।। iti heto mahārāja vilamvo jāyate tathā । tat kṣamasva prabho mātra raukṣyaṃ kṛthāḥ prasīda me ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājā vismayānvitaḥ ।
tad darśanotsuko dṛṣṭvā taṃ senam etad abravīt ।। aho āścaryyam atra yad vasudhārā vrataṃ śrutaṃ । pratyakṣadarśanam api labdhaṃ seneha nirjane ।। mayā na śrūyate kvāpi dṛśyate na kadā cana ।
tad draṣṭuṃ sena me cittaṃ samabhilaṣati dhruvaṃ ।। tasmāt tvaṃ tatra māṃ nītvā tā devī darśaya drutaṃ । iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā sa senaḥ sacivaḥ sudhīḥ । tatheti prativijñapya tatra rājñā saha caran ।।
sahasā tau pragachaṃtau taddevīdarśanotsukau । daivayogāt kṣaṇāt prāptau tatra sthāne samaikṣatāṃ ।। tadā tatra na tā devyaḥ sthitāḥ sarvā divaṃ gatāḥ । vratanirmālyapuṣpādi tatrādrāṣṭāṃ na tāḥ kvacit ।।
tatra sa nṛpatis tāsāṃ devīnāṃ darśanaṃ kvacit । alabhyamāne udvignaparikhinnāśayo abhavat ।। tatra sa nṛpatir natvā vratasthāne kṛtāṃjaliḥ । sarvatrāpi samālokya khaṃ paśyann evam abravīt ।।
hā mayā labhyate nātra devīnāṃ darśanaṃ kvacit । kiṃ mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ maṃdabhāgyo asmy ahaṃ yataḥ ।। vrataṃ caritum ichāmi tat kathaṃ jñāsyate vidhiṃ । aho me daivayogena śrutam eva na darśanaṃ ।।
tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi ko atra me vidhim ādiśet । yadichāmi na tat siddhaṃ vṛthaivetye pariśramaṃ ।। iti proktvā viṣaṇṇātmā nṛpatiḥ sa vimohitaḥ । nirāśayā vibhinnāsyo nirjale mīnajātivat ।।
hā heti ninditātmānaṃ hā me bhāgyam apīha dhik ।। ity evaṃ vilapann aśrupūrṇāsyo gadgadaḥ svaraḥ । hṛdi lalāṭe vāhubhyāṃ tāḍayan mūrchito muhuḥ ।। smṛtimāṃś ca svayam api tasthau tatra viniḥsvasan ।।
ity evaṃ taṃ sthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । ākāśān mahadāghoṣaṃ tatraivaṃ niracārayat ।। rājan mātra viṣīda tvaṃ setsyate te abhilāṣitaṃ । sarvaṃ seno vijānāti tat senaṃ pṛcha tad vidhiṃ ।।
ity ākāśāt samuccāraṃ ghoṣaṃ śrutvā sa bhūpatiḥ । sāṃjaliḥ praṇato aṣṭauṣīd ūrddhvāsyaḥ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ ।। yā susmṛtā suruciraṃ suṣṭhutaraṃ pravṛddhaṃ dāridryaduḥkhaduritaṃ śamate narāṇāṃ । tāṃ kalpavṛkṣasadṛśīṃ vasudhārasaṃjñāṃ bhaktyā namāmi śirasā jagato hitāya ।।
praṇamāmi sadā vasudhāṃ jananīṃ karuṇārdrahṛdaṃ parivīkṣya janaṃ । bahudheti bhayānvitaduḥkhataraṃ praṇamāmi sadā vasudhāṃ jananīṃ ।। pāpācārasya durbuddher durbhagasya sadā mama । kṣaṃtavyo bhūyaśaś cāgaḥ śrīvasudhe namo astu te ।।
namas te bho mahādevi prasīda me kṛpāṃ kuru । bhavaṃty atra yathādiṣṭaṃ kariṣyāmi tathā khalu ।। ity uktvā sa nṛpo bhūyas tatra natvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ । taṃ senaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā tato acarat pramoditaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpatir gachan sahasā muditāśayaḥ । tatrāśokatalāsīnam aśvaṃ paśyann upācaran ।। tatra prātaḥ sa bhūyas tam aśvaṃ dṛṣṭvā pramoditaḥ । rājā taṃ senam ānatvā dṛṣṭvā evam abhāṣata ।।
sena tam aśvam āruhya gacha tvaṃ puram āśrame । mama tavānugachāmi sahasā gachatu dhruvaṃ ।। iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā sa senaḥ sāṃjalir naman । nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
naivam atra mahārāja yan me svāmi bhavān prabhuḥ । tad bhavadvāhanaṃ hīnaṃ katham ārohayeya vai ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sūryodaya ātmavit । rājā taṃ senam ānatvā punar evam abhāṣata ।।
mā tvayaivaṃ pravaktavyaṃ yad adyārabhya bhavān guruḥ । yathākāśasamādiṣṭaṃ tat tathā karttum arhasi ।। iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā mamānukaṃpayā adhunā । śāstar agre aśvam āruhya pravrajatāmayānvitaḥ ।।
iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā tatheti sa prabodhitaḥ । svayam agre aśvam āruhya pṛṣṭhe prārohayen nṛpaṃ ।। tataḥ sa aśvas tadārūḍho vāyur iva samuccaran । mahāvegāt puropāṃtaṃ tatkṣaṇāt samupāyayau ।।
tatra taṃ nṛpam āyātaṃ samaṃtrijanapaurikāḥ । sarve te samupālokya pratyujjagmuḥ pramoditāḥ ।। tatrāśvapṛṣṭham ārūḍhaṃ nṛpaṃ senaṃ puraḥ sthitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā te maṃtriṇaḥ sarve paurāś ca vismayaṃ yayuḥ ।।
tatas te maṃtriṇo amātyā paurāḥ sarve pramoditāḥ । praṇatvā taṃ nṛpaṃ rājakule anayan mahotsavaṃ ।। tatrāśvapṛṣṭhato rājā so avaruhya svayaṃ tataḥ । senaṃ puraḥ sthitaṃ paścād avārohayad ādarāt ।।
tato rājakule gatvā nṛpaḥ pṛṣṭhataś caran । pādaprakṣālanasthāne taṃ senam evam abravīt ।। he sene sumater atra pādaprakṣālayāgrataḥ । tvattaḥ paścād ahaṃ pādau prakṣālayāmi sāṃprataṃ ।। iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā sa senaḥ sāṃjalir naman ।
nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। vibhramo asi kathaṃ rājan bhavān svāmi narādhipaḥ । tat prathamaṃ tvam evātra pādau prakṣālaya prabho ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ sa kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।
namaṃs taṃ senam ālokya tatraivaṃ saṃnyavedayat ।। bho sena yad bhavāṃ chāstā mama sanmārgadeśakaḥ । tad atra prathamaṃ pādau prakṣālayitum arhati ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa senaḥ paribodhitaḥ ।
rājña ājñā hy alaṃghyeti pādau prakṣālayet puraḥ ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatiḥ pādau prakṣālyānusaran mudā । taṃ senaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā prāsāde samupācarat ।। tatrāsane purodhāya taṃ senaṃ gurum ādarāt ।
nṛpatiḥ sa sabhāmadhye tasthau lokān vilokayan ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatir dṛṣṭvā sarvāl lokān sabhāśritān । sarvavṛttāntam ākhyāya vyanodayad vratotsave ।। tan nṛpādeśitaṃ śrutvā sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ ।
śrīdevyās tad vrataṃ dharttuṃ samaichanta dhanārthinaḥ ।। tatas sarve api te lokā natvā taṃ senam ādarāt । nṛpatiṃ ca samālokya svasvālayaṃ yayur mudā ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatis tena senena guruṇā saha ।
sānaṃdaṃ prerayām āsa dināni katicin mudā ।। tataḥ sa bhūpatī rājā tadvratasamayāgate । sāmātyān maṃtriṇān sarvān samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। bho maṃtriṇo janāḥ sarve vratasamayam āgataṃ ।
tasmāt sarve mayā sārddhaṃ vrataṃ caritum arhatha ।। tad enaṃ senam evātra pravrajyāsadguruṃ kuru । iti maṃtribhir ākhyātaṃ śrutvā nṛpas tatheti saḥ । taṃ senaṃ śāsane bauddhe prāvrājayad yathāvidhi ।।
sātha pravrajito nāmnā śrīsenagupta ity abhūt । khikkhirīpātrabhṛn muṇḍaḥ kāṣāyacīvarāvṛtaḥ ।। tatas tad vratam utsṛjya vajradharapadāptaye । vajrābhiṣekam āsādya vajrācāryo abhavat sa ca ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā tad vrataṃ karttum ādarāt । śāstāraṃ taṃ samārādhya saṃprārthayed yathāvidhiṃ ।। tataḥ śrīsenaguptaḥ sa vajrācāryo yathāvidhiḥ । śrīdevīṃ tāṃ samārādhya pūrvasevāṃ samādadhat ।।
tato bhādrapade māse dvitīyāyāṃ site tare । prātas tīrthe śubhe snātvā śuddhavastrāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ ।। prāsādopari mṛdgavyaparilipte subhūtale । vidhivan maṃḍalaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpyādhivāsayet ।।
tad rātrau ca samārādhya śrīdevīṃ vidhinārcayet । dīpadhūpādibhiś cāpi baliṃ datvābhyatoṣayat ।। tataḥ prātaḥ sa ācāryyas tīrthe snātvā suvastrabhṛt । madhyāhne svāsanāsīna uttarādiṅmukhasthitaḥ ।।
tataḥ ca gurur ācāryas trisamādhisamāhitaḥ । śrīdevīṃ sagaṇāṃ samyag āvāhya vidhinārcayet ।। tataḥ snānaviśuddhāṅgān pariśuddhāmvarāvṛtān । vratinaḥ sanṛpān sarvān paṃcagavyair vyaśodhayat ।।
tatas te vratinaḥ sarve guruṃ natvā yathākramaṃ । nṛpatipramukhā evaṃ vrataṃ caritum āśrayat ।। tatas te vratinaḥ sarve śridevīsaṃmukhasthitāḥ । yathācārya samādiṣṭaṃ tathācaran vrataṃ mudā ।।
tatra tāṃ śrīmahādevīṃ sagaṇāṃ vidhinā kramāt । samāvāhya samabhyarcya pūjāṅgaiḥ samatoṣayan ।। japastotrādikaṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā ca pāpadeśanāṃ । puṇyānumodanāṃ cāpi kṛtvā ca sthitiyācanāṃ ।।
kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve te ca kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ । aṣṭāṅgaiḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā saṃprārthayan susaṃpadaṃ ।। piṣṭakaṃ pāyasaṃ cāpi paṃcāmṛta samanvitaṃ । phalamūlādikaṃ cāpi samupāḍhokayan mudā ।।
tato lokādhipebhyo api sa bhūtebhyo mahāvaliṃ । yathāvidhi pradatvā saṃprārthayac chrī samṛddhitāṃ ।। tataḥ śāstā sa ācāryaḥ prārthayitvā kṣamāṃ mudā । sarvebhyo vratilokebhyaḥ pratyekaṃ sūtram ārppayet ।।
tat sūtraṃ vratinaḥ sarve ādāya guruṇārppitaṃ । svasvahaste abhivaṃdhitvā rakṣārtham ādarād dadhuḥ ।। yā rājño mahiṣī bhāryā cūḍadevīti viśrutā । saikā tat sūtram ādāya ca vandhan evam ādarāt ।।
tato vratasamāpte sā svālayaṃ samupāśritā । tad vratasūtram ālokya karavaddhaṃ vyaciṃtayat ।। kiṃ mamānena sūtreṇa sarvaratnādibhūṣaṇaiḥ । maṇḍitā yā kare vaddham iti tyaktuṃ samaihata ।।
tataḥ sā durmatī rājñī rakṣāsūtram api svayaṃ । karavaddham api chitvā gavākṣāt sahasākṣipat ।। tasminn avasare tatra nimvadevyāḥ sakhī vanāt । svāminyai bhojanaṃ rājñai yācituṃ samupācarat ।।
tatra sā tad vratotsāhaśabdaṃ śrutvā sa kautukā । tac chabdanihitasvāntā tasthāv ekānta āśritā ।। cūḍadevyā yad utkṣiptaṃ sūtraṃ vātāyanād bahiḥ । niścaran mūrddhani tasyāḥ sakhāḥ saṃnyapatad drutaṃ ।।
sā tat sūtraṃ samādāya paśyantī kim idaṃ nv iti । vratasūtram iti jñātvā praṇatvā muditāgrahīt ।। tataḥ sa preṣikā devyā bhogyam aprārthayaṃty api । tat sūtram eva dhṛtvāśu nimvavanaṃ mudācaran ।।
tatra sā sahasā gatvā bhartṛkāyāḥ purogatāḥ । tat sūtraṃ samupasthāpya praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat ।। jayo astu te mahādevi yad ahaṃ rājamaṃdire । tataḥ śrīvasudhārāyā vrataṃ śṛṇomi cāritaṃ ।।
cūḍadevyā svayaṃ chitvā vratasūtram idaṃ bahiḥ । kṣiptaṃ gavākṣaraṃdhrān me mūrddhni sajati niścarat ।। dṛṣṭvā tad aham ādāya vratasūtram idaṃ khalu । iti matvātra te bhogyam ayācitvā vraje drutaṃ ।।
tathāvām api he devi dhṛtvedaṃ vratasūtrakaṃ । śrīvasudhāṃ mahādevīṃ smṛtvā vrataṃ carāvahe ।। sā śrīdevī vasuṃdhārā dṛṣṭvā nau bhaktisādhanaṃ । svayam atra samāśritya saṃdadyād api saṃpadaṃ ।।
yadi nau daivayogena saṃpattir nātra vidyate । puṇyaṃ tu khalu vidyeta tataḥ syāj janma sāphalaṃ ।। iti matvātra bho devi snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtau । śrīdevīṃ manasā dhyātvā smṛtvā vrataṃ carāvahe ।।
iti sakhyā samākhyātaṃ nimvadevī niśamya sā । tathety abhyanumoditvā tathā caritum aichata ।। tatas tatheha evaṃ te snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛte । sanmṛdgomaya saṃlipte svagṛhe samupāśrite ।।
manasā śrīmahādevīṃ vasundharāṃ samādarāt । dhyātvā smṛtvā samādhāya saṃcarate vrataṃ mudā ।। tasminn avasare tatra sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । vṛddhīrūpadharā rājakuladvāram upācarat ।।
tatra sā jyāyasī vṛddhā prakīrṇaśuklamūrddhajā । upasṛtya sakhīm ekāṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। bhadrike tvam ihāgacha cūḍadevyāḥ puro gatā । tava mātāmahī dvare tiṣṭhatīti nivedaya ।।
iti tayā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā ceṭī tatheti sā । cūḍadevyāḥ purogatvā samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। devī mātāmahī vṛddhā jyāyasī te ihāgatā । bhavaṃtyo darśanaṃ kartum ichantī dvāri tiṣṭhati ।।
tad bhavaṃtī samāgacha tasyā darśanam ādarāt । datvā saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā vinodayitum arhati ।। iti tayā samākhyātaṃ cūḍadevī niśamya sā । na me mātāmahī kā sā dhyātvety evaṃ ca prāvadat ।।
mama mātāmahī nāsti kāsāv iha samāgatā । iti proktvā tvayā dvārāt sahasā preṣyatāṃ balāt ।। iti devyoditaṃ śrutvā tatheti sā sakhī gatā । vṛddhāṃtikam upāśritya dṛṣṭvā tām evam abravīt ।।
mātāmahī na me kā cid iti devī vadaty api । ataḥ sā te mukhaṃ draṣṭuṃ naiveha samupāvrajet ।। atas tvam iha mā tiṣṭha gachātaḥ sahasā vahiḥ । na vrajer yadi sā devī praiṣayet tvāṃ balād api ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā vṛddhā tata utthitā । na tiṣṭheyam iti proktvā tataḥ śanair yayau vahiḥ ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī vṛddhī rūpadharā tathā । nimvavane sthitāṃ rājñīṃ samuddharttum upācarat ।।
tatra sā jyāyasī vṛddhā śanair dvāram upāśritā । dṛṣṭvā ceṭīṃ samāhūya mṛdugiraivam abravīt ।। dārike tvam ihāgacha kiṃ cin me vacanaṃ śṛṇu । rājñā vicāraṇārthe ahaṃ śanair iha samāvraje ।।
etan me vacanam śrutvā nimvadevyā purogatā । vṛddhekā te mukhaṃ draṣṭum āgateti nivedaya ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā ceṭī sādaraṃ mudā । paśyaṃti sāṃjalir natvā tāṃ vṛddhām evam abravīt ।।
mātāmahi samāgacha bhavaṃtyā gaditaṃ yathā । tathā devyā niveditvā sahasātrāvrajāmy ahaṃ ।। ity uktvā sā sakhī tasyā nimvadevyāḥ puro gatā । muditā suprasannāsyā samālokyaivam abravīt ।।
