devi tava vicārārthe vṛddhaikeha samāgatā । tad bhavaṃtī samāmaṃtrya saṃmānayitum arhati ।। iti sakhyoditaṃ śrutvā nimvadevī samutthitā । sahasā samupāgatya tāṃ vṛddhām evam abravīt ।।
svāgataṃ bhadrike jeṣṭhe mātāmahi samāvraja । śanai dhairyaṃ samālamvya samādhāya samāsara ।। ity uktvā sā subhadrāṃśā nimvadevī samādarāt । tāṃ vṛddhāṃ samupāmaṃtrya svāsane samupāśrayat ।।
tatra sā jyāyasī vṛddhā svāsane samupāśṛtā । tāṃ rājñīṃ sudṛśālokya suprasannaivam abravīt ।। kiṃ ve atra carase vatse tan me vaktuṃ tvam arhasi । kasminn arthe abhilāṣaṃ te tavāpi me puro vada ।।
iti tayā samākhyātaṃ nimvadevī niśamya sā । tāṃ vṛddhāṃ suprasannāsyā samālokyaivam abravīt ।। kim atrāhaṃ vadiṣyāmi mandabhāgyāsmi duḥkhitā । daridritā na me saṃpad vidyate atra gṛhe kvacit ।।
vratopahārasāmagrim api kiṃ cin na vidyate । tad idaṃ kadarīpatrakṛtam arghādi bhājanaṃ ।। tan mayā śraddhayā bhaktimātreṇa śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । dhyātvā smṛtvā samārādhya saṃcaritam idaṃ vrataṃ ।।
vratasādhanasāmagrīsaṃpūrṇaṃ vidyate na me । tad vidhinā vrataiḥ karttuṃ śakyate na mayā tathā ।। tan manobhāvanāmātrapūjāṅgaiḥ śrivasuṃdharāṃ । mahādevīṃ samārādhya vratam evaṃ carāvahe ।।
etat tayā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā jyāyasī mudā । taṃ rājñīṃ sasakhīṃ bhadrāṃ samālokyaivam adiśat ।। siddhyatu te vrataṃ pūrṇaṃ carasvevaṃ samāhitā । śraddhayā bhaktibhāvena smṛtvā devīṃ sadā bhaja ।।
tathā sā śrīmahādevī vasulakṣmīḥ prasāditā । parituṣṭā gṛhe te atra sadāpi sagaṇāśnayet ।। tatas tasyā mahādevyāḥ prabhāvena sadā tava । sarvatrāpi bhaven nūnaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।।
tatas te sarvasaṃpattiparipūrṇaṃ bhaved gṛhe । tatas tvaṃ svechayā dānaṃ datvārthibhyaḥ śubhe cara ।। etatpuṇyaparītā tvaṃ sarvadā sadgatīṃ gatāḥ । pariśuddhāśayā dhīrā suśīlā śubhabhāvinī ।।
sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāptā saṃbuddhālayam āpnuyāḥ । evaṃ vijñāya bho vatse saṃbuddhapadalabdhaye । triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā śrīdevīṃ bhaja sarvadā ।। ity uktvā sā mahādevī tyaktvā vṛddhākṛtiṃ tathā ।
dhṛtvā rūpaṃ vasuṃdharyyā tasthau sarvagaṇair vṛtā ।। tāṃ devīṃ śrīprabhāsvaṃtīṃ sagaṇān samavasthitān । ālokya nimvadevī sā tasthau kṣaṇaṃ suvismitā ।। tataḥ svapnavibuddheva sākṣāt tāṃ śrīvasuṃ dharāṃ ।
dṛṣṭvā sā sahasotthāya sāṃjali nyapatat puraḥ ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī tāṃ rajñīṃ purato natāṃ । dhṛtvā hastena he vatsa uttiṣṭhety evam abravīt ।। vatse dāridryaduḥkhaṃ te naśyate sāṃprataṃ khalu ।
sarvadātra gṛhe saṃpat parivṛddhā bhaved api ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ tayā devyā nimvadevī niśamya sā । utthāya sāṃjali devīṃ prādrākṣīt tāṃ vasuṃdharāṃ ।। gṛhe cāpi mahāsaṃpat paripūrṇaṃ samaṃtataḥ ।
paśyantī kim idaṃ svapnam ity uktvā samalokayat ।। tataḥ sā śrivasuṃdhārā mahādevī gaṇaiḥ saha । bhadre anubhūyatāṃ saukhyam ity uktvānudadhau tataḥ ।। tatra sā nimvadevī tāṃ śrīdevīṃ sagaṇāṃ tathā ।
aṃtardhānagatāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇaṃ tasthau vimūrchitā ।। tataś caitanyam āṣādya sā rājñī paribodhitā । tāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ dhātvā smṛtvā tasthau samāhitaṃ ।। tatas tasyā nimvadevyā udyāneṣu samaṃtataḥ ।
sarvapuṣpadrumā jātās tathā sarvaphaladrumāḥ ।। aṣṭāṅgaguṇasaṃpanna jalapūrṇā manoramāḥ । padmotpalādi puṣpāḍhyāḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ samudbhavāḥ ।। gṛhaṃ cāpi manoramyaṃ prāspādaṃ divyasaṃnibhaṃ ।
sarvasaṃpatti saṃpūrṇaṃ śrīdapuram ivābhavat ।। tad īdṛg bhavanaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathodyānaṃ manoramaṃ । naṃditā nimvadevī sā tasthau divyasukhānvitā ।। tadā sa nṛpatiś cūḍadevyā vrataṃ na dhāritaṃ ।
vratasūtraṃ visṛṣṭaṃ ca śrutvātiruṣitābhavat ।। tataḥ so nṛpatī rājā maṃtribhiḥ paribodhitaḥ । mahiṣīṃ tāṃ priyāṃ bhāryāṃ sametyevam abhāṣata ।। are re hetunā kena tvayā na dhāritaṃ vrataṃ ।
vratasūtraṃ kathaṃ chitvā visṛṣṭaṃ tad vadasva me ।। iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā cūḍadevī pragarvitā । svāminaṃs api taṃ bhūpam anādṛtyyaivam abravīt ।। mamaitac chrīsamṛddhāsti gṛhe ratnādi saṃyutā ।
kiṃ tena vratasūtreṇa vratenāpi prayojanaṃ ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ sa prakopitaḥ । prayatnād api tāṃ bhāryāṃ bodhayituṃ śaśāka na ।। tataḥ sa nṛpati rājā tadvratadhāraṇotsukaḥ ।
sakhīm ekāṃ samāhūya pura evam abhāṣata ।। sakhī tvaṃ me vacaḥ śrutvā gacha nimvavane adhunā । nimvadevyāḥ puro gatvā vadasvaivaṃ samādarāt ।। svāmī sa nṛpatī rājā vrataṃ caritum ichati ।
vasulakṣmyās tvayā sārddhaṃ tad āśu gamyatām iti ।। sā tatheti pratiśrutya drutaṃ nimvavane gatā । dṛṣṭvodyānaṃ manoramyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ tasthau savismayā ।। tataḥ sā kautukākrāṃtahṛdayā samupāviśat ।
tatra tad bhavanaṃ ramyaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthau sakautukā ।। tataḥ sā suciraṃ dṛṣṭvā muditā vismayānvitā । nimvadevyāḥ puro gatvā pādau natvaivam abravīt ।। devi tvadantike rājñā preṣitāhaṃ samāgatā ।
tad bhavaṃtī prabhor ājñāṃ śrotum arhati sāṃprataṃ ।। sa svāmī śrīvasuṃdharyyā vrataṃ carati sapriyaḥ । cūḍadevyā vrataṃ samyakparitaṃ na pramādataḥ ।। tattvayā saha sa svāmī vrataṃ caritum ichati ।
tat tvadāhūtaye rājñā preṣitāhaṃ tathātra hi ।। tad bhavaṃtī prabhor ājñāṃ śiro dhṛtvā samādarāt । tad vrataṃ carituṃ bharttrā sahāśv āgaṃtum arhati ।। iti tayā samākhyātaṃ nimvadevī niśamya sā ।
tāṃ ceṭīṃ svāmino dūtīṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। sakhy atra śrīvasuṃdhārāvrataṃ mayā vidhāryate । paśya me saṃpado jātāḥ śrīdevīsaṃprasādataḥ ।। tad ahaṃ sāṃprataṃ tatra nechāmi carituṃ vrataṃ ।
tadarthāgamanenāpi prayojanaṃ na me adhunā ।। tad ahaṃ nāgamiṣyāmi tacchaitat kathitaṃ mayā । nṛpateḥ purato gatvā vaktavyaṃ nānyathā tvayā ।। iti tayā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā ceṭī tatheti sā ।
tāṃ rājñīṃ sāṃjalī natvā pratyāyayau nṛpālayaṃ ।। tatra sā nṛpateḥ pādau praṇamya sāṃjaliḥ puraḥ । uvācaitat pravṛttāṃtaṃ nimvadevyā yathoditaṃ ।। tat tayā kathitaṃ śrutvā sa rājā vismayāhataḥ । bhūyas tāṃ ceṭikāṃ dūtīṃ samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।।
bhūyo api tatra gacha tvaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । nimvadevīṃ samāhūya sahasānetum arhati ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ narendreṇa śrutvā sā ceṭikāpi ca । nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahārājaṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat ।।
kiṃ tatrāhaṃ gamisyāmi nimvadevīha māvrajet । yat sā tatra mahāsaukhyaṃ bhuktvā tiṣṭhati sāṃprataṃ ।। yat tasyā bhavanaṃ ramyaṃ prāsādaṃ bhavate adhunā । sarvasaṃpattisaṃpūrṇaṃ śrīdasyeva kim ucyate ।।
udyāne api manoramyāḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ samudbhavāḥ । nānāvṛkṣāś ca saṃjātāḥ phalapuṣpasamanvitāḥ ।। kim atra vahimoktena divyaśrī saṃpadānvitaṃ । yadi tad ichasi draṣṭuṃ tatra gatvābhilokaya ।।
evaṃ tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājā tṛṣitānvitaḥ । tathā tad bhavanaṃ draṣṭuṃ sahasā gaṃtum aichata ।। tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā sakhimaṃtrijanaiḥ saha । yānārūḍho vrajans tatra nimvavane upāsarat ।।
tatrodyānaṃ manoramyaṃ sarvavṛkṣāḥ samanvitaṃ । puṣkariṇīś ca dūrāt sa rājādrākṣīn manoharāḥ ।। bhavanaṃ ca manoramyaṃ prāsādaṃ divyakalpitaṃ । dṛṣṭvā sa mudito rājā sa śīghraṃ dvārāntike yayau ।।
tan nṛpaṃ samupāyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā devyāḥ sakhī drutaṃ । purataḥ sahasopetya samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। devī prasīda yad bharttā svāmīha svayam āgataḥ । tad bhavaṃtī prasannāsyā darśanaṃ dātum arhati ।।
iti sakhyoditam śrutvā nimvadevī praharṣitā । sahasotthāya paryaṅkaṃ prājñapayat sukomalaṃ ।। tatra sa bhūpatī rājā praviśya maṃdire caran । tāṃ devīṃ samupāmaṃtrya prayayau sahite janaiḥ ।।
tatra taṃ prabhum āyātaṃ nimvadevī samīkṣya sā । sahasotthāya paśyaṃtī nanāma caraṇe prabhoḥ ।। tatra sa prabhur ālokya tāṃ bhāryāṃ śrīsamāṃśikāṃ । sarvatra kuśalaṃ praśnaṃ kṛtvāsane samāśrayat ।।
tatra tāṃ śrīsamākāraṃ nimvadevīṃ nirīkṣya saḥ । rājā prabhuḥ svayaṃ dhṛtvā sahāsane nyaveśayat ।। tatas tau daṃpatī tatra sahāsane samāśritau । parasparaṃ samāśritya niṣedatuḥ pramoditau ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpatī svāmī sakautukapramoditaḥ । tāṃ bhāryāṃ śrīsamānāṃśaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ paryapṛchata ।। kathaṃ te bhavanaṃ ramyaṃ prāsādaṃ bhavane adhunā । udyānaṃ ca manoramyaṃ jāyate tad vadasva me ।।
iti pṛṣṭe nareṃdreṇa nimvadevī vinoditā । taṃ prabhuṃ sāṃjalir natvā samālokyaivam abravīt ।। śṛṇu svāmin mahārāja yadi śrotuṃ tvam ichasi । tathāhaṃ kathayiṣyāmi yan me saṃpat prajāyate ।।
pratyahaṃ yat tvayā dattaṃ tad bhogyaṃ yācituṃ sakhī । amuṣmin divase tatra mayeyaṃ preṣitācarat ।। tatreyaṃ sahasā gatvā prāsādaikāṃtam āśritā । tadā vātāyanāt kṣiptaṃ vratasūtram adho apatat ।।
tad dṛṣṭvaivaṃ sakhī gṛhya kim idam iti vīkṣya sā । vismitā sahasāgatvā mamāgre samadarśayat ।। tad dṛṣṭvāyaṃ mayā pṛṣṭā tyaktvāhāram idaṃ kutaḥ । sūtram ādāya praiṣi tvaṃ tat katham ucyatām iti ।।
tatheyaṃ paripṛṣṭā me vistareṇaivam abravīt । svāmini yadi te śrotuṃ vāṃchāsti śrūyatām iti ।। pratyahaṃ svāmināhāraṃ dattaṃ tad yācituṃ tadā । tatra rājakule devyā vratotsāhaṃ śṛṇomy ahaṃ ।।
tad vrataśabdam ākarṇya tatraikāṃte samāśritā । tadā vātāyanāt kṣiptaṃ sūtraṃ patati me mama ।। tad idaṃ sūtram ālokyamiti vismayānvitā ।ālokya kim iti? tyaktvāhāram idaṃ sūtram ādāya sahasā vraje ।। ity uktveyaṃ sakhī me agre upasthāyāpy adarśayat ।
vratasūtraṃ tad ālokya natvāgṛhnān mudādarāt ।। tataś ceyaṃ sakhi dṛṣṭvā premnā hitārthavāṃchinī । mātevānunayaṃ kṛtvā mamāgre evam abravīt ।। bhavaṃty api tathā śraddhābhaktimātreṇa sarvadā ।
śrīdevīṃ manasā dhyātvā smṛtvārādhya vrataṃ cara ।। ity asyā vacanaṃ śrutvā tathāhaṃ bhaktimātrataḥ । śrīdevīṃ manasā dhyātvā smṛtvārādhyācaraṃ vrataṃ ।। tadaikā jyāyasī vṛddhā mātāmahī tavāgatā ।
ity ākhyāya śanair atra mamāgre samupāgatā ।। mayāpi sādareṇātra natvāsane niveśitā । tataś ca māṃ samālokya kuśalaṃ samapṛchata ।। tataś cāsau parijñāya mayātra vratasādhanaṃ ।
kiṃ vrataṃ sadhyate vatsa iti māṃ paryapṛchata ।। tatas tāṃ sāṃjalir natvā nyavedayan samādarāt । mātāmahi nu me kiṃ cid api dravyaṃ na vidyate ।। tad ahaṃ śraddhayā bhaktibhāvamātreṇa sādaraṃ ।
śrīdevīṃ manasā dhyātvā smṛtvārādhya vrataṃ care ।। iti mayoditaṃ śrutvā sā vṛddhā parimoditā । tadvratavidhipuṇyāni yathā kramam upādiśat ।। tad upādiṣṭam ākarṇya muditā saṃpramoditā ।
sāṃjalis tanpadābje ahaṃ natvā tiṣṭham adhomukhaḥ ।। tadā sā tajjyāyasī rūpaṃ tyaktvātra ca kṣaṇād api । śrīdevīmūrttim ādhāya sagaṇāṃ samadarśayat ।। ato ahaṃ sahasotthāya dṛṣṭvā tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ ।
gaṇavṛtāṃ samālokya yathāśakti samarcyaṃ ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahadevī madbhaktiparitoṣitā । sagaṇā me varaṃ datvā vyavadhānam ito avrajat ।। tatas tasyā mahālakṣmyā kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ ।
idaṃ me bhavanaṃ ramyaṃ prāsādaṃ bhavate kṣaṇāt ।। udyānaṃ ca manoramyaṃ nānāpuṣpaphaladrumaiḥ । padmotpalādi puṣpāḍhyāḥ puṣkariṇyo codbhavāḥ ।। sadhāturatnajātādi sarvadravyābhipūritaṃ ।
koṣṭhāgāraṃ samudbhūtaṃ savastrālaṃkārapūritaṃ ।। sarvavrīhisamāpūrṇam ṣaḍraradravyapūritaṃ । ghṛtadadhimadhukṣīramodakādiprapūritaṃ ।। vividhapānabhojyāni paṭṭapuṣpāsanāni ca ।
phalapuṣpādi bhogyāni saṃjāyaṃte kṣaṇād iha ।। īdṛśī mahatī saṃpat samudbhūtā mama kṣaṇāt । tat sarvaṃ śrīmahādevyāḥ prasādād api nānyathā ।। iti vijñāya rājendra tasyā devyāḥ sadā mudā ।
śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā vrataṃ caritum arhati ।। etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarvadā sadgatīṃ vrajeḥ । yāvadbhavaṃ vrajer naiva durgatīṃ ca kadā cana ।। sadgatau satsukhāny eva labdho sadā śubhe caran ।
triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā bodhicaryāṃ caret kramāt ।। tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ pūrayitvā yathākramāt । svayaṃ caraṃ parāṃ cāpi bodhimārge niyojayet ।। tato māragaṇān sarvāṃ jitvā śuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ ।
arhan saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt ।। iti tayā mahādevyāḥ samupādiṣṭam atra me । tac chrutvā sarvadā svāmi mano atirocate vrataṃ ।। tad ahaṃ sarvadā tasyāḥ śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatā ।
śraddhayā bhaktibhāvena cariṣyāmi vrataṃ prabho ।। tathā bhavān api svamiñ chrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । śraddhābhaktiprasannātmā vrataṃ caritum arhati ।। iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājābhyanumoditaḥ ।
tathā sadā mahādevyā vrataṃ caritum aichata ।। tatraivaṃ sa mahīpālo nimvadevyā tayā saha । yathākāmaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā tasthau krīḍan yathechayā ।। evaṃ krīḍan sa rājendro nimvadevyā sahārataḥ ।
tatrānaṃdasukhotsāhair nyuvāsa rājyanispṛtaḥ ।। tatraivaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ nimvadevyā saha sthitaṃ । cūḍadevī samākarṇya cukopātipraroṣitā ।। tataḥ sā cūḍadevī taṃ svāminaṃ tatra saṃsthitaṃ ।
svayaṃ gatvā samākramya saṃmānayitum aichata ।। tataḥ sā krodhitā caṇḍī cūḍadevī pradhāvitā । vrajaṃtī sahasā tatra nimvavana upāsarat ।। tatra tadvratanirmālyaprakṣiptaḥ puṣpasaṃkulaṃ ।
sthānaṃ sātiprakopāṃdhā laṃghitvā sahasācarat ।। tallaṃghitātipāpena sā devī tatkṣaṇād api । kolamukhī mahāghorarūpāvichaṃditā bhavat ।। tatra tāṃ sahasāyātāṃ lokān dṛṣṭvā bhayotthitāḥ ।
kolamukhī praviṣṭeti śabdaṃ kṛtvā vicerire ।। tad virāvaṃ janāḥ sarve śrutvā tatra samutthitāḥ । kolāhalamahāśabdaṃ prakurvanta upādruvan ।। tat kolāhalaṃ śabdaṃ śrutvā saṃtrasitāśayā ।
parāyitvā tato anyatra pradudrāva vanāṃtare ।। tatraikā vibhramaṃtī sā daivasaṃpreritā vane । nirjane durgame araṇye parikhinnāpy adhāvata ।। tathā sā dūrato gatvā prādrākṣīt sarasī dvayaṃ ।
dṛṣṭvā sā tatra tṛṣṇārttā jalaṃ pātum upācarat ।। tadā te sarasī yuddhaṃ parasparaṃ pracakratuḥ । dṛṣṭvā sā vismitā apītvā jalaṃ tasthau savismayā ।। tatra te sarasī dṛṣṭvā tāṃ kolavadanāṃ striyaṃ ।
kutra gaṃtum ihaiṣi tvam ity evaṃ paryapṛchatāṃ ।। tat pṛṣṭaṃ sā samākarṇya sā śaṃkavismayāhatā । kim etad iti saṃciṃtya kṣaṇaṃ tasthau vimohitā ।। tatra sā daivayogena pratilabhya sucetanāṃ ।
kiṃ mayātrāpi vaktavyam iti dhyātvā vyaciṃtayat ।। hā katham iha prāptāhaṃ bhramāmi nirjane vane । kiṃ mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yena bhraṣṭā carāmy ahaṃ ।। hā kiṃ kuryāṃ kva gacheyaṃ sahāyaikāpi me asti na ।
sarvathātra vinaṣṭāsmi ko māṃ rakṣed ihā adhunā ।। iti ciṃtāviṣaṇṇā sā tasthau tatra nirāśitā । tataḥ sā daivayogena sasmāra śrīvasuṃdharāṃ ।। tad devīsmṛtipuṇyena sā karmabhāvinī sudhīḥ ।
yat svayaṃ prakṛtaṃ karma tat sarvaṃ paryyabudhyatāṃ ।। hā mayā durdhiyā tatra samyan na dhāritaṃ vrataṃ । etatpāpena nūnaṃ me jāte ayam īdṛśī vipat ।। tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi kolamukhī yato asmy ahaṃ ।
tat tatra kathaṃ evaṃ hi pratiyāyaṃ nṛpālayaṃ ।। yac cāhaṃ durmatir duṣṭā svakṛtapāpabhāginī । tad daivapreṣitā hy atra bhramāmi nirjane vane ।। tad atra kiṃ careyāhaṃ jīvite api na me ruciḥ ।
sarveṣām api jaṃtūnāṃ sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ।। iti matvāham atrāpi nirapekṣaḥ svajīvite । śrīdevyā darśanaṃ karttuṃ smṛtvā gacheya sāṃprataṃ ।। iti niścitya sā rājñī cūḍadevī samudyatā ।
śrīdevyā darśanaṃ kartuṃ smṛtvā caritum aichata ।। tataḥ sā cūḍadevī te sarasī dve samīkṣya ca । upetya taj jalaṃ pītvā tīre sthitvaivam abravīt ।। sarasī yad ahaṃ mūḍhā durmatī maṃdabhāginī । tac chrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ draṣṭum ihāvrajāmi hi ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā puṣkariṇyāv ubhe api te । tāṃ rājñīṃ samupāmaṃtrya nṛgiraivam abhāṣatāṃ ।। sādhu sādhu mahābhāge vrajāstu maṃgalaṃ tava । puna nau vacasā devīm evaṃ pṛcha tvam ādarāt ।।
kenāvāṃ hetunā yuddhaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhāvahe sadā ।। ity etat kathitaṃ tābhyāṃ śrutvā rājñī tatheti sā । pratijñāya tatrānyatra svadaivapreṣitācarat ।। tatrāraṇye bhramaṃtī sā kiṃ cid dūraṃ gatā tataḥ ।
mahāṃtaṃ śūkaraṃ ghoraṃ dadarśa bhīṣaṇākṛtiṃ ।। tatra sā dūrataḥ sthitvā paśyaṃs taṃ bhīmaśūkaraṃ । mātrā tiṣṭha vrajānyatra sahaseti tam abravīt ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa śūkaraḥ samutthitaḥ ।
sahasopetya tāṃ rājñīṃ samālokyaivam abravīt ।। kā tvaṃ kuta ihāyāsi kutra gaṃtuṃ pradhāvasi । ekākinī kathaṃ bhrāṃto vana etad vadasva me ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sā devī praticitritā ।
śanair upetya taṃ pretaṃ saṃpaśyann evam abravīt ।। sūryodayanarendrasya bhāryāhaṃ mahiṣī priyā । śrīdevyā darśanaṃ kartuṃ vāṃchaṃtīha samāvraje ।। iti tad gaditaṃ śrutvā śūkaraḥ so ativismitaḥ ।
tāṃ devīṃ samupāśritya paśyann evam abhāṣata ।। sādhu sādhvi mahābhāge vrajāstu te sumaṃgalaṃ । tāṃ śrībhagavatīdevīṃ mannāmnā praṇamādarāt ।। bhūyo me vacasā sādhvī tāṃ devīṃ paripṛchatāṃ ।
kenāhaṃ śūkarībhūtas tiṣṭhāmīti bhavaṃty api ।। etat tat kathitaṃ śrutvā cūḍadevī tatheti sā । pratijñāya tato anyatra vrajaṃtī sahasācarat ।। tatra sūcīmukhapretam asthikāyaṃ mahodaraṃ ।
svakeśaromasaṃchannam apaśyad dūrato vane ।। tatra sa preta ālokya tāṃ devīṃ samupāgatāṃ । sahasopetya saṃpaśyan purastha evam abravīt ।। ko tvaṃ kuta ihāyāsi kutra gaṃtum ihāgatā ।
niḥsahāyā kathaṃ bhrāṃtā carate tad vadasva me ।। iti tat kathitaṃ śrutvā sā devī vismayānvitā । śanair upetya taṃ pretaṃ paśyaṃty evam avocata ।। sūryodayamahībharttu bhāryāhaṃ mahiṣī satī ।
śrīdevyā darśane gaṃtuṃ pathānenāvrajāmi hi ।। iti tad uditaṃ śrutvā sa preto ativicitritaḥ । tāṃ devīṃ sāṃjalir natvā pura evam avocata ।। sādhu sādhvi mahābhāge carāstu te subhadrakaṃ ।
tāṃ śrībhagavatīlakṣmīṃ mannāmnā praṇamādarāt ।। bhūyo api vacasā me tāṃ śrīdevīṃ paripṛchatu । kenāhaṃ pāpakenaivaṃ tiṣṭhāmi duḥkhabhāginī ।। etat tat kathitaṃ śrutvā cūḍadevī tatheti sā । pratiśrutya gatānyatra prādrākṣīd daśapāpinaḥ ।।
te api tāṃ samupāyātāṃ dṛṣṭvopetyevam abruvan । kā tvaṃ kuta ihāyāsi kutra gaṃtuṃ ca tad vada ।। iti tair gaditaṃ śrutvā sā devī samupāsthitā । tān sarvān pāpino dṛṣṭvā pura evam abhāṣata ।।
sūryodayanarendrasya bhāryāhaṃ mahiṣī priyā । śrīdevyā darśane gaṃtuṃ pathānenāvrajāmy ahaṃ ।। iti tad gaditaṃ śrutvā sarve te daśapāpinaḥ । kṛtāṃjalipuṭā natvā tāṃ devīm evam abruvan ।।
sādhu devī mahābhāge pravrajāstu jayaṃ tava । asmākaṃ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tāṃ devīṃ paripṛchatu ।। iti tad deśitaṃ śrutvā cūḍadevī tatheti sā । tato anyatra vrajaṃty evaṃ dadarśa kṛṣṇapaṃnagaṃ ।।
tatra sa kṛṣṇasarpas tām ālokya samupāgatāṃ । sahasā samupākramya viṣāgninātyatāpayat ।। tataḥ sā mūrchitā devī cirāt svayaṃ samutthitā । tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ smṛtvā tatra tasthau kṣaṇaṃ tathā ।।
tataḥ sā suṃdarīrūpā tyaktakolamukhābhavat । kālasarpaḥ sa tām āha kā tvaṃ kutaḥ samāgatā ।। cūḍadevī tataḥ prāha sūryodayapriyāsmy ahaṃ । śrīdevīdarśanārthaṃ tu āgatā mānyatha phaṇi ।।
tataḥ pātakamuktā sā pracaraṃtī bubhukṣitā । bījapūrakam ālokya tad ādātum upācarat ।। tatra tat phalam ālokya hastābhyāṃ sahasāgrahīt । tasya hi daivayogena tatphalaṃ na vyamuṃcyata ।।
tatra sā tatphale lagnahastā tasthau tathā kṣaṇaṃ । tataḥ sā trasitā dṛṣṭvā na gṛhnāmīti cāvadat ।। etad ukte bhujau tasyās tat phalaṃ sahasātyajat । tataḥ sā vismitānyra bhramaṃtī dūrato avrajat ।।
tataḥ sā dūrato nadyāḥ śabdaṃ śrutvā pradhāvitā । svadaivapreṣitā tatra tīram avāpatat kṣaṇāt ।। tatra sā taj jalaṃ pātuṃ sahasā samupācarat । tatra sā taj jalaṃ pītvā snātvā caiva samāśrayat ।।
tatra sā dūrataḥ pūrṇahemaghaṭaśirovahāḥ । surāṃgaṇāḥ subhadrāṃgā dadarśa samupāgatāḥ ।। tatra sā tāḥ samālokya sahasopetya sāṃjaliḥ । praṇatvā samupāsīnā samīkṣyaivam apṛchata ।।
aho bhāgyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ yad bhavatyātra darśitā । tad dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā sarvā snātum arhanti sarvathā ।। bhavaṃtyo amṛtasaṃpūrṇahaimaghaṭaśirovahāḥ । kutra gaṃtuṃ caraṃty atra satyam etad vadaṃtu me ।।
iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā tāsām ekā pradhānikā । sālokya cūḍadevīṃ tāṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। bhadre tvaṃ na jānāsi yā śrīdevī vasuṃdharāḥ । tasyā ime amṛtā pūrṇā nīyaṃte snapane ghaṭāḥ ।।
devīsnānodakaiḥ sarvair eṣā nadī vahaty api । etan nadyamṛtenātra netre prakṣālya dṛśyatāṃ ।। evaṃ devyā tayādiṣṭaṃ cūḍadevī niśamya sā । tathety abhyanumodaṃtī tathā kartuṃ samaichata ।।
tataḥ sā tan nadītīre sthitvāmṛtena cakṣuṣī । saṃprakṣālya tataḥ sasne papau tad amṛtaṃ mudā ।। tato nirmuktapāpā sā cūḍadevī pavitritā । sudṛṣṭir abhavat tatra samaṃtāpratihatekṣaṇaḥ ।।
tatrasthā cūḍadevī sā prādrākṣīt tat kṣaṇād api । śrīvasudhāṃ mahādevīṃ sagaṇāṃ maṇḍalāsthitāṃ ।। tatra tāṃ śrīmahādevīṃ dṛṣṭvā sā pratimaṃḍitā । sahasā sāṃjalir natvā paśyaṃtī samupācarat ।।
tatra sā samupetyāśu kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ mudā । sagaṇāṃ sa mahādevīṃ praṇanāma kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī cūḍadevīṃ samīksya tāṃ । svāgatāsi samehi tvam ity evaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
evaṃ devyā tayādiṣṭaṃ cūḍadevī niśamya sā । sāṃjalir aśru mocaṃtī devyāḥ pādāmbuje apatat ।। tataḥ sā śrīvasuṃdhārā mahādevī vilokya tāṃ । pādābje patitāṃ dhṛtvā samāśvāsyaivam ādiśat ।।
bhāgini bhadra uttiṣṭha dhairyam ālaṃvya paśyatāṃ । mā viṣīda prasīdātra pūrayāmi tavaihitaṃ ।। etat tayā mahādevyā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya sā । cūḍadevī prasannāsyā praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat ।।
bhagavati jagadbhartti vasudhāre maheśvari । bhavatyāḥ śaraṇaṃ yāmi kṣamasva me aparādhatāṃ ।। prasīda me mahādevi kṛpānugrahatāṃ kuru । yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat sarvaṃ kṣaṃtum arhati ।।
yad etad dūrato cāhaṃ samāyātāsmy avighnataḥ । tad bhavatyāḥ prasādena nānyatheti hi manyate ।। tad iha te mahādevyā śraddhayā śaraṇāsthitā । vrataṃ caritum ichāmi tat prasīda kṛpānidhe ।।
iti tayārthitaṃ śrutvā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । tāṃ śraddhābhisaṃśuddhāṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu vatse punar gatvā svapure svāminā saha । ācāryeṇa yathādiṣṭaṃ vrataṃ kuru samāhita ।।
tadā tatra gṛhe te ahaṃ svayam āgatya saṃsthitā । kariṣyāmi sadā bhadraṃ sarvatra nirupadravaṃ ।। tadā te sarvadā gehe dehe ca maṃgalaṃ bhavet । tataḥ sarvārthasaṃpattiḥ parivṛddhāḥ susaṃsthitā ।।
tatas tad artham ādāya dehe arthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā carasva sarvadā śubhe ।। tathā saṃpārapūrya tvaṃ sarvāḥ pāramitāḥ kramāt । trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyasi ।।
etad devyā samādiṣṭaṃ cūḍadevī niśamya sā । tathety abhyanumodaṃtī pratyaśroṣīt praṇāmitā ।। tataḥ sā cūḍadevī ca tāṃ śrīdevīṃ vasuṃdharāṃ । suprasannā samānamya samīkṣyaivaṃ nyavedayat ।।
yan mārgasthitair lokaiḥ saṃdarśitaṃ vaco asti me । dadehaṃ praṣṭum ichāmi bhagavati samādiśa ।। mārge ahaṃ sarasī dṛṣṭvā jalaṃ pātum upācaraṃ । tadā te sarasī yuddhaṃ prākurvatāṃ parasparaṃ ।।
tatas te vigrahāṃte māṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ paryapṛchatāṃ । kutra gaṃtum ihāyāsi tat satyaṃ kathyatām iti ।। tac chrutvā vismayākrāṃtahṛdayāhaṃ vilokya te । śrīdevīdarśanaṃ gaṃtum ihaimīty avadam api ।।
evaṃ mayoditaṃ śrutvā sarasī ta ubhe api ca । māṃ sa kṛtāṃjalir natvā samīkṣyaivam abhāṣatāṃ ।। yad āvāṃ vigrahaṃ nityaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhāvahe mithaḥ । tan no pāpena keneti śrīdevīṃ paripṛchatu ।।
kiṃ tābhyāṃ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yad evaṃ vigrahaṃ mithaḥ । kṛtvā te tiṣṭhato devi tat samādeṣṭum arhati ।। iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । samīkṣya cūḍadevīṃ tāṃ samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।।
bhaginyau tau purābhūtaṃ bhojane samaye sadā । ākruṣya vigrahaṃ kṛtvā pratikṣepaṃ pracakratuḥ ।। tena pāpena tau dve api sarasī bhūtvā parasparaṃ । sarvadā vigrahaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhataḥ sāṃprataṃ tathā ।।
evaṃ tayoḥ puraḥ proktvā citte tvaṃ paribodhaya । etac chrutvaiva te vākyaṃ pāpān muktvai cyato divaṃ ।। tato asau cūḍadevī ca natvā tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । sāṃjaliḥ suprasannātmā samīkṣyevaṃ nyavedayat ।।
bhūyo api śrīmahādevi śūkaro dṛśyate pathi । so api māṃ samupāyātaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ paryapṛchata ।। kutra gaṃtum ihāyāsi vadasveti niśamya tat । śrīdevīdarśane gaṃtum ihaimīty avadam ahaṃ ।।
tataḥ sa śūkaraś cāhaṃ prarudat purāto mama । kiṃ mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpam iti devy abhipṛchyatāṃ ।। kiṃ tena prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ purā kutra kadā kathaṃ । tat sarvaṃ samupādiśya prabodhayatu me manaḥ ।।
iti tat pṛchitaṃ śrutvā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । samīkṣya cūḍadevīṃ tāṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। bhaṇḍāgārī purābhūt sa viśvāsaghātakaḥ kudhīḥ । janebhyo bhojanaṃ kiṃ cid datvā sarvaṃ gṛhe anayat ।।
etatpāpavipākena bhavati śūkaro adhunā । etat mayā yathākhyātaṃ tathā tasya puro vada ।। sa tvatkathitam ākarṇya pāpamukto divaṃ vrajet ।। iti devyā samādiṣṭaṃ cūḍadevī niśamya sā ।
tatheti prativijñapya punar evaṃ nyavedayat ।। punar mārge mayā dṛṣṭaḥ pretaḥ sūcīmukho mahān । kiṃ tena prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tava devi samādiśa ।। iti tat kathitaṃ śrutvā sā śrīdevī maheśvarī ।
samīkṣya cūḍadevīṃ tāṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt ।। purā sa brāhmaṇo vidvān vedavid vādasaṃrataḥ । siddhāṃtavādino bauddhān pratikṣipyābhiniṃdayan ।। lobherṣyāmadamātsaryaparītātmā hi mānikaḥ ।
āgṛhītapariṣkāraḥ svārthātilālasaḥ kudhīḥ ।। parebhyo dattam ālokya lobhātikaluṣāśayaḥ । sa chidravacasākruṣya bauddhe dānaṃ nyavārayat ।। saddharmaśrāvakān sarvān dṛṣṭvā sa duritāśayaḥ ।
praduṣṭavacasākṣipya niṃdayan pratyavārayat ।। kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ saddharmavighnakāriṇā । triratnabhajanotsāhavighātābhyanurāginā ।। etatpāpavipākena brāhmaṇaḥ sa durāśayaḥ ।
sūcīmukho mahākāyaḥ preto bhavati sāṃprataṃ ।। etan mayā yathākhyātaṃ tathā tasya puro vada । etat te kathitaṃ śrutvā smṛtimān sa sudhīr bhavet ।। tataḥ sa svakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ sarvaṃ smṛtvādiśan svayaṃ ।
triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā samichec carituṃ śubhe ।। tato vimuktapāpaḥ sa pariśuddhāśayaḥ sudhīḥ । namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vadan bhajet ।। tatas tat pretalokāt sa samutthāya vikalpakaḥ ।
pretāśayaṃ parityajya tato api hi divaṃ vrajet ।। iti tasyā mahādevyā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya sā । cūḍadevī prasannāsyā punar evaṃ nyavedayat ।। bhūyo api pathi bho devi dṛśyate duḥkhitā mayā ।
kiṃ kiṃ taiḥ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat sarvaṃ samupādiśa ।। iti saṃprārthite rājñyā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā । niśamya cūḍadevīṃ tāṃ samīkṣyaivam upādiśat ।। te sarve pāpino duṣṭā daśākuśalacāriṇaḥ ।
adyāpi duḥkhasaṃtaptā bhramaṃti bhavasāgare ।। yo hatvā prāṇino bhuṃkta so alpāyuṣko bhave bhraman । adyāpi tadvipākena tiṣṭhaty evaṃ suduḥkhitaḥ ।। yo adattaṃ dravyam ādāya prābhuṃkta mithyayāharan ।
sa daridro mahāduṣṭo bhavaty adyāpi duḥkhabhāk ।। yo mithyākāmarāgāṃdho agamyā api prabhuktavān । sa sveṣṭasujanais tyakto bhavaty arivaśe sthitaḥ ।। mṛṣāvādena yo lokañ jayann abhyavaṃcayat ।
sa kuṣṭharogavān pūtigaṃdhavaho bhavaty api ।। piśunavacanai yo sanmitrabhedaṃ bhave akarot । so puṇyakalahonmādī sarvaśatrur bhavaty api ।। yo asau vibhratsito lokair durākṛtir durāśayaḥ ।
sa pāruṣyavacasā lokāt purākruyyaty abhaṃdayat ।। sarvabhinneva vā yo asau nighnito nādritaḥ kudhīḥ । sa purā bhinnavādena lokaṃ bhinnāśayaṃ vyadhāt ।। yo asau vimohito mūrkhā vipannabuddhir unmanāḥ ।
sābhidhyāyatasā loke saṃpattīś chadmanāhatat ।। vidveṣī durmatā mohī yo asau sajjanagarhitaḥ । sa vyāpādakhilacittena satvāpakāra udyataḥ ।। yo asau nīcā viṣaṇṇātmā hīneṃdriyo durāśayaḥ ।
mithyādṛṣṭi sa saddharmam adhikṣiptvābhyaniṃdayat ।। iti ye daśā pāpāni prakurvanto caren mudā । sarve te pāpino duṣṭā bhavaṃti duḥkhino adhunā ।। evaṃ mayā yathākhyātaṃ tathā teṣāṃ puro vada ।
etat tvaduktam ākarṇya smareyus te purākṛtaṃ ।। tatas te durgate bhītāḥ sadgatītamanotsukāḥ । saddharmasādhanaṃ karttuṃ samicheyuḥ samādarāt ।। tadā tāṃ pura āmaṃtrya sarvān evaṃ vadādarāt ।
yadi cāsti śubhe vāṃchā triratnaṃ sevyatām iti ।। tataḥ sarve ime yūyaṃ nirmuktapātakā dhruvaṃ । sahasā sadgatau saukhyaṃ labhedhvam iti cābruhi ।। tatas te te vacaḥ śrutvā sarve satsaukhya ālasāḥ ।
triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayāyuḥ surālayaṃ ।। ye buddhe śaraṇaṃ yāṃti na te gaṃchaṃti durgatīṃ । kramāt pāramitāḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ ।। śṛṇvaṃti ye ca saddharmaṃ na te gachaṃti durgatīṃ ।
sarvadā sadgatiṃ yātāḥ pracareyuḥ śubhe mudā ।। ye bhajaṃti mudā saṃghe te api na yāṃti durgatīṃ । sadā lokaśubhaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ ।। kālasarppo mayā dṛṣṭo bhūyo mārge maheśvari ।
kiṃ tena prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tad vadasva vasuṃdhare ।। purā āḍhyo gṛhastho abhūd vistīrṇaparivārakaḥ । saṃpadām udayair nityaṃ dānadasyeva saṃyutaḥ ।। tena kākavaliṃ dātuṃ na prasehe kadā cana ।
dvijān vinīpakān dṛṣṭvā cittaiḥ prāduṣāyet sadā ।। kasmai cid api kiṃcid vā hy adatvā bubhuje svayaṃ । sarvadhanasvakodyāne sthāpayām āsa durmatiḥ ।। pātakenā adhunā tena kṛṣṇasarppo bhavaty asau ।
tasyāpi purataḥ sarvaṃ madādiṣṭaṃ tathā vada ।। so api nirmuktapāpaś ca mṛtaḥ svargaṃ vrajed dhruvaṃ ।। yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva paribhujyate । abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana ।।
ity etad evam ākhyataṃ śrutvā tvaṃ ca samādarāt । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara me vratam uttamaṃ ।। tathā lokeṣu sarvatra pracāraya mama vrataṃ । etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadā te bhavec chubhaṃ ।।
tato bodhimatiṃ prāptaḥ purāyitvā yathākramaṃ । sarvāḥ pāramitā hodhiṃ prāpya buddhapadaṃ vrajeḥ ।। iti vijñāya kalyāṇi gatvā taṃ svapure punaḥ । śraddhayā svāminā sārddhaṃ vrataṃ cara samādarāt ।।
ity uktvā sā mahādevī sagaṇā śrīvasuṃdharā । tataś cāṃtarhitā svarge svālayam āgamad drutaṃ ।। tatra sā cūḍadevī tāṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । aṃtardhānagatāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇaṃ tasthau savismayā ।।
tataḥ sā cūḍadevī tām sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । smṛtvā kṛtāṃjalir natvā tataḥ pratyāyayau mudā ।। tataḥ sā cūḍadevī tāṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । manasānusmaranty eva pracaraṃti nyavarttataḥ ।।
taṃ kṛṣṇasarpam ālokya cūḍadevī bravīti sā । devyā yathā copadiṣṭaṃ tathā tena purākṛtaṃ ।। tannāmasmaraṇāt so hityaktvā dehaṃ divaṃ yayau । tatra mārge sametyāsau cūḍadevī yathākramaṃ ।
tāṃ daśapāpinaḥ sarvān samīkṣya samupācarat ।। tatra sā cūḍadevī tān daśākuśalacāriṇaḥ । pṛṣṭvā devyā yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā sarvam upādiśat ।। tac chrutvānusmṛtiṃ prāptāḥ sarve te vismayānvitāḥ ।
satyam iti prabhāṣaṃtaḥ śrīdevīśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। tatas te pāpinaḥ sarve śrīdevīdṛkprabhānvitāḥ । trimaṇḍalaviśuddhāś ca śubhe caritum īchire ।। tatas te śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ dhyātva vrataṃ samācaran ।। tatas te śuddhitātmānaḥ sarve api nirmalāśayāḥ । tatraivaṃ tāṃ mahādevīṃ dhyātvā mṛtā divaṃ yayuḥ ।। tataś ca cūḍadevī sā pracaraṃtī samāgatā ।
sūcīmukhaṃ tam ālokya dūrataḥ samupācarat ।। tatra sā sahasā tasya pretasya purato gatā । śrīdevyāḥ samupādiṣṭaṃ tathā sarvam abhāṣata ।। tac chrutvā sa purāvṛttam anusmṛtvā niciṃtayat ।
paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptaḥ kṣaṇaṃ tasthau viniḥśvasan ।। tataḥ sa manasā dhyātvā tāṃ śrīdevīṃ vasuṃdharāṃ । smarantī sāṃjalir natvā dideśa sarvapātakaṃ ।। tataḥ sa pariśuddhātmā nimuktapātakaḥ sudhīḥ । śrīdevīśaraṇaṃ gatvā dehaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau ।।
tataś ca cūḍadevī sā pracaramṭī samāgatā । śūkaraṃ taṃ samālokya dūrataḥ samupācarat ।। tataḥ sopasthitā tasya śūkarasya purākṛtaṃ । yathādiṣṭaṃ mahādivyā tathā sarvam upādiśat ।।
tac chrutvā śūkaraḥ so api samanusmṛtim āptavān । tatrānutāpasaṃtaptaḥ kṣaṇaṃ tasthau viciṃtayan ।। tataḥ sa manasā dhyātvā tāṃ śrīdevīṃ vasuṃdharāṃ । saṃsmṛtvā sāṃjalir natvā dideśa sarvapātakaṃ ।।
tato nirmuktapāpo asau pariśuddhāśayaḥ sudhīḥ । śrīdevīśaraṇaṃ gatvā dehaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau ।। tataś ca cūḍadevī sā pracaraṃtī samāgatā । durāt te sarasī dṛṣṭvā sahasā samupāsarat ।।
tatra sā samupāsṛtya puṣkariṇyos tayoḥ puraḥ । mahādevyā yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā sarvam upādiśat ।। tac chrutvā puṣkariṇyau tau samanusmṛtim āptuḥ । tatrānutāpataptā tau nidhāya taṣṭhatuḥ kṣaṇaṃ ।।
tatas te manasā dhyātvā taṃ śrīdevīvasuṃdharāṃ । saṃsmṛtvā sāṃjalir natvā dideśatuḥ svapāpakaṃ ।। tato vimuktapāpau tau pariśuddhāśayo drutaṃ । puṣkariṇyāśrayaṃ tyaktvā prayayatuḥ surālayaṃ ।।
tatra sarve api te svarge gatās tat smṛtibhāvinaḥ । dhyātvā tāṃ śrīmahādevīṃ smṛtvā nityaṃ prabhejire ।। tatra teṣāṃ mahādevyāḥ prasādāc chrī pravarddhitāḥ । tac chrīsaṃpanmahatsaukhyaṃ bhuktvā sarve te araman ।।
tataḥ sā cūḍadevī tān sarvān kṛtvā vimuktitān । svadeśyābhimukhāyātā sva purāṃtikam āyayau ।। tatra tāṃ samupāyātāṃ dṛṣṭvā lokāḥ pramoditāḥ । sahasā nṛpater agre gatvaivaṃ saṃnyavedayat ।।
jaya deva mahārāja cūḍadevī nivarttitā । tad bhavān sahasopetya tāṃ samānetum arhati ।। iti niveditaṃ taiḥ sa rājā śrutvā pramoditaḥ । sahasā maṃtriṇo amātyān samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।।
cūḍadevī samāyātā tad yūyaṃ sahasādarāt । pratyudgamya mahotsāhair ihānayata tāṃ priyāṃ ।। iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te maṃtriṇo janāḥ । amātyāḥ sahasā sarve tathety uktvā mudācaran ।।
tatas te maṃtriṇo amātyāḥ sajanāḥ paurikā api । sarve pratyudgatā tatra cūḍadevī samāyayuḥ ।। tatra sarve api te lokā dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sahasādarāt । praṇatvā yāta āropya mahotsāhaiḥ pure anayat ।।
tatra sā mahiṣī devī mahotsāhapramoditā । praviśya maṃdire rājñaḥ svāminaḥ samupācarat ।। tatra sā svāminaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasopetya sāṃjaliḥ । praṇatvā svāminā tena sahāsane samāśrayat ।। tatra sa nṛpatiḥ svāmi tāṃ devīṃ supriyāṃ mudā ।
saṃpaśyan kauśalaṃ pṛṣṭvā puna evam apṛchata ।। kena tvaṃ hetunā kutra gatā kuto adhunāgatā । etat sarvaṃ samākhyāya mano me paribodhaya ।। ity etat svāminā tenādiṣṭaṃ cūḍadevī niśamya sā ।
svapravṛttāṃtam ākhyāya mārgavṛttiṃ nyavedayat ।। tato ahaṃ sahasā yātā draṣṭuṃ devīṃ vasuṃdharāṃ । tatra dūrān nadīśabdaṃ śrutvāhaṃ samupācaraṃ ।। tatra tīre mayā dṛṣṭā devyā jalaghaṭāvahāḥ ।
bhavaṃtyaḥ kuta āyātā iti pṛṣṭe avadaṃ ca tāḥ ।। vasudhārāmahādevyāḥ snānārtham ime ghaṭāḥ । nīyaṃte amṛtasaṃpūrṇā asmābhir iti manyatāṃ ।। eṣā nadī mahādevīsnānāmṛtapravāhitā ।
tad etad amṛte nātra mukhaṃ prakṣālya dṛśyatāṃ ।। iti tābhiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā tatheti bodhitā । tan nadyā amṛtenāsyaṃ prakṣālya kṣam ahaṃ tathā ।। tadā tatra sabhāsīnāṃ sagaṇāṃ śrivasuṃdharāṃ ।
apaśyaṃ tāṃ nadīm āśu laṃghitvā samupācaraṃ ।। tatrāhaṃ samupāśritya tān devīṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ । sagaṇāṃ sāṃjalir natvā tatraikāṃte upāśrayaṃ ।। tadā sā śrīmahādevī māṃ dṛṣṭvaivam apṛchata ।
kutaḥ kim artham āyāsi tad iha kathyatām iti ।। tac chrutvā sāṃjalir natvā kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇāṃ । sagaṇāṃ tāṃ mahādevīm upāśrityaivam abruvaṃ ।। sūryodayanarendrasya bhāryāhaṃ mahiṣī priyā ।
bhavatyā darśanaṃ karttuṃ mudātra samupācare ।। yan mayā maṃdabhāvinyā vrataṃ samyag na dhāritaṃ । tan mahad aparādhaṃ me bhavatā kṣaṃtum arhati ।। sarvadāhaṃ mahādevī bhavatyāḥ śaraṇe sthitā ।
samyag vrataṃ punar dharttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ khalu ।। tad bhavaṃtī mahādevī kṛtvā me anugrahaṃ punaḥ । kṛpayā tadvratālaṃbhaṃ kārayituṃ samarhati ।। iti mayārthitaṃ śrutvā sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā ।
kṛpādṛṣṭyā samālokya mām evaṃ samupādiśat ।। sādhu vatse asti te vāṃcā yadi me vratadhāraṇe । gatvā tvaṃ svagṛhe bhartrā saha vrataṃ carādarāt ।। tadāhaṃ svayam āgatya drakṣyāmi maṃdiraṃ tava ।
tatrāhaṃ samupāśritya dāsyāmi prārthitaṃ varaṃ ।। ity ādiṣṭaṃ mahādevyā śrutvāhaṃ paribodhitā । tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīm apṛchaṃ punar ādarāt ।। devi mārgasthitair lokaiḥ saṃdarśitaṃ mayocyate ।
tad bhavaṃtī samākhyāya māṃ bodhayitum arhati ।। tac chrutvā sā mahādevī taiḥ sarvaiḥ prakṛtaṃ yathā । tat tat sarvaṃ tathā teṣāṃ karma me samupādiśat ।। tato ahaṃ śraddhayā bhaktimātreṇa taṃ vasuṃdharāṃ ।
śrīdevīṃ sagaṇāṃ cāpi samārcayaṃ samādarāt ।। tataḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā । aṣṭāṃgaiḥ śrīmahādevyāḥ pādābje praṇatāpataṃ ।। tataḥ sā sagaṇā devī kṣaṇād aṃtarhitābhavat ।
tata utthāya tāṃ devīṃ naivāpaśyat kuhāpi ca ।। tato ahaṃ vismayākrāṃtahṛdayā tatra kṛtāṃjaliḥ । smṛtvā sagaṇāṃ devīṃ natvā śanais tato acaraṃ ।। tatra mārge samāsādya sarvāns tān pāpinaḥ kramāt ।
mahādevyā yad ādiṣṭaṃ tathākhyāya vyanodayaṃ ।। tatas te pāpinaḥ sarve vacasā me anutāpitāḥ । śrīdevīśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dehaṃ tyaktvācaran divaṃ ।। etān satvān samuddhṛtya śrīdevyāḥ saṃprasādataḥ ।
kṣemeṇeha samāyātā bhavatāṃ darśanaṃ labhe ।। ity evaṃ sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ cūḍādevyā niveditaṃ । śrutvā sa nṛpatiḥ svāmī vismitaś caivam abravīt ।। aho bhāgyena saṃprāptā śrīdevyā saṃprasādataḥ ।
bhāryā tvaṃ mahiṣī cāpi vrataṃ śrīsaṃpado api me ।। tathā bhūyo apy ahaṃ devyā yathādiṣṭaṃ samādarāt । saha tvayā mahiṣyātra carāṇi sarvadā vrataṃ ।। kim etad rājyabhogyena vinā tvāṃ mahiṣīṃ mama ।
etad eva hi saṃsāraṃ yat sabhāryā vrataṃ caret ।। tad āvāṃ sarvadāpīha śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatau । śraddhayā vratam ārādhya prabhajeva samādarāt ।। ity evaṃ samupādiśya nṛpatiḥ saṃpramoditaḥ ।
tābhyāṃ yuto mahotsāhaiḥ śrīnagaraṃ samāyayau ।। tayā devyā subhāvinyā sahābhyānaṃdito aramat । dinaikasmiṃś cūḍadevī tato garbhan dadhau kramāt ।। prāsūta saptame māsi rājalakṣaṇamaṃḍitaṃ ।
prāsādikaṃ supīnāṃgaṃ putraṃ brāhme muhurttake ।। tataḥ pitā samāhūya sarvān amātyamaṃtriṇaḥ । śrīsenaguptam ācāryaṃ papracha janmakāraṇaṃ ।। senagupto vicāryaivaṃ bodhayan nṛpam abravīt ।।
mā viṣīdātra rājendra yuto yad rājalakṣaṇaiḥ । yogo ayaṃ sārvabhaumaḥ syāt saptamāsaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।। prathame kalalaṃ vidyād dvitīye ghanam eva ca । tṛtīyamāsyaṃ krūraṃ ca caturthe asthisamuccayaḥ ।।
paṃcame carmasaṃchannaḥ ṣaṣṭhe aṃgajasamudbhavaḥ । saptame cetanāvāptir iti garbhasthalakṣaṇaṃ ।। yo bālaḥ saptame māsi jāyate sa tu bhāgyabhāk । sārvabhauma nṛpo bhūtvā mahīṃ śāsti sunītitaḥ ।।
tasmān nṛpeṃdra taṃ bālaṃ rakṣaṇīyaḥ prayatnataḥ । ity ācāryavacaḥ śrutvā sa rājā parimoditaḥ । jātakarmādikaṃ karma mahotsavair akārayat ।। tadācāryaḥ senagupto vratamaṃgalakārakaṃ ।
iti matvā nāma cakre maṃgalodaya ity api ।। tato bālaḥ śuklapakṣe caṃdra iva dine dine । pupoṣa vṛddhiṃ sahasā tejobalasamanvitaḥ ।। tato rājakule rājā bhāryāputrasamanvitaḥ ।
vasuṃdharāvratotsāhī muditaḥ samupasthitaḥ ।। tato vratadinaprāpte bhāryayā saha saṃmataṃ । kṛtvā sa bhūpatī rājā vrataṃ caritum aichata ।। tatas tad vratasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvā yathāvidhi ।
ācāryeṇa yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā sarvaṃ samācarat ।। śrīdevyā vratam ārādhya samahiṣī sa bhūpatiḥ । yathāvidhi susaṃpūrṇa pracacāra samādarāt ।। tasminn avasare tatra sā śrīdevī vasuṃdharā ।
sagaṇā svayam āgatya bhāsayaṃtī samāśrayat ।। tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ samupāśritāṃ । sākṣād ālokya rājā sa sabhāryaḥ samupasthitaḥ ।। pādārghaṃ sahasā datvā pūjāṃgaiś ca samarcayat ।
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ natvā sāṃjalir nyapatat puraḥ ।। tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī vasulakṣmī vilokya taṃ । sabhāryaṃ nṛpam utthāya samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā te yat samīpsitaṃ ।
sarvaṃ te ahaṃ pravakṣyāmi satyam etad vaco mama ।। ity ādiṣṭe mahālakṣmyā sabhāryaḥ sa nṛpo mudā । tāṃ devīṃ sāṃjalir natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt ।। namas te śrīmahādevī prasīda parameśvaśrī ।
yathā te īhitaṃ kāryaṃ tad eva dehi me varaṃ ।। etat saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā sā śrīmaheśvarī । sabhāryaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।। sādhu rājan svayaṃ dhṛtvā vrataṃ sarvatra cāraya ।
kṛtvaitan me mahatkāryaṃ tataḥ praihi mamālayaṃ ।। ity ādiśya tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī vasuṃdharā । sagaṇā tat kṣaṇād aṃtarhitā svaṃ bhuvanaṃ yayau ।। tataḥ sa sapriyo rājā tāṃ devīṃ sagaṇām api ।
sarvām antarhitāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇaṃ tasthau savismayaḥ ।। tatas tathā sa bhūmīndro bhāryayā saha sarvadā । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā vrataṃ dhṛtvā samācarat ।। tathā sarvatra lokeṣu śrīdevyā vratam ādiśat ।
bodhayitvā prayatnena prācārayat samaṃtataḥ ।। tathā sa nṛpatir devyā vrataṃ sarvatra cārayan । sarveṣām api satvānāṃ maṃgalaṃ sarvadākarot ।। etatpuṇyavipākena sa rājā śrīsamanvitaḥ । divyātiriktasaukhyāni labdhvā sadā śubhe acarat ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā sarvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । saṃbodhipraṇidhānena datvā vrataṃ sadācarat ।। tathā sa bhūpatī rājā bhāryayā saha moditaḥ । śrīdevyāḥ pradadhe bhaktyā vrataṃ sāṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ।।
tataḥ sa bhāryayā sārddham abhiṣiṃcyātmajaṃ sutaṃ । svapade lokadharmārthaṃ kṛtvānte tuṣite yayau ।। tataḥ sa sapriyas tatra śrīdevyāḥ samupasthitaḥ । sarvadā bhajanaṃ kṛtvā śrīmāns tasthau śubhe caran ।।
tatra sa sarvadā satvahitaṃ kṛtvā sukhānvitaḥ । sarvāḥ pāramitāḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyati ।। tadārabhya sadā sarvalokeṣu satataṃ śubhaṃ । triratnabhajanotsāhaṃ pravarttate kṛtāv iva ।।
tadā bhuvi tathā devyā svayaṃ vrataṃ pracāritaṃ । ity etan munibhiḥ sarvaiḥ khyātam iti śrutaṃ mayā ।। etan me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ maya tathocyate । tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ mahārāja śrīdevyāś cara tad vrataṃ ।।
tathā te sarvadā kṣemaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । śrīdasyeva mahāsaṃpad akṣīṇā saṃbhavet khalu ।। tatas tvaṃ śrīsamādhārā datvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
evaṃ matvā mahārāja prajāś cāpi prabodhayan । śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇe sthāpya sadā vrataṃ pracāraya ।। tathā satvahitaṃ kartuṃ saṃbodhiratnalabdhaye । śrīdevyā dhāraṇīvidyā pradhātavyā sadādarāt ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarvatra sarvadā bhave । bhavetaṃ maṃgalotsāhaṃ satataṃ nirupadravaṃ ।। atītair api saṃbuddhaiḥ sarvair api munīśvaraṃ । śrīdevyā dhāraṇīvidyāratnair lokahitaṃ kṛtaṃ ।।
tathādhunāpi sarvaiś ca varttamānair munīśvaraṃ । tridevyā dhāraṇīvidyāratnaiḥ satvaśubhaṃ kṛtaṃ ।। tathā cānāgataiḥ sarvai munīndrair api sarvataḥ । śrīdevyā dhāraṇīvidyāratnaiḥ kariṣyate śivaṃ ।।
sarve api sugatā nāthā bodhisatvāḥ kṛpālavaḥ । śrīdevīsaṃprasādena caranto bhadracārikāṃ ।। āryyasaddharmam ādiśya prakurvate jagaddhitaṃ । evaṃ jagaddhitaṃ karttuṃ saṃbodhiratnam īpsubhiḥ ।
śrīdevyā dhāraṇīṃ dhṛtvā caritavyaṃ jagaddhite ।। ye cāpi śrīmahādevyā dhāraṇīṃ śraddhayādarāt । bhaktyā paṭhaṃti śṛṇvaṃti pāṭhayanty api sarvadā ।। likhitvā pustake vāpi gṛhe sthāpya sadādarāt । satkṛtya śraddhayābhyarcya dhṛtvāṃjaliṃ namaṃti ye ।।
tathā bhurje likhitvā ca vāhau kaṇṭhe ca mastake । śrīdevyā dhāraṇīvidyāratnaṃ dadhati ye sadā ।। eteṣām api sarveṣāṃ gṛheṣu viṣayeṣv api । sarvatra maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ nirvighnaṃ sarvadā bhavet ।।
ītaya upasargāś ca mahotpātā upadravāḥ । na teṣāṃ viṣaye kvāpi pracareyuḥ kadā cana ।। jvarāś ca vividhā rogāḥ sarvasaṃhārakārakāḥ । tesāṃ kāyeṣu sarvatra na spṛśeyuḥ kadā cana ।।
apathyam api pathyaṃ syād viṣo api cāmṛtaṃ bhavet । teṣāṃ deheṣu sarvatra hitāyate ahito api ca ।। brahmaśakrādayo devā ye duṣṭā vahnayo api ca । yamasya kiṃkarāś cāpi rākṣasā garuḍā api ।।
nāgāś ca vāyavaś cāpi yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnarāḥ । bhūtapretapiśācāś ca kumbhāṇḍāḥ kaṭapūtanāḥ ।। evam anye api ye duṣṭāḥ sarvasatvabhayaṃkarāḥ । sarve te viṣaye teṣāṃ vighnaṃ karttuṃ na śaknuyuḥ ।।
sarve devādayo apy ete tridhātubhuvanasthitāḥ । teṣāṃ devīprabhāvena rakṣeyuś ca prasāditāḥ ।। teṣāṃ kāryāṇi sarvāṇi saṃsiddhyeyur avighnataḥ । teṣāṃ sarvatra kāyeṣu kiṃcid vighnaṃ bhaven na hi ।।
sarvatra gachatāṃ teṣāṃ salābhasiddhimaṃgalaṃ । bhaved eva sadā naiva vighnatā syāt kadā cana ।। śrīdevīkṛpādṛṣṭiprabhāvena samaṃtataḥ । sarvārthasādhane siddhir bhaven na tu vighātatā ।।
sarve api lokapālāś ca devādayo maharddhikāḥ । yatayo yoginaḥ siddhā ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। grahās tārāgaṇāḥ sarvā yoginyo bhairavā api । ḍākinyo mātṛkāṣṭāś ca mahākālagaṇā api ।।
evam anye api vīreśāḥ sarvaduṣṭapramardakāḥ । sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhārakārakā bhīmarūpiṇaḥ ।। te api sarve samālokya śrīdevīsevakān mudā । kṛpārddāḥ samupāśritya rakṣeyuḥ sarvadānugāḥ ।।
sarve api bhikṣavo buddhā arhanto brahmacāriṇaḥ । śrīdevī bhāvino dṛṣṭvā saṃrakṣeyuḥ prasāditāḥ ।। sarve pratyekabuddhāś ca tāñ chrīdevyā upāśrikān । dūrataḥ sudṛśālokya saṃrakṣeyuḥ prasāditāḥ ।।
bodhisatvāś ca sarve api tāṃc chrīdevyā upāsakān । yathepsitaṃ varaṃ datvā pālayeyuḥ kṛpānvitāḥ ।। sarve api sugatā buddhāḥ śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇe sthitān । sudṛśā sarvadālokya sa bhaveyur dayānvitāḥ ।।
evaṃ sarve api lokeśā brahmā viṣṇuśivādayaḥ । śrīdevīdhāraṇīvidyādharāṃ rakṣeyur ādarāt ।। evaṃ sarvair mahābhijñair munīndrair gaditaṃ khalu । iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate ।। śrutvā rājaṃs tvam apy evaṃ tac chrīdevīvrataṃ cara ।
tatas te śrīmahādevīvratapuṇyānubhāvataḥ ।। mahāsaṃpat pravṛddhā syād akṣīṇā sarvadā sthirā ।। tatas tvaṃ tad dravyam ādāya sarvārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ । datvā carac chubhe saukhyaṃ bhuṃkṣva saṃpālayan prajāḥ ।।
etatpuṇyavipākena durgatīṃ na vrajeḥ kvacit । sarvadā sadgatīṃ yātā dharme caran sukhaṃ vaseḥ ।। iti matvā mahārāja śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । saddharmaṃ svayam ākarṇya lokāś ca śrāvaya prabho ।।
sarveṣām api saṃsāre dharma eva suhṛt sakhā । tasmād atra prayatnena dharma eva samarjyāṃ । dharmaṃ tu sarvadharmāṇāṃ praśreṣṭhaṃ saugataṃ varaṃ ।। yataḥ sarvatra lokeṣu saṃsāre bhadratā sadā ।
tasmāt sarvatra saṃsāre sadā bhadraṃ samīpsubhiḥ । satkṛtya saugataṃ dharmaṃ śrotavyaṃ śraddhayādarāt ।। ye apy atra saugataṃ dharmaṃ śṛṇvaṃti śraddhayādarāt । durgatīṃ te na gachaṃti saṃyāṃti sadgatīṃ sadā ।।
ye cāpi saugataṃ dharmaṃ śrāvayaṃti parān api । te api na durgatīṃ yāṃti yāṃti sadgatim eva hi ।। yaś cāpi saugataṃ dharmaṃ prabhāṣati prabedhayan । so api na durgatiṃ yāti saṃprayāyāt sukhāvatīṃ ।।
yasyāpi syāt kalau paṃcakaṣāyakleśasaṃkule । durlabhaṃ saugataṃ dharmaṃ vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ ।। tadā tān kleśitāl lokān dṛṣṭvā ghṛṇādayāhataḥ । svakāyajīvitasnehaṃ tyaktvā yo dharmam ādiśet ।।
sa eva hi mahābhijño dhīraḥ sudhīr vicakṣaṇaḥ । sarvakleśavijetā ca mārajit syāj jinātmajaḥ ।। yaś cāpi ca tadā kleśasaṃghasamākule tathā । tyaktaḥ svaprāṇakāyo yaḥ saddharmaṃ śṛṇuyān mudā ।।
sāpi dhīro mahāvīraḥ sarvakleśābhimardakaḥ । saṃbodhimārgasaṃprāpto jñātavyo hi jinapriyaḥ ।। yaś cāpy eva kalau kāle saddharmāntarhite tathā । nisnehasvāsukāyo yaḥ saddharmaṃ śrāvayet parān ।।
sa api syāt sugataputro mahādhīro viśāradaḥ । sarvasarvahitākāṃkṣī bodhisatvaḥ sudhīḥ kṛtī ।। yaś cāpi parataḥ śrutvā saddharmaṃ saugatoditaṃ । anumodet prasannātmā so api syāt sugatātmajaḥ ।।
sarvatīrthābhiṣeke yat puṇyaṃ tat sarvam āpnuyuḥ । sarvatra sajjanā nūnaṃ karttavyaṃ nātra saṃśayaṃ ।। yāvaṃtaḥ prāṇinaḥ satvās tān sarvān yo hi pālayet । tasya yāvan mahatpuṇyaṃ tat sarvaṃ te samāpnuyuḥ ।।
yāvaṃto bhikṣavo arhantas tān sarvān yaḥ samarcayet । tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yāvat tat sarvaṃ te hy avāpuyuḥ ।। yāvat pratyekabuddhāś ca tān sarvān yo bhajen mudā । yāvat puṇyaphalaṃ tasya labheyus te tato arthikaṃ ।।
yāvaṃtaḥ sugatāś cāpi tān sarvān yaḥ sadā bhajet । yāvat puṇyaṃ mahat tasya labheyus te tato adhikaṃ ।। yāvaṃto bhūtale gavas tān sarvāñ chraddhayā dadet । tasya yāvan mahatpuṇyaṃ prāpnuyus te tato adhikaṃ ।।
merupramāṇasauvarṇaratnarāśiṃ ca yo dadet । tasya puṇyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ prayāyus te tato adhikaṃ ।। sābdhiśailaṃ mahīṃ sarvāṃ śraddhayā yaḥ samarppayet । tasya bahutaraṃ puṇyaṃ samyāyus te tato adhikaṃ ।।
sauṣadhīdravyabhogyādīn pradadyāc chraddhayāpi ca । tasya puṇyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ labheyus te tato adhikaṃ ।। yasya kalpasahasrāṇi tṛṇāmbuprāśanastayet । yāvaṃtasya mahatpuṇyaṃ labheyus te tato adhikaṃ ।।
yajñakoṭisahasrāṇi kuryād yaḥ śraddhayā mudā । tāvat tasya mahatpuṇyaṃ prāpnuyus te tato adhikaṃ ।। evaṃ yāvaṃti puṇyāni dānavratodbhavāny api । saṃti tato adhikaṃ puṇyaṃ te sarve samavāpnuyuḥ ।।
iti satyaṃ samākhyātaṃ sarvair api munīśvaraiḥ । etan me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā ca vakṣyate ।। etat satyaṃ parijñāya yadi saṃbodhim ichasi । sadā saddharmam ākarṇya triratnabhajanaṃ kuru ।।
prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ । bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ ।। tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ ।।
etat tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ । tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ ।। tataḥ sa upagupto arhan vihāre samupāśrayet । so aśoko api mahārājas tathā dharmaṃ sadācarat ।।
etad evaṃ samākhyāya jayaśrī sa jinātmajaḥ । sarvāsāṃ śiṣyasaṃghāṃś ca samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat ।। subhāṣitamahāratnamālām imāṃ prabhāṣati । yo yatra meva śṛṇvaṃti śrāvayaṃty api ye mudā ।।
śrutvānumodaṃti ye ca dṛṣṭvā namaṃti ye mudā । satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ samabhyarcya bhajaṃti ye ।। eteṣāṃ tatra sarveṣāṃ bhavaṃtu maṃgalaṃ sadā । jayaśrī parivṛddhāstu sarvatra sarvadāpi ca ।।
ītaya upasargāś ca sarve vighnagaṇā api । duṣṭā māragaṇāṃś cāpi vilayaṃ yāṃtu sarvadā ।। gṛheṣu sarvadā teṣaṃ lakṣmīs tiṣṭhatu susthirāḥ । dharmārthakāmabhogyāś ca saṃsiddhyaṃtu sa medhitāḥ ।। nīrogā sucirāyuṣkā bhavaṃtu te sukhānvitāḥ ।
viratapāpakarmāṇaḥ pracaraṃtu śubhe sadā । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā bhavaṃtu brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। sarvasatvahitaiḥ kṛtvā bhuktvā bhadrasukhaṃ sadā । kramāt pāramitāḥ pūrya vrajaṃtu saugataṃ padaṃ ।।
etatpuṇyānubhāvena tatra sarvatra sarvadā । bhavaṃtu maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ subhikṣaṃ nirupadravaṃ ।। sarve satvāś ca saddharmaṃ sādhayaṃtu samudyatāḥ । triratnabhajanotsāhaiḥ sarve vrajaṃtu saugatiṃ ।।
kāle varṣaṃtu meghāś ca bhūyāc chasyavatī mahī । bahukṣīrapradā gāvo bhavaṃtu vatsalānvitāḥ ।। sarvadā suphalaiḥ puṣpaṃ vṛkṣāḥ saṃtu samanvitāḥ । rājā bhavaṃtu dhārmiṣṭho nayasthāḥ saṃtu maṃtriṇaḥ ।।
sarve sainyāś ca yodhāro jayaṃtu dūrjanān narīn । sarvetayaḥ praśāmyaṃtu saṃtu saukhyānvitāḥ prajāḥ ।। nīrujāḥ sukhasaṃpannāḥ śrīsaṃpattisamanvitāḥ । brahmādi lokapālāś ca daśadikpā maharddhikāḥ ।
vighnāñ jitvā śubhaṃ kṛtvā pālayaṃtu prajāḥ sadā ।। sarve traidhātulokāś ca kṛtvā maitrīṃ parasparaṃ । triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caraṃtu bodhicārikāṃ ।। sarve bhadrāṇi paśyaṃtu mā kaścit pāpam ācarat ।
sarvatra śāsanaṃ bauddhaṃ dhṛtvā yāṃtu jinālayaṃ ।। evaṃ jayaśrīr munirājakalpaḥ saṃbodhicaryāpravikāśahetoḥ । sarvān svaśiṣyān paribodhayan saḥ samādideśa śryavadānamālāṃ । śrutvāpi te sarva udāracittāḥ śrutvā salokā abhinaṃdyamānāḥ ।
saddharmam āśritya sadā triratnaṃ bhaktyā bhajaṃta vyaharan pramādā ।। yatredaṃ sūtrarājeṃdraṃ prāvarttayet kalāv api bhāṣed yaḥ śṛṇuyād yaś ca śrāvayed yaś ca cārayet । eteṣāṃ tatra sarveṣāṃ saṃbuddhāḥ sakalā sadā kṛpādṛṣṭyā samālokya kurvaṃtu bhadram ābhavaṃ sarvāḥ pāramitā devyas tesāṃ tatra sadā śivaṃ । kurvantyo bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayaṃtu jagaddhite ।
anena saddharmarasāmṛtena sarvajñabhāsvadvadanodbhavena । kleśānalaprahvarir āturāsu prajāsu duḥkhaṃ praśamo astu nityaṃ ।। śreyo astu samvat māghamāse kṛṣṇapakṣe dvitīyāyāṃ tithau pūrvaphālguṇīnakṣatre suddhayoge budhavāsare kuṃbharāśigate savitari siṃharāśigate caṃdramasi etaddine saṃpūrṇam idaiḥ pustakaṃ mānadevasaṃskāritacakramahāvihāre nivāsitaḥ vajrācāryyaśrīdharmmarājena likhitam idaṃ pustakam etatpuṇyena dharmmārthakāmamokṣān prāptim astu śvapustakasunānaṃ lobhayāyamadu ।।
